[I,001,2_I,001,4]	 pramiti viśiṣṭa anantarya pratipādanāt ca tad abhāva nirāsaḥ atas śabdaḥ api hetau vartamānaḥ viśiṣṭa deśa kula prasūtam aviplutena brāhmaṇena aviplutāyām brāhmaṇyām vighnu deśa avasitāyām upajātam śuśrūṣā śravaṇa grahaṇa dhāraṇa ūha apoha tattva abhiniveśa vat antevāsinam āha iti tathā ca sa aṅgāḥ catur vedān va sumatiḥ brāhmaṇaḥ bhagavantam ulūkam ājagāma na ha vai sa śarīrasya priya apriyayoḥ upahatiḥ asti aśarīram vāva santam na priya apriye spṛśataḥ iti vākyāt aśarīra avasthāyām sukha duḥkham aniśam pratipadyate pakāṇāt adarśanam āpta vat tat ca yathā upapannam bhagavān adhikāriṇam dṛṣṭvā samādhi balāt ekasmin aṇau utpanna ṣaṭpadārtha tattva jñānaḥ maheśvareṇa upadiṣṭa sūtra karaṇe pravṛttaḥ 
[I,001,15_I,002,1]	tad artha siddhaye sūtra sandarbhasya ca ati saṃkṣipta tvāt avedyatayā vā asmad ādeḥ tattva jñānam na syāt iti praśasta pāda saṃkṣepaḥ tvādivat apratibhāsanāt adhikārya bhāvaḥ tat asat upadeśa vyaṅgya tvāt tathā hi dravya ādiṣu iva kṛta samayasya anugatam jñānam i brāhmaṇaḥ ayam iti jñāne paścāt bhā vi bādhaka anupapatteḥ pramāṇa tayā śiṣṭa padārtha adhikāri siddheḥ nirviṣaya tvāt na doṣaḥ nirabhidheya tvam avisiddham dravya ādi bhāvaḥ ca nirastaḥ eva tad abhidhānāt tathā prayojana upanyāsāt tad abhāvaḥ ca iti atha kim punar ca vijñānam kim vā niḥśreyasam iti vācyam avasthita padārtha vi na vānām ātma viśeṣa guṇānām atyanta ucchittiḥ na dharma artha kāmāḥ teṣām alpa sādhana sādhya tvāt 
[I,002,5]	atha niḥśreyasa astitve kim pramāṇam vibhu cetanam anumāna bhāga va tathā hi navānām ātma viśeṣa guṇānām santānaḥ atyantam ucchidyate santāna tvāt yaḥ yaḥ santānaḥ sa saḥ atyantam ucchidyamānaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ yathā pradīpa santānaḥ tathā ca ayam santānaḥ tasmāt tam ucchidyate iti santāna tvasya ca vyāptyā buddhayā ādiṣu sambhavāt pakṣa dharma tayā asiddha tva abhāvaḥ tad samānarmiṇi ca pradīpa ādau upalambhāt aviruddha tvam na ca pakṣe paramāṇu ādau asti saṃ iti anaikāntika tva abhāvaḥ viparīta artha upasthāpakayoḥ pratyakṣa āgamayoḥ anupalambhāt na kāla atyaya apadiṣṭaḥ na ca ayam sat pratipakṣaḥ iti pañca rūpa tvāt pramāṇam 
[I,002,15]	atha nirhetukāvinā prati vaśya anta ādeḥ eva hetuḥ vācyaḥ yatas samucchidyate iti sa tu uktaḥ eva tattva jñānam niḥśreyasa hetuḥ iti nirdeśāt ca tattva jñānam aviśiṣṭa tvāt na prativyakti apekṣam kintu ityādi lakṣaṇāt tathā hi dravya ādi lakṣaṇa lakṣiteṣu utpadyate tattva jñānam iti 
[I,002,20]	atha tattva jñānasya niśreyasa kāraṇa tve samutpanna tattva jñānaḥ tu anantaram eva apamṛdyam manasi asambhave asmad ādīnām tattva jñāna anupapattiḥ atha yoga ja dharmāt upajāta tattva jñānaḥ asmad ādeḥ tattva jñāna sampādanāya kaṇādaḥ sūtrāṇi karoti iti avasthām iṣyate gata arha tattva jñānasya niḥśreyasa kāraṇe sati api abhāvāt na eṣa doṣaḥ viśiṣṭa tattva jñānasya niḥśreyasa kāraṇa tva abhyupagamāt tathā hi upajāte api śraute tattva jñāne asmad ādīnām niḥśreyasam yoga abhyāsa janita tattva jñānasya asambhavāt śraute hi tattva jñāne samutpanne yoga abhyāse pravartamānasya abhyāsa vaśāt ātmani aśeṣa viśeṣa āliṅgite antyam tattva jñānam upajātam niśśreyasa kāraṇam iti 
[I,003,1_I,003,5]	tathā hi upalabdham samyak jñānasya mithyājñāna nivṛttau sāmarthyam śuktikā ādau iti samyak jñānasya jñāna antara virodhi tvāt uttara kāla bhāvinā mithyājñānena api samyak jñānasya virodhaḥ sambhavati eva yadi sā manaḥ santāna ucchittiḥ vivakṣitā iti yathā hi samyak jñānāt mithyājñānasya santāna ucchedaḥ na evam mithyājñānāt samyak jñānasya iti nivṛtte ca mithyājñāne tad mūla tvāt rāga ādayaḥ naśyanti kāraṇa abhāvena kāryasya anutpādāt iti rāga ādi abhāve ca tad kārya apravṛttiḥ vyāvartate tad abhāve ca dharma adharmayoḥ anutpattiḥ ārabdha kāryayoḥ ca upabhogāt prakṣayaḥ iti 
[I,003,8_I,003,13]	katham tattva jñānāt eva iti yathā uktam yathā edhāṃsi samiddhaḥ agniḥ bhasmasāt kurute kṣaṇāt jñāna agniḥ sarva karmāṇi bhasmasāt kurute tathā iti nanu upabhogāt eva prakṣayaḥ iti api āgama uktam yathā uktam na abhuktam kṣīyate karma kalpa koṭi śataiḥ api avaśyam anubhoktavyam kṛtam karma śubha aśubham 
[I,003,17_I,003,21]	tathā ca viruddha artha tvāt ubhayoḥ katham prāmāṇyam iti bhogāt ca prakṣaye api anumānam api asti pūrva karmāṇi upabhogāt eva kṣīyante karma tvāt yat yat karma tat tat upabhogāt eva kṣīyate yathā ārabdha śarīram karma tathā ca amūni karmāṇi tasmāt upabhogāt eva kṣīyante iti upabhogena ca prakṣaye karma antarasya avaśyambhāvāt saṃsāra anucchedaḥ tat asat samādhi balāt utpanna tattva jñānaḥ hi karmaṇā añca sādhyam artham viditvā yugapad śarīrāṇi nirmāya upabhoga ktaḥ iti na ca karma antara utpattiḥ mithyājñāna janita anusandhāna ākhyasya sahakāriṇaḥ abhāvāt 
[I,003,24]	atha mithyājñāna abhāve abhilāṣasya abhāvāt bhoga anupapattiḥ tat na upabhogam vinā hi karma yāḥ anupapatteḥ jānan api tad arthi tayā pravartate eva vaidya upadeśāt ātura vat auṣadha āvaraṇe jñānam api evam aśeṣa śarīra utpatti dvāreṇa upabhogāt karmaṇām vināśe vyāpārāt agni iti vyākhyeyam na tu sākṣāt na ca etat vācyam tattva jñāninām karma vināśaḥ tattva jñānāt itareṣa antu upabhogāt iti jñānena karma vināśe prasiddha udāharaṇa abhāvāt 
[I,004,3_I,004,6]	anye tu mithyājñāna janita saṃskārasya sahakāriṇaḥ abhāvāt vidyamānāni api karmāṇi na janma antare śarīra ārambha kāṇi iti manyante atra ca kārya vastunaḥ nitya tvam syāt iti dūṣaṇam atha anāgatayoḥ dharma adharmayoḥ utpatti pratiṣedhe tattva jñāninaḥ nitya naimittika anuṣṭhānam tarhi katham pratyavāya parihāra artham tathā hi nitya naimittikaiḥ eva kurvāṇaḥ durita kṣayam jñānañca vimalīkurvan abhyāsena tu pācayet abhyāsāt pakva vijñānaḥ kaivalyam labhate naraḥ iti 
[I,004,11_I,004,15]	kevalantu kāmye niṣiddhe ca pravṛtti pratiṣedhaḥ iti yat vā tattva jñāninaḥ nitya naimittika anuṣṭhāne na nivartate dharma utpattiḥ tathā eva abhisandhānāt tad phala sannyāsaḥ vā tathā hi sarva karmaṇām parama gurau arpaṇam iti śrūyate na vā pravṛttiḥ pratisandhānāya hīna kleśasya iti alam atha astu tattva jñānam niḥśreyasa kāraṇam avadhāraṇantu niṣidhyate sannyāsa ādi kriyāyāḥ ca mokṣa hetu tvena śravaṇāt tathā hi sannyasyantam dvijam dṛṣṭvā sthānāt calati bhāskaraḥ mama eṣa maṇḍalam bhitvā prayātā lokam akṣayam dvau etau puruṣau loke sūrya maṇḍala bhedinau parivrāj yoga yuktaḥ ca raṇe ca abhimukhe hataḥ iti ādi uktam 
[I,004,23_I,004,26]	satyam sannyāsa ādi kriyāyāḥ sūrya maṇḍala bhedi tvena ūrdhva gamana hetu tvam iṣyate eva yadi nāma lokam iti abhidhānāt akṣaya tvam adhastana loka apekṣayā kriyā antara phala apekṣayā vā draṣṭavyam tathā hi sannyāsa ādi lakṣaṇa kriyā bhautikāni akriyā apekṣayā pradhāna bhūtā iti na ca navānām ātma viśeṣa guṇānām atyanta ucchittiḥ niḥśreyasam sūrya maṇḍala bhedi tvena bhavati iti tasya viśeṣa guṇa viyukta ātma rūpa tayā sarvatra bhāvāt atas eva na tattva jñāna kārya tvāt anitya tvam iti vācyam viśeṣa guṇa ucchedasya pradhvaṃsa rūpa tvāt tad upalakṣita ātmanaḥ eva nitya tvāt iti kārya vastunaḥ ca anitya tvam iti na ca buddhi ādi nāśe guṇinaḥ tathā bhāvaḥ tādātmya pratiṣedhasya vakṣyamāṇa tvāt 
[I,005,4_I,005,7]	atha mokṣa avasthāyām caitanyasya api ucchedāt na kṛtabuddhayaḥ pravartante iti ānanda rūpaḥ mokṣaḥ iṣyatām iti manuṣe yathā uktam ānandam brahmaṇaḥ rūpam tat ca mokṣe abhipadyate iti tathā sukhena aham asva apsam iti suṣupti avasthā uttara kālam smaraṇāni atha anupapattyā anubhavaḥ jñāyate tatra ca abhidhāna anumānayoḥ vyāpāraḥ anupalabdhaḥ bāhya indriyāṇāñcaḥ iti antaḥkaraṇasya vyāpāraḥ jñāyate iti mānasam pratyakṣam anumānañca ātmā sukha svabhāvaḥ atyantam priya buddhi viṣaya tvāt ananya paratayā upādīyamāna tvāt ca yat yat evaṃvidham tad tad sukha svabhāvam yathā vaiṣayikam sukham tathā ca ātmā evaṃvidhaḥ tasmāt sukha svabhāvaḥ iti 
[I,005,12_I,005,18]	tat etat asat bādhaka upapatteḥ tathā hi tasya anitya tāyām utpatti kāraṇam vācyam na ca mokṣa avasthāyām ātma antaḥkaraṇa sambandhaḥ śarīra sambandha apekṣaḥ sambhavati śarīra ādeḥ abhāvāt na ca asamavāyi kāraṇam vinā vastu utpattiḥ dṛṣṭā atha nityam tat sukham iti ced ajñāta saṃvedanantu yadi nityam muktā avasthāyām iva saṃsāra avasthāyām api bhāvāt aviśeṣa prasaṅgaḥ smaraṇa anupapattiḥ ca anubhavasya eva avasthānāt saṃskāra anupapattiḥ ca anubhavasya niratiśaya tvāt atha saṃsāra avasthāyām vā anya viṣaya vyāsaṅgāt vidyamānasya api anubhavasyā saṃvedanam tad abhāvāt ca mokṣa avasthāyām vedanam iti asti viśeṣaḥ 
[I,005,20]	tat asat nitya sukhe hi anubhavasya api nitya tvāt vyāsaṅga anupapattiḥ tathā hi ātmanaḥ rūpa ādi viṣayaka jñāna utpattau viṣaya antare jñāna anutpattiḥ vyāsaṅgaḥ evam indriyasya api ekasmin viṣaye jñāna janaka tvena pravṛttasya viṣaya antare jñāna ajanaka tvam vyāsaṅgaḥ na ca evam ātmanaḥ rūpa ādi viṣayaka jñāna utpattau nitya sukhe jñāna anupapattiḥ tat jñānasya api nitya tvāt na ca śarīra ādinā pratibadhya tvāt asaṃvedanam iti vācyam nitya tvāt eva tathā hi pratibandhakam kārya vyāghāta kṛt ucyate na ca nitya sukha jñānasya anutpattiḥ sambhavati tathā upabhoga artha tvāt ca śarīra ādeḥ bhoga pratibandhaka tva anupapattiḥ yat yad artham tat tasya eva pratibandhakam iti na upalabdham pratibandhaka tvena tad apahantuḥ hiṃsā phalam na syāt tathā hi pratibandha vighātakaḥ upakārakaḥ eva iti dṛṣṭam tena hi nitya sukha saṃvedana pratibandhakasya śarīra ādeḥ apahantuḥ hiṃsā phalasya abhāvaḥ iti alam 
[I,006,4_I,006,7]	atha anityam tad saṃvedanam iti ced na utpatti kāraṇa abhāvāt atha yoga ja dharma apekṣaḥ puruṣa antaḥkaraṇa saṃyogaḥ asamavāyi kāraṇam iti ced na yoga ja dharmasya api anitya tayā vināśe apekṣā kāraṇa abhāvāt atha ādya saṃyoga ja dharmāt upajātam vijñānam apekṣya uttaram vijñānam tasmāt ca uttaram iti santānaḥ tat na pramāṇa abhāvāt tathā ca śarīra sambandha anapekṣam vijñānam eva ātma antaḥkaraṇa saṃyogasya apekṣā kāraṇam iti na dṛṣṭam na ca dṛṣṭyā viparītam śakyate hi anujñātum ākasmikantu kāryam na bhavati eva atas eva nitya sukha jñānasya abhāvāt sukhena aham asva apsam iti jñānam na idam smaraṇam kim tarhi duḥkha kāraṇa anusmaraṇa abhāvena tad abhāva anumiti jñānam etat sukhena aham asva apsam iti viparyaye vā nitya sukha vat duḥkhena aham asva apsam iti smaraṇāt nitya duḥkham api syāt atha suṣupti avasthā antarāle duḥkha kāraṇa saṃvedanāt duḥkhena aham asva apsam iti jñānam etat evam tarhi tad abhāvāt sukhena aham iti bhaviṣyati iti 
[I,006,15_I,006,18]	atha āgamaḥ tarhi katham ānandam brahmaṇaḥ rūpam ityādi mukhye hi bādhaka upapatteḥ gauṇaḥ iti tathā hi duḥkha abhāve ayam ānanda śabdaḥ prayuktaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ sukha śabdaḥ duḥkha abhāve yathā bhāra ākrāntasya vāhakasya tad apāyaḥ iti yat ca anumānam ātmā sukha svabhāvaḥ iti tatra yadi sukha svabhāva tvam sukha tva jāti sambandhi tvam tat na ātmani sambhāvyate guṇaḥ eva upalambhāt na hi ekāḥ ahaṅkāra ādi vat aparā jātiḥ dravya guṇayoḥ sādhāraṇi upalabdha iti atha sukha adhikaraṇa tvam tat na asti nitya anitya tva vikalpa anupapatteḥ tathā sukha tva adhikaraṇa tve sukha adhikaraṇa tāyām vā tat jñānasya nitya anitya tva vikalpaḥ sādhanam vā atyanta priya buddhi viṣayam ananya paratayā upādīyamāna tvañca anaikānta āt asādhanam duḥkha abhāve api bhāvāt ananya para tayā upādīyamāna tvañcā siddham sukha artham upādānāt tathā atyanta priya buddhi viṣaya tvam api asiddham duḥkhitāyām apriya buddheḥ api bhāva āt iti anumāna dvayam apramāṇam 
[I,006,26_I,007,3]	yadi ca mokṣa avasthāyām nityam sukham asti iti abhilāṣeṇa pravarteta na muktaḥ syāt rāgasya bandhana rūpa tvāt atha buddhi ādikam upacchedayāmi iti dveṣāt api pravartamānasya tat eva dūṣaṇam na anukūla tvāt tathā ca pratikūlasya adoṣasya pratiṣedhasya tad rāge api samānam iti adūṣaṇam etat iti anya dūhyam atha sarva guṇa ucchedāt varam vaiṣayikam sukham duḥkha sādhana parihāreṇa bhoktavyam iti manyase tat na tasya duḥkha anuṣaṅgeṇa duḥkha rūpa tayā heya tvāt yeṣāñca etat upādeyam na tān prati idam arthavat śāstram santi ca vaiṣayika sukha dveṣiṇaḥ puruṣāḥ tān pratīdam śāstram te ca yadi upadeśam apekṣante na upāya antarāt eva artham pratipadya anuṣṭhāne pravartante iti mokṣa astitve ca pramāṇa upapatteḥ śeṣam vacana mātram iti upekṣyate 
[I,007,8]	anye tu anyathā bhūtāt eva sādhanāt anyathābhūtam mokṣam manyante yathā uktam guṇa puruṣa antara viveka darśanam niḥśreyasa sādhanam iti tathā hi puruṣa arthena hetunā pradhānam pravartate puruṣa arthaḥ ca dvedhā śabda ādi upalabdhiḥ guṇa puruṣa antara viveka darśanañca sampanne hi puruṣa arthe caritārtha tvāt na pradhānam śarīra ādi bhāvena pariṇamate iti draṣṭuḥ sva rūpeṇa avasthānam bhavati iti vijñātam vā draṣṭṛ tayā kuṭṭinī strī vat bhoga sampādanāya puruṣam na upasarpati iti 
[I,007,13]	tat etat sarvam asat pradhāna asattvasya vakṣyamāṇa tvāt sthite hi pradhāna sadbhāve puruṣasya tad viveka darśanam upapadyate upetya vā brūmaḥ yadi pradhānam puruṣa stham nimittam anapekṣya pravartate mukta ātmani api śarīra ādi sampādanāya pravarteta aviśeṣāt atha adarśana apekṣam iti ced yasya hi guṇa puruṣa antara viveka darśana anupapattiḥ tam prati pradhānam pravartate na ca asau mukta ātmani iti tat na mukta ātmani api viveka darśanasya vināśena pravṛtti prasaṅgāt na ca anutpatti vināśayoḥ adarśana tvena viśeṣam paśyāmaḥ atha adṛṣṭa apekṣam pravartate iti ced tat asat tasya api pradhāne śakti rūpa tayā vyavasthitasya ubhayatra aviśeṣāt tathā śarīra ādi vaicitrya abhāvaḥ ca tasya eka rūpa tvāt na ca pariṇāma vaicitryāt śarīra ādi vaicitryam tad vaicitrye kāraṇa abhāvāt kathañca sāmyena avasthitam tad pradhānam vaiṣamyam avāpnuyāt puruṣa arthasya pravṛtti hetoḥ abhāvāt sadbhāve vā puruṣa arthasya tad arthā pravṛttiḥ na bhavet vidyamāna tvāt eva na ca pravṛtti hetum vinā karmaṇi pravartamānasya uparamaḥ yuktaḥ hetu abhāvāt 
[I,007,25_I,008,5]	yat ca idam draṣṭuḥ sva rūpeṇa avasthānam iti uktam tat iṣyate eva viśeṣa guṇa rahitasya avasthāna abhyupagamāt atha cit rūpasya avasthānam tat na asti anitya tvena cit rūpa tāyāḥ vināśāt na ca akṣa ādi anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāyinaḥ caitanyasya nitya tve pramāṇam asti ātma rūpa tā iti ced tasyāḥ ca ātma tādātmye paryāya mātram vyatireke tu saṃyoga ādibhiḥ anaikāntyam guṇa guṇinoḥ ca tādātmya pratiṣedham vakṣyāmaḥ yat ca idam draṣṭṛ tayā vijñātantu puruṣam na upasarpati iti asat etat acetana tvāt tathā hi acetana tayā pradhānasya aham anena draṣṭṛ tayā vijñātam iti vijñāna abhāve pūrvavat pravṛtiḥ aviśiṣṭa iti alam ati prasaṅgena 
[I,008,8]	anye tu asthira ādi bhāvanā vaśāt rāga ādi viyukta jñāna utpattiḥ niḥśreyasam iti manyante tathā hi sarvam kṣaṇikam iti bhāvayataḥ viṣayeṣu āsaktiḥ vyāvartate mama idam iti sambandha abhāvāt tathā sarvam nirātmakam iti bhāvanāyām na aham paraḥ na mama ayam iti parigraha dveṣa abhāve bhavati eva viśuddha citta santāna utpattiḥ iti tathā ca paṭa ādi arthasya pratiṣedhāt sarvam śūnyam iti ca evam hi duḥkha samudaya nirodha mārgeṣu viśiṣṭa jñānam niḥśreyasa kāraṇam iti tathā hi duḥkham rūpa ādi skandha pañcakam tasya samudayaḥ kāraṇam samudeti asmāt iti tayoḥ nirodhaḥ vināśaḥ tasya upāyaḥ mārgaḥ iti eṣu viśiṣṭa jñāna vaśāt śuddha citta santānaḥ tad ucchedaḥ vā niḥśreyasam iti yuktam 
[I,008,16^1]	na etat evam kṣaṇikā ādi bhāvanāyāḥ mithyā rūpa tvāt na ca mithyājñānasya niḥśreyasa kāraṇa tvam atiprasaṅgāt yathā ca na kṣaṇika tvam śūnya tvam nairātmyam vā tathā vakṣyāmaḥ atha āsakti pratiṣedha artham evam bhāvanīyam tat na anyathā api bhāvāt tathā hi padārtha tattva jñānam pravṛtteḥ kāraṇam doṣa darśanañca nivṛtteḥ iti dṛṣṭam yathā madhu viṣa saṃpṛkte anne doṣa adarśanāt guṇa buddhitaḥ pravartate doṣa darśanāt ca nivartate 
[I,008,16^2]	na artha pratiṣedhāt evam putra ādau api ātmīya vairūpya darśanam eva nivṛtti kāraṇam iti vācyam na sambandha abhāvaḥ tad pratiṣedhaḥ bhāvyaḥ uktañca nyāya bhāṣya kṛtāḥ rūpa ādiṣu nimitta saṃjñā bhāvanīyāḥ na anuvyañjana saṃjñā iti ittham dantāḥ ittham keśāḥ ityādi yā ca iyam duḥkha samudaya nirodha mārgeṣu bhāvanā sā yadi duḥkham tad kāraṇam tayoḥ nirodhaḥ tad upāyaḥ ca iti iṣṭam na pratiṣidhyate tathā hi duḥkham svarūpataḥ eva anyat duḥkha kāraṇa tvāt tat ca rūpam saṃjñā vedanā saṃskāraḥ vijñānam iti rūpa ādi skandha pañcakam anyat vā bhavatu sukham api duḥkham duḥkha anuṣaṅgāt iti sarvam duḥkham tasya viccheda upāyaḥ tattva jñānam iṣyate eva 
[I,009,1^1]	yat ca idam rāga ādi viyukta jñānam viśiṣṭa bhāvanātaḥ iti tat na asti kṣaṇika tve kārya kāraṇa bhāva pratiṣedhasya vakṣyamāṇa tvāt upetya vādena tu ucyate na rāga ādi mataḥ vijñānāt tad rahitasya utpattiḥ yuktā iti tathā hi yathā hi bodhāt bodha rūpa tā jñāna antare tadvat rāga ādiḥ api syāt tad tādātmyāt viparyaye vā tad abhāva prasaṅgāt iti na ca vilakṣaṇāt api kāraṇāt vilakṣaṇa kāryasya utpatti darśanāt bodhāt bodha rūpa tā iti pramāṇam asti atas eva asya jñānasya jñāna antara hetu tvena pūrva kāla bhāvi tvam samāna jātīya tvam eka santāna tvam vā na hetuḥ vyabhicārāt tathā hi pūrva kāla bhāvi tvam tad samāna kṣaṇaiḥ 
[I,009,1^2_I,009,1^3]	samāna jātīya tvañca santāna antara jñānaiḥ vyabhicāri iti teṣām hi pūrva kāla bhāvi tvena samāna jātīya tve api na vivakṣita jñāna hetu tvam iti eka santāna tvañca antya tā jñānena vyabhicāri iti atha neṣyate eva antyam jñānam sarvadā ārambhāt tathā hi maraṇa śarīra jñānam api jñāna antara hetuḥ jāgrat avasthā jñānañca suṣupti avasthā ajñānasya api iti nanu evam maraṇa śarīra jñānasya antarābhava śarīra jñāna hetu tve garbha śarīra jñāna hetu tve vā santāna antare vijñāna janaka tva prasaṅgaḥ niyama hetoḥ abhāvāt atha iṣyate eva upādhyāya jñānam śiṣya jñānasya anyasya kasmāt na bhavati iti atha karma vāsanā niyāmikā iti ced na tasya api jñāna vyatirekeṇa asambhavāt tathā hi tad tādātmye sati vijñānam bodha rūpa tayā viśiṣṭam bodhāt ca bodha rūpa tā iti aviśeṣeṇa vijñānam vidadhyāt iti alam 
[I,009,17]	yat ca idam suṣupti avasthā jñānasya jāgrat avasthā jñāne kāraṇa tvam iti asat etat suṣupti avasthāyām jñāna sadbhāve jāgrat avasthātaḥ na viśeṣaḥ syāt ubhayatra api sva saṃvedya jñānasya sadbhāva aviśeṣāt yat vā nidrayā anabhibhūta tvam viśeṣaḥ iti ced asat etat tad dharma tayā tasya api tādātmyena abhibhāvaka tva asambhavāt vyatireke tu rūpa ādi padārthānām eva sattvāt tad svarūpam nirūpyam abhibhavaḥ ca yadi vināśaḥ na vijñānasya sattvam vināśasya vā nirhetuka tvam atha tirobhāvaḥ na vijñānasya sattvena tat sattā eva saṃvedanam iti abhyupagame tasya anupapatteḥ atha suṣupti avasthāyām vijñāna asattvena antya jñāna sadbhāvāt eka santāna tvam vyabhicāri iti 
[I,009,25_I,010,3]	yat ca idam viśiṣṭa bhāvanā vaśāt rāga ādi vināśaḥ iti asat etat nirhetuka tvāt vināśasya abhyāsa anupapatteḥ ca abhyāsaḥ hi avasthitasya arthasya atiśaya ādhāyaka tvāt upapadyate na kṣaṇika jñāna mātraḥ iti atas eva yogini sakala kalpanā vikalam vijñānam utpadyate na ca santāna apekṣayā atiśayaḥ tasya eva asambhavāt aviśiṣṭāt viśiṣṭa utpatteḥ ayogāt ca tathā hi pūrvasmāt aviśiṣṭāt uttarottaram sa atiśayam katham upajāyate iti cintyam yat ca santāna ucchittiḥ niḥśreyasam iti tat na nirhetuka tayā vināśasya upāya vaiyarthya mayatna sādhya tvāt 
[I,010,5]	anye tu anekānta bhāvanātaḥ viśiṣṭa pradeśe akṣaya śarīra ādi lābhaḥ niḥśreyasam iti manyante tathā ca nitya bhāvanāyām graha anitya tve ca dveṣaḥ iti ubhaya parihāra artham anekānta bhāvanā iti evam sat asat ādiṣu api yojyam pratyakṣañca sva deśa kāla kāraṇa ādhāra tayā sattvam para deśa ādiṣu asattvam iti ubhaya rūpa tā tathā ghaṭa ādiḥ mṛd ā ādi rūpa tayā nityaḥ sarva avasthāsu upalambhāt ghaṭa ādi rūpa tayā ca anityaḥ tat apāyāt evam ātmā api ātma rūpa tayā nityaḥ sarvadā sadbhāvāt sukha duḥkha ādi paryyāya rūpa tayā ca anityaḥ tad vināśāt evam sarvatra sva kāryeṣu kartṛ tvam kārya antareṣu ca akartṛ tvam iti ūhyam atha sva śabda abhidheya tvam śabda antara anabhidheya tvañcā iti 
[I,010,12^1]	tat etat asāmpratam mithyājñānasya niḥśreyasa kāraṇa tvena pratiṣedhāt anekānta jñānañca mithyā eva bādhaka upapatteḥ tathā hi nitya anityayoḥ vidhi pratiṣedha rūpa tvāt abhinne dharmiṇī abhāvaḥ evam sat asat tva ādeḥ api iti yat ca idam ghaṭa ādiḥ mṛd ā ādi rūpa tayā nityaḥ iti asat etat mṛd rūpatāyāḥ tatas artha antara tvāt tathā hi ghaṭāt artha antaram mṛd rūpatā mṛd tvam sāmānyam tasya tu nitya tvena ghaṭasya ātathā bhāvaḥ tatas anya tvāt ghaṭasya tu kāraṇāt vilaya upalabdheḥ anitya tvam eva yat ca idam sva deśa ādiṣu sattvam para deśa ādiṣu asattvam iṣi ate eva itaretara abhāvasya abhyupagamāt tathā hi 
[I,010,12^2]	itarasmin deśa ādau itarasya ghaṭasya abhāvaḥ na anutpattiḥ na pradhvaṃsaḥ tatra tasya sarvadā sattvāt dvairūpye tu sva deśa ādiṣu anupalambha prasaṅgaḥ evam ātmanaḥ api nitya tvam eva sukha duḥkha ādeḥ tad guṇa tvena tatas artha antarasya vināśe api avināśāt kārya antareṣu ca akartṛt tvam na pratiṣidhyate tathā hi yat yasya anvaya vyatirekābhyām utpattau vyāpriyate iti upalabdham tat tasya kāraṇam na anyasya iti abhyupagamyate evam śabda antara anabhidheya tve api na sarvam sarva śabda abhidheyam iti abhyupagamāt 
[I,010,24]	na ca anekānta bhāvanātaḥ viśiṣṭa śarīra ādi lābhe asti pratibandhaḥ na ca utpatti dharmāṇām śarīra ādīnām akṣaya tvam nyāyyam tathā muktau api anekāntaḥ na vyāvartate iti muktaḥ na muktaḥ ca iti syāt evañca sati saḥ eva muktaḥ saṃsārī ca iti prasaktam evam anekānte api anekānta abhyupagame dūṣaṇam vastunaḥ hi sat asat rūpa tā anaikāntikaḥ tasya api anaikāntika abhyupagame rūpa antaram api pratyakṣam evam nitya anitya rūpa tā vyatiriktañca rūpa antaram ityādi vācyam 
[I,011,4_I,011,7]	anye tu ātmā eka tva jñānāt paramātmani layaḥ sampadyate iti bruvate tathā hi ātmā eva parama arthaḥ san tatas anyeṣām bhede pramāṇa abhāvāt pratyakṣam hi padārthānām sadbhāva grāhakam eva na bhedasya iti avidyā samāropitaḥ eva ayam bhedaḥ iti manyante tat api asat ātma ekatva jñānasya mithyā rūpa tayā niḥśreyasa sādhanatva anupapatteḥ mithyā tvañca ātma adhikāre vakṣyāmaḥ vyavasthātaḥ nānā ātmānaḥ iti sūtreṇa 
[I,011,10]	evam śabda advaita vijñānam api mithyā rūpa tayā na niḥśreyasa sādhanam iti draṣṭavyam tathā hi sarva arthānām śabda rūpa tā iti pramāṇa abhāvaḥ atha bhede api pramāṇa abhāvaḥ iti ced tat asat cakṣuḥ ādinā śabda rūpa tā viyuktānām arthānām pratibhāsanāt śabda rūpa tā hi śrāvaṇa tvam arthasya sataḥ na ca artheṣu etat asti śrotreṇa agrahaṇāt atha śabdasya eva avasthā bhedāt grahaṇa vaicitryam iti ced tat na śabda rūpa tāyām eva tat syāt tatra ca pramāṇa abhāvaḥ eva atha śabda samparkeṇa pratibhāsaḥ eva pramāṇam iti ced na akṛta samayasya vāyu ādeḥ tad antareṇa api pratibhāsanāt na ca śabda antareṇa samparkaḥ yuktaḥ samaya vaiyarthya prasaṅgāt iti śabda rūpa tāyām sādhyāyām na śabda sampṛkta pratibhāsaḥ pramāṇam atas eva vaikharī madhyamā paśyantī sūkṣmā ca iti bheda pratipādanam unmatta bhāṣitam na ca śabdāt vaita jñānāt sūkṣma avasthā sampadyate iti asti pratibandhaḥ 
[I,011,20_I,011,22]	ekasmin ca advaite pratiṣiddhe pratibandha samāna tayā sarve eva advaita bhedāḥ pratiṣiddhāḥ bhavanti iti ātma eka tva pratiṣedhāt eva idam pratiṣiddham bhaviṣyati iti uparamyate anye tu maheśvara prasādāt aśuddha aiśvarya vināśe tad guṇa saṃkrāntim manyante tat ca asat anya guṇānām anyatra vṛtteḥ adarśanāt maheśvara prasādaḥ ca muktau na pratiṣidhyate tasyāḥ tad adhīna tvāt iti sthitam asa dvāda pratiṣedhāt ṣaṣ padārtha sādharmya vaidharmya tattva jñānam muktasya niḥśreyasa kāraṇam iti 
[I,012,2_I,012,8]	atha iti ādi vākyasya sūtreṇa api sambandhaḥ vyākhyāna antaram iti manyante tat ca asat sarvasmin vyākhyāne sūtrita tva upadarśanam bhāṣyasya iṣyatas eva atha atas dharmam vyākhyāsyāmaḥ yatas abhyudaya niḥśreyasa siddhiḥ sa dharmaḥ iti pūrva sūtre atha śabdaḥ api ānantarye vartate iti anyasya asambhavān namaskāra anantaram iti labhyate sa ca jñāna prastāvāt īśvarasya eva iti bhāṣya kāraḥ ca sūtra kāra abhimatam parasya guroḥ namaskāra manūdya aparasya namaskāram karoti iti vyākhyeyam na tu kaṇādaḥ eva sva ātmani kriyā virodhāt na api kaṇān atti iti kaṇādaḥ iti kaṇa śabdena sva karma phalasya abhidhānāt kaṣṭa vyutpattyā saṃsārya ātmanaḥ tad namaskāre prayojana abhāvāt 
[I,012,10]	atha śabda arthaḥ anu śabdena uktaḥ eva atas śabdaḥ api vacana vṛttyā dharmam vyākhyāsyāmaḥ iti vividham aneka prakāreṇa yat utpadyate yatas ca na utpadyate iti pratibodham yāvat tāvat pratipādayiṣyāmaḥ iti dharma vyākhyāna artham eva ṣaṭpadārtha upavarṇanam atas eva padārthaḥ dharmaiḥ saṃgṛhyate iti padārtha dharma saṅgrahaḥ iti uktam uttara sūtrasya tu vivaraṇam mahā udayaḥ mahān udayaḥ svarga apavarga lakṣaṇaḥ asmāt bhavati iti mahā udayaḥ iti uktam dharmāt sukham jñānañca iti jñāna utpattau tasya eva prādhānyāt tad upasarjana tayā śeṣam vyākhyāyate iti 
[I,012,16_I,012,20]	atha avayava arthaḥ praṇamya hetum īśvaram iti preti upasargeṇa praṇāma atiśayam darśayati hetu tvam nimitta kāraṇa tvam tat ca anyeṣām api asti iti īśvara padam īśvara śabdaḥ ca anyatra vartamānaḥ api jñāna prastāvān maheśvaraḥ eva vartate śaṅkarāt jñānam anvicchet iti vacanāt nanu vyartham tarhi hetu padam jñāna prastāvāt viśeṣaṇa siddheḥ na etat evam stuteḥ guṇa saṃkīrtana rūpa tayā sakala kārya kartṛ tva abhidhānāt anyathā hi anyatara abhidhānena eva gata artha tvāt vyatham syāt ubhaya abhidhānam 
[I,012,23_I,013,1]	tat evam īśvara praṇāma anantaram munim praṇamati munayaḥ ca anye api viśiṣṭa jñāna vairāgyavantaḥ bhavanti iti viśeṣaṇam kaṇādaḥ iti viśiṣṭa jñāna sambandhi tvañca tad abhihita padārthānām pramāṇa antareṇa asādhanāt vijñāyate atas eva tattva jñāna sadbhāve mithyājñānasya rāga dveṣa hetoḥ abhāvāt dveṣa vairāgyam niścīyate kaṇā natti iti kaṇā daḥ tam iti viśiṣṭa āhāra nimitta saṃjñā upadarśanena āsat codya nirāsaḥ tat ca kaṇān vā bhakṣayet kāmam māhiṣāṇi dadhīni ca ityādi yukti yuktam 
[I,013,4]	yukti bodhaḥ ca na pravṛtteḥ kāraṇam pravṛttau satyām tad bhāvāt tathā hi śravaṇe pravartamānaḥ vijānāti yuktam ayuktam vā iti na tad avabodhe pravṛttiḥ itaretara āśraya tva prasaṅgāt atas viśiṣṭa puruṣa praṇīta tva upabodhe satya ādau śravaṇe pravṛttiḥ yuktā tathā hi manunā praṇītam vyāsena praṇītam iti matvā pravartante janāḥ 
[I,013,8_I,013,12]	tat evam para apara guru namaskāra apekṣa dharma viśeṣe adharma pratibandhāt tad tad kāryāṇām abhāve bhavati eva avighnataḥ śāstra parisamāptiḥ iti nanu ca ayuktam etat sati api namaskāre śāstra parisamāpteḥ adarśanāt kādambarī ādau asati api darśanāt pramāṇataḥ artha pratipattau iti evamādau satyam śāstra parisamāpteḥ kārya tvāt avaśyam kāraṇam vācyam iti anyasya asambhavāt dharma viśeṣaḥ kāraṇam iti sa ca namaskārāt anyasmāt vā bhavatu na niyamyate iti eke anye tu sādhana viśeṣāt viśiṣyate iti namaskārāt eva upajāyate dharma viśeṣaḥ kāraṇam iti 
[I,013,15]	atha namaskāra abhāve tarhi katham śāstra parisamāptiḥ iti na tatra api kārya sadbhāvena kāraṇa sadbhāva siddheḥ vācika namaskāra abhāve api mānasaḥ namaskāraḥ jñāyate iti ekadā hi viśiṣṭa namaskāra sadbhāve parisamāpteḥ upalambhāt iti tathā hi mānasa namaskāra upacitaḥ vācikaḥ namaskāraḥ parisamāpteḥ kāraṇam iṣyate mānasaḥ tu kevalaḥ api iti atas eva kvacid vācika sadbhāve api mānasa namaskāra abhāvāt apari samāptiḥ yuktā iti tasya ca abhāvaḥ kārya anutpādena eva jñāyate iti namaskārāt ca dharmaḥ sampadyate iti āgamāt vyāpti grahaṇam tathā laukikaḥ api puruṣaḥ kṛta namaskriyaḥ kriyā karaṇe pravartamānaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ kim punar bhagavān muniḥ anavadya vādī 
[I,013,23_I,013,26]	anye tu asat codya nirāsa artham kaṇān dadāti iti dayate iti vā vyutpatti antaram āśrayante atra kila vaiśeṣika sūtra racanā karaṇaḥ iti ucyate iti cintyam etat prasiddhi aparijñāna parihāra artham ca upāttam iti alam asat vyākhyānaiḥ iti tat evam parāpara guru namaskārāt yatas antarāya pradhvaṃsaḥ yatas vā antevāsī yathā ukta lakṣaṇa sampannaḥ atas anantaram eva pratipakṣa kriyā anantaritaḥ padārtha dharma saṃgrahaḥ pravakṣyate iti na ca ktvā apratyayāt eva viśiṣṭa anantarya pratipattiḥ tasya hi samāna kartṛka tve sati pūrva kāla bhāvi tva mātre bhāvāt tathā hi bhojana anantaram śayana ādi kriyā vyavadhāne api bhuktvā vrajati iti prayogaḥ bhavati eva atra ca īśvara praṇāma anantaram eva muneḥ namaskāraḥ tad anantaram eva pravacana kriyā iti na ca apratipakṣa kriyā vyudāsaḥ avayava calana ādeḥ bhāvāt iti 
[I,014,5]	padārtha dharma saṃgrahaḥ iti padārthānām dharmāḥ teṣām saṃgrahaḥ iti uttara pada prādhānye api dharmāṇām dharmi niṣṭha tayā saṃgrahaḥ bhavati eva dharmiṇām saṃgrahaḥ iti sukha duḥkha sādhana tva dharma avabodhe sati pravṛtti nivṛttyoḥ bhāvāt dharmāṇām iha prādhānyam na niṣidhyate tattva jñānañca atra pradhāna tayā vivakṣitam tat dharmiṣu upasarjana tayā api labhyate eva 
[I,014,9]	yat vā tattva jñāna pradhāna kriyā sambandhāt ubhayeṣām prādhānyam iti padārthāḥ ca dharmāḥ ca iti samāsaḥ svātantryam hi pradhāna kriyā sambandhaḥ eva na dharmi tādātmyam dharmāṇām iti vakṣyāmaḥ padārtha dharmāṇām saṃgrahaḥ iti nibandha antaraiḥ vistara uktānām saṃkṣepeṇa abhidhānam bhāva vyutpattyā tattva jñānam iti apare 
[I,014,13_I,014,17]	sa ca pravakṣyate kathayiṣyate kiṃviśiṣṭaḥ mahān udayaḥ tad kāryañca niḥśreyasam asmāt bhavati iti mahā udayaḥ iti padārtha dharma saṅgrahaḥ ityādi sāmānya ukteḥ vibhajanāya dravya ādi vākyam tat ca viśeṣa upadarśanāt śeṣa pratiṣedha param bhavati eva vibhāgāt ceyattā avadhāraṇam iti ṣaṇṇām eva abhidhānāt ṣaṣ eva padārthāḥ iti labhyate 
[I,014,20]	atha abhāvaḥ kasmāt na upasaṃkhyāyate bhāva upasarjana tayā pratibhāsanāt tathā hi na aprasiddha bhāva sadbhāvasya nārikera dvīpa vāsinaḥ tad abhāva pratītiḥ iti bhāva parijñāna apekṣi tvāt abhāvasya na pṛthak upasaṃkhyānam jñāte hi bhāve tad abhāvaḥ pratīyate eva tathā hi dravya parijñānāt tad abhāva parijñāname jñānam labhyate teṣāñca prādhānyam upadarśitam eva 
[I,014,24]	tattva jñānam iti samyaktvasya viśeṣyam jñānam iti na tu tat tvañca tat jñānañca iti ubhaya pada vyabhicāre sāmānādhikaraṇya abhāvāt tattvam hi pṛthivyām gandhaḥ na ca jñānam jñānañca mithyājñānam api na ca tattvam iti vyabhicāre api dharma dharmi śabdāt na sāmānādhikaraṇyam tattvam hi samyaktvam jñāna dharmaḥ eva 
[I,015,3_I,015,9]	anye tu tattve pradhāna tvāt ātmani sādharmya vaidharmyābhyām upajātam iti manyante prādhānyantu dravya ādi padārthānām madhye puruṣasya tatra hi abhyāsa vaśāt upajātasya niḥśreyasa kāraṇa tva abhyupagamāt na ca mithyājñāne prasaṅgaḥ niḥśreyasa hetu tvena viśeṣaṇāt mithyājñānasya niḥśreyasa hetu tva asambhavāt iti niḥśreyasasya ca hetuḥ yathā tattva jñānam tathā uktam eva ādi vākye tat ca ātma jñānam itaravi vikta tvāt itara padārtha jñāna apekṣam iti arthavat dravya ādi sādharmya vaidharmya jñānam 
[I,015,10]	atha astu saṃgrahāt tattva jñānam avadhāraṇe tu vyāghātaḥ tathā hi yadi saṃgrahāt eva tattva jñānam sūtrakārasya na syāt saṃgraha abhāvāt atha saṃgrahāt bhavati eva tat asat manda mateḥ sati api saṃgrahe tad abhāvāt atha saṃgrahāt tattva jñānam eva tat na asti duḥkha ādeḥ api darśanāt iti āśaṅkā parihāra artham tat ca īśvara codanāḥ ityādi tathā hi asmad ādeḥ saṃgrahāt eva tattva jñānam yat ca sūtrakārasya jñānam tat ca īśvara codanā abhivyaktāt dharma ādi viśeṣāt eva iti na ca saḥ eva astu iti vācyam asmad ādeḥ tathāvidha dharma abhāvāt tathā saṃgrahāt bhavati eva tattva jñānam yadi nāma tat ca īśvara codana abhivyaktāt dharmāt eva samuccīyamāna avadhāraṇam anirdiṣṭa pratiṣedha artham manda mateḥ tu viśiṣṭa dharma abhāvāt na bhavati api astu vā saṃgrahāt tattva jñānam eva na duḥkha ādikam yadi nāma īśvara codanā abhivyaktāt dharmāt eva yasya viśiṣṭa dharma sadbhāvaḥ tasya alpīyasā prayāsena tattva jñānam sampadyate iti 
[I,015,21]	yat vā kasmāt dharmasya ādau sūtre vyāvarṇanam īśvarasya vā namaskāraḥ iti codya parihāra artham tat ca tattva jñānam īśvara codanā abhivyaktāt dharmāt eva bhavati iti atas tasya ādau pratijñānam īśvarasya ca namaskāraḥ iti īśvarasya codanā saṅkalpa viśeṣaḥ asya idam asmāt sampadyatām iti tayā abhivyaktāt saha kṛtāt dharmāt tattva jñānam iti tathā adharmasya sadbhāve kim pramāṇam iti apekṣāyām idam eva āvartanīyam īśvarasya codanā iti codanā hi pravartakam vākyam tad pradhāna tvāt vedaḥ codanā iti sā ca īśvara praṇīta tvāt pramāṇam tayā abhivyaktāt prakāśitāt dharmāt eva iti 
[I,016,1_I,016,8]	tat evam dravya ādi sādharmya vaidharmya jñānasya niḥśreyasa kāraṇa tvam abhyupagamya tad svarūpa parijñāna artham āha atha ke dravya ādayaḥ padārthāḥ kiṃsvarūpāḥ kiñca teṣām sādharmyam kiṃrūpañca vaidharmyam iti dravya ādiṣu vā nānā rūpa tayā paraiḥ abhidhānāt saṃśaye sati idam tathā hi viśeṣyam dravyam iti kecid kraya vikraya yogyañca ityādi viparyastaḥ vā dravya ādīnām asattvam manyamānaḥ atha ke dravya ādayaḥ padārthāḥ na santi iti āha tad abhāvāt na sādharmyam na api vaidharmyam iti 
[I,016,10^1]	tathā hi cakṣuḥ sparśanābhyām rūpa sparśayoḥ pratibhāsanāt na tad vyatiriktam dravyam asti yat ca idam ghaṭa ādi jñānam tat na pramāṇam kalpanā jñāna tvāt bādha kañca pramāṇam asti vṛtti vikalpa ādi tathā ca avayavāḥ avayavini vartante iti na abhyupagatam avayavī ca avayaveṣu vartamānaḥ kim eka deśe vartate vyāptyā vā eka deśena vṛttau avayava antara prasaṅgaḥ atha eka deśe vartate aneka vṛtti tva vyāghātaḥ eka dravyañca dravyam syāt tatra ca avayava vibhāga abhāvāt nitya tvam ekasya ca krama yaugapadyābhyām ajanaka tvam rūpa ādi anutpattiḥ ca aneka rūpa ādeḥ janaka tva abhyupagamāt avayaveṣu ca avayavi iti pratibhāsā bhāvaḥ tasya eka dravya tvāt atha na pratyekam parisamāptyā vartate kim tarhi sarva avayaveṣu ekaḥ eva iti

[I,017,9_I,017,21]	atha idam kalpanā jñānam iti ced kim idam kalpanā jñānam nāma iti atha kṣaṇika tvāt nirvikalpaka jñāna sama kālam artha vināśe smaraṇa anantaram eva tat bhavati iti nirviṣaya tvāt apramāṇam iti ced na kṣaṇika tva asiddhau smaraṇa anantara bhāvinaḥ api nirvikalpaka jñāna vat artha anvaya vyatireka anuvidhānāt artha ja tvam eva atha artha ja tve nirvikalpaka jñāna sama kālam eva arthasya sadbhāvāt indriyāṇāñca avicāraka tvena syāt etat iti tat na saha kārya bhāvāt tathā hi indriyam artheṣu sa vikalpaka jñāna utpattau saṅketa smaraṇa apekṣam atha smaraṇe vā arthasya indriyasya ca kim atiśaya ādhānam anatiśaya nivṛttiḥ iṣyate na tasya eva atiśaya tvāt tathā hi yat yasya sadbhāve kāryam karoti tat tasya atiśayaḥ smaraṇa sadbhāve ca indriyam kārya kṛt iti smaraṇam eva tasya atiśayaḥ smaraṇāt vā kāraka sākalyam eva atiśayaḥ sampadyate tat vaikalyañcān atiśayaḥ nivartate sākalye hi kārya karaṇāt iti ete yat āhuḥ yaḥ prāc ajanakaḥ buddheḥ upayoga aviśeṣataḥ sa paścāt api tena syāt artha apāye api netra dhīḥ iti etad apāstam bhavati upayoga aviśeṣasya asiddha tvāt tathā hi nirvikalpaka bodhe na indriyasya saṅketa smaraṇam asti sa vikalpake tu asti iti upayoga viśeṣaḥ 
[I,017,24]	atha śabda ākāram sa vikalpakam jñānam śabda rūpa tā ca arthe na asti prathama indriya sannipātaḥ eva sa vikalpaka utpatti prasaṅgāt cakṣuḥ ādinā vā paricchedaḥ śrotra paricchedya tvena darśanāt iti nirviṣaya tvam sa vikalpaka jñānasya tat asat ākāra vāda pratiṣedhasya vakṣyamāṇa tvāt na śabda rūpa tā jñāne asti jñāna vailakṣaṇye tu sahakāri vailakṣaṇyam eva kāraṇam iti uktam 
[I,018,4]	dravya asattve ca anyat nimittam vācyam pratisandhānasya atha asti eva anādi kāla paripuṣṭa vāsanā iti ced na tasyāḥ sadbhāve pramāṇa abhāvāt atha sa vikalpakam jñānam eva pramāṇam iti ced na anyathā api bhāvāt tathā hi artha sadbhāve api upapadyate iti katham vāsanā sadbhāve pramāṇam anvaya vyatirekābhyām anyatra api ca kārya kāraṇa bhāva avagatiḥ tau vā indriyasya iha api staḥ iti atha nirvikalpaka jñāna utpattau indriyasya vyāpārāt tad adhīna tayā ca sa vikalpake api vyāpāraḥ iva saṃlakṣyate na vastutas tat na akṣaṇika tve sati ubhayatra api vyāpāra sambhavāt na ca nirvikalpaka jñānam eva saṅketa smṛti dvāreṇa sa vikalpaka jñāna utpattau kāraṇam iti asti pratibandhaḥ pratyakṣasya niyamena sva lakṣaṇa viṣaya tvena krama aviṣaya tvāt anumānantu sāmānya viṣayam eva iti na ca pratibaddham liṅgam asti kāryañca anyathā sambhavati iti na krame pramāṇam 
[I,018,14]	sva saṃvedana vādinaḥ ca vijñānam sva paricchede eva pramāṇam na artha antarasya iti yadi ca vāsanā eva nimittam sā na vijñānāt artha antaram rūpa rasa gandha sparśa śabda jñāna vyatiriktasya nimittasya anabhyupagamāt tādātmye tu bodha rūpa tayā sarvatra aviśeṣāt vikalpa vaicitryam na syāt atha vikalpa vaicitryāt eva vāsanā vaicitryam na kāryate iti ced tāsāñca vijñānāt abhede vijñāna vat ekatā prasaṅgaḥ vijñānasya vā aneka tvam aneka artha tādātmyāt viparyaye vā tādātmya anupapatteḥ yadi ca vāsanā viśiṣṭa jñāna hetuḥ bāhyā ca iti saṃjñā mātram bhidyeta arthaḥ vāsanā iti atha vastu rūpā eva vāsanā na tarhi tasyāḥ jñāna janaka tvam artha kriyā kāritvasya vastu lakṣaṇa tvāt 
[I,018,22]	atha smaraṇa anantara bhāvi tvam sa vikalpaka tvam tat ca artha ja tvasya prasādhita tvāt na dūṣaṇam abhyupagame vā nirvikalpakasya api sa vikalpaka tva prasaṅgaḥ tathā hi rūpa smaraṇa anantaram rasa rasana sannipāte rasa jñānam utpadyate tatra ca rūpa smṛteḥ pūrva kāla bhāvi tvāt samanantara kāraṇa tvam bodhāt bodha rūpa tā iti nyāyāt aḥ tu tasya api kalpanā tvam smaraṇa anantara bhāvi tvāt na ca atra bodha rūpa tayā samanantara kāraṇa tvam anyatra smṛti rūpatayā iti vācyam bodhāt artha antarasya smṛti rūpasya tādātmye satyabhāvāt na ca abhede sati vyavasthā upapadyate kvacid bodha rūpa tayā samanantara kāraṇa tvam kvacid rūpa antareṇa iti atas na smaraṇa anantara bhāvi tvam sa vikalpaka tvam na ca artha ja tu a siddhau nāma jāti ādi ullekhena utpattiḥ dūṣaṇam iti kalpanātu asya asambhavāt pratisandhānam dravya siddhau pramāṇam

[I,019,11]	atha asti vṛtti vikalpa ādi bādhakam iti ced na tasya apramāṇa tvāt tathā hi vṛtti anupapatteḥ asattvam iti kim idam svatantra sādhanam uta prasaṅga sādhanam iti yadi svatantra sādhanam avayavī dharmī na asti iti sādhyam iti pratijñā vākye padayoḥ vyāghātaḥ yathā idam na asti ca iti hetoḥ āśraya asiddha tvañca dharmiṇaḥ aprasiddha tvāt tathā sva mate rūpa ādīnām sattvam na ca vṛttiḥ asti iti vyabhicāraḥ samavāya anabhyupagamāt atha para vyāptyā parasya aniṣṭa āpādanam iti pareṇa hi avayavī abhyupagataḥ iti dharmi tvena upāttaḥ tasya pratipādya tvāt iti tatra yadi pareṇa pramāṇāt pratipannaḥ tena eva bādhyamāna tvāt anutthānam viparīta anumānasya na ca anena eva tasya bādhāt tad antareṇa pakṣa dharma tvāt iti atha apramāṇena pratipannaḥ tarhi pramāṇam vinā prameyasya asiddhiḥ iti vācyam kim anumāna upanyāsena tasya apakṣa dharma tayā apramāṇa tvāt na ca parasya vṛttyā sattvam vyāptam tad antareṇa api ākāśa ādau upalambhāt iti anekāntar svarūpa asiddhaḥ ca vṛtteḥ samavāyasya siddha tvāt

[I,020,17]	tatra dravyeṣu pratijñām karoti dravyāṇi paramārtha santi iti a bādhyamāna jñāna viṣaya tvāt yat yat abādhyamāna jñāna viṣayam tat tat paramārtha sat yathā vijñānam tathā abādhyamāna jñāna viṣayāṇi amūni tasmāt paramārtha santi iti atra pakṣīkṛteṣu abādhyamāna jñāna viṣaya tvam iti pakṣa dharma tvam parama artha sati ca jñāne jñāna viṣaya tvam vakṣyāmaḥ iti sa pakṣe sattvam vipakṣāt ca khara viṣāṇa ādeḥ vyāvṛttiḥ iti viparīta artha upasthāpakayoḥ pratyakṣa āgamayoḥ anupalambhāt abādhita viṣaya tvam asat pratipakṣa upapatteḥ ca prāmāṇyam iti 
[I,020,23]	evam pṛthivī ap tejaḥ vāyu ākāśa kāla diś ātma manāṃsi iti atra dvandvaḥ samāsaḥ sarveṣām svātantryāt atra ca dravyāṇi iti pratijñāyām dravya tva yogaḥ sādhanam vakṣyati tathā pṛthivī ādi bhede ca pṛthivī tva ādi viśeṣa lakṣaṇam iti etāni ca sāmānya viśeṣa saṃjñayā uktāni sāmānya saṃjñā dravyam iti viśeṣa saṃjñā ca pṛthivī tva ādayaḥ tābhiḥ uktāni kiyanti nava eva iti avadhāryante nyūna adhika pratipādaka pramāṇa abhāvāt tathā hi pṛthivī ādi sadbhāvasya vakṣyamāṇa tvāt na nyūna tā 
[I,021,1]	atha ādhikya upalabdheḥ tad abhāvaḥ asiddhaḥ tathā hi chāyā dravyam kriyāvat tvāt guṇavat tvāt ca iti kriyāvat tvan ca pratyakṣeṇa api jñāyate cakṣuḥ vyāpārāt gacchati iti jñāna utpatteḥ deśa antara prāpteḥ ca tathā hi gatimatī chāyā deśa antara prāptimat tvāt yaḥ yaḥ deśa antara prāptimān sa sa gatimān upalabdhaḥ yathā devadattaḥ tathā deśa antara prāptimatī chāyā tasmāt gatimatī guṇavat tvañca ātapaḥ kaṭukaḥ rūkṣaḥ chāyā madhura śītalā iti āgamāt 
[I,021,7^1]	tat etat asat bhāsām abhāva rūpa tvāt chāyāyāḥ tathā hi yatra yatra vāraka dravyeṇa tejasaḥ sannidhiḥ niṣidhyate tatra tatra chāyā iti vyavahāraḥ vāraka dravya gatāñca kriyām ātapa abhāve samāropya pratipadyate chāyā gacchati iti anyathā hi vāraka dravya gatam kriyā apekṣi tattvam na syāt yat ca idam deśa antara prāptimat tvam tat kim deśa antareṇa saṃyogaḥ samavāyaḥ vā na saṃyogaḥ tasya api sādhya tvāt tathā hi dravya tva siddhau saṃyogaḥ sidhyati saṃyogāt dravya tvam iti itaretara āśraya tvam syāt atha deśa antara prāptiḥ samavāyaḥ 
[I,021,7^2]	saḥ api asiddhaḥ na hi ekatra samavetaḥ anyatra samavaiti iti chāyā tu ekatra sambaddha upalabdhā punar deśa antare api upalabhyate na ca kriyāvat tvam deśa antara samavāyāt sidhyati tasya ayuta siddheṣu eva bhāvāt iti kriyāvat tvam asādhanam yat ca idam āgamāt mādhuryam śaityam vā chāyāyāḥ tat api upacārāt ye hi madhura dravyasya śīta dravyasya vā guṇāḥ te chāyā saṃsevanāt bhavanti iti tad kārya kartṛ tvena tathā uktāḥ tasmāt kriyāvat tvāt guṇavat tvāt ca dravyam chāyā iti na vācyam na ca dravya antaram asti iti upapannam nava eva dravyāṇi iti avadhāraṇāt 
[I,021,19_I,021,24]	atra kecid dravyāṇi nava eva nyūna adhika pratipādaka pramāṇa abhāve sati vyavacchedya vyavacchedaka bhāva āpanna nava lakṣaṇa yogi tvāt ubhaya abhimata ghaṭa ādi nava dravya ādi vat iti hetum bruvate tathā hi ādhikya pramāṇa abhāvaḥ darśitaḥ eva na ca lakṣa yathāvasaram vakṣyāmaḥ iti tathā sarvajñena muninā pṛthivī ādi saṃjñā vyatirekeṇa saṃjñā antara anabhidhānāt dravya antara asattvam iti yat iha bhāva rūpam tat sarvam mayā upasaṃkhyātavyam iti hi pratijñā muneḥ 
[I,022,1]	tathā guṇeṣu pratijñām karoti guṇāḥ parama artha santaḥ pūrva uktāt eva sādhanāt tathā guṇa vyavahāre guṇa tva yogam sādhanam vakṣyati rūpa ādi bhede ca tad viśeṣa lakṣaṇam iti te tu rūpa rasa gandha sparśa saṃkhyā parimāṇa pṛthaktva saṃyoga vibhāga paratva aparatva buddhi sukha duḥkha icchā dveṣa prayatnāḥ ca iti kaṇṭha uktāḥ sūtra kāreṇa iti vacana vṛttyā abhihitāḥ tān ca vakṣyāmaḥ samāsaḥ ca atra dvandvaḥ nyūna adhika vyavaccheda artham sāmarthya labdhāḥ punar ucyante saṃkhyayā saptadaśaḥ iti caśabda samuccitāḥ ca gurutva drava tva sneha saṃskāra adṛṣṭa śabdāḥ ca iti adṛṣṭa śabdena dharma adharmayoḥ abhidhānāt sapta bhavanti iti 
[I,022,8]	atha saṃskāra stham traividhyāt ādhikyam syāt na saṃskāra tva jāti apekṣayā eka tvāt na ca evam adṛṣṭa tvam sāmānyam asti iti na ca anyeṣām api kāma krodha ādīnām sambhavāt upasaṃkhyānam katham iti vācyam atra eva antarbhāvasya vakṣyamāṇa tvāt iti evam ukta prakāreṇa caturviṃśati guṇāḥ iti nyūna adhika vyavaccheda artham tad pratipādaka pramāṇa abhāve sati parasparam vyavacchedya vyavacchedaka bhāva āpanna caturviṃśati lakṣaṇa yogi tvāt ubhaya abhimata ghaṭa ādi caturviṃśati dravya vat iti 
[I,022,14]	atha nirguṇa tvāt guṇānām saṃkhyā yogaḥ anupapannaḥ na upacāra abhyupagamāt tathā hi mukhye bādhaka pramāṇa sadbhāve sati upacāraḥ kalpyate sa ca nimitta apekṣaḥ iti asādhāraṇa dharma yogaḥ nimittam yatra hi saṃkhyā upalabdhā tatra asādhāraṇa dharma yogaḥ api iti tad smaraṇāt adhi āropaḥ pravartate iti vyāpakantu nimittam artha kriyā janaka tvam vā na eka artha samavāyaḥ tasya avyāpaka tvāt tathā hi guṇa karmaṇām ekārtha samavāyaḥ na sāmānya ādīnām iti avyāpakam upacāre animittam etat iti na api dharma rūpa saṃkhyā tad vyatireke pratiṣedhasya vakṣyamāṇa tvāt 
[I,022,21]	anye tu viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvena eva saṃkhyā atra viśeṣaṇam iti upacāra asambhavam manyante tathā hi saṃkhyā viśiṣṭa jñānāni atha anupapattyā viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvasya dravyaḥ iva guṇa ādau ca aviśeṣa upalabdheḥ upacāraḥ katham saṃyuktam samavetam vā viśeṣaṇam iti niyama anabhyupagamāt ca na etat evam guṇa karma sāmānyānām samavetānām eva viśeṣaṇa tva upalabdheḥ na ca guṇeṣu nirguṇa tayā saṃkhyā samavāyaḥ sambhavati asamaveta anāñca guṇa karma sāmānyānām viśeṣaṇa tve mithyājñāna ādi a bhāvaḥ tad viśiṣṭa jñānasya ubhayatra aviśeṣāt iti vakṣyāmaḥ tasmāt upacaritaḥ eva guṇa ādiṣu eka ādi vyavahāraḥ vyākhyeyaḥ 
[I,023,1_I,023,4]	tathā karmaṇi pratijñām karoti karmāṇi paramārtha santi pūrva uktāt eva sādhanāt karmāṇi iti vyavahāre karma tva yogam sādhanam iti vakṣyati utkṣepaṇa ādi bhede ca tat tad sāmānyam iti tathā utkṣepaṇa apakṣepaṇa ākuñcana prasāraṇa gamanāni iti dvandvaḥ samāsaḥ nyūna adhika vyavaccheda arthañca pañca eva karmāṇi iti avadhāraṇam atra tu pañca lakṣaṇa yogi tvam sa viśeṣaṇam pūrvavat sādhanam 
[I,023,9_I,023,14]	atha bhramaṇa ādīnām upalambhāt avadhāraṇa anupapattiḥ na gamanaḥ eva antarbhāvāt iti āha gamana grahaṇāt bhramaṇa recana syandana ūrdhva jvalana tiryak pavana patanana manonnamana ādayaḥ gamana viśeṣāḥ gamana saṅgṛhītāḥ tad bhedāḥ eva na jāti antarāṇi anye tu gamana viśeṣāḥ eva na bhavanti bhramaṇa ādayaḥ kim tarhi jāti antarāṇi iti manyante etat ca asat vyākhyānam iti vakṣyāmaḥ karma parīkṣāyām 
[I,023,18^1]	evam sāmānye pratijñām karoti sāmānyam parama artha sat iti pūrvavat sādhanam sāmānya vyavahāre tu lakṣaṇam vakṣyamāṇam sādhanam iti bhedam nirūpayati dvividham kena rūpeṇa iti āha parama parañcaḥ iti anuvṛtti pratyaya kāraṇam iti kāryeṇa sattām darśayati tathā hi yat anugata jñānam dravya guṇa karma animittam tad artha antara sambandhāt bhavati iti vakṣyāmaḥ tad parīkṣāyām tat etat asādhāraṇa tvāt sāmānyasya itarasmāt bhedakam api bhavati tathā hi dravya guṇa karma animittam abādhyam ānañca anugatam jñānam na sāmānyam vinā bhavati iti asādhāraṇam eva tatra parāpara bhedam nirūpayan āha sattā param sāmānyam iti kutas 
[I,023,18^2]	mahā viṣaya tvāt tathā hi dravyeṣu eva dravya tvam guṇeṣu eva guṇa tvam karmasu eva karma tvam sattāyāḥ dravya ādi viṣaya vyāpaka tvena mahā viṣaya tvāt paratvam iti yaḥ hi yat viṣayam vyāpnoti sa tad apekṣayā paraḥ yathā alpa viṣaya pārthiva apekṣayā mahā viṣayaḥ iti sā ca sattā anuvṛtteḥ eva kāraṇam iti sāmānyam eva yadi api asāmānya ādibhyaḥ vyāvartate tathā api sāmānyam vastu anuvṛtta jñānasya eva kāraṇam iti sāmānyam eva tathā dravya tva ādi aparam iti dravya tvam ādiḥ yeṣām ityādi grahaṇāt guṇa tva karma tva pṛthivī tva ādeḥ grahaṇam tat ca sattāpekṣayā alpa viṣaya tvāt aparam iti tat hi sāmānya lakṣaṇa yogi tvena sāmānyam sat upacārataḥ atra viśeṣa ākhyām api labhate na ca upacāraḥ nimittam vinā pravartate iti āha vyāvṛtteḥ api hetu tvāt iti na kevalam anuvṛtteḥ eva kim tarhi vyāvṛtta jñānasya api hetu tvāt viśeṣaṇe hi vyāvṛtta jñāna janaka tvam dṛṣṭam tat ca iha api asti iti upacāraḥ pravartate mukhyāḥ tu viśeṣāḥ tad lakṣaṇa yoginaḥ eva 
[I,024,11_I,024,13]	evam viśeṣeṣu pratijñām karoti viśeṣāḥ paramārtha santaḥ iti pūrvavat sādhanam nitya dravya vṛttayaḥ iti tathā buddhi ādayaḥ api nitya dravyeṣu eva vartante iti vipakṣa eka deśa vṛtti vyavaccheda artham nitya dravyeṣu vṛttiḥ eva iti avadhāraṇam na ca evam buddhi ādayaḥ iti nitya dravyeṣu eva vṛttiḥ eva eṣām iti sa avadhāraṇam vākyam etat dravya guṇa karmāṇi tu nitya dravyeṣu anitya dravyeṣu ca vartante iti sāmānyañcā dravye api iti upapannam avadhāraṇam nitya dravyeṣu eva iti anya yoga vyavacchedena nitya dravyeṣu vartamāna tvāt viśeṣāḥ itarasmāt bhidyante iti 
[I,024,20_I,024,23^1]	anye tu padārtha apekṣayā lakṣaṇam vivakṣitam iti nitya dravyeṣu eva vartamāna tvam hetuḥ iti bruvate tat ca ayuktam vipakṣa eka deśa vṛtteḥ agamaka tvāt na ca padārtha apekṣa yā api ayoga vyavacchedam vinā vipakṣa eka deśāt buddhi ādeḥ asya vyāvṛttiḥ iti nitya dravya vṛttayaḥ iti antya padasya vivaraṇam etat tathā ca vakṣyati nitya dravyāṇi utpatti vināśayoḥ ante vyavasthita tvāt anta śabda vācyāni teṣu bhavāḥ tad vṛttayaḥ antyāḥ iti vyākhyāyante te ca viśeṣāḥ viśeṣayanti vyāvartayanti sva āśrayam āśraya antarāt iti parīkṣā artham āha te ca atyantam sarvadā vyāvṛtti buddheḥ eva hetu tvāt viśeṣāḥ eva 
[I,024,23^2]	na sāmānyam api iti tathā hi samāna jāti guṇa kriyā dhārāḥ paramāṇavaḥ viśeṣa sambandhinaḥ vyāvṛtta buddhi viṣaya tvāt yaḥ yaḥ vyāvṛtta jñāna viṣayaḥ sa sa viśeṣa sambaddhaḥ yathā sthāṇu ādi tathā ca vyāvṛtta jñāna viṣayāḥ paramāṇavaḥ tasmāt viśeṣa yoginaḥ iti vyāvṛtta jñāna viṣaya tvañca ghaṭa ādiṣu upalabdham iti nityeṣu api sādhyate dravya tvena eva hetunā na ca guṇa ādīnām anyatarasya eva paramāṇuṣu vyāvṛtta jñāna kāraṇa tvam samāna jāti guṇa kriyā ādhāra tvena viśeṣita tvāt na ca dṛṣṭānte guṇa ādi viśeṣa upalabdheḥ iti dṛṣṭānta dārṣṭa antikayoḥ vaiṣamya āpādanena vilakṣaṇa viśeṣa asiddhiḥ iti vācyam sarva anumāneṣu samāna tvāt iti vyāvṛtta jñāna janaka tvena nityeṣu viśeṣāṇām sadbhāvaḥ iti sthitam vistareṇa tu viśeṣa parīkṣāyām parīkṣiṣyante iti alam 
[I,025,9_I,025,11]	atha ayuta siddhānām ityādinā samavāye pratijñām karoti samavāyaḥ paramārtha san pūrva uktāt eva sādhanāt iti lakṣaṇam ucyate ihapratyaya hetu tvam antarālā darśanasya api iti sambandha grahaṇam tathā hi dūrāt grāma āra āmayoḥ antarālam apaśyatām iha grāme vṛkṣāḥ iti jñānam dṛṣṭam tathā api ākāśa śakuni sambandhena vyabhicāraḥ tat iha pratyaya hetuḥ sambandhaḥ ca iti tathā hi iha ākāśe śakuniḥ iti jñānam dṛṣṭam tad vyavaccheda artham ādhārya ādhāra grahaṇam na ca ākāśasya ādhāra tvam ādheya tvam vā adhara uttara bhāvasya abhāvāt yatra hi saṃyogi dravyeṣu adhara uttara bhāvaḥ tatra eva ādhāra ādheya bhāvaḥ kuṇḍa badara ādau upalabdhaḥ tad abhāvaḥ ca ākāśe tasya vyāpaka tvena śakunim vyāpya sadbhāvāt 
[I,025,19_I,025,22]	atha ākāśasya atīndriya tvāt iha iti jñānam na syāt tasya hi aparokṣeṣu eva bhāvāt tat asat atīndriye api ākāśe iha iti jñānam kevalam bhrāntam tasya vyavaccheda artham upapanna mādhārya ādhāra padam iṣṭañca bhrānta iha jñānasya vyavaccheda artham sambandha padam anye tu asya ca udyasya parihāra artham ā samantāt kāśataḥ iti ākāśam vartate iti upacāreṇa ākāśam raśmayaḥ abhidhīyante te ca pratyakṣam iti upapannam iha ākāśe śakuniḥ iti jñānam iti manyante tat ca asat mukhya sadbhāve api upacāra kalpanāyām atiprasaṅgāt uktañca atīndriye api ākāśe aparokṣa jñānam bhrāntam tad vyavaccheda artham viśeṣaṇam iti mūrta dravya abhāvena ca ākāśena sambandha abhāvaḥ eva iti 
[I,026,1]	tathā hi ādhārya ādhāra bhūtānām yaḥ sambandhaḥ ihapratyaya hetuḥ sa samavāyaḥ iti ukte kuṇḍa badara sambandhena vyabhicāraḥ tad artham ayuta siddhānām iti padam yuta siddhiḥ vakṣyamāṇā sā vidyate yeṣām te yuta siddhāḥ tad niṣedhena ca ayuta siddhāḥ teṣām iti tathā api ayuta siddhānām yaḥ sambandhaḥ saḥ samavāyaḥ iti ukte vyabhicāra abhāvaḥ tat na vācya vācaka bhāvena viṣaya viṣayi bhāvena ca vyabhicārāt tathā hi ākāśa mahat tvam ākāśe samavetam mahat tva śabda vācyam iti ākāśa mahat tva tad śabdayoḥ vācya vācaka bhāvaḥ sambandhaḥ na ca yuta siddhiḥ vibhinna āśraya samavāyi tva abhāvāt tathā hi ākāśa mahat tvam ākāśe samavetam tat vācakaḥ ca śabdaḥ tatra eva iti ayuta siddha tvam evam icchā ādi a ālambanam vijñānam ātmani samavetam icchā ādayaḥ ca tatra eva iti ayuta siddha tve sati eṣām viṣaya viṣayi bhāvaḥ iti anayoḥ vyavaccheda artha mādhārya ādhāra padam na ca atra ākāśa mahat tva śabdaḥ tat mahat tva ādhāraḥ na api icchā ādi ālambana vijñānam tad ādhāram iti 
[I,026,11]	nanu evam api ābhyām eva vyabhicāraḥ tathā hi ayuta siddhānāmādhārya ādhāra bhūtānām yaḥ sambandhaḥ saḥ samavāyaḥ iti ukte api vācya vācaka bhāva viṣaya viṣayi bhāvābhyām eva vyabhicāraḥ tathā hi ākāśa śabdena ākāśam abhidhīyate iti anayoḥ ādhārya ādhāra bhāve sati vācya vācaka bhāvaḥ na ca asti yuta siddhiḥ evam ātma ālambanam aham iti jñānam ātmani eva iti ayuta siddha tve satya adhārya ādhāra bhūtayoḥ asti viṣaya viṣayi bhāva iti tad vyavaccheda artham avadhāraṇa mādhārya ādhāra bhūtānām eva yaḥ sambandhaḥ sa samavāyaḥ iti vācya vācaka viṣaya viṣayi bhāvayoḥ ca adhārya ādhāra bhūteṣu tad viparīteṣu ca sadbhāvaḥ iti vyavacchedaḥ 
[I,026,18_I,026,21]	nanu evam ayuta siddhānām iti vyartham eva na asya api sa avadhāraṇasya lakṣaṇa antara tvāt tathā hi ayutasiddhānām eva yaḥ sambandhaḥ sa samavāyaḥ iti vācya vācaka viṣaya viṣayi bhāvau tu yuta siddhānām ayutasiddha anāñca iti atra kecid asat dūṣaṇam udbhāvayanti samavāya asiddhau yuteṣu āśrayeṣu samavāyaḥ na yuta siddhiḥ sā vidyate yeṣām te na yuta siddhāḥ tad pratiṣedhena ca ayuta siddhānām abhāve na samavāyaḥ iti etat ca asat dūṣaṇam lakṣaṇasya vidyamāna vyavacchedaka tvāt yadi hi avidyamānam lakṣaṇena utpādyeta bhavet etat dūṣaṇam ayuta siddhānām iti lakṣaṇena samavāya akaraṇe yuta siddhānām abhāvena ayuta siddhānām abhāvaḥ iti lakṣaṇā sambhavaḥ iti na ca etat lakṣaṇasya jñāpaka tvāt iti 
[I,027,1]	atha ayuta siddhānām eva adhārya ādhāra bhūtānām eva yaḥ sambandhaḥ sa samavāyaḥ iti lakṣaṇa dvaya parisamāptau iha pratyaya hetuḥ iti vyartham na parīkṣā artha tvāt tathā hi tantuṣu paṭaḥ ityādi ihapratyayaḥ sambandha kāryaḥ abādhyam ānā iha pratyaya tvāt yaḥ yaḥ abādhyam āna iha pratyayaḥ sa sa sambandha kāryaḥ yathā iha kuṇḍe dadhi iti pratyayaḥ tathā ca ayam abādhyam āna iha pratyayaḥ tasmāt sambandha kāryaḥ iti na ca atra samavāya pūrvaka tvam sādhyate dṛṣṭāntasya sādhya vikalatā prasaṅgāt na api saṃyoga pūrvaka tvam kim tarhi sambandha mātra kārya tvam sa ca saṃyoga ādi vilakṣaṇa tvāt samavāyaḥ eva iti vakṣyāmaḥ tad parīkṣāyām iti alam ati vistareṇa 
[I,027,8_I,027,9]	evam dravya ādiṣu padārtheṣu ukteṣu sāmānya viśeṣa samavāyānām lakṣaṇa parīkṣā śravaṇāt antevāsinaḥ prāktanam prakaraṇam kim uddeśa param lakṣaṇa param parīkṣā param vā iti saṃśaye sati tad nirāsa artham upasaṃhāra vākyam evam ityādi pradhāna tayā prādhānyam tasya sarvatra uddeśa vidhānāt uddeśaḥ tu saṃjñā mātreṇa padārtha abhidhānam iti lakṣaṇa parīkṣayoḥ ca sāmānya ādiṣu eva bhāvāt anuṣaṅgataḥ abhidhānam iti yat vā dravya ādi padārtha parijñānāt niḥśreyasam iti matvā pravṛttaḥ tad uddeśa parijñāna mātrāt niḥśreyasa alābhe ati pratāraka tām manyamānaḥ śravaṇāt antevāsī mā vyāvartatām iti tad āśvāsana artham vākyam evam dharmaiḥ vinā dharmiṇām kevalānām uddeśaḥ kṛtaḥ na lakṣaṇam na api parīkṣā tad tad dvāreṇa sādharmya vaidharmya parijñānam śrautam upajātam abhyāsa vaśāt ātmani aśeṣa viśeṣa āliṅgite vijñānam aparokṣam kurvan niḥśreyasam upajanayati iti 
[I,027,19]	nanu ṣaṣ eva padārthāḥ iti avadhāraṇa abhyupagame dharmāṇām vyatireka asambhavāt katham astitva ādibhiḥ vinā dharmiṇām uddeśaḥ kṛtaḥ iti na avadhāraṇasya dharmi viṣaya tva abhyupagamāt tat na astitva ādayaḥ api sva adhikaraṇa dharma apekṣayā dharmiṇam eva iti tat apekṣayā api vyāhatam avadhāraṇam tathā hi astitvam abhidhīyamāna tvāt abhidheya tva adhikaraṇam evam abhidheya tvam astitva adhikaraṇam ityādi yojyam 
[I,027,24_I,028,5]	atha asādhāraṇa dharma adhikaraṇa tvena avadhāraṇam arthavat tat asat astitva ādeḥ api asādhāraṇa dharma adhikaraṇa tvāt tathā hi astitvam abhidheya tvāt bhidyate abhidheya tvañca astitvāt bhidyate iti na ca asādhāraṇa dharma samparkam vinā vyāvṛttiḥ ghaṭate iti asādhāraṇa dharma adhikaraṇa tvena avadhāraṇā sambhavaḥ iti ced na etat evam kriyāvat guṇavat samavāyi kāraṇam iti dravya lakṣaṇam ayoga ani ayoga vyavacchede dravya āśrita tvam guṇānām tathā kṣaṇika tve sati niyamena mūrta dravya vṛtti tvam karmaṇām nitya tva ekatve sati samavāyena aneka vartamāna tvam sāmānyasya ayoga anya yoga vyavacchedena nityeṣu eva dravyeṣu vartamāna tvam viśeṣāṇām niyamena ayuta siddha sambandha tvam samavāyasya iti evam dharma adhikāriṇaḥ ṣaṭ eva iti avadhāraṇe api adoṣaḥ atha vyatiriktānām api īyat tā asambhavāt asaṃkhyāta tvena tattva jñāna aviṣaya tvam iti ced na pṛthivyām iva ānantye api ekasya nimittasya upagrahāt tattva jñāna viṣaya tvam iti nimittantu tatra pṛthivyām pṛthivī tvam dharmeṣu dharma rūpa tā iti 
[I,028,8]	atha dharmeṣu nitya tvam uta anitya tvam iti ced nitya tve api dharmi vināśe sattāvat avasthāna abhyupagamāda doṣaḥ anitya tve api dravyasya eva samavāyi kāraṇa tvāt guṇa ādiṣu na utpatti abhāvaḥ vināśa vat nimitta kāraṇāt eva utpatti abhyupagamāt tathā hi dravya guṇa karma ātmakam kāyam samavāyi ādi kāraṇebhyaḥ niṣpadyamānam dṛṣṭam viparītantu nimittāt eva tathā ca dharmāḥ nimittāt eva utpadyante dravya guṇa karma vyatireki kārya tvāt yat yat dravya guṇa karma vyatireki kāryam tad tad nimitta kāraṇāt eva utpadyamānam dṛṣṭam yathā vināśaḥ tathā ca dharmāḥ dravya guṇa karma vyatireki kāryāḥ tasmāt nimitta kāraṇāt eva utpadyante utpatti dharmāṇāñca anitya tvam dṛṣṭam iti astitva ādayaḥ api anityāḥ iti astitvañcā asti iti pratyaya nimittam yena saḥ asti iti pratyayaḥ bhavati iti abhidheya tvam vā abhidheya pratyaya kāraṇam ityādi sarvatra yojyam 
[I,028,17_I,028,20]	avyatireke tu vyatiriktaiḥ dharmaiḥ vinā dharmiṇām uddeśaḥ kṛtaḥ iti vyākhyānam vyatireke bādhaka pramāṇa upapatteḥ vyatiriktā iti viśeṣaṇam sāmarthyāt labhyate eva tathā hi avadhāraṇa anupapattiḥ vyatireka pakṣe atha uktam viśiṣṭa dharma adhikaraṇa tvena avadhāraṇam vivakṣitam iti tat na ukta lakṣaṇānām ṣaṣ eva padārthāḥ iti avadhāraṇe sādhāraṇa dharma adhikaraṇānām padārtha antarāṇām aparisaṃkhyāta tvāt tattva jñāna asambhavaḥ eva tattva jñāna arthañcā avadhāraṇam na ca padārtha antarāṇām ajñeya tvam sarvasya bhāva prapañcasya jñeya tayā upakṣepāt teṣu ca sāmānya viśeṣa rūpa tayā tattva jñānam kāryam sāmānyam bhāva rūpa tā viśeṣaḥ tu dravya ādi vat lakṣaṇa yogaḥ tad atirikteṣu ca padārtheṣu sāmānyatas jñānam na viśeṣate iti 
[I,028,26_I,029,5]	atha dravya ādi lakṣaṇa vat dharma rūpa tā viśeṣasya sadbhāva viśeṣeṇa api tattva jñāna viṣaya tvam iti ced tarhi padārtha antara sadbhāve api niyata lakṣaṇa apekṣayā avadhāraṇa abhyupagame ṣaṭ eva iti api na vācyam samavāya sadbhāve api pūrva lakṣaṇa apekṣayā pañca eva iti syāt evam uttarottara padārtha sadbhāve api pūrva pūrva lakṣaṇa apekṣayā avadhāraṇa abhyupagame sati ekaḥ eva padārthaḥ syāt tathā hi dravya lakṣaṇa yoge ekaḥ eva padārthaḥ na anyaḥ tasya hi dravya lakṣaṇa yogi tve dravyaḥ eva antar bhāvāt atha guṇa ādiṣu vibhinna lakṣaṇa sambandhiṣu tattva jñāna abhāva prasaṅgāt na evam avadhāraṇam evam tarhi dharmeṣu ṣaṣ lakṣaṇa ālakṣiteṣu tattva jñāna abhāva prasaṅgāt ṣaṭ eva iti avadhāraṇam anyāyyam pratijñā tañca padārtheṣu sādharmya vaidharmya pratijñānam

[I,029,20_I,029,23]	atha yat eva dharma tvam astitvādeḥ ādheyam tat eva anyeṣām ādhāraḥ tad ādheyaḥ ca iti na yuktam etat ekasmin kāle yat yasya ādhāraḥ tat tasya eva ādheyam iti anupalambhāt tathā astitva ādeḥ api ekasya nimittasya anekatra anuvṛttau sāmānya antarbhāvaḥ tad lakṣaṇa yogi tvāt yadi ca ekam nityam astitvam sarvatra padārtheṣu asti iti pratyaya janakam syāt kim sattayā svarūpa sattvena vā atha anekam pratipadārtham astitva abhidheya tva ādi iti ced na dharmi vināśe api sat tāvat avasthānam tathā hi eka āśraya vināśe api ekatayā sattāyāḥ padārtha antare api sat sat iti pratyaya janaka tvena avasthānam dharmāṇāntu pratipadārtha niyata tvāt āśraya antare asti iti pratyaya janakaḥ anyaḥ eva dharmaḥ iti na āśraya vināśe api avasthāne pramāṇam asti iti 
[I,030,1]	atha dravyasya eva samavāyi kāraṇa tvena guṇa ādiṣu utpatti kāraṇa abhāvāt āśraya vināśe api avasthānam iti ced evam tarhi dravyeṣu anityam guṇa ādiṣu ca nityam iti syāt iṣyate eva iti ced tarhi vināśa vat nimitta kāraṇāt eva utpadyante astitva ādayaḥ iti vyāhatam etat tathā astitva ādeḥ pratipadārtha niyata tvena ānantyāt teṣu eva asti ityādya bhinna vyavahāra darśanāt ekam astitveṣu asti tvam abhidheya tveṣu abhidheya tvam tatra api anye astitva ādayaḥ iti prāktanam eva dūṣaṇam abhyūhyam

[I,030,13^1]	yat ca anumānam nimitta kāraṇāt eva utpadyante dharmāḥ dravya guṇa karma vyatireki kārya tvāt vināśa vat iti atra kāryatvasya sva kāraṇa sattā sambandha rūpa tā āyām asiddhaḥ hetuḥ vināśasya ca sva kāraṇa sattā sambandha abhāvāt sādhana vikalaḥ ca dṛṣṭāntaḥ dravya ādi vyatireke ca pramāṇa abhāvāt sandigdha viśeṣaṇaḥ hetuḥ atha ṣaṣ padārtheṣu asti iti jñānam vyatireke pramāṇam tathā hi dravya ādiṣu asti ityādi jñānāni ṣaṭpadārtha vyatirikta vidhīyamāna nimitta nibandhanāni ṣaṣ padārtheṣu utpadyamāna tvāt yāni tu ṣaṣ padārtha vyatirikta vidhīyamāna nimitta nibandhanāni na bhavanti na tāni ṣaṭsu utpadyante yathā dravya ādi jñānāni tathā ṣaṭsu na utpadyante asti ityādi jñānāni tasmāt ṣaṭpadārtha vyatirikta vidhīyamāna nimitta nibandhanāni iti vyatirekī tathā hi 
[I,030,13^2]	ṣaṣ padārtheṣu asti iti jñānam tathā abhidheyaḥ iti utpadyamānam dṛṣṭam iti pakṣa dharma tvam na ca ṣaṭpadārtha vyatirikta bhāva rūpa nimitta nibandhanam ubhaya abhimatam vijñānam asti iti sa pakṣa abhāvaḥ dravya ādi jñānantu ṣaṭpadārtha vyatirikta bhāva rūpa nimitta nibandhanam na bhavati iti vipakṣaḥ tasmāt ca ṣaṣ padārtheṣu utpadyamāna tvam hi dravya ādi vyāvṛttam tathā hi dravya jñānam dravyaḥ eva na tu guṇa ādiṣu evam guṇa jñānam guṇaḥ eva na karma ādiṣu api iti na ṣaṭsu utpattiḥ iti vipakṣa vyāvṛttiḥ eva vipakṣe pratyakṣa āgamābhyām virudhyate iti na kāla atyaya apadiṣṭaḥ viśeṣa anupalabdheḥ ayogāt na prakaraṇa samaḥ iti tasmāt vyatireka siddhau na sandigdha viśeṣaṇaḥ hetuḥ iti 
[I,030,13^3]	na etat evam ṣaṭsu padārtheṣu utadyamāna tvam vyakti apekṣayā asiddham tathā hi ekam asti iti jñānam ṣaṭsu padārtheṣu utpadyate evam abhidheya jñānañca iti atha asti dravyam asti guṇaḥ iti evaṃjātīyakam jñānam ṣaṭsu utpadyate iti na asti asiddha tā tarhi dravya guṇa ādi jñānam jñāna jātīyam ṣaṭsu utpadyate na ca ṣaṣ padārtha atirikta bhāva rūpa nimitta nibandhanam iti vyabhicāraḥ yat ca ṣaṭpadārtha atiriktam bhāva rūpa nimittam tasya anuvṛtta vyāvṛtta tāyām prāktanam eva dūṣaṇa m ūhyam sattā sambandhena ca padārtheṣu bhāva vyatirekābhyām asti iti jñānam utpadyamānam dṛṣṭam iti virodhaḥ astitva dharmāt eva astitva jñānam iti ced tarhi sattāyāḥ sadbhāve kim pramāṇam iti vācyam

[I,032,6]	tathā āśritānām bhāvaḥ āśrita tvam āśraya āśrayi bhāva lakṣaṇā vṛttiḥ sā ca ākāśa ādiṣu na teṣām āśraya abhāvāt na ca āśraya āyi bhāvasya samavāya rūpa tāyām samavāye asambhavāt na ṣaṣ padārtha vyāpi tvam atha pañcānām samavāya lakṣaṇā vṛttiḥ āśrita tvam samavāyaḥ tu sva ātma vṛttiḥ iti ced evam tarhi pañcānām samavāyi tvam iti punaruktam syāt tathā hi samavāyi tvam samavāya lakṣaṇā vṛttiḥ sā ca pañcānām āśrita tva padena uktā iti āśrita tvapadena āśrita tva upalakṣitasya iha abhidhānāt adoṣaḥ
