[I,038,24]	tasmāt yat bhūtvā na bhavati ātmānam jahāti tat anityam iti kecid tat api asat vināśasya vastu kāle asambhavi tvena viśeṣaṇa tva ayogāt atha avidyamānaḥ api vināśaḥ anumīyamānaḥ bhavati upalakṣaṇam iti ced tathā api vinaṣṭaḥ iti syāt na anityam iti na paryāya tvāt tathā hi anityāḥ viṣayāḥ vināśinaḥ iti vyavahāraḥ yadi ca anitya jñāne anyat nimittam na syāt pratipadyemahi ubhayānta upalakṣitā sattā viśeṣaṇam iti yathā anutpatti vināśayoḥ avidyamānayoḥ api kayācid bhaṅgyā satta upalakṣaṇa tvam tathā vastu upalakṣaṇa tāyām api na kiñcid bādhakam asti iti tathā hi prāc abhāvaḥ smaryamāṇaḥ pradhvaṃsa abhāvaḥ ca ānumīyamānaḥ vastu upalakṣaṇam iti 
[I,039,7_I,039,11]	atha vināśānutpattiḥ anutpatti vināśaḥ ca vidyamāna tvāt sattā viśeṣaṇam iti ced parama arthasya viśeṣaṇa tvam tayoḥ kalpyatām kim atiprayāsena atha anitya jñānam abhāva anuraktam na bhavati iti viśiṣṭa sattā viśeṣaṇam upakalpyate na sattā anurāgasya anupalabdheḥ kevalam anitya tva anuraktam anityam iti jñānam utpadyate anitya tvantu prāc abhāva pradhvaṃsa abhāva upalakṣitāḥ vastunaḥ sattā iti udyota kara kalpanāyām kalpanā gauravam syāt iti pradhvaṃsaḥ eva anitya tvam iti iṣṭam bhāṣya kāreṇa iti 
[I,039,14_I,039,15]	tathā kāraṇānām bhāvaḥ kāraṇa tvam kāraṇa tvañca samavāyi asamavāyi kāraṇa tvam samavāyinaḥ asamavāyanaḥ ca ātmīyam svarūpam na nimitta kāraṇa tvam sāmānya ādiṣu api bhāvāt tat ca pratiniyatam api avivakṣita viśeṣam sādharmyam tat kim sarveṣām iti atas āha anyatra pārimāṇḍalī ādibhyaḥ iti pārimāṇḍalī ādīni varjayitvā parimaṇḍalāḥ paramāṇavaḥ teṣām bhāvaḥ pārimāṇḍalyam paramāṇu parimāṇam tat ca dvi aṇu kāṇu parimāṇa utpattau akāraṇam iti vakṣyāmaḥ parimāṇa avasare ādipadena ākāśa ādi vibhudravyam antyaḥ śabdaḥ paratva aparatva pṛthaktva ādya kāraṇam iti 
[I,039,24_I,039,25]	na ca param pūrva sādharmyam dravya āśritānām bhāvaḥ dravya āśrita tvam tat ca anyatra nitya dravyebhyaḥ teṣām āśraya abhāvāt yadi api ṣaṇṇām āśrita tva abhidhānena dravya ādīnām āśrita tvam uktam tathā api dravya upalakṣitasya iha abhidhānāt apunaruktam iti 
[I,040,3_I,040,9]	idānīm sāmānya ādīnām na ekasya dvayoḥ vā kim tarhi trayāṇām api sādharmyam sva ātmanā sādhāraṇa dharmeṇa upacāra nimittena sattvam sat sat iti pratyaya janaka tvam mukhye hi anavasthā ādi bādhaka upapatteḥ anye tu sva ātma sattvam sattān adhikaraṇānām sat saditi pratyaya janaka tvam iti bruvate atra hi nimittān abhidhāne satām bhāvaḥ sattvam iti na kiñcid uktam syāt 
[I,040,11_I,040,14]	atha sattān adhikaraṇānām sva ātmanā nimittena sat sat iti pratyaya janaka tvam tarhi tasya anuvṛtti rūpa tāyām doṣa upapatteḥ vyāvṛtta rūpa tā yāñca anugata jñāna janaka tvam na syāt iti upacāra nimitta tvam eva nyāyyam nanu evam sāmānya ādiṣu upacaritam sattvam syāt iṣyate eva sattvam sat sat iti jñāna janaka tvam upacaritam 
[I,040,16_I,040,18]	atha upacarita sattva abhyupagame paramārthataḥ asattvam tat iṣṭam eva na paramārthataḥ sāmānya ādau sat saditi jñānam upacāra abhyupagamāt atha sattān adhikaraṇa tve sāmānya ādeḥ abhāvaḥ syāt tat asat asādhāraṇa dharma adhikaraṇa tayā pramāṇa siddhasya abhāva abhyupagame dravya ādiṣu tathā abhāvaḥ syāt atas sāmānya ādau ukta rūpe svarūpa sattve na doṣaḥ iti 
[I,040,21]	tathā buddhiḥ lakṣaṇam yeṣām buddhyā lakṣyante iti vā buddhi lakṣaṇāḥ teṣām bhāvaḥ buddhi lakṣaṇa tvam sāmānya śabdena api arthāt anugata vyāvṛtta iha buddhi anyatama buddhi lakṣaṇa tvam vivakṣitam iti vijñātam anugatā hi buddhiḥ na viśeṣe na api samavāye vyāvṛttā ca na sāmānya samavāyayoḥ tathā iha buddhiḥ na sāmānya viśeṣeṣu iti vyāvṛtta tvāt vaidharmyam syāt iti anyatama grahaṇam tat ca sarveṣu samāna tvāt eva sādharmyam 
[I,041,1]	yat vā buddhiḥ viśeṣaṇa antara upacaritā lakṣaṇam itarasmāt bhedakam tat ca avivakṣita viśeṣam sādharmyam tathā hi dravya guṇa karmasu anugata sāmānya vaśāt anugata jñāna janaka tvam sāmānye tu svarūpa tayā eva tathā atyanta vyāvṛttyā viśeṣeṣu eva ayutasiddheṣu abādhyam ānā iha buddhiḥ samavāyaḥ eva iti vyāvṛttau api buddhi vedya tvam samāna tvāt sādharmyam 
[I,041,5_I,041,10]	evam kāryāṇām bhāvaḥ kārya tvam tad abhāvaḥ akārya tvam sva kāraṇa sattā sambandha abhāvaḥ tathā kāraṇānām bhāvaḥ kāraṇa tvam tad abhāvaḥ akāraṇa tvam samavāyi asamavāyikāraṇa tva abhāvaḥ nimitta kāraṇa tvañca jñāna utpatta āviṣyate eva tathā na sāmānya viśeṣavat tvam asāmānya viśeṣavat tvam apara sāmānya abhāvaḥ na tad upalakṣitaḥ samavāyaḥ samavāye tad abhāva prasaṅgāt 
[I,041,11]	nityānām bhāvaḥ nitya tvam avināśi tvam ubhayānta upalakṣita sattā sambandha abhāvaḥ vā tathā hi kārya vastunaḥ vināśi tvam dṛṣṭam sāmānya ādeḥ ca akārya tvāt avināśaḥ na ca āśraya vināśāt vināśaḥ tasya eka āśraya vināśe api āśraya antare sva anurakta pratyaya janaka tvāt tathā hi eka āśraya vināśe api āśraya antare sattā sat sat iti jñāna hetuḥ samavāyaḥ ca iha pratyaya hetuḥ iti anayoḥ āśraya vināśāt na vināśaḥ 
[I,041,16_I,041,20]	anitya āśrayam sāmānyam samasta āśraya vināśena nirādhārasya abhāvāt vinaṃkṣyati iti na etat evam akārya vastu tvena avināśi tva siddheḥ samasta āśraya vināśe api avasthānam iṣyate atas eva kevalam āśraya abhāvāt go tva ādi rūpa tayā na vyapadiśyate iti akārya vastunaḥ ca vināśe gagana ādīnām api uccheda prasaṅgaḥ atha anitya āśrayasya āśraya utpatti anantaram rūpa ādi vat upalambhāt asiddham akārya tvam iti ced na upalambhasya ubhayatha abhāvāt 
[I,041,22]	na jñāyate kim vastu utpatti anantaram utpadyate atha abhivyajyate iti utpāde bādhaka upapatteḥ abhivyajyate iti iṣyate tathā hi dravyasya eva samavāyi kāraṇa tva vidhānena guṇa karmaṇoḥ tad pratiṣedhāt tad ādhārasya utpatti abhāvaḥ tat yathā sāmānya ādhārasya yugapad utpattim vinā samavāyikāraṇa abhāvāt ca iti tathā hi yatra samavetam kāryam tat avaśyam samavāyi kāraṇam sāmānyasya krama bhāviṣu sva ādhāreṣu sarveṣu samavāya upalabdheḥ sarvam samavāyikāraṇam iti sakala ādhāra niṣpattau eva utpattiḥ iti pūrva bhāviṣu upalambhaḥ na syāt 
[I,042,4]	atha sarga ādau bhūyasām sva ādhārāṇām utpādāt utpannam sāmānyam krama bhāviṣu ādhāreṣu samaveṣyati iti ced na kārya antareṣu adarśanāt na hi rūpa ādi kāryam sva ādhāreṣu samavetam upajātam anyena samavāya vṛttyā sambadhyamānam dṛṣṭam iti na ca krameṇa utpadyamāneṣu anyat sāmānyam iti vācyam bhede pramāṇa abhāvāt abhede tu anugatam jñānam eva pramāṇam iti vakṣyāmaḥ sāmānya parīkṣāyām 
[I,042,9_I,042,11]	tat evam utpatti pakṣe bādhaka upapatteḥ vastu utpatti anantaram samabhivyajyate iti akārya tvāt nitya tvam siddham evam artha śabdān abhidheya tvañca sva samaya artha śabda abhidheya tva abhāvaḥ iti yadi api dravya ādeḥ eva kāryatva ādi vidhānāt iha akārya tvādiḥ labhyate tathā api sādharmyasya vivakṣita tvāt abhidhānam iti sāmānya ādīnām kārya tva ādi abhāvaḥ api sādharmyam iti 
[I,042,15_I,042,17]	evam padārthānām sādharmyam abhidhāya dravyāṇām sādharmya nirūpaṇa artham āha pṛthivī ādīnām ityādi pṛthivī ādiḥ yeṣām tāni pṛthivī ādīni teṣām na jñāyate kiyatām atas navānām api dravya tva yogaḥ sādharmyam dravya tvena yogaḥ dravya tva upalakṣitaḥ samavāyaḥ iti yadi api samavāyaḥ pañca padārtha vṛttiḥ tathā api dravya tvena upalakṣitaḥ asādhāraṇa tvāt bhavati eva lakṣaṇam iti 
[I,042,22_I,043,1]	na ca dravyāṇām bhāvaḥ dravya tvam iti ukte arthāt avagamyate yogaḥ iti vācyam gamya vṛtti āśrayaṇena śabda vṛtti pratiṣedhe ati prasaṅgāt na ca upacarita bheda tvāt avāstavam lakṣaṇam iti dūṣaṇam śrotrasya iva viśiṣṭa artha kriyā janaka tvāt na api asamartha viśeṣaṇa tā yoga padam vinā hi asambhavitvā āśaṅkā anativṛtteḥ iti śeṣam lakṣaṇa dūṣaṇasya pratisamādhānam vakṣyāmaḥ pṛthivī adhikāre 
[I,043,3]	lakṣaṇañca bheda artham vyavahāra arthañca iti tathā hi pṛthivī ādīnītarasmāt bhidyante dravyāṇi iti vā vyavahartavyāni dravya tva yogāt ye tu na bhidyante na api dravyāṇi iti vyavahriyante na te dravya tva yuktāḥ yathā rūpa ādayaḥ na ca tathā na dravya tva yuktāni pṛthivī ādīni iti tasmāt itarasmāt bhidyante dravyāṇi iti vā vyavahartavyāni iti 
[I,043,7_I,043,10]	evam dravya śabdasya pravṛttau pṛthivī ādīnām navānām api dravya tva yogaḥ nimittam iti śabda artha nirūpaṇa paratvena api sambadhyate vākyam tathā ca na sāmānyavataḥ śabda artha tve kiñcid bādhakam asti iti vakṣyāmaḥ tathā atīndriya śakti pratiṣedha arthañca tat tu pṛthivī ādīnām navānām api dravya tva yogaḥ nijā śaktiḥ iti 
[I,043,13_I,043,17]	atha akṛta samayasya gopiṇḍeṣu iva anugata ākāra jñānasya anupapatteḥ na dravya tvam sāmānyam asti iti yathā hi nārikela dvīpa vāsinaḥ gopiṇḍa upalambhāt eka ākāra tā pratibhāsate na evam pṛthivī ādiṣu upalabhyamāneṣu iti atha asti kṛta samayasya dravyam dravyam iti jñānam tat ca saṅketa vaśāt eva bhaviṣyati iti tat asat sāmānyasya niyata vyañjaka vyaṅgya tayā vyañjaka anupalabdhau api anupalabdheḥ abhāvāt tathā hi dravya tvam kriyāvat tva ādi dharma upalambhāt abhivyajyate atiśaya dravya āśrita tva upalabdheḥ guṇa tvam evam karma lakṣaṇa upalabdheḥ karma tvam iti śeṣeṣu api cintyam vyañjakam api ūhyam 
[I,043,21_I,043,24]	na ca sarveṣām vyañjaka upalabdhiḥ vidyate iti sāmānya anupalambhaḥ vighātakaḥ eva kṛta samayasya vyañjaka upalabdheḥ bhavati eva dravya ādiṣu anugata jñānam sāsnādinā vā kṛta samayena api saṃvedyate iti yuktam gavā ādiṣu anugata ākāra vijñānam iti yatra ca dravya guṇa karma ātmakam nimittam na sambhāvyate abādhita anugatāyām saṃvidi tatra sāmānyam eva nimittam na ca dravya ādiṣu anugata saṃvedane abhāvaḥ iva kiñcid bādhakam asti iti tathā hi abhāvaḥ abhāvaḥ iti anugata saṃvedanam dravya guṇa karma animittam api na sāmānyāt bhavati sāmānyasya abhāvena samavāya abhāvāt samavetan ca sāmānyam viśeṣam upalabdham 
[I,044,2]	atha idam eva abhāvatva anuraktam abhāvaḥ abhāvaḥ iti jñānam abhāva tvasya abhāvena samavāyam darśayati iti ced na anekāntāt tathā hi sāmānya ādau sat sat iti jñānam vinā sattā samavāyam iti ukta pūrvam sāmānyavat tve ca abhāvasya bhāva rūpa tā eva syāt evañca anutpatteḥ anādi tvāt nitya tvam vināśasya ca ādima tvāt anitya tvam prasajyeta prāgabhāvasya ca nitya tvena vastu upalambhaḥ na syāt tayoḥ sva rūpa parihāra sthiti virodhāt 
[I,044,7]	na ca abhāva upamarda ātmanaḥ bhāvasya utpattiḥ yuktā iti prāk iti viśeṣaṇā sambhavaḥ pradhvaṃsa anutpattiḥ ca tasya hi utpattimat apekṣita tvāt sambhave api utpattimat tvena vināśasya vināśe bhāva grahaṇam syāt yathā hi vināśānutpatteḥ pūrvam bhāvaḥ gṛhyate tadvat vināśa apāye api gṛhyeta virodha abhāvasya aviśeṣāt na ca etat dṛṣṭam atas sāmānya vat vyatirekaḥ 
[I,044,11]	na ca upādhim vinā abhāvaḥ abhāvaḥ iti jñānam śakyam bhavitum kintarhi ghaṭa abhāvaḥ paṭa abhāvaḥ iti jñāna utpatteḥ vailakṣaṇyam eva atha asti ghaṭābhāvaḥ ghaṭa abhāvaḥ iti anugata jñānam iti ced atrāpi upādhi vaśāt upalakṣaṇa tvam sāmānyam eva jñāna hetuḥ iti draṣṭavyam mukhyam bādhaka upatteḥ na ca evam dravyam dravyam iti jñāne kiñcid bādhakam asti iti sāmānya siddheḥ na asambhavi idam lakṣaṇam iti 
[I,044,16_I,044,19]	evam svaḥ ca asau ātmā ca iti sva ātmā tasmin ārambhaka tvam sva ātma samaveta kārya janaka tvam samavāyikāraṇa tvam iti yāvat tat ca pṛthivī ādiṣu eva bhāva āditarasmāt bhedakam tathā hi kārya samavāyaḥ na ṛte pṛthivī ādibhyaḥ sambhavati iti tathā guṇāḥ vidyante yeṣām te guṇavantaḥ teṣām bhāvaḥ guṇavat tvam guṇa upalakṣitaḥ samavāyaḥ samavetāḥ vā guṇāḥ te api asādhāraṇa tvāt bhedakāḥ yathā na guṇa ādiṣu guṇavat tvam tathā vakṣyāmaḥ guṇa avasare 
[I,044,22_I,044,25]	tathā kārya kāraṇayoḥ avirodhaḥ kārya kāraṇa avirodhaḥ sa vidyate yeṣām te kārya kāraṇā virodhinaḥ teṣām bhāvaḥ kārya kāraṇā virodhi tvam kārya kāraṇayoḥ paraspara avirodhi tvam ekaḥ eva dharmaḥ yadi vā dharma dvayam kārya avirodhi tvam kāraṇa avirodhi tvañcā iti tadā kāryeṇa na virudhyante na vināśyante iti kārya avirodhinaḥ teṣām bhāvaḥ kārya avirodhi tvam kāryeṇa vināśa abhāvaḥ sa ca sarveṣu pṛthivī ādiṣu asti iti sādharmyam na punar lakṣaṇam vipakṣa eka deśe api bhāvāt tathā hi kāryeṇa virudhyante śabda buddhi ādayaḥ na sarve guṇāḥ tathā karmāṇi api kāryeṇa virudhyante na kāryeṇa eva āśraya vināśe api vināśāt 
[I,045,3]	na ca padārtha apekṣayā api lakṣaṇa vivakṣāyām vipakṣa eka deśe vartamānasya gamaka tvam tathā kāraṇa avirodhi tvam yadi kāraṇena na virudhyante iti kāraṇa avirodhinaḥ teṣām bhāvaḥ kāraṇa avirodhi tvam kāraṇena vināśa abhāvaḥ sa ca ākāśa ādiṣu asti kāraṇa abhāvāt iti pakṣe vyāpakasya api sataḥ na vipakṣāt vyāvṛttiḥ iti alakṣaṇa tvam tathā hi na kāraṇena guṇāḥ vināśyante na api karma iti 
[I,045,8]	atha kāraṇam na virundhanti na vināśayanti iti kāraṇa avirodhinaḥ teṣām bhāvaḥ kāraṇa avirodhi tvam kāraṇa avināśaka tvam kārya dharmaḥ iti atra nitya dravyeṣu kāraṇa abhāvāt kāraṇa avirodhi tvam kāraṇa avināśaka tvam cintanīyam iti vipakṣa eka deśe vartamānasya āgamaka tvam eva tathā hi śabda buddhi ādeḥ yadi api kāraṇa vināśaka tvam tathā api na rūpa ādīnām asti iti ativyāptiḥ evam karma api na kāraṇam vināśayati iti 
[I,045,13_I,045,21]	na ca kārya avirodhi tvena aviśeṣaḥ tatra hi kāryeṇa avināśa tvam kāraṇa dharmaḥ kāraṇa avirodhi tvam kāraṇa avināśaka tvam kārya dharmaḥ iti apunaruktam tat evam ubhayathā api vipakṣa eka deśa avyāvṛttaḥ sādharmyam eva na tat lakṣaṇam iti siddham evam antyāḥ viśeṣāḥ vidyante yeṣām te tadvantaḥ teṣām bhāvaḥ antya viśeṣavat tvam antya viśeṣa upalakṣitaḥ samavāyaḥ samavetāḥ vai antya viśeṣāḥ tathā anāśrita tvañca nitya tvañca iti anāśrita tva nitya tve anāśrita tvam āśrita tva abhāvaḥ nitya tvam avināśi tvam ubhaya anta anupalakṣitāḥ vastu sattā vā kim etat dharma trayam sarveṣu pṛthivī ādiṣu asti vyāpakañca iti āha anyatra avaya vi dravyebhyaḥ iti avayavi dravyāṇi varjayitvā nitya dravyeṣu eva iti 
[I,045,23]	nanu dharma trayasya sa apavāda tva aviśeṣe api antya viśeṣavat tvena asamāsa karaṇe kim prayojanam iti antya viśeṣāṇām avyāpaka tve asādhāraṇa tā jñānena eva anāśrita tva niya tvayoḥ ca anyatra api sadbhāvāt sādhāraṇa tvena asamāsa karaṇam tathā hi nitya tvam guṇa ādiṣu api asti iti sādhāraṇam anāśrita tvam samavāyasya api mukhya vṛttau bādhaka upapatteḥ gauṇa vṛtti āśrayaṇena sambhāvyate na paramārthataḥ iti sādhāraṇam 
[I,046,4_I,046,10]	evam pṛthivī ādīnām navānām padārtha antarāt vyāvṛtam sādharmyam abhidhāya punar teṣām sva bhedāt vyāvṛttam sādharmyam darśayati pṛthivī udaka jvalana pavana ātma manasām iti ca arthe dvandvaḥ samāsaḥ aneka tvañca apara jātimat tvañcā iti aneka tva apara jātimat tve aneka tvañca kṣiti ādeḥ viśeṣa lakṣaṇa yoginaḥ vyakti bhedaḥ aneka tva saṃkhyā vā na ākāśa ādeḥ vyakti bhedaḥ na aneka tva saṃkhyā vā sambhavati iti tasmāt vyāvṛttiḥ iti aneka tvāt eva apara jātimat tvam apara jātiḥ dravya tva apekṣayā pṛthivī tva ādi rūpā sā vidyate yeṣām tāni tadvanti teṣām bhāvaḥ apara jātimat tvam apara jāti upalakṣitaḥ samavāyaḥ samavetā vā apara jātiḥ iti 
[I,046,14_I,046,15]	evam kṣiti jala jyotiḥ anila manasām sādharmyam kriyāvat tvan ca mūrta tvañca paratvañca aparatvañca vegavat tvañca iti tathā uktāni tathā ca kriyā calana rūpā sā vidyate yeṣām tāni tadvanti teṣām bhāvaḥ kriyāvat tvam samavetā kriyā tad samavāyaḥ vā tathā mūrtiḥ avyāpi dravya parimāṇam sā vidyate yeṣām tāni mūrtāni teṣām bhāvaḥ mūrta tvam samavetā mūrtiḥ tad samavāyaḥ vā mūrta tvāt eva ca paratva aparatva ādi sadbhāvaḥ kriyāvat tvañca iti parāparāṇām bhāvaḥ paratva aparatve yat sadbhāve kṣiti ādiṣu parāpara vyavahāraḥ iti samavetau paratva aparatva guṇau tad samavāyaḥ vā vegaḥ vidyate yeṣām tāni vegavanti teṣām bhāvaḥ vegavat tvam samavetaḥ vega guṇaḥ tad samavāyaḥ vā etāni ca kṣiti ādiṣu eva iti niyamyante na tu sarvadā teṣu bhavanti iti 
[I,046,25_I,046,27]	evam ākāśa kāla diś ātmanām sarva gata tva ādi sādharmyam sarva śabdaḥ ca anantara ukta mūrteṣu eva vartate sarveṣu gatāḥ sarva gatāḥ sarva prāptāḥ teṣām bhāvaḥ sarva gata tvam sarva mūrtaiḥ saṃyogaḥ sa ca anyatara karma jaḥ saṃyoga jaḥ vā sa tu ubhaya niṣṭhatva aviśeṣe api ākāśa ādeḥ eva sādharmyam tasya hi sarva mūrtaiḥ saha saṃyogaḥ na mūrtānām anyatamasya iti 
[I,047,3_I,047,7]	tathā parama mahatām bhāvaḥ parama mahat tvam niratiśaya parimāṇam tad samavāyaḥ vā tathā sarva saṃyogi samāna deśa tvam sarvāṇi ca tāni saṃyogīni ca mūrta dravyāṇi taiḥ samānāḥ saṃyogāḥ teṣām ākāśa ādayaḥ deśāḥ ādhārāḥ teṣām bhāvaḥ sarva saṃyogi samāna deśa tvam sarva saṃyogi saṃyoga ādhāra tvam na ca saṃyogasya ubhaya niṣṭhatvāt mūrtānām api eṣa dharmaḥ iti vācyam yathā hi ekam ākāśam sarva mūrta saṃyoga ādhāraḥ na evam ekam mūrtam iti arthāt viśeṣaḥ labhyate na ca sarva gata tvena aviśeṣaḥ sarva gata tvam hi sarva saṃyogaḥ tad upalakṣitaḥ vā samavāyaḥ sarva saṃyogi saṃyoga ādhāra tvam iti 
[I,047,11_I,047,16]	yat vā sarve ca te saṃyogaḥ vidyate yeṣām te saṃyoginaḥ te ca sarva saṃyoginaḥ ghaṭa ādayaḥ śarāva ādayaḥ ca teṣām samānāḥ saṃyogāḥ iti śeṣam pūrvavat anye tu upacāreṇa eva vyutpattyā vā saṃyogi śabdena saṃyogaḥ eva ucyate iti manyante saṃyujyante iti saṃyogāḥ te vidyante yeṣām te saṃyoginaḥ saṃyogāḥ eva sthānāt upacāraḥ vā iti sarva saṃyoginā antu samānāḥ ca te deśāḥ ca iti ekatve satya ādhāraḥ iti atra ca eka tve satī iti viśeṣaṇam śabda vṛttyā labhyate iti sāmarthya aśravaṇam apāstam bhavati tat ca asat indriya sāmānya lakṣaṇe viśeṣa guṇa lakṣaṇa ādau ca tasya eva samāśrayaṇāt iha prayāsa mātram eva iti 
[I,047,19_I,047,25]	tathā pṛthivī ādīnām sādharmyam āha pṛthivī ādīnām pṛthivī ādiḥ yeṣām tāni pṛthivī ādīni teṣām na jñāyate kiyatām atas pañcānām api sādharmyam bhūta tvañcaḥ indriya prakṛti tvañca bāhya ekaika indriya grāhya viśeṣa guṇavat tvañca iti tathā uktāni bhūtānām bhāvaḥ bhūta tvam tat ca sāmānyam eva tathā hi dravya guṇa karmaṇi nimitte ca abādhyamānam anugata jñānam sāmānyāt bhavat dṛṣṭam yathā gauḥ ityādi jñānam asti ca bhūtam tam ityādi kṣiti ādiṣu jñānam atas samā anyāt bhavati iti na ca asya sāmānya ādau anumata jñānasya iva kiñcid bādhakam asti tathā ca sāmānye sāmānya kalpanāyām anavasthā syāt iti sāmānyam dravya tvam sāmānyam guṇa tvam iti jñānam sāmānyam vinā bhavati iti uktam na ca tat bhūtam bhūtam iti jñāne bādhakam asti 
[I,048,4]	atha nārikela dvīpa vāsinām kasmāt eka ākāra tā pratibhāsaḥ na bhavati iti vyañjaka anupalabdheḥ yathā hi guṇa tva ādi sāmānyam nārikela dvīpa vāsinām vyañjaka anupalambhāt vidyamānam api na upalabhyate tathā bhūta tvam api iti kim asya tarhi vyañjakam iti brāhmaṇa tvasya iva upadeśaḥ yathā hi brāhmaṇa tvam upadeśāt vijñāyate tadvat bhūta tvam api iti 
[I,048,8_I,048,11]	atha upadeśaḥ eva astu alam sāmānya kalpanayā yathā anyaiḥ uktam bhūta tvam bhūta śabdasya vācya tvam iti abhidhāna abhidheya niyama niyoga pratipattiḥ sā ca śabdāt vṛddha vyavahārāt vā anvaya vyatirekābhyām bhavati iti etat ca asat abādhyamāna anugata jñānasya nimitta antara kalpanāyām dravya tva ādeḥ api asattvam syāt asti ca kṛta samayasya bhūtam bhūtam iti jñānam brāhmaṇaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ iti vat dravyam dravyam iti jñāna vat ca tatas asti bhūta tvam sāmānyam iti 
[I,048,14_I,048,16]	atha yathā dravyeṣu asādhāraṇaḥ samavāyi kāraṇa tva ādiḥ vyāpakaḥ dharmaḥ kṛta samayasya dravya tva abhivyañjakaḥ asti na evam bhūteṣu iti ced na indriya prakṛti tva ādeḥ asādhāraṇa tvāt atha tad upalambhe api akṛta samayasya na anugatam jñānam iti ced dravya tva ādiṣu api samānam tatra api samavāyi kāraṇa tva ādeḥ upalambhe api akṛta samayasya dravyam dravyam iti jñānam na dṛṣṭam iti 
[I,048,19_I,049,1]	atha kṛta samayasya utpatteḥ asti dravyat tva ādi sāmānyam tat ca bhūta tve api samānam iti alam tathā indriya prakṛtīnām bhāvaḥ indriya prakṛti tvam ghrāṇa rasana cakṣuḥ tvac śrotra kāraṇa tvam yathāsaṃkhyam tat ca vakṣyāmaḥ pṛthivī adhikāre bhūyas tvāt gandhavat tvāt ityādi sūtraiḥ iti śrotre tu karṇa śaṣkulī ākāśa saṃyoga upalakṣitasya ākāśasya kārya tvāt tad apekṣayā ākāśasya kāraṇa tvāt svabhāva arthaḥ vā prakṛti śabdaḥ iti 
[I,049,3]	nanu āhaṅkārika tvāt indriyāṇām ayuktam etat tathā ca prakāśaka tvam sattva dharmaḥ iti sāttvikāt ahaṅkārāt indriyāṇām udayaḥ kim atra pramāṇam iti ced aprāpya kāri tvam tat ca śākhā candramasoḥ yugapad grahaṇāt vijñātam anyathā hi śākhā sambandha uttara kālam cireṇa candramasā ca sambandhāt yugapad grahaṇam na syāt asti ca atas aprāpya kāri tvam tat ca bhautikeṣu na sambhavati pradīpa ādiṣu adarśana āditya bhautika tvam anyeṣām api pratipattavyam cakṣuḥ dṛṣṭānta balāt eva 
[I,049,9]	tathā mahat aṇu prakāśaka tvāt ca yat hi yāvat parimāṇam tāvat eva kriyām kurvat dṛṣṭam iti tathā hi alpa parimāṇam vā asya ādi mahāntam vaṭa vṛkṣam vyāpya cchidām na karoti iti dṛṣṭam kim tarhi sva vyāpta pradeśaḥ eva iti cakṣuḥ api alpa parimāṇa tvāt na parvata ādi paricchedakam syāt tat tu dṛṣṭam atas na bhautikam iti 
[I,049,13_I,049,16]	tathā niyata viṣaya tvāt ca yadi hi cakṣuḥ taijasam syāt rūpasya eva tad guṇa tvāt grāhakam na dravya sāmānya ādeḥ iti evam śeṣeṣu api niyamena sva guṇa grāhaka tva prasaṅgaḥ na ca etat dṛṣṭam atas na bhautikam iti itas ca na bhautikāni indriyāṇi indriya tvāt yat yat indriyam tat tat abhautikam dṛṣṭam yathā manaḥ tathā ca indriyāṇi tasmāt na bhautikāni iti 
[I,049,18]	yat tāvat aprāpya kāri tvāt iti sādhanam tat asiddham vyavahita artha anupalabdhyā prāpteḥ upalambhāt anyathā hi vyavahitasya agrahaṇam antike ca grahaṇam na syāt aprāpteḥ ubhayatra aviśeṣāt āvaraṇa anupapattiḥ ca prāpti pratiṣedhaka tvāt tathā ca prāpti pratiṣedham kurvat āvaraṇam agrahaṇāya kalpyate dṛṣṭañca āvaraṇa sāmarthyam dūre vā prakāśaka tvam atas pradīpasya iva prāpta artha paricchedaka tvam tathā ca cakṣuḥ prāpta artha paricchedakam vyavahita aprakāśaka tvāt yat yat vyavahita aprakāśakam tat tat prāptau artha paricchedakam yathā pradīpaḥ tathā vyavahita aprakāśakam cakṣuḥ tasmāt prāpta artha paricchedakam iti 
[I,049,25_I,050,1]	prāpti sadbhāve pramāṇa upapatteḥ śākhā candramasoḥ kāla bhedena grahaṇa sadbhāve api āśu bhāvāt utpala patra śata vyatibheda abhimāna vat yugapad grahaṇa abhimānaḥ yat ca mahat anuprakāśaka tvam tat api anyathā siddha tvāt asādhanam tathā hi cakṣuḥ bahis gatam bāhya āloka sambandhāt viṣaya parimāṇam utpadyate iti mahat ādi artha prakāśakam nābhautika tvāt iti 
[I,050,4_I,050,9]	yat ca uktam taijasa tvāt rūpasya eva prakāśakam syāt iti etat asat pradīpe darśanāt na hi pradīpaḥ taijasa tvāt rūpasya eva prakāśakaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ kim tarhi rūpa dravya sāmānya ādeḥ iti etāvān eva viśeṣaḥ cakṣuṣaḥ atas taijasa tvam na virudhyate iti rūpa ādiṣu madhye niyamena rūpasya eva prakāśaka tvam taijasa tve anumānam iti vakṣyāmaḥ niyamena gandha ādi prakāśaka tvañca pārthiva tva ādiṣu ghrāṇa ādeḥ iti na ca eka prakṛtika tve viṣaya vyavasthā upalabdha iti nānā prakṛtika tvam tathā hi ekasmāt kāraṇāt upajātāḥ pradīpa bhedāḥ samāna viṣayāḥ iti upalabdham tadvat indriyeṣu api samāna viṣaya tvam syāt dṛṣṭā tu ghrāṇa ādeḥ gandha ādiṣu vyavasthā iti nānā prakṛtika tvam 
[I,050,12]	tathā nānā jāti upādānāni indriyāṇi dravya tve sati pratiniyata viṣaya tvāt yat yat dravya tve sati pratiniyata viṣayam tat tat nānā jāti upādānam dṛṣṭam yathā vyaṃjana anila pradīpa kastūrikā ādīni iti tathā ca etāni dravya tve sati pratiniyata viṣayāṇi tasmāt nānā jāti upādānāni iti tathā hi jñāna śabdeṣu eka jāti upādāna tvam pratiniyata viṣaya tvañca iti vyabhicāraḥ tad artham dravya tve sati iti viśeṣaṇam na ca asya pakṣa dharma tva ādimataḥ aprāmāṇyam ati prasaṅgāt 
[I,050,18_I,050,21]	yat ca abhautika tve anumānam indriya tvāt iti tatra bhūtāt anivṛttam abhautikam tat pratiṣedhe ca kāraṇa antara prabhava tvam viśeṣa pratiṣedhasya śeṣa abhyanujñā viṣaya tvāt iti sādhya vikalaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ tathā ca manasi na bhautika tvam na api abhautika tvam iti atha bhūtāt utpatti pratiṣedhena nitya tvam atra api abhyupagama vyāghātaḥ manasi api nitya tva abhyupagamāt indriya tvañca ukta viśeṣaṇasya aparokṣa jñāna janaka tvena bhūtāt utpatti pratiṣedhena iti anyathā siddham 
[I,050,24_I,051,4]	nirmūlañcaḥ indriyāṇām ahaṅkāra prabhava tvam tad sadbhāve pramāṇa asambhavāt tathā hi pradhāna sadbhāve sati eṣā prakriyā tasya ca asattvam vakṣyamāṇam iti yeṣāñca āsaṃsāra maṇḍala vyāpīni indriyāṇi teṣām aśeṣa viṣaya grahaṇa prasaṅgaḥ atha adṛṣṭa vaśāt niyata deśe vṛtti vyajyate iti ced atra pravṛttīnām tādātmye na kiñcid uktam syāt vyatireke tu tat eva indriyam iti saṃjñā bheda mātram eva atha niyata viṣaya avabodhāni atha anupapattyā tad ākāra tayā eva indriyasya pariṇāmaḥ niścīyate tat na anyathā api upalambhāt tathā hi niyata artha sannikarṣe api upalambhaḥ ghaṭataḥ eva na ca vyāpi tvam parasya abhīpsitataram iti na iha pratanyate pariṇāma pakṣaḥ ca na sambhavati iti vakṣyāmaḥ iti alam 
[I,051,8]	tathā bāhyena ekaika indriyeṇa gṛhyante iti bāhya ekaika indriya grāhyāḥ te ca te viśeṣa guṇāḥ ca iti te vidyante yeṣām tāni tadvanti teṣām bhāvaḥ bāhya ekaika indriya grāhya viśeṣa guṇavat tvam samavetāḥ hi yathā uktāḥ guṇāḥ tad upalakṣitaḥ vā samavāyaḥ guṇavat tvam sarveṣu asti iti viśeṣa grahaṇam viśeṣa guṇavat tvam sva ātmani asti iti bāhya indriya grāhya grahaṇam indriya grāhyāḥ ca saṃkhyā ādayaḥ api bhavanti na ca viśeṣa guṇāḥ tathā hi ekaika grahaṇam anarthakam bāhya indriya grāhya viśeṣa guṇavat tvasya anyatra abhāvāt satyam tathā api dvitīyam sādharmyam iti adoṣaḥ tathā hi saṃkhyā ādeḥ dvi indriya grāhya tvāt eka indriya grāhya grahaṇam eka indriya grāhya tvañca rūpa ādiṣu asambhavi syāt na hi ekam indriyam sarveṣām prakāśakam iti ekaika grahaṇam tathā api antaḥkaraṇasya bāhya indriya ādi adhiṣṭhāna dvāreṇa vyāpārā sambhavi tvam eva iti bāhya grahaṇam evañca bāhya ekaika indriya grāhya guṇavat tvam viśeṣa pada tyāgena dvitīyam sādharmyam iti 
[I,051,19_I,051,22]	tathā caturṇām dravya ārambhaka tvam sparśavat tvañca iti dravya ārambhaka tva sparśavat tve tat na jñāyate keṣām iti viśeṣa anabhidhānāt pṛthivī ādīnām iti anuvartanīyam anantara tvāt iti kim punar dravya ārambhakāṇām bhāvaḥ dravya ārambhaka tvam dravya utpattau samavāyi kāraṇa tvam kārya dravyasya samavāyaḥ tena hi satā dravyam dravya utpattau samavāyi kāraṇam iti vyavahārāt tathā hi dravya ārambhakāṇām bhāvaḥ dravya ārambhaka tvam yena satā dravyam utpādayanti iti na vivakṣitam kim tarhi yena satā dravyam ārabhante iti dravya utpattau samavāyi kāraṇāni iti vyavahāraḥ sa ca dravya samavāyena satā bhavati iti dravya ārambhaka tvam dravya samavāyaḥ eva 
[I,052,1_I,052,4]	atha yena satā sva samaveta dravya ārabhante iti vivakṣā tat yadi sparśavatām eva dravya ārambhaka tva darśanāt sparśaḥ eva tathā api sparśavat tvena gata artha tvāt vyartham syāt dravya ārambhaka tvam atra eke sahakāri viśeṣa upacita sparśe dravya ārambhaka tvam sparśavatām bhāvaḥ sparśavat tvam sparśa upalakṣitaḥ samavāyaḥ iti parihāram bruvate

[I,052,12]	anye tu artha tayā bhāvāt dvi indriya vivakṣayā pratyakṣa tvam atra vivakṣitam tat ca ātma ādiṣu na asti iti vyāvṛttam sādharmyam iti manyante nirvikalpaka sa vikalpaka jñāna viṣaya tvañca na vyāvṛttam ātmani api bhāvāt tathā ca aham iti śabdaḥ pṛthivī ādi śabda vyatirekāt ātmani vartate iti upalabdha samayasya tad smaraṇād bhavati eva sa vikalpaka jñānam iti

[I,053,4_I,053,5]	evam bhūtāni ca ātmānaḥ ca iti tathā uktāḥ teṣām vaiśeṣika guṇavat tvam sādharmyam viśeṣāḥ eva vaiśeṣikāḥ te vidyante yeṣām guṇānām te vaiśeṣika guṇavantaḥ teṣām bhāvaḥ tattvam tad upalakṣitaḥ samavāyaḥ te vā samavetāḥ 
[I,053,9_I,053,10]	evam kṣitiḥ ca uda kañca ātmānaḥ ca iti tathā uktāḥ teṣām sādharmyam caturdaśa guṇavat tvam tathā hi caturdaśa guṇāḥ vidyante yeṣām te tadvantaḥ teṣām bhāvaḥ tattvam samavetāḥ te tad samavāyaḥ vā atra ca anya guṇānām anyatra āvṛtteḥ saṃkhyā mātram sādharmyam vivakṣitam iti jñeyam 
[I,053,15_I,053,16]	ākāśaḥ ca ātmānaḥ ca iti tathā uktāḥ teṣām sādharmyam kṣaṇika eka deśa vṛtti viśeṣa guṇavat tvam kṣaṇikāḥ ca te eka deśa vṛttayaḥ ca iti tathā uktāḥ te ca te viśeṣa guṇāḥ ca iti te vidyante yeṣām te tat vantaḥ teṣām bhāvaḥ tattvam tad samavāyaḥ te vā samavetāḥ guṇavat tvam sarveṣu asti iti viśeṣa grahaṇam tat kṣiti ādiṣu api samānam iti eka deśa vṛtti padam 
[I,053,20]	tathā api kṣaṇika grahaṇam anarthakam eka deśa vṛtti viśeṣa guṇavat tvasya anyatra abhāvāt tat na dvitīya sādharmyasya vivakṣita tvāt tathā hi viśeṣa guṇavat tvam anyatra api asti iti kṣaṇika grahaṇam kṣaṇika tvañca āśraye vidyamāne sati āśutara vināśi tvam kṣaṇika guṇavat tvan ca vibhāga apekṣayā anyatra api asti iti viśeṣa grahaṇam kṣaṇika viśeṣa guṇavat tvañca anyatra abhāvāt vyāvṛttam sādharmyam iti 
[I,054,1_I,054,5]	tathā diś kālayoḥ pañca guṇavat tvam viśeṣāt sādharmyam pañcaguṇāḥ vidyante yayoḥ tau pañca guṇavantau tayoḥ bhāvaḥ pañca guṇavat tvam pañca guṇa upalakṣitaḥ samavāyaḥ te vā samavetāḥ etat ca saṃkhyā mātra sāmyena sādharmyam tathā ca sarve ca te utpattiḥ vidyate yeṣām te utpattimantaḥ ca iti tathā uktāḥ teṣām utpattau nimitta kāraṇa tvam iti nimitta padasya kāraṇa paryāyasya api abhidhānam samavāyi asamavāyi vyavaccheda artham anyathā hi samavāyi asamavāyi sādhāraṇa tvāt tad apekṣayā asambhavi tvam eva syāt 
[I,054,9_I,054,20]	tathā hi nimitta kāraṇasya bhāvaḥ nimitta kāraṇa tvam yena satā nimitta kāraṇam iti vyavahāraḥ sa ca kāraṇayoḥ satoḥ samavāyi asamavāyi lakṣaṇa abhāvaḥ tena satā tathā vyavahārāt yadi api sva gata saṃkhyā ādi utpattau asti samavāyikāraṇa tvam tathā api sarveṣām eva iti viśeṣaṇāt adoṣaḥ evam kṣitiḥ ca tejaḥ ca iti kṣiti tejasī tayoḥ naimittika drava tva yogaḥ sādharmyam nimittāt upajātam naimittikam iti nimitta śabdaḥ sāmānya śabdaḥ api arthāt agni saṃyoge vartate naimitti kañca tat drava t vañca iti etena yogaḥ samavāyaḥ sādharmyam iti idānīm upasaṃhāra vyājena śiṣyam śikṣayati yat etat vyākhyātam mayā sādharmyam tat eva sarvatra viparyayāt vyāvṛttam bheda antarāt vaidharmyam vācyam iti yat vā sādharmyam vyākhyātam iti upasaṃhāraḥ viparyayāt vaidharmyam vakṣyamāṇam iti anāgata artha sūcanam iti 
[I,055,1_I,055,3]	pṛthivī ādīnām navānām punar pañcānām ityādi rūpeṇa sādharmyam abhidhāya pratyekam teṣām vaidharmyam āha iha ityādinā iha iti kṣiti ādi manaḥ paryanteṣu prakaraṇeṣu idānīm sāmpratam ekaikaśas vaidharmyam ucyate iti nanu eka ekaśas iti vīpsāyām śaspratyayasya vidhānāt vyartham vīpsā abhidhānam 
[I,055,7_I,055,11]	ekaikaśas vinighnanti viṣayāḥ viṣa sannibhāḥ iti vyāsa prayogāt adoṣaḥ iti eke pratyekam kṣiti ādeḥ vīpsāyām vaidharmya lābhe punar vīpsā karaṇam avāntara bhedena śarīra ādīnām vaidharmya jñāpana artham iti guravaḥ vadanti vaidharmyantu viśiṣṭaḥ itarasmāt vyāvṛttaḥ dharmaḥ yasya asau vidharmā tasya bhāvaḥ vaidharmyam asādhāraṇaḥ tattva vyavasthāpakaḥ dharmaḥ kevala vyatireki anumānam iti yāvat 
[I,055,14_I,055,19]	tatra ādau uddiṣṭa tvāt pṛthivyāḥ tat ucyate pṛthivī tva abhisambandhāt iti pṛthivī iti lakṣya nirdeśaḥ pṛthivī tva abhisambandhāt iti lakṣaṇam asādhāraṇaḥ dharmaḥ pṛthivī tvena abhisambandhaḥ pṛthivī tvena upalakṣitaḥ samavāyaḥ iti pṛthivī dharmiṇī itarebhyaḥ bhidyate iti sādhyaḥ dharmaḥ pṛthivī tva abhisambandhāt yaḥ tu itarasmāt na bhidyate na ca asau pṛthivī tvena sambaddhaḥ yathā udaka ādi na ca tathā pṛthivī tvena nābhisambaddhā pṛthivī tasmāt itarebhyaḥ bhidyate iti samavāyaḥ hi ati vyāpaka tvāt alakṣaṇaḥ syāt iti pṛthivī tvam viśeṣaṇam 
[I,056,5_I,056,8]	nanu evam pṛthivī tvam eva asādhāraṇa tvāt vyavaccheda samartham iti asamartha viśeṣaṇatā hetoḥ doṣaḥ na pakṣe asambhavi tvā śaṅkā parihāra artha tvāt tathā hi pṛthivī tvāt pṛthivī iti ukte pakṣe asti na asti iti āśaṅkā na nivarteta atas samartham abhisambandha padam nanu bhāva pratyayāt eva sambandha adhigateḥ ṣaṣṭhyā vā pṛthivyāḥ bhāvaḥ pṛthivī tvam iti sva śabdena tasya abhidhānam vyartham tat na bhāva pratyayaḥ śabda vṛttyā bhāvam abhidhatte nābhi sambandham na ca gamyām vṛttim āśritya sambandha padasya vaiyarthyam śāstre tathā abhāve ati prasaṅgāt ṣaṣṭhī ca aniyata sambandha abhidhāyikā iti viśiṣṭa sambandha lābhāya abhisambandha padam 
[I,056,12]	nanu ca evam upādhi bhedāt avāstavaḥ bhedaḥ samavāyasya iti avārakam lakṣaṇam katham itarebhyaḥ bheda jñāpakam iti syāt na kalpita bhedasya api artha kriyā karaṇāt yathā śrotrasya tathā hi śrotram karṇa śaṣkulī ākāśa saṃyoga upalakṣitaḥ nabhaḥ deśaḥ sa ca āvāstava bhedaḥ api śabda upalabdhi lakṣaṇām artha kriyām vidadhāti tadvat samavāye api adoṣaḥ samavetam vā pṛthivī tvam lakṣaṇam pṛthivī tvañca tat abhisambadhyate iti abhisambandhaḥ ca iti karma dhāraya parigrahāt 
[I,056,17_I,056,20]	nanu ubhaya pada vyabhicāra abhāvāt viśeṣaṇa samāsaḥ katham tathā sati abhisambadhyate iti abhisambandhaḥ samavetam rūpa ādi dṛṣṭam iti arthavat pṛthivī tvam pṛthivī tvañca iti ukte na asamavetam pṛthivī tvam sambhavati iti vyabhicāra abhāvaḥ atha apṛthivī vyāvṛtti rūpam pṛthivī tvam asamavetam tad nirāsāya arthavat abhisambandha padam na tasya asiddha tvāt pramāṇena hi prasiddhasya viśeṣaṇena vyudāsaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ yathā nīlena ānīla ādeḥ na vai apohaḥ siddhaḥ vṛtti vikalpa anupapatteḥ bādhakasya apramāṇa tayā vāstava sāmānya sadbhāvāt eka pada avyabhicāre api karma dhāraya samāsa abhyupagamāda doṣaḥ iti 
[I,056,24_I,057,1]	kecid abhigrahaṇam abhi samantāt sambandhaḥ iti pakṣe vyāpti artham ābhimukhyena ca sambandhaḥ iti kevala vyatireka avyabhicāreṇa gamaka tva pradarśana artham nanu kim itarasmāt vyāvṛttā pramāṇa siddhā pṛthivī pakṣīkriyate atha aprasiddhā iti yadi aprasiddhā pakṣīkaraṇam ayuktam atha pramāṇa prasiddhā vyāvṛtta tayā tarhi lakṣaṇa vaiyarthyam atha avyāvṛtta tayā upalabdhā tat asat vyāvṛttam hi padārthānām svarūpam tena ca vapuṣā gṛhyamāṇāḥ dharmiṇaḥ na rūpa antareṇa iti dṛṣṭam na etat evam loka prasiddhi vaśena pṛthivyāḥ pakṣīkaraṇāt tathā hi yatra janānām pṛthivī iti vyavahāraḥ sā pakṣīkṛta iti abādhaḥ 
[I,057,7]	nanu itaretara āśraya tvam pṛthivī itarebhyaḥ bhidyate iti atra itarebhyaḥ bhedaḥ sādhyaḥ teṣān tu pṛthivī itas bhedena pratipattau avadhibhāvaḥ ghaṭataḥ iti eka apratipattau itara apratipatteḥ ubhaya abhāva prasaṅgaḥ tat na asādhāraṇa dharma upalambha sahakāriṇa indriyeṇa vyāvṛtta rūpa tayā nirvikalpaka jñāne pṛthivī pratibhāsate tathā ap ādayaḥ api asādhāraṇa dharma upalambha vyāvṛttyā naḥ parasparam cakṣuḥ vyāpārāt eva prathante svayam pratipanne api bhede para pratipādanāya anumāna upanyāsaḥ tathā hi vipratipadyamānaḥ paraḥ para artha anumānena eva pratipādyate iti 
[I,057,13_I,057,17]	atha itarebhyaḥ bhede sādhye abādayaḥ api itarebhyaḥ bhidyante iti vidyamāne sa pakṣe katham kevala vyatireka avyabhicāraḥ na sādhya aparijñānāt tathā hi pṛthivī itarebhyaḥ bhidyate iti pṛthivī itarebhyaḥ niravaśeṣebhyaḥ bhidyate iti sādhya arthaḥ tathā ca sa pakṣa abhāvaḥ na hi udaka ādayaḥ sva ātmabhyaḥ bhedinaḥ iti atha pṛthivī tvam yadi asā dhāraṇa dharmāt bhidyate tatas api anyasmāt bhidyate iti anavasthā abhede tu sādhya sādhana bhāva anupapattiḥ atas svatas bhidyate kṣiteḥ api tathā abhāvena bādhāt 
[I,057,19]	atha pṛthivī tvam pṛthivyāḥ viśeṣyate pṛthivī ca pṛthivī tvena iti itaretara āśraya tvam na etat evam pṛthivyām anuvartamāna vapuṣaḥ bheda antarāt vyāvṛttasya indriya vyāpārāt nirvikalpaka jñāne pratibhāsanāt tathā hi anugata svabhāvasya apīta rasmāt vyāvṛttam svarūpam sāmānyasya tat ca pratyakṣeṇa svayam pratītam api para pratipādanāya hetu tvena abhidhīyate iti anavasthā ādi a bhāvaḥ na ca sarvathā vipratipadyamānaḥ pratipādyaḥ syāt iti dharmi jñānam sāmānyena sādhana jñānañca abhyupeyam kevalam itarebhyaḥ bhinnā pṛthivī na pratipadyate iti sādhana upanyāsaḥ 
[I,057,25]	tathā ekam vākyam āvartyamānam bhūyāṃsam artham āha iti śabda artha nirūpaṇa paratvena abhisambadhyate pṛthivī tva abhisambandhāt iti vākyam tathā ca sāmānyam śabda arthaḥ tasya ekatayā saṅketa kāraṇāt iti jaiminīyāḥ viśeṣāḥ tu aniyata diś deśa sambandhi tayā na kārtsnyena upalabdhi bhājaḥ bhavanti iti katham saṅketa viṣayāḥ 
[I,058,3]	atha yāvatām upalambhaḥ tāvatsu eva saṅketakaraṇāt vyavahāraḥ tarhi viśeṣa antare saṃketā sambhavāt vyavahāra anupapattiḥ na ca ayoginaḥ pratyekam aśeṣa viśeṣa upalambhaḥ na ca anupalabdheṣu idam asya vācyam idam asya vācakam iti abhidhāna abhidheya niyama niyoga pratipattiḥ samaya pratipattiñca vinā śabda śravaṇāt artha pratibhāsā bhāvaḥ atha abhinna nimittam upādāya viśeṣeṣu saṅketaḥ tat api asat abhinna nimitta sadbhāve api viśeṣāṇām ānantvam na ativartate iti sāmānye saṅketāt sāmānyam śabda arthaḥ 
[I,058,9_I,058,9]	na ca sāmānyavati saṅketa upalambhena sāmānyam abhidhāya anantaram viśeṣeṣu vartiṣyate iti vācyam viramya vyāpāra abhyupagamena śabda karma buddhi ādīnām viramya vyāpāra asambhavāt iti sūtra virodhāt tathā ca viśeṣaṇa pratipattau eva kṣīṇa tvāt viśeṣya apratipādakam tat uktam viśeṣyam na abhidhā gacchet kṣīṇa śaktiḥ viśeṣaṇe atha sāmānya pratipatteḥ apuruṣa artha tvāt viśeṣa artha tayā pratipattuḥ pravṛtti nivṛttī na syātām iti tat na sāmānya pratipatti anyathā anupapattyā viśeṣa avabodhe sati pravṛtti nivṛttyoḥ bhāvāt tathā hi nirādhāram hi sāmānyam bhavet śaśa viṣāṇa vat iti ādhāra pratipattiḥ iti alam ati kalpitena 
[I,058,19]	sarvam etat ayuktam abhinna nimitta upādāne sati sāmānyavati saṅketa kāraṇāt sāmānyavān śabda arthaḥ tat yathā ānantyena avasthitāḥ viśeṣāḥ tathā hi ekam teṣu abhinnam sāmānyam ekatra upalabdham tad upalambhāt anupalabhyamānāḥ api viśeṣāḥ sāmānyavantaḥ saṅketa viṣayāḥ śabdāḥ ca anitya tve api viśiṣṭa ānupūrvī sacivāḥ iti tathā hi yatra yatra īdṛśam sāmānyam paśyasi tatra tatra ayam śabdaḥ prayoktavyaḥ ittham bhūtāt ca śabdāt ayam arthaḥ pratipattavyaḥ iti saṅketa grahaḥ viśeṣāṇām ānantye api ghaṭataḥ iti tathā ca śabda śravaṇāt sāmānyavati arthe pratipattiḥ dṛṣṭā sā ca saṅketa pratipattim ākṣipati saṅketaḥ ca anena eva prakāreṇa ghaṭate na anyathā iti 
[I,059,1]	atha go śabda śravaṇāt śāvaleya ādi viśeṣa apratipatteḥ na viśeṣaḥ śabda arthaḥ satyam kim tarhi sāmānya yuktaḥ arthaḥ pratīyate na śāvaleya ādi viśeṣaḥ sa ca śāvaleya ādi śabdebhyaḥ eva pratīyate iti na ca etāvatā sāmānyam eva śabda arthaḥ pradhāna upasarjana bhāvena ubhayoḥ pratibhāsanāt tathā gāmānaya ityādi prayogeṣu sāmānyavataḥ arthasya ānayana ādi kṛtyā sambandhāt 
[I,059,6]	atha sāmānyam abhidhāya katham viśeṣe vartate sūtra virodhāt na sūtra artha aparijñānāt tathā ca sūtrasya arthaḥ śabdaḥ hi ekadā viśeṣaṇam pratipādya punar viśeṣaṇam na pratipādayati iti viramya vyāpāraḥ niṣiddhaḥ na punar viśeṣaṇam pratipādya viśeṣyam na abhidhattaḥ iti tathā karma vibhāgam kṛtvā uttara saṃyogam karoti akṛta saṃyogasya vināśa abhāvāt na ca vibhāgam kṛtvā saṃyogam karoti iti viramya vyāpāra pratiṣedhaḥ tathā viśeṣaṇa buddhiḥ viśeṣya buddhim kṛtvā na kārya antaram ārabhate iti evam sukha ādiṣu api pratiṣedhaḥ 
[I,059,12]	nanu uktam kṣīṇa śaktiḥ viśeṣaṇe iti viśeṣyam na abhidadhyāt iti tāvat śakteḥ kārya viṣaya tvāt kāryañca viśeṣaṇa pratipatti vat viśeṣya pratipatti lakṣaṇam upalabhyamānam śakteḥ vyavasthāpakam atha kāryasya eva abhāvam brūyāt sa ca evam bruvāṇaḥ sva saṃvedanam api bādhate viśeṣya pratipatteḥ saṃvedanāt bhinna jñāna ālambanayoḥ ca viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāva pakṣe codyam na eka jñāna ālambane iti samānañca etat upalabhyamānasya śabdasya artha pratipādaka tva abhyupagamāt sva ātma pratipattau ca kṣīṇa tvāt sāmānya pratipādaka tvam na syāt atha sāmānya pratipatteḥ dṛṣṭa tvāt na tatra śabda śakteḥ prakṣayaḥ tarhi viśeṣa pratipatteḥ api dṛṣṭa tvāt na śakti prakṣayaḥ artha pratipādana arthaḥ ca śabda prayogaḥ iti 
[I,059,20]	yat ca uktam śabda sāmānya pratipatti anyathā anupapattyā viśeṣa adhyavasāye pravṛtti nivṛttī syātām iti tatra kim sāmānya mātra pratipatti anyathā anupapattyā viśeṣa avabodhaḥ tad viśeṣa pratipatti anyathā anupapattyā vā yadi sāmānya mātra pratipatti anyathā anupapattyā tathā sati sāmānya mātra pratipattau viśeṣa mātra pratipattiḥ iti pravṛtti abhāvaḥ atha viśiṣṭa sāmānya pratipatti anyathā anupapattyā sa tarhi viśeṣa pratipannaḥ viśeṣaṇam iti śabdāt eva pratīyate 
[I,059,25]	atha pramāṇa antarāt iti yadi śabdāt katham sāmānyam eva śabda arthaḥ viśeṣasya api abhidhāyaka tvāt atha pramāṇa antaram na vā pramāṇa antara vyāpārān anubhavāt na ca sāmānyam para pakṣe viśeṣāt bhinnam sambhavati iti abhede sāmānya pratipatti vat viśeṣa pratipatti prasaṅgaḥ anyathā hi etad pratipattau itara pratipatteḥ bhedaḥ atha iṣyate eva kenacid rūpeṇa abhinnam bhinnañca iti na bheda abhedayoḥ vidhi pratiṣedha rūpa tvāt abhinne dharmiṇī asambhavaḥ tathā hi kim yena rūpeṇa bhinnam tena eva rūpeṇa abhinnam uta rūpa antareṇa iti vācyam yadi deśa bheda apekṣayā bhinnam rūpa bhedena tu abhinnam iti avipratipattiḥ paraḥ vibhinna deśa bheda apekṣayā bhedam pratipadyate iti 
[I,060,7]	atha anugata vyāvṛtta ātma tayā pratibhāsāt vastu bodha ātmaka tvam tat asat anugata sāmānya sambandhāt anugatam svarūpeṇa tu vyāvṛttam iti iṣyate eva dvi rūpa tā na ca eka tve tādātmye sati dvi rūpa tā upapadyate iti samavāya lakṣaṇaḥ sambandhaḥ abhyupagantavyaḥ svarūpa bhedena tu bhede samavāyam vinā niyata viśeṣeṇa vyapadeśa anupapattiḥ pṛthivyāḥ pṛthivī tvam iti ādi sambandham vinā yāvat pṛthivyāḥ vyapadiśyate tad avasthā antareṇa kasmāt na iti niyama abhāvaḥ 
[I,060,12]	yadi ca pṛthivī śabdaḥ pṛthivī tvam abhidadhyāt pṛthivī tva śabdasya arthaḥ vaktavyaḥ na ca abhede tad hita sāphalyam paśyāmaḥ iti sāmānyavān arthaḥ pṛthivī śabdasya iti yuktam atha ekatra saṅketitaḥ pṛthivī śabdaḥ katham artha antare pravartiṣyate iti āha pṛthivī tva abhisambandhāt nimittāt pṛthivī śabdaḥ ekatra saṅketitaḥ sa ca artha antare api tad vaśāt pravartate iti saṅketa anupapatteḥ viśeṣaḥ eva śabda arthaḥ na sambhavati iti sāṃkhya śākta pakṣaḥ api niṣiddhaḥ eva 
[I,060,17]	tathā śaktayaḥ sarva bhāvānām kārya arthāpatti gocarāḥ iti tad nirāsaḥ yat pṛthivī tva abhisambandhāt pṛthivī kāryam karoti iti pṛthivī tvam eva nijā śaktiḥ anyā tu caramasahakāri rūpā tad sadbhāve kārya karaṇāt tad abhāve ca akaraṇāt iti tathā hi vidyamānāḥ api tantavaḥ kāryam na ārabhante antya tantu saṃyogam vinā iti sā eva śaktiḥ atha artha antaram artha antarasya katham śaktiḥ anartha antara tve api samānam etat sā eva tasya eva śaktiḥ iti atha yadi pūrveṣām caramasahakāryā iva śaktiḥ tasya api aśaktasya akāraṇa tvāt anyā śaktiḥ vācyā iti anavasthā na etat evam caramasya hi sahakāriṇaḥ pūrva sahakāriṇaḥ eva śaktiḥ itaretara abhisambandhena kārya karaṇāt saḥ eva ca samagrāṇām bhāvaḥ sāmagri iti bhāva pratyayena ucyate tena hi satā samagra vyapadeśa darśanāt 
[I,060,26]	nanu yadi atīndriyā śaktiḥ na iṣyate maṇi mantra ādinā tarhi pratibaddhaḥ agniḥ na sphoṭa ādi kāryam ārabhataḥ iti kasya pratibandhaḥ na ca agneḥ na ca agni saṃyogasya upalabhyamāna tvāt iti śakteḥ pratibandhaḥ tat asat maṇi mantra ādi pratibandhaka abhāvasya api kārya utpattau sahakāri tvāt tad abhāve tu na kāryasya udayaḥ iti tad viśiṣṭa saṃyogaḥ eva śaktiḥ na punar śakteḥ pratibandhaḥ na anutpattiḥ vināśaḥ vā sambhavati iti cira utpanna tvāt vinaṣṭāyāḥ ca punar utpatti kāraṇa abhāvāt anutpatti prasaṅgaḥ aśaktasya kārya anutpādaka tvāt iti anvaya vyatirekābhyām pratibandhaka abhāva viśiṣṭaḥ agni saṃyogaḥ eva agni śaktiḥ iti jñātam evam atra api pṛthivī tvam nijā śaktiḥ aparā tu sahakāri bhūta iti 
[I,061,7]	pṛthivī ādīnām navānām guṇavat tvam samavāyi kāraṇa tvam kṣiti udaka ātmanām caturdaśa guṇavat tvañca uktam tatra kaiḥ guṇaiḥ guṇavatī keṣām utpattau samavāyi kāraṇa tvam ke vā caturdaśa guṇāḥ kiñca guṇa ātmakam lakṣaṇam iti āha rūpa ādi vākyam rūpa ādayaḥ saṃskāra paryantam vidyante yasyāḥ sā rūpa ādi saṃskāravatī kim ete svatantra tayā vṛtti kṛtā pratipādyante uta sūtrakārasya abhipretāḥ iti āśaṅkya āha ete ca guṇa viniveśa adhikāre ityādi ete ca sūtra kāreṇa abhihitāḥ kasmin adhikāre guṇāḥ vividham aneka prakāreṇa viniveśyante yasmin adhikāre sa tathā uktaḥ dvitīyaḥ adhyāyaḥ tatra sūtrakāreṇa pratipāditāḥ 
[I,061,14_I,061,17]	tathā ca rūpa rasa gandha sparśavatī pṛthivī iti anena viśeṣa guṇāḥ catvāraḥ abhihitāḥ tathā cākṣuṣa vacanāt iti saṃkhyāḥ parimāṇāni pṛthaktvam saṃyoga vibhāgau paratva aparatve karma ca rūpi dravya samavāyāt cākṣuṣāṇi iti sūtram darśayati sūtrasya arthaḥ rūpi dravyam upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptam mahat tva ādi upetam tatra samavāyāt saṃkhyā ādayaḥ ca pratyakṣa grāhyāḥ iti anya pareṇa api sūtreṇa rūpavati dravye saṃkhyā ādīnām sadbhāvaḥ abhihitaḥ anyathā hi avidyamāna tva ādev tatra teṣām upalambhaḥ na syāt iti 
[I,061,20]	padārthaḥ ca saṃkhyā iti bahuvacanam saṃkhyā tu a vyatirekeṇa eka tva tva ādi apara sāmānya pradarśana artham parimāṇāni iti tathā parimāṇa tva apekṣayā aṇu tva ādi apara sāmānya jñāpana artham pṛthaktvam iti eka vacanam pṛthaktva tva sāmānya apekṣayā eka pṛthaktva tva ādi apara sāmānya śūnyatā pradarśana artham saṃyoga vibhāgau iti dvivacanena saṃyoga tva vibhāga tva vyatirekeṇa apara sāmānya abhāve api vibhāgasya saṃyoga apekṣita ājñāpana artham samāsa karaṇam tathā paratva aparatve iti api dvivacanam paratva aparatvam sāmānya apekṣayā apara sāmānya abhāve api sāhacarya jñāpana artham samāsa karaṇam iti 
[I,062,1]	tathā patana upadeśāt iti guru tvāt patamam iti sūtram darśayati yathā ca patane guru tvam kāraṇam tathā vakṣyāmaḥ guru tva parīkṣāyām adbhiḥ sāmānya vacanāt iti sarpiḥ jatu madhūcchiṣṭhānām pārthivānām agni saṃyogāt drava tvam adbhiḥ sāmānyam iti sūtram darśayati sarpiḥ ādīnām agni saṃyogāt drava tvam sampadyate adbhiḥ tathā sāmānyam yathā bhavati iti sūtra arthaḥ uttara karma vacanāt iti nodanāt ādyam iṣoḥ karma tad karma kāritāt ca saṃskārāt tathā uttaram uttarañcaḥ iti sūtram darśayati iṣoḥ śarasya ādyam karma nodanāt bhavati iti karma ca nodana apekṣam saṃskāram ārabhate karma kāritāt ca saṃskārāt tathā uttarañca ekaḥ saṃskāraḥ anekam karma ārabhate patanam yāvat iti iṣoḥ samavāyi kāraṇasya avagatāyām sambhavini āmiṣoḥ iti ṣaṣṭhī abhidhānam tad avayaveṣu api karma jñāpana artham yat vā ṣaṣṭhī arthasya vidyamāna tvāt tad abhidhāne api adoṣaḥ 
[I,062,12_I,063,7]	rūpa ādayaḥ hi asādhāraṇa tvāt bhedakāḥ iti pratijñāta artha samarthana artham asādhāraṇa tvam āha kṣitau eva gandhaḥ ityādi atha udake tejasi vā upalambhāt gandhasya avadhāraṇam anupapannam na saṃyukta samavāyena upalambhāt tathā hi udake vāsaka dravya samparkāt gandha abhivyaktiḥ dṛṣṭā tejasi vai indhana viśeṣa anuvidhānāt iti yadi punar svabhāvataḥ eva syāt gandhaḥ tejasi indhana viśeṣam vinā vāsaka dravya samparkañca vinā vāriṇi upalabhyeta na ca evam atas yuktam etat kṣitau eka gandhaḥ iti 
[I,063,13_I,063,16]	rūpam śukla ādi aneka prakāram kṣitau eva na udake na tejasi niyamena śuklam eva udake bhāsvarañca tejasi upalabhyate pṛthivī āntu aneka prakāram tathā hi paṭa ādi bheda bhinna tvāt pṛthivyāḥ kācid śuklā kācid harita iti upalambhaḥ nanu yuktam vyakti bheda apekṣayā aneka rūpa sambandhi tvam pṛthivyāḥ yā tu golaka rūpāḥ na tasyām aneka prakāram atha tatra api kecid bhāgāḥ śuklāḥ kecid kṛṣṇā ityādi upalambhāt aneka rūpa sambandhi tvam na avayava avayavinoḥ anya tvāt avayavānām aneka rūpa sambandhi tve katham avayavinaḥ tathā bhāvaḥ abhyupagame vā sūtra vyāghātaḥ avibhuni dravye samāna indriya grāhyāṇām viśeṣa guṇānām asambhavāt iti vyāhanyeta iti 
[I,063,22]	vyāpake hi dravye samāna indriya grāhyāṇām bahūnām api sambhavaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ yathā śabdānām ākāśaḥ iti tad nirāsāya avibhu grahaṇam tathā avibhuni dravye vibhinna indriya grāhyāṇām rūpa rasa ādīnām sambhavāt iti samāna indriya grāhya padam samāna indriya grāhyāṇām api saṃkhyā ādīnām bahūnāma vibhuni dravye sambhavaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ tad vyavacchedāya viśeṣa grahaṇam 
[I,064,1]	atas bahūnām rūpāṇām ekasyām pṛthivyām abhyupagame vyāghātaḥ abhyupagamya api brūmaḥ śukla ādīnām bahūnām ekatra sadbhāve kim āśraya vyāpi tvam pradeśa varti tvam vā āśraya vyāpi tve sati eka avayava sahite api avayavinī upalabdhe para avayava āvaraṇe api aneka rūpam gṛhyeta āśraya vyāpi tvāt eva atha pradeśa vṛtti tvam tathā api viśeṣaṇam āśraya vyāpi tvam iti nirudhyate 
[I,064,5_I,064,9]	atha ekam citram tat rūpam iti yathā śuklam pītam ityādi viśeṣaḥ tathā citram rūpa viśeṣaḥ eva atra uktam citram tat ekam iti ced idam citrataram tatas yadi ekam tat katham citram citrañcet ekatā katham ekam citrañcā iti atiśayena āścaryam iti na paraspara viruddhānām rūpāṇām eka rūpa ārambhaka tvam nyāyyam samāna rūpa ārambhaka tvena upalambhāt śuklāt śuklam iti 
[I,064,11_I,064,15]	atha pṛthivyām apsu ca śukla ādi viśeṣa rūpa mātram upalambhāni atha anupapattyā niścīyate anyathā hi nīrūpa tvāt cakṣuḥ grāhya tvam na syāt rūpavataḥ dravyasya cakṣuḥ grāhya tvāt iti na ca avayava rūpāt eva cakṣuḥ viṣaya tvam anya rūpeṇa anyasya cakṣuḥ viṣaya tve vāyoḥ api tathā abhāva prasaṅgāt atas cakṣuḥ viṣaya tvāt rūpa mātram kṣitau iti nanu evam aneka prakāram kṣiteḥ rūpam iti virudhyate rūpa mātrasya śukla ādi antar bhāva abhāvāt tathā hi aneka prakāram śukla ādi bheda bhinnam iti ucyate rūpa mātrañca viśeṣa rahitam iti virodhaḥ 
[I,064,18]	tat etat sarvam avidita artham śukla ādi aneka prakārasya rūpasya kṣitau abhyupagamāt nanu uktam sūtra virodhaḥ iti na sūtra artha aparijñānāt tathā ca sūtrasya arthaḥ avibhuni avyāpake dravye samāna indriya grāhyāṇām viśeṣa guṇānām eka ākārāṇām asambhavaḥ iti pratiṣedhaḥ na tu aneka prakārāṇām katham etat aneka ākāra svarūpasya kṣitau upalambhāt tathā rasasya ṣaṣ bhedasya iti 
[I,064,23_I,065,1]	artha eka ākārāṇām bahūnām rūpāṇām rasa anāñca ekatra sadbhāvaḥ tasmāt na iṣyate vaiyarthyāt tathā hi ekena eva śukla rūpeṇa rūpa pratyayasya janita tvāt dvitīyasya vaiyarthyam eva tathā madhura rasena madhura pratyayasya iti atha śukla ādīnām ekasya sadbhāve kim vyāpya vṛtti tvam uta avyāpya vṛtti tvam iti uktam tatra avyāpya vṛtti tve na virodhaḥ śeṣāṇām āśraya vyāpi tvam eva iti avadhāraṇa anabhyupagamāt atas eva eka avayava sahitasya paṭasya upalambhāt tad eka rūpa upalambhaḥ api āśraya vyāpitayā aneka rūpāṇām anupalambhāt citra pratibhāsā bhāvaḥ 
[I,065,5]	atha kim citrāt utpadyate citram atha acitrāt iti citrāt utpatti abhyupagame paṭa kāraṇa kāraṇeṣu api citra pratibhāsa prasaṅgaḥ atha acitrāt utpadyate tadā hi eka rūpaḥ sarvatra citra rūpa utpatti prasaṅgaḥ na etat yuktam nānā rūpāṇi hi kāraṇāni nānā rūpam kāryam ārabhantaḥ iti upalabdham na ca evam tad kāraṇa kāraṇeṣu nānā rūpāṇi santi iti citra anutpādaḥ na ca tantūnām nīla ādi aneka rūpa sambandhi tvāt paṭe api aneka rūpa ārambhaka tve kiñcid bādhakam asti kāraṇa guṇa pūrva prakrameṇa tathāvidhasya rūpasya upādānāt tathā hi pratyekam kāraṇeṣu avicitrāt api rūpāt nīlāt nīlam pītāt pītam iti yuktam bhavatu ca eva ekam citram rūpam nīla ādi rūpaiḥ eka rūpa ārambhāt yathā hi śukla ādiḥ viśeṣaḥ rūpasya tathā citram rūpa ādi viśeṣaḥ eva yadi api śukla ādi śabdaiḥ na vyapadiśyate tathā api sva śabdena vyapadeśāt astitvam 
[I,065,14]	atha viruddhānām nīla ādīnām katham eka rūpa ārambhaka tvam yathā śuklānām iti yathā hi bahūni śukla rūpāṇi ekam śukla rūpam ārabhante iti upalabdham tathā nīla ādīnām api citra rūpa ārambhaka tvam dṛṣṭa tvāt abhyupagantavyam atha citra śabdasya nānā paryāya tvāt ekam citrañcaḥ iti idam eva citram āścaryam iti tat asat yathā nānā rūpeṣu citra vyapadeśaḥ citrāḥ tantavaḥ nīla ādi rūpa sambandhinaḥ iti tathā tad ārabdhe api paṭe citra vyapadeśaḥ citraḥ paṭaḥ iti citram rūpam asya iti na ca avaśyam nānā rūpa sambandhiṣu api paṭa ādiṣu citra vyapadeśaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ nānā rūpaiḥ tu kāraṇaiḥ ārabdhe avaśyam bhavati iti 
[I,065,21]	atha eka tvāt citra rūpasya eka avayava sahite api avayavinī upalabdhe śeṣa avayava āvaraṇe vicitra pratibhāsaḥ syāt na saha kārya bhāvāt tathā hi avayaveṣu nānā rūpa upalambha saha kāri indriyam avayavini citra pratibhāsam janayati iti anvaya vyatirekābhyām upalabdham tena śeṣa avayava āvaraṇe tad rūpāṇām agrahaṇāt avayavini citra pratibhāsā bhāvaḥ na ca apratibhāsāt ekāntena asattvam saha kārya bhāvena api anupalambhāt 
[I,065,26]	yat ca rūpa mātram upalambhāni atha anupapattyā jñāyate iti kaiścid uktam tatra api na doṣaḥ vipratipadyamānasya anumāna upanyāsāt tathā hi śukla ādi viśeṣa vyatiriktam citram rūpam kṣitau vidyamānam api vaijātyāt yaḥ na manyate tam pratyanumānam kṣiteḥ upalambhāt rūpavat tvam vijñāyate iti cakṣuṣā upalambhāt ca siddhe rūpavat tve śukla ādi śabdaiḥ vyapadeśa asambhavāt citra śabdena abhidhīyate iti siddham 
[I,066,4_I,066,7]	etena rasaḥ vyākhyātaḥ rasaḥ ṣaḍvidhaḥ madhura ādiḥ kṣitau eva vyakti bhedena ekasya añca vyaktau iti tathā ca ekasyām api harītakyām upalabhyate ṣaḍvidhaḥ rasaḥ iti atas eva ṣaṭ bhedasya anyatra anupalambhāt itarebhyaḥ bhedaka tvam tathā gandhaḥ dvividhaḥ surabhiḥ asurabhiḥ ca ekasyām pṛthivyām vyakti bhedena ekasyām ca iti pūrvavat atha surabhi gandhā bhāvaḥ eva asurabhiḥ iti vyavahāra sambhavāt gandhasya dvaividhyam anupapannam na ubhayoḥ tīvratara ādi bheda bhinna tvāt yathā hi surabhi gandhe tīvratara ādi vyavahāraḥ tathā asurabhi gandhe api iti surabhi gandha abhāve ca etat na upapannam abhāvasya niratiśaya tvāt iti

[I,066,21]	nanu evam sāmānya guṇānām api pāka ja tvaprasaṅgaḥ pārthiva guṇa tvāt rūpavat iti na etat yuktam sāmānya guṇānām pakṣīkaraṇe agni saṃyogena eva anekāntaḥ tathā hi pārthiva paramāṇau agni saṃyogaḥ agni saṃyoga jaḥ na bhavati pārthiva guṇaḥ ca iti na ca evam pārthiva viśeṣa guṇa tvam vyabhicarati iti sa pakṣa eka deśe vartamānasya atyantam vipakṣāt vyāvṛtteḥ gamaka tvam eva na ca pakṣe pratyakṣa āgamābhyām virudhyate iti na kāla atyaya apadiṣṭaḥ na ca prakaraṇa samaḥ tattva anupalabdheḥ aprayojaka tvāt atas pākaja sparśa ādi kāraṇa tvāt itarebhyaḥ bhidyate pṛthivī iti 
[I,067,1_I,067,5]	samānānām bhāvaḥ sāmānyam bheda adhiṣṭhānam atas bhedam āha sā tu dvividhāḥ iti sā tu pṛthivī dvividhā kena rūpeṇa iti āha nityā ca anityā ca nityā paramāṇu lakṣaṇā paramāṇu svabhāvā kārya lakṣaṇā kārya svabhāvā tu anityā iti bhedaḥ bhede ca sati sāmānya lakṣaṇam upapadyate iti asambha vitva āśaṅkā vyudāsaḥ sarvasya kāryasya vināśe samavāyikāraṇa abhāvāt punar utpattiḥ na syāt iti āśaṅkā nirāsa arthañca vākyam sā tu dvividhā nityā ca anityā ca anityāyāḥ ca nāśe nityā punar dvi aṇuka ādi prakrameṇa svarga ādau kāryam ārabhate iti siddham 
[I,067,8]	katham punar paramāṇu svabhāvā pṛthivī jñāyate iti āśaṅkya āha kārya lakṣaṇā kāryeṇa lakṣyate jñāyate iti tathā hi kāryam samavāyi kāraṇa pūrvakam tad kāraṇam api anya samavāyi kāraṇa janyam iti yāvat ādyam kāryam tat api samavāyi kāraṇa janyam iti tad janakāḥ paramāṇavaḥ tathā kāryāt alpa parimāṇam samavāyi kāraṇam tasya api anyat alpa parimāṇam iti ādyam kāryam niratiśaya aṇu parimāṇaiḥ ārabdham iti jñāyate 
[I,067,13]	atha tad avayavānām api paryavasānam na iṣyate nitya kāraṇa anabhyupagamāt tarhi kāryasya ākasmikasya asambhavāt tad kāraṇe api anyam samavāyi kāraṇam iti anavasthāyām kārya dravyasya alpatara ādi bhedaḥ na syāt tathā hi alpa kāraṇa ārabdham alpam bhūyas kāraṇa ārabdham mahat iti dṛṣṭam na ca kārya dravyasya nitya kāraṇa anabhyupagamena anavasthāyām etat upapadyate sarvasya api ananta kāraṇa janya tva aviśeṣāt iti yathā ananta kāraṇaiḥ ārabdhā golaka rūpā pṛthivī tathā ghaṭa ādi kāryam api iti eka ākāra tā prasaṅgaḥ na ca saṃkhyā pala parimāṇaiḥ eka ākāra tā upalabdhā ghaṭa ādeḥ bhinna parimāṇa tvāt bhinna pala tvāt ca iti tathā hi kiñcid hīnam pañca palam adhika tarañca daśa palam samāna kāraṇaiḥ ārabdham bahubhiḥ ca iti vaicitryam tat ca anavasthāyām na syāt

[I,068,7]	sarvam etat āśraya asiddham paramāṇu sadbhāva asiddheḥ atha iṣyate eva paramāṇoḥ sadbhāvaḥ tarhi paramāṇu sadbhāva āvedaka pramāṇasya abhyupagamāt tad viparīta anumānam nirviṣaya tvāt apramāṇam iti abhedyāḥ paramāṇavaḥ pareṇa abhyupagamāt tasya aniṣṭa āpattiḥ kriyate iti prasaṅga sādhanam tatra yadi pramāṇena abhyupagatāḥ pareṇa paramāṇavaḥ tasya prāmāṇya abhyupagame anutthānam viparīta anumānasya atha apramāṇāt evam tarhi tasya apramāṇa tayā paramāṇu sadbhāvaḥ na sidhyati iti kim anumāna upanyāsena āśraya asiddha tā prasaṅgāt 
[I,068,13]	tathā paramāṇavaḥ sa avayavāḥ ca iti pratijñā vākye padayoḥ virodhaḥ tathā hi paramāṇu śabdasya niratiśaya aṇu vāci tvam sāvayava tve vā avayava apekṣayā adhika parimāṇa tvam iti virodhaḥ na ca samāna adhika parimāṇa tve samavāyikāraṇa tvam iti tad avayavāḥ paramāṇavaḥ teṣām api sāvayava tve tad avayavāḥ teṣām api sāvayava tve tad avayavāḥ iti anavasthāyām uktam dūṣaṇam alpatara ādi bheda anupapattiḥ iti

[I,071,11_I,071,13]	anye tu asyāḥ paramāṇu lakṣaṇāyāḥ trividham kāryam śarīra ādi rūpam iti manyante vyavahitasya api idaṃśabdena kvacid parāmarśāt iti tatra śarīrasya itarasmāt vaidharmyam āha śarīram dvividham iti viśeṣasya sāmānya apekṣi tvāt viśeṣa abhidhāne avaśyam sāmānya lakṣaṇam vidyamānam antevāsinohyatām iti ūhana śakteḥ saṃvardhanāya na sāmānya lakṣaṇam avocat tathā hi śarīra abhidhāne śarīra tvam śarīra vyavahāra kāraṇam jñāyate eva lakṣaṇam iti tathā icchā anuvidhāyi kriyā āśraya tvam na ṛte śarīrāt sambhavati iti śarīra vacanāt arthāt labhyate iti sva śabdena avacanam grantha ādau tu śarīra ādi dvāreṇa iti ati vyāpti abhāvaḥ 
[I,071,19]	atha śarīra tvam sakala śarīra vyāpaka tvāt bheda antarāt vyāvṛtteḥ ca yuktam lakṣaṇam na ca evam icchā anuvidhāyi kriyā āśraya tvam tasya hi vipakṣāt vyāvṛttasya api sataḥ pakṣe sarvatra asambhavāt tathā hi mṛta ādi avasthāyām etat na sambhavati iti avyāpakam atha jīvat śarīrasya etat lakṣaṇam iti ced tat na supta mūrchita ādi avasthāyām api anupalabdheḥ katham tarhi idam lakṣaṇam yogyatā āśrayaṇāt tathā hi śarīram itarasmāt bhidyate sākṣāt icchā anuvidhāyi kriyā āśraya yogya tvāt śarīra tva sambandhāt ca yaḥ tu evam na bhavati na ca asau sākṣāt icchā anuvidhāyi kriyā āśraya yogyaḥ śarīra tva yuktaḥ ca yathā indriya ādiḥ iti 
[I,071,26_I,072,5]	āmaraṇāt yasya paṭutva āpaṭu tvābhyām indriyāṇām paṭu tva apaṭu tve tat śarīram iti kecid tathā hi auṣadha upayogāt api indriyeṣu paṭu tvam sambhavati iti āmaraṇāt iti padam tathā ca avyādhitasya śarīra paṭu tvena amaraṇam indriya paṭu tvam dṛṣṭam vyādhitasya tu auṣadha upayogena vyādhi upaśame śarīra paṭu tvāt eva indriya paṭu tvam iti paśyāmaḥ śarīrasya apaṭu tvāt eva indriyeṣu ca kāca kāmalā ādi doṣāḥ sambhavanti iti tad paṭu tvena vyāvṛttaḥ iti pārthivantu śarīram māṃsa ādi avayava janya tve satyanti āvayavi tvāt iti draṣṭavyam māṃsa ādi avayava janyasya api aṅgyulyādeḥ śarīra vyavahāra aviṣaya tvāt iti anti a avayavi padam antya avayavi tvañca aśarīrasya api sambhāvyate iti māṃsa ādi avayava janya padam 
[I,072,8]	sāmānya lakṣaṇa lakṣitasya pārthiva śarīrasya viśeṣa lakṣaṇa artham vibhāgaḥ śarīram dvividham kena rūpeṇa yoni jam ayonijañca pūrvam uddiṣṭe api yoni je artha prakāśasya vivakṣita tvāt ayonijam āha tatra ayonijam iti yoni śabdasya kāraṇa paryāya tvāt tad niṣedhe mā bhūt ākasmikam iti āha anapekṣa śukra śoṇitam iti yoni śabdaḥ sāmānya śabdaḥ api kāraṇa viśeṣe śukra śoṇita lakṣaṇe vivakṣitaḥ iti tad niṣedhena kāraṇa antaram labhyate śukra śoṇitam anapekṣya kāraṇa antarāt utpannam ayoni jam keṣām deva ṛṣīṇām śarīram iti ayonijantu śarīram deva rṣīṇām na tu ayoni jam eva yoni ja tvasya api śravaṇāt 
[I,072,16_I,072,22]	anye tu vyabhicāra niṣedha artham ekasya deva padasya lopena samāsam kurvate devāḥ ca devarṣayaḥ ca devarṣayaḥ teṣām iti atra devāḥ tu aṣṭadhā piśāca ādayaḥ tatra api kasyacid yoni ja tu a śravaṇe anyat viśeṣaṇam na cintyam atha kebhyaḥ tat śarīram bhavati iti āha dharma viśeṣa sahitebhyaḥ aṇubhyaḥ jāyate iti tathā hi tad śarīra utpattau aṇavaḥ samavāyi kāraṇam tad saṃyogaḥ ca asamavāyi kāraṇam dharma viśeṣaḥ nimitta kāraṇam iti kāryā eka artha samavāyaḥ ca dravya utpattau saṃyogasya iti atha deva rṣīṇām ayonijam śarīram asti iti atra kim pramāṇam āgamaḥ tathā ca ayonija śarīrāṇi bhavanti adbhuta karmaṇām yoni jāni eva maudgalya na mātā pitṛ jāni tu 
[I,072,25]	tathā hi adbhutam utkṛṣṭam karma yeṣām te tathā uktāḥ teṣām utkṛṣṭa karma vaśāt yoni jāni śarīrāṇi bhavanti kāraṇa mātra niṣedhaḥ mā bhūt iti āha yoni jāni kāraṇa jāni eva katham tarhi teṣām ayonija tvam iti āha na mātā pitṛ jāni iti pitṛ mātṛ śabdena śoṇita śukrayoḥ abhidhānam upacāreṇa iti tathā utkṛṣṭam karma dvedhā dharma rūpam adharma rūpañca iti tatra dharma rūpāt deva rṣīṇām adharma rūpāt ca kṣudra jantu yātanā śarīrāṇi kṣudra jantavaḥ yūka ādayaḥ yātanā śarīrāṇi nārakīya śarīrāṇi iti tāni adharma viśeṣa sahitebhyaḥ aṇubhyaḥ jāyante atha deva ṛṣīṇām śarīrāṇi dharma viśeṣāt upajātāni api anumānena yoni jāni iti pratīyante tathā hi deva ṛṣi śarīrāṇi yoni jāni śarīra tvāt asmad ādi śarīra vat iti tat ca āgamena bādhyamāna tvāt apramāṇam iti tathā anumānena ca āgamasya bādhāt deva ṛṣi śarīrāṇām sadbhāva asiddheḥ nija anumānasya āśraya asiddha tvāt apramāṇa tva prasaṅgaḥ 
[I,073,9_I,073,13^1]	na ca anumānasya āgama viṣaye tad upaghātena pramāṇa tā sambhavati yuktañca āgama anugrāhaka tvam tathā hi deva ṛṣi śarīrāṇi ayonijāni utkṛṣṭa karma ārabdha tvāt śarabha ādi śarīra vat utkṛṣṭam karma adharma rūpam śarabha ādi śarīre deva ṛṣi śarīre tu dharma rūpam iti viśeṣe api utkṛṣṭa karma ārabdha tvam ubhayatra aviśiṣṭam iti na sādhana hīnam udāharaṇam yonijam āha śukra śoṇita sampāta jam iti śukra śoṇitayoḥ sannipātāt sambandhāt jāyate iti śukram pituḥ mātuḥ śoṇitam iti tayoḥ sannipāta sama kālam bhoktaḥ karma vaśāt antaḥkaraṇa sambandhaḥ śukra śoṇitayoḥ saṃyogāt majjita ākāram dravyam utpannam 
[I,073,13^2]	tad anantaram āntareṇa tejasā sambandhāt vega apekṣā t avayave kriyā tad anantaram vibhāgāt dravya ārambhaka saṃyoga vināśaḥ tad vināśāt tad ārabdhasya dravyasya vināśaḥ punar anyasmāt agni saṃyogāt pūrvarūpa ādayaḥ vyāvartante anyasmāt ca apūrvarūpa ādi utpattiḥ evam utpanna pāka jeṣu aṇuṣvātma aṇu saṃyogāt adṛṣṭa apekṣāt utpannā kriyā vibhāgam ārabhate tasmāt pūrva saṃyoga vyāvṛttāt uttara saṃyogāt dvi aṇuka utpattiḥ evam dvi aṇukaiḥ tri aṇuka utpattiḥ ityādi krameṇa śarīra utpattiḥ iti punar mātrā bhuktam pītam tanmātrayā avatāryate tatas punar āntarālena ca sambandhāt avayave kriyā punar vibhāgāt saṃyoga vināśaḥ tatas dravya vināśaḥ anyasmāt agni saṃyogāt pūrvarūpa ādi vināśaḥ anyasmāt ca rakta ādi utpattiḥ tatas dvi aṇuka ādi prakrameṇa śarīra utpattiḥ iti nyāyaḥ śarīre api etat lakṣaṇam draṣṭavyam yāvat bhasmībhāvaḥ iti anyathā hi āhāra upayogasya āśraya upacaya akāraṇa tvāt vaiyarthyam syāt 
[I,073,26]	na ca ārabdha śarīrāḥ ye vā avayavāḥ sahakāri prāptau śarīra antaram ārabhante punar saha kāri antara prāptau anyat śarīram iti vācyam ārabhya ārambhaka vāda prasaṅgāt atha iṣyate vā ekam dravyam ārabhya tasmin avinaṣṭe punar dravya antara ārambhaka tvam na yuktam etat sarvasya api kārya dravyasya paramāṇu vṛtti tva prasaṅgāt tathā hi paramāṇubhyām dvi aṇukam ārabdham tasmin avinaṣṭe tābhyām eva anya paramāṇu sahitābhyām anyat ārabdham punar anya paramāṇu sahitaiḥ anyadārabhyate iti mūrtānām samāna deśatā prasaṅgaḥ tathā hi paramāṇubhyām ārabdham paramāṇvoḥ vartate punar anya sahitābhyām ārabdham tayoḥ tasmin ca iti mūrtānām eka deśa tvam syāt teṣāntu paraspara vyatirikta ādhāra samavāyi tvam dṛṣṭam yatra hi ekam mūrtam samavetam na tatra anyat samavaiti 
[I,074,8]	artha eka deśatā parihāra artham paramāṇubhyām anya sahakāribhyām ārabdham ekasmin eva paramāṇau vartate punar anya sahitaiḥ taiḥ ārabdham ekasmin eva iti ucyate evam api ekasmin dravye vartamānam kārya dravyam kāraṇa vibhāga abhāvāt avināśi syāt tathā adravyam dravyam aneka dravyañca dravyam iti vacana vyāghātaḥ tathā hi na vidyate janyam jana kañca dravyam iti adravyam paramāṇūnām janakam na asti ākāśa ādīnām janyam na api janakam iti adravyam nitya dravyam iti yāvat aneka dravyantu aneka dravyam janakam asya iti anena sva rūpeṇa dvividham eva dravyam adravyam nityam aneka dravyam janyam kāryam iti eka dravyasya ca kārya dravyasya abhyupagame vyāhatam etat bhavati iti 
[I,074,16_I,074,19]	na ca ekasya krama yaugapadyābhyām ārambhaka tvam nyāyyam eka svarūpa tayā yāvat kartavyam tāvat ekasmin kāle kuryāt aśeṣa kārya utpattau samarthasya anya anapekṣita tvāt iti yugapad aśeṣa kāryam kṛtvā punar akaraṇe hetuḥ na asti iti atha pūrvam ārabdham kārya dravyam avekṣya ārabhante tarhi pūrvasya ārabdha kāryasya api samavāyi tve katham ekasmin eva dravye vartate pūrvasmin sva vṛttau anekam dūṣaṇam abhyūhyam samāna asamāna jātīyayoḥ ārambhaka tva āsambhavāt ityādi tathā sarvasya api kārya dravyasya paramāṇu vṛtti tāyām iha tantuṣu paṭaḥ iha vīraṇeṣu kaṭaḥ ityādi prayogaḥ na syāt tantu ādeḥ samavāyi tvā abhāvāt iti kārya dravyasya vināśe ca antara kāryasya anutpanna tvāt upalambha abhāvaḥ 
[I,074,24]	atha paramāṇubhiḥ pūrva pūrvasya kāryasya avināśe sati uttarottara kārya ārambhāt anekam kārya dravyam iti antyasya vināśe pūrva pūrvasya avasthānāt aneka kārya upalambhaḥ iti ced nanu evam tarhi kapāla saṃyoga vināśe api ghaṭasya avināśa prasaṅgaḥ tad avayava tad avayava saṃyoga vināśe ca tad avayava tad avayavānām teṣām samavāyi tvā abhāvena tad saṃyogasya asamavāyi tva abhāvāt iti samavāyi kāraṇa vināśena asamavāyi kāraṇa vināśena vā dravyasya vināśa darśanāt 
[I,075,3]	atha paramāṇau utpannā kriyā saṃyoga vināśa dvāreṇa dravya vināśika iṣyate tatra yadi ādya dravya ārambhake paramāṇau utpannā kriyā vibhāgāt saṃyoga vināśe sati dravyam vināśayet tarhi pūrva pūrva saṃyogasya uttarottara saṃyoga sahakāri tayā śeṣa kārya utpattau asamavāyi kāraṇa tva abhyupagamāt tad vināśe avaśyam sakala kārya vināśaḥ iti na kiñcid kāryam upalabhyeta 
[I,075,7_I,075,13]	atha antya paramāṇu saṃyogasya pūrva pūrva paramāṇu saṃyoga upacitasya eka kārya utpattau asamavāyikāraṇa tvam iti tad vināśe tad ā ārabdhasya eva vināśāt avāntara kāryasya upalambhaḥ eva iti ced nanu evam api paramāṇu saṃyogasya vināśāt upajātaḥ ghaṭa ādi nāśaḥ asmad ādeḥ ati indriyaḥ syāt yathā hi āpāka nikṣipteṣu ghaṭeṣu agni saṃyogāt vināśaḥ para māṇu kriyā dvāreṇa iti pratyakṣaḥ ca kapāla saṃyoga vināśāt ghaṭasya vināśaḥ tena jñāyate kapālānām samavāyi tvam iti alam ati vistareṇa atas śarīre pratikṣaṇam āhāra upayoga anupayoge sati upacaya apacaya prapañca darśanāt pūrva dravya nimittāt utpanna pāka jaiḥ dvi aṇuka ādi prakrameṇa ca utpattiḥ vācyā iti yathā ca paramāṇuṣu pākaḥ dvi aṇuka ādi prakrameṇa ca utpattiḥ tathā vakṣyāmaḥ pākaja utpattau iti

[I,075,22_I,075,25]	anye tu ekasya mānuṣa śabdasya lopena samāsam kurvate mānuṣāḥ ca mānuṣa paśavaḥ ca mṛgāḥ ca iti atra mānuṣa śabdena abhihitānām paśu śabdena abhidhānena tat eva dūṣaṇam iti prayojanañca cintyam tathā mṛga śabdena sarva paśūnām abhidhāna asambhavāt avyāptiḥ iti aṇḍa jam keṣām iti āha pakṣi sarīsṛpāṇām iti pakṣiṇaḥ ca sarīsṛpāḥ ca iti pakṣi sarīsṛpāḥ teṣām iti sarīsṛpāḥ kuṭilam sarpanti iti sarpa ādayaḥ rūḍhi vaśāt ca iti 
[I,076,1^1]	śarīrasya śarīrāt samāna jātīyāt ca vaidharmyam abhidhāya indriyasya vaidharmya nirūpaṇa artham āha indriyam gandha vyañjakam iti tathā indriyāṇām nānātvāt tat vyāpi sāmānya lakṣaṇam arthāt labhyate eva karaṇa tva ati indriya tva dravya tva niyata adhiṣṭhāna vṛtti tve satya parokṣa jñāna janaka tvāt iti aparokṣa jñāna janaka tvam kartuḥ ātmanaḥ saṃbhavati iti tad nirāsāya karaṇa tva grahaṇam anindriyasya pradīpa ādeḥ karaṇa tve satya parokṣa jñāna janaka tvam dṛṣṭam iti tad nirākaraṇa artham atīndriya padam tathā indriya artha sannikarṣaḥ karaṇa tva ati indriya tve satya parokṣa jñāna janaka
[I,076,1^2]	iti dravya tva padam tathā diś kālayoḥ sarva utpattimatām nimitta tvāt karaṇa tva ati indriya tva dravya tve satya parokṣa jñāna janaka tvam asti iti niyata adhiṣṭhāna vṛtti tva padam diś kālayoḥ tu vyāpaka tvena sakala kārya janaka tvena niyata adhiṣṭhāna asambhavāt atha ātmā api vyāpaka tvāt anena viśeṣaṇena vyavacchinnaḥ iti vyartham karaṇa tva padam na vyāpakasya api bhoktṛ tvena śarīra adhiṣṭhāna tvāt atas indriya m itarasmāt bhidyate karaṇa tva ati indriya tva dravya tva niyata adhiṣṭhāna vṛtti tve satya parokṣa jñāna janaka tvāt yaḥ tu na bhidyate na ca asau ukta sādhanaḥ yathā śarīra ādiḥ iti 
[I,076,14]	sāmānya lakṣaṇa lakṣitasya samāna jātīyāt bhedam āha indriyam ghrāṇam indriya sāmānya lakṣaṇa lakṣita tve sati gandha vyañjaka tvāt itarebhyaḥ bhidyate tathā indriyam gandha vyañjakam iti kāryeṇa sadbhāvam darśayati tathā hi gandha upalabdhiḥ karaṇa kāryā kriyā tvāt yā yā kriyā sā sā karaṇa kāryā dṛṣṭā yathā cchidi kriyā tathā ca iyam kriyā tasmāt karaṇa kāryā iti 
[I,076,19]	yat ca gandha upalabdhi sampādakam karaṇam tat ghrāṇam tat ca pārthivam rūpa rasa gandha sparśeṣu madhye niyamena gandha vyañjaka tvāt yat yat rūpa ādiṣu madhye niyamena gandha vyañjakam tat tat pārthivam dṛṣṭam yathā kastūrikā ādi dravyam tathā ca ghrāṇam rūpa ādiṣu madhye niyamena gandha prakāśakam tasmāt pārthivam iti nanu niyamena gandha vyañjaka tvam asiddham gandha tva guṇa tva sat tā ādeḥ api vyañjaka tvāt iti atas rūpa rasa gandha sparśeṣu madhye iti viśeṣaṇam 
[I,076,24]	atha pārthiva tva aviśeṣāt ghrāṇam gandhasya iva rūpa ādi prakāśakam api syāt rūpa ādeḥ api pārthiva guṇa tvāt saṃyukta samavāyasya ca sambandhasya aviśeṣāt anyasya ca viśeṣa hetoḥ abhāvāt iti atas āha jala ādi anabhibhūtaiḥ pārthiva avayavaiḥ ārabdham ghrāṇam atas gandhasya eva prakāśakam iti katham etat jñāyate kiñcid jala ādinā sampṛktaiḥ anabhibhūtaiḥ pārthiva avayavaiḥ ārambhaḥ ghrāṇasya iti kārya niyamāt tathā ghrāṇasya vyāpārāt gandhasya eva upalambhaḥ na rūpa ādeḥ iti dṛṣṭam na ca kāraṇa niyamam vinā kārya niyamaḥ sambhavati iti kiñcid jala ādi asampṛktaiḥ utpādaḥ jñāyate ca adṛṣṭa viśeṣāt gandha upalabdheḥ sampādakāt anyathā hi ghrāṇa vyāpārāt gandhasya eva upalabdhiḥ na bhavet sā ca dṛṣṭā atas jñāyate anyasya kāraṇatva asambhavāt viśiṣṭa utpādaḥ nimittam sa ca adṛṣṭa vaśāt adṛṣṭasya ca vyavasthā kāraṇa tvāt iti abhipretañca etat sūtrakartuḥ iti 
[I,077,7_I,077,10]	bhūyas tvāt gandhavat tvāt ca gandha jñāne prakṛtiḥ pṛthivī iti vacanāt gandhaḥ jñāyate anena iti gandha jñānam ghrāṇam tasmin utpādye prakṛtiḥ kāraṇam pṛthivī bhūyastvāt nimittāt iti yathā bhūyasām pārthiva avayavānām gandha upalabdhi sampādaka adṛṣṭa viśeṣa upagṛhītānām jala ādinā ca atiraskṛta vapuṣām ghrāṇa janaka tvam niyamena gandha upalabdheḥ jñāyate bhūyasā añca pārthiva avayavānām kāraṇa tva abhidhānāt alpīyasām api jala ādi avayavānām akāraṇa tvam labdham atas eva teṣām pārthiva avayavānām abhibhāvaka tvam tathā na param viśiṣṭa adṛṣṭa upagrahe satīṣat jala avayava ādi sampṛktaiḥ ārambhāt gandhasya eva prakāśaka tvam gandhavat tvāt ca iti pārthiva tvāt ghrāṇasya rūpa ādimattvam api sambhavati iti gandhavat tvam utkarṣaḥ vivakṣitaḥ sva gata gandha utkarṣāt ca rūpa ādiṣu ca madhye saṃyukta samavāya aviśeṣe api gandhasya eva prakāśakam iti 
[I,077,18_I,077,22]	yadi vā kācid eva pṛthivī gandha upalabdheḥ kāraṇam na sarva iti viśeṣa hetuḥ na asti iti ukte vākyam saṃbadhyate bhūyas tvāt gandhavat tvāt ca gandha jñāne prakṛtiḥ iti gandhe jñaptiḥ jñānam gandha viṣaya ka jñānam tasmin prakṛtiḥ kāraṇam pṛthivī bhūyas tvāt vyākṛtāt gandhavat tvāt ca iti anyaḥ vā arthaḥ gandhavat tvāt niyamena gandha upalabdheḥ kāraṇam viśeṣa hetuḥ na asti iti ukte vākyam saṃbadhyam ghrāṇam tat ca gandha vat pārthiva tva aviśeṣāt ghrāṇam kutas iti āha bhūyas tvāt ukta rūpāt iti 
[I,077,25]	anye tu jala ādya sampṛktaiḥ śuddhaiḥ pārthiva avayavaiḥ ārambhaḥ viśiṣṭa adṛṣṭa apekṣaiḥ bhūyastvam iti manyante tathā ca bhāṣyam jala ādi anabhibhūtaiḥ asampṛktaiḥ kevalaiḥ pārthiva avayavaiḥ ārabdham ghrāṇam iti atra ca īṣat jala ādi samparke api anabhibhavasya sambhavāt asaṃpṛktaiḥ iti viśeṣaṇam na budhyāmahe na ca bhūyasām bhāvaḥ bhūyas tvam iti ukte anyeṣām atyanta asambhavaḥ upalabhyate iti alam 
[I,078,4]	indriyam sarva prāṇinām gandha vyañjakam iti sāmānya viśeṣa ātmatayā abhidhāya viṣaya svarūpa nirūpaṇa artham āha viṣayaḥ tu dvi aṇuka ādi prakrameṇa ārabdhaḥ iti nanu dvi aṇuka ādi prakrameṇa ārambhaḥ śarīrasya indriyasya ca asti iti ati vyāpi idam viṣaya lakṣaṇam iti na etat evam śarīra indriyayoḥ lakṣaṇa abhidhānena viṣayāt bheda siddhau tad anya tve satī iti viśeṣaṇa lābhāt tathā hi śarīra indriya anya tve sati dvi aṇuka ādi prakrameṇa ārabdha tvāt viṣayaḥ tasya hi viṣaya bhāva upakāraka tvāt viṣayaḥ tu upabhogyaḥ indriya grāhyaḥ vā asmad ādeḥ 
[I,078,10_I,078,17]	atha tri aṇukam dvi aṇuka ādi prakrameṇa utpannam śarīra indriya anya tve satyasmad ādi indriyam grāhyañca na bhavati avyāpi idam viṣaya lakṣaṇam iti dvi aṇuka ādi prakrameṇa ārabdhaḥ iti viśeṣaṇena vyavacchedāt tathā hi dvi aṇukam ādiḥ yasya prakramasya ityādi grahaṇam tri aṇukasya api avarodhakam iti asau dvi aṇuka ādiḥ sa ca asau prakramaḥ ca iti tena ārabdhaḥ viṣayaḥ dvi aṇuka tri aṇuka ādi prakrameṇa ārabdhaḥ iti yāvat tri aṇu kantu dvi aṇukaiḥ ārabdham dvi aṇuka ādi prakrameṇa iti tri aṇukāna an tva niyamena ārambhaka tvam dvayoḥ bahūnāñca iti tad ārabdhasya indriya viṣaya tā sambhāvyate iti viṣayasya ca sāmānya lakṣaṇa lakṣitasya api avāntara bhedena ānantyāt saṃgraham āha trividhaḥ kena rūpeṇa mṛd pāṣāṇa sthāvara lakṣaṇaḥ iti mṛd ca pāṣāṇaḥ ca sthāvarāḥ ca iti lakṣaṇam svabhāvaḥ yasya asau tathā uktaḥ svabhāvaḥ tu mṛdi mṛd tvam pāṣāṇeṣu pāṣāṇa tvam iti
