[I,084,22]	śarīrasya sāmānya lakṣaṇa muktam iti utpattiḥ eva ucyate śarīram ayonijam eva iti ayonijam hi śukra śoṇita sannipāta anapekṣam dharma viśeṣa sahitebhyaḥ aṇubhyaḥ iti taijasāḥ paramāṇavaḥ samavāyi kāraṇam tad saṃyogāḥ ca asamavāyi kāraṇam pārthiva ādi avayavāḥ ca nimitta kāraṇam iti tat ca āditya loke siddham āgamāt atha tejaḥ avayavinaḥ kṣaṇikatāyām tadā ārabdham viśiṣṭa upabhoga ajanakam iti āha pārthiva avayava upaṣṭambhāt ca upabhoga samartham iti tat ca śarīram sāmānya lakṣaṇa lakṣita tve sati tejaḥ avayavaiḥ ārabdha tvāditarasmāt bhidyate iti viśeṣa lakṣaṇam jñeyam 
[I,085,1]	atha indriya svarūpa nirūpaṇa artham āha indriyam sarva prāṇinām rūpa vyañjakam iti rūpa upalabdhiḥ karaṇa kāryā kriyā tvāt yā yā kriyā sā sā karaṇa kāryā yathā chidi kriyā tathā ca iyam kriyā tasmāt karaṇa kāryā iti yad rūpa upalabdheḥ sampādakam karaṇam tat cakṣuḥ iti tat ca taijasam rūpa ādiṣu madhye niyamena rūpa vyañjaka tvāt yat yat rūpa ādiṣu madhye niyamena rūpa vyañjakam tad taijasam yathā pradīpaḥ tathā ca rūpa ādiṣu madhye niyamena rūpa vyañjakam cakṣuḥ tasmāt taijasam iti cakṣuṣaḥ hi rūpa vat dravya ādi prakāśaka tva upalabdheḥ niyamena rūpa prakāśaka tvam asiddham syāt iti rūpa ādiṣu madhye iti padam rūpa rasa gandha sparśeṣu madhye niyamena rūpa vyañjaka tvam vivakṣitam iti 
[I,085,9_I,085,13]	atha taijasa tvāt cakṣuṣaḥ rūpasya iva ūṣma prakāśaka tvam api syāt tasya hi taijasa tvāt saṃyukta samavāyasya aviśeṣāt anyasya ca viśeṣa hetoḥ abhāvāt iti āha anya avayavān abhibhūtaiḥ tejaḥ avayavaiḥ ārabdham cakṣuḥ atas rūpasya eva vyañjakam iti tathā hi īṣat pārthiva avayava saṃyuktaiḥ anabhibhūtaiḥ tejaḥ avayavaiḥ ārabdham cakṣuḥ iti rūpasya eva vyañjakam atha ittham bhūta ārambhe kim pramāṇam kārya niyamaḥ tathā hi cakṣuḥ vyāpārāt rūpa ādiṣu madhye rūpasya eva upalabdhiḥ dṛṣṭā sā ca kāraṇa niyamam vinā na syāt iti anyasya asambhavāt viśiṣṭa utpādaḥ atra nimittam sa ca adṛṣṭāt rūpa upalabdhi sampādakāt tasya hi vastu vyavasthā hetu tvāt iti 
[I,085,17]	bhūyas tvāt rūpavat tvāt ca rūpa jñāne prakṛtiḥ kāraṇam tejaḥ iti asya ca sūtrasya idam bhāṣyam rūpam jñāyate anena iti rūpa jñānam cakṣuḥ tasmin utpādye prakṛtiḥ kāraṇam tejaḥ bhūyastvāt nimittāt atas rūpasya eva prakāśakam indriyañca iti bhūyas tvam hi bhūyasām tejaḥ avayavānām viśiṣṭa adṛṣṭa upagṛhītānām īṣat itara avayava samparke ca ārambhaka tvam iti yat vā rūpe jñaptiḥ jñānam tasmin eva rūpa ādiṣu madhye kāraṇam cakṣuḥ kutas iti āha bhūyas tvāt vyākṛtāt rūpavat tvāt ca iti rūpavat tvam hi rūpa utkarṣaḥ vivakṣitaḥ anyathā hi taijasa tvāt uṣṇa sparśavat tvam api sambhāvyate iti viśeṣa abhidhānam anarthakam syāt yat vā rūpa ādiṣu madhye rūpasya eva upalambhāni atha anupapattyā jñāyate rūpa utkarṣaḥ kutas bhavati iti āha bhūyas tvāt ukta rūpāt iti 
[I,085,26]	atha mahat tvāt aneka dravya tvāt cakṣuṣaḥ kasmāt indriyeṇa upalambhaḥ na bhavati pradīpasya iva viśiṣṭa rūpa abhāvāt yatra hi rūpavat dravyasya cakṣuḥ sparśanābhyām upalambhaḥ iti rūpa viśeṣaḥ tu yad kṛtā kvacid viṣaye rūpa upalabdhiḥ yat abhāvāt ca mahat aneka dravya āśrayasya api anupalabdhiḥ saḥ udbhava samākhyānaḥ rūpa dharmaḥ sahakāri viśeṣaḥ iti dṛṣṭañca rūpa viśeṣa abhāvāt vāri sthite tejasi mahat aneka dravya tve api agrahaṇam udbhūta rūpasya pradīpasya andhakāre api grahaṇam upabhoga arthāḥ hi sṛṣṭiḥ bhāvānām iti rūpasya udbhave cakṣuṣaḥ andhakāre api grahaṇe duṣṭa sattvānām upabhoga anutpattiḥ syāt iti tad upabhoga prāpaka adṛṣṭa vaśena anudbhūta rūpam cakṣuḥ janitam prajāpatinā tathā uṣṇa sparśa udbhave api aneka cakṣuḥ sannipātāt prīti kare vastuni nartakī ādau grīṣma samaye ati uṣṇaiḥ marīcibhiḥ iva dāhaḥ syāt iti adṛṣṭa vaśāt eva uṣṇa sparśasya api anudbhavaḥ kalpyate iti 
[I,086,9^1]	viṣaya svarūpa nirūpaṇa artham āha viṣaya lakṣaṇam viṣaya svarūpam caturvidham iti kena rūpeṇa iti āha bhaumam divyam udaryam ākara jañcaḥ iti viṣaya lakṣaṇena śarīra indriyāt vyāvṛttasya viṣayasya avāntara vaidharmyam etat iti tatra bhūmau bhavam bhaumam kāṣṭhāni eva indhanāni yasya tebhyaḥ prabhavati utpadyate iti tad prabhavam iti indhana viśeṣa āditarasmāt bhidyate tat ca ūrdhva jvalana svabhāvaḥ yasya iti ūrdhva jvalana svabhāvakam iti amuṣmāt apītarasmāt bhidyate eva yat eva artha kriyā kāri tat eva parama artha sat iti darśanasya sattā sambandhena api sattva abhyupagame api abhyupagama vādena pratiṣedha artham kriyā nirūpaṇañca pacanasvedana ādi samartham iti divyam abindhana viśeṣāt viśiṣyate iti āha ap indhanam iti āpaḥ indhanam yasya 
[I,086,9^2_I,086,22]	na tvāpaḥ eva iti tat ca sauram iti āditya sambaddham vidyut ādi iti ādi padena ulkā pāta ādeḥ grahaṇam iti evam udare bhavam udaryam tat ca bhuktasya āhārasya rasa ādi pariṇāma artham iti rasa mala dhātu pariṇāma artham pariṇāmaḥ ca paramāṇuṣu pūrvarūpa ādi nivṛttau utpanna pāka jaiḥ dvi aṇuka ādi prakrameṇa rasa ādi dravya ārambhaḥ iti vakṣyāmaḥ pākaja utpattau ākarajañca iti ākarāt jātam suvarṇa ādi ādi grahaṇāt trapu sīsa loha rajatānām grahaṇam artha eteṣām taijasa tve kim pramāṇam āgamaḥ tathā ca agneḥ apatyam prathamam suvarṇam dyauḥ vaiṣṇavī sūrya sutāḥ ca gāvaḥ 
[I,086,24]	atha agneḥ jātam atajjātīyam bhavati iti anekānta āda sādhanam etat tathā ca agneḥ jātam dhūma ādi na tad jātīyam tat asat apatya vyavahārasya sājātya apekṣayā eva dṛṣṭa tvāt tathā hi na kārya mātre apatya vyavahāraḥ dṛṣṭaḥ kim tarhi samāna jātīye yathā mānuṣa apatyam iti nanu evam cetaneṣu eva apatya vyavahāra upalabdheḥ acetane anupapattiḥ na tejaḥ adhiṣṭhānasya cetanatayā tad apekṣayā asya upapatteḥ yat vai agni kāryasya aneka tve api agneḥ apatyam suvarṇam iti viśeṣa abhidhānāt samāna jātīya tvam labhyate aviśeṣa vivakṣāya antu kārya antaram apatyam iti abhidadhyāt āgama antarāt vā viśeṣa pratipattiḥ iti alam tathā prathamam suvarṇam iti abhidhānāt agneḥ apatyam rajata ādikam api labhyate anyathā hi prathamam iti anarthakam syāt viśeṣaṇam evañca sati guru tva adhikaraṇa tvāt pārthivam suvarṇa ādi iti anumānam āgama bādhita tvāt apramāṇam āgamike hi viṣaye anumāna pravṛtteḥ pratiṣedhāt 
[I,087,7_I,087,13]	atha eteṣām taijasa tve rasa ādi upalabdhiḥ tarhi katham saṃyukta samavāyāt tathā hi saṃyuktam suvarṇa ādau pārthivam dravyam tatra samavetāḥ rasa ādayaḥ upalabhyante iti āha tatra saṃyukta samavāyāt rasa ādi upalabdhiḥ iti atha drava tvam api evam astu kimartham tasya tejaḥ guṇa tvam iti ced na pārthivāt asya viśeṣa upalabdheḥ tathā hi pārthivam lākṣā ādi agni saṃyogāt bhasma tām āpadyamānam dṛṣṭam suvarṇa ādau ca bhṛśam api agni saṃyoga atiśayena drava tvam eva uṣṇa sparśān udbhavaḥ ca atra adṛṣṭāt 
[I,088,3]	idānīm vāyoḥ uddeśavataḥ lakṣaṇa parīkṣā artham vāyu tvā abhisambandhāt iti ādi prakaraṇam vāyuḥ iti lakṣya nirdeśaḥ vāyu tvā abhisambandhāt iti lakṣaṇam vāyu tvena abhisambandhaḥ vāyu tvena upalakṣitaḥ samavāyaḥ iti samavāyaḥ hi ati vyāpaka tvāt alakṣaṇam syāt iti vāyu tva padam vāyu tvañcā sambaddham apakṣa dharma tayā gamakam na syāt iti pakṣa dharma tā ājñāpana artham abhisambandha padam tathā ca vāyu tvena itarasmāt bhidyate vāyu tvā abhisambandhāt ye tu na bhidyante na te vāyu tvena abhisambaddhāḥ yathā kṣiti ādayaḥ na ca tathā vāyu tvena anabhisambaddhaḥ vāyuḥ tasmāt itarasmāt bhidyate iti vyavahāraḥ vā sādhyate śeṣañca lakṣaṇasya dūṣaṇa pratisamādhānam pṛthivī adhikāre jñeyam tathā vāyu śabdasya sāmānyavān arthaḥ iti jñāpana artham atīndriya śakti pratiṣedha arthañca pūrvavat vākyam vyākhyeyam 
[I,088,12]	samavāyi tva guṇavat tva pratipādana artham sparśa ādi vākyam sparśa ādayaḥ saṃskāra paryantāḥ vidyante yasya asau tat vān iti sparśasya sādhāraṇa tvāt anyasmāt bhedaka tva abhāva āditya sādhāraṇa tām āha sparśaḥ asya anuṣṇa aśīta tve satya pāka jaḥ iti anuṣṇaḥ iti uṣṇa sparśa vyavacchedaḥ aśītaḥ iti śīta sparśāt apākajaḥ iti pārthivāt sa ca guṇa viniveśāt dvitīya adhyāye siddhaḥ vāyuḥ sparśavān iti anena sūtreṇa 
[I,088,17_I,088,20]	atra ca sparśavān iti sāmānya śabdena api artha ādayam viśeṣaḥ vivakṣitaḥ anuṣṇa aśīta tve satya pākaja sparśavān iti arūpiṣu acākṣuṣa tvāt iti sūtreṇa saṃkhyā ādayaḥ siddhāḥ tathā hi rūpa viśeṣavati dravye cākṣuṣāḥ tad viparīte ca ācākṣuṣāḥ iti apareṇa api sūtreṇa arūpiṣu saṃkhyā ādīnām sadbhāvaḥ abhihitaḥ eva tathā cārūpiṣu samavetāḥ saṃkhyā ādayaḥ param cakṣuḥ grāhyāḥ na bhavanti iti pratiṣedhaḥ tathā tṛṇa karma vacanāt iti vāyu saṃyogāt tṛṇe karma iti sūtram darśayati 
[I,088,24_I,089,5]	vāyu saṃyogaḥ ca tṛṇa karma utpattau sa apekṣaḥ kāraṇam iti prayatna ādeḥ abhāvāt vega apekṣaḥ kāraṇam iti saṃskāraḥ siddhaḥ tathā vāyu tva sāmānyasya bheda adhiṣṭhāna tvāt iti tat samarthena arthāt lakṣaṇena lakṣyamāṇasya eka aneka tva upalabdhau saṃśaye sati tad nirāsa artham advaitava ādi pratiṣedha artham bīja sadbhāva pratipādana arthañca sa ca ayam dvividhaḥ aṇu kārya bhāvāt iti vākyam tathā hi aṇu svabhāvaḥ nityaḥ kārya svabhāvaḥ tu anityaḥ iti avāntara vaidharmyam darśayati kārya lakṣaṇaḥ kārya svabhāvaḥ caturvidhaḥ iti kena rūpeṇa iti āha śarīram indriyam viṣayaḥ prāṇaḥ iti 
[I,089,7]	śarīra utpattim āha śarīram ayonijam eva iti ayonijañca śukra śoṇita sannipātam anapekṣya upajātam dharma viśeṣa sahitebhyaḥ vāyu paramāṇubhyaḥ iti tathā hi vāyavīyāḥ paramāṇavaḥ samavāyi kāraṇam tad saṃyogāḥ ca asamavāyi kāraṇam kṣiti ādi ca nimitta kāraṇam iti tat ca marutām loke siddham āgamāt atha vāyoḥ tiryak gati śīla tvāt kṣaṇika tvāt ca tadā ārabdha śarīram upabhoga ajanakam syāt iti āha pārthiva avayava upaṣṭambhāt ca upabhoga samartham iti 
[I,089,13]	indriya svarūpa nirūpaṇa artham āha indriyam sarva prāṇinām sparśa upalambhakam iti tathā hi sparśa upalabdhiḥ karaṇa kāryā kriyā tvāt yā yā kriyā sā sā karaṇa kāryā yathā chidi kriyā tathā ca iyam kriyā tasmāt karaṇa kāryā iti yat yat sparśa upalabdheḥ sampādakam karaṇam tat vāyavīyam rūpa ādiṣu madhye niyamena sparśa vyañjaka tvāt yat yat rūpa ādiṣu madhye niyamena sparśa vyañjakam tat vāyavīyam dṛṣṭam yathā vyajana anilaḥ tathā ca rūpa ādiṣu madhye niyamena sparśa vyañjakam tvac indriyam tasmāt vāyavīyam iti tvac indriyasya sparśavat dravya ādi vyañjaka tva upalabdheḥ niyamena sparśa vyañjaka tvam asiddham syāt iti rūpa ādiṣu madhye iti viśeṣaṇam vyajana anile tu tad gata sparśa vyaktau yadi api rūpa ādi asambhavaḥ tathā api śīta ādi sparśa vyañjaka tva sadbhāvāt viśeṣaṇa sadbhāvaḥ 
[I,089,22]	atha vāyavīya tva aviśeṣe kasmāt kiñcid eva sparśa vyañjakam indriyam iti tvac indriyañca iti āha pṛthivī ādi anabhibhūtaiḥ vāyavīyaiḥ viśiṣṭa adṛṣṭa upagṛhītaiḥ īṣat itara avayava saṃpṛktaiḥ śuddhaiḥ vā ārabdham atas sparśasya eva abhivyañjakam indriyañca iti tat ca śarīra vyāpi sarvatra sparśa upalambhāt vijñātam tasya ca saṃjñā tvac indriyam iti tvak iti śarīra avaguṇṭhakam carma tad sthānam indriyam upacāreṇa tvac indriyam iti uktam 
[I,090,1_I,090,4]	atha tvac indriyasya viśiṣṭa utpāde kim pramāṇam kārya niyamaḥ tathā ca rūpa ādiṣu madhye sparśasya eva upalambhāni atha anupapattyā jñāyate kāraṇa niyamaḥ sa ca anyasya asambhavāt viśiṣṭa utpāde nimittam iti kalpyate asya ca sūtrasya idam bhāṣyam bhūyastvāt sparśavat tvāt ca sparśa jñāne prakṛtiḥ vāyuḥ iti sparśaḥ jñāyate anena iti sparśa jñānam indriyam iti tasmin utpādye prakṛtiḥ kāraṇam vāyuḥ bhūyastvāt nimittāt atas tat eva indriyam rūpa ādiṣu madhye sparśasya eva vyañjakam iti bhūyastvāt iti bhūyasām viśiṣṭa adṛṣṭa upagṛhītānām vāyu avayavānām īṣat itara avayava samparkaiḥ ārambhaka tvam 
[I,090,9_I,090,14]	yat vā sparśe jñaptiḥ jñānam tasmin eva rūpa ādiṣu madhye prakṛtiḥ kāraṇam vāyuḥ kutas iti āha bhūyas tvāt vyākṛtāt sparśavat tvāt ca iti sparśavat tvañca asya sparśa utkarṣaḥ vivakṣitaḥ yat vā sparśasya eva upalambhāni atha anupapattyā jñātaḥ sparśa utkarṣaḥ kasmāt bhavati iti āha bhūyastvāt nimittāt iti nanu sarvam etat asambaddham vāyu sadbhāve pramāṇa abhāvāt na pratyakṣeṇa upalambhāt tathā hi spārśana vyāpārāt aparokṣa jñānam utpadyamānam dṛṣṭam vāyuḥ vāti śītaḥ vāyuḥ uṣṇaḥ vāyuḥ iti na ca idam liṅga liṅgi sambandha anusmaraṇa parāmarśa jñāna anantaram utpadyate iti na anumāna prabhavam śabdam vinā api utpatteḥ na śābdam iti indriya anuvidhānāt indriya jam yat ca aparokṣa jñānam tat pratyakṣam 
[I,090,19]	atha mahat tvāt aneka dravyavat tvāt rūpa viśeṣāt ca dravyam pratyakṣam iti sūtra virodhaḥ na sūtra artha aparijñānāt tathā ca sūtra arthaḥ aparokṣa jñāna sadbhāve sati samastam vyaḥ tañca lakṣaṇam iti jñeyam yatra hi aparokṣam jñānam tatra amīṣām samasta vyastānām kāraṇa tvam tathā hi ātmā mahat tvāt eva pratyakṣaḥ vāyuḥ tu mahattvāneka dravyavat tva abhyāñca yatra ca cakṣuḥ sparśanābhyām vijñānam dravye tatra samastam lakṣaṇam iti prādhānyantu yathā darśanam abhyupeyam tathā hi rātrau agniḥ dūre api upalabhyate rūpa atiśayāt mahattva aneka dravyavat tve api agrahaṇam parvata ādeḥ iti rūpasya prādhānyam evam āloka sadbhāve dūre api parvata ādeḥ grahaṇam mahat tve tu alpa prādhānyam iti utprekṣyam 
[I,091,1]	atha yatra spārśana pratyakṣa tvam tatra darśanasya api vyāpāraḥ dṛṣṭaḥ ogha śabda ādau saṃkhyā ādayaḥ ca pratyakṣāḥ iti iha api tathā abhāvaḥ syāt na ca asti atas sparśa mātram eva pratyakṣam vāri sthite tejasi uṣṇa tāvat iti yathā vāri sthite tejasi āśraya apratyakṣa tve api uṣṇa tā grahaṇam tadvat iha api āśraya apratyakṣa tve api sparśasya eva grahaṇam iti 
[I,091,5_I,091,9]	na etat evam vāri sthite tejasi rūpasya anudbhūta tvāt sparśa mātrasya pratyakṣa tvam yuktam yatra hi rūpa udbhavaḥ kāraṇam pratyakṣa tve tatra avaśyam cakṣuṣā api grahaṇam saṃkhyā ādayaḥ ca pratyakṣāḥ rūpān udbhave ca na grahaṇam iti dṛṣṭaḥ ca vāyau na rūpa viśeṣaḥ pratyakṣatāyām kāraṇam iti cakṣuṣā agrahaṇam saṃkhyā ādera pratyakṣa tvam yuktam atha rūpa viśeṣa abhāve apratyakṣa tvam eva syāt iti ced na ātmanā vyabhicārāt tathā hi ātmā rūpa viśeṣa abhāve api antaḥkaraṇa pratyakṣaḥ saṃkhyā ādayaḥ pratyakṣāḥ api ātmani rūpa viśeṣa abhāvāt eva apratyakṣāḥ iti 
[I,091,12]	atha dravya spārśana pratyakṣa tvam rūpa viśeṣa sadbhāve sati eva dṛṣṭam ghaṭa ādau tathā rūpa sparśa vyatirikta dravya ālambana tve anusandhān a jñāne ca pramāṇam asti yam aham adrākṣam cakṣuṣā tam eva etarhi spṛśāmi yam vā asprākṣam spārśanena tam paśyāmi iti na ca vāyau etat asti iti sparśa mātra ālambanam iti ced tat etat asat rūpam vinā api vāyoḥ spārśanena pratyakṣa tvāt atha sādhyam etat na dṛṣṭasya sādhya tve sati ati prasaṅgāt tathā hi sparśana vyāpārāt vāyau aparokṣa jñānam indriya bhāva vyatirekābhyām utpadyamānam dṛṣṭam iti uktam tasya ca sādhya tve ghaṭa ādau api darśana spārśana pratyakṣam sādhyam eva syāt atha indriya anuvidhānāt na sādhyam etat samānam vāyau api tathā idam anusandhānam tat dvi indriya grāhya tvāt ghaṭa ādau upapannam vāyoḥ eka indriya grāhya tvāt asambhavena atīndriya tvāt iti 
[I,091,21]	na ca anusandhānāt eva ghaṭa ādi jñānasya rūpa ādi vyatirikta vyālambana tvam kim tarhi ghaṭa ādi jñānasya vilakṣaṇa tvāt rūpa ādi vyatirikta artha ālambana tvam tatra ca anusandhānasya api prāmāṇyam iti na evam vāyuḥ vāti śītaḥ vāyuḥ iti jñānasya sparśa jñāna vilakṣaṇa tvāt tad vyatirikta artha ālambana tvam na ca sparśa upalambhanāt anumāna jam jñānam etat iti vācyam avinā abhau a sambandha anusmaraṇa ādeḥ abhāvāt ananubhūyamānasya api sambandha anusmaraṇa ādeḥ api vyāpāra tva kalpanā anyāyyā ghaṭa ādi jñānasya api anumāna tā prasaṅgāt vāyu pratyaya samāna adhikaraṇaḥ ca ayam pratyayaḥ iti vāyu ālambanaḥ eva 
[I,092,3]	anye tu anumānena api vāyoḥ pratyakṣatām vyavasthāpayanti svayam pratyakṣeṇa upalabdhaḥ api arthaḥ parasmai pratipādyamānaḥ anumānena eva pratipādyate iti manyamānāḥ tathā ca asmad ādi upalabhyamāna sparśa adhiṣṭhānaḥ vāyuḥ asmad ādi tvac indriya pratyakṣaḥ anudbhūta rūpa anya tve sati asmad ādi upalabhyamāna sparśa adhiṣṭhāna tvāt yaḥ yaḥ anudbhūta rūpa anya tve sati asmad ādi upalabhyamāna sparśa adhiṣṭhānaḥ sa saḥ asma ādi tvac indriya pratyakṣaḥ yathā ghaṭa ādiḥ tathā ca anudbhūta rūpa anya tve satyasmad ādi upalabhyamāna sparśa adhiṣṭhānaḥ vāyuḥ tasmāt asmad ādi tvac indriya pratyakṣaḥ iti 
[I,092,10]	nanu evam sarveṣām api atīndriyāṇām asmad ādi pratyakṣa tvam syāt prameya tvāt iti hetunā na para pratipattyā eva bādhyamāna tvāt tathā hi paraḥ vijānāti na me asti paramāṇu ādi viṣaya jñānam iti svayam aparokṣa jñāna sadbhāve sati para pratipādanāya anumāna upanyāsaḥ yuktaḥ sa ca vāyau asti na paramāṇu ādau iti tathā paramāṇu ādiḥ asmad ādi indriya viṣaya tve paramāṇu ādi rūpa tām jahyāt mahat tva ādi yoginyasmad ādi indriya vyāpāra upalabdheḥ iti 
[I,092,15]	idānīm pratyakṣeṇa vāyu sadbhāve vyavasthāpite viṣaya nirūpaṇa artham āha viṣayaḥ tu upalabhyamāna sparśa adhiṣṭhānam iti upalabhyamānaḥ ca asau sparśa adhiṣṭhāna bhūtaḥ ca iti tathā uktaḥ apratyakṣa vādinām upalabhyamānaḥ ca asau sparśaḥ ca tasya adhiṣṭhāna bhūtaḥ iti vyākhyā tatra ca asmad ādi pratipādanāya śāstrasya ārambhāt asmad ādi viśeṣaṇam api ūhyam upalambhaḥ api indriya dvāreṇa eva vivakṣitaḥ iti anyathā hi pramāṇa antareṇa upalambhaḥ śarīra ādau api asti iti upalabhyamāna sparśa adhiṣṭhāna tvam vyabhicāri viṣaya lakṣaṇam syāt evam asmad ādi indriya upalabhyamāna sparśa adhiṣṭhāna tvāt itarasmāt bhidyate viṣayaḥ iti vā vyavahartavyaḥ 
[I,092,22]	tathā na param viṣaya lakṣaṇaḥ vāyuḥ asmad ādi indriya pratyakṣaḥ anumānau agamyaḥ ca iti āha sparśa śabda dhṛti kampa liṅgaḥ iti sparśaḥ ca śabdaḥ ca dhṛtiḥ ca kampaḥ ca iti liṅgāni yasya asau tathā uktaḥ iti tathā hi anuṣṇa aśīta tve sati apājakaḥ sparśaḥ kvacid āśritaḥ guṇa tvāt yaḥ yaḥ guṇaḥ sa saḥ āśritaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ yathā rūpa ādiḥ tathā ca ayam guṇaḥ tasmāt āśritaḥ iti guṇa tvañca asya sāmānyavat tve adravya tve ca sati niyamena ācākṣuṣa pratyakṣa tvāt rasa vat iti acākṣuṣa pratyakṣa tvam ghaṭa ādau asti iti niyama grahaṇam tathā api sparśa tva ādi sāmānye niyamena ācākṣuṣa pratyakṣa tvam na ca guṇaḥ iti vyabhicāraḥ tad artham sāmānyavat tve sati iti viśeṣaṇam sāmānyavat tvam dravya ādi trayasya asti iti niyamena ācākṣuṣa pratyakṣa padam sāmānyavat tve sati niyamena ācākṣuṣa pratyakṣa tvam vāyu ādau asti iti adravya tve sati iti padam asya pakṣa dharma tve sati sa pakṣa eka deśe vartamānasya atyantam vipakṣāt vyāvṛttasya abādhita viṣaya tvāt asat pratipakṣa tvena gamaka tvam 
[I,093,7^1_I,093,7^2]	atha astu anuṣṇāśīta tve satya pākaja sparśasya āśrita tvam apākaja tve tu kim pramāṇam pākaja rūpa ādi viyogāt tathā hi pākaja sparśaḥ pākaja rūpa ādi sahitaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ ghaṭa ādau iti asya api pākaja tve tathā abhāvaḥ syāt atha sadbhāve api anudbhūta tvāt teṣām anupalambhaḥ tat na anyatra abhāvāt na hi pākaja sparśa upalambhe api rūpa ādīnām anyatra atyanta anupalambhaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ iti na ca atra rūpa ādīnām astitve pramāṇam asti iti anubhava anupapattiḥ sadbhāve anudbhava kalpanā upapatteḥ atha asadbhāve kim pramāṇam iti ced atyanta anupalabdhiḥ eva tathā hi vivakṣita sparśa adhikaraṇam guru tva rahitam sambhavati iti sahacaritāḥ rūpa ādayaḥ na kadācid upalabhyante pramāṇataḥ iti asantaḥ tathā pāka ja sparśasya guru tva sāhacaryā upalabdheḥ asya api pākaja tve tad sadbhāvaḥ syāt guru tva sambandhe ca ūrdhvam parṇa ādi dhāraṇa anupapattiḥ tasya api guru tva sambandhi tayā tad prasaṅgāt na ca pākaja sparśa adhikaraṇam guru tva rahitam sambhavati iti pārthiva sparśa vilakṣaṇa tvāt na pṛthivyām vartate na api udaka tejasoḥ anuṣṇa aśīta tvāt anyatra asambhavaḥ eva iti yatra ayam vartate asau vāyuḥ iti 
[I,093,19]	tathā ādyaḥ śuka śukā śabdaḥ santata anumitaḥ sparśavat dravya sambandha kāryaḥ vibhāga ja śabda ja śabda anya tve sati śabda tvāt yaḥ yaḥ vibhāga ja śabda ja śabda anya tve sati śabdaḥ sa sparśavat dravya saṃyoga kāryaḥ yathā bherī daṇḍa saṃyoga jaḥ śabdaḥ tathā ca ayam tasmāt yathā ukta sādhyaḥ iti nanu vibhāga ja śabdāt asya viśeṣa anupalabdheḥ sandigdham tad anya tve sati iti viśeṣaṇam na rūpa ādimatām ghana avayava sanniveśa bhājām kāraṇa vibhāga pūrvaka vibhāgasya śabda ārambhaka tva upalabdheḥ tad abhāvaḥ tu avivāda āspadaḥ iti vibhāga jatvā abhāvāt tathā vibhāga ja tve śuka śuka ādi śabdasya śākhā ādiṣu kampa samāna kāla upalabdhiḥ na syāt sā tu dṛṣṭā na ca atra śākhā ādi vāyu vibhāgasya śabda ārambhaka tvam yuktam kāraṇa vibhāga jatvā anupapatteḥ atas tad anya tve sati iti viśeṣaṇam asandigdham eva 
[I,094,1_I,094,5]	dhṛtiḥ dhāraṇam ākāśe parṇa ādīnām avasthānam tat ca sparśavat dravya saṃyoga kāryam prayatna ādi abhāve sati dhāraṇa tvāt yat yat prayatna ādi abhāve sati dhāraṇam tat tat sparśavat dravya saṃyoga kāryam yathā ādhāra gata udakam tathā ca idam tasmāt sparśavat dravya saṃyoga kāryam iti pakṣīṇām sannipatitānām mūrchanam iti āha saṃmūrchanam punar samāna javayoḥ vāyvoḥ viruddha diś kriyayoḥ sannipātaḥ hi sambandhaḥ sa ca kayoḥ vāyvoḥ kiṃviśiṣṭayoḥ iti āha samāna javayoḥ samānaḥ tulyaḥ javaḥ vegaḥ yayoḥ tau samāna javau tayoḥ iti anyathā hi ekasya alpa java tve balīyasā abhibhavāt na saṃmūrchanam iti tathā hi eka diś kriyayoḥ na saṃmūrchanam iti āha viruddha dikkriyayoḥ viruddhe diś kriye yayoḥ tau viruddha dikkriyau iti tathā hi ekasya prācīnadiggamanam anyasya ca tad abhimukham āgamanam iti kriyayoḥ virodhaḥ 
[I,094,12_I,094,17]	anye tu viruddhāyām diśi kriye yayoḥ tau tathā uktau iti manyante atra avirodhaḥ cintanīyaḥ atha ittham sannipātaḥ kutas pratīyate iti āha saḥ api sannipātaḥ sāvayavinoḥ ūrdhva gamanena anumīyate saha avayavibhiḥ vartete yau tau sāvayavinau iti tad avayavāḥ api mahāntaḥ avayavinaḥ iti jñāpana artham idam uktam anyathā hi sāvayavayoḥ iti syāt anye tu avayavinaḥ atra tṛṇa ādayaḥ vivakṣitāḥ na tad avayavāḥ iti manyante 
[I,094,18]	atha vāyoḥ eva ūrdhva gamanam katham pratīyate iti āha tat api tṛṇa ādīnām ūrdhva gamanena iti tathā hi tṛṇa ādīnām ūrdhva gamanam acetana tvāt na upapannam bhavati na api vegāt kvacid manda gati tvāt ādya karma utpattau ca tad abhāvāt anyasya ca sāmarthya anupalabdheḥ vegavat dravya sambandhaḥ anumīyate na ca tat pārthivam āpyam vā tasya api guru tva adhikaraṇa tayā ūrdhva gamane guru tva rahitam nimitta antaram vācyam na ca atra agneḥ ūrdhva jvalana svabhāva tayā tad saṃyogāt tṛṇa ādīnām ūrdhva gamanam indhana viśeṣa abhāvena ūrdhva jvalanā sambhavāt tad anupalabdheḥ ca na ca anyasya atra sāmarthyam iti vāyu sambandhāt tṛṇa ādīnām ūrdhva gamanam iti jñāyate tasya tiryaggati śīla tayā na ūrdhvam gamanam antarāle anyathā sambhāvyate iti vāyu antareṇa pratibandhaḥ tathā hi vāyuḥ balīyān apareṇa ca balīyasā pratibandhāt sannipātāt svām gatim virahayya ūrdhvam gacchati tad saṃyogāt ca tṛṇa ādīnām ūrdhva gamanam iti siddham tṛṇa ādīnām ūrdhva gamanena vāyoḥ ūrdhva gamanam tena ca sannipātaḥ tasmāt nānātvam iti 
[I,095,3]	atha prāṇa ākhyasya vāyoḥ upalabhyamāna sparśa adhiṣṭhāna tayā viṣaya antarbhāve api prādhānya jñāpana artham viśiṣṭa artha kriyā kāritayā pṛthak abhidhānam tathā tattva jñāninaḥ yoga abhyāse pravartamānasya prāṇaḥ atyantam upakārī iti pṛthak ucyate iti āha prāṇaḥ antar śarīre rasa mala dhātūnām preraṇa ādi hetuḥ iti tathā hi antar śarīre vartamāna tvāt prāṇaḥ iti ukte rasa ādibhiḥ vyabhicāraḥ tad artham rasa mala dhātūnām preraṇa ādi hetuḥ iti tathā api rasa ādi preraṇa hetu tvāt prāṇaḥ iti ukte adṛṣṭa ādiṣu vyabhicāraḥ tad artham antar śarīre vartamānaḥ iti na ca adṛṣṭa ādayaḥ antar śarīre vartante adṛṣṭasya ca ātma vṛtti tvāt īśvarasya ca āvṛttimat tvāt iti tat evam antar śarīre vartamānaḥ rasa ādi preraṇa hetutvāt itarasmāt bhidyate prāṇaḥ iti vā vyavahartavyaḥ 
[I,095,12_I,096,17]	yat vā vāyu sāmānya lakṣaṇa anuvṛttau satyām antar śarīre vartamāna tvāt rasa ādi preraṇa hetu tvāt ca prāṇaḥ iti ukte vyabhicāra abhāvaḥ atha asau kim ekaḥ anekaḥ iti āha ekaḥ san kriyā bhedāt apāna ādi saṃjñām labhate iti atha vāstava bhedaḥ kasmāt na iṣyate bādhaka upapatteḥ tathā hi pañca vāyavaḥ śarīre yadi vyāptyā vartante tadā sambandhāt ekaḥ vāyuḥ bhavati iti pañcatva nivṛttiḥ atha avyāptyā tathā api ekena śarīrasya vyāpanāt apareṣām asambhavaḥ iti manyamānaḥ kriyā bhedena bhedam āha saḥ eva mukha nāsikābhyām niṣkramaṇa śīlaḥ vāyuḥ prāṇa ākhyaḥ adhas nayanāt mala ādeḥ apānaḥ samam nayanāt samānaḥ ūrdhvam nayanāt udānaḥ vividham aneka prakāreṇa nayanāt vyānaḥ iti 
[I,097,2]	atha idānīm bhūtānām parīkṣā śeṣa nivartana dvāreṇa īśvara parīkṣā artham caturṇām iti ādi prakaraṇam tathā hi bhūtānām uddeśa anantaram pūrva prakaraṇeṣu lakṣaṇa parīkṣā abhidhāne api sṛṣṭi saṃhāra vidhiḥ na uktaḥ tathā īśvaraḥ ūrdhvam namaskāra vyājena uddiṣṭaḥ lakṣaṇataḥ ca pradhāna tvāt dharma parīkṣām antareṇa parīkṣitum na śakyate iti prakaraṇa ārambhaḥ sṛṣṭi saṃhāra vidhiḥ ca tulyatayā ekasmin eva prakaraṇe abhidhīyate pratiprakaraṇa abhidhāne tu prakaraṇa catuṣṭayam etāvat syāt iti saṅgraha rūpa tā vyāghātaḥ 
[I,097,8]	nanu evam vaidharmya avasare sādharmya pratipādanam anyāyyam na pratyekam bhūteṣu sṛṣṭi saṃhāra vidheḥ vailakṣaṇye api ekatra abhidhānāt sādharmya jñānam na paramārthataḥ na ca vaidharmye abhidhīyamāne yat yat sādharmyam tasya pratiṣedhaḥ yathā pṛthivī ādīnām paramāṇu kārya rūpa tayā dvaividhyam kāryañca śarīra ādi trayam paraspara vailakṣaṇyāt vaidharmye api na sādharmya rūpa tām vijahāti iti 
[I,097,13]	atha caturṇām iti ukte na jñāyate keṣām atas mahābhūtānām iti mahat grahaṇam aṇu vyavaccheda artham nanu evam dvi aṇukasya api sṛṣṭi saṃhāravataḥ vyavacchedaḥ syāt na mahat ārambhaka tvena tasya api mahat śabda vācya tvāt tathā hi dvi aṇuka ādi prakrameṇa utpatti vidhānāt saṃhārasya ca paramāṇu antasya dvi aṇuke api sṛṣṭi saṃhāra vidhau pratijñā kāryā eva sā ca evam kṛtā syāt tathā api mahābhūtānām iti ukte na jñāyate kiyatām iti tathā api caturṇām bhūtānām iti ukte na jñāyate keṣāmataḥ pṛthivī ādīnām iti labhyate na ca ākāśasya etat vyākhyāna avasara saṃgatyā astu avasaraḥ tat evam caturṇām mahābhūtānām sṛṣṭi saṃhārayoḥ vidhiḥ prakāraḥ tau eva abhidhīyete anena iti vidhiḥ pramāṇam tābhyām vā pramāṇa bhūtābhyām vidhiḥ vidhātā kartā ucyate iti āvartyamānam aneka artham etat eva vākyam 
[I,097,22^1]	tat brāhmeṇa mānena ityādinā saṃhāra vidheḥ vyākhyānam krama atikrameṇa ādau saṃsārasya anādi tva jñāpana artham tathā hi saṃhārāt pūrvam sṛṣṭiḥ labhyate tatas api saṃhāraḥ iti anādi tvam sa ca saṃhāraḥ katham bhavati iti āha maheśvara icchā ātmā aṇu saṃyoga ja karmabhyaḥ śarīra indriya kāraṇa aṇu vibhāgebhyaḥ tad saṃyoga nivṛttau teṣām āparamāṇu antaḥ vināśaḥ iti teṣām śarīra indriyāṇām ārambhakeṣu aṇuṣu dravya ārambhaka saṃyoga nivṛttau dvi aṇuka vināśe tadārabdhasya api nivṛttiḥ iti āha maheśvara icchā ātmā aṇu saṃyoga ja karmabhyaḥ śarīra indriya kāraṇa aṇu vibhāgebhyaḥ paramāṇuḥ yāvat tāvat vināśaḥ iti dravya ārambhaka saṃyoga nivṛttiḥ sva kāraṇa aṇu vibhāgebhyaḥ te ca maheśvara icchā ātmā aṇu saṃyoga ja karmabhyaḥ tathā hi maheśvara icchā nimitta kāraṇam ātmanām aṇubhiḥ saṃyogaḥ ca asamavāyi kāraṇam aṇavaḥ tu samavāyinaḥ iti aṇuṣu karmāṇi utpadyante kasmin avasaraḥ iti āha sarva ātma gata adṛṣṭānām sarva ātmasu gatāḥ ca te adṛṣṭāḥ ca teṣām kiṃviśiṣṭānām 
[I,097,22^2]	śarīra indriya mahā bhūta upanibandhakānām śarīra indriya mahābhūtāni upanibadhyante sampādyante yaiḥ teṣām vṛttiḥ phala dāna sāmarthyam tasya upabhogāt yugapad nirodhe vināśe sati sa ca sañjihīrṣā sama kālam yadā hi sakala bhuvana pateḥ maheśvarasya saṃhartum icchā sampadyate sā ca kimartham saṃsāra khinnānām prāṇinām saṃsāre śarīra upādāna parityāga dvāreṇa khinnānām niśi rātrau iva viśrāma artham yathā hi śarīra vyāpārāt ahani khinnāmām tad abhāvāt rātrau viśrāmaḥ tathā iha api iti 
[I,098,12]	kadā ca sañjihīrṣā brahmaṇaḥ apavarga kāle yadā hi adhikāra samāptau brahmā apavṛjyate sa ca varṣa śata avasāne vartamānasya brahmaṇaḥ bhavati iti kena mānena iti āha brāhmeṇa brahmaṇaḥ idam brāhmam tena iti tat punar divyam dvādaśa sāhasram kalpam viddhi caturyugam etat sahasra paryantam tat ahar brāhmam ucyate 
[I,098,17_I,098,21]	iti evaṃvidhaiḥ dinaiḥ māsa ādayaḥ api vaktavyāḥ iti mānam evam yathā brahmaṇaḥ apavarga kāle maheśvarasya sañjihīrṣā sama kālam viśiṣṭa adṛṣṭānām vṛtti nirodhe sati śarīra indriyāṇām vināśaḥ tathā pṛthivī udaka jvalana pavanānām api mahābhūtānām anena eva krameṇa iti paramāṇuṣu karma utpattau vibhāgebhyaḥ sat saṃyoga nivṛtti dvāreṇa uttarasmin uttarasmin sati pūrvasya pūrvasya vināśaḥ iti utpatti apekṣayā yat yat pūrvam utpannam tat tat uttarasmin uttarasmin vidyamāne sati vinaśyati iti tathā hi uttarasmin sati pūrvam vāyoḥ vināśaḥ tad anantaram udakasya ityādi 
[I,098,25]	anye tu etat vākyam pāṭhā apekṣayā eva vivakṣitam iti manyante tathā hi yathā śarīra indriyāṇām vināśaḥ tathā pṛthivī udaka jvalana pavanānām api mahābhūtānām vināśaḥ anena eva krameṇa iti pāṭha krameṇa na krama antareṇa iti evañca śarīra indriya mahābhūtānām vināśe tad āśritānām guṇa karmaṇām api vināśaḥ tatas pravibhaktāḥ kārya anādhārāḥ paramāṇavaḥ avatiṣṭhante tathā na param paramāṇavaḥ dharma adharma saṃskāraiḥ anuviddhāḥ sambaddhāḥ ātmānaḥ ca avatiṣṭhante 
[I,099,4_I,099,8]	atha anyeṣām api sāmānya ādīnām avasthāne kim artham viśeṣa abhidhānam iti ced dravya vināśasya paramāṇu anta tā ājñāpana artham ātmanā añca dharma ādi vināśa kāraṇa tva abhāvāt dharma adharma saṃskāra anuviddhānām avasthānam na kevalānām iti anyathā hi nimitta abhāvāt punar utpattiḥ na syāt atha kiyantam kālam evam avasthānam iti āha tāvantam eva kālam iti brāhmeṇa mānena varṣa śatam yāvat iti 
[I,099,10]	tatas punar varṣa śata ante api viśrāma prāpaka adṛṣṭa nivṛttau prāṇinām karma vipāka upalambhāt bhoga bhūtaye bhoga bhūti artham maheśvarasya sisṛkṣā sraṣṭum icchā sampadyate tad anantaram pavana paramāṇuṣu samavetāni karmāṇi utpadyante kebhyaḥ kāraṇebhyaḥ iti āha tad saṃyogebhyaḥ teṣām bhoginām saṃyogāḥ paramāṇubhiḥ tebhyaḥ iti asamavāyi kāraṇa nirdeśaḥ te ca karma ārambhe sa apekṣā iti āha sarva ātma gata vṛtti labdha adṛṣṭa apekṣebhyaḥ iti sarva ātmasu bhogiṣu gatāḥ sarva ātma gatāḥ te ca te vṛtti labdha adṛṣṭāḥ ca iti vṛttyā sahakāri kāraṇena labdhāḥ ca te adṛṣṭāḥ ca iti tathā uktāḥ tān apekṣyante iti tad apekṣāḥ tebhyaḥ iti na tu vṛttiḥ labdhā yaiḥ iti vyākhyānam atra niṣṭhā antasya pūrva nipāta prasaṅgāt

[I,099,24]	tat evam pavana paramāṇuṣu kārya utpattau satyām anantaram vibhāgaḥ tasmāt saṃyoga nivṛttau teṣām paramāṇūnām paraspara saṃyogebhyaḥ dvi aṇukāni utpannāni tri aṇukāni ārabhantaḥ ityādi krameṇa mahān vāyuḥ samutpannaḥ nabhasi a ākāśe dodhūyamānaḥ iti atiśayena kampamānaḥ tiṣṭhati sa ca ādau utpannaḥ atiśaya vega sambandhāt gurutvavatām apāta hetuḥ bhavati dṛṣṭañca vāyoḥ parṇa ādi patana pratibandhe sāmarthyam ayañca atiśayena mahat tve sati vega sambandhāt udadhi sahitām pṛthivīm tṛṇam iva dhārayate iti na citram

[I,100,14_I,100,24]	anye tu virodha parihāra artham tasmin eva mahā udadhau iti vākyam pṛthivyām sambandhayanti tad anantaram tasmin pṛthivī utpāde sati taijasebhyaḥ paramāṇubhyaḥ dvi aṇuka ādi prakrameṇa mahān tejaḥ rāśiḥ iti pūrvam anena evam ukta prakāreṇa samutpanneṣu caturṣu mahābhūteṣu satsu maheśvarasya abhidhyāna mātrāt icchā mātrāt na śarīra ādi vyāpārāt iti tathā tatas eva nimittāt taijasebhyaḥ paramāṇubhyaḥ pārthiva paramāṇu sahitebhyaḥ mahat aṇḍam ārabhyate kiṃviśiṣṭam mahat iti atra hi taijasāḥ paramāṇavaḥ samavāyi kāraṇam tad saṃyogāḥ ca asamavāyi kāraṇam pārthiva avayavāḥ ca nimitta kāraṇam maheśvara abhidhyānañca iti dvi aṇukāni utpannāni tri aṇuka ādi prakrameṇa mahat aṇḍam ārabhante iti tasmin ca aṇḍa antar deśe brahmāṇam utpādayati kiṃviśiṣṭam iti āha catur vadana kamalam iti catvāri kamalāni iva vadanāni yasya asau tathā uktaḥ tam iti sarveṣān ca lokānām bhūḥ ādi satya antānām pitāmaham svāminam tathā sakala bhuvanaiḥ sahitañca iti tam utpādya maheśvaraḥ prajā sarge viniyuṅkte brahman prajā sargam kuru iti 
[I,101,1]	sa ca maheśvareṇa viniyuktaḥ brahmā atiśayena jñānañca vairāgyam ca aiśvaryañca iti tathā uktāni taiḥ sampannaḥ yuktaḥ atas eva prāṇinām karma vipākam viditvā sutān sṛjati kiṃviśiṣṭān prajāpatīn prajāyāḥ svāminaḥ karma anurūpam jñānañca bhogaḥ ca āyuḥ ca yeṣām te tathā uktān karma anurūpa jñāna bhoga āyuṣaḥ iti tathā manasi bhavān mānasān manaḥ vyāpāreṇa saṅkalpa mātreṇa sampāditān na kāyika vyāpāreṇa iti atas tān iti tathā manavaḥ ca devāḥ ca ṛṣayaḥ ca pitaraḥ ca iti tathā uktāḥ teṣām gaṇāḥ samūhāḥ tān ca sṛjati tathā hi caturaḥ varṇān brāhmaṇa kṣatriya viś śūdrān karma anurūpa bhoga jñāna āyuṣaḥ sṛjati kebhyaḥ iti āha mukha bāhu ūru pādataḥ yathāsaṅkhyam iti tathā anyāni ca uccāvacāni uttama adhama bhāvena avasthitāni bhūtāni sṛjati etān ca pūrva uktān sṛṣṭvā āśaya anurūpaiḥ dharma jñāna vairāgya aiśvaryaiḥ saṃyojayati yasya hi yādṛśam karma tasya tādṛśāni dharma jñāna vairāgya aiśvaryāṇi sampādayati iti 
[I,101,13]	nanu sarvam etat asambaddham īśvara sadbhāve pramāṇa asambhavāt tat na anumāna āgamābhyām tad sadbhāva siddheḥ tathā ca anumānam kṣiti ādiṣu sṛṣṭi saṃhārau kartṛ pūrvakau iti atha sṛṣṭi saṃhārayoḥ bhūteṣu aprasiddheḥ anumāna abhāvaḥ iti ced racanāvat tvena tad siddheḥ tathā hi kṣiti ādīni kāryāṇi racanāvat tvāt yat yat racanā vat tat tat kāryam yathā ghaṭa ādi tathā racanā vat kṣiti ādi tasmāt kāryam iti 
[I,101,18_I,102,1]	na ca racanāvat tvam antareṇa api kāryatvam upalabhyate iti aprayojaka tvam vācyam sarvasya api sa pakṣa eka deśe vartamānasya āgamaka tva prasaṅgāt tathā hi dhūmasya api aprayojaka tvam tad antareṇa api agnimat tva upalabdheḥ atha yatra dhūmaḥ tatra agniḥ iti vyāptiḥ evam tarhi yatra racanāvat tvam tatra kāryatvam iti samānam tathā ca ghaṭa ādau api abhūtvā bhāvi tvam pratyakṣeṇa anupalabdhañca racanāvat tvena eva sādhyate tathā idam saṃhāre api samānam iti siddhe ca kāryatve kartṛ pūrvaka tvañca sādhyate tathā ca vivāda āspadam bodha ādhāra kāraṇakam kāryatvāt yat yat kāryam tat tat bodha ādhāra kāraṇakam yathā ghaṭa ādi tathā ca idam kāryam tasmāt bodha ādhāra kāraṇakam iti asya ca pakṣa dharma tve sati sa pakṣe vartamānasya vipakṣāt atyantam vyāvṛtteḥ abādhita viṣaya tvāt asat pratipakṣa tvena gamaka tvam nanu evam aśeṣa jñeya jñāna ādhāra vidhātṛ pūrvaka tve sādhye sādhya vikalaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ kumbha ādā a sarvajña pūrvaka tvena vyāptasya kāryatvasya upalabdheḥ tathā viruddhaḥ ca hetuḥ na vivāda āspadam sarva pūrvakam kāryatvāt ghaṭa vat asarvajña pūrvaka tve ca sādhye abhipretasya asiddhiḥ iti 
[I,102,5]	na etat evam bodha ādhāre adhiṣṭhātari sādhye na sādhya vikala tvam na api viruddha tvam na ca kārya tvam buddhimantam adhiṣṭhātāram vyabhicarati iti avyabhicāra upalambha sāmarthyāt upalabhyamānam pakṣe kṣiti ādi sampādana samartham eva adhiṣṭhātāram sādhayati iti na ca kṣiti ādi upādāna upakaraṇa anabhijñaḥ kṣiti ādi sampādana samarthaḥ iti paramāṇu ādi viṣaya jñānam tat kartuḥ labhyate pakṣa dharma tā prasādāt sarvañca anumānam sāmānyena vyāpti grahaṇa balāt pravartamānam pakṣa dharma tā balāt sādhya viśeṣam sādhayati iti dṛṣṭam na ca visphūrjata api pareṇa atra bodha ādhāra kāraṇaka tva kāryatvayoḥ sāmānya vyāpteḥ vyāghātaḥ śakyā sādhanaḥ viśeṣeṇa tu vyāpti virahāt asādhana tve dhūmasya api asādhana tva prasaṅgaḥ tatra api apāsta aśeṣa viśeṣeṇa agni mātreṇa dhūma mātra vyāpteḥ upalambhāt iti tathā ca atra api viśeṣa virodhaḥ sambhavati eva ayam parvataḥ parvata avaṣṭabdha agnimān na bhavati dhūmavat tvāt yaḥ yaḥ dhūmavān sa sa viśiṣṭa agnimān na bhavati yathā rasavatī pradeśaḥ tathā ca ayam tasmāt yathā ukta sādhyaḥ iti 
[I,102,17_I,102,22]	atha dhūmasya agni mātreṇa vyāpteḥ upalambhāt yatra upalambhaḥ tatra eva agniḥ tatra eva agni prasādhaka tvāt viruddha tā anavakāśaḥ iti ced iha api samānam kāryatvasya buddhimatā vyāpteḥ upalambhāt pakṣe tad sādhaka tvam iti atha dhūma pradeśaḥ agninā vyāptaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ iti pradeśa antare api agnimat tvam prasādhayati iti yuktam nanu evam tarhi kāryatvam api yatra upalabdham tat eva utpādana samarthena eva kartrā vyāptam iti pakṣe api kṣiti ādi sampādana samartham kartāram gamayet yat ca idam anumānam na vivāda āspadam sarvajña pūrvakam iti tatra viśeṣa pratiṣedhasya śeṣa abhyupagame sāmarthya upalabdheḥ asarvajña pūrvaka tvam syāt kāryatvasya kartṛ avyabhicārāt iti yaḥ ca asau asarva jñaḥ sa yadi kṣiti utpādana samarthaḥ saṃjñā mātram bhidyeta iti atha asamarthaḥ katham kṣiti ādeḥ kartā 
[I,102,26_I,103,6]	atha parasya sarvajña tva viśeṣaḥ kāryatvena hetunā abhipretaḥ tad pratiṣedha artham vidhiḥ asarvajña pūrvakam iti tatra viśeṣa pratiṣedhasya śeṣa abhyanujñā abhyupagame sāmarthya upalabdheḥ viruddha anumānam na kartṛ mātrasya iti ced na katham atra kṣiti ādi sampādana sāmarthyam saṃjñā bheda mātram asāmarthye tu kārya anutpattiḥ iti dṛṣṭañca kāryam tathā samasta viśeṣa pratiṣedhe nirādhārasya sāmānyasya aprasiddheḥ nirviṣaya tvena apramāṇa tā prasaṅgaḥ na ca idam apramāṇam sāmānya vyāpteḥ pratiṣeddhum aśakyatvāt atha viśiṣṭa viśeṣa pratiṣedhaḥ tadā viśeṣa abhyanujñāyām viśeṣa antara upagama prāptiḥ vāmena akṣṇā na paśyati iti yathā atha agni dhūmayoḥ pratyakṣeṇa sambandha siddheḥ anumāna pravṛttiḥ yuktā na evam atra iti ced na iha api kāryatvasya adhiṣṭhātṛ pūrvaka tvena sambandha siddheḥ anumānam pravartate eva 
[I,103,8]	atha agniḥ anumānāt ūrdhvam api pratyakṣaḥ na evam īśvaraḥ iti anumānam katham iti ced na atyanta parokṣasya api cakṣuḥ ādeḥ upalabdhi anumeya tvāt atha atra sāmānyena kriyāyāḥ kāraṇa kāryatva upalabdheḥ anumānam tarhi kāryatvasya sāmānyena kartṛ pūrva katva upalabdheḥ anumānam iti abhyupapannañca kāryatvasya śarīra ādimatā kartrā vyāpta tvāt ghaṭa ādau tathābhūtasya eva atra siddhiḥ iti vācyam dṛṣṭānta dārṣṭa antikayoḥ utkarṣa apakarṣeṇa pratyavasthānasya sarva anumāna ucchedaka tvāt tathā hi avidyamānasya śarīra ādeḥ āpādanam utkarṣaḥ vidyamānasya ca sarvajña tva ādeḥ apakarṣaṇam apakarṣaḥ na ca sarve dṛṣṭānta dharmā dārṣṭa antike api bhavanti abhede dṛṣṭānta dārṣṭa antika vyavahāra uccheda prasaṅgāt na hi chidi kriyāyāḥ karaṇam kuṭhāra ādi dṛṣṭam iti rūpa upalabdhi kriyāyām api tathā bhavati yathā ca atra apāsta viśeṣeṇa karaṇena kriyāyāḥ vyāpta tvāt anumānam evam īśvara anumāne api iti anutthānam jāti prayogasya 
[I,103,19_I,103,23]	etena yat āha kasyacid hetu mātrasya yadi adhiṣṭhātṛtā ucyate karmabhiḥ sarva bījānām tat siddheḥ siddha sādhanam iti tad apāstam bhavati tathā hi buddhimatī adhiṣṭhātari sādhye katham acetanena karmaṇā siddha sādhanam tasya api acetana tayā adhiṣṭhātra pekṣa tvāt tathā hi sarvam acetanam cetanā adhiṣṭhitam pravartamānam dṛṣṭam yathā tantu ādi tathā ca karma ādi na ca asmad ādi ātmā eva adhiṣṭhāyakaḥ tasya tad viṣaya jñāna abhāvāt tathā ca asmad ādi ātmanaḥ na karma viṣayam jñānam indriya jam na api paramāṇu ādi viṣayam na ca tad abhāve tasya preraka tvam dṛṣṭam na ca acetanasya akasmāt pravṛttiḥ upalabdhā pravṛttau vā pariniṣpanne api kārye pravarteta viveka śūnya tvāt 
[I,104,3]	atha acetana ātmanā adhiṣṭhitam ca kṣīram pravartate tat na go vatsa prayatna abhāve mṛta avasthāyāma pravṛtteḥ sarvañca asmad ādi anadhiṣṭhitam pakṣe antarbhūtam iti na sādhyena eva sādhanasya vyabhicāraḥ sarva anumāna uccheda prasaṅgāt tathā ca acetanāni asmad anyena adhiṣṭhitāni kārya utpattau buddhimat adhiṣṭhitāni acetana tvāt yat yat acetanam tat tat buddhimatā adhiṣṭhitam pravartamānam dṛṣṭam yathā tantu ādi tathā ca etāni tasmāt yathā ukta sādhyāni 
[I,104,8]	atha kartuḥ śarīra ādi mattva upalabdheḥ īśvare api tathā abhāvaḥ kim atra sādhyate yadi śarīra ādimattve api kṣiti ādi kartṛ tvam abhyupagamyate atha śarīra ādimattvāt asarva jñasya na kṣiti ādi kartṛ tvam tarhi kāryasya kartṛ vyabhicārāt aśarīrasya eva kartṛ tvam abhyupeyam na ca śarīra ādimattve pramāṇam asti atha kartṛ tvam eva pramāṇam tat vyāhatam eva kartṛ tvena śarīra ādimat tvam śarīra ādimat tvāt ca kṣiti ādi akartṛ tvam iti 
[I,104,13_I,104,15]	na ca idam svatantra sādhanam āśraya asiddha tvāt tathā hi siddhe kartṛ sadbhāve kartṛ tvasya śarīra ādimattvasya ca pakṣa dharma tvam syāt na ca etat abhyupagatam atha pareṇa kṣiti ādikartā abhyupagataḥ iti aniṣṭa āpādanam etat na yadi pramāṇa āyattaḥ tad upagamaḥ tena eva bādhyamāna tvāt anutthānam viparīta anumānasya na ca etasya anena eva bādhaḥ syāt tad mūla tvāt atha pramāṇam vinā eva abhyupagataḥ pareṇa tarhi pramāṇam vinā prameyasya asiddheḥ kim viparīta anumānena tasya āśraya asiddha tā prasaṅgāt samānañca etat anyeṣu api īśvara pratiṣedha hetuṣu iti 
[I,104,20]	tathā śarīra sambandhe sati niyata deśa tayā yugapada niyata deśam kāryam na syāt tat tu dṛṣṭam atha ekam aniyata deśasya kāryasya utpattyā vyāpi śarīram nityam atīndriyañca iṣyate tat na dṛṣṭa viparīta tvāt parañca aśarīrasya eva kartṛ tvam abhyupeyam iti tathā hi nitya śarīrā sambhavāt tat śarīram tad sampādyam eva iti kim śarīra antareṇa śarīra antara abhyupagame tat anya śarīra yuktena sampādyate iti śarīra paramparāyām upakṣīṇa tvāt bhagavataḥ na anyat kāryam prādurbhavet iti atha śarīrasya eva śarīra kartṛ tvam tad kārya avasare api na bādhyate iti ced tathā sati saṃhāra avasthāyām śarīrasya nāśe punar sarga ādau aśarīrasya akartṛ tve kārya utpattiḥ na syāt iti aśarīrasya eva kartṛ tvam abhyupeyam 
[I,105,4]	atha prayojana apekṣitayā kartṝṇām pravṛtteḥ upalambhāt tad abhāvāt ca īśvare pravṛtti abhāvaḥ iti ced tat asat kārya sadbhāvena kartṛ sadabhāva siddheḥ tasya ca svayam paripūrṇa tvāt para arthā pravṛttiḥ gamyate yat vā pravṛtti śīla tvāt bhagavataḥ na ayam paryanuyogaḥ iti yathā hi bhāsvān prakāśana śīla tvāt padārthān prakāśayati evam itaraḥ api kārya kāraṇa rūpa tvāt kāryam karoti iti 
[I,105,9_I,105,12]	atha aśarīrasya icchā mātreṇa katham preraka tvam yathā asmad ādi ātmanaḥ śarīra ādi preraka tvam iti atha sati eva śarīre prerya preraka tvam iha api sati eva paramāṇau prerya preraka tvam iti samānam atha sisṛkṣā sañjihīrṣā vā maheśvarasya yadi nityā satatam kārya utpattiḥ atha anityā sā api īśvara icchām vinā na bhavati iti aparam icchā antaram tat api anitya tvāt īśvara icchā adhīnam iti anavasthāyām tad sampādane eva upakṣīṇa tvāt bhagavataḥ na kārya antare vyāpāraḥ syāt atha īśvara icchām vinā api īśvara icchā sampādyate tarhi kārya antare api evam astu 
[I,105,16_I,105,19]	atha nityā api sahakāri prāptau kāryam karoti sahakāriṇām api nitya tve satatam kārya utpattiḥ anitya tve vā tān api sahakāriṇaḥ sampādayantī sahakāri antaram apekṣate teṣām api anitya tve punar sahakāri antaram iti anavasthāyām pūrva doṣa anuṣaṅgaḥ na eṣa doṣaḥ cira utpanna adṛṣṭa sadbhāve sati icchāyāḥ kārya karaṇāt tathā hi sahakāri sampādane api anyam sahakāriṇam apekṣate tatra api anyam iti anādi tvam parihāraḥ uktañca icchāyāḥ sṛṣṭau saṃhāre ca sahakāritā iti tathā viśvatas cakṣuḥ uta viśvatomukhaḥ viśvatobāhūruta viśvataspād sam bāhubhyām dhamati saṃpatatraiḥ dyāvābhūmī janayan devaḥ ekaḥ iti āgamena prasiddhaḥ 
[I,105,25_I,106,2]	na ca svarūpa pratipādakānām aprāmāṇyam pramājanaka tvasya sadbhāvāt tathā hi pramājanaka tvena pramāṇasya prāmāṇyam na pravṛtti janaka tvena tat ca iha api asti eva pravṛtti nivṛttī tu puruṣasya sukha duḥkha sādhana tvāt vyavasāye samarthasya arthi tvāt bhavataḥ iti atha vidhi aṅga tvāt amīṣām prādhānyam na svarūpa artha tvāt iti ced tat asat sva artha pratipādaka tvena vidhi aṅga tvāt tathā hi stuteḥ sva artha pratipādaka tvena apravartaka tvam nindāyāḥ ca nivartaka tvam anyathā hi tad artha aparijñāne vihita pratiṣiddheṣu aviśeṣeṇa pravṛtti nivṛttī syātām tathā vidhi vākyasya api sva artha pratipādana dvāreṇa eva puruṣa preraka tvam dṛṣṭam evam svarūpa pareṣu api vākyeṣu syāt vākya rūpa tayā aviśeṣāt viśeṣa hetoḥ ca abhāvāt iti 
[I,106,8]	tathā svarūpa arthānām aprāmāṇye medhyāḥ āpaḥ darbhāḥ pavitram amedhyam maśuciḥ iti evaṃrūpā parijñāne vidhi aṅga tāyām a viśeṣeṇa pravṛtti nivṛtti prasaṅgaḥ na ca etat asti medhyeṣu eva pravartante amedhyeṣu ca nivartante iti upalambhāt tat evam svarūpa arthebhyaḥ vākyebhyaḥ artha svarūpa avabodhe sati iṣṭe pravṛtti darśanāt aniṣṭe ca nivṛttiḥ iti jñāyate svarūpa arthānām pramājanaka tvena pravṛttau nivṛttau vā vidhi sahakāri tvam iti aparijñānena tu pravṛttau ati prasaṅgaḥ 
[I,106,14]	atha svarūpa arthānām prāmāṇye grāvāṇaḥ plavante ityādīnām api yathārtha tā syāt na mukhye bādhaka upapatteḥ yatra hi mukhye bādhakam pramāṇam asti tatra upacāraḥ kalpyate tad abhāve tu prāmāṇyam eva na ca īśvara sadbhāva pratipādakeṣu asti kiñcid bādhakam iti tat evam sṛṣṭi saṃhāra pratipādakānām api vākyānām svarūpe arthe prāmāṇyāt viparīta artha kalpanā anyāyya iti 
[I,106,18]	etena śākyapakṣaḥ api pratiṣiddhaḥ eva tathā hi śākyāḥ api dṛṣṭānta dārṣṭa antikayoḥ utkarṣa apakarṣeṇa pratyavatiṣṭhante tatra ca uktam eva pratisamādhānam iti tat ca jāti uttaram yat kāryam yādṛśa kartrā vyāptam upalabdham yat upalabdheḥ etad kriyā darśinaḥ kena api etat sampāditam iti buddhiḥ bhavati tat eva upalabhyamānam tādṛśam eva kartāram gamayet tat uktam siddham yādṛś adhiṣṭhātṛ bhāva abhāva anuvṛttimat sanniveśa ādi tat yuktam tasmāt yat anumīyate 
[I,106,25]	na ca kṣiti ādi kāryam kartṛ avinābhūtam dṛṣṭam iti katham kartāram gamayet atha sati api bhede kārya śabda sāmyāt anumānam evam tarhi dhūme pāṇḍu tvam agninā vyāptam upalabdham iti prāsāda deśa ādau api upalabhyamānam agnim gamayet tat uktam vastu bhede prasiddhasya śabda sāmyāt abhedinaḥ na yuktā anumitiḥ pāṇḍu dravyāt iva hutāśane 
[I,107,3_I,107,8]	yadi kiñcid kāryam kartṛ avinābhūtam dṛṣṭam iti aparidṛṣṭa avinā bhāvasya api tat pūrvaka tvam syāt tathā sati ghaṭa ādeḥ mṛd vikārasya kulāla pūrvakatva upalambhāt valmīka ādīnām api tat pūrvaka tvam syāt tat uktam anyathā kumbhakāreṇa mṛd vikārasya kasyacid ghaṭa ādeḥ karaṇāt sidhyet valmīkasya api tad kṛtiḥ katham tarhi idam kṣiti ādi kāryam karma jam iti katham hi karma jam jagatām vaicitryam iti uktam tat ca cetanā mānasam karma iti na vijñānāt artha antaram iti 
[I,107,10]	sarvam etat asambaddham sāmānyena kāryatvasya kartṛ vyāpya tvam buddhimatā vyāpteḥ upalambhāt kṣitau api tad siddheḥ sarvañca anumānam anyatra sāmānyena vyāpti grahaṇa apekṣam pravartate iti uktam na kiñcid api anumānam pakṣe vyāpti grahaṇa apekṣam sambhavati iti adūṣaṇam etat kṣiti ādi kāryam na kartṛ vyāptam upalabdham iti na cettham bhūtam kāryam kartṛ vinābhūtam na upalabdham iti anumāna abhāvaḥ iti vācyam sarva anumāna uccheda prasaṅgāt tathā hi kṛtaka tvāt anitya tvam śabde abhyupagatam atra api śakyate vaktum yat śabde kṛtaka tvam tat na anyatra anitya tva avinā bhāvitayā upalabdham iti anumāna abhāvaḥ atha sāmānyena kṛta ka tva anitya tvayoḥ anyatra vyāpti grahaṇe sati anumānam na pakṣe iti ced samānam īśvara anumāne api iti na ca atra śabda sāmyam eva kāryatvasya ubhayatra avyabhicāriṇaḥ sadbhāvāt na ca evam pāṇḍu tvam agneḥ gamakam tasya agnim antareṇa sadbhāvena vyabhicāri tvāt iti evañca valmīka ādau api mṛd vikāra tvam na kulāla pūrvaka tve liṅgam vyabhicārāt tasya hi prākāra iṣṭaka ādiṣu akulāla pūrvakeṣu api sadbhāvāt 
[I,107,22]	yat ca idam karma jam jagatām vaicitryam iti tat iṣyate eva yadi nāma acetana tvāt karma cetanā adhiṣṭhitam kārya karaṇe pravartate iti īśvarasya api sadbhāvaḥ kāryasya api sadbhāvaḥ yadi api cetanena eva karma tathā api na api tasya vidādhāra tvam cetana tvam eva na ca tasya bodhena tādātmyam ātma guṇa tvasya vakṣyamāṇa tvāt na api idam eka śākhā prabhava tva anumānena tulyam tatra hi eka śākhā prabhava tvena hetunā phala antarāṇām pāke sādhye pratyakṣeṇa bādha udayāt aprāmāṇyam yuktam na ca evam īśvara anumānaḥ iti 
[I,108,1_I,108,22]	na ca śarīra ādimattvena kartṛ tvam vyāptam iti sat abhāvāt tasya api abhāvaḥ iti ca vācyam kārya anumānasya ca avyabhicāri tve kartṛ sadbhāva siddheḥ na ca atra vyāpaka an upalabdheḥ bādhaka tvam anumāna stha anumāna antareṇa bādhā yogāt pūrva anumānena ca dharmi sadbhāva siddhau upakṛta viṣaya tvam asiddhau vā na pakṣa dharma tvam atha nityasya avyatireki tvāt sāmarthyañca duranvayam iti akartṛka tvam eva īśvarasya tat na kṣaṇika tva pratiṣedhasya vakṣyamāṇa tvāt ayañca īśvara vādaḥ asmad gurubhiḥ vistareṇa uktaḥ iti na iha pratanyate 
[I,109,3_I,109,8]	idānīm ākāśasya uddeśavataḥ lakṣaṇa parīkṣā artham prakaraṇam ākāśa kāla diśām ekaika tvāt apara jāti abhāve pāribhāṣikyaḥ tisraḥ saṃjñāḥ bhavanti iti etāḥ ca samuccayam vinā ākāśa ādīnām lakṣaṇam iti āha ākāśam kālaḥ diś iti yathāsaṃkhyam tathā hi iti śabdasya pratyekam abhisambandhāt ākāśam iti saṃjñā ākāśe kālaḥ iti kāle diś saṃjñā diśi na tisraḥ api ekasmin iti atha kasmāt imāḥ pāribhāṣikyaḥ dravya guṇa karma ātmakasya nimittasya abhāvāt atha ākāśa tva ādi sāmānya lakṣaṇam nimittam bhaviṣyati iti āha apara jāti abhāve iti aparā hi jāti dravya tva apekṣayā ākāśa tva kāla tva diktva rūpā sā tu na sambhavati eva ākāśa ādeḥ eka tvāt sāmānyasya ca nānā adhiṣṭhāna tvāt iti 
[I,109,12]	na ca ākāśa ādīnām pāribhāṣikyaḥ tisraḥ saṃjñāḥ bhavanti iti sādharmya abhidhānam na sambaddham vaidharmya avasareṇa saṃjñānām paraspara vyāvṛtta tayā vaidharmya rūpa tvāt ekatra abhidhānañca śāstrasya saṅgraha rūpa tvāt iti tathā ca ākāśam iti saṃjñā anādi kāla pravāha āyātā na anyatra sambhavati iti asādhāraṇa tvāt lakṣaṇam etat ca viśeṣaṇam arthāt labhyate tathā hi ākāśam itarasmāt bhidyate anādi kāla pravāha āyāta ākāśa śabda vācya tvāt yaḥ tu itarasmāt anākāśa ādeḥ na bhidyate na ca asau evam yathā kṣiti ādi na ca tathā ākāśaḥ tasmāt bhidyate iti 
[I,109,19]	nanu pāribhāṣikyaḥ saṃjñā na sambhavanti eva nimitta catuṣṭaya abhāvasya iva nimitta tvāt iti ced tathā hi yatra dravya guṇa karma sāmānya ātmakam nimittam na sambhavati tatra eva pravartate na anyatra iti tad abhāvaḥ nimittam na etat evam sva anurakta pratyaya hetoḥ nimittasya atra vivakṣita tvāt yathā hi dravya guṇa sāmānya anuraktaḥ daṇḍī ityādi vyavahāraḥ tathā ca na ayam ākāśa ādi vyavahāraḥ tad abhāva anuraktaḥ iti pāribhāṣikyaḥ eva 
[I,109,24]	pūrvam hi dravyāṇām samavāyi tvam guṇa tvañca uktam tatra kaiḥ guṇaiḥ guṇavat keṣām utpattau samavāyi kāraṇam kiñca guṇa ātmakam lakṣaṇam iti āha tasya guṇāḥ śabda saṃkhyā parimāṇa pṛthaktva saṃyoga vibhāgāḥ iti etaiḥ guṇaiḥ guṇavat atra keṣāñcid utpattau samavāyi kāraṇam śabdaḥ ca asādhāraṇa tvāt lakṣaṇam iti 
[I,110,3_I,110,7]	nanu sarvam etat āśraya asiddham ākāśa sadbhāve pramāṇa abhāvāt na pratyakṣeṇa anupalambhe api anumānena sadbhāva siddheḥ kim anumānam iti āha śabdaḥ iti tathā hi śabdaḥ kvacid āśritaḥ guṇa tvāt yaḥ yaḥ guṇaḥ sa sa kvacid āśritaḥ yathā rūpa ādiḥ tathā ca ayam guṇaḥ tasmāt āśritaḥ iti atha pṛthivī ādeḥ guṇaḥ bhaviṣyati iti āha na sparśavat viśeṣa guṇaḥ asmad ādi pratyakṣa tve satya kāraṇa guṇa pūrvaka tvāt yaḥ yaḥ asmad ādi pratyakṣa tve satya kāraṇa pūrvakaḥ sa sa sparśavatām viśeṣa guṇaḥ na bhavati yathā sukha ādiḥ tathā ca ayam yathā ukta sādhanaḥ tasmāt sparśavatām viśeṣa guṇaḥ na bhavati iti 
[I,110,11^1]	nanu ca atra viśeṣa guṇa pratiṣedhe sādhye sāmānya guṇa prāptiḥ viśeṣa pratiṣedhasya śeṣa abhyanujñāyām sāmarthya upalabdheḥ atha sāmānya guṇa pratiṣedhaḥ tathā api viśeṣa guṇa prāptiḥ iti na etat evam pratiyogi apekṣa tvāt pakṣa ādi vyavasthāyāḥ tathā hi pareṇa kṣiti ādi viśeṣa guṇa tvam śabdasya abhyupagatam tasya eva pratiṣedhaḥ sāmānya guṇa tvañca na iṣṭam eva śeṣa abhyanujñā tu yatra ubhayoḥ pramāṇena prasiddhiḥ tatra eka pratiṣedhe anyasya apratiṣiddhasya avasthānam yathā darśanam savya itara cakṣurbhyām saṃpādyam dṛṣṭam iti eka pratiṣedhe anyasya apratiṣedhāt avasthānam iti na ca evam śabdasya kṣiti ādi sāmānya guṇa tvam parasya siddham iti adūṣaṇam etat atas eva yadi api saṃyoga vibhāga ādeḥ asmad ādi pratyakṣa tve satya kāraṇa guṇa pūrvaka tvam 
[I,110,11^2]	tathā api sparśavat viśeṣa guṇa tvam na asti iti sa pakṣe antar bhāvāt anaikāntika tva abhāvaḥ rūpa ādayaḥ ca vipakṣāḥ te ca kāraṇa guṇa pūrvakāḥ iti sādhana śūnyāḥ eva tathā api pārthiva paramāṇu rūpa ādayaḥ akāraṇa guṇa pūrvakāḥ sparśavatām viśeṣa guṇāḥ ca iti vyabhicāraḥ tad artham asmad ādi pratyakṣa tve sati iti viśeṣaṇam te tu yoginām eva pratyakṣāḥ iti asmad ādi pratipādanāya śāstrasya ārambhāt asmad ādi viśeṣaṇantu labhyate 
[I,110,23]	anye tu saṃyoga ādibhiḥ vyabhicāra parihārāya śeṣa apratijñā vākyāt uddhṛtya viśeṣa padam hetu padena saha sambandhayanti tathā hi na sparśavatām guṇaḥ śabdaḥ asmad ādi pratyakṣa tve viśeṣa guṇa tve ca satya kāraṇa guṇa pūrvaka tvāt sukha ādi vat atra hi sāmānyatas viśeṣa yogāt sāmānya pratiṣedhāt viśeṣa pratiṣedhaḥ bhavati eva brāhmaṇya niṣedhāt vājasana ādi pratiṣedha vat iti atra ca pratijñā vākye samāsa antargatam padam hetu padena katham sambadhyate iti cintyam 
[I,111,3]	nanu akāraṇa guṇa pūrvaka tvāt iti hetuḥ asiddhaḥ para dṛṣṭyā saṃyogāt vibhāgāt śabdāt ca kāraṇa guṇāt śabdasya niṣpatti abhyupagamāt tathā hi śabdasya kāraṇam ākāśam tad guṇāḥ ca saṃyoga ādayaḥ kāraṇa guṇāḥ te kāraṇam asya iti kāraṇa guṇa pūrvaka tvam na evam abhiprāya aparijñānāt tathā ca ayam arthaḥ vivakṣitaḥ samavāyi kāraṇeṣu guṇāḥ kāraṇa guṇāḥ te pūrvam kāraṇam yasya guṇasya asau kāraṇa guṇa pūrvakaḥ yathā paṭa rūpa ādiḥ tantu rūpa ādi pūrvakaḥ iti na ca evam śabdasya ākāśasya akārya tvena samavāyi kāraṇa guṇa abhāvāt iti 
[I,111,9_I,111,12]	atha sva dṛṣṭyā kāraṇa guṇa pūrvaka tvam tathā ca bherī śabdaḥ tad avayava śabda pūrvakaḥ tathā śaṅkha śabdaḥ ca iti na teṣām anupalambhāt tathā hi śaṅkha śabda kāle śaṅkha avayava śabdāḥ na anubhūyante iti yathā paṭa rūpa anubhava kāle tantu rūpāṇām anubhavaḥ iti atha abhibhūta tvāt anupalambhaḥ na tad astitve pramāṇa abhāvāt tathā hi tad avayava śabdāḥ cira utpannāḥ eva avayavini śabdam ārabhante iti na pramāṇam asti yadi vā avayava śabdānām avayavi śabdaiḥ abhibhūta tvāt vidyamānānām api anupalambhaḥ tadā tad abhāve sati tad upalambhaḥ syāt rāsabha śabda abhāve vīṇā śabdasya iva yathā hi vādyamānāyām vīṇāyām rāsabha sannidhau vidyamānasya api vīṇā śabdasya abhibhavāt anupalambhaḥ punar abhibhāvaka abhāvāt upalambhaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ na ca evam avayavi śabdānām asti saṃvedanam 
[I,111,18_I,111,22]	na ca kāraṇa guṇa pūrvakeṣu kāraṇa abhibhāvaka tvam dṛṣṭam tathā śabda abhibhave api iti api tu śabdasya tīvrasya grahaṇāt mandasya agrahaṇam iti na ca avayavi śabda upalambha kāle eva avayava śabdānām agrahaṇam pūrvam api anupalambhāt yāvat dravya bhāvi tvañca kāraṇa guṇa pūrvakāṇām na ca satya kārya vāda balena avayava avayavi śabdānām sadbhāve api vyañjaka abhāvāt anupalambhaḥ iti vācyam tad niṣedhasya vakṣyamāṇa tvāt 
[I,111,24_I,112,3]	na ca avayava śabdānām avayavi śabda vailakṣaṇyāt asamavāyi tvam vācyam tasya hi samāna jātīyeṣu atyanta vijātīyeṣu ca darśanāt yathā hi kāraṇa gatāt rūpāt śuklatamāt kārye tathābhūtam rūpam evam rasa ādiṣu api iti tathā atyanta vijātīyasya asamavāyi kāraṇa tvam yathā pracaya ākhyaḥ saṃyogaḥ saṃkhyā ca parimāṇa utpattau na ca evam śabdaḥ tathā hi bherī śabde gambhīraḥ tad avayava śabdāḥ ca tad vidharmāṇaḥ iti evam śaṅkha ādi śabdeṣu api ūhyam na ca sarvasya sukha duḥkha moha ātmaka tvāt sukha ādi dṛṣṭāntāt sādhya sādhanam iti mantavyam pradhāna vāda pratiṣedhāt sukha ādīnāñca ātma guṇa tvāt 
[I,112,5]	tathā na sparśavatām guṇaḥ śabdaḥ asmad ādi pratyakṣa tve satya yāvat dravya bhāvi tvāt yaḥ yaḥ asmad ādi pratyakṣa tve satya yāvat dravya bhāvī sa sa sparśavatām viśeṣa guṇaḥ na bhavati yathā sukha ādiḥ tathā ca ayam asmad ādi pratyakṣa tve satya yāvat dravya bhāvī tasmāt na sparśavatām viśeṣa guṇaḥ iti ye ca sparśavatām viśeṣa guṇāḥ te asmad ādi prayakṣa tve sati yāvat dravya bhāvinaḥ yathā rūpa ādayaḥ atra api pārthiva paramāṇu rūpa ādi vyavaccheda artham asmad ādi pratyakṣa tve sati iti padam na ca saṃyoga ādibhiḥ vyabhicāraḥ pūrva ukta nyāyāt na api yāvat dravya bhāvi tvam śabdasya rūpa ādi vat apratīyamāna tvāt 
[I,112,12]	tathā āśrayāt anyatra upalabdheḥ ca iti hetu antaram ca samuccaye na param pūrva uktābhyām āśrayāt anyatra upalabdheḥ ca na sparśavat viśeṣa guṇaḥ śabdaḥ iti nanu śabdasya yathā ākāśam āśrayaḥ tasmāt anyatra upalabdhiḥ asiddhā tena eva upalambhāt na para abhyupagamena bherī ādeḥ āśraya śabdena abhidhānāt tathā hi bherī śabdaḥ tad guṇaḥ na bhavati tatas anyatra upalabhyamāna tvāt yaḥ yaḥ tatas anyatra upalabhyate sa sa tad guṇaḥ na bhavati yathā sukha ādiḥ yaḥ ca tad guṇaḥ sa tatra eva upalabhyate yathā rūpa ādiḥ na ca tathā śabdaḥ tasmāt tad guṇaḥ na bhavati iti na ca siddham etat śabdasya tatra eva upalambhāt yathā hi bheryām śabdaḥ iti pratibhāsaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ rūpavat na ca anyathā bhavitum arhati iti 
[I,112,20]	na ca śrotrasya tatra āsannidhānam āhaṅkārika tvena vyāpakasya tatra sadbhāvāt na api sarva śabdānām upalabdhi prasaṅgaḥ adṛṣṭa vaśena niyata deśaḥ eva vṛtteḥ ātma lābhāt iti avyāpakasya vā tad deśam yāvat parimāṇa abhyupagamaḥ yatra āśraya pratibhāsā bhāvaḥ tatra śabdasya eva sva āśraya parimāṇa dvāreṇa śrotra deśam āgamanam 
[I,112,24_I,113,1]	tat etat asāmpratam iha bheryā śabdaḥ iti pratibhāsasya santāna anumāna dvāreṇa adhiṣṭhāna deśaḥ eva pratibhāsāt nanu ca atra viśeṣa hetoḥ abhāvāt niścaya abhāvaḥ eva kim tad sthasya eva śabdasya upalambhaḥ santāna anumitasya vā iti na tad sthasya eva upalambhaḥ kvacid āśraya viyuktasya api śrotra deśe pratibhāsāt na ca evam sparśavatām guṇāḥ ca āśraya viyuktāḥ gṛhyante iti na asiddhatvam hetoḥ 
[I,113,5]	atha sparśa vat guṇa tve api gandhasya iva tad āśraya āgamanāt upalambhaḥ bhaviṣyati iti ced na gandhasya sparśa vat guṇa tva prasiddhau āśraya avicchedena ghrāṇa adhiṣṭhāna deśaḥ eva pratibhāsāt sūkṣmasya tad ādhārasya āgamanam yuktam na ca evam śabdasya tathā sūkṣma dravya ādhārasya bherī śabdasya āgamanam eva na yuktam bheryā samavetasya utpādāt na hi anyatra samavetam anyatra samavaiti iti samavetyavādena tu āgamane api tad avayava śabdāḥ bherī śabdāḥ ca iti pratibhāsaḥ eva prasaṅgaḥ sūkṣma dravya samavāyasya aviśeṣāt 
[I,113,11]	tathā bherī daṇḍa abhidhātāt bheryām utpannaḥ śabdaḥ na āgacchati eva āśrayasya tatra avasthānāt tad avayaveṣu ca sūkṣmeṣu ye jātāḥ śabdāḥ tad āśrayasya āgamanāt āgacchanti iti abhyupagame bherī ādi gambhīra dhvaneḥ aśravaṇam eva syāt na ca ahaṅkārika tvāt vyāpakasya bherī ādi deśe vṛttiḥ ghaṭate iti mantavyam pūrvam eva ahaṅkārika tva pratiṣedhāt na ca śrotreṇa bherī ādi deśa grahaṇam sambhavati iti tad avacchedena śabdasya grahaṇa abhāva prasaṅgaḥ 
[I,113,16_I,113,19]	atha prasiddha samayasya śabda śravaṇāt āśraya anumāne sati ayam bherī śabdaḥ iti avacchedena pratibhāsate iti ced āyātaḥ tarhi madīyam panthānam katham śabda śravaṇāt santāna dvāreṇa āśraya anumitau iha bheryām śabdaḥ iti pratibhāsā abhyupagamāt tat evam āśrayāt anyatra upalabhyamāna tvāt na sparśavat viśeṣa guṇaḥ śabdaḥ iti siddham 
[I,113,20]	tathā ekasmin eva vādye vādyamāne bahūnām ṣaḍja ādīnām upalambhāt na tad guṇa tvam tathā hi yadi ātodya guṇaḥ syāt śabdaḥ katham bahūnām śabdānām samāna indriya grāhyāṇām avibhuni dravye sadbhāvaḥ syāt atha citra rūpavat etat syāt na tatra eka rūpasya ārambhāt tathā hi nānā rūpāṇi ekam kāryam ārabhantaḥ iti uktam na ca evam nānā śabdaiḥ ekaḥ śabdaḥ ārabhyamāṇaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ iti na ca atra citra rūpavat ekasmin kāle citra śabda pratibhāsaḥ sambhavati krameṇa pratibhāsanāt tathā rūpa ādi vat citra utpāde abhyupagate yugapad upalabdhi prasaṅgaḥ na ca krameṇa abhivyaktiḥ sadbhāve pramāṇa abhāvāt iti ukta tvāt saṃyogāt ca krameṇa utpatti abhyupagame śabdasya na sparśavat viśeṣa guṇa tvam tad vaidharmyāt iti alam ati vistareṇa 
[I,114,3]	nanu ca atra hetu upanyāsa anantaram pratijñopanya āsāt avayava vyatyaye kim prayojanam śāstre na ayam niyamaḥ iti upadarśanam eva tathā hi avayava viparyāsa vacanam aprāpta kālam nāma nigraha sthānam jalpaḥ eva na śāstre iti upadarśayati udāharaṇa ādi a vayava lābha artham iti anye tat ca īṣadvyatyayam vinā api artha kathanāt eva tasya anekadhā abhyupagāt 
[I,114,8]	nanu ekena eva pramāṇena arthasya paricchedāt ekasmin arthe aneka hetu upanyāsaḥ vyarthaḥ eva yat vā pramāṇa antara upanyāsāni atha anupapattyā jñāyate na prāktanasya artha paricchede sāmarthyam apūrva artha paricchedaka tvam vā adhigata arthasya anuvādaka tvāt tathā hi adhigate api arthe pramāṇa antara pravṛttau aviśrāma prasaṅgaḥ tasmāt anyaḥ anya vyāvṛtta viṣaya tvāt pramāṇānām aneka hetu upanyāsaḥ parijñānāya eva na etat evam sarvatra vyavasthā anabhyupagamāt tathā hi ekasmin eva arthe aneka upāya darśanam śāstre na doṣāya tasya hi para anugrāhaka tvāt tathā vibhinna abhiprāyāḥ pratipādyāḥ iti aneka hetu upanyāsāt kaścid kenacid alpa prayāsena eva pratipadyate iti na ca atra kasyacid aprāmāṇyam sarveṣām api pramājanaka tvāt 
[I,114,16]	na ca pramāṇa paramparā prasaṅgaḥ paricchinne api arthe avaśyam pramāṇa antara upanyāsa anabhyupagamāt tathā hi yatra pramāṇa antara sadbhāvaḥ tatra eva tad apekṣā na tad abhāve api iti yathā śabdena avagate anumānena api bubhutsite anumānena api adhigate pratyakṣeṇa iti tathā pratyakṣe api ekena karaṇena upalabdhe punar karaṇa antareṇa iti tathā ekasmin sukha sādhane arthe aneka pramāṇa pravṛttau sukha atiśayaḥ ca prayojanam iti 
[I,114,21_I,114,23]	na ca anadhigata artha gantṛ tvam pramāṇa sāmānya lakṣaṇam pratyabhijñā na ādeḥ aprāmāṇya prasaṅgāt tathā hi adhigataḥ eva arthe pratyabhijñānam anumānañca pravartate iti vakṣyāmaḥ atha eka deśa vṛtti viśeṣa guṇa tvāt kṣaṇika viśeṣa guṇa tvāt ca sukha ādi vat ātma guṇaḥ bhaviṣyati iti āha na bāhya indriya pratyakṣa tvāt ityādi 
[I,115,1]	atha prāktana anumānasya nirduṣṭa tāyām anumāna antarasya anutthānam eva na ātma guṇa tve sati śabdasya śrotreṇa aparicchedāt āśraya asiddha tvam anumānayoḥ tathā hi śrotram ātmā na bhavati akartṛ tvāt na api antaḥkaraṇam eva śrotram tasya hi bahis karaṇa tvāt abhyupagame vā yāvat sukha ādi upalabdhiḥ tāvat śabda upalabdhyā bhavitavyam iti bādhiryam na syāt 
[I,115,6]	atha śabda grahaṇam antaḥkaraṇasya uparata vyāpārāt evam tarhi sukha ādīnām agrahaṇam syāt na ca karaṇam cakṣuḥ ādi ekatā uparata vyāpāram anyatra artha prakāśakam dṛṣṭam kṣiti āt ivāyu paryantañca śrotram na bhavati eva ghrāṇa ādi sampādane sāmarthya avadhāraṇāt dikkālayoḥ ca śrotra rūpa tā na sambhavati eva bhautika tvāt bāhya indriyāṇām pāriśeṣyāt anyat śrotram tena ca ātma guṇasya śabdasya agrahaṇam eva syāt iti āśraya asiddha tvam gṛhyate ca bāhya indriyeṇa śabdaḥ tasmāt ātma guṇaḥ na bhavati iti tathā ca śabdaḥ na ātma guṇaḥ bāhya indriya pratyakṣa tvāt yaḥ yaḥ bāhya indriya pratyakṣaḥ sa saḥ ātma guṇaḥ na bhavati yathā rūpa ādiḥ tathā ca ayam bāhya indriya pratyakṣaḥ tasmāt ātma guṇaḥ na bhavati iti vaidharmyeṇa tu sukha ādayaḥ tatas ca na ātma guṇaḥ śabdaḥ ātma antara grāhya tvāt rūpa ādi vat ātma guṇāḥ ca ātma antara grāhyāḥ na bhavanti yathā sukha ādayaḥ 
[I,115,16]	nanu śabdasya ātma antara grāhya tvam vyakti apekṣayā na sambhavati eva tathā hi yā śabda vyaktiḥ ekasmin śrotre samaveta upajātāḥ na sā anyatra iti jāti apekṣayā tu sukha ādeḥ api ātma antara grāhya tvāt iti aneka antika tvam na etat evam yena ātmanā kriyate śabdaḥ tasmāt anyena api gṛhyate na ca evam sukha ādiḥ iti tathā hi tīvratara abhighātāt ekā śabda vyaktiḥ mahāntam ākāśa deśam vyāpya upajāyate iti anekaiḥ upalabhyate eva na ca avyāpya vṛtti tvena virodhaḥ sva āśraya avyāpaka tvāt na ca santāna abhyupagamaḥ virudhyate tīvratara ādi bheda bhinnānām śabdānām utpatti abhyupagamāt tathā hi asti tīvratara abhighātāt ekā śabda vyaktiḥ mahāntam ākāśa deśam kalpitam vyāpya upajāyate tatas tīvrataraḥ ityādi krameṇa anubhavāt tathā vyakti apekṣāyām ātma antara grāhya tvam na sambhavati iti bruvataḥ santāna abhyupagamāt apasiddhānta prasaṅgaḥ iti 
[I,115,25]	na ca itas api ātma guṇaḥ śabdaḥ ātmani asamaveta tvāt rūpa ādi vat ye ca ātma guṇāḥ te tatra eva samavetāḥ sukha ādayaḥ iti atha ātmani asamaveta tvam sādhyāt na viśiṣyate iti āha ahaṅkāreṇa vibhakta grahaṇāt ca iti tathā hi na ātmani samavetaḥ śabdaḥ ahaṅkāreṇa vibhakta grahaṇāt rūpa ādi vat te ca ātma nimittam vinā na pravartante iti prayoga darśanāt ātma upakāri tvam nimittam iti kalpyate 
[I,116,3]	atha diś kāla manasām guṇaḥ bhaviṣyati iti tad niṣedha artham āha śrotra grāhya tvāt ityādi tathā ca śabdaḥ na diś kāla manasām guṇaḥ śrotra grāhya tvāt yat yat śrotra grāhyam tat tat diś kāla manasām guṇaḥ na bhavati yathā śabda tva ādi tathā ca śabdaḥ śrotra grāhyaḥ tasmāt diś kāla manasām guṇaḥ na bhaviṣyati iti ye tu tad guṇāḥ te tu śrotra grāhyāḥ na bhavanti yathā saṃkhyā ādayaḥ iti tathā ca diś kāla manaḥ vyatiriktasya śrotrasya pratipādanāt tad tad guṇa tve tena grahaṇa abhāva prasaṅgaḥ tathā hi diś kālābhyām na sambaddham iti tad samavetasya śabdasya agrahaṇam 
[I,116,10]	manasaḥ ca aṇu parimāṇa tvāt tad guṇa tve gambhīra dhvaneḥ aśravaṇa prasaṅgaḥ tad abhāve ca kvacid pradeśe śabdasya anutpattiḥ syāt na ca kāryeṇa eva kāraṇasya tatra sadbhāvaḥ kāryasya anyathā api bhāvāt na api vibhu dravya viśeṣa guṇānām sukha ādīnām iva paramāṇu viśeṣa guṇānām indriyeṇa upalambhaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ paramāṇu parimāṇañca manaḥ tat evam diś kāla manaḥ guṇa tve śabdasya śrotra grāhya tvam na syāt iti bādha kañcā idam vaiśeṣika guṇa bhāvāt ca iti tathā viśeṣa guṇaḥ eva vaiśeṣikaḥ tasya bhāvāt iti tathā hi diś kāla manasām pakṣīkaraṇe vaiśeṣika guṇa abhāvaḥ asiddhaḥ syāt asya ca viśeṣa guṇa tvāt iti vyatireka mukhena anyā hetuḥ vyākhyāyate diś kāla manasām vaiśeṣika guṇa abhāvaḥ iti ukte śabdaḥ tu viśeṣa guṇaḥ iti hetuḥ labhyate eva tathā ca śabdaḥ diś kāla manasām guṇaḥ na bhavati viśeṣa guṇa tvāt yaḥ yaḥ viśeṣa guṇaḥ sa sa diś kāla manasām guṇaḥ na bhavati yathā rūpa ādiḥ tathā ca ayam viśeṣa guṇaḥ tasmāt na diś kāla manasām guṇaḥ śabdaḥ iti 
[I,116,21]	anye tu na diś kāla manasām guṇaḥ śabdaḥ iti sādhye vaiśeṣika guṇa abhāvaḥ sādhyāt na viśiṣyate iti manyamānāḥ hetu antaram bruvate tathā hi na diś kāla manasām guṇaḥ śabdaḥ guṇa tvena guṇinaḥ liṅga tvāt yaḥ yaḥ guṇa tvena guṇinaḥ liṅgaḥ sa sa diś kāla manasām guṇaḥ na bhavati yathā sukha ādayaḥ tathā ca ayam śabdaḥ guṇa tvena guṇinaḥ liṅgaḥ tasmāt tad guṇaḥ na bhavati iti ye tu dikkālayoḥ liṅgam na te guṇa tvena guṇinaḥ liṅgam yathā pūrva apara ādi pratyayāḥ yugapad ādi pratyayāḥ ca iti te hi tad viśiṣṭa tvāt tayoḥ liṅgam guṇa tvena ca ātmanaḥ tathā yugapad a ādi śabdāḥ pūrva apara ādi śabdāḥ ca yadi api tad viśiṣṭha tvāt tayoḥ liṅgam tathā api guṇa tvena āśraya antara anumāpakāḥ iti alam ati vistareṇa 
[I,117,3]	manaḥ guṇa tve ca uktam eva dūṣaṇam iti pariśeṣāt guṇaḥ bhūtvā ākāśasya adhigame paricchede kartavye liṅgam iti pariśeṣaḥ tu prasakta pratiṣedhe anyatra aprasaṅgāt tat evam sādhanam vyatireka avyabhicāreṇa eva viṣaya vyavasthāpanāya alam tathā hi śabdaḥ pṛthivī udaka jvalana pavana dikkāla ātma manaḥ vyatirikta dravya āśrayaḥ tad vṛtti bādhaka pramāṇa sadbhāve sati guṇa tvāt yaḥ tu tad vyatirikta āśrayaḥ na bhavati na ca asau tad vṛtti bādhaka pramāṇa sadbhāve sati guṇaḥ yathā rūpa ādiḥ na ca tathā śabdaḥ tasmāt tad vyatirikta dravya āśrayaḥ śabdaḥ iti siddham ākāśam tat kim ekam uta anekam iti āha śabda liṅga aviśeṣāt eka tvam siddham śabdaḥ hi liṅgam ākāśasya aviśiṣṭa tayā nānātva apratipādakam iti 
[I,117,11]	nanu asiddham aviśiṣṭa tvam vicitra tvāt śabdānām tathā hi kārya vaicitryam kāraṇa vaicitryam vinā na syāt iti tīvra ādi bheda bhinnānām śabdānām vicitreṇa eva kāraṇena bhavitavyam iti nānātva siddhiḥ tad āśrayasya yadi ca kāraṇa vaicitryam vinā api kārya vaicitryam iṣyeta paramāṇūnām api cāturvidhyam na syāt tatra api ekasmāt eva kāraṇāt vicitram kṣiti ādi kāryam bhaviṣyati iti atha tatra kārya vaicitryeṇa kāraṇa vaicitrya anumānam iti ced tad śabda vaicitrye api samānam iti alam 
[I,117,17]	tat asat sahakāri vaicitryeṇa api śabda vaicitrya upalabdheḥ na tad āśrayasya nānātvam tathā ca tīvratamāt abhighātāt tīvratamaḥ śabdaḥ mandāt ca mandaḥ ityādi na ca kṣiti ādau api evam astu iti vācyam tatra hi caturvidham kāryam itaretara vyāvṛttāt upādānāt utpadyamānam dṛṣṭam iti tad jātīyāḥ paramāṇavaḥ caturvidhāḥ eva pratīyante kārya vaicitryantu sāmagrī vaicitryāt eva tatra kvacid kāraṇa bhedaḥ kvacid karma bhedaḥ anyasya ca iti yathāsambhavam grāhyam atra kāraṇa bhedena api śabda vaicitrya upapatteḥ na samavāyi kāraṇāt bhedaḥ iti satyam etat śabda liṅga aviśiṣṭa tvāt nānātva apratipādanakam iti 
[I,117,24]	atha nānātva aprasiddhau api eka tvam pramāṇam vinā na sidhyati iti abhidheyam pramāṇam iti ced na dravya tvāt eva saṃkhyā asadbhāva siddhau nānātve pramāṇa abhāvāt eka tvam eva sidhyati iti tathā saṃkhyā anantaram parimāṇam avasara prāptam parityajya krama atikrameṇa pṛthaktva nirūpaṇam kasmāt iti āha tad anuvidhānāt tena ekatvena anuvidhānam sāhacaryam yatra hi ekatvam tatra avaśyam eka pṛthaktvam iti na tu evam parimāṇe api tad anuvidhānam asti eva tathā hi yatra ekatvam tatra avaśyam eka pṛthaktvam bhavati iti viśeṣa anuvidhānam na ca evam yatra ekatvam tatra avaśyam aṇu tvam sthūla tvam vā iti viśeṣa anuvidhānam asti iti pūrvam pṛthaktvam nirūpyate 
[I,118,5]	tathā parama mahat parimāṇam ākāśe kutas pramāṇāt iti āha vibhava vacanāt iti vibhavān mahān ākāśaḥ tathā ca ātmā tad abhāvāt aṇu manaḥ iti sūtre darśayati vibhavāt kāraṇāt mahān ākāśaḥ iti sāmānya śabdena asya arthāt parama mahat tvam vivakṣitam tathā hi vibhunaḥ dravyasya parama mahat tvam siddham ātma ādau iti iha api tathā sādhyate ākāśam parama mahad vibhu tvāt ātma vat iti sarveṣāñca avibhūnām pakṣīkaraṇe kevala vyatireka anumānam ākāśa ādīnām ātma paryantānām parama mahat tvam vibhu tvāt iti ukte yeṣāntu parama mahat tvam na asti na teṣām vibhu tvam iti vyatirekaḥ 
[I,118,12]	atha kim idam vibhu tvam sarvaiḥ bhūtaiḥ saṃyogaḥ iti anye tu sarvatra upajātānām śabdānām ākāśe samavāyaḥ tad sadbhāve apūrṇa udreka tā vibhu tvam iti manyante yat vā aṇu parimāṇān adhikaraṇa tve sati nitya dravya tvāt parama mahat tvam iti sādhyate tathā śabda kāraṇa vacanāt saṃyoga vibhāgau iti saṃyogāt vibhāgāt śabdāt ca śabda niṣpattiḥ iti sūtram darśayati tathā hi saṃyoga vibhāgau śabda utpatteḥ asamavāyi kāraṇam iti abhidhānāt ākāśe samavāyaḥ labhyate anyathā hi pratyāsatteḥ abhāvāt asamavāyi kāraṇa tvam na syāt na ca anyat asamavāyi kāraṇam asti iti yatas evam guṇavat ākāśam atas guṇavat tvāt anāśrita tvāt ca dravyam paramāṇu vat iti tathā hi paramāṇoḥ guṇavat tvam anāśrita tvañca dṛṣṭam dravya tvañca asti adravye ca etat na sambhavati iti 
[I,118,21]	atha kim ākāśam nityam uta anityam iti āha samāna asamāna jātīya kāraṇā bhāvāt ca nityam tathā hi na samāna jātīyam samavāyi kāraṇam ākāśasya eka tvāt na api asamāna jātīyam asamavāyi kāraṇam asti samāna jātīya abhāvena tad saṃyogasya api abhāvāt na ca samavāyi asamavāyi kāraṇam vinā vastu bhūtasya kāryasya utpattiḥ sambhavati iti akārya tvāt nitya tvam siddham ākāśasya atas ca sarva prāṇinām śabda upalabdhau nimittam kāraṇam ākāśasya eka tve api aneka artha kriyā kāri tvam darśayati na ca sattā mātreṇa ākāśam śabda upalabdheḥ kāraṇam sarvatra sarva prāṇinām aviśeṣeṇa śabda upalabdhi prasaṅgaḥ sarva śabdānām ākāśe samavāya aviśeṣāt atas āha śrotra bhāvena śrotra tvena iti 
[I,119,3]	kim tat śrotram iti āha śrotram punar śravaṇa vivara saṃjakaḥ nabhaḥ deśaḥ iti śrūyate anena iti śravaṇam tat ca tad vivarañcā iti tathā uktam śravaṇa vivaram iti saṃjñā yasya nabhaḥ deśasya asau śravaṇa vivara saṃjñakaḥ karṇa śaṣkulī saṃyoga upalakṣitaḥ ākāśaḥ iti tathā śabda nimitta upabhoga prāpaka dharma adharma upanibaddhaḥ iti śabdaḥ nimittam yasya asau tathā uktaḥ sa ca asau upabhogaḥ ca tam prāpyate iti tad prāpakaḥ ca tau dharma adhamau tābhyām upanibaddhaḥ saha kṛtaḥ iti 
[I,119,9]	nanu evam api karṇa śaṣkulī a ākāśa saṃyoga upalakṣita viśiṣṭa adṛṣṭa upagṛhītaḥ nabhaḥ deśaḥ tasmāt artha antaram na bhavati iti sarva śabda upalabdhiḥ syāt na etat evam karṇa śaṣkulī saṃyoga upalakṣitasya nabhasaḥ śrotra tve tasya api avyāpya vṛtti tayā na sarveṣām grahaṇam yadi api karṇa śaṣkulī saṃyoga eka artha samavāyi tvāt śabdānām tathā api viśiṣṭa pratyāsatteḥ abhāvāt agrahaṇam yaḥ hi karṇa śaṣkulī saṃyogasya sānnidhya bhāj śabdaḥ saḥ eva upalabhyate na ca evam sarva śabdāḥ teṣām avyāpya vṛtti tvāt 
[I,119,15_I,119,18]	na ca karṇa śaṣkulī saṃyoga avaruddha nabhaḥ deśa vyatirikta deśe sarveṣām utpāda nāda grahaṇam eva iti vācyam śabda upalambhāni atha anupapattyā santāna nyāyena śrotra deśam āgatasya pratipādyamāna tvāt iti alam atha kasmāt badhirāṇām karṇa śaṣkulī saṃyoga avaruddha nabhaḥ deśa sadbhāve api śabda agrahaṇam saha kārya bhāvāt iti āha tasya ca nitya tve sati upabhoga nibandhakaḥ ityādi śabda upalabdhau sahakāriṇaḥ adṛṣṭasya abhāvāt śabda upalabdhiḥ na bhavati iti bādhiryam upapadyate iti 
[I,119,21_I,120,11]	idānīm uddeśavataḥ kālasya lakṣaṇa parīkṣā artham kālaḥ parāpara vyatikara yaugapadya ayaugapadi acira kṣipra pratyaya liṅgaḥ ityādi prakaraṇam atra ca kāla sadbhāva pratipādakam eva liṅga m itarasmāt bhedakam bhavati iti manyamānaḥ lakṣaṇa antaram na avocat tathā hi kālaḥ itarasmāt bhidyate parāpara vyatikara yaugapadya ayaugapadi acira kṣipra pratyaya liṅga tvāt yaḥ tu na bhidyate na ca asau ukta liṅgaḥ yathā kṣiti ādiḥ na ca tathā kālaḥ tasmāt bhidyate iti vyavahāraḥ vā sādhyate vivāda gocaratā āpannam dravyam kālaḥ iti vyavahartavyam parāpara vyatikara ādi liṅga tvāt iti 
[I,120,16]	atha pratibandha anupalabdheḥ katham etāni kāla sadbhāve liṅgam bhavanti viśiṣṭa kārya tayā viśiṣṭam kāryam viśiṣṭāt kāraṇāt utpadyamānam dṛṣṭam parāpara vyatikara yaugapadyāyaga padi acira kṣipra pratyayāḥ ca viśiṣṭam kāryam iti viśiṣṭa kāraṇa pūrvaka tvam sādhyate tathā ca para aparayoḥ dikkṛtayoḥ vyatikaraḥ viparyayaḥ gṛhyate yatra hi diś vivakṣayā utpannam paratvam tatra eva aparatvam yatra eva aparatvam tatra eva paratvam utpadyamānam dṛṣṭam iti artha antarañca vyavahartṛ nimittāt vyatirekaḥ sambhavati iti tathā ca adhama jātīye diś vivakṣayā parasmin sthavira piṇḍe balī palita ādi sānnidhyam apekṣamāṇasya utkṛṣṭa jātīyam yuvānam avadhim kṛtvā itarasmāt paraḥ viprakṛṣṭaḥ ayam iti buddhiḥ bhavati tām apekṣya pareṇa kāla pradeśena yogāt paratvam iti sthavirañca avadhim kṛtvā utkṛṣṭa jātīye yūni para digbhāga vyavasthite api rūḍha śmaśru kārkaśyam apekṣyamānasya sannikṛṣṭā buddhiḥ utpadyate tām apekṣya apareṇa kāla pradeśena yogāt aparatvasya utpattiḥ iti 
[I,121,3_I,121,6]	atra diś sampādita para tva vailakṣaṇyāt na tat eva nimittam na api nikṛṣṭa jātīya tayā jāti kṛtam paratvam sambhavati na ca kṣiti ādeḥ anyatamam nimittam sāmarthya an avadhāraṇāt yaḥ tu śiṣyate sa kālaḥ iti nanu ekasmin eva dine pākaja utpatti nyāyena piṇḍayoḥ samutpādāt katham paratva aparatvam utpatteḥ prabhṛti āditya parivartana apekṣayā tathā hi janmanaḥ prabhṛti ekasya āditya parivartanāni bhūyāṃsi iti paratvam anyasya ca alpīyāṃsi iti aparatvam 
[I,121,9_I,121,13]	atha āditya parivartanam eva astu kim kālena iti ced na yugapad ādi pratyaya anumeya tvāt na ca āditya parivartanāt eva yugapad ādi pratyayāḥ sambhavanti iti ekasmin eva āditya parivartane sarveṣām anutpādāt vyapadeśa abhāvāt ca tathā hi yugapad kālaḥ iti vyapadeśaḥ na yugapad a āditya parivartanam iti na ca kriyā eva kālaḥ iti vācyam yugapad a ādi pratyaya abhāva prasaṅgāt tathā hi kriyāyāḥ kriyā rūpa tayā viśeṣa abhyupagamāt iti pratyaya abhāvaḥ parāpara vyatikara abhāvaḥ ca na ca kriyā kālaḥ iti pratīyate yadi ca kartṛ karma vyatiriktā viśiṣṭa pratyaya sampādikā kriyā syāt saṃjñā bheda mātram avyatireke tu viśiṣṭa pratyaya abhāvaḥ eva iti alam vistareṇa 
[I,121,18]	tathā yugapad bhāvaḥ yaugapadyam bahūnām kartṝṇām kārya karaṇe bahūnām kāryāṇām ātma lābhaḥ iti tathā hi yugapad ete kurvanti iti kartṛ ālambanam jñānam yugapad etāni kṛtāni iti kārya ālamba nañca dṛṣṭam na ca atra kartṛ mātram kārya mātrañca ālambana mati prasaṅgāt tathā hi yatra krameṇa kāryam tatra api kartṛ karmaṇoḥ sadbhāvāt syāt etat vijñānam na ca katarasmāt viśiṣṭam kartāram kāryam vā ālambya utpadyate vijñānam etat iti jñāyate yat ca tad viśeṣaṇam kṣiti ādi vilakṣaṇam sa kālaḥ iti na yaugapadya ayaugapadya kramaḥ iti ayugapad ete kurvanti iti kartṛ ālambanam jñānam ayugapad etāni kṛtāni iti kārya ālambanam jñānam atra api viśiṣṭayoḥ kartṛ karmaṇoḥ ālambana tvāt kṣiti ādi vilakṣaṇam nimittam vācyam iti kāla siddhiḥ 
[I,122,1]	tathā ekaḥ eva kartā kiñcid kāryam cireṇa karoti vyāsaṅgāt anarthi tvāt vā kiñcid kṣipram tad arthi tayā tatra cireṇa kṛtam kṣipram kṛtam iti pratyayaḥ vilakṣaṇa tvāt vilakṣaṇam kāraṇam ākṣipati iti na ca kāryam eva nimittam tasya ubhayatra samāna tvāt na api kartā eva tasya api sādhāraṇa tvāt na ca nirnimittam kadācid bhavati iti atas vilakṣaṇena nimittena bhavitavyam iti atas āha teṣām yugapad a ādi pratyayānām viṣayeṣu kartṛṣu kāryeṣu kiṃviśiṣṭānām pūrva pratyaya vilakṣaṇānām pūrva pratyayāḥ kartṛ kāryeṣu tad pratyayāḥ tad vilakṣaṇānām utpattau anyasya kṣiti ādi rūpasya nimittasya asambhavāt yad nimittam sa kālaḥ iti 
[I,122,9]	atha kālasya eka rūpa tayā vilakṣaṇa pratyayānām abhāva prasaṅgaḥ eva atha kriyā vailakṣaṇyāt vilakṣaṇaḥ kālaḥ tad vaiśiṣṭyāt ca pratyaya vaiśiṣṭyam iti ced evam tarhi duruttaram itaretara āśraya tvam tathā hi kriyāyāḥ kriyā rūpa tayā viśeṣa abhāvāt katham kāla viśeṣaka tvam atha yugapad kriyā viśeṣitaḥ yugapad kālaḥ tad viśeṣitā ca yugapad kriyā iti itaretara āśraya tvam eva 
[I,122,14_I,122,19]	na etat evam nirvikalpikāyām saṃvidi paraspara vyāvṛtta kriyā svarūpa avagame sati tad viśiṣṭaḥ kālaḥ tasmāt ca yugapad a ādi pratyayāḥ iti upagamāt nirvikalpakāt ca sa vikalpa utpattiḥ iṣyate yat vā sva rūpeṇa eva kriyāyāḥ viśiṣṭa tvam tad sahakārī kālaḥ yugapad ādi pratyaya sampādakaḥ iti na ca atra viśeṣaṇam kālaḥ kim tarhi viśiṣṭa kārya utpattau viśiṣṭena nimittena bhavitavyam iti anye tu viśeṣaṇa tvena gṛhītasya vyāpāraḥ iti anumāna ādeḥ vyāpāra anupalabdheḥ pramāṇañca vinā asambhavāt iti kālasya pratyakṣatām bruvate tathā hi viśeṣya jñānāni atha anupapattyā viśeṣaṇe jñānam kalpyate tat ca pramāṇa antara vyāpāra anupalabdheḥ pratyakṣam eva 
[I,122,23_I,123,3]	nanu sarveṣām eva kārakāṇām viśeṣya jñāna utpattau vyāpāra viśeṣe api ekam eva viśeṣaṇam na anyat iti viśeṣa hetuḥ na asti iti na sva ālambana jñāna sahitasya viśeṣya jñāna utpattau ekasya eva vyāpārāt ayam eva anurāgaḥ sva anurakta pratyaya jana kañca viśeṣaṇam na ākāra arpakam na api sva śabda abhilapya jñāna janakam asambhavāt na hi sva ākāra arpaka tvam viśeṣaṇasya ākāra vāda pratiṣedhāt na api viśeṣaṇa śabda abhilapyam viśeṣye jñānam sambhavati puruṣe daṇḍaḥ iti jñāna anutpatteḥ atha daṇḍasya atiśaya ādhāyaka tva anupapatteḥ viśeṣaṇa tva abhāvaḥ iti ced na viśiṣṭa jñāna janaka tvena asya eva atiśaya tvāt tad jñānañca atiśayaḥ tad sadbhāve kārya sadbhāvāt 
[I,123,5]	atha viśeṣaṇa viśeṣyayoḥ vibhinna jñāna ālambana tve na pramāṇam asti iti ced tathā hi viśeṣya jñānam utpatteḥ pūrvam viśeṣaṇasya na tad rūpa tām darśayati na krameṇa pramāṇam iti na ca vibhinna jñāna ālambana tvam viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvena vyāptam na api viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ krameṇa iti ubhayathā api vyabhicārāt tathā hi liṅga liṅginoḥ vibhinna jñāna ālambana tve api na viśeṣya viśeṣaṇa bhāvaḥ iti vyabhicāraḥ na ca krame sādhye viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ hetuḥ sādhāraṇa tvāt tasya sa pakṣa vipakṣābhyām vyāvṛtteḥ iti tathā api bhinna jñāna ālambana tve viśeṣaṇa viśeṣyayoḥ anumeya pratipatteḥ pratyaya lakṣaṇa tvam syāt tathā hi anumānāt gṛhītam viśeṣaṇam indriya artha sannikarṣeṇa saha vyāpārāt pratyakṣa sāmagryām antarbhūtam iti tad janitā pratipattiḥ agnimān eṣa deśaḥ iti pratyakṣaphalā syāt 
[I,123,14]	na ca agneḥ nirādhārasya pūrvam anumānam sambhavati tathā agniḥ api anumīyamānaḥ agni tva viśiṣṭaḥ pratīyate iti pūrvam agni tva grahaṇam tatra api agniḥ viśeṣaṇam iti anyonya āśraya tvam atha agnau samavāyaḥ agni tvasya viśleṣaṇam tatra api agni tvam agniḥ vā viśeṣaṇam iti tat eva dūṣaṇam aviśiṣṭasya sarvatra sadbhāvāt viśeṣaka tva anupapattiḥ atha parvataḥ agneḥ viśeṣaṇam tatra api parvata tvam tatra ca samavāyaḥ viśeṣaṇam iti pūrvavat dūṣaṇam atha agni saṃyogaḥ parvatasya agneḥ ca viśeṣaṇam tasya api saṃyoginau tayoḥ api saṃyogaḥ iti pūrva doṣa prasaṅgaḥ tasmāt anumānam pramāṇīkurvatā viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya ālambanam ekam vijñānam abhyupeyam ekañca dhūma viśiṣṭasya parvatasya upalambhāt agni viśiṣṭe pratipattiḥ bhavati 
[I,123,22_I,124,1]	atha eka jñāna ālambanayoḥ aṅgulyoḥ ivā eka jñāna ālambana pakṣe katham viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ pradhāna upasarjana bhāvena saḥ eva kasmāt iti ced vibhinna jñāna ālambana tve api samānam tathā hi idam viśeṣaṇam idam viśeṣyam iti vibhinna jñāna ālambana tva aviśeṣe katham niyamaḥ pradhāna upasarjana bhāvāt iti ced iṣṭam tad eka jñāna ālambana tve api iti doṣa abhāvāt artha ekaḥ cāryam viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ na dharma padārtha antargataḥ tad tat vyatireka pratiṣedhāt na api dravya ādi padārtha antargataḥ ṣaṭsu upalambhāt iti na hi dravya ādīnām anyatamaḥ ṣaṭsu upalabhyate iti 
[I,124,4]	atha viśiṣṭa pratyaya hetuḥ adṛṣṭaḥ viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ iti ced tasya ca eka tāyām idam viśeṣaṇam idam viśeṣyam iti vyavasthā anupapattiḥ viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya tvasya eka tvāt iti tathā hi yat eva viśeṣaṇa tvam tat eva viśeṣya tvam iti ekasya puruṣasya ekasmin eva kāle tat eva viśeṣaṇam viśeṣyañca iti syāt na ca etat asti tasmāt viśiṣṭa adṛṣṭaḥ na viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ atha na ekaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya pratiniyataḥ tathā api viśeṣaṇa viśeṣyayoḥ bhāvaḥ na syāt 
[I,124,10]	atas yathāsambhavam viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ grāhyaḥ kvacid saṃyogaḥ kvacid samavāyaḥ iti tathā ca abhāve api viśeṣa cakṣuḥ ādi sambandhaḥ eva viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ tena satā ca viśiṣṭa pratyaya jananāt na ca adṛṣṭasya atra kāraṇa tvam niṣidhyate sakala kāryeṣu sādhāraṇa tvāt na api adṛṣṭaḥ dṛṣṭa kāraṇam pratyācaṣṭe śarīra ādeḥ api abhāva prasaṅgāt tathā hi sukha ādi sampādakaḥ adṛṣṭaḥ eva astu alam śarīra ādi parikalpanayā iti atha adṛṣṭa sadbhāve api śarīra ādayaḥ dṛṣṭa tvāt abhyupagamyante tarhi viśeṣya cakṣuḥ ādi sambandhaḥ eva dṛṣṭa tvāt viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ abhyupagantavyaḥ
