[I,124,17]	atha viśeṣaṇe tasya āvṛtteḥ katham tat bhāvaḥ iti ced na adṛṣṭvat vyāpāra apekṣayā tad avṛtti tvāt atha eka jñāna ālambana tve surabhi dravyam iti vibhinna indriya grāhyayoḥ viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ na syāt na hi vibhinna indriyābhyām ekam vijñānam sampādyam dṛṣṭam iti na viśeṣaṇa viśeṣyayoḥ vibhinna jñāna ālambana tve bādhaka upapatteḥ anusandhāna jñānam etat tathā hi ghrāṇena gandham upalabhya cakṣuṣā sparśanena vā dravyam paścāt manasā anusaṃdhatte surabhi dravyam iti na ca sarvam viśeṣya jñānam anusandhāna jñānam iti vācyam tatra hi bādhaka anupapatteḥ tathā viśeṣaṇa viśeṣyayoḥ vibhinna jñāna ālamba natāyām eka daṇḍinam aham adrākṣam iti smaraṇam na syāt tasya hi anubhava rūpa tvāt 
[I,124,25_I,125,1]	atha puruṣa pratyaya sāmānā adhikaraṇyāt daṇḍinam ānayaḥ ityādi prayogeṣu puruṣasya eka kriyā sambandhāt tad ālambanam eva viśeṣya jñānam iti ced na puruṣasya viśeṣya tayā prādhānyāt kriyā sambandhaḥ sāmānādhikaraṇī añca upapadyate eva iti alam ati vistareṇa anye tu eka jñāna ālambana tve viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ na syāt tayoḥ karaṇa karma rūpa tvāt iti manyante tathā hi viśiṣyate anena iti viśeṣaṇam karaṇam viśeṣyate iti viśeṣyam karma tat ca eka jñāna ālamba natāyām na syāt ubhayoḥ karma tvāt iti na api ajñāta vyāpāre sahakāri tva aviśeṣāt cakṣuḥ ādibhyaḥ viśeṣaḥ syāt iti tat jñānam kalpyate yadi ca daṇḍa tva viśiṣṭaḥ daṇḍaḥ puruṣasya viśeṣaṇam iṣyeta tasya api anyat iti anavasthā daṇḍaḥ ced daṇḍa tvasya viśeṣaṇam itaretara āśraya tvañca syāt iti viśeṣya jñāna abhāva prasaṅgaḥ asti ca viśeṣya jñānam iti tat anyathā anupapattyā viśeṣaṇa jñāna mātram jñāyate 
[I,125,9]	yat ca idam viśeṣya jñānam utpatteḥ pūrvam viśeṣaṇasya na tat rūpa tām darśayati iti uktam tatra kā iyam viśeṣaṇa rūpa tā iti vicāryam na hi daṇḍe daṇḍa tva ādi vat viśeṣaṇa rūpa tā pratibhāti atha sva anurakta pratyaya janaka tvam viśeṣaṇa tvam tat ca yadi sva ālambana jñāna sahitasya viśeṣya jñāna janaka tvam abhyupagama vyāghātaḥ na ca eka vijñāna ālambana tve anurāga artham paśyāmaḥ tad śabda abhilapya tva ādeḥ pratiṣedhāt na api kramaḥ viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāva hetuḥ anabhyupagamāt viśeṣyajñānantu viśeṣaṇa jñānam darśayati eva anyathā hi tad viśiṣṭa tva ayogāt yat ca idam anumānāt apratipatteḥ pratyakṣa phalaka tvam iti tat ca asat bādhaka sadbhāvena atra eka jñāna ālambana tva abhyupagamāt na ca evam sarvatra bādhakam asti iti 
[I,125,17_I,125,20]	anye tu dhūma upalambha anantaram agni anumāne sati agni mānayam parvataḥ iti jñānam pratyakṣam eva iti bruvate anyathā hi ayam iti aparokṣata anirdeśaḥ na syāt atra ca sādhya dharma viśiṣṭa dharmiṇaḥ sādhya tve katham etat sādhanam syāt iti vācyam yat ca idam viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ kim ekaḥ anekaḥ vā iti tatra ekatva abhyupagame api na viśeṣaṇa viśeṣyayoḥ avyavasthā nimitta antarasya asādhāraṇasya sadbhāvāt tathā hi viśeṣaṇam sva anurakta pratyaya utpādaka tvena iti uktam viśeṣyantu viśeṣya jñāna viṣaya tvena viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ tu param viśeṣya jñāna utpattau sahakārī na punar vyavasthā kāraṇam iti 
[I,125,24]	na ca saṃyoga samavāyau eva viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ tayoḥ samavāye abhāve ca abhāvāt atra api viśeṣya indriya sambandhaḥ asti iti ced na tasya viśeṣaṇa āvṛtti tvāt na api adṛṣṭa vat vyāpāra apekṣayā tad vṛtti tvam saṃyoga samavāyayoḥ anyatra anupalabdheḥ tathā hi saṃyoga samavāyayoḥ yadi vyāpāra apekṣayā viśeṣaṇa vṛtti tvam iṣyeta viśeṣya sambandham vinā abhāva samavāyayoḥ grahaṇam syāt yatra hi tayoḥ vṛttiḥ tatra eva grahaṇa janaka tvā upalabdheḥ adṛṣṭasya tu ātma samavetasya api sakala kārya utpattau sādhāraṇa tvāt saṃyoga ādi sadbhāve tad abhāve ca kevalasya vyāpāraḥ abhyupagamyate eva sa ca ubhayatra vyāpāra apekṣayā sambaddhaḥ iva sambaddhaḥ na paramārthataḥ 
[I,126,6]	na ca upacaritasya indriya asahakāri tvam aparokṣa jñānasya anyathā sambhavena tad abhāva siddheḥ dṛṣṭañca śrotra anya upacaritasya api śabda jñāna sahakāri tvam iti yat ca idam surabhi dravyam ityādi anusandhāna jñānam iti uktam tat asat anyatra api evam prasaṅgāt na ca atra vibhinna jñāna ālambana tve kiñcid bādhakam asti iti tat eva abhyupeyam 
[I,126,10_I,126,12]	na api daṇḍinam aham adrākṣam iti smaraṇa anupapattiḥ viśeṣaṇa jñāna janita saṃskārasya viśeṣya jñāna sahakāriṇaḥ saṃskāra ārambheṇa api tad bhāvāt yat ca idam eka jñāna ālambana tve api viśeṣyasya prādhānyāt kriyā sambandhaḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyañca ghaṭataḥ iti tat na prādhānyasya eva vicārya tvāt eka jñāna ālamba natāyām hi kim kṛtam prādhānyam iti cintyam sāmāna adhikaraṇyantu eka jñāna ālambanatva aviśeṣe puruṣa pratyayena na ca daṇḍa pratyayena iti viśeṣaṇa hetu abhāvaḥ 
[I,126,16]	atha vibhinna viśeṣaṇa nimittayoḥ ekasmin arthe vṛtteḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyam daṇḍī iti pratyaye daṇḍaḥ viśeṣaṇam puruṣe iti na ca evam daṇḍasya viśeṣaṇa tve anyat viśeṣaṇam asti iti sāmānādhikaraṇyam na etat evam anekasya prameyasya pratibhāsā abhyupagamāt tathā hi na daṇḍī iti jñāne daṇḍa tva ādi api prameyam pratibhāsate iti abhyupagame kathanam sāmānādhikaraṇyam tathā sūtra vyāghātaḥ ca samavāyinaḥ śvaityāt śvaitya buddheḥ śvete buddhiḥ tad kārya kāraṇa bhūte kārya kāraṇa svabhāve iti 
[I,126,22_I,127,1]	na punar bhūta abhidhānam upamāyām mukhye bādhaka anupapatteḥ na api prameya viśeṣāt eva pratyaya viśeṣaḥ sahakāri vailakṣaṇyena api bhāvāt nanu evam tarhi viśeṣaṇa vat sambandhe api jñānam kalpanīyam tatra tad anurāgasya apratibhāsena cakṣuḥ ādi vat agṛhītasya api vyāpāra abhyupagamāt na api abheda upacārāt viśeṣaṇā viśeṣya bhāvaḥ puruṣe daṇḍaḥ iti jñāna anupapatteḥ atha viśeṣaṇam viśeṣyan ca sambandham laukikīm sthitim gṛhītvā saṅkalyyā eva tathā pratyeti na anyathā iti saṅkalanā jñānam iti ced na etat yuktam etāvataḥ jñāna kalāpasya sadbhāve pramāṇa abhāvāt tathā hi param viśeṣya jñānam utpadyamānam dṛṣṭam tat ca anyathā ca ghaṭataḥ iti viśeṣaṇe api jñānam luptam na punar jñāna antara sadbhāve pramāṇam asti iti 
[I,127,7_I,127,9]	na ca idam niriviṣayam kalpanā jñānam artha anvaya vyatireka anuvidhānāt bādhaka anupapatteḥ ca tat evam gṛhītasya viśeṣaṇasya viśeṣya jñāna janaka tvāt liṅga ādi vyāpāra anupalabdheḥ ca pratyakṣa tvam kālasya iti satyam tathā eka jñāna ālambana tve api yugapādi pratyayāḥ na kālasya liṅgam tasya api viśeṣaṇa tayā ālambana tvāt amīṣāñca indriya anuvidhānena pratyakṣa phala tvāt iti alam 
[I,127,13]	sarva kāryāṇām utpattau kāraṇa tvam pratijñātam āha sarva kārya aṇāñca utpatti sthiti vināśa hetuḥ iti utpattiḥ ātma lābhaḥ bhāvānām sthitiḥ krama bhāvi aneka kārya kartṛ tvam vināśaḥ pradhvaṃsaḥ teṣām kāraṇam iti atra tu yadi api sarva kāryāṇām hetuḥ iti ukte sarvam etat labhyate tathā api avāntara viśeṣa apekṣayā bheda kathanam 
[I,127,17]	atha teṣām hetuḥ kālaḥ iti katham jñāyate iti āha tad vyapadeśāt iti tathā hi utpattau kālena vyapadeśaḥ madhyāhne utpannaḥ aparāhṇe utpannaḥ iti sthitau ca madhyāhnam yāvat sthitaḥ aparāhṇañcaḥ iti vināśe tu prātar vinaṣṭaḥ varṣa ante vinaṣṭaḥ ityādi kāraṇena tu kāryasya vyapadeśaḥ yathā cākṣuṣam vijñānam mānasam vijñānam iti 
[I,127,21]	atha akāraṇena api vyapadeśaḥ sambhavati eva mūrtāḥ paramāṇavaḥ daṇḍī puruṣaḥ iti satyam tathā api sambandhe sati vyapadeśa upalabdheḥ na ca anyaḥ sambandhaḥ atra sambhavati iti kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ jñāyate atha asti saṃyogaḥ na guṇa karma ādeḥ avyapadeśya tā prasaṅgāt asti ca tatra api vyapadeśaḥ pūrvāhṇe śabdaḥ tathā utkṣepaṇam ityādi 
[I,128,1]	atha ayam vyapadeśaḥ saṃyukta samavāyāt bhaviṣyati iti na abhāve tad abhāva prasaṅgāt atas kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ eva sambandhaḥ abhyupeyaḥ tasya hi vyāpaka tvāt iti tathā niyata kāle kusuma ādeḥ kāryasya upalambhaḥ na kāla antare iti anvaya vyatirekābhyām tasya kāraṇa tvam vijñāyate tathā hi vasanta samayaḥ eva pāṭalā ādi kusumānām udgamaḥ na kāla antare iti evam kārya antareṣu api ūhyam tathā prasava kālam apekṣate iti vyavahārāt kāraṇa tvam kālasya tathā hi sahakāriṇam apekṣya upalabdheḥ kālasya sahakāritām antareṇa prasūtau ayam vyavahāraḥ na syāt 
[I,128,8]	tathā na param yugapad a ādi pratyaya hetuḥ kṣaṇa lava nimeṣa kāṣṭhākalā muhūrtayāmāhorātra ardha māsa māsartu ayana saṃvatsara yuga kalpa manvantara pralaya mahāpralaya vyavahāra hetuḥ iti tathā hi paramāṇoḥ ca avaruddha nabhaḥ deśa tyāga upalakṣitaḥ kālaḥ kṣaṇaḥ tat dvayam lavaḥ iti uktaḥ nimeṣaḥ ca lava dvayam kāṣṭhāḥ nimeṣāḥ pañcadaśa ca iha prakīrtitāḥ triṃśat kāṣṭhāḥ kalā proktā kalāḥ triṃśat muhūrtakaḥ iti evam māsa ādeḥ api lakṣaṇam prasiddham grāhyam 
[I,128,15]	sa ca ayam kṣaṇa ādi vyavahāraḥ viśiṣṭa tvāt viśiṣṭam nimittam ākṣipati na ca anyat nimittam sambhavati iti kriyā ādeḥ pratiṣedhāt iti kāla sadbhāva siddhiḥ tasya samavāyi tva guṇavat tva pratipādana artham tasya guṇāḥ saṃkhyā parimāṇa pṛthaktva saṃyoga vibhāgāḥ iti vākyam atra keṣāñcid utpattau samavāyi kāraṇam etaiḥ guṇaiḥ guṇavān kālaḥ iti 
[I,128,19]	atha dravya tvāt eva saṃkhyā asadbhāva siddhau kim ekaḥ anekaḥ vā iti saṃśayaḥ tat nirāsāya āha kāla liṅga aviśeṣāt eka tvam siddham iti kālasya yat liṅgam yugapad a ādi pratyaya rūpam tat viśiṣṭam iti nānātva apratipādakam nanu ca asiddham etat yugapad ādi pratyayānām parasparam viśiṣṭa tvāt na ca kārya vailakṣaṇyam kāraṇa vailakṣaṇyam vinā bhavati iti nānātvam eva nyāyyam satyam kārya vailakṣaṇyāt vijñāyate eva sāmagrī vailakṣaṇyam tat ca sahakāri antara anupraveśena api ghaṭate iti katham kālasya nānātvam uktañca atra viśiṣṭa kriyā upacitasya viśiṣṭa pratyaya janaka tvam iti na ca evam paramāṇūnām cāturvidhyam vyāhanyate iti pūrvavat vācyam tat evam nānātve pramāṇa abhāvāt dravyasya ca saṃkhyeya tvāt iti eka tvam siddham 
[I,129,1_I,129,4]	tathā tad anuvidhānāt pṛthaktvam iti tena ekatvena anuvidhānam sāhacaryāt yatra hi ekatvam tatra avaśyam eka pṛthaktvam bhaviṣyati iti na ca evam parimāṇa viśeṣeṇa sāhacaryam asti iti jñāna artham krama atikrameṇa pṛthaktvanirūpaṇam iti tathā kāraṇe kālaḥ iti vacanāt parama mahat parimāṇam iti yugapad ādi pratyayānām kāraṇe kāla ākhyāḥ iti sūtram darśayati tathā hi yugapad ādi pratyayānām kāraṇe kālaḥ iti ākhyā saṃjñā iti te ca pratyayāḥ sarvatra bhavanti iti vyāpaka tvam kālasya tasmāt ca parama mahattvam iti yat vā aṇu parimāṇān adhikaraṇa tve sati nitya dravya tvāt parama mahat tvam iti pūrvavat vācyam 
[I,129,9_I,129,15]	tathā kāraṇa para tva ādi vacanāt saṃyogaḥ iti kāraṇa para tvāt kāraṇa apara tvāt ca kārye paratva aparatve iti sūtram darśayati kāraṇa para tvam hi kāla piṇḍa saṃyogaḥ paratva utpādaka tvāt upacāreṇa vivakṣitaḥ iti vakṣyāmaḥ paratva parīkṣāyām tad vināśaka tvāt vibhāgaḥ iti tasya hi saṃyogasya kṛtaka tvāt avaśyam vināśena bhavitavyam sa ca sarvatra āśraya vināśa abhāvāt vibhāgāt eva vinaśyati iti vibhāgaḥ siddhaḥ iti atha kālasya katham dravya tvam nitya tvañca iti āha tasya ākāśa vat dravya tva nitya tve siddhe iti tathā hi guṇavat tvāt anāśrita tvāt ca dravyam kālaḥ samāna asamāna jātīya kāraṇā sambhavāt ca akārya tvena nityaḥ iti atideśa arthaḥ 
[I,129,18]	nanu ca atra kālasya ekatāyām vartamāna ādi vyavahāraḥ katham syāt iti āha kāla liṅga aviśeṣāt añjasā eka tve api ityādi yadi api kāla liṅga aviśeṣāt añjasā mukhyayā vṛttyā eka tvam siddham tathā api sarva kāryāṇām prārambhaḥ ca kriyā abhinirvṛttiḥ ca sthitiḥ ca nirodhaḥ ca iti tathā uktāḥ te eva upādhayaḥ tad bhedāt nānātvam iti tathā ca prārambha kriyā upalakṣitaḥ anāgataḥ kālaḥ abhinirvṛttiḥ ātma lābhaḥ tad upalakṣitaḥ ca vartamānaḥ tathā sthitiḥ krama bhāvi aneka kārya kartṛ tvam tad upalakṣitaḥ api vartamānaḥ eva tasya yāvat vastu sadbhāva vyāpya tvāt yāvat vivartate vastu tāvat vartamānaḥ iti tathā nirodhaḥ vināśaḥ tad upalakṣitaḥ ca atītaḥ iti 
[I,130,1]	atha katham nānātvam upacaryate iti āha maṇi vat pācaka vat vā iti yathā maṇeḥ svarūpa aparityāgena eva upādhi bhedāt upacaryate nānātvam pītaḥ raktaḥ iti tadvat iha api bhinna kriyā upādhi vaśāt vartamāna ādi bhedaḥ iti yathā vā svarūpa aparityāgena eva puruṣasya nānā kriyā vaśāt pācaka ādi bhedaḥ tadvat iha api iti vāstave hi bhede bādhaka upapatteḥ tathā hi yadi vartamāna ādeḥ vāstavaḥ bhedaḥ vyāpaka tvañca syāt ekasya vastunaḥ aneka kāla sambandhāt avyapadeśya tā prasajyeta na hi vartamānena vyapadeśaḥ atīta anāgatābhyām api sambandhāt na api atītena itarābhyām api sambandhāt avyāpaka tvam tarhi na anekasya puruṣasya ekasmin eva deśe atīta anāgata vartamāna pratyayāḥ prāpnuvanti te tathā dṛṣṭāḥ tathā ca ekasya vidyamāna kriyā upalambhāt ekasmin eva deśe vartamāna pratyayaḥ tatra eva anyasya kriyā uparamāt atīta pratyayaḥ anyasya ca utpadyamāna kriyā upalambhāt anāgataḥ iti kriyā vaśāt eva nānā pratyaya janaka tvam na punar vāstavaḥ asya bhedaḥ iti sthitam 
[I,130,12_I,131,5]	idānīm diśaḥ avasara prāptāyāḥ lakṣaṇa parīkṣā artham diś pūrva apara ādi pratyaya liṅgāḥ ityādi prakaraṇam diś iti lakṣya nirdeśaḥ pūrva apara ādi pratyaya liṅga iti lakṣaṇam tathā pūrvaḥ ca aparaḥ ca pūrva aparau tau ādiḥ yeṣām iti tathā uktāḥ te ca te pratyayāḥ ca iti te liṅgam yasyāḥ sā tathā iti saṅgraha ukteḥ vivaraṇa artham āha mūrtam avadhim kṛtvā mūrteṣu eva dravyeṣu viṣaya bhūteṣu etasmāt mūrta dravyāt idam mūrtam pūrveṇa dakṣiṇena ityādi daśa pratyayāḥ yatas nimittāt bhavanti sā diś iti tathā ca diś itarebhyaḥ bhidyate pūrva apara ādi pratyaya liṅga tvāt yaḥ tu na bhidyate na ca asau evam yathā kṣiti ādiḥ iti vyavahāraḥ vā sādhyaḥ 
[I,131,9]	nanu ca pūrva apara ādi pratyayāḥ paraspara apekṣitayā mūrteṣu eva bhavanti iti asiddham lakṣaṇa abhidhānam na etat evam paraspara apekṣitāyām ubhaya abhāva prasaṅgāt tathā hi yadi pūrvam apekṣya apara pratyayaḥ aparañca apekṣya pūrva pratyayaḥ iti eka abhāve anyatara abhāvāt ubhaya abhāva prasaṅgaḥ na ca nirnimittaḥ kadācid utpanna tvāt anvaya vi atirekābhyām mūrta dravyasya vyāpāra upalabdheḥ aṅguli ādi vyapadeśāt ca ālambana tvam na ca tasya aviśiṣṭasya pratyaya janmani vyāpāraḥ sarvatra aviśeṣeṇa pūrva ādi pratyaya aviśeṣa prasaṅgāt 
[I,131,15]	atha mūrta dravyam eva avadhi bhūtam nimittam iti ced na tasya sarva pratyayeṣu aviśeṣāt tathā hi tasya nimitta tāyām yatra eva pūrva pratyayaḥ tatra eva dakṣiṇa ādi pratyayāḥ prasajyeran aviśeṣāt na api saṅketa eva nimittam tasya hi nimittam vinā sarvatra apravṛtteḥ tathā hi ekam nimittam vinā ekatra saṅketitaḥ pūrva śabdaḥ na artha antare pravartate atha asti pūrva ādi śabdānām saṅketa pravṛtteḥ kāraṇam ekam yat sadbhāvāt artha antare api pravṛttiḥ iti ced sā tarhi diś iti atha aviśiṣṭa tayā diśaḥ na viśiṣṭa pratyaya janaka tvam iti ced na eka tve api viśiṣṭa saṃyoga vaśāt viśiṣṭa pratyaya janaka tvam iti anantaram vakṣyāmaḥ 
[I,131,22]	atha vikalpa jñāna tvāt nirviṣayāḥ pūrva ādi pratyayāḥ vāsanā vaśāt bhavanti iti ced tat na abādhyamāna tvāt abādhyamānam jñānam nirviṣayam na bhavati eva śukla ādi vijñāna vat viṣayasya ca aṅguli ādi vyapadiśyamānasya anvaya vyatirekābhyām vyāpāra upalabdheḥ iti uktam na ca vāsanā eva atra nimittam tasyāḥ bodha vyatirekeṇa asambhavāt iti pūrva nyāyāt atas viśiṣṭa pratyayāḥ pūrva apara ādayaḥ na viśiṣṭam nimittam antareṇa bhavanti na ca anyat nimittam kṣiti ādi rūpam sambhavati iti atas nimitta antarā sambhavāt yat atra nimittam sā diś iti viśeṣaṇa viśeṣyam nyāyaḥ sarva utpattau kāraṇa tvam kāla vat draṣṭavyam 
[I,132,4_I,132,7]	samavāyi tva guṇavat tva pratipādana artham āha tasyāḥ tu guṇāḥ saṃkhyā parimāṇa pṛthaktva saṃyoga vibhāgāḥ iti tatra ca ati deśam karoti kāla vat ete siddhāḥ iti tathā diś liṅga aviśeṣāt viśeṣa liṅga abhāvāt ca eka tvam diśaḥ siddham nanu pūrva apara ādi pratyayāḥ parasparam vilakṣaṇasya eva nimittasya pratipādakāḥ iti nānātvam eva yuktam na sahakāri vailakṣaṇyena api pratyaya vailakṣaṇya upapattiḥ iti ukta nyāyāt atas dravya tvāt eva saṃkhyā yoga siddhau nānātve pramāṇa abhāvāt ekatvam siddham 
[I,132,10]	tena ekatvena anuvidhānāt sāhacaryāt eka pṛthak tvañca iti pūrva apara ādi pratyayānām kāraṇe diś ākhyāḥ iti vākyena parama mahat tvam tathā ca pūrva apara ādi pratyayāḥ sarvatra nimittam vinā na sambhavanti iti diśaḥ vyāpaka tvāt parama mahat tvam tathā kāraṇa para tvāt kāraṇa apara tvāt ca paratva aparatve iti sūtreṇa saṃyogaḥ siddhaḥ tathā hi kāraṇa para tvam paratva utpādakaḥ diś piṇḍa saṃyogaḥ apara tvañca aparatva utpādakaḥ vivakṣitaḥ iti vakṣyāmaḥ paratva parīkṣāyām saṃyogaḥ ca kṛtaka tvāt avaśyam vināśī iti āśraya vināśasya sarvatra asambhavāt vibhāgāt api naśyati iti vibhāgaḥ siddhaḥ iti atideśa arthaḥ tathā guṇavat tvāt anāśrita tvāt ca dravyam samāna asamāna jātīya kāraṇā sambhavāt ca akārya tvena nitya tvañca iti draṣṭavyam 
[I,132,19]	atha ekasyāḥ diśaḥ prācya ādi vyavahāraḥ katham syāt iti āha diś liṅga aviśeṣāt añjasā eka tve api ityādi tatra hi yadi api diśaḥ liṅgānām aviśeṣāt nānātva aprasiddhau añjasā mukhyayā vṛttyā eka tvam siddham tathā api savituḥ ye saṃyogāḥ lokapāla parigṛhīta diś pradeśaiḥ saha iti vibhakti vipariṇāmaḥ yat vā bhagavataḥ savituḥ ye saṃyogāḥ te keṣām iti vivakṣāyām sambandhasya api vidyamāna tvāt yuktā eva ṣaṣṭhī 
[I,132,24]	lokapāla parigṛhīta diś pradeśānām iti anvarthāḥ anugata arthāḥ prācī a ādi bhedena daśavidhāḥ daśa prakārāḥ saṃjñāḥ kṛtāḥ parama ṛṣibhiḥ iti kimartham iti āha śruti smṛti loka vyavahāra artham śrutiḥ ca smṛtiḥ ca lokaḥ ca iti tathā uktāḥ teṣām saṃvyavahāra artham iti śrautaḥ hi vyavahāraḥ vāyavyām gavayam ālabheta smārtaḥ tu prāṅmukhaḥ bhuñjīta laukikaḥ api asmad vṛddhāḥ prāṅmukhāḥ yajante smaḥ iti ādi vyavahārasya prasiddhi artham iti 
[I,133,5]	atha lokapāla parigṛhīta diś pradeśaiḥ saṃyogaḥ bhagavataḥ katham bhavati iti āha merum pradakṣiṇam āvartamānasya iti pradakṣiṇam hi yathā bhavati tathā merum paribhramataḥ api viśiṣṭa saṃyogāḥ tad vaśāt ca prācī ādi vyavahāraḥ anvaya vyatirekābhyām upalambhāt ca tathā hi udaya samaye savituḥ diś pradeśena yogāt prācī iti vyavahāraḥ tatra hi prāk prathamam añcati iti kṛtvā evam madhyāhna samaye diś pradeśena saṃyogāt dakṣiṇā iti vyavahāraḥ tathā ca aparāhṇe tad yogāt pratīci iti ca evam udīcya ādiṣu api vācyam 
[I,133,11_I,134,16]	nanu evam tarhi saḥ eva āditya saṃyogaḥ astu pūrva ādi vyavahārasya nimittam alam diśaḥ kalpanayā iti na ādityasya api pūrva apara ādi vyavahāra viṣaya tve anya āditya parikalpanāyām anavasthā syāt iti nimitta antaram eva nyāyyam na ca āditya parivartanam sarvatra sambhavati iti tatra pūrva apara ādi vyavahāra abhāva prasaṅgaḥ tasmāt ekā api aneka saṃyoga upacitā viśiṣṭa vyavahāra samartha iti abhyupagantavyam atas bhaktyā upacāreṇa daśa diśaḥ siddhāḥ tāsāñca upacarita diśām devatā parigraha vaśāt punar daśa saṃjñā bhavanti mahā indreṇa parigṛhītā māhendrī vaiśvānareṇa parigṛhītā vaiśvānarī iti evam anyāsu api iti 
[I,134,22]	idānīm ātmanaḥ lakṣaṇa parīkṣā artham ātma tva abhisambandhāt iti ādi prakaraṇam ātma tvena abhisambandhaḥ ātma upalakṣitaḥ samavāyaḥ vā lakṣaṇam iti tathā hi ātmā itarasmāt bhidyate ātma tva abhisambandhāt yaḥ tu itarasmāt anātmanaḥ na bhidyate na ca asau ātma tvena abhisambaddhaḥ yathā kṣiti ādiḥ iti na ca tathā ātmā tasmāt bhidyate iti vyavahāraḥ vā sādhyaḥ tathā śabda artha nirūpaṇa paratvena pūrvavat vākyam yojanīyam tathā lakṣaṇasya ākṣepa pratisamādhānam pūrvavat vācyam 
[I,135,5]	nanu sarvam etat asambaddham ātma sadbhāve pramāṇa abhāvāt tathā hi na pratyakṣeṇa upalabhyate rūpa ādi vat svabhāva an avadhāraṇāt na api anumānam asti ātma pratibaddham iti āśaṅkya āha tasya saukṣmyāt apratyakṣa tve sati karaṇaiḥ śabda ādi upalabdhi anumitaiḥ śrotra ādibhiḥ samadhigamaḥ kiyate iti saukṣmyam rūpa viśeṣa eka artha samaveta mahat tva ādi abhāvaḥ abhipretaḥ na aṇu parimāṇa sambandhi tvam atas eva tasya apratyakṣa tvam 
[I,135,10]	nanu ca ayuktam etat aham iti pratyaye tasya pratibhāsanāt tathā ca sukhī aham duḥkhī aham icchāvān aham iti pratyayaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ na ca ayam anumāpu urvakaḥ liṅga liṅgi sambandha anusmaraṇa vyāpārasya asaṃvedanāt na api śabdaḥ tena vinā api utpadyamāna tvāt na api viparyaya jñānam etat abādhyamāna tvāt na api saṃśaya jñānam tad rūpasya asaṃvedanāt atas pramā rūpa tvāt avaśyam pramāṇa antara pratiṣedhe pratyakṣasya eva vyāpāraḥ na śarīra ālambanam antaḥkaraṇa vyāpāreṇa utpatteḥ tathā hi na śarīram antaḥkaraṇa paricchedyam bahis viṣaya tvāt 
[I,135,17]	nanu evam kṛśaḥ aham sthūlaḥ aham iti pratyayaḥ tarhi katham mukhye bādhaka upapatteḥ upacāreṇa tathā hi madīyaḥ bhṛtyaḥ iti jñāna vat madīyam śarīram iti bheda pratyaya darśanāt bhṛtya vat eva śarīre api aham iti jñānasya aupacārika tvam eva yuktam upacāraḥ tu nimittam vinā na pravartate iti ātma upakāraka tvam nimittam kalpyate ātmani tu mukhya tvam sukhī iti jñānena samāna adhikaraṇa tvāt tathā hi yatra sukhī iti jñānam tatra eva aham iti jñānasya upalambhaḥ sukha ādi yogaḥ ca śarīra ādi vyatirekeṇa ātmani eva iti vakṣyāmaḥ 
[I,135,23]	yat ca idam rūpa ādi vat svabhāva an avadhāraṇāt iti tat asat aham iti svabhāvasya pratibhāsanāt na ca artha antarasya artha antara svabhāvena apratyakṣa tvam doṣaḥ sarva padārthānām apratyakṣata aprasaṅgāt na ca parakīye api ātmani aham iti pratibhāsa prasaṅgaḥ syāt tasya ātma antara apratyakṣa tvāt pratyakṣa jañcā idam vijñānam na pramāṇa antara prabhavam iti uktam na ca ātmā antareṇa ātma antarasya apratyakṣatāyām sva ātmanaḥ api tathā abhāva prasaṅgaḥ sva saṃvidā bādhyamāna tvāt na api rūpa antarasya saṃkhyā ādeḥ pratyakṣatā prasaṅgaḥ tasya pratibhāsā bhāvena apratyakṣa tvāt tathā yatra hi rūpa viśeṣasya pratyakṣa tvam tatra eva saṃkhyā ādayaḥ pratyakṣāḥ iti ukta pūrvam 
[I,136,6]	atha ātmanaḥ kartṛ tvāt ekasmin kāle karma tva asambhavenā pratyakṣa tvam tat na lakṣaṇa bhedena tad upapatteḥ tathā hi jñāna cikīrṣā dhāra tvasya kartṛ lakṣaṇasya upapatteḥ kartṛ tvam tadā eva ca kriyayā vyāpya tva upalabdheḥ karma tvañca iti na doṣaḥ lakṣaṇa tantra tvāt vastu vyavasthāyāḥ na ca anayoḥ ekasmin dharmiṇī ekasmin ca kāle kartṛ karaṇayoḥ iva astu virodhaḥ tathā hi svātantryam kartṛ tvam pāratantrī añca karaṇa tvam iti tu anayoḥ vidhi pratiṣedha rūpa tvāt abhinne dharmiṇī a sambhavaḥ yuktaḥ na ca evam kartṛ tva karma tvayoḥ iti 
[I,136,12]	atas eva madīyam śarīram ityādi pratyayeṣu ātma anurāga sadbhāve api ātmanaḥ avacchedaka tvam śraiharṣam devakulam iti jñāne śrī harṣasya iva ubhayatra api bādhaka sadbhāvāt yatra hi anurāga sadbhāve api viśeṣaṇa tve bādhakam asti tatra avacchedaka tvam eva kalpyate iti asti ca śrī harṣasya vidyamāna tvam ātmani iti kartṛ tva karaṇa tvayoḥ asambhavaḥ iti bādhakam 
[I,136,17]	na ca ekasmin eva dharmiṇi kartṛ ādi vibhāgasya upalabdheḥ avāstava tvam eva nyāyyam lakṣaṇa bhedasya vāstava tvāt yeṣāntu lakṣaṇa bhedaḥ na asti teṣām eva doṣaḥ iti kalpanā jñānañca pūrvam eva nirastam iti na kalpanā samāropitā kāraṇa ādi vyavasthā tat evam kartṛ ādi pravibhāgasya bhinna nimitta tvāt ekasmin eva ātmani anumānena pratyakṣeṇa vā paricchedyamānena tat eva kartṛ tvam na doṣāya iti 
[I,136,22]	nanu evam ātmani aham iti pratyayasya pratyakṣa phala tvāt tasya saukṣmyāt apratyakṣa tve sati iti asambaddham vākyam na bāhya indriya vivakṣayā asya abhidhānāt tathā hi kasmāt ātmā kṣiti ādi vat bāhya indriya pratyakṣaḥ na bhavati iti ukte vākyam sambadhyate tasya saukṣmyāt rūpa viśeṣa eka artha samavāyasya mahat tvasya aneka dravya tva sahacaritasya abhāvāt na bāhya indriya pratyakṣa tvam tatra pratyakṣe api apratyakṣa abhidhānāt labhyate tasmin ca sati karaṇaiḥ śrotra ādibhiḥ samadhigamaḥ kriyate śrotra ādibhiḥ iti ubhayatra api yojyam tathā hi śabda upalabdhiḥ karaṇa kāryā kriyā tvāt chidi kriyāvat evam śeṣeṣu api iti tasya saukṣmyāt yathā uktāt karaṇaiḥ śrotra ādibhiḥ apratyakṣa tve sati taiḥ eva liṅga bhūtaiḥ tasya adhigamaḥ kriyate 
[I,137,5_I,137,8]	śrotra ādīnām api sadbhāve anumānam āha śabda ādi upalabdhi anumitaiḥ iti śabda sparśa rūpa rasa gandha upalabdhi kriyābhiḥ anumīyante iti tad anumitāni taiḥ iti tathā hi śabda upalabdhiḥ karaṇa kāryā kriyā tvāt chidi kriyāvat evam śeṣeṣu api iti vyāpti pratipādana artham āha vā asya ādīnām iva karaṇānām kartṛ prayojya tva darśanāt iti yathā vāsya ādīni karaṇāni kartṛ prayojyāni iti tadvat śrotra ādīni api karaṇāni tasmāt kartṛ prayojyāni tathā hi śrotra ādīni karaṇāni kartṛ prayojyāni karaṇa tvāt vā asya ādi vat iti 
[I,137,12]	atha atra sarva gata ātma prayojya tve sādhye sādhya vikala tvam viparyaye vā siddha sādhanam iti na sarva anumāneṣu sāmānyena eva sādhya sādhana bhāva upapatteḥ viśeṣeṇa anuvyāpti abhāve sarva anumāna uccheda prasaṅgaḥ pramāṇañca anumānam iti vakṣyāmaḥ tad adhikāre siddhe ca kartṛ sadbhāve tasya śarīra ādi vyatirekaḥ pariśeṣāt tathā na param karaṇaiḥ śabda ādiṣu prasiddhyā ca prasādhakaḥ anumīyate śabda ādiṣu viṣayeṣu prasiddhiḥ vijñānam tayā prasādhakaḥ samavāyi kāraṇam ātmā anumīyate tathā hi śabda ādi jñānam kvacid āśritam guṇa tvāt yaḥ yaḥ guṇaḥ sa saḥ āśritaḥ yathā rūpa ādiḥ tathā ca guṇaḥ jñānam tasmāt āśritam samavāyi kāraṇa pūrvaka tvam kāryatvāt rūpa ādi vat eva 
[I,137,20]	atha śarīra ādi āśritam bhaviṣyati iti siddha sādhanam iti āśaṅkya āha na śarīra indriya manasām iti tathā hi pare manyante prāṇa vat śarīre sati bhāvāt tad abhāve ca abhāvāt śarīra dharmaḥ eva caitanyam iti evam indriya ādiṣu api ūhyam tad niṣedha artham na śarīra indriya manasām caitanyam iti vyavahāre sādhye na sādhya aviśiṣṭaḥ hetuḥ ajña tvāt iti yat vā sva siddhānta upadarśanam etat asmad siddhānte na amīṣām caitanyam iti nanu evam yadi śarīrasya caitanyam na asti tarhi kim artham paraiḥ uktaḥ caitanya viśiṣṭaḥ kāyaḥ puruṣaḥ tathā indriya bhāva vyatireka anuvidhānāt indriyāṇāñca iti āśaṅkya āha ajña tvāt iti na hi viduṣaḥ bādhakam upalabhamānasya evam vacāṃsi pravartante iti tathā manyante ebhiḥ iti manāṃsi śarīra indriyāṇi eva teṣām na caitanyam tad karaṇānām ajña tvāt acetana kāraṇa ārabdha tvāt iti arthaḥ iti kecid 
[I,138,3]	atha karaṇānām ajña tvam kutas kārya ajñānāt nanu evam itaretara āśraya tvam na ghaṭa ādi kāryasya acetanatayā ubhaya vādi sampratipatteḥ karaṇānām ajña tvam siddham tad jātīyāḥ ca paramāṇavaḥ śarīra ārambhakāḥ iti acetana kāraṇa ārabdha tve tasya api acetana tvam evam indriyeṣu api yadi ca paramāṇuṣu caitanyam syāt ekasmin eva śarīre puruṣa ānantyāt pratisandhāna ādi vyavahāra uccheda prasaṅgāt 
[I,138,8_I,138,11]	śarīra indriya aṇāñca caitanyasya utpattau anvaya vyatirekau kāraṇa tvāt api sambhavataḥ katham tad ādhāra tvam iti atha evam adṛṣṭa kalpanā doṣaḥ iti ced na pramāṇa upalambhāt tathā hi pratyakṣa vat anumeyasya api arthasya asti eva sadbhāvaḥ tatra śarīrasya caitanya pratiṣedha artham āha na śarīrasya caitanyam iti atra tu caitanyasya pakṣīkaraṇe bhūta kārya tvam asiddham syāt iti śarīram eva pakṣīkriyate tathā hi śarīram para parikalpita caitanya śūnyam bhūta tvāt kārya tvāt ca yat bhūtam yat ca kāryam tat caitanya śūnyam yathā ghaṭaḥ tathā ca śarīram tasmāt acetanam iti 
[I,138,15]	anye tu ekaḥ eva bhūta kārya tvāt iti hetuḥ vivakṣitaḥ iti manyante tat ca asat bhūta tvāt iti uktena eva vyabhicāra abhāvāt atha bhūta kārya tvāt iti ukte asti ātmanā vyabhicāraḥ iti ced na tasya sādhya tvāt siddhe ca vyabhicāraḥ bhavati iti yasya ca ātmā prasiddhaḥ tam pratyanumāna upanyāsaḥ vyarthaḥ eva tathā kārya tvāt iti ukte na asti vyabhicāraḥ iti vyartham eva syāt bhūta padam na ca cetanayā vyabhicāraḥ tasyāḥ caitanya śūnya tvena sa pakṣa tvāt iti hetu dvitayam eva yuktam avayava vyatyaye tu uktam eva pratisamādhānam 
[I,138,21^1]	tathā mṛte ca asambhavāt iti mṛta avasthāyām caitanyasya rūpa ādi vat anupalabdheḥ na śarīra viśeṣa guṇa tvam tathā hi caitamyam śarīra viśeṣa guṇaḥ na bhavati sati śarīre nivartamāna tvāt ye hi sati śarīre nivartante te tad viśeṣa guṇāḥ na bhavanti yathā saṃyoga ādayaḥ ye tu śarīra viśeṣa guṇāḥ te tasmin sati na nivartante yathā rūpa ādayaḥ iti na ca viśeṣa guṇa tva pratiṣedhena sāmānya guṇa tva prāptiḥ pratiyogi apekṣita tvāt pakṣa ādi vyavasthāyāḥ tathā hi caitanyasya pareṇa śarīra viśeṣa guṇa tvam eva iṣṭam tasya eva pratiṣedhaḥ kriyate na ca atra śarīrasya eva pakṣīkaraṇam 
[I,138,21^2]	mṛte ca asambhavāt caitanyasya iti hetoḥ vyadhikaraṇa tā prasaṅgāt tathā indriyāṇām caitanya pratiṣedhaḥ na indriyāṇām caitanyam karaṇa tvāt vā asya ādi vat bhūta tvāt kāryatvāt iti api draṣṭavyam itas api na indriyāṇām caitanyam tad upaghāte api smṛti darśanāt na ca guṇi vināśe guṇasya sadbhāvaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ tathā hi smaraṇam indriya guṇaḥ na bhavati tad vināśe api utpadyamāna tvāt yaḥ yat vināśe api utpadyate sa tasya guṇaḥ na bhavati yathā ghaṭa vināśe api paṭa rūpa ādiḥ iti tathā ca smaraṇam indriya vināśe api bhavati tasmāt na tad guṇaḥ iti 
[I,139,8]	yadi ca indriyāṇām caitanyam syāt karaṇam vinā kriyāyāḥ ca anupalabdheḥ iti karaṇa antaraiḥ bhavitavyam tāni karaṇāni indriyāṇi vivāda āspadāni ca ātmānaḥ iti ekasmin eva śarīre puruṣa bahu tvam abhyupagatam syāt evañca sati devadatta upalabdhe arthe yajñadattasya iva indriya antara upalabdhe arthe na syāt indriya antareṇa pratisandhānam tat tu dṛṣṭam atas na indriyāṇām caitanyam yadi ca ekam indriyam aśeṣa karaṇa adhiṣṭhāyakam cetanam iṣyeta saṃjñā bheda mātram eva syāt 
[I,139,13]	atha viṣaya guṇaḥ caitanyam bhaviṣyati iti tad niṣedha artham āha viṣayāsān nidhye ca anusmṛti darśanāt tathā hi viṣayāsān nidhye tad vināśe vā anusmṛtiḥ dṛṣṭā na ca tad guṇaḥ tad vināśe bhavati iti atha manaḥ guṇaḥ bhaviṣyati iti tad pratiṣedha artham āha na api manasaḥ caitanyam guṇaḥ karaṇa tvāt vā asya ādi vat yat kartṛ manaḥ tat api sukha ādi upalabdhau yadi karaṇa antaram apekṣeta saṃjñā bheda mātram eva syāt tathā hi yat tad sukha ādi upalabdheḥ karaṇam tat eva antaḥkaraṇam yat cetanam manaḥ saḥ eva ātmā syāt atha karaṇa antaram na apekṣate tarhi karaṇa antara anapekṣi tve yugapad a ālocana smṛti prasaṅgaḥ tathā hi manasaḥ caitanye yugapad rūpa rasa sparśa śabda jñānāni prasajyeran cakṣuḥ ādīnām manaḥ sambandhe sati karaṇa antara anapekṣāṇām sva viṣayaiḥ sambandhāt 
[I,139,22_I,139,25]	tathā hi smṛti yaugapadyañca karaṇa anapekṣi tvāt na ca ekasya krameṇa kārya janaka tvam pūrva svarūpasya aparibhraṃśāt na api yugapad eva sarvam kṛtvā punar akaraṇe hetu abhāvāt pratikāryañca pūrva svarūpa vyāvṛtti abhyupagame kṣaṇika tā prasaṅgaḥ atha karaṇasya api manasaḥ caitanyam tat na svayam karaṇa bhāvāt ca iti tathā hi caitanyam pradhāna kriyā sā ca kartari karmaṇi vā samavaiti na karaṇe bhavitum arhati anupalambhāt na hi karaṇam pradhāna kriyā āśrayaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ iti svakīya apekṣayā tu sarvasya kartṛ tvam eva iti tat evam pariśeṣāt ātma kārya tvāt caitanyasya tena ātmā samadhigamyate 
[I,140,4]	kaḥ punar ayam pariśeṣaḥ prasakteṣu śarīra ādiṣu jāti ādiṣu viṣayeṣu caitanya pratiṣedhe tathā tad āśrayasya vyavasthāpanāt nānā tva adhigamāt ākāśa ādīnām eka tvena aprasakteḥ śiṣyate ca dravya antaram iti pariśeṣaḥ kevala vyatireki anumānam tathā ca jñānam kṣiti jala jyotiḥ ākāśa diś kāla manaḥ vyatirikta dravya āśrayam tad vṛttau bādhaka pramāṇa sadbhāve sati guṇa tvāt yaḥ tu tad vyatirikta āśrayaḥ na bhavati na ca asau tad vṛtti bādhaka pramāṇa sadbhāve sati guṇaḥ yathā rūpa ādiḥ na ca tathā jñānam tasmāt vyatirikta āśrayam iti 
[I,140,10]	nanu sarvam etat asambaddham kṣaṇika tvena āśraya āśrayi bhāva anupapatteḥ tathā ca padārthānām artha kriyayā sattvam vyāptam sā ca krama yaugapadyābhyām akṣaṇikeṣu na sambhavati krameṇa janaka tvam eka svarūpa tvāt yat eva hi pūrva kārya utpattau svarūpam tat eva uttara kāryeṣu api iti sarveṣām eka tā prasaṅgaḥ kāraṇa vailakṣaṇyam vinā kārya vailakṣaṇyasya aśakya sādhana tvāt 
[I,140,14]	atha kārya vailakṣaṇyāt eva jñāyate pratikāryam pūrva svarūpa nivṛttau anyat eva svarūpam bhāvānām bhavati iti tarhi svarūpasya avasthāna anabhyupagamāt tathā asattva prasaṅgaḥ atha avasthitasya api krama yaugapadyābhyām sahakāri prāptau tathā eva janaka tvam iti ced na tasya tasmin atiśaya ādhāyaka tvena atiśaya nivartaka tvena ca tayoḥ avyatirekāt anya tvam eva vyatireke api tad bhāve api bhāvasya katham kāryasya janaka tvam dṛṣṭam iti na hi artha antara janmani artha antarasya kriyā janaka tvam dṛṣṭam iti anupakārake vastuni apekṣā eva na syāt iti sahakāri tva abhāvaḥ atha sahakāriṇām api sahakāri antara adhīnam sāmarthyam tat api yadi sahakāri antarāt iti anavasthā eva syāt atha sahakāri antaram vinā eva sahakāriṇām svatas eva sāmarthyam iti ced etat ca anyatra api samānam iti alam 
[I,140,23_I,141,1]	tat evam akṣaṇikebhyaḥ vyāvartamāna artha kriyā sva vyāptam sattvam gṛhītvā vyāvartate iti asantaḥ akṣaṇikāḥ tat evam bādhaka upalambhāt para pakṣaḥ eva akṣaṇika śaṅkā vyavaccheda siddhau sattvam eva kṣaṇika sādhanam iti tathā nirhetuka tvāt vināśasya utpatti anantaram eva abhāvaḥ iti kṣaṇika tvam nanu mudgara ādi vyāpāreṇa ghaṭa ādi vināśasya utpāda upalambhāt ayuktam eva tat na ātma bhāga saṅgatau tad vyāpārāt yadi ca hetoḥ artha antara bhūtaḥ vināśaḥ utpādyeta tadā tad abhāvasya anupalambhaḥ na syāt tad svarūpasya aparibhraṃśāt tathā abhāvasya eva kārya janaka tva abhyupagame bhāva rūpa tva prasaṅgaḥ ca 
[I,141,5]	na ca artha antara tva aviśeṣāt tasmin upajāte kasyacid bhāvasya anupalambhaḥ na sarvasya iti viśeṣa hetuḥ asti na api kāraṇa apekṣitāyām avaśyambhāvaḥ syāt vastre rāgasya iva sa apekṣi tvā avaśyambhāvi tvayoḥ virodhāt tathā hi vastre rāgaḥ sampadyamānaḥ kāraṇa sadbhāvāt bhavati abhāve na bhavati evam kvacid vastunaḥ vināśaḥ hetu pratibandhāt abhāvāt vā vināśi tvam api syāt yadi ca avinaśvara svarūpāṇām ahetutaḥ vināśaḥ gagana ādīnām api nitya tayā abhyupagatānām vināśaḥ prasajyeta atha naṅkṣoḥ bhāvasya hetu tā tatas vināśa vat kim tad kalpanayā tad svarūpa tvāt eva avaśyam vinā api hetum vināśaḥ bhavati iti 
[I,141,13_I,141,16]	yadi karaṇa kārya tvañca syāt vināśasya kṛtaka tvāt tad vināśe avaśyam bhāva unmajjanam syāt tasmāt na tasya kiñcid bhavati na bhavati eva kevalam iti bhāva lakṣaṇa sthita dharma anāśaḥ iti na ca akṣaṇika tve pratyabhijñānam pramāṇam tasya kalpanā jñāna tvāt tat etat sarvam avidita artham kalpanā jñānasya pūrvam eva nirasta tvāt 
[I,141,18_I,141,21]	atha saḥ eva ayam iti jñāne viruddha ullekhāt eka tvam ayuktam tathā hi saḥ iti atīta ākāram jñānam ayam iti ca vartamāna ākāram na ca viruddha ākārayoḥ ekatra sambhavaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ iti tat asat ākāra vāda pratiṣedhe pūrva anubhava janita saṃskāra smaraṇa sahakāri indriyeṇa saḥ eva ayam iti ubhaya ullekhi jñānam janyate tasya ca artha anvaya vyatireka anuvidhānāt nirviṣaya tvam ayuktam 
[I,141,24]	atha astu pratyabhijñānāt avasthāyi tvam arthānām artha kriyā kāritvantu katham sahakāri sānnidhye sati iti tathā hi krameṇa sahakāri sadbhāve sati krameṇa janaka tvam yugapad sadbhāve ca yugapad ca iti yat ca uktam kim tasya sahakāriṇā kriyate iti na kiñcid kim tarhi sadbhāve kāryam eva anyathā sahakāri tva ayogāt yat vā tasya sāmarthyāt kāraka sākalyam eva kriyate tad sadbhāve kārya jananāt asāmarthyantu vaikalyam nivartate sākalya vaikalyayoḥ paraspara sadbhāva sthiti virodhāt na ca tayoḥ āvirbhāva tirobhāvābhyām arthasya tathā abhāva prasaṅgaḥ tayoḥ tad vyatirekāt 
[I,142,6]	na ca sahakāriṇām artha antara tva aviśeṣāt aviśeṣeṇa sarva bhāva sahakāri tvam niyatasya eva sadbhāve bhāva vyatirekābhyām kārya janaka tva darśanāt na api sahakāriṇām sahakāri antarāt sāmarthyam tad nirapekṣāṇām api parasparasānnidhye tad samudāyasya eka kārya janakatva upalabdheḥ dṛṣṭañca cakṣu ūru upāloka manaskārāṇām paraspara sānnidhye sati eka kārya janaka tvam 
[I,142,11]	na ca atra itara ādhipatyena antya avasthāyām atiśayaḥ sampadyate iti vācyam avyatireke tad abhāvāt na hi saḥ eva tasya eva atiśayaḥ bhavati iti tathā atiśaya rahitānām atiśaya janaka tvam iti kārya antare api na bādhā asti atha atiśaya yuktānām atiśaya janaka tvam evam tarhi teṣām api anyasmāt atiśayaḥ sampadyate iti abhyupagame anavasthāyām vivakṣita kārya anutpatti prasaṅgaḥ tasmāt sahakāriṇām paraspara sānnidhyam eva atiśayaḥ iti yuktam utpaśyāmaḥ tat evam kārya vailakṣaṇyam sāmagrī vailakṣaṇyāt bhavati iti na pratikāryam anya tvam bhāvānām 
[I,142,17_I,142,20]	yaḥ ca ayamakṣaṇikānām krama yaugapadyābhyām artha kriyā pratiṣedhaḥ sa viśeṣa pratiṣedhasya avaśyam śeṣa abhyanujñāyām samarthaḥ iti prakāra antareṇa artha kriyā prasaṅgaḥ na ca tat asattva grāhakam pramāṇam asti iti tathā paraspara ādhipatyena kārya janaka tva abhyupagamāt rūpa ādīnām ekaikam aneka rūpa ādeḥ yugapad kāraṇam iti abhyupagame yaugapadya pratiṣedhāt eva tad antarbhūtaḥ kramaḥ niṣiddhaḥ iti tasya sva śabdena punarvacanam punaruktam eva syāt tathā hi yathā rūpam yugapad rūpa rasa gandha sparśān ārabhate tathā rasa ādayaḥ api ekaika vivakṣāyām tatra eva kramaḥ iti ekasya eva pratiṣedhaḥ vācyaḥ na ca ekam ekasmāt eva utpadyate tadārabhate ca iti niyamaḥ sambhavati 
[I,142,25]	na ca anyathā ekasya krameṇa aneka kārya janaka tvam pratikṣaṇam anya tva abhyupagamāt tasmāt sahakāri sadbhāve sati krama yaugapadyābhyām artha kriyā jananāt akṣaṇikānām na asattvam iti na api nānātvam iti sattvāt iti hetoḥ avyatirekaḥ na ca pakṣaḥ eva tasya vyatirekaḥ tasya rūpa antara tvāt yat ca idam akṣaṇika tvena virodhāt bhāvat ka pakṣaḥ eva akṣaṇika śaṅkā vyavaccheda siddhaḥ bādhakaḥ iti etat asat virodhi pratipattim antareṇa virodha pratipatteḥ ayogāt atha akṣaṇikaḥ tad virodhī pratīyate eva sa tarhi pratipatti rūpa artha kriyā kāri tvāt asat na bhavati iti katham asya asmāt vyatirekaḥ yadi ca akṣaṇika śaṅkā vyavacchedaḥ bādhakāt eva pratīyeta sattvāt iti hetoḥ vaiyarthyam syāt tasya api atad rūpa vyavaccheda viṣaya tvāt iti atha maulena hetunā kṣaṇika tvam eva sādhyate tat ca yadi sva lakṣaṇa ādi bhinnam katham anumāna paricchedyam tasya hi sāmānya viṣaya tvāt iti 
[I,143,9]	na ca sattvāt iti hetoḥ sa pakṣa vipakṣābhyām anvaya vyatirekābhyām antareṇa gamaka tvam nyāyyam asādhāraṇasya api gamaka tva prasaṅgāt sarvasya ca pakṣa antarbhāvāt sa pakṣa vipakṣa abhāvaḥ eva atha kalpanā samāropita tvāt pakṣa ādi vyavasthāyāḥ kalpanā samāropite sa pakṣe anvayaḥ tad āropitaḥ eva vipakṣe vyatirekaḥ iti gamaka tvam evam tarhi kalpanā samāropita pakṣa ādi vyavasthā apekṣam kālpanikam anumānam iti avāstavam kṣaṇika tvam eva syāt 
[I,143,14]	atha vināśasya nirhetuka tvena kṣaṇika tvam tat na nirhetuka tvasya api katipaya kāla avasthāyi tvena vināśe virodha abhāvāt na ca nirhetuka tvam yuktam bhāvaḥ iva abhāve api anvaya vyatirekābhyām hetoḥ vyāpāra upalambhāt atha mudgara ādi vyāpārāt kapāla santānasya utpādaḥ na tasya virodhi utpanna tvāt na ca kapāla santānaḥ tasya āvaraṇam iti prāk iva tad kāle api upalabhyeta āvaraṇa tve api tad vināśe tasya upalambhaḥ syāt na ca kapāla santānena ghaṭasya virodhaḥ tad kāraṇa tvāt kapālānām 
[I,143,20]	atha artha antare vināśe bhāvasya upalambhaḥ iti uktam tat na tayoḥ saha avasthiti virodhāt tathā hi bhāve tu utpanne abhāvasya agrahaṇam tad kāle tu bhāvasya iti dṛṣṭam nanu evam ghaṭa kāle tad prāgabhāvasya vināśe tasya api anyaḥ prāgabhāvaḥ tasya api anyaḥ vināśaḥ iti anavasthā syāt tad bhāve api na doṣaḥ kārya niṣpatteḥ darśanāt iti kecid 
[I,143,24_I,144,1]	anye tu anavasthāyām kila kāryasya parisamāptiḥ na syāt iti ghaṭa tad prāgabhāva vināśayoḥ ekaḥ eva prāc abhāvaḥ iti manyante guravaḥ tu ghaṭa kāle tad prāgabhāvasya anupalabdheḥ saḥ eva tasya pratiṣedhaḥ prāgabhāvaḥ tu ghaṭasya iti tayoḥ saha avasthiti virodhāt iti bruvate atha abhāvasya artha antara tva aviśeṣāt tasmin upajāte sarveṣām anupalambhaḥ svāt na tasmin utpanne kasyacid anupalambhena tayoḥ eva virodha siddheḥ yathā artha antara tva aviśeṣe api kiñcid eva kāraṇam kasyacid eva kāryasya hetuḥ na tu sarvasya iti pratiniyamaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ tadvat abhāvasya niyatena eva bhāvena virodhaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ iti adūṣaṇam etat 
[I,144,5]	yat ca idam vināśasya kāraṇa apekṣitāyām avaśyambhāvaḥ na syāt iti vastre rāgasya iva sa apekṣi tvā avaśyambhāvi tvayoḥ virodhāt tat asat ekatra vyabhicāreṇa sarvatra tathā abhāvasya anupalabdheḥ tathā sa apekṣi tve api sa vitṛ graha nakṣatra tārāṇāñca udaya astamaya upalabdheḥ nirapekṣa tve ca udaya anantaram eva astamayaḥ syāt samarthasya upakṣepa ayogāt iti avaśyañcaḥ uditasya savituḥ astamayaḥ bhavati iti 
[I,144,10_I,144,14]	atha uktam naṅkṣoḥ bhāvasya vināśa abhyupagame kim hetunā iti tatra vināśa ātmaka tva asambhavāt avaśyam naṅkṣoḥ vināśa yogyasya eva hetau sati vināśaḥ na gagana ādeḥ iti tathā sva kāraṇāt itthambhūtaḥ eva utpannaḥ bhāvaḥ yena asya avaśyam vināśa hetunā bhavitavyam iti atha tarhi kāraṇāt utpadyamāna tvāt abhāvasya bhāvāt aviśeṣa prasaṅgaḥ tat na svarūpa bhedasya upapatteḥ yathā hi kāraṇāt utpadyamānāḥ rūpa ādayaḥ parasparam svarūpa bhedāt bhidyante tathā abhāvaḥ api bhāvāt iti asti ca dravya ādi ṣaṣ lakṣaṇa ālakṣita tvam bhāva pāratantryeṇa gṛhyamāṇa tvam abhāvasya rūpam iti 
[I,144,18_I,144,23]	atha utpattimat tvāt abhāvasya vināśe bhāva unmajjana prasaṅgaḥ iti uktam tat na sadbhāva dharma vilakṣaṇa tvāt abhāva dharmāṇām yathā ca anutpattimataḥ prāgabhāvasya vināśaḥ tathā utpattiḥ dharmiṇaḥ api vināśasya avināśaḥ iti na ca vināśa vināśe bhāva unmajjanam tasya atad rūpa tvāt atad kāraṇa tvāt ca tathā hi ghaṭa vināśa vināśaḥ na ghaṭa rūpaḥ na api tat kāraṇam iti katham tasya unmajjana prasaṅgaḥ na ca bhāvasya asattvam pratyakṣa ādi pramāṇaiḥ vyavasīyamāna tvāt tathā hi iha bhū tale ghaṭaḥ na asti iti jñānam indriya bhāva vyatireka anuvidhānāt indriya jam na ca nirviṣayaḥ ghaṭa abhāva viśiṣṭa bhū tala ālambana tvāt 
[I,145,1]	atha ghaṭa vivikta bhū tala upalambhaḥ eva ghaṭa anupalambhaḥ na abhāvāt iti ced avyatireke tu ghaṭa avaṣṭabdhe api bhū tale syāt na asti iti jñānam tasmāt ghaṭa abhāva upalambhaḥ eva ghaṭasya anupalambhaḥ na upalambha abhāva mātram iti na ca vināśa anabhyupagame bhāvasya prāk iva paścāt api avasthānāt anupalambhaḥ ghaṭate atha kṣaṇa sthāyi tvāt eva dvitīya kṣaṇe tasya anavasthānam iti tarhi saḥ eva tasya abhāvaḥ yat sadbhāve dvitīya kṣaṇe tasya anupalambhaḥ iti anyathā hi indriyā ādeḥ tādavasthyāt vināśa abhāve nityasya anupalambhaḥ na syāt 
[I,145,7]	yat ca idam na tasya kiñcid bhavati na bhavati eva kevalam iti unmatta bhāṣitam etat anutpanna vināśasya pūrvam api upalambhaḥ na syāt vinaṣṭa tvāt eva abhāvena ca avirodhe paścāt api avasthānam iti nitya tvam syāt tathā kṣaṇika tve sati anubhavituḥ vinaṣṭa tvāt anyasya smaraṇam na syāt na hi devadatta anubhūte arthe yajñadattasya smaraṇam iti 
[I,145,11]	atha nānā santāneṣu kārya kāraṇa bhāvasya abhāvāt asmaraṇam ekaḥ ca santāne buddhīnām asti kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ iti āhita sakala pūrva vāsanākam kārya jñānam utpadyate iti kāraka anubhūte arthe tasya smaraṇam yuktam eva na etat evam kārya kāraṇa bhāve api nānā tvasya tādavasthyāt devadatta ādi santāneṣu iva katham syāt smaraṇam na ca santāna sadbhāve pramāṇam asti buddheḥ buddhi antara kārya tve pramāṇa abhāvāt 
[I,145,16]	atha asti bodhāt bodha rūpa tā iti ced tathā hi bodha rūpam kāryam bodhāt eva bhavati yathā śuklāt śuklam ityādi nanu evam tarhi dhūmasya agni janya tvam na syāt samāna jātīyasya dhūma kṣaṇasya bhāvāt atha vilakṣaṇāt api agni kṣaṇāt dhūmasya utpattiḥ iṣyeta bodhasya api vilakṣaṇāt śarīra ādeḥ utpattiḥ bhaviṣyati iti na bodha antara sadbhāve pramāṇam asti atha kiñcid sadṛśa tayā agniḥ dhūmasya kāraṇam tadā jñāna utpattau śarīra ādau api samānam tathā kṛṣṇāt api śuklasya utpattiḥ bhavet kiñcid sādṛśya sadbhāvāt 
[I,145,22]	atyanta samāna jātīyañca samanantara kāraṇam iti abhyupagamyamāne rūpa jñānāt eva rūpa jñānam rasa jñānāt eva rasa jñānam sukhāt eva sukham duḥkhāt eva duḥkham iti santān a ānantyam syāt na ca asti saṃvedanam iti atha eteṣām yugapada saṃvedanam ananubhūyamāna kṣaṇānām utpatteḥ tarhi tena vinā tasya anutpatteḥ tad santānaḥ api abhyupagantavyaḥ tathā ca sati tadā eva teṣām saṃvedanañca iti prāptam na ca etat asti tasmāt na sarvam jñānam jñāna antara janyam iti pratibandhaḥ asti 
[I,146,1_I,146,5]	na ca vināśasya avyatirekāt anubhavasya avasthāne smaraṇam yuktam atha dvitīya kṣaṇe tasya anubhavasya abhāvāt anavasthānam iti ced na avyatireke hi tena avirodhāt avasthānam eva vyatireke tu saha avasthiti virodha abhyupagame asmad darśana anupraveśaḥ tasmāt smaraṇam avasthitam ātmānam prasādhayati iti na ca kṣaṇika tve sati kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ ghaṭate tathā ca yadā eva kāryasya utpādaḥ tadā eva kāraṇasya vināśaḥ sa ca utpādāt na bhidyate iti abhyupagame saha utpannayoḥ na syāt kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ savya itarayoḥ viṣāṇayoḥ iva vinaśyat avasthañca kāraṇam iṣṭam vaiśeṣikaiḥ vināśasya hetumat tvāt 
[I,146,9_I,146,15]	nirhetuka vināśa vādināñca bhāva vināśa vyatirekeṇa vinaśyat avasthānam sambhavati eva tasya vināśa kāraṇa sākalya rūpa tvāt na api sva saṃvid vādinaḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāva grahaṇam asti kāraṇa saṃvidaḥ sva ātmani eva paryavasānāt tathā kārya saṃvidaḥ api iti na kāraṇa jñānam kārya sattām anubhavati tad sattā kāle tasya atīta tvāt na ca jñāna antaram ekam kāraṇa sattā kāle kārya sattām tad abhāve ca asattām vijānāti iti atha kārya kāraṇa jñānābhyām vāsanā krameṇa asti vikalpa jñānam kārya kāraṇa bhāva grāhakam iti ced tasya api etad rūpa samāropa tva abhyupagame apramāṇa tvena kārya kāraṇa bhāvasya asiddhiḥ eva tathā hi yat yatra samāropyate tat tatra avāstavam eva yathā śaṅkhe pīta ādiḥ iti 
[I,146,18]	atha pūrva upalabdha anusandhānam vikalpam iti ced evam tarhi kārya kāraṇa bhāva grahaṇam vinā na vāsanā tad abhāvāt tad adhyavasāya vikalpaḥ katham bhaviṣyati iti anubhava anurūpa tvāt vāsanāyāḥ na ca bodhāt anyā vāsanā sambhavati iti ukta pūrvam tasmāt avasthitam pratisandhā tāram antareṇa tu kārya kāraṇa bhāvasya agrahaṇam eva iti ayantu kṣaṇa bhaṅgaḥ asmad gurubhiḥ vistareṇa nirastaḥ iti na iha pratanyate tat evam akṣaṇika tve satya āśraya āśrayi bhāvasya upapattau satyām etat pariśeṣāt vijñānasya ātma āśrita tvam iti 
[I,146,24]	tathā pravṛtti nivṛttibhyām ātmā jñāyate kiṃviśiṣṭābhyām śarīra samavāyinībhyām hita ahita prāpti parihāra yogyābhyām iti hitam sukham ahitam duḥkham tayoḥ prāpti parihārau tad yogyābhyām tat samarthābhyām iti vyāpti pratipādana artham āha rathakarmaṇā sārathiḥ rathasya adhiṣṭhātā tadvat ātmā vigrahasya śarīrasya adhiṣṭhātā anumīyate tathā hi jīvat śarīram prayatna vat adhiṣṭhitam jīvat śarīra samavāyi hita ahita prāpti parihāra samartha pravṛtti nivṛtti āśraya tvāt ratha vat pravṛtti nivṛtti āśraya tvam vāyu ādau vyabhicarati iti hita ahita prāpti parihāra samartha padam tathā śākhāyantra nipīḍitasya prāṇinaḥ śākhā akarma ahita nivartakam adhastanasya phala ādi prāpteḥ hita prāpakañca iti tad artham śarīra samavāyi padam tathā api nadī srotaḥ patita śava karmaṇā vyabhicāraḥ tat api adhastanasya śunaḥ tad upayogāt sukham bhakṣyate iti sukha prāpakam upariṣṭāt ca snānam kurvataḥ tapasvinaḥ durgandha tayā duḥkham janayati iti tat nivartakañcā iti tad artham jīvat śarīra padam 
[I,147,10]	nanu evam api idam viśeṣaṇam vipakṣāt iva sa pakṣa ādeḥ api ratha ādeḥ nirvṛttim darśayati iti asādhāraṇa tvam eva syāt na hi rathe jīvat śarīra samaveta kriyā āśraya tvam asti atha jīvat śarīra samavāyi hita ahita prāpti parihāra yogyā kriyā prayatna vat kāryā viśiṣṭa kriyā tvāt ratha kriyā vat iti iha api na sa viśeṣaṇasya hetoḥ sa pakṣa sadbhāvaḥ tathā suptasya nauvā ārūḍhasya yathā ukta viśeṣaṇa kriyāḥ abhipretena prāpti hetuḥ ahitena nivṛtti hetuḥ ca na ca prayatna vat kārya iti vyabhicāraḥ tasmāt icchā anuvidhāyi kriyā āśraya tvam hetuḥ iti tathā hi jīvat śarīram prayatna vat adhiṣṭhitam icchā anuvidhāyi kriyā āśraya tvāt ratha vat kriyā vā prayatna vat kāryā icchā anuvidhāyi kriyā tvāt ratha kriyāvat 
[I,147,18_I,147,21]	tathā prāṇa ādibhiḥ ca iti prāṇa apāna nimeṣa unmeṣa jīvana manaḥ gati indriya antara vikārāḥ sukha duḥkha icchā dveṣa prayatnāḥ ca ātma liṅgāni iti sūtram darśayati atha ātmanā sārdham anupalabdheḥ katham eṣām gamaka tvam iti āha śarīra parigṛhīte vāyau vikṛta karma darśanāt bhastrā ādhmāpayitā iva anumīyate iti vyāpti pratipādanam etat prayogaḥ tu jīvat śarīram prayatna vat adhiṣṭhitam jīvat śarīra parigṛhīta vikṛta vāyu āśraya tvāt bhastrāvat vāyu āśraya tvam anyeṣām api asti iti vikṛta grahaṇam vikāraḥ tu tiryak gati śīlasya vāyoḥ yat etat ūrdhvam adhas ca gamanam tathā api vāyuḥ vāyu antareṇa pratihataḥ ūrdhvam gacchati iti parigṛhīta padam tathā hi antar suṣira vṛkṣe chidra pradeśena praviṣṭasya vāyoḥ ūrdhvam adhas ca gamanam sambhavati iti śarīra padam tathā api śuṣka anubaddha śarīre praviṣṭasya vikāraḥ sambhavati iti jīva grahaṇam 
[I,148,1_I,148,5]	nanu evam api jīvat śarīra parigṛhīta vikṛta vāyu āśraya tvam bhastrā ādeḥ na sambhavati iti sādhana vikalatā prasaṅgaḥ tat na bhastrā sādharmyāt bhastrā śabdena mahiṣī śarīrasya vivakṣita tvāt upacāreṇa yathā hi bhastrā dhmāpyate prayatnavatā tathā mahiṣī śarīram iti dṛṣṭam atas sādhya sādhana adhikaraṇa tvam yat vā jīvat śarīra parigṛhīta vikṛtaḥ vāyuḥ prayatna vat adhiṣṭhitaḥ jīvat śarīra parigṛhīta vikṛta vāyu tvāt bhastrā parigṛhīta vikṛta vāyu vat yathā ukta vikṛta vāyu karma prayatna vat kāryam yathā uktasya vāyoḥ vikṛta karma tvāt bhastrā parigṛhīta vikṛta vāyu karma vat

[I,149,1]	yat ca idam pāda prasāraṇa ādi tat ayasaḥ ayaskānta abhisarpaṇa vat vastu svābhāvyāt bhaviṣyati iti āgamaḥ tu sulabha tvāt upacāreṇa api vyākhyātum śakyataḥ eva iti anaikāntika tvam eva atha tad adhiṣṭhāyakasya sadbhāvāt na anaikāntika tvam iti ced na tasya loṣṭa ādiṣu api sadbhāvena vṛddhi kṣata bhagna saṃrohaṇa ādi prasaṅgāt 
[I,149,5_I,149,10]	tat etat sarvam asāmpratam vṛkṣa ādeḥ api pakṣa antarbhāvāt na ca sādhyena eva sādhanasya vyabhicāraḥ na api sūtra vyāghātaḥ tatra api pravṛtti nivṛttyoḥ sadbhāvāt tathā ca dravya sannidhāne ca pāda prasāraṇam na vastu svābhāvyāt śarīre api tad bhāva prasaṅgāt niyata dravya abhilāṣaḥ ca vṛkṣāyurvede paripaṭhitaḥ teṣām jñāyate tad upabhoge puṣpa ādi darśanāt āgamasya ca aupacārika tvam ayuktam mukhye bādhaka anupapatteḥ iti alam atha vālukā ādi nicayeṣu prayatnam vinā api vṛddheḥ upalambhāt vyabhicāraḥ na īśvara prayatnasya tatra api sadbhāva abhyupagamāt tasya api pakṣe antarbhāvāt śarīra vat puruṣa guṇa pūrvaka tvam sadhanīyam iti 
[I,149,13^1]	tathā abhimata viṣaya grāhaka karaṇa sambandha nimittena manaḥ karmaṇā gṛha koṇeṣu pelaka prerakaḥ iva dārakaḥ ātmā anumīyate iti vyāpti pratipādanam eva yathā hi gṛhe dārakaḥ pelakaiḥ saṃkrīḍamānaḥ hasta sthita pelakena madhyastha pelakam abhihatya pelaka antareṇa sambandhayati tadvat ātmā api śarīre manasā cakṣuḥ ādikam abhihatya viṣayaiḥ saṃyojayati iti tathā ca abhimataḥ ca asau viṣayaḥ ca rūpa ādiḥ tat gṛhṇāti iti tad grāhakam tat ca grahaṇam cakṣuḥ ādi tena saha sambandhaḥ tad nimittena manaḥ karmaṇā jñāyate prayogaḥ tu jīvat śarīram prayatna vat adhiṣṭhitam abhimata viṣaya grāhaka karaṇa ādhāra tvāt 
[I,149,13^2]	gṛha vat manaḥ vā prayatna preryam abhimata viṣaya grāhaka karaṇa sambandhi tvāt hasta sthita pelaka vat manaḥ karma vā prayatna vat kāryam abhimata viṣaya grāhaka karaṇa sambandhi karma tvāt hasta sthita pelaka karma vat manasaḥ vā cakṣuḥ ādi sambandhaḥ prayatna vat kāryaḥ abhimata viṣaya grāhaka karaṇa sambandha tvāt pelaka antara sambandhi sambandha vat cakṣuḥ ādayaḥ vā prayatna vat preryāḥ abhimata viṣaya grāhaka karaṇa tvāt pelaka antara vat viṣaya sambandhaḥ vā prayatna vat kāryaḥ abhimata viṣaya grāhaka karaṇa sambandhi sambandha tvāt koṇa sthita pelaka sambandha vat 
[I,149,26]	tathā nayana viṣaya ālocana anantaram rasa anusmṛti krameṇa rasana vikriyā darśanāt aneka gavākṣa antargata prekṣaka vat ubhaya darśī kaścid ekaḥ vijñāyate iti vyāpti pratipādanam eva tathā hi yena rūpa ādi viśiṣṭa rasa avinābhāvitayā upalabdham tasya nayana viṣaya ālocana anantaram iti nayanasya viṣayaḥ rūpam tatra ālocanāt vijñānam tad anantaram avinābhūte rase anusmṛtiḥ bhavati tad krameṇa rasana vikriyā iti rasa anusmaraṇa anantaram rasa buddhiḥ tatas prayatne sati manasi kriyā prabandhāt rasanā indriya sambandhaḥ tasmāt radana antargata udaka saṃplava lakṣaṇaḥ vikāraḥ sampadyate iti utpatti kramaḥ 
[I,150,6_I,150,9]	jñaptikramaḥ tu rasanā indriya vikārān manaḥ sambandhaḥ tena api manasi kriyā prabandhaḥ anumīyate tasmāt prayatnaḥ tatas api icchā tathā ca smaraṇam tatas saṃskāraḥ tasmāt ca anubhavaḥ tena anubhavena anubhavitā iti atra tu mama iti pratisaṃdhānam sarvatra upalabdham iti eka kartṛka tvam niścīyate bhinna kartṛkeṣu mama iti pratisandhāna vyāvṛtteḥ na hi devadatta ādiṣu utpannāḥ smaraṇa ādayaḥ yajñadattena mama smaraṇam mama icchā iti saṃvedyante indriyāṇa an tu pratiniyata viṣaya tvāt sāhacarya anupalabdhau indriya antareṇa upalabdhe arthe na syāt indriya antareṇa smaraṇam tad abhāvāt rasanā indriyasya vikāra asambhavaḥ eva syāt sa ca upalabdhaḥ iti ubhaya darśī ekaḥ jñāyate 
[I,150,14]	atha śarīrasya eva cakṣūrasana adhiṣṭhāyaka tve rūpa rasayoḥ sāhacarya upalabdhau smaraṇam iti ced na tasya api anyatvāt tathā hi kuvalaya āmalaka bilva ādīnām iva parimāṇa bhedasya śarīre sadbhāvāt anya tvam na hi anya parimāṇe api avatiṣṭhamāne parimāṇavati parimāṇa pratiṣedhāt uttara parimāṇena śakyam bhavitum iti parimāṇāni atha anupapattyā pūrva parimāṇa nivṛttiḥ sā ca āśraya vināśāt eva iti anya tvam na ca śarīrasya śarīra antara ārambhaka tvam ekasya ārambhaka tva pratiṣedhāt kārya kāraṇa virodhena sarveṣām upalambha prasaṅgāt atha avasthā bheda mātram na avasthāyinaḥ bhedaḥ iti ced tat na yadi avasthā parimāṇam tad bhede tasya api avaśyam bhedaḥ atha avayava viśeṣaḥ tad vināśe api tad ā ārabdhasya vināśāt na api rūpa ādayaḥ teṣām api āśraya vināśena vināśāt na ca saṃyogi samavāyi vā dharma antaram asti iti śarīrasya anya tvena smaraṇa ādi asambhavaḥ eva 
[I,150,24]	atha buddhau kāraṇa vāsanā saṅkrānti krameṇa smaraṇa utpattau rasanā indriya vikāraḥ sampadyate iti ced na kṣaṇika tve sati smaraṇasya pūrvam eva pratiṣedhāt tasmāt eka kartṛkāḥ smaraṇa icchā ādayaḥ mama iti pratisandhīyamāna tvāt vibhinna kartṛkeṣu pratisandhāna abhāvaḥ eka kartṛkeṣu tu nartakī bhrū vikṣepe kṛta samayānām asti mama iti pratisandhānam 
[I,151,1]	atha nityasya anupakāri tvāt ātmanaḥ kim anubhava ādyaiḥ kriyate iti ced na kiñcid anubhava ādeḥ eva upakāri tvāt tena hi satā anubhavitā smartā iti vyapadeśāt tat kāryam vā tasya upakāraḥ tathā ca anubhavena tasya saṃskāraḥ kriyate tena tu smaraṇam upakāraḥ tena api sva kāryam iti uttarottaram abhyūhyam na ca anubhava ādeḥ āvirbhāva tirobhāvābhyām anubhavituḥ tathā abhāvaḥ tad vyatirekāt atha vyatireke katham ātmanaḥ anubhava ādiḥ na anyasya iti ced tena sambandhāt sambandhasya tu sambandha antara anapekṣasya api sambandhi niṣṭhasya upalabdheḥ na api anavasthā iti vakṣyāmaḥ 
[I,151,8]	na ca anyasya anubhava utpāde anyasya anubhavitā iti vyapadeśaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ atha anubhava ādeḥ ātmani atiśaya ādhāyaka tva asambhave vyapadeśa asambhavaḥ iti ced na asya eva atiśaya tvāt tad prāc abhāvaḥ ca anatiśayaḥ nivartate iti kāraka sākalī añca atiśayaḥ tat vaikalyañcān atiśayaḥ iti ukta pūrvam na ca avyatireke atiśayaḥ sambhāvyate iti alam ati vistareṇa 
[I,151,12]	tathā pūrva uktaiḥ sukha duḥkha icchā dveṣa prayatnaiḥ ca guṇaiḥ guṇyanumīyate tathā hi sukha ādayaḥ kvacid āśritāḥ guṇa tvāt rūpa ādi vat atha śarīra indriya guṇāḥ bhaviṣyanti iti atas āha te ca na śarīra indriya guṇāḥ kasmāt iti āha ahaṅkāreṇa eka vākya tva abhāvāt iti aham pratyayena asamāna adhikaraṇa tvāt vijñāma vat ye tu śarīra indriya guṇāḥ te ahaṅkāreṇa samāna adhikaraṇāḥ na bhavanti rūpa ādayaḥ iti 
[I,151,17^1]	atha rūpavān aham iti pratyaya darśanāt yuktam eva tat na mukhye bādhaka sadbhāvena asya gauṇa tvāt tathā ca na aham iti pratyaya ālambana tvam pūrvam eva uktam iti śarīra guṇaiḥ upacaritam eva sāmānādhikaraṇyam smaraṇa jñānena tu sāmānādhikaraṇyam aham smartā iti dṛṣṭam na ca smaraṇam śarīre samavetam iti uktam itas ca na śarīra indriya guṇāḥ sukha ādayaḥ pradeśa vṛtti tvāt viśeṣa guṇāḥ ca āśraya vyāpakāḥ rūpa ādayaḥ iti śarīra viśeṣa guṇa pratiṣedhe sādhye na saṃyoga ādibhiḥ anekāntaḥ teṣām api ca pakṣa tvāt tathā na śarīra indriya viśeṣa guṇāḥ sukha ādayaḥ yāvat dravya abhāvi tvāt śabda vat ye tu tad viśeṣa guṇāḥ te yāvat dravya bhāvinaḥ rūpa ādayaḥ iti na ca pārthiva paramāṇu rūpa ādibhiḥ vyabhicāraḥ 
[I,151,17^2]	teṣām api sādhya adhikaraṇa tayā sa pakṣa tvāt tathā hi śarīra indriya viśeṣa guṇa pratiṣedhe sādhye te api saṃyoga ādi vat tad viśeṣa guṇāḥ na bhavanti iti sa pakṣāḥ eva itas api na śarīra indriya viśeṣa guṇāḥ sukha ādayaḥ bāhya indriya apratyakṣa tvāt vijñāna vat ye tu tad viśeṣa guṇāḥ te bāhya indriya pratyakṣāḥ rūpa ādayaḥ iti guru tva ādīn āntu bāhya indriya apratyakṣa tve api na śarīra indriya viśeṣa guṇa tvam iti vyabhicāra abhāvaḥ bāhya indriya pratiṣedhena ca antaḥkaraṇa pratyakṣa tvam vivakṣitam iti tathā śarīra viśeṣa guṇāḥ ca pratyakṣāḥ na ca evam sukha ādayaḥ iti atha triguṇa ātmaka tvāt sarvam sukha duḥkha ādi samanvitam iti na ātma viśeṣa guṇa tvam na triguṇa ātmaka tva pratiṣedhasya vakṣyamāṇa tvāt pradhāna pratiṣedha avasare 
[I,152,6]	yathā ca sukha duḥkha ādibhiḥ guṇaiḥ tathā aham śabdena api ātmā jñāyate iti ahamśabdaḥ abādhita eka pada tvāt avaśyam vācyam apekṣate na ca pṛthivī ādi eva abhidheyam pṛthivī ādi śabda vyatirekāt vaiyadhikaraṇyam iti yadi punar pṛthivī ādikam artham abhidadhyāt aham iti śabdaḥ tad śabdena sāmānādhikaraṇyam syāt aham pṛthivī aham udakam ityādi na ca etat dṛṣṭam tasmāt ātmani eva aham iti śabdasya pravṛttiḥ yuktā iti viṣaya antare hi pravartamānaḥ śabdaḥ na artha antaram abhidhatte iti abādhita eka padam atha śabdānām vācya vācaka bhāva anupapatteḥ nirviṣaya tvam asya iti ced na vācya vācaka bhāvasya vakṣyamāṇa tvāt 
[I,152,14]	tat evam ātmani avasthite tasya dravya tva samavāyikāraṇa tva kṣaṇika eka deśa vṛtti viśeṣa guṇa tva pratipādana artham caturdaśa guṇa pratijñā tām darśayati tasya guṇāḥ buddhi sukha duḥkha icchā dveṣa prayatna dharma adharma saṃskāra saṃkhyā parimāṇa pṛthaktva saṃyoga vibhāgāḥ iti ete tu sūtrakāreṇa pratipāditāḥ iti āha ātma liṅga adhikāre buddhi ādayaḥ prayatna antāḥ siddhāḥ iti 
[I,152,19]	tathā dharma adharmau ātma antara guṇānām akāraṇa tva vacanāt iti ātma guṇānām ātma antara guṇeṣu akāraṇa tvāt iti sūtram darśayati tathā hi dāna dharmaḥ pratigraha dharmaḥ sampadyate iti anayoḥ pūrva apara bhāva niyamāt kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ iti āśaṅkā parihāra artham etat sūtram ātma antara guṇānām ātma antara guṇeṣu akāraṇa tvāt dharma adharmau ca ātma guṇau iti na ātma antara guṇa utpattau kāraṇam syāt na hi ātma guṇāt sukhāt ātma antare sukham duḥkhāt ca duḥkham utpadyamānam upalabdham 
[I,152,25_I,153,3]	atha duhitari vartamānam sukham mātari sukha sampādakam dṛṣṭam iti ayuktam etat na tad anubhavena tad upapatteḥ tathā hi duhitari mukha prasāda ādikam upalabhya sukham asyāḥ samutpannam iti anumānāt manyamānāyāḥ sva anubhavān mānasam sukham utpadyate na tat sukhāt tad vināśe hi kāla antareṇa utpatteḥ iti tat evam dāna dharmasya pratigraha dharma utpattau kāraṇa tva pratiṣedha pareṇa api sūtreṇa ātmani dharma adharmayoḥ sadbhāvaḥ abhihitaḥ tathā vakṣyāmaḥ ca tad parīkṣāyām 
[I,153,5]	saṃskāraḥ smṛti utpattau iti smṛtiḥ vāsanā ākhyāt iti sūtram darśayati tathā hi smṛtiḥ kārya tvāt avaśyam kāraṇam apekṣate na ca anubhavaḥ kāraṇam tad vināśe api utpatteḥ atha anubhava pradhvaṃsaḥ kāraṇam anvaya vyatirekavat tvāt tat asat tasya niratiśaya tvāt tīvra ādi bheda bhinnasya smaraṇasya anupapatti prasaṅgāt na hi kāraṇa atiśayam vinā kāryasya atiśayaḥ yuktaḥ abhyāsa vaiyarthyañca pradhvaṃsa atiśayasya kartum aśakyatvāt atas sa atiśayam ātma samavetam kiñcid asādhāraṇam kāraṇam asti yatas tad samavetā smṛtiḥ jāyate na ca adṛṣṭaḥ eva tasya sakala kārya utpattau sa ādhāra tvāt asādhāraṇantu ātma samavetam sukha duḥkha lakṣaṇam kāryam dṛṣṭam iti smṛteḥ anyadasā dhāraṇam kāraṇam vācyam tathā hi smṛtiḥ ātma samavetāḥ asādhāraṇa kāraṇe sati utpadyate ātma sama vetā sādhāraṇa kārya tvāt sukha vat tasmāt anubhavena ātmani saṃskāra ādhāne sati smaraṇam utpadyate iti sthitam smṛtiḥ vāsanā ākhyāt bhavati iti 
[I,153,16]	tatra vyavasthā vacanāt saṃkhyā iti sukha duḥkha vyavasthātaḥ nānā ātmānaḥ iti sūtram darśayati kā punar iyam vyavasthā sukha duḥkha ādīnām niyamaḥ tathā hi ekasya sukham anyasya duḥkham anyasya icchā iti vyasthā upalabdhā aikātmye tu ekasya sukhi tve sarveṣām sukhi tvam duḥkhi tve sarveṣu duḥkhitvañca iti avyavasthā prasaṅgaḥ niyama hetoḥ abhāvāt 
[I,153,21^1]	atha asti śarīra bhedaḥ niyāmakaḥ iti ced na anusandhāna prasaṅgāt yathā hi bāla kaumāra yauvana avasthā bhedena śarīrasya bhede api eka tvāt ātmanaḥ pratisandhānam mama sukham āsīt bālya avasthāyām iti upalabdham evam sarva śarīreṣu api prasaṅgaḥ na ca etat asti tasmāt eka tva vyāpakam pratisandhānam ātmanaḥ aśva mahiṣa ādi śarīrebhyaḥ vyāvartamānam su a vyāptam eka tvam gṛhītvā vyāvartate iti nānātvam tathā hi aśva mahiṣa ādi śarīre api ātmā dharmī ātma tve sati vyakti bhedena nānā iti sādhyam śarīra antara upalabdhe arthe śarīra antareṇa apratisandhāyaka tvāt 
[I,153,21^2]	yatra ca ekaḥ tatra asti pratisandhānam yathā bāla kaumāra yauvana śarīreṣu iti vyatirekaḥ kevala vyatireka avyabhicāreṇa hetoḥ gamaka tvam vakṣyāmaḥ laiṅgika jñāne tathā ekasmin api śarīre mama pāde vedanā śirasi vedanā iti eka tvāt ātmanaḥ pratisandhānam dṛṣṭam na ca janma antara śarīra anubhūte garbha śarīra anubhūte ca smaraṇa vat aśva ādi śarīra upalabdhe api asmaraṇam yuktam garbha śarīra anubhavasya apaṭu tvāt janma antara saṃskārasya ca maraṇa duḥkhena abhibhavāt na ca evam aśva ādi śarīra anubhūteṣu smaraṇe kāraṇam asti 
[I,154,5]	atha bheda sadbhāve pramāṇa anupapatteḥ sarvam ekam iti kalpyate na pratyakṣeṇa eva paraspara vyāvṛtta ātmanām padārthānām bheda pratibhāsāt vidhi pratiṣedha grāha kañca pratyakṣam nirvikalpaka jñānena padārthānām bheda pratibhāse sati etasmāt ayam bhinnaḥ iti sa vikalpa jñāna utpatti abhyupagamāt na itaretara āśraya tvam anavasthā vā aniyamena tu viśeṣaṇa viśeṣyayoḥ vidhi pratiṣedhayoḥ grahaṇam iṣṭam yat atra viśeṣaṇam tat pūrvam gṛhyate viśeṣyantu paścāt aniyataḥ tu viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ iti 
[I,154,11]	nanu ca atra bhedaḥ vyāvṛttiḥ itaretara abhāvaḥ iti abhyupagame vyāvṛtteḥ bhedaḥ katham svayam vyāvṛtti rūpa tvāt tad viparītāḥ tu vyāvṛttim apekṣante atha ayam bheda pratibhāsaḥ avidyā samāropitaḥ iti ced na ātma vyatirekeṇa tad asambhavāt vyatireke tu eka tva nivṛttiḥ yadi ca vidyā nivṛtti rūpā syāt avidyā sā katham tuccha svabhāva tayā bhedena vyavahāram janayet na ca bādhaka anupapatteḥ bheda pratibhāsaḥ bhrāntaḥ na api kalpita rūpāṇām vāstava artha kriyā janaka tvam nyāyyam rajjvām tu sarpa jñānāt vāstavāt eva bhakṣaṇam dravaṇam kāryam na kalpita arthāt iti na ca sarvasya ekatve pramāṇam asti iti katham vidyā nibandhanam eka tva jñānam yathā ca pramāṇam vinā sarvasya ekatvam evam nānātvam api syāt pramāṇa abhāvasya ubhayatra aviśeṣāt atha asti eka tve pramāṇam āgamaḥ iti ced eka tva nivṛttiḥ pramāṇa ādeḥ vāstava bheda tvāt abhede tu pramāṇa prameya vyavasthā anupapattiḥ iti 
[I,154,21]	katham svayaṃjyotiḥ eva ayam ātmā iti atha amī padārthāḥ yadi paramātmanaḥ vyatirekiṇaḥ katham prakāśante aprakāśasya prakāśa ayogāt atha prakāśante na paramātma vyatirekiṇaḥ tasya eva prakāśa svarūpa tvāt iti ced na etat evam vibhinna svarūpa sambandhinām pratyakṣa ādi pramāṇaiḥ saṃvedanāt prakāśa rūpa tā bhāva svarūpa sambandhi tvam bodha rūpa tā vā syāt sā tu padārtheṣu na sambhavati iti asattvena paramātmanaḥ api asattva prasaṅgaḥ padārtha antara svarūpasya padārtha antare sattva aviśeṣāt yadi ca ekaḥ eva syāt ātmā tasya ekatra vimokṣe sarvatra tathā abhāvaḥ iti aprayāsa sādhyaḥ mokṣaḥ syāt tathā kasyacid amuktau anyasya api amuktiḥ iti sarveṣām anirmokṣa prasaṅgaḥ 
[I,155,1]	atha paramātmanaḥ jīva ātmanām niḥsaraṇam saṃsāraḥ tasmin eva layaḥ muktiḥ iti ced na teṣām tasmāt abhede kasya muktiḥ saṃsāraḥ vā abhede vā dvaita hāniḥ iti tathā vidyā paricchinna ātma pradeśānām muktiḥ avidyā paricchinna ātma pradeśānām saṃsāraḥ iti atra api etat eva dūṣaṇa m ūhyam paramāṇavaḥ tu kṣiti ādeḥ kāryasya upādāna kāraṇam kārya parimāṇāt hīna parimāṇasya kāraṇasya upalabdheḥ na ca paramātmā tasya vyāpaka tvāt na ca amūrta upādāna samavetam mūrtam utpadyamānam dṛṣṭam iti yadi ca aneka maṇu parimāṇañca upādānam paramātmā iti syāt saṃjñā bheda mātram paramāṇavaḥ tu pūrvam eva vyavasthāpitāḥ yat ca ekatva pratipādakam vākyam tat paramātma apekṣayā vyākhyeyam tasya hi kārya anumānena pūrvam eva vyavasthāpanāt yat ca idam ekaḥ eva ayam ātmā dehe dehe vyavasthitaḥ iti ekasmin śarīre aneka tva pratiṣedha artham etat tathā hi ekasmin śarīre anekam vijñānam ātmā iti śākyāḥ manyante tad pratiṣedha artham pratiśarīram ekaḥ na anekaḥ tathā nānā tva pratipādakam eva vākyam asti iti alam ati jalpitena 
[I,155,13]	pṛthaktvam api atas eva iti yatas eva nānā tvam atas eva nānā pṛthaktvam tathā ca ātmā iti vacanāt parama mahat parimāṇam iti vibhavān mahān ākāśaḥ tathā ca ātmā iti sūtram darśayati yathā vibhavāt mahān ākāśaḥ tathā ātmā api iti vibhu tvāt eva parama mahat tvam siddham atha śarīra parimāṇa tvāt ātmanaḥ asiddham parama mahat tvam tathā ca alpa śarīre alpaḥ mahati mahān ātmā iti na śarīra vyatirekeṇa ātmanaḥ astitve pramāṇam asti iti 
[I,155,19_I,155,22]	nanu etasmin pakṣe saṅkoca vikāśa dharmaka tvāt bāla śarīre api ātmanaḥ vināśe vṛddha avasthāyām nānā ātmā sampadyate iti anya tve smaraṇam na syāt na ca pūrva parimāṇasya anivṛttau uttara parimāṇena śakyam bhavitum iti pūrva parimāṇasya āśraya vināśāt eva nivṛttiḥ na ca vyāpakasya amūrta tve gamanam sambhavati iti svarga ādi sthāneṣu śarīra sambandha anupapattau upabhogaḥ na syāt atas iṣyate evam gamanam tarhi mūrta tve sati mahā parimāṇa tvāt yatas utpattiḥ tat kāraṇam vācyam iti bhūta caitanya vat pratiṣedhaḥ 
[I,155,25]	tathā dharma adharmayoḥ ātma guṇa tvāt tad āśrayasya avyāpaka tve na syāt agneḥ ūrdhva jvalanam vāyoḥ tiryak gamanam aṇu manasoḥ tu ādyam karma iti tayoḥ sva āśraya saṃyoga apekṣi tvāt yathā prayatnaḥ hasta karmaṇi ātma saṃyoga apekṣaḥ tathā dharma adharmau ātma saṃyogam vinā na karma kuryātām ātma guṇa tvāt na ca tatra anyat kāraṇam asti iti sva āśraya saṃyoga apekṣaḥ adṛṣṭaḥ eva kāraṇam atas vyāpaka tvāt ca parama mahat tvam tathā yogaḥ khalu ṛddhau prādurbhūtāyām sa indriyāṇi śarīrāṇi nirmāya yugapad bhogān upabhuṅkte iti śrūyate tat ca vibhāva ātmani upapadyate na avyāpake iti 
[I,156,4_I,156,19]	tathā sukha ādīnām sannikarṣa ja tvāt saṃyogaḥ siddhaḥ sukha ādayaḥ hi kārya tvāt asamavāyi kāraṇam apekṣante na ca anyat sambhavati iti ātma antaḥkaraṇa saṃyogaḥ siddhaḥ sa ca kṛtaka tvāt avaśyam vināśī iti āśraya vināśa abhāvāt vibhāgāt eva vinaśyati iti vibhāgaḥ siddhaḥ idānīm manasaḥ lakṣaṇa parīkṣā artham manaḥ tu ayogāt manaḥ ityādi prakaraṇam manaḥ tvena yogaḥ manaḥ tva upalakṣitaḥ samavāyaḥ lakṣaṇam iti tathā hi manaḥ itarasmāt bhidyate manaḥ tu ayogāt yaḥ tu itarasmāt amanasaḥ na bhidyate na ca asau manaḥ tvena yuktaḥ yathā kṣiti ādiḥ iti vyavahāraḥ vā sādhyaḥ śeṣam lakṣaṇasya dūṣaṇa pratisamādhānam pūrvavat jñeyam tathā śabda artha nirūpaṇa paratvañca iti 
[I,156,24]	atha pratyakṣeṇa anupalabdheḥ manasaḥ sadbhāve kim pramāṇam anumānam iti āha sati api ātma indriya artha sānnidhye jñāna sukha duḥkhānām abhūtvā utpatti darśanāt iti tathā hi ātmā sarva gata tvāt eva sarvaiḥ indriyaiḥ sambaddhaḥ indriyāṇi tu sva viṣayaiḥ iti tathā api na yugapad rūpa ādi jñānāni utpadyante iti karaṇa antaram anumīyate 
[I,157,1]	atha indriyāṇām sva viṣayaiḥ sambandhaḥ katham jñāyate anumānāt tathā hi ghrāṇam sva vyāpta saṃyoginā saṃyuktam tad saṃyukta vyāpaka tvāt yaḥ yaḥ saṃyukta vyāpakaḥ sa sva vyāpta saṃyogi saṃyujyamānaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ yathā vīraṇa saṃyukta tantu vyāpakaḥ paṭaḥ vīraṇena saṃyuktaḥ iti sthāna saṃyuktam vā karpūra ādi dravyam sva saṃyukta vyāpinā saṃyujyate tad vyāpta saṃyogi tvāt yaḥ yat vyāpta saṃyogī sa sva saṃyukta vyāpinā saṃyujyamānaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ yathā paṭavya āpta tantu saṃyogi vīraṇam paṭena saṃyujyamānam iti 
[I,157,7]	evam rasanā indriyam sva vyāpta saṃyoginā saṃyuktam tad saṃyukta vyāpaka tvāt vīraṇa saṃyukta tantu vyāpaka paṭa vat sthāna saṃyuktam vā dravyam sva saṃyukta vyāpinā saṃyujyate tad vyāpta saṃyogi tvāt paṭavya āpta tantu saṃyogi vīraṇa ādi vat iti evam śeṣeṣu api iti gīta dhvaniḥ tu sannihitasya tad śravaṇa sātatyena śrotra sambandhe eva 
[I,157,11]	yadi etāvat kāraṇam jñāna sukha duḥkhānām tad sadbhāve anutpattiḥ na syāt na hi kāraṇa sākalye api kāryasya anutpattiḥ dṛṣṭā iti tasmāt eṣām sadbhāve api kāryasya pūrvam abhūtvā paścāt utpatti darśanāt kāraṇa antaram anumīyate yasya sadbhāva asadbhāvābhyām kāryasya utpatti anutpattī atha adṛṣṭaḥ asyām eva kāraṇam bhaviṣyati iti na śrotra ādīnām api abhāva prasaṅgāt tasya api ca idānīm tad sādhanasya ananuṣṭhānāt cira utpāde saḥ eva doṣaḥ 
[I,157,16]	tat evam ātma indriya arthāḥ kāraṇa antara apekṣāḥ sadbhāve api anutpādya utpādaka tvāt ye hi sadbhāve api kāryam anutpādya paścāt utpādayanti te sa apekṣāḥ yathā tantu ādayaḥ anya tantu saṃyoga apekṣāḥ iti anye tu ātmā kramavat kāraṇa apekṣaḥ itarasā kalye api krameṇa kārya janaka tvāt yaḥ hi itara kāraṇa sākalye api krameṇa kāryam karoti sa krama vat kāraṇa apekṣaḥ yathā aneka śilpa abhijñaḥ puruṣaḥ iti cakṣuḥ ādayaḥ vā kramavat kāraṇa apekṣāḥ sadbhāve api krameṇa kārya janaka tvāt yaḥ hi vidyamānaḥ krameṇa kāryam karoti saḥ avaśyam kramavat kāraṇam apekṣate yathā vāsīkartari ādi hastam iti anumānam bruvate 
[I,157,23]	tathā ātmā indriya artha sānnidhye api krameṇa eva kāryam karoti iti dṛṣṭam evam cakṣuḥ ādayaḥ api ātmanā adhiṣṭhitāḥ viṣaya sambandha krameṇa eva kāryam kurvanti iti kramavat kāraṇam apekṣante tathā śrotra ādi avyāpāre smṛti utpatti darśanāt asti karaṇa antaram tathā hi smṛtiḥ karaṇa janyā kriyā tvāt chidi kriyāvat na ca śrotra ādi eva karaṇam tat avyāpāre api smṛti utpatti darśanāt yat yat avyāpāre api utpadyate tat tasya kāryam na bhavati eva yathā vinaṣṭeṣu tantuṣu utpadyamānaḥ ghaṭaḥ iti smṛtiḥ tu badhira ādīnām śrotra ādi avyāpāre api utpadyate iti na tad kāryā atas karaṇa antareṇa bhavitavyam 
[I,158,3]	tathā bāhya indriyaiḥ agṛhīta sukha ādi grāhya antara sadbhāvāt ca karaṇa antaram asti tathā hi sukha ādayaḥ karaṇa paricchedyāḥ grāhya tvāt rūpa ādi vat na ca cakṣuḥ ādi eva karaṇam bāhya indriyaiḥ agṛhītasya sukha ādeḥ grāhya antarasya sadbhāvāt iti abhidhānāt yathā cakṣuṣā gandhaḥ na gṛhyate iti karaṇa antaram ghrāṇam anumīyate tābhyāñca rasasya aparicchedāt rasanā anumānam taiḥ ca sparśasya tathā śabdasya ca iti karaṇa antara anumānam iti tadvat bāhya indriyaiḥ sukha ādayaḥ na gṛhyante iti tad paricchedakam manaḥ anumīyate 
[I,158,9]	siddhe ca manaḥ sadbhāve dravya tva samavāyi kāraṇa tva pratipādana artham tasya guṇāḥ saṃkhyā parimāṇa pṛthaktva saṃyoga vibhāga paratva aparatva saṃskārāḥ iti vākyam dravya tvāt eva saṃkhyā asadbhāva siddhau kim ekam anekam veta saṃśaye tad nirāsa artham āha prayatna jñāna ayaugapadya vacanāt prati śarīram eka tvam siddham iti prayatna ayaugapadyāt jñāna ayaugapadya vacanāt ca pratiśarīram ekam manaḥ iti sūtram darśayati asamāsa karaṇañca atra sukha duḥkha ādyayaugapadya avarodha artham sūtra arthaḥ tu na ekam anekasmin śarīre na api ekasmin anekam vā manaḥ kim tarhi pratiśarīram ekam kutas prayatna ayaugapadyāt jñāna ayaugapadyāt ca yadi punar ekam syāt vyāpakam manaḥ sarva indriyāṇām tad adhiṣṭhita tvāt yugapad rūpa ādi jñānāni utpadyeran prayatnāḥ ca iti na ca evam dṛṣṭam 
[I,158,18]	atha dīrghaśaṣkulīm bhakṣayataḥ kapila brahmaṇaḥ yugapad pañca jñānāni utpadyante tathā adhyāpakasya yugapad vākya uccāraṇa gamana mārga anveṣaṇa kamaṇḍalu dhāraṇeṣu prayatnāḥ utpadyante iti asiddham etat tat na yaugapadye prasiddha udāharaṇa abhāvāt utpala patra śata vyatibheda abhimāna vat āśu bhāvi tvena yaugapadya abhimānaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ krame tu anekam prasiddham udāharaṇam asti tasmāt aṇu parimāṇasya manasaḥ krameṇa indriya sambandhāt krameṇa eva jñānāni bhavanti iti yuktam aṇu parimāṇasya api ekasmin śarīre aneka tva abhyupagame kiñcid indriyam kenacid manasā adhiṣṭhitam iti jñāna yaugapadyam eva syāt krameṇa tu jñānāni utpadyamānāni saṃvedyante iti prati śarīra maṇu parimāṇam ekam manaḥ na ca evam api manasā cakṣuḥ adhiṣṭhitam aneka artha sambaddham yugapad jñānāni utpādayet na etat evam ekasya karaṇasya eka kriyā nirvṛttau sāmarthya upalabdheḥ na hi ekam karaṇam ekasmin kāle anekām kriyām kurvat dṛṣṭam iti 
[I,158,28_I,159,1]	atha kuṭhāra abhighātāt aneka tṛṇeṣu yugapad aneka kriyā upalabdheḥ ayuktam etat na bodha ātmaka tvena viśeṣita tvāt yat vā kuṭhāra avayavānām karaṇa tvam yathā tīkṣṇaḥ avayavī tṛṇaiḥ sambaddhaḥ tathā tad avayavāḥ taiḥ sambaddhāḥ eva iti karaṇa bahu tvāt yuktam kriyā yaugapadyam abhighātāḥ tu karaṇāni iti anye tathā hi kuṭhārasya tṛṇaiḥ sambandhāḥ vega apekṣāḥ avayavāḥ parasparam vibhinnāḥ eva na etat yuktam karmaṇā sambaddhasya eva kuṭhārasya karaṇa tvāt anyathā hi cakṣuṣaḥ api sambandhi bhedāt sambandha bheda upapatteḥ teṣām api karaṇa tvena cakṣuḥ dvāreṇa manasā adhiṣṭhita tvāt yugapad ghaṭa ādi jñāna utpatti prasaṅgaḥ na ca etat asti asaṃvedanāt iti tasmāt yugapad prakāśanam eva ghaṭa ādīnām na grahaṇāni iti cakṣuḥ aneka padārtha sambaddham karaṇam iti nyāyyam atas karaṇasya eka kriyā nirvṛttau sāmarthyam siddhe ca nānātve tad anuvidhānāt sāhacaryāt nānā pṛthaktvam sidhyati eva 
[I,159,8_I,159,11]	tathā tad abhāva vacanāt aṇu parimāṇam iti vibhavāt mahān ākāśaḥ tathā ca ātmā tad abhāvāt aṇu manaḥ iti sūtre darśayati tasya vibhu tvasya abhāvāt aṇu manaḥ iti nanu evam ghaṭa ādau api vibhu tvasya abhāvāt aṇu tvam syāt na nitya dravyasya iti viśeṣaṇāt tathā hi manaḥ aṇu parimāṇa sambandhi nitya dravya tve sati vibhu tva rahita tvāt yat yat nitya dravya tve sati vibhu tva rahitam tat tathā dṛṣṭam yathā paramāṇu ādiḥ tathā ca idam vibhu tva rahitam tasmāt aṇu parimāṇam iti ghaṭa ādau vibhu tva rahita tve api na aṇu parimāṇam iti nitya tva grahaṇam nitya tvam guṇa ādau api asti iti dravya padam 
[I,159,16]	tathā apasarpaṇa upasarpaṇa vacanāt saṃyoga vibhāgau iti apasarpaṇam upasarpaṇam aśita pīta saṃyogāḥ kārya antara saṃyogāḥ ca iti adṛṣṭa kāritāni iti sūtram darśayati apasarpaṇantu mṛta śarīrāt vibhāga artham karma pratyagreṇa śarīreṇa saṃyoga arthaḥ ca upasarpaṇam iti aśita pītam bhuktam udaka ādi tayoḥ nāḍī antareṇa sañcaraṇam kārya antaram śarīra antaram tena saṃyogaḥ manasaḥ tad artham manaḥ karma yoginām iti etat sarvam adṛṣṭa kāritam iti anya pareṇa api sūtreṇa saṃyoga vibhāgau uktau tathā mūrta tvāt paratva aparatve tayoḥ mūrti anuvidhānāt yatra hi mūrta tvam tatra tad darśinaḥ parāpara vyavahāraḥ sambhavati iti dikkṛte tu paratva aparatve manasi kāla kṛtayoḥ nitya tvena asambhavāt kārya dravya apekṣayā tu tad darśinaḥ kāla kṛtam paratvam manasi sambhāvyate eva param manaḥ aparañca kārya dravyam iti na ca ayam niyamaḥ samāna jātīyayoḥ eva parāpara vyavahārasya dṛṣṭa tvāt tathā na param paratva aparatve saṃskāraḥ ca mūrta tvāt eva vega ākhyaḥ 
[I,159,27]	atha manaḥ paraspareṇa sambaddham kim iti dravyam na ārabhate samāna jātīya mūrta dravya sambandhasya antya avaya vi vyatirekeṇa dravya ārambhaka tva darśanāt iti āha asparśavat tvāt dravya anārambhaka tvam iti sparśavataḥ hi dravyasya dravya ārambhaka tva darśanāt yathā paramāṇūnām na ca manasaḥ sparśava tve pramāṇam asti manaḥ tu ajātīyasya sparśavat kāryasya anupalabdheḥ yathā hi pṛthivī tva jātīyam sparśavat kāryam upalabhyamānam tad ārambhakāṇām aṇūnām sparśavat tām jñāpayati na evam manaḥ tu ajātīyam kāryam asti iti katham manasaḥ sparśavat tvam tathā sparśavat tve sati śarīre sañcarataḥ vāyoḥ iva pratisañcalanāt kvacid indriya antareṇa asambandhāt aneka kālam rūpa ādeḥ viṣayasya agrahaṇam api syāt na ca etat suṣupti avasthām antareṇa dṛṣṭam iti tasmāt asparśavat tvena dravya anārambhaka tvam iti 
[I,160,8_I,160,11]	aṇu parimāṇa vyavasthāpanāt siddhe api mūrta tve punar sādhanam āha kriyāvat tvāt mūrta tvam iti tad anuvidhānāt kriyāyāḥ sā ca indriya sambandhāt vijñāyate anyathā hi aṇu parimāṇam manaḥ katham indriya antareṇa sambadhyate pūrvam manaḥ caitanya pratiṣedhe api punar bādhakam āha sādhāraṇa vigraha vat tva prasaṅgāt ajña tvam iti yadi hi cetanam manaḥ syāt ubhayāḥ sādhāraṇam śarīram upabhogyam iti viruddha abhiprāya tve bhoga anupapattiḥ syāt 
[I,160,14_I,160,18]	atha kim sva artham para artham vā iti āha karaṇa bhāvāt pārārthyam iti karaṇam hi vā asya ādi para puruṣa artha sampādakam dṛṣṭam tathā ca karaṇam manaḥ tasmāt kartuḥ ātmanaḥ puruṣa artha sampādakam iti atha kim dravyam guṇaḥ karma vā manaḥ iti āha guṇavat tvāt dravyam iti kṣiti ādi vat guṇāḥ tu uktāḥ eva atha aṇu parimāṇa tvāt manasaḥ katham rūpa ādi jñānāni āśu utpadyante iti āha āśu sañcāri tat ca prayatna adṛṣṭa parigraha vaśāt prayatnena jīvana pūrvakeṇa adṛṣṭa viśeṣeṇa ca parigraha vaśāt āśu sañcāritvam iti 
[II,001,3_II,001,4]	idānīm uddeśa krameṇa avasara prāptānām guṇānām itara padārtha vaidharmyeṇa vyāpakam sādharmyam punar pratiniyata anāñca sva bheda antarāt vyāvṛttim api darśayan āha rūpa ādīnām sarveṣām guṇānām guṇa tva abhisambandhaḥ iti ādi prakaraṇam guṇa tvena abhisambandhaḥ tad upalakṣitaḥ samavāyaḥ sa ca keṣām rūpa ādīnām tathā api ādi śabdasya aniyata artha grāhaka tvāt na jñāyate kiyatām atas sarveṣām utkṣepaṇa ādi avarodha parihāra arthañca guṇānām iti 
[II,001,10_II,001,14]	nanu evam sarveṣām guṇānām iti ukte vyabhicāra abhāvāt vyartham rūpa ādīnām iti padam na guṇa tva abhisambandha āśrita tva viśeṣaṇābhyām sarvaḥ guṇaḥ iti darśanasya vyavaccheda artha tvāt tathā hi rūpa ādīnām eva guṇa tva abhisambandhaḥ sādharmyam na anyeṣām iti na ca sāṃkhya abhyupagatasya guṇatrayasya vyavaccheda artham rūpa ādi grahaṇam iti nyāyyam tasya pramāṇa anupalabdheḥ prasiddhañca viśeṣaṇena vyavacchidyamānam dṛṣṭam yathā nīlena ānīlam iti tat evam rūpa ādayaḥ itarasmāt bhidyante guṇāḥ iti vyavahartavyā vā guṇa tva abhisambandhāt ye tu na bhidyante na ca guṇāḥ iti vyavahriyante na te guṇa tva abhisambaddhāḥ yathā kṣiti ādayaḥ iti śeṣam pūrvavat 
[II,001,19]	tathā dravya āśrita tvañca sādharmyam rūpa ādīnām tat ca sa avadhāraṇam vivakṣitam anyathā hi dravya ādīnām api dravya āśrita tvāt ati vyāpi sādharmyam syāt na vyāvṛttam iti avadhāraṇantu dravyeṣu eva āśrita tvam eva iti dravya karma viśeṣā dravyeṣu eva āśritā na ca āśritā eva iti sāmānya samavāyau tu dravyeṣu āśritau na tu dravyeṣu eva guṇa ādau api sadbhāvāt guṇāḥ tu dravyeṣu eva āśritāḥ na guṇa ādau tathā āśritāḥ eva dravyeṣu na anāśritā nirguṇasya dravyasya anupalabdheḥ tat evam ayoga anya yoga vyavacchedena dravya āśrita tvāt itarebhyaḥ bhidyante iti sādhyam 
[II,002,4_II,002,8]	tathā nirgatā calana lakṣaṇa kriyāḥ yebhyaḥ te niṣkriyāḥ teṣām bhāvaḥ niṣkriya tvam guṇāḥ vidyante yeṣām te guṇavantaḥ teṣām bhāvaḥ guṇavat tvam tad pratiṣedhena ca aguṇavat tvam iti nanu niṣkriya tvam aguṇavat tvan ca guṇa ādīnām pañcānām api iti uktam atas na idam padārtha antarāt vyāvṛttam sādharmyam na ca sādharmya mātreṇa iha prayojanam asti pūrvam eva abhidhānāt atha guṇa tva sahacaritam vyāvṛttam sādharmya mātram etat iti 
[II,002,11_II,002,15]	yat vā dravya padārthāt eva bheda pratipādana artham etat tathā hi pare manyante na guṇāḥ karma vā dravyāt artha antaram iti niṣkriya tva aguṇa tvābhyām tad upapatteḥ tathā hi kriyāvat guṇavat ca dravyam tad rahitāḥ ca guṇāḥ iti dharma bhedāt bhidyante eva atha niṣkriya tvam aguṇavat tvañca katham rūpa ādīnām dravyasya eva samavāyi kāraṇa tvena tad ādhārāṇām utpatti abhāvāt atha rūpa ādi samavetānām rūpa ādīnām utpatteḥ yuktam samavāyi kāraṇa tvam tat na anupalabdheḥ yathā hi rūpavat dravyam iti jñānam na evam rūpavat rūpam iti pratibhāsaḥ asti 
[II,002,19]	abhyupagamya api ucyate yadi ca rūpam rūpa utpattau samavāyi kāraṇam anyena asamavāyi kāraṇena bhavitavyam na ca kāraṇa rūpam eva asamavāyi kāraṇam tasya api svagata rūpa utpattau samavāyi kāraṇa tvāt na ca tat eva samavāyi kāraṇam asamavāyikāraṇañca iti dṛṣṭam na api saṃyogaḥ tasya dravya utpattau asamavāyi tvāt yadi ca tantu saṃyogaḥ tad rūpa utpattau asamavāyi kāraṇam tad utpatteḥ pūrvam tad abhāvaḥ syāt eva iti rūpa rūpeṣu api saṃyogasya kāraṇa tve tad utpatteḥ pūrvam abhāvaḥ vācyaḥ na ca ekasmāt eva rūpāt rūpa antaram iti vācyam ekasya krama yaugapadyābhyām ārambha pratiṣedhāt

[II,004,2_II,004,7]	atha idānīm ekāneka āśrita tvam darśayan āha saṃyoga vibhāga dvi tvat vipṛthaktva ādayaḥ aneka āśritāḥ ityādi padena tri tva ādikā parārdha antā saṃkhyā tad viśiṣṭañca pṛthaktvam gṛhyate aneka āśrita tvañcā atra vyakti apekṣayā vivakṣitam na jāti apekṣayā rūpa ādeḥ api tad bhāva prasaṅgāt yadi api rūpa tva ādi jātīyam anekasmin na vartate tathā api ekā tad vyaktirekasmin eva na ca evam saṃyoga ādiḥ tad vyakteḥ aneka āśrita tva upalabdheḥ 
[II,004,10_II,004,11]	śeṣāḥ tu ekaika dravya vṛttayaḥ iti uktabhyaḥ anye śeṣāḥ te hi ekaikasmin eva dravye vartante ekā hi vyaktiḥ ekasmin eva samavetā tathā rasa ādi vyaktayaḥ api avadhāraṇantu eṣām ekaika dravya vṛtti tvam eva na tu eṣām eva ubhaya vṛttīnām api tad bhāvāt

[II,005,10_II,005,15]	rūpañca sva samaveta śukla tva ādi aneka viśeṣaṇa upetam eka jātīyāyāḥ kṣiteḥ vyavacchedakam niyamena śukla tva viśiṣṭam udakasya śukla bhāsvarañca tejasaḥ ityādi viśeṣaḥ pūrva uktaḥ eva draṣṭavyaḥ tat evam sva samaveta viśeṣa viśiṣṭa tve sati sva āśraya eka jātīya vyavacchedaka tvāt viśeṣa guṇāḥ eva ete eva viśeṣa guṇāḥ iti avadhāraṇam saṃkhyā ādayaḥ vega antāḥ sāmānya guṇāḥ eva viśeṣa guṇa lakṣaṇa rahita tvāt ete eva sāmānya guṇāḥ

[II,005,24_II,006,6]	saṃkhyā ādayaḥ vega antāḥ dvi indriya grāhyāḥ eva niyamena ete eva dvi indriya grāhyāḥ bāhya grahaṇam antaḥkaraṇa vyavaccheda artham anuvartanīyam atha snehasya katham dvi indriya grāhya tvam tvac vyāpāre sati snigdha pratyaya darśanāt yathā hi cakṣuḥ vyāpāreṇa snigdhāḥ keśāḥ iti pratibhāsaḥ tathā snāna uttara kālam api tvac vyāpāreṇa snigdha pratyayaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ iti anvaya vyatirekābhyām dvi indriya grāhya tvam niścīyate atha kim ayam āpyaḥ pārthivaḥ vā iti vicārayiṣyāmaḥ sneha parīkṣāyām
