[II,006,16_II,006,20]	apākaja rūpa ādi vega antāḥ kāraṇa guṇa pūrvakāḥ iti apākaja grahaṇam pārthiva paramāṇu rūpa vyavaccheda artham nanu te api kāraṇa guṇa pūrvāḥ bhavanti eva tathā hi kāraṇam paramāṇuḥ tad guṇaḥ pārthiva paramāṇu agni saṃyogaḥ tat pūrvāḥ rūpa ādayaḥ iti katham na kāraṇa guṇa pūrvakāḥ tat na abhiprāya aparijñānāt tathā ca ayam abhiprāyaḥ samavāyi kāraṇeṣu eva guṇāḥ kāraṇa guṇāḥ te pūrvam kāraṇam yeṣām kārya guṇānām te atra kāraṇa guṇa pūrvakāḥ vivakṣitāḥ na ca evam pāka jāḥ iti vyavacchidyante 
[II,006,25_II,007,8]	atha salila ādi paramāṇu rūpa ādayaḥ pāka ja tva abhāve api na kāraṇa guṇa pūrvakāḥ iti tat na paryudāsa pratiṣedhasya vivakṣita tvāt tathā hi pākāt jātāḥ pāka jāḥ tad pratiṣedhena anya guṇa pūrvaka tvam labhyate iti nityānām vyavacchedaḥ nanu evam api vyartham apākaja grahaṇam ete kāraṇa guṇa pūrvakāḥ eva iti avadhāraṇā sambhavāt tathā hi drava tva vega avakāraṇa guṇa pūrvakau api iti na spaṣṭa artha tvāt ete eva kāraṇa guṇa pūrvakā na tu ete kāraṇa guṇa pūrvakāḥ eva iti avadhāraṇam abudhyamānasya pākajaiḥ doṣa āśaṅkā syāt iti spaṣṭa artham apāka ja grahaṇam atra ca eka tva eka pṛthaktva grahaṇam dvi tvat vipṛthaktva ādi vyavaccheda artham te hi akāraṇa guṇa pūrvakāḥ iti 
[II,007,11_II,007,23]	buddhi ādayaḥ śabda antāḥ tu akāraṇa guṇa pūrvakāḥ eva sama vāyi guṇa pūrvakāḥ kārya guṇāḥ na bhavanti iti na tu ā itas eva saṃyoga vibhāga paratva aparatva dvi tvat vipṛthaktva ādīnām api akāraṇa guṇa pūrvaka tvāt atha akāraṇa guṇa pūrvakatva aviśeṣe api asmin vākye saṃyoga ādīnām avacane kim prayojanam iti cintyam atha apākaja rūpa ādi vega antānām eva kāraṇa guṇa pūrvakatva abhidhānāt śeṣāṇām akāraṇa guṇa pūrvaka tvam vijñāyate evam tarhi buddhi ādayaḥ api na abhidheyāḥ śeṣāṇām akāraṇa guṇa pūrvakatvam iti vā abhidheyam sakala bheda saṅgrāhakam vākyam alam buddhi ādi viśeṣa abhidhānena iti na etat evam viśeṣa vacanam spaṣṭa artham anekadhā śāstra abhihitam iti antevāsinām ṛju artha parijñānam eva syāt iti ūha śakteḥ saṃvardhana artham saṃyoga ādīnām sva śabdena avacanam anye tu eka vṛttīnām eva viśeṣa guṇānām atra abhidhānam vivakṣitam iti manyante tat tu na buddhyāmahe dūṣaṇasya apratisamādhānāt 
[II,007,26_II,008,2]	tathā buddhi ādayaḥ pāka jāntāḥ saṃyoga jāḥ iti atra buddhi ādayaḥ bhāvanā antāḥ puruṣa antaḥkaraṇa saṃyogāt utpadyante śabdaḥ ca bherī ākāśa saṃyogāt tūla parimāṇañca pracayāt uttara saṃyogaḥ sūtra pāṭhā apekṣayā saṃyoga ja saṃyogaḥ naimittika drava tvam agni saṃyogāt paratva aparatve tu diś kāla piṇḍa saṃyogāt pāka jāḥ iti pārthiva paramāṇu rūpa ādayaḥ te api agni saṃyoga jāḥ iti ete eva saṃyoga jāḥ na tu ete saṃyoga jāḥ eva tathā hi śabdaḥ vibhāga jaḥ śabdajaḥ api asti iti 
[II,008,9_II,008,10]	saṃyoga vibhāga vegāḥ karmabhyaḥ jātāḥ karma jāḥ iti ete eva na tu ete karma jāḥ eva tathā hi saṃyogaḥ saṃyogāt utpadyate vibhāgaḥ ca vibhāgāt vegaḥ vegāt api iti 
[II,008,13_II,008,14]	śabda uttara vibhāgau vibhāgāt jātau vibhāga jau iti etau eva vibhāga jau na tu etau vibhāga jau eva tathā hi śabdaḥ saṃyoga jaḥ śabdajaḥ api asti iti uttara vibhāgaḥ ca sūtra pāṭhā apekṣayā vibhāga ja vibhāgaḥ eva parigṛhyate 
[II,008,18_II,008,24]	idānīm ke buddhi apekṣāḥ ke ca samāna jāti ārambhakāḥ iti upadarśayati paratva aparatva dvi tvat vipṛthaktva ādayaḥ buddhim apekṣante sva utpattau iti buddhi apekṣāḥ iti ādipadena tri tva ādikā parārdha antā saṃkhyā tad avacchinnañca pṛthaktvam gṛhyate avadhāraṇantu ete eva buddhi apekṣāḥ tathā ete buddhi apekṣāḥ eva buddhim vinā na bhavanti iti 
[II,009,3]	rūpa ādayaḥ sneha antāḥ samāna jāti ārambhakāḥ iti samānā tulyāḥ jātiḥ yeṣām te samāna jātayaḥ tān ārabhante iti tad ārambhakāḥ eva na tu ā itas eva samāna jāti ārambhakāḥ ubhaya ārambhakāṇām api sadbhāvāt atra ca anuṣṇa grahaṇam uṣṇa sparśa vyavaccheda artham tasya api ubhaya ārambhaka tvāt ekatva eka pṛthaktva grahaṇam dvi tvat vipṛthaktva ādi vyavaccheda artham dvi tva ādeḥ asamāna jāti ārambhaka tvāt dvi pṛthaktva ādeḥ ca akāraṇa tvāt iti 
[II,009,9_II,009,12]	tathā hi udaka avayaveṣu vartamānāḥ rūpa ādayaḥ sneha paryantāḥ kārye tān ārabhante gandhaḥ tu kṣiti avayaveṣu vartamānaḥ tad avayavini gandham ārabhate śabdaḥ ca ākāśe vartamānaḥ tatra eva śabdam iti sukha ādayaḥ prayatna antāḥ tu asamāna jāti ārambhakāḥ iti asamāna jātīyam eva ārabhantaḥ iti tad ārambhakāḥ na tvā ite eva anyeṣām api sadbhāvāt tathā ca sukhāt icchā dveṣāt dveṣaḥ tābhyām prayatnaḥ tasmāt kriyā iti 
[II,009,15]	saṃyoga ādayaḥ saṃskāra antāḥ samāna asamāna jāti ārambhakāḥ iti samānāḥ jātiḥ yeṣām te samāna jātayaḥ tad pratiṣedhena ca asamāna jātayaḥ tān ārabhantaḥ iti tad ārambhakāḥ ete eva samāna asamāna jāti ārambhakāḥ na anye tathā ete samāna asamāna jāti ārambhakāḥ eva niyamena tathā hi saṃyogāt saṃyogaḥ vijātīyañca buddhi ādi vibhāgāt vibhāgaḥ vijātīyaḥ ca śabdaḥ saṃkhyātaḥ saṃkhyāḥ vijātīyañca parimāṇam guru tvāt guru tvam vijātīyañca patanam drava tvāt drava tvam vijātīyañca syandanam uṣṇa sparśāt uṣṇa sparśaḥ vijātīyāḥ ca pāka jāḥ jñānāt ca jñānam vijātīyāḥ ca saṃskārāḥ dharma adharmābhyām dharma adharmau vijātīye ca sukha duḥkhe saṃskārāt saṃskāraḥ vijātīyañca smaraṇam 
[II,009,25_II,010,9]	idānīm sva para āśraya samaveta ārambhakān darśayati buddhi ādayaḥ śabda antāḥ sva āśraya samavetam eva ārabhante iti sva āśraya samaveta ārambhakāḥ na tu ā itas eva ubhayatra ārambhakāṇām api sadbhāvāt tathā hi buddhiḥ ātmani vartate tatra eva jñānam saṃskāra hetuḥ bhavati sukhāt icchā ātmani eva duḥkhāt dveṣaḥ tatra eva icchātaḥ smaraṇa prayatnau ātmani eva tathā dveṣāt api bhāvanātaḥ bhāvanā smaraṇañca ātmani eva śabdaḥ ca ākāśe vartamānaḥ tatra eva śabdam ārabhate iti rūpa ādayaḥ prayatna antāḥ paratra iti parasmin eva ārabhante iti paratra ārambhakāḥ na tvā ite eva tathā hi rūpa rasa gandha sparśa parimāṇa snehāḥ kāraṇeṣu vartamānāḥ paratra kārye tān ārabhante tathā prayatnaḥ puruṣe vartamānaḥ paratra hasta ādau kriyām ārabhate 
[II,010,13]	saṃyoga ādayaḥ adharma antāstu ubhayatra ārambhakāḥ ete eva ubhayatra ārambhakāḥ tathā eta ubhayatra ārambhakāḥ eva niyamena bherī ākāśa saṃyogaḥ hi ākāśe vartamānaḥ tatra eva śabdam ārabhate bherī daṇḍa saṃyogaḥ tu paratra tathā vaṃśa dala ākāśa vibhāgaḥ sva āśraye vaṃśa dala vibhāgaḥ tu paratra ākāśe śabda ārambhakaḥ saṃkhyā kāraṇe vartamānā dvi tva tri tva ādikā kārye parimāṇam eka tva saṃkhyā ca eka tvam sva āśraye tu dvi tva ādikam ārabhate iti eka pṛthaktva grahaṇam dvi pṛthaktva ādi vyavaccheda artham teṣām akāraṇa tvāt kāraṇeṣu vartamānam eka pṛthaktvam kārye api eka pṛthaktvam ārabhate sva āśrayeṣu dvi pṛthaktva ādikam iti guru tva drava tva vegāḥ tu kāraṇa gatāḥ kārye api guru tva ādīn ārabhante sva āśrayeṣu patana syandana gamana kriyā iti dharma adharmau ca sva āśraya samavete sukha duḥkhe para āśraye tu kriyām ārabhete 
[II,010,24_II,010,25]	idānīm kriyā hetūn āha guru tva ādi saṃyoga viśeṣa antāḥ kriyā hetavaḥ iti tathā hi guru tvāt patanam drava tvāt syandanam vegāt gamanam prayatnāt hasta ādau kriyā dharma adharmābhyām agni ādau kriyā saṃyoga viśeṣāḥ tu nodana abhighāta saṃyukta saṃyogāḥ te api kriyā hetavaḥ eva guru tva ādīnām guru tva janaka tvasya api upalabdheḥ 
[II,011,5_II,011,15]	idānīm asamavāyi nimitta ubha yathā kāraṇāni āha rūpa ādi śabda antānām asamavāyi kāraṇa tvam iti atha kim idam asamavāyi kāraṇa tvam nāma pratyāsannasya kārya janaka tvam yat yasya pratyāsannam sat janaka tvena upalabdha sāmarthyam vyāptyā tat tasya utpattau asamavāyi kāraṇam kā punar iyam pratyāsattiḥ eka artha samavāyaḥ sā tu bhidyate kāryā eka artha samavāya lakṣaṇā kārya kāraṇa eka artha samavāya lakṣaṇā ca iti kāryeṇa saha ekasmin arthe samavāyaḥ lakṣaṇam cihnam asyāḥ iti tad lakṣaṇā yathā śabdasya śabda utpattau iti kārya śabdaḥ hi ākāśe vartate tatra eva kāraṇa śabdaḥ api iti kāryā eka artha samavāyaḥ asya pratyāsattiḥ iti tathā buddhi ādi utpattau ātmā antaḥkaraṇa saṃyogasya sa hi ātmani vartate buddhi ādayaḥ api tatra eva iti 
[II,011,21]	nanu evam buddhi ādīnām api sva kārya utpattau eka artha samavāyi tvāt asamavāyi kāraṇa tvam eva na nimitta tvam na eṣa doṣaḥ saṃyogasya aśeṣa kārya utpattau vyāptyā sāmarthya upalabdheḥ na ca evam buddhi ādeḥ anyatarasya iti tasya pratiniyata kārya utpattau eva sāmarthya avadhāraṇāt ātma antaḥkaraṇa saṃyogaḥ tu aśeṣa buddhi ādi utpattau upalabdha sāmarthyam iti saḥ eva asamavāyi kāraṇam na jātucit manaḥ saṃyogāt ṛte buddhi ādayaḥ bhavanti iti tathā ca suṣupti avasthā avasāne vijñāna ādikam utpadyate iti manaḥ saṃyogaḥ tatra kāraṇam 
[II,012,1]	nanu evam api dharma adharmayoḥ aśeṣa buddhi ādi utpattau vyāptyā kāraṇa tvāt asamavāyi tvam syāt na vibhu viśeṣa guṇānām viśiṣṭa pratyāsatteḥ upalambhāt yathā hi śabdaḥ śabda antaram ārabhamāṇaḥ sva avaruddha nabhaḥ deśa samanantaram eva ārabhate na eka artha samavāyi tvāt deśa antare tathā sati brahma bhāṣitasya api upalambha prasaṅgāt tadvat dharma adharmau api svāvaruddha ātma pradeśa anantaram sukha duḥkha ādikam āra bheyātām iti svarga ādi sthāneṣu tad abhāvaḥ syāt ārabhete tu sthāna antareṣu api sukha duḥkha ādikam iti nimitta kāraṇa tvam eva tasmāt ātma antaḥkaraṇa saṃyogaḥ eva buddhi ādi utpattau eka artha samavāyitayā asamavāyi kāraṇam iti sthitam 
[II,012,9_II,012,11]	tathā kāryam rūpa ādi paṭe vartate paṭaḥ ca tantuṣu tad gatāḥ ca rūpa ādayaḥ tatra eva iti kārya kāraṇa eka artha samavāyaḥ teṣām pratyāsattiḥ iti nanu evam api tantu rūpam rasa ādi utpattau pratyāsannam rasaḥ ca rūpa utpattau iti a samavāyi tvam syāt na janaka tvam iti viśeṣaṇāt yat yasya utpattau pratyāsannam sat janakam tad asamavāyi kāraṇam na ca evam rūpam rasa ādi utpattau kāraṇam tad anuvidhānasya adarśanāt yathā hi śuklāt rūpāt śuklam pītāt ca pītam iti kāraṇa rūpa anuvidhānam asti na evam rasa ādinā iti na hi madhurāt amlāt vā tat śuklam pītam vā rūpam iti anvayaḥ gṛhyate tasmāt pratyāsattau api na asamavāyi tvam kāraṇasya sataḥ tad viśeṣa nirūpaṇāt 
[II,012,18_II,012,21]	na ca evam samavāyi kāraṇe prasaṅgaḥ tasya ukta pratyāsatti abhāvāt na hi kāryeṇa tad kāraṇena ca saha eka artha samavāyaḥ tasya asti tatra eva tad kāryasya samavāyāt tathā hi rūpa rasa gandha anuṣṇa sparśa parimāṇa snehāḥ kārya kāraṇa eka artha samavāyādeva asamavāyi kāraṇam saṃkhyā tu dvi tva ādikā parimāṇa utpattau kārya kāraṇa eka artha samavāyena asamavāyi kāraṇam tathā kāraṇa eka tvam eka pṛthak tvan ca kāryā ekatva eka pṛthaktvā utpattau iti dvi tvat vipṛthaktva ādi utpattau eka tva eka pṛthaktva ādīnām kāryā eka artha samavāyena eva asamavāyi kāraṇa tvam eva evam śabdasya api iti uktam 
[II,012,26_II,013,1]	eteṣām asamavāyi kāraṇa tvam eva na tu eteṣām eva anyeṣām api sadbhāvāt atra ca anuṣṇa grahaṇam uṣṇa sparśa vyavaccheda artham tasya ubhayathā kāraṇa tvāt buddhi ādi bhāvanā antānām nimitta kāraṇa tvam iti samavāyi asamavāyi lakṣaṇa rahitasya janaka tvam na ca asiddham viśeṣaṇam pratyāsannasya buddhi ādeḥ janaka tvāt iti vācyam pūrva ukta nyāyāt avadhāraṇantu eteṣām nimitta kāraṇa tvam eva na tu eteṣām eva 
[II,013,5_II,013,8]	tathā hi buddhiḥ jñānam saṃskāra utpattau kāraṇam sukham icchāyāḥ duḥkham dveṣasya icchā dveṣau prayatnasya sa ca kriyāyāḥ dharma adharmau sukha duḥkhayoḥ bhāvanā smaraṇasya iti saṃyoga ādi vega antānām ubhayathā kāraṇa tvam iti asamavāyi nimitta kāraṇa tvam iti eteṣām eva ubhayathā kāraṇa tvam tathā eteṣām ubhayathā kāraṇa tvam eva iti niyamena 
[II,013,11]	tathā hi bherī ākāśa saṃyogasya asamavāyi kāraṇa tvam bherī daṇḍa saṃyogasya nimitta tvam evam vaṃśa dala ākāśa vibhāgasya asamavāyi kāraṇa tvam vaṃśa dala vibhāgasya nimitta tvam uṣṇa sparśasya utpattau asamavāyi kāraṇa tvam pāka jeṣu nimitta tvam evam guru tva drava tva vegānām sva āśraya kriyā utpattau asamavāyi kāraṇa tvam āśraya antare nimitta tvam iti 
[II,013,16_II,013,18]	paratva aparatva dvipṛthaktva ādīnām akāraṇa tvam ityādi padena tripṛthaktva ādīnām grahaṇam nanu eteṣām jñāna ādi utpattau asti eva kāraṇa tvam satyam tad vyatirekeṇa anyatra akāraṇa tvam vivakṣitam iti samāna jātīya ārambhaka ādi vākye api idam viśeṣaṇa m ūhyam eteṣām akāraṇa tvam eva na tu eteṣām eva pārimāṇḍalī ādeḥ api akāraṇa tvāt 
[II,013,23_II,014,15]	idānīm keṣām pradeśa vṛtti tvam āśraya vyāpi tvañca iti āha saṃyoga vibhāga śabda ātma viśeṣa guṇānām pradeśa vṛtti tvam āśraya avyāpaka tvam vivakṣitam na tu pradeśe avayave vṛttiḥ niṣpradeśānām tad abhāva prasaṅgāt eteṣām eva āśraya avyāpi tvam eteṣām pradeśa vṛtti tvam eva śeṣāṇām āśraya vyāpi tvam iti uktebhyaḥ anye śeṣāḥ teṣām āśraya vyāpi tvam katham etat āśraya upalambhe sati tad jighṛkṣāyām avaśyam grahaṇam yathā paṭa upalambhe rūpa jighṛkṣāyām avaśyam tat grahaṇam iti yeṣa antva āśraya avyāpi tvam na teṣām āśraya upalambhe satyām api jighṛkṣāyām indriya artha sannikarṣe ca avaśyam grahaṇam asti yathā parvatasya apara bhāga vartinām saṃyogaḥ na avaśyam tad upalambhe api upalabhyate iti apākaja ādi sneha antānām yāvat dravya bhāvi tvam iti yāvat dravyam bhavanti tad śīlāḥ ca iti yāvat dravya bhāvinaḥ teṣām bhāvaḥ yāvat dravya bhāvi tvam āśraye satya vināśi tvam iti yāvat śeṣāṇām ayāvat dravya bhāvi tvam iti uktebhyaḥ anye śeṣāḥ teṣām sati api āśraye vināśaḥ iti 
[II,015,2_II,015,3]	atha idānīm vaidharmyam pratiniyatam āha rūpa ādīnām sarva guṇānām pratyekam apara sāmānya sambandhāt rūpa ādi saṃjñāḥ bhavanti ityādi rūpam ādiḥ yeṣām te rūpa ādayaḥ teṣām na jñāyate kiyatām atas sarva guṇānām iti sarve ca te guṇāḥ ca iti sarva guṇāḥ te ca rūpa ādayaḥ eva abhipretāḥ na anyaḥ iti teṣām ekam ekam prati pratyekam apara sāmānya sambandhāt iti guṇa tva apekṣayā apara sāmānyam rūpa tva ādi tad sambandhāt rūpa ādi saṃjñāḥ bhavanti rūpa tva sambandhāt rūpam iti saṃjñā rasa tva sambandhāt ca rasaḥ iti evam anyeṣu api iti 
[II,015,11_II,015,18]	tatra ādau uddiṣṭa tvāt rūpasya sadbhāve pramāṇam lakṣaṇam āśrayam artha kriyā bhedam nitya tvam utpatti vināśa kāraṇañca darśayan āha rūpam cakṣuḥ grāhyam ityādinā tatra rūpam eva cakṣuḥ grāhyam na rasa ādi rūpam cakṣuṣā eva gṛhyate anya indriya paricchedyam na bhavati iti avadhāraṇasya prakrama apekṣitayā na dravya ādau cakṣuḥ grāhya tva pratiṣedhaḥ tathā hi dravya ādeḥ cakṣuḥ grāhya tva siddhau aneka dravyeṇa samavāyāt sva gata viśeṣāt ca rūpam pratyakṣam etena rasa ādiṣu jñānam vyākhyātam iti atideśe cakṣuḥ grāhya tva āśaṅkāyām tad vyavaccheda artham eva avadhāraṇam na dravya ādau tad vṛtti tva pratiṣedha param abhipretan ca samudgīyamāna avadhāraṇam śākyaiḥ iti vakṣyāmaḥ laiṅgika jñāne 
[II,016,1_II,016,5]	sūtra arthaḥ tu anekam dravyam janakam asya iti iti aneka dravyam tena saha samavāyāt sva gata viśeṣa niyata sadbhāve kvacid rūpa upalabdhiḥ yat abhāvāt ca anupalabdhiḥ saḥ eva sahakāri viśeṣaḥ apadiśyate tasmāt ca rūpam pratyakṣam etat ca rasanā ādi pratyakṣe samānam iti pṛthivī udaka jvalana vṛtti iti āśraya nirūpaṇam pūrva pada apekṣam vā lakṣaṇam iti tathā hi cakṣuḥ grāhya tvam dravya tvasya api asti iti cakṣuṣā eva gṛhyate iti sa avadhāraṇam viśeṣaṇam tathā api cakṣuṣā eva gṛhyate rūpa tva sāmānyam iti pṛthivī udaka jvalana vṛtti padam pṛthivī ādi vṛtti tvañcāni eṣām api asti iti niyama grahaṇam atas rūpam itarasmāt bhidyate niyamena pṛthivī udaka jvalana vṛtti tve sati cakṣuṣā eva gṛhyamāṇa tvāt yaḥ tu na bhidyate na ca asau evam yathā rasa ādiḥ iti 
[II,016,12_II,016,17]	dravya ādi upalambhakam iti artha kriyā kathanam dravya ādīn upalambhayati iti dravya ādi upalambhakam dravya upalabdheḥ kāraṇam iti tathā mahat tvāt aneka dravyavat tvāt rūpa viśeṣāt ca dravyam pratyakṣam tad samavāyāt ca guṇa ādayaḥ api pratyakṣāḥ iti upalabdhau rūpa viśeṣasya kāraṇa tvam uktam pūrva pada apekṣam etat lakṣaṇam abhyūhyam nayana sahakārī iti sva gata rūpa utkarṣāt bāhya rūpa prakāśakam iti upadarśayati na ca pūrveṇa aviśeṣaḥ karaṇa sthasya rūpa utkarṣasya abhidhānāt prāktanena tu karma gatasya iti 
[II,016,20]	śukla ādi aneka prakāram iti bheda nirūpaṇam tat api asādhāraṇam eva salila ādi paramāṇuṣu nityam vināśa kāraṇa abhāvāt pārthiva paramāṇuṣu agni saṃyoga virodhi iti agni saṃyogena virodhaḥ vināśaḥ asya iti na ca anutpattimataḥ vināśaḥ sambhavati iti anyasya utpatti vināśa kāraṇasya abhāvāt agni saṃyogāt eva utpadyate sarva kāryeṣu kāraṇa guṇa pūrva prakrameṇa utpattiḥ āśraya vināśāt eva vināśaḥ iti vakṣyāmaḥ pākaja rūpa parīkṣāyām 
[II,016,27_II,017,3]	rasaḥ rasana grāhyaḥ iti sadbhāve pramāṇam pṛthivī udaka vṛttiḥ iti āśraya nirūpaṇam pūrva pada apekṣam vā lakṣaṇam iti tathā hi pṛthivī udaka vṛtti tvam anyeṣām api asti iti rasana grāhya padam rasana grāhyañca rasa tva ādi sāmānyam bhaviṣyati iti pṛthivī udaka vṛtti padam atas rasaḥ itarasmāt bhidyate pṛthivī udaka vṛtti tve sati rasana grāhya tvāt yaḥ tu itara smāt arasa ādeḥ na bhidyate na ca asau evam yathā gandha ādiḥ iti 
[II,017,9]	jīvana puṣṭi bala ārogya nimittam iti artha kriyā nirūpaṇam jīvanantu upabhoga dāyaka karma sacivasya ātmanaḥ sva śarīra avaruddhena manasā saṃyogaḥ tasya tu nimittam śarīra āpyāyana nimitta tvāt puṣṭiḥ avayava upacayaḥ sā ca viśiṣṭa rasa upayogāt bhavati iti tathā hi rasa upayogādāntareṇa tejasā pūrva dravya nivṛttau svatantreṣu paramāṇuṣu śyāma ādi nivṛtti dvāreṇa utpanna pāka jaiḥ dvi aṇuka ādi prakrameṇa śarīra ārambhaḥ pratikṣaṇam āhāra upayoge sati draṣṭavyaḥ na ca ārabhi a ārambhaka vādaḥ sambhavati iti uktam pṛthivī adhikāre balam utsāhaḥ tasya prāṇa saṃvardhana dvāreṇa nimittam ārogyam roga abhāvaḥ tasya api nimittam viśiṣṭa rasa upayoge sati tad śravaṇāt 
[II,017,17_II,017,19]	rasana sahakārī iti svagata rasa utkarṣāt bāhya rasasya abhivyañjakaḥ iti uktam pūrvam madhura amla lavaṇa tikta kaṭu kaṣāya bheda bhinnaḥ iti vibhāgaḥ saḥ api asādhāraṇa tvāt lakṣaṇam asya api nitya anitya tva niṣpattayaḥ pūrvavat iti salila paramāṇuṣu nityam pārthiveṣu agni saṃyogāt utpadyate vinaśyati ca kāryeṣu kāraṇa guṇa pūrvaḥ ādhāra vināśāt eva vinaśyati iti atideśa arthaḥ 
[II,017,24_II,018,6]	gandhaḥ ghrāṇa grāhyaḥ iti sadbhāve pramāṇam pṛthivī vṛttiḥ iti āśraya nirūpaṇam pūrva pada apekṣam vā lakṣaṇam tathā hi ghrāṇa grāhya tvam gandha tva ādeḥ api asti iti pṛthivī vṛttiḥ iti viśeṣaṇam pṛthivī vṛtti tvam anyasya api asti iti ghrāṇa grāhya padam ghrāṇa grāhya tve sati pṛthivī vṛtti tvam lakṣaṇam iti ghrāṇa sahakārī iti sva gata gandha utkarṣāt bāhya gandha prakāśakam iti artha kriyā nirūpaṇam punar api surabhiḥ asurabhiḥ ca iti vibhāgaḥ asya api utpatti ādayaḥ pūrvavat iti paramāṇuṣu agni saṃyogāt utpadyate vinaśyati ca kārye tu kāraṇa guṇa pūrvakaḥ ādhāra vināśāt eva vinaśyati iti atideśa arthaḥ 
[II,018,10_II,018,13]	sparśaḥ tvac indriya grāhyaḥ iti pratyakṣa paricchedya tvam darśayati pṛthivī udaka jvalana pavana vṛttiḥ iti āśraya nirūpaṇañca caturṇām sparśavat tvam iti anena na punaruktam tatra dravya dharmasya abhidhānāt iha tu sparśa dharmasya iti pūrva pada apekṣam vā lakṣaṇam tathā ca pṛthivī ādi vṛtti tvam anyeṣām api asti iti tvac indriya grāhya padam tat grāhyañca sparśa tu a ādi sāmānyam iti pṛthivī ādi vṛtti padam 
[II,018,18_II,018,22]	yadi saṃkhyā ādīnām api tvac indriya grāhya tve sati pṛthivī ādi vṛtti tvam sambhāvyeta avadhāraṇam kāryam atas sparśaḥ itarasmāt bhidyate tvac indriya grāhya tve sati niyamena pṛthivī ādi catur dravya vṛtti tvāt yaḥ tu itarasmāt na bhidyate na ca asau evam yathā rūpa ādiḥ iti tvac sahakārī iti sva gata sparśa utkarṣāt tvac indriyam bāhya sparśa prakāśakam iti artha kriyā nirūpaṇam 
[II,018,24]	atha tvac indriyam sparśasya prakāśakam kasmāt saṃyukta samavāyāt tvac indriyeṇa saṃyuktam dravyam tat samavāyāt sparśaḥ gṛhyate iti nanu evam saṃyukta samavāyasya aviśeṣāt rūpa ādi prakāśakam api syāt viśeṣaḥ vā vācyaḥ tat na sparśa utkarṣa vat rūpa ādi utkarṣasya abhāvāt tathā hi rūpa ādiṣu madhye sparśasya eva upalambhāni atha anupapattyā jñāyate niyāmakam kāraṇam niyama hetum vinā niyatasya kāryasya anupapatteḥ tatra sparśa utkarṣaḥ niyāmakaḥ sparśa tvam vā viṣaya gatam na ca etat rūpa ādiṣu sambhavati iti sparśa tvasya tatra asambhavāt rūpa ādi utkarṣasya api tvac indriyeṇa kārya abhāvena eva abhāva prasiddheḥ tathā ca sūtra kāreṇa api uktam rūpa ādiṣu spārśanam jñānam iti kasmāt na bhavati iti tad abhāvāt sparśa tva sāmānyasya abhāvāt yatra eva sparśa tva sāmānyam tatra eva spārśanam jñānam iti vyatirekaḥ labhyate eva sparśa tva abhāvaḥ tu tvac grāhya tva abhāvasya jñāpakaḥ na kārakaḥ iti na ca viśiṣṭa sannikarṣa vyatirekeṇa anyā yogyatā sambhāvyate anvaya vyatirekābhyām tasya eva vyāpāra upalabdheḥ iti alam 
[II,019,10]	rūpa anuvidhāyī iti sāhacaryam darśayati rūpam anuvidadhāti tad śīlaḥ ca iti tad anuvidhāyī yatra rūpam tatra avaśyam sparśaḥ iti evam rasa gandhā anuvidhāyi tvam api iti śīta uṣṇa anuṣṇa aśīta bhedāt trividhaḥ iti vibhāga kathanam asya api nitya anitya tva niṣpattayaḥ pūrvavat iti salila ādi paramāṇuṣu nityaḥ pārthiveṣu agni saṃyoga virodhī kāryeṣu kāraṇa guṇa pūrvakaḥ tad vināśāt vinaśyati iti atideśa arthaḥ 
[II,019,17_II,019,21]	atha idānīm pārthiva paramāṇu rūpa ādīnām iti parīkṣā śeṣa nivartana aprakaraṇam tathā hi rūpa ādīnām pūrvam uddeśa lakṣaṇa abhidhāne api sparśaḥ na parīkṣitaḥ pratijñā tañca tat atas parīkṣā artham idam ārabhyate pṛthivyāḥ ime pārthivāḥ nanu ca atra bheda anupapatteḥ katham ṣaṣṭhī tad hita pratyayaḥ ca iti tayoḥ bhede sati upalambhāt na kārya rūpāyāḥ pṛthivyāḥ vivakṣita tvāt tad janakāḥ ca paramāṇavaḥ tatas bhinnāḥ eva iti pārthivāḥ iti ucyante jātiḥ vā pṛthivī śabdena vivakṣitā tasyāḥ ime tad sambandhinaḥ pārthivāḥ te ca te paramāṇavaḥ ca teṣām rūpa ādayaḥ iti ādipadena rasa gandha sparśāḥ eva gṛhyante na saṃkhyā ādayaḥ tad parīkṣā śeṣa paratvena eva sambandhāt 
[II,020,1]	atas teṣām pākaja utpatti vidhānam prakāraḥ iti atha pākāt jātāḥ pāka jāḥ iti utpatti arthasya janinā pratipādita tvāt vyartham utpatti grahaṇam na uttara padena sambandhāt tathā hi pāka jānām utpattiḥ eva vidhīyate anena iti vidhānam pramāṇam upeyam pūrva guṇa vilakṣaṇānām rūpa ādīnām utpattiḥ kārye sā eva pramāṇam iti vakṣyāmaḥ 
[II,020,6_II,020,14]	yat vā pacyate anena iti pākaḥ tejaḥ dravyam pacyate iti vā pākaḥ pārthiva paramāṇavaḥ ca iti pākau tābhyām jātaḥ pākajaḥ pārthiva paramāṇu agni saṃyogaḥ tasmāt utpattiḥ pārthiva paramāṇu rūpa ādīnām śyāma ādi vināśaḥ ca iti uttara vākya sāmarthyāt anye tu śyāma ādi vināśaḥ adhyāhāreṇa labhyate iti manyamānāḥ pacyate anena iti pākaḥ agni saṃyogaḥ tasmāt jātaḥ pākajaḥ śyāma ādi vināśaḥ tatas eva pākāt utpattiḥ viśiṣṭa rūpa ādīnām iti kaṣṭa vyākhyānam kurvate tat ca asat adhyāhāra ādeḥ dūṣaṇasya aparihārāt na ca abhivyakti nivṛtti artham utpatti grahaṇam iti vācyam paramatasya aprasiddha tvāt 
[II,020,17_II,020,24]	atha kena prakāreṇa pāka jāḥ jāyante iti upadarśayati ghaṭa ādeḥ āma dravyasya ityādinā ghaṭa ādeḥ iti ādi padena śarīra ādeḥ api avarodhaḥ tatra hi pākaja utpatti parijñānāt tad āsakti nivṛttau viraktasya śreyaḥ sampadyate iti āma dravyasya iti pakva vyavaccheda artham yadi api pārthiva paramāṇuṣu ahetukasya rūpa ādeḥ asambhavāt te api pākāt utpannāḥ tathā api viśiṣṭa rūpa apekṣayā śyāma ādayaḥ iti ucyante tad āśrayasya āma dravyasya ye ārambhakāḥ pāramparyeṇa paramāṇavaḥ teṣu karmāṇi utpadyante kutas agni abhighātāt nodanāt vā 
[II,021,1_II,021,9]	abhighātaḥ tu vega apekṣaḥ paraspara vibhāga hetoḥ ekasya karmaṇaḥ kāraṇam na udanantu avibhāga hetoḥ anekasya iti vakṣyāmaḥ karma adhikāre anye tu ghaṭasya ādiḥ dvi aṇukam tad ārambhakāḥ paramāṇavaḥ sākṣāt iti manyante tatra karma utpattau aṇavaḥ samavāyi kāraṇam tad saṃyogaḥ asamavāyi kāraṇam vega ādi nimitta kāraṇam iti tebhyaḥ vibhāgāḥ te tu dravya ārambhaka saṃyoga pratidvandvinaḥ tatra api asamavāyi kāraṇam karma paramāṇvoḥ samavāyi tvam śeṣam nimitta kāraṇam iti vibhāgebhyaḥ saṃyoga vināśāḥ teṣām samavāyi ādi kāraṇa anupalabdheḥ nimittādeva utpattiḥ na hi abhāvaḥ samavetaḥ kvacid utpadyamānaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ atas eva asamavāyi kāraṇam na asti eka artha samavāya abhāvāt nimittakāraṇantu anvaya vyatirekābhyām vyāpriyamāṇam tad utpattau upalabdham saṃyoga vināśebhyaḥ kārya dravyam dvi aṇuka lakṣaṇam vinaśyati iti jāti apekṣayā eka vacanam

[II,021,17_II,021,24]	tasmin vinaṣṭe paramāṇuṣu anyasmāt agni saṃyogāt śyāma ādīnām nivṛttiḥ punar anyasmāt agni saṃyogāt auṣṇya apekṣyāt pāka jāḥ jāyante tatra paramāṇuḥ samavāyi kāraṇam agni saṃyogaḥ asamavāyi kāraṇam uṣṇa sparśaḥ nimitta kāraṇam iti tad anantaram rakta ādi utpatti kṣaṇa anantaram utpanna pāka jeṣu aṇuṣu samavetāni kāryāṇi utpadyante asamavāyi kāraṇam āha ātmā aṇu saṃyogāt adṛṣṭa apekṣāt adṛṣṭañca keṣām iti āha bhoginām iti 
[II,022,1]	karma utpattau satyām anantaram vibhāgāḥ tebhyaḥ saṃyoga vināśāḥ tatas paramāṇūnām paraspareṇa saṃyogāt dvi aṇukāni utpadyante tatra paramāṇvoḥ samavāyi tvam tad saṃyogasya asamavāyi kāraṇa tvam śeṣam nimittam iti tad ādi krameṇa kāryam utpadyate iti tribhiḥ dvi aṇukaiḥ tri aṇukam ārabhyate tri aṇukaiḥ ca aniyamena sva kāryam iti tāvat yāvat ghaṭaḥ sarvatra kāraṇa guṇa pūrva prakrameṇa rūpa ādi utpattiḥ iti 
[II,022,6_II,022,9]	nanu sarvam etat asambaddham etasmin krame pramāṇa abhāvāt tathā hi paramāṇau kriyāyāḥ sadbhāve pramāṇa abhāvāt tad kāryasya asiddhau tat dvi aṇukasya vināśena pramāṇam asti agni saṃyogasya nānā tve dravya vināśe śyāma ādi nivṛttau rakta ādi utpattau utpanna pāka jeṣu kriyā krameṇa tat dvi aṇukasya eva utpattiḥ iti sarvam pramāṇa śūnyam eva 
[II,022,12_II,022,15]	bādhaka upapatteḥ ca tathā hi āpāka nikṣipteṣu ghaṭa ādiṣu kulālasya chidra pradeśena nirīkṣamāṇasya akṣajam vijñānam ghaṭaḥ pacyate iti na ca idam saṃśaya viparyaya svarūpam tad lakṣaṇa alakṣita tvāt bādhaka anupapatteḥ ca tathā pāka uttara kālam saḥ eva ayam ghaṭaḥ iti abādhyamānasya pratyabhijñānasya upalabdheḥ 
[II,022,17_II,022,20]	avasthānam upari sthāpita anāñca tṛṇa karpara ādīnām apātāt ca avasthāyi tvam yadi hi paramāṇavaḥ pacyeran ūrdhva sthāpitānām karpara ādīnām pātaḥ syāt paramāṇūnāñca dhāraṇa sāmarthya abhāvāt tad deśa tva tad parimāṇa tva tad saṃkhyā tva upalabdheḥ ca yadi ca utpanna pāka jāḥ paramāṇavaḥ dvi aṇuka ādi prakrameṇa ghaṭa ādikam ārabheran tad deśam tāvat parimāṇam tad saṃkhyā ca na syāt niyama hetoḥ abhāvāt dṛṣṭaḥ ca ayam niyamaḥ tasmin eva deśe tāvat parimāṇam tad saṃkhyā ca evam ghaṭa ādīnām avasthāyi tvam 
[II,022,24]	na ca ghaṭa ādeḥ vināśe kartṛ ādibhiḥ vinā punar utpattiḥ yuktā atha īśvara ādeḥ sadbhāvāt yuktam iti ced tathā hi īśvaraḥ kartā kāraṇam adṛṣṭa ādi paramāṇavaḥ karma iti na etat yuktam kṣiti ādi kāryeṣu iva asmad ādi sambandha āditaḥ kārya anapekṣasya ghaṭa ādi sampādane api sāmarthya anivṛtteḥ kulāla vyāpāra vaiyarthyam eva syāt 
[II,023,1]	āvaraṇa abhāvaḥ ca tathā hi vegāt agni sambandhāt avayava kriyā krameṇa ghaṭa ādeḥ vināśaḥ tathā vegāt ca cakṣuḥ sambandhāt kāca abhra sphaṭika ādeḥ kriyā krameṇa vināśe tad vyavahitena sambaddhasya cakṣuṣaḥ prakāśaka tvam iti āvaraṇa abhāvaḥ syāt atha svaccha tayā sphaṭika ādi dravyam indriya vyavadhāyakam na bhavati iti upapannam eva āvṛtasya api grahaṇam tarhi ghaṭa ādi dravyam api tathā asvabhāva tayā tejaḥ dravya vyavadhāyakam na bhavati iti aṇu praveśāt antar deśe api upapadyate evam pākaḥ anyathā hi āvṛta anāvṛtayoḥ tulya upalabdhiḥ syāt āvaraṇa abhāvasya ubhayatra aviśeṣāt 
[II,023,8_II,023,19]	yadi cāṇu praveśāt dravyasya vināśaḥ tarhi bahis deśe śīta sparśa upalambhāni atha anupapattyā udakasya niḥsaraṇāt ādhārasya vināśe tad pātaḥ syāt atha sa chidra dravyam iti udakasya niḥsaraṇam tarhi tad mārgeṇa eva tejaḥ aṇu praveśāt antar deśe pākaḥ sampadyate iti kim tad vināśena iti alam sarvam etat abādhakam anaikāntika tvāt tathā hi udaka paripūrṇe ghaṭe vegavat sucī dravya sambandhāt avaśyam kaṇṭha pradeśe kriyā sā ca utpannā dravya ārambhaka saṃyoga pratidvandvinam vibhāgam ārabhate iti pratyakṣa siddham tasmāt saṃyoga vināśe tad ā ārabdhasya dravyasya nivṛttiḥ tasya api dravya antara ārambhaka tvāt tad nivṛttau tadārabdha nivṛttiḥ iti vināśa kāraṇa sānnidhyāt ghaṭasya vināśaḥ anyathā hi vināśa kāraṇa sānnidhye api avināśe kāryasya nitya tvam eva syāt upalabhyate tu ghaṭaḥ iti avasthita saṃyogaiḥ dravya antara ārambhaḥ niścīyate tatra ca pratyakṣam saḥ eva ayam iti pratyabhijñānam na vyāvṛttam upari sthāpita dravyasya pātaḥ tad deśa tvam tad saṃkhyā tvam tad parimāṇa tvam pratyakṣeṇa ca kartṛ ādeḥ anupalabdhiḥ tatra asti iti anekānta āda sādhanam na ca ghaṭasya vināśe api udakasya ānāśita tvam pātaḥ vā dṛśyate iti 
[II,023,24_II,024,1]	atha paramāṇuṣu pāka jāḥ jāyante iti kim atra asmad ādīnām pramāṇam ghaṭa ādiṣu pūrva guṇa vilakṣaṇasya guṇa antarasya utpādaḥ iti sa ca ghaṭa ādiṣu vartamānaḥ katham paramāṇuṣu pāka jāḥ jāyante iti gamayet tatra agni saṃyogena tathā anupapatteḥ tat eva āha na ca kārya dravye rūpa ādi vināśaḥ utpattiḥ vā sambhavati kasmāt sarva avayaveṣu antar bahis ca vartamānasya agninā vyāpti abhāvāt tathā hi avayavī sarva avayaveṣu antar bahis ca vartate na ca antar deśe agneḥ anupraveśaḥ asti iti vyāptyā sambandha abhāvāt apāka prasaṅgaḥ 
[II,024,8_II,024,14]	atha sūkṣmasya tejasaḥ anupraveśāt antar deśe pākaḥ sampadyate iti āha aṇu praveśāt api vyāptiḥ na sambhavati kasmāt kārya dravya vināśāt iti tathā hi vegavat dravya sambandhasya anyatra kriyā hetu tvena upalambhāt iha api avayave kriyā janaka tvam sā ca avayava antareṇa vibhāgam dravya ārambhaka saṃyoga pratidvandvinam ārabhate tasmāt saṃyoga nivṛttau tad ā ārabdhasya kārya dravyasya vināśe tad ā ārabdhasya api nivṛttiḥ iti krameṇa ghaṭasya api avaśyam vināśaḥ atha ghaṭa avayavāḥ patryante tatra api antar deśe pākaḥ na syāt iti tejaḥ aṇu praveśena vināśaḥ tat evam uttarottara avayaveṣu agni aṇu praveśāt tad vināśe svatantrāḥ paramāṇavaḥ pacyante 
[II,024,17]	na ca kārya dravye pūrvarūpa ādīnām avasthāne rakta ādi utpattiḥ syāt guṇavati guṇa antara pratiṣedhāt atas rakta ādi utpatti anyathā anupapattyā jñāyate pūrvarūpa ādi nivṛttiḥ sā ca āśraya vināśāt eva kārya dravye tathā ca sūtram rūpa rasa gandha sparśāḥ dravya anitya tvāt anityāḥ iti āśraya vināśena vināśaḥ abhihitaḥ kārya dravye agni saṃyogāt ca etena nityeṣu anitya tvam vyākhyātam iti agni saṃyogasya nityeṣu eva rūpa ādi nivartaka tvam uktam atas kārya dravye guṇa antara prādurbhāvāt pūrvarūpa ādi nivṛttiḥ jñāyate sā ca āśraya vināśāt eva agni saṃyogasya nitya viṣaya tvena niyamāt 
[II,024,25_II,025,3]	evam kapālānām api avasthāne pūrvarūpa ādi anivṛttau rakta ādi utpattiḥ na syāt atas kārye api kāraṇa rūpa anuvidhāyitayā śyāma ādikam utpadyate tat evam tad kāraṇa kāraṇeṣu api pūrva guṇa vilakṣaṇasya guṇa antarasya utpattiḥ vācyā anyathā hi tad kāryeṣu api na syāt sā ca utpattiḥ pūrvarūpa ādīnām avasthāne na ghaṭate rūpavati rūpa antara ārambha pratiṣedhāt iti pūrvarūpa ādi nivṛttiḥ vācyā sā ca āśraya vināśāt eva iti sakalasya api kārya dravyasya api vināśaḥ 
[II,025,6]	na ca paramāṇuṣu api pūrvarūpa ādīnām avasthāne rakta ādi utpattiḥ syāt tad abhāvāt dvi aṇukasya api kāraṇa guṇa pūrva krameṇa śyāma ādikam eva utpadyate iti vilakṣaṇa rūpa ādi asambhavaḥ eva dṛṣṭaḥ ca kārye guṇa antara prādurbhāvaḥ tena paramāṇuṣu rūpa ādi nivṛttau rakta ādi utpattiḥ iti na ca tatra āśrayasya vināśaḥ sambhavati iti agni saṃyogasya eva nivartaka tvam kāraṇa antarasya asambhavāt tasya eva utpādaka tvam iti 
[II,025,11_II,025,14]	yat api idam sa chidra dravyam iti uktam tatra yadi kapāla randhra apekṣayā tasya antar deśe pākaḥ na syāt atha tad avayava randhra apekṣayā tasya antar deśe pāka abhāvaḥ tat evam uttarottara avayaveṣu api vācyam tāvat yāvat dvi aṇukam atha tasya antardeśa abhāvāt pākaḥ bhaviṣyati iti na tasya api vegavat agni sambandhena avaśyam vināśa upapatteḥ śyāma ādi vināśañca vinā rakta ādi utpattiḥ na syāt tad vināśaḥ ca āśraya vināśāt eva iti ukta pūrvam sa ca saṃyoga vināśāt saḥ api vibhāgāt vibhāgaḥ ca kriyātaḥ iti guṇa antara prādurbhāvaḥ eva kriyā ādi krama astitve pramāṇam iti 
[II,025,19_II,025,24]	atra tu prayogaḥ pārthiva paramāṇu rūpa ādayaḥ saṃyoga jāḥ vibhāga ja vibhāga śabda ja śabda anyatva anitya tve sati nityasya viśeṣa guṇa tvāt sukha ādi vat vibhāga ja vibhāga śabda ja śabdena vyabhicāra parihāra artham tad anya tve sati iti salila ādi paramāṇu rūpa ādi vyavaccheda arthañca anitya padam sāmānya guṇa vyavaccheda artham viśeṣa guṇa grahaṇam anitya vyavacchedaḥ ca nitya padena iti anye tu ghaṭa ādi gatāḥ rūpa ādayaḥ pāramparyeṇa agni saṃyoga jāḥ sākṣāt ghaṭamāna tve sati agni saṃyoga tad bhāva bhāvi tvena utpadyamāna tvāt śrūyamāṇā agni śabda vat iti anumānam bruvate na ca asiddham viśeṣaṇa mukta nyāyāt 
[II,025,27]	yat ca idam agni saṃyogasya nānātve pramāṇa abhāvaḥ iti etat asat tasya eva kārya bhedena nānātva upacārāt yadā śyāma ādi nivartikā vahnau kriyā utpannā tadā prāktana ākāśa ādi deśena vibhāgam ārabhate tadā eva tad avayave rakta ādi utpādake ca vahnau karma iti ekaḥ kālaḥ tatas vibhāgāt saṃyoga vināśaḥ avayava karmaṇā ca avayava antarāt vibhāgaḥ kriyate rakta ādi utpādaka agni karmaṇā ca ākāśa ādi deśena iti ekaḥ kālaḥ tatas śyāma ādi nivartakasya agneḥ paramāṇunā saṃyogaḥ śyāma ādīnām vinaśyattā avayava vibhāgāt ca dravya ārambhaka saṃyoga vināśaḥ śyāma ādi ucchedakasya agneḥ vinaśyattā rakta ādi utpādakasya agneḥ prāktana saṃyoga vināśaḥ paramāṇunā ca saṃyogasya utpadyam āna tā iti ekaḥ kālaḥ tatas śyāma ādīnām vināśaḥ tad ucchedakasya agneḥ vināśaḥ saṃyogasya vinaśyattā rakta ādi janakasya agni saṃyogasya utpādaḥ rakta ādīnām utpadyamāna tā iti ekaḥ kālaḥ tatas rakta ādīnām utpādaḥ śyāma ādi nivartaka agni saṃyogasya vināśaḥ iti agni saṃyogasya nānātvam na ca śyāma ādi ucchedaka agni saṃyogasya vinaśyat avastha tvāt rūpa ādi utpattau asamavāyikāraṇa tvam iti 
[II,026,14_II,026,16]	anye tu śyāma ādi nivartakasya agneḥ karma sama kālam tad avayave api karma sañcintanāt śyāma ādi nivṛtti sama kālam eva tad saṃyogasya vināśaḥ iti bruvate atha utpanna pāka jeṣu kriyā kramasya sadbhāve kim pramāṇam kārya dravyasya utpattiḥ eva anyathā hi kriyām antareṇa parasparam aprāptānām dravya ārambhaka tvam na syāt 
[II,026,19]	atha paramāṇūnām dvi aṇuka ārambhaka tvam eva iti pramāṇa abhāvaḥ tat na ekatva vat bahu tva pakṣe bādhaka sadbhāvāt dvi tva saṃkhyā upetānām eva ārambhaka tva prasiddheḥ tathā hi bahūnām ārambhaka tve śata ādi saṃkhyā upetānām api ārambhaka tvam eva syāt evañca sati ghaṭa ādi kāryam paramāṇubhiḥ ārabdham iti ced bhaṅge avāntara kāryasya anutpanna tvāt upalambhaḥ na syāt upalabhyate tu ghaṭasya vināśe tad avayavāḥ iti tad avayave api tad avayavāḥ iti dvi aṇuka ādi krameṇa ārambhaḥ niścīyate 
[II,026,25]	atha dravyāṇi dravya antaram ārabhante saṃyogānām dravyam iti ca sūtra vyāghātaḥ na dvi vacana bahuvacanābhyām vigraha āśraya tvāt tathā hi dravye ca dravyāṇi iti eka śeṣaḥ kārya dravya apekṣayā tu bahuvacanam bahūni kārya dravyāṇi eva dravyam ārabhante dvi tva saṃkhyā upetāni eva ca nityāni na tu nityāni eva kārya dravye api sadbhāvāt 
[II,027,3_II,027,6]	na ca ekasya krama yaugapadyābhyām ārambhaka tvam eka svabhāva tvāt tathā hi ekaḥ paramāṇuḥ na krameṇa kāryam karoti samarthasya kṣepā yogāt yugapad kṛtvā punar akaraṇe hetu abhāvaḥ na ca samāna parimāṇa tāyām kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ kṣaṇa bhaṅga pratiṣedhāt kāraṇa vibhāga abhāvāt avināśi tvam kārya dravyasya ca prasajyate 
[II,027,8_II,027,14]	tathā saṃyogaḥ ca saṃyogau ca saṃyogāḥ ca iti saṃyogāḥ teṣām dravyam kāryam iti nitya apekṣayā saṃyogasya eva kārya dravye ca aniyamaḥ iti avirodhaḥ tat evam dvi tva saṃkhyā upetāḥ paramāṇavaḥ kārya dravyam ārabhante eka tva bahutva pakṣe bādhaka pramāṇa sadbhāve satya ārambhaka tvāt dvi tvantu dvi aṇuka ārambhakaḥ tantu dvitaya vat na hi bahubhiḥ tantubhiḥ dvitantukam ārabhyate na api ekena iti sa viśeṣaṇasya hetoḥ asadbhāvaḥ atha dvi aṇukāni dvi tva ādi saṃkhyā upetāni aniyamena kim iti kāryam na ārabhante bādhaka upapatteḥ tathā hi dvayoḥ dvi aṇu kayoḥ ārambhaka tve aṇu parimāṇa utpattau eva kāraṇa tvam asti iti vyartha ārambha prasaṅgaḥ 
[II,027,17]	na ca dvi aṇuka dvayasya kāraṇa paramāṇu apekṣayā bahu tvam sambhavati iti vācyam na kāraṇa avṛtti bahutvasya parimāṇa utpattau akāraṇa tvāt kāraṇa vṛtti ca bahu tvam mahat tva utpattau kāraṇam iti dṛṣṭam anyathā hi dvi aṇuke api mahat tvam syāt akāraṇa apekṣitayā bahu tvasya tatra api sambhavāt tathā dvi aṇukasya api bahu tva saṃkhyā upetasya eva mahat ārambhaka tvam iti param dvi aṇukasya etat kalpanīyam iti ekasya ca ārambhaka tvam pratiṣiddham 
[II,027,23]	atha catuṣṭvādi saṃkhyā upetānām aniyamena ārambhaka tvam iti na iṣyate sākṣāt ghaṭa ādi ārambhaka tva prasaṅgāt tad bhaṅge ca avāntara kāryasya anupalabdhiḥ eva anutpanna tvāt na ca bahu tvam vinā mahat tvam sambhāvyate iti tritva saṃkhyā upetānām eva ārambhaka tvam tathā hi dvi aṇukāni tritva saṃkhyā upetāni eva dravyam ārabhante dvi tva catuṣṭu ādi pakṣe bādhaka pramāṇa sadbhāve sati ārambhaka tvāt tri tantuka ārambhe tantu tritaya vat 
[II,028,1_II,028,2]	atra tu kiyatā kālena dvi aṇuke rūpa ādi utpattiḥ iti kriyā nirūpyate tatra sva kāraṇāt dvi aṇukasya vināśaḥ tad kāryasya vinaśyattā śyāma ādi ucchedaka agni saṃyogasya utpādaḥ śyāma ādīnām vinaśyattā rakta ādi utpādaka agni saṃyogasya utpadyamāna tā vibhāga ja vibhāgasya utpādaḥ paramāṇvoḥ ākāśa ādi deśena saṃyogasya vinaśyatta iti eṣām ekaḥ kālaḥ 
[II,028,6_II,028,10]	tatas tri aṇukasya vināśaḥ tad kāryasya vinaśyattā śyāma ādīnām vināśaḥ śyāma ādi ucchedaka agni saṃyogasya vinaśyattā rakta ādi utpādaka agni saṃyogasya utpādaḥ rakta ādīnām utpadyamāna tā ākāśa dvi aṇuka saṃyogasya vināśaḥ uttara saṃyogasya utpadyam āna tā iti eṣām ekaḥ kālaḥ tatas tad kāryasya vināśāt tad kāryasya vinaśyattā śyāma ādi ucchedaka agni saṃyogasya vināśaḥ rakta ādīnām utpādaḥ rakta ādi utpādaka agni saṃyogasya vinaśyattā tathā uttara saṃyogasya utpādaḥ vibhāga vibhāga ja vibhāga karmaṇām vinaśyattā kriyāyāḥ utpadyam ānatā iti eṣām ekaḥ kālaḥ 
[II,028,14_II,028,19]	tatas tad kārya vināśaḥ tad kāryasya vinaśyattā vibhāga vibhāga ja vibhāga karmaṇām vināśaḥ rakta ādi utpādaka agni saṃyogasya vināśaḥ kriyāyāḥ utpādaḥ vibhāgasya utpadyamāna tā iti eṣām ekaḥ kālaḥ tatas tad kārya vināśāt tad kāryasya vinaśyattā vibhāgasya utpādaḥ saṃyogasya vinaśyatta iti eṣām ekaḥ kālaḥ tatas tad kārya vināśāt tad kāryasya vinaśyattā saṃyogasya vināśaḥ uttara saṃyogasya utpadyamāna tā iti ekaḥ kālaḥ 
[II,028,21_II,028,25]	tatas tad kārya vināśāt tad kāryasya vinaśyattā uttara saṃyogasya utpādaḥ dvi aṇukasya utpadyamāna tā vibhāga karmaṇoḥ vinaśyat ta iti eṣām ekaḥ kālaḥ tatas tad kāryasya vināśāt tad kāryasya vinaśyattā dvi aṇukasya utpādaḥ rūpa ādīnām utpadyamāna tā vibhāga karmaṇoḥ vināśaḥ iti eṣām ekaḥ kālaḥ tatas utpanne dvi aṇuke kāraṇa guṇa pūrva prakrameṇa navame kṣaṇe rūpa ādi utpattiḥ iti 
[II,028,27_II,029,4]	yadā tu kārya vināśa viśiṣṭam kālam apekṣya iti asya dravya nāśa viśiṣṭam kālam apekṣya kāraṇayoḥ vartamānaḥ vibhāgaḥ kārya saṃyukta ākāśa deśena vibhāgam ārabhate iti vyākhyātam tadā śyāma ādi nivṛtti sama kālam vibhāga ja vibhāga sañcintanāt daśame kṣaṇe dvi aṇuke rūpa ādi utpattiḥ iti cintanīyam tathā ca dvi aṇuka vināśe śyāma ādi nivṛttiḥ tatas rakta ādi utpattiḥ uttara saṃyogaḥ kriyā vibhāga saṃyoga vināśaḥ paramāṇūnāñca saṃyogāt dvi aṇuka utpattau kāraṇa guṇa pūrva prakrameṇa rūpa ādi utpattiḥ iti śeṣam pūrvavat iti idam ekasmin paramāṇau dravya utpādikā tad vināśikā iti ca kriyā dvayam adhikṛtya uktam 
[II,029,8_II,029,10]	yadā tu ekasmin paramāṇau dravya vināśikāni asmin ca dravya utpādikeṣyate tadā katham tatra dravya ārambhaka saṃyoga vināśa sama kālam dvitīya paramāṇau dravya ārambhakam karma tatas dravya ārambhaka saṃyoga vināśāt dvi aṇukasya vināśaḥ tad kāryasya vinaśyattā śyāma ādi ucchedaka agni saṃyogasya utpādaḥ śyāma ādīnām ucchidyamāna tā rakta ādi utpādaka agni saṃyogasya utpadyamāna tā vibhāga ja vibhāgasya utpādaḥ paramāṇoḥ ākāśa ādi deśena saṃyogasya vinaśyattā dvitīya paramāṇau vibhāgasya utpādaḥ prāktana saṃyogasya vinaśyatta iti eṣām ekaḥ kālaḥ 
[II,029,16]	tatas tri aṇukasya vināśaḥ tad kāryasya vinaśyattā śyāma ādīnām vināśaḥ tad ucchedaka agni saṃyogasya vinaśyattā rakta ādi utpādaka agni saṃyogasya utpādaḥ rakta ādīnām utpadyamāna tā ākāśa dvi aṇuka saṃyogasya vināśaḥ tasya paramāṇoḥ ākāśa ādi deśena saṃyogasya utpadyamāna tā dvitīya paramāṇau prāktana saṃyoga vināśaḥ paramāṇunā ca saṃyogasya utpadyam āna tā iti eṣām ekaḥ kālaḥ 
[II,029,21]	tatas tad kārya vināśāt tad kāryasya vinaśyattā śyāma ādi ucchedaka agni saṃyogasya vināśaḥ rakta ādīnām utpādaḥ paramāṇoḥ ākāśa ādi deśena saṃyogasya utpādaḥ vibhāga ja vibhāga karmaṇoḥ vinaśyattā dvitīyasya paramāṇoḥ paramāṇu antareṇa saṃyogasya utpādaḥ tad vibhāga karmaṇoḥ vinaśyattā dvi aṇukasya utpadyam āna tā iti eṣām ekaḥ kālaḥ 
[II,029,26_II,030,4]	tatas tad kārya vināśāt tad kāryasya vinaśyattā vibhāga ja vibhāga karmaṇām vināśaḥ dvitīya paramāṇau api vibhāga karmaṇoḥ vināśaḥ dvi aṇukasya utpādaḥ rakta ādīnām utpadyamāna tā iti eṣām ekaḥ kālaḥ tatas dvi aṇuka utpatti anantaram pañcame kṣaṇe kāraṇa guṇa pūrva prakrameṇa rūpa ādi utpattiḥ iti tathā dvi aṇuka vināśa sama kālam dvitīya paramāṇau karma sañcintanāt ṣaṣ kṣaṇā pākaja utpattiḥ tathā śyāma ādi nivṛtti sama kālam karma cintāyām saptakṣaṇā rakta ādi utpatti sama kālam karma cintanāt aṣṭakṣaṇā tad anantarañca karma cintāyām na vakṣaṇāḥ ityādi cintyam 
[II,030,8_II,030,10]	tatra ādau dvi aṇukāni pakva apakvaiḥ api paramāṇubhiḥ ārabhyante iti pakva apakvāni utpadyante tatas taiḥ tri aṇukam iti ādi prakrameṇa ghaṭasya pakvāpakvasya utpādaḥ tatas punar anutpanna pāka jeṣu kriyā ādi krameṇa dravya vināśe svatantreṣu paramāṇuṣu rakta ādi utpattiḥ tatas punar kriyā krameṇa uttara saṃyoga utpattau dvi aṇukāni utpadyante tatra ca kāraṇa guṇa pūrva prakrameṇa pakveṣu eva rūpa ādi utpadyate taiḥ tri aṇukam pakvam eva ārabhyate punar dvi aṇuka antareṣu api evam eva krameṇa rūpa ādi utpattiḥ tatas tri aṇuka ādeḥ iti vācyam yāvat ghaṭe viśiṣṭa rūpa ādi utpattiḥ iti 
[II,030,15_II,030,19]	nanu agni sambandhasya api śeṣāt anutpanna pāka jeṣu iva paramāṇuṣu utpanna pāka jeṣu api kriyā kim iti na iṣyate ghaṭa ādeḥ anutpatti prasaṅgāt yadi ca paramāṇuṣu utpanna pāka jeṣu ārabdha kāryeṣu kriyā syāt pratikṣaṇam utpatti anantaram dvi aṇuka ādi vināśe ghaṭa ādeḥ utpattiḥ na syāt atha sarveṣām paramāṇūnām pāke sati dvi aṇuka ādi prakrameṇa ghaṭa ādi utpadyate iti manuṣe tat asat upari sthāpitānām karpara ādīnām pāta prasaṅgāt paramāṇūnām dhāraṇa sāmarthya abhāvāt na ca etat asti tasmāt kārya utpatti anyathā anupapattyā jñāyate anutpanna pāka jeṣu eva kriyā utpadyate na utpanna pāka jeṣu upabhoga prāpaka adṛṣṭasya niyāmaka tvāt iti alam ati vistareṇa 
[II,030,24_II,031,3]	atha dvi aṇuka tri aṇuka ādīnām pakva apakvānām utpāda pūrvam punar pakvānām eva iti kalpanāyām kim pramāṇam kāryasya tathā adarśanam eva tathā hi ghaṭa ādi kāryam ādau pakva apakvam upalabhyate punar pakvam eva iti kāraṇa kāraṇeṣu api anumeyaḥ atra ca prayogaḥ dvi aṇukam ādau pakva apakvam utpadyate mahataḥ pārthiva dravyasya ārambhaka tvāt kapāla vat tathā ca tri aṇukam ādau pakva apakvam utpadyate mahataḥ pārthiva dravyasya kāryatvāt ghaṭa vat iti na ca yugapad aśeṣa paramāṇuṣu karma utpatti dvāreṇa pākaja utpattiḥ vyākhyeyā śīghra pāka anupalabdheḥ upari sthāpita anāñca pāta prasaṅgāt ca iti 
[II,031,6_II,031,10]	atha idānīm uddeśa krameṇa avasara prāptāyāḥ saṃkhyāyāḥ lakṣaṇa parīkṣā artham eka tva ādi vyavahāra hetuḥ saṃkhyā iti ādi prakaraṇam vyavahṛtiḥ vyavahāraḥ jñānam vyavahriyate anena iti vyavahāraḥ abhidhānam tayoḥ hetuḥ saṃkhyā iti ucyamāne sarve api padārthāḥ tathā bhavanti iti eka ādi grahaṇam tathā api eka ādi rūpasya vyavahāra hetu tvam ākāśa ātmanoḥ vidyate iti viśeṣaṇa tve satī iti viśeṣaṇa m ūhyam tathā api ekatva ādi sāmānyam evam bhavati iti dravya viśeṣaṇa tve sati iti padam ūhyam tathā hi saṃkhyā itarebhyaḥ bhidyate dravya viśeṣaṇa tve sati eka ādi vyavahāra hetu tvāt yaḥ tu na bhidyate na ca asau evam yathā rūpa ādiḥ iti vyavahāraḥ vā sādhyaḥ 
[II,031,18]	tatra saṃkhyāyāḥ tu āśraya dvāreṇa bheda nirūpaṇa artham lakṣaṇena lakṣyamāṇasya eka aneka tva upalabdhau saṃśaye sati tad nirāsa arthañca sā punar eka dravyā ca aneka dravyā ca iti vākyam ekam eva dravyam āśrayaḥ asyāḥ iti eka dravyā anekam eva dravyam āśrayaḥ asyāḥ iti aneka dravyā tatra eka dravyāyāḥ salila ādi paramāṇu rūpa ādīnām iva nitya anitya tva niṣpattayaḥ iti atideśam karoti 
[II,031,23]	nanu ca atra nitya tve sādhye hetuḥ na asti anitya tve tu dṛṣṭānta abhāvaḥ iti nyūnam vākyam na vyatireka mukhena hetoḥ lābhāt vigraha bhedena dṛṣṭāntasya iti tathā hi niṣpadyamāna tvāt anitya tvam iti ukte sāmarthyāt gamyate eva aniṣpadyamāna tvena nitya tvam iti dṛṣṭāntaḥ api salilam ādau yasya asau salila ādiḥ tasya paramāṇavaḥ tad rūpa ādīnām iva nitya tvam yathā hi salila ādi paramāṇuṣu aniṣpadyamāna tvāt rūpa ādayaḥ nityāḥ tadvat eka tvam nityeṣu aniṣpadyamāna tvena eva nityam iti 
[II,032,3_II,032,6]	anitya āyāntu salilasya ādi pāṭhā apekṣayā pṛthivī tasyāḥ paramāṇavaḥ tad rūpāṇām iva iti dṛṣṭāntaḥ tu yathā hi pārthiva paramāṇu rūpa ādayaḥ niṣpadyamāna tvāt anityāḥ tadvat eka tvam kāryeṣu niṣpadyamāna tvāt anityam iti na ca pārthiva paramāṇu rūpa ādīnām iva eka tva ādīnām agni saṃyogāt utpattiḥ vailakṣaṇya apratipatteḥ sparśe tu vailakṣaṇya apratipattau api agni saṃyoga ja tve anumānam uktam pṛthivī adhikāre na ca tad sāmānya guṇeṣu sambhavati iti 
[II,032,9_II,032,12]	anye tu salilañca tad ādi paramāṇavaḥ ca iti tad śabda lopena samāsam kurvate anitya tve salila rūpa ādi dṛṣṭāntaḥ nitya tā yāñca tad ādi paramāṇu rūpam iti alam aneka dravyā tu dvi tvam eva ādiḥ yasyāḥ sā dvi tva ādikā parārdham eva ante avasāne yasyāḥ sā parārdha antā na hi parārdhāt ūrdhvam iyattā vyavahāraḥ sambhavati iti āgame paṭhyate 
[II,032,16_II,032,22]	tasyāḥ khalu eka tvebhyaḥ aneka viṣaya buddhi sahitebhyaḥ niṣpattiḥ apekṣā buddhi vināśāt vināśaḥ iti saṃkṣepeṇa utpatti vināśa kāraṇam darśayati nanu ca atra bahu tva nirdeśāt dvi tva utpattiḥ na labhyate na hi dvi tvam eka tvebhyaḥ bhavati iti na dvi vacana bahuvacanābhyām vigraha āśrayaṇāt tathā hi ekatve aneka tvāni ca iti eka śeṣaḥ prakṛti sārūpyasya vivakṣita tvāt vacana sārūpyeṇa tu eka śeṣa abhyupagame dhava khadira ādiṣu eka śeṣa prasaṅgaḥ syāt atas ekatvebhyaḥ aneka tva saṃkhyā utpattiḥ iti anena dvi tva utpattiḥ vyākhyātā eva 
[II,033,2_II,033,4]	kiṃviśiṣṭebhyaḥ iti āha anekaḥ viṣayaḥ yasyāḥ sā aneka viṣayā sā ca asau buddhiḥ ca tayā sahitāni eka tvāni tebhyaḥ niṣpattiḥ iti apekṣā kāraṇa nirdeśaḥ anye tu tri tva ādi utpattiḥ eva atra saṅgraha vākye vivakṣitā dvi tva utpattiḥ ca upariṣṭāt bhaviṣyati iti manyante tat ca asat tri tva ādi utpatteḥ api upari sadbhāvena anarthakya prasaṅgāt 
[II,033,7]	evañca saṃkṣepeṇa utpatti vināśa kāraṇe prajñāpite viśeṣa ākāṅkṣitayā ajñasya praśnaḥ katham iti kena rūpeṇa utpattiḥ ca vināśaḥ ca bhavati iti āha yadā boddhuḥ ityādi tathā hi budhyate iti boddhā tasya boddhuḥ ātmanaḥ cakṣuṣā saha samāna asamāna jātīyayoḥ dravyayoḥ sannikarṣe sati iti aniyamam darśayati samāna asamānaḥ iti samāna jātīyayoḥ asamāna jātīyayoḥ ca dravyayoḥ sannikarṣe sati iti tad saṃyukta samaveta samaveta eka tva sāmānye jñānam utpadyate iti tena cakṣuṣā saṃyuktam dravyam tad samavetam eka tva guṇam tad samavetañca tad eka tva sāmānyam tasmin jñānam utpadyate pūrvam viśeṣaṇa tvāt tathā hi viśeṣaṇa jñānam ādau kāraṇa tvāt viśeṣyajñānantu paścāt kāryatvāt 
[II,033,16_II,033,20]	atas eva eka tva sāmānya jñāna utpattau satyām ekatva sāmānyañca tad sambandhaḥ ca tat jñānañca iti eka tva sāmānya tad sambandha tad jñānāni tebhyaḥ aneka viṣayiṇī ekā buddhiḥ utpadyate anekaḥ ca asau viṣayaḥ ca iti aneka viṣayaḥ saḥ asyāḥ vidyate iti aneka viṣayiṇī ekā ca na viṣaya bhede api bhidyate kaḥ ca asau anekaḥ viṣayaḥ iti āha eka tva guṇayoḥ iti eka tva guṇaḥ ca ekatva guṇaḥ ca iti eka tva guṇayoḥ viṣaya bhūtayoḥ yathā uktā buddhiḥ utpadyate eka tva sāmānya buddheḥ ca vinaśyattā tatas tām apekṣya eka tvābhyām sva āśrayayoḥ dvi tvam ārabhyate atra ca sva āśrayayoḥ iti samavāyi kāraṇa nirdeśaḥ tathā eka tvābhyām itya samavāyi kāraṇasya tām apekṣya iti apekṣā buddheḥ nimitta kāraṇa tvam eka tva sāmānya jñānasya ca vināśaḥ 
[II,033,26_II,034,3]	tatas samutpanne dvi tve tad saṃyukta samaveta samavāyāt dvi tva sāmānye jñānam utpadyate pūrvam viśeṣaṇa tvāt tasmāt sāmānya jñānāt apekṣā buddheḥ vinaśyattā vināśa kāraṇa sānnidhyam jñānasya jñāna antara virodhi tvāt dvi tva sāmānya tad jñāna tad sambandhebhyaḥ dvi tva guṇa buddheḥ utpadyamāna tā iti dvi tva sāmānyāt dvi tva sāmānya jñānāt dvi tva sāmānya guṇa sambandhāt dvi tva guṇa buddheḥ utpadyamāna tā utpatti kāraṇa sānnidhyam iti eṣām ekaḥ kālaḥ 
[II,034,10_II,034,13]	tatas idānīm apekṣā buddheḥ vināśaḥ tad vināśāt dvi tva guṇasya vinaśyattā dvi tva guṇa buddheḥ utpādaḥ tad sāmānya buddheḥ api vinaśyattā dvi tva guṇa tad jñāna tad sambandhebhyaḥ iti dvi tva guṇaḥ ca tat jñānañca tad sambandhaḥ ca iti tathā uktāḥ tebhyaḥ nimittebhyaḥ dve dravye iti dravya buddheḥ utpadyamāna tā iti ekaḥ kālaḥ 
[II,034,17_II,034,24]	tad anantaram dravya jñānasya utpādaḥ tasmāt dvi tva guṇa buddheḥ vinaśyattā sāmānya buddheḥ vināśaḥ apekṣā buddhi vināśāt guṇasya vināśaḥ saṃskārasya utpadyamāna tā iti eṣām ekaḥ kālaḥ jñānāt dvi tva guṇa buddheḥ vināśaḥ dravya buddheḥ api saṃskārāt iti ) tatas saṃskāra utpāde sati dravya buddheḥ guṇa buddheḥ vināśaḥ tatas dravya buddheḥ api saṃskārāt vināśaḥ iti 
[II,035,1]	nanu sarvam etat asambaddham saṃkhyā sadbhāve pramāṇa abhāvāt atha ekam dve trīṇi ityādi vyavahāraḥ pramāṇam tat na asya kalpanā jñāna tvāt na ca kalpanā jñānam artha vyavasthāpanāya alam tad abhāve api bhāvāt tathā hi nimitta nirvikalpaka jñāna krameṇa smaraṇa anantaram sa vikalpakam jñānam utpadyate na ca arthasya avasthānam kṣaṇika tvāt iti nirviṣaya tvam 
[II,035,6]	bādhaka upapatteḥ ca tathā hi utpadyamānam dvi tva ādi na dravya utpatteḥ pūrvam utpadyate tad abhāvāt na sama kālam kārya kāraṇa bhāva anupapatti prasaṅgāt atha uttara kālam tatra api kim tat svabhāvāt viparītāt vā iti tad svābhāvye kim dvi tva ādinā dravyasya eva tad svarūpa tvāt viparyaye tu katham tad svabhāvāt tasya utpattiḥ ekasmāt bahubhyaḥ ca dvi tva utpatti prasaṅgāt tad svabhāvatāyāḥ sarvatra aviśeṣāt 
[II,035,12_II,035,16]	tathā vṛtti anupapatteḥ ca dvi tvam anekasmin vartamānam eka deśena sarva ātmanā vā vartate na eka deśena tad abhāvāt na sarva ātmanā ubhaya vṛtti tva abhāva prasaṅgāt na ca yena eva sva rūpeṇa eka vṛttiḥ tena eva dravya antare api tayoḥ eka tā prasaṅgāt iti vṛtti anupapatteḥ asattvam tathā upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya sarvaiḥ agrahaṇāt yadi hi dvi tva ādeḥ sattvam upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta tvāt rūpa ādi vat sarva puruṣaiḥ gṛhyeta na tu upalabhyate tasmāt na asti iti 
[II,035,19_II,035,21]	samāna indriya grāhya tvāt ca yena indriyeṇa dravyam upalabhyate tena eva saṃkhyā api iti na tatas artha antaram bhede tu rūpa ādīnām iva asamāna indriya grāhya tvam api syāt itas api asattvam deśa bhedena anupalabdheḥ tad agrahe tad buddhi abhāvāt ca tathā grahaṇa anupapatteḥ ca tathā hi dvi tvam anekatra vartamānam katham indriyeṇa paricchidyeta yugapad sannikarṣa dvayasya manasā anadhiṣṭhita tvāt atha cakṣuḥ adhiṣṭhīyate tathā api aneka padārtha grahaṇa prasaṅgaḥ tasya manaḥ adhiṣṭhitasya aneka padārthaiḥ sambandhāt 
[II,035,25]	yathā ca saṃkhyā sambandhāt dravyeṣu eka ādi vyavahāraḥ tathā eka tva ādi guṇeṣu api eka ādi vyavahāre nimitta antara kalpanāyām tatra api eka ādi vyavahārasya sambhavāt anavasthā prasaṅgaḥ atha eka tva ādau eka ādi vyavahāraḥ tad svarūpa tayā dravye api tathā abhāva prasaṅgaḥ atha eka tva ādi sāmānye tad sāmānya anupapatteḥ eka ādi vyavahāraḥ tat ca kalpanā jñānam iti 
[II,036,4]	tat etat sarvam asāmpratam eka ādi vyavahārasya bādhakā sambhavena prāmāṇyāt tathā hi eka ādi jñānam artha anvaya vyatireka anuvidhānāt nīla ādi jñāna vat artha jam na ca artha adhīna tayā nirvikalpaka jñāna utpatti sama kālam eva tasya utpattiḥ saṅketa smaraṇasya sahakāriṇaḥ abhāvāt na api smṛti jam eva arthasya api tatra vyāpāra upalabdheḥ na ca smṛteḥ atiśaya ādhāyaka tvam anatiśaya nivartaka tvam vā kintu artha sadbhāve sati jñāna janaka tvam eva 
[II,036,10_II,036,13]	na ca arthasya indriyāṇām vā avicāraka tvāt prāk iva paścāt api ajanaka tvam iti dūṣaṇam tathā vṛtti anupapatteḥ deśa bhedena agrahaṇāt tad agrahe tad buddhi abhāvāt ca iti pūrvam eva avayavi samarthana avasare pratiṣedhāt na ca abādhyamānam api eka ādi jñānam apramāṇam iti nyāyyam nīla ādi jñānasya api apramāṇa tā prasaṅgāt atha nīlam vinā tat jñāne na syāt nīla ākāra tā tad eka tva ādi jñāne api samānam 
[II,036,16_II,036,18]	atha ekatva ādi jñānam śabda ākāram na ca arthe tad rūpa tā asti iti nirviṣaya tvam na nīla jñānasya api śabda ākāra tayā nirviṣayatā prasaṅgāt atha ādyam nīla jñānam nirvikalpakam artha jam uttarantu sa vikalpa kamaneka kṣaṇa vyavadhānāt artha apāye api utpadyate arthasya kṣaṇika tvāt śabda ākārātāyāḥ ca tatra asambhavāt iti nirviṣaya tvam iṣyate eva 
[II,036,21]	tat asat kṣaṇika tvasya pūrvam eva pratiṣedhāt nirvikalpaka jñāna utpattau iva arthasya sa vikalpaka jñāna utpattau anvaya vyatirekābhyām indriyeṇa saṅketa smaraṇena ca saha kṛtasya vyāpāra upalabdheḥ tathā hi idantayā jñāna utpatteḥ tatra indriyasya vyāpāraḥ niścīyate aṅgulyā vyapadiśyamāna tvāt arthasya ca iti anyathā hi indriyā arthayoḥ eka ādi jñāna utpattau vyāpāram antareṇa idantaya upalabdhiḥ aṅguli ādinā ca vyapadeśaḥ na syāt atha indriya jñānam manaḥ vijñāna krameṇa sa vikalpaka jñāna utpattau kāraṇam iti idantaya upalabdhiḥ aṅguli ādinā vyapadeśaḥ na artha jau iti ced na etasmin krame pramāṇa abhāvāt 
[II,037,3_II,037,6]	atha saṅkalpāt sadbhāva siddheḥ anyathā eka ādi vyavahāraḥ na syāt iti eṣā kalpanā kriyate tat asat vṛtti vikalpa ādeḥ bādhakasya pūrvam eva pratiṣedhāt saṃkhyā asadbhāva siddhau eka ādi vyavahārasya sākṣāt artha jatvā upapatteḥ śabda ākāra tā tu sa vikalpaka jñāne na sambhavati eva sa ākāravāda pratiṣedhasya vakṣyamāṇa tvāt kevalantu smṛti janita tvāt sa vikalpakam jñānam śabda ullekhena utpadyate nirvikalpa kantu ullekha śūnyam saṅketasmṛteḥ avyāpārāt 
[II,037,9]	na ca vāsanā prabhava tvam vāsanāyāḥ pūrvam eva pratiṣedhāt tathā hi bodha vyatirekeṇa anyā vāsanā na sambhavati iti uktam eva avayavi samarthana avasare yā tu vaiśeṣika upagatā smṛti anumeyā vāsanā sā na kāraṇam eka ādi vyavahāre tasyāḥ parokṣa kāraṇa tayā smṛti vilakṣaṇa tvāt tathā hi eka ādi jñānam aparokṣam indriya vyāpāreṇa idantayā utpadyate na ca smṛteḥ etat rūpa tvam asti iti na vāsanā prabhavam tathā ittham bhūta vāsanā prabhava tve api paramparayā artha vyavasthāpaka tvam artha anubhava pūrvaka tvāt vāsanāyāḥ yā tu eka tva ādi śabdebhyaḥ vikalpāt vāsanā sā api artham vyavasthāpayati eva śabdasya anubhava pūrvaka tvena abhyupagamāt dṛṣṭe dṛṣṭa vādi tvam iti anena 
[II,037,18]	yat tu utpatti vikalpanāt eka tva ādeḥ asattvam iti uktam tat asat uttara kālam tad utpatti abhyupagamāt atha kim tat svabhāvāt viparītāt vā iti uktam tatra yadi tat svābhāvyam tad utpādana sāmarthyam vivakṣitam tat iṣyate eva atha ekatva ādi āśraya tvam tat na asti utpatteḥ pūrvam tad abhāvāt siddhe ca saṃkhyā sadbhāve pramāṇataḥ tasyāḥ kārya dravye kṛtaka tvāt avaśyam utpatti kāraṇam vācyam tatra ca eka tva dvi tva ādi āśrayasya tad janaka tve tad abhāvaḥ syāt dṛṣṭā ca utpattiḥ tasmāt dravyam itara kāraka upacitam teṣām kāraṇam iti utpatti vikalpa anupapattiḥ 
[II,037,25]	yat ca idam upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya anupalabdheḥ dvi tva ādeḥ asattvam iti tat na asiddha tvāt tathā ca yadīyayā apekṣā buddhyā sampāditam dvi tva ādi tasya eva upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptam na puruṣa antarasya tasya eva tad upalambhāt yatra upalambhaḥ tatra eva rūpi dravye samavāyi kāraṇa tvam iṣṭam na tad abhāve api iti tasmāt na sakala puruṣa apekṣayā tad upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptam iti asiddhaḥ hetuḥ 
[II,038,4_II,038,8]	yat ca idam eka tva ādeḥ na dravya vyatirekeṇa astitvam samāna indriya grāhya tvāt iti tatra pratijñā vākye padayoḥ vyāghātaḥ yathā idañca na asti ca iti na ca eka tva ādeḥ pakṣīkaraṇam yuktam aprasiddha tvāt prasiddhañca pakṣīkriyamāṇam dṛṣṭam śabda ādi na ca parasya eka tva ādi prasiddham iti atha para vyāptyā parasya aniṣṭa āpādanam prasaṅga sādhanam iti ced tatra yadi pramāṇa pūrvikā para prasiddhiḥ tayā eva bādhyamāna tvāt anutthānam viparīta anumānasya atha apramāṇa pūrvikā tarhi pramāṇam vinā prameyasya aprasiddheḥ ekatva ādīnām pakṣīkaraṇam ayuktam 
[II,038,12]	tathā samāna indriya grāhya tvāt iti yena indriyeṇa dravyam upalabhyate tena eva saṃkhyā api iti sādhanasya rūpa ādi bhedaiḥ anaikāntika tvam tathā hi yena eva indriyeṇa śukla rūpasya grahaṇam tena eva pīta ādeḥ na ca tasya tasmāt bhedaḥ asattvam vā iti na ca parasya dravyam prasiddham iti katham tasmāt abhedaḥ sādhyate atha rūpam eva dravyam na tarhi samāna indriya grāhya tvam rūpasya eka indriya grāhya tvāt saṃkhyāyāḥ tu dvi indriya paricchedya tvāt iti 
[II,038,17]	atha rūpa ādi samudāyaḥ dravyam tathā api samāna indriya grāhya tvam asiddham rūpa ādeḥ pratiniyata indriya grāhya tvāt na ca rūpa ādīnām pratiniyata indriya grāhya tvāt bhedaḥ śukla ādi bhedānām ekatā prasaṅgāt kim tarhi pratibhāsa bhedāt sa ca iha api asti eva tathā hi ekatra dravya pratibhāsaḥ anyatra ca eka tva ādi pratibhāsaḥ iti atha saṃkhyā dravyayoḥ pratyakṣeṇa bheda prasiddheḥ eka tā sādhanam pratyakṣeṇa bādhyamāna tvāt kāla atyaya apadiṣṭam bhavati iti 
[II,038,23]	yat ca idam utpannasya dvi tva ādeḥ grahaṇa anupapatteḥ asattvam tat asat indriya vyāpāreṇa asya dvi tva ādeḥ aparokṣasya dṛṣṭa tvāt na ca manasā anadhiṣṭhitasya indriyasya paricchedaka tvam yugapad jñāna utpatti prasaṅgāt atas cakṣuḥ manasā adhiṣṭhīyate na sambandhaḥ teṣām aṇu parimāṇa sambandhi tayā na yugapad adhiṣṭhāyakam manaḥ iti dvi tva ādeḥ agrahaṇam eva syāt asti ca grahaṇam atas cakṣuḥ eva manasā adhiṣṭhīyate nanu evam api aneka padārtha sambandhāt yugapad aneka jñāna utpādakam syāt na karaṇasya eka pratyaya nirvṛttau sāmarthyāt tathā hi ekam karaṇam ekasmin kāle anekām kriyām na karoti iti tasmāt yugapad prakāśanam eva ghaṭa ādīnām na grahaṇāni iti ukta pūrvam 
[II,039,4]	yat ca idam eka ādi vyavahāraḥ guṇa antarāt svabhāvāt vā iti uktam tatra ekatva sāmānya vaśāt iti brūmaḥ tathā hi dravye guṇa sambandhāt eka ādi vyavahāraḥ guṇe ca sāmānya sambandhāt sāmānye api guṇa sambandhāt na ca grahaṇa paramparā viśeṣaṇa jñānasya niyamena jñāna pūrva katva anabhyupagamāt atha saṃyukta samaveta samavāyāt eka tva sāmānye jñānam utpadyate viśeṣaṇa tvāt iti uktam aneka guṇa viṣayasya viśeṣya jñānasya eva asaṃvedanāt na dvi tvasya utpatti anyathā anupapattyā tad sadbhāva siddheḥ tathā hi yadi kāraṇa guṇa pūrva prakrameṇa rūpa ādi vat utpadyate dvi tvam prathama akṣa sannipāta velāyām eva grahaṇam syāt cira utpanna tvāt gaṇanā vaiyarthyañca na ca etat tasmāt aneka guṇa viṣayasya jñānasya ātma vartinaḥ api dvi tva utpattau kāraṇa tvam niścīyate tad vināśāt ca vināśaḥ anyathā hi samavāyi asamavāyi kāraṇayoḥ vināśāt vināśa abhyupagame tayoḥ aneka kālam avasthānāt sthāyi tvam eva syāt kvacid nitya tvañca tayoḥ avināśāt anyasya ca virodhi guṇasya asambhavāt tasmāt nimitta kāraṇāt eva vināśaḥ kalpyate 
[II,039,17]	na ca evam ghaṭa ādeḥ nimitta kāraṇa vināśāt vināśa prasaṅgaḥ adarśanāt atra tu samavāyi asamavāyi kāraṇayoḥ avasthāne api dvi tva ādeḥ vināśasya dṛṣṭa tvāt apekṣā buddhi vināśāt vināśaḥ kalpyate anyathā hi rūpa ādi vat avasthāne prathama akṣa sannipāta kāle eva grahaṇam syāt iti uktam atha avasthitasya api dvi tva ādeḥ vyañjaka abhāvāt anupalambhaḥ upalambhaḥ tu idānīm utpannasya api ghaṭataḥ iti apekṣā buddhi ādeḥ janaka tvam eva nyāyyam tasmāt dvi tva ādi vyavahāra uttara kālam tad abhāvasya saṃvedanāt tad utpattau kāraṇa antarasya asambhave sati apekṣā buddhi vināśasya kāraṇa tvam uktam 
[II,039,25_II,040,6]	atha pūrvam dvi tva sāmānya jñānam anantaram guṇa jñānam dravya jñānañca iti kalpanāyām kim pramāṇam viśeṣaṇa tvam iti ced na viśeṣaṇe api viśeṣaṇa antara kalpanāyām anavasthā prasaṅgāt tathā hi dve dravye iti dravya jñāna utpattau guṇasya viśeṣaṇa tvāt yuktam ādau tat jñānam guṇasya ca viśeṣaṇa tvāt na tad sāmānya jñānam yuktam abhyupagame vā tasya api anyat viśeṣaṇam iti anavasthā syāt na niyama anabhyupagamāt tathā hi viśeṣaṇe avaśyam viśeṣaṇa antara kalpanā iti niyamaḥ pratiṣidhyate anavasthā bhayāt na punar viśeṣaṇe viśeṣaṇam eva na asti iti vivakṣi tañca etat bhāṣya kartuḥ dravya viśeṣaṇasya api guṇasya sāmānya viśeṣaṇa abhidhānāt iti atha saṃskārāt dravya buddheḥ vināśaḥ iti atra kim pramāṇam kāryasya ākasmikasya anupalabdheḥ dravya jñāna vināśasya pratyakṣeṇa saṃvedanāt saṃskārasya kāraṇa tvam niścīyate tasya ca smṛtyā sadbhāva siddhiḥ iti vakṣyāmaḥ 
[II,040,10_II,040,16]	tat evam dvi tvasya utpatti vināśa kāraṇe prajñāpite sati etena tri tva ādi utpattiḥ vyākhyātāḥ iti atideśam karoti yathā hi dvi tvam eka tvābhyām aneka buddhi viṣaya sahitābhyām ārabhyate tathā tri tva ādeḥ api eka tvebhyaḥ aneka buddhi viṣaya sahitebhyaḥ niṣpattiḥ iti utpanne ca tritva ādau tad sāmānya jñānam tatas apekṣā buddheḥ vinaśyattā sāmānya tad jñāna tad sambandhebhyaḥ guṇa buddheḥ utpadyamāna tā iti ekaḥ kālaḥ 
[II,040,18_II,040,24]	tatas tri tva ādi guṇa buddheḥ utpādaḥ guṇa tad jñāna tad sambandhebhyaḥ dravya buddheḥ utpadyamāna tā apekṣā buddheḥ vināśaḥ sāmānya jñānasya vinaśyattā guṇasya vinaśyatta iti eṣām ekaḥ kālaḥ tatas dravya jñānasya utpādaḥ saṃskārasya utpadyamāna tā guṇa jñānasya vinaśyattā sāmānya jñānasya vināśaḥ apekṣā buddhi vināśāt ca guṇasya api nāśaḥ iti ekaḥ kālaḥ tatas saṃskārāt dravya jñānasya api iti atideśa arthaḥ 
[II,040,25]	ādipadena tu śata saṃkhyā ādeḥ avarodhaḥ tatra ca dvi tva utpatti atideśaḥ na sambhavati eva tathā hi dravya śatasya yugapad indriyeṇa sambandha abhāvāt tad gata eka guṇānām agrahaṇe apekṣā kāraṇa abhāvāt katham śata saṃkhyā utpattiḥ iti na ca indriyeṇa ekatva sāmānyasya ekasmin dravye saṃyukta samaveta samavāya lakṣaṇasya sambandhasya utpatteḥ tasya ekatāyāḥ dravya antara guṇeṣu api sadbhāvāt tad ākṛṣṭānām ekaika guṇānām yugapad grahaṇāt śata saṃkhyā utpattiḥ iti vācyam sarvatra tathā abhāvena śata saṃkhyā ādi utpatti prasaṅgāt tathā hi indriyasya eka tva sāmānyena saṃyukta samaveta samavāya lakṣaṇasya sambandhasya aviśeṣāt tad upagrahāt ekaika guṇānām grahaṇa abhyupagame sarvasmin dravye śata saṃkhyā ādi utpattiḥ syāt na ca etat tasmāt apekṣā kāraṇa abhāvāt anutpattiḥ iti na ca apekṣā buddhim vinā eva utpattiḥ gaṇanā vaiyarthya prasaṅgāt iti ukta nyāyāt 
[II,041,9_II,041,12]	tat etat sarvam asat saṃkhyā vyavahārasya vāstava tvāt śata saṃkhyā ādi sadbhāva siddhau tasyāḥ kṛtaka tvāt avaśyam utpatti kāraṇam vācyam iti anyasya asambhavāt vilakṣaṇā eva apekṣā buddhiḥ kalpyate iti tathā ca ekasmin ekaguṇe jñāna utpattau satyām saṃskārasya utpāde dvitīya eka guṇa jñānasya utpadyamāna tā pūrva jñānasya vinaśyatta iti ekaḥ kālaḥ 
[II,041,14_II,041,17]	tatas dvitīya eka guṇa jñānasya utpādaḥ pūrva guṇa smaraṇasya utpadyamāna tā prāktana saṃskāra sahakāriṇā ca jñānena saṃskārasya utpadyamāna tā prāktana jñānasya vināśaḥ iti ekaḥ kālaḥ tatas smaraṇasya utpādaḥ saṃskārasya utpādaḥ dvitīya guṇa jñānasya vinaśyattā smaraṇa anubhavau ca apekṣā buddhiḥ tatas dvi tvasya utpadyamāna tā iti ekaḥ kālaḥ 
[II,041,19_II,041,23]	tatas dvi tvasya utpādāt tad jñānasya utpadyamāna tā dvitīya eka guṇa jñānasya api vināśaḥ iti ekaḥ kālaḥ tatas dvi tva guṇa jñānasya utpādaḥ dravya jñānasya utpadyamāna tā smaraṇasya vinaśyatta iti ekaḥ kālaḥ tatas dravya jñānasya utpādaḥ guṇa jñānasya vinaśyattā smaraṇasya vināśaḥ tad vināśāt dvi tvasya vinaśyattā tṛtīya eka guṇa jñānasya utpadyamāna tā iti ekaḥ kālaḥ 
[II,041,25_II,042,3]	tatas tṛtīya eka guṇa jñānasya utpādaḥ dravya jñānasya vinaśyattā dvi tva guṇa jñānasya vināśaḥ pūrva eka guṇa dvitaye smaraṇasya utpadyamāna tā pūrva saṃskāra sacivena eka guṇa jñānena saṃskāra antarasya utpadyamāna tā dvi tva guṇasya vināśaḥ iti ekaḥ kālaḥ tatas smaraṇasya utpādaḥ saṃskārasya utpādaḥ eka guṇa jñānasya vinaśyattā smaraṇa anubhavau ca apekṣā buddhiḥ tatas tri tva guṇasya utpadyamāna tā dravya jñānasya vināśaḥ iti ekaḥ kālaḥ 
[II,042,6_II,042,10]	tatas tri tva guṇasya utpādaḥ tat jñānasya utpadyamāna tā eka guṇa jñānasya vināśaḥ iti ekaḥ kālaḥ tatas tri tva guṇa jñānasya utpādaḥ dravya jñānasya utpadyamāna tā smaraṇasya vinaśyatta iti ekaḥ kālaḥ tatas dravya jñānasya utpādaḥ guṇa jñānasya vinaśyattā smaraṇasya vināśaḥ tad vināśāt tritva guṇasya vinaśyattā caturtha eka guṇa jñānasya utpadyamāna tā iti ekaḥ kālaḥ 
[II,042,13_II,042,17]	tatas caturtha eka guṇa jñānasya utpādaḥ dravya jñānasya vinaśyattā guṇa jñānasya vināśaḥ tri tva guṇa vināśaḥ saṃskārasya utpadyamāna tā iti ayam kramaḥ catuṣṭu ādiṣu api ūhyaḥ tāvat yāvat anti adravya eka guṇe jñānam kalpanayā tad saṃskāreṇa ca smaraṇasya utpadyamāna tā iti tatas prāktana aśeṣa eka guṇa viṣaya smaraṇasya utpādaḥ antya dravya eka guṇa jñānasya vinaśyattā smaraṇa anubhavau ca apekṣā buddhiḥ tatas śata saṃkhyāyāḥ utpadyam ānatā iti ekaḥ kālaḥ 
[II,042,20_II,042,24]	tatas śata saṃkhyāyāḥ utpattiḥ tat jñānasya utpadyamāna tā antya dravyasya eka guṇa jñānasya vināśaḥ iti ekaḥ kālaḥ tatas guṇa jñānasya utpādaḥ dravya jñānasya utpadyamāna tā smaraṇasya vinaśyatta iti ekaḥ kālaḥ tad anantaram etāni śatam iti dravya jñānasya utpādaḥ guṇa jñānasya vinaśyattā saṃskārasya utpadyamāna tā smaraṇasya vināśaḥ tad anantaram saṃskārāt dravya jñānasya api iti 
[II,043,1]	anye tu ekasmin ekaguṇe jñānam tena kriyate saṃskāraḥ punar dvitīya eka guṇe jñānam tena prāktanena ca anyaḥ saṃskāraḥ iti eṣā kalpanā tāvat yāvat antya guṇe jñānam tatas kalpanayā tad saṃskārasya abhivyakta tvāt aśeṣa eka guṇa viṣayasya smaraṇasya utpattiḥ anubhavasya vinaśyattā iti apekṣā buddhiḥ śata saṃkhyā janikā iti manyante na ca antarāle dvi tva ādi anubhavasya api saṃvedanāt anubhavena bādhā iti vācyam kāraṇa aṃśasya eva kīrtanāt tathā hi eka guṇa anubhava janitaḥ saṃskāraḥ smṛti dvāreṇa śata saṃkhya utpattau kāraṇam na ca evam dvi tva ādi anubhavaḥ iti tasya anupanyāsaḥ na asattvāt iti 
[II,043,9]	atha astu evam utpattiḥ śata saṃkhyāyāḥ grahaṇantu katham iti cintyate tathā hi dravya śatasya yugapad indriyeṇa sambandha abhāvāt tad vartinī śata saṃkhyā api apratyakṣā iti katham etāni śatam iti pratyayaḥ syāt atha antya dravyeṇa indriyasya saṃyogāt tad samavetā ca śata saṃkhyā utpannā iti saṃyukta samavāyāt upalabhyate eva tad ākṛṣṭāni ca pūrva upalabdha dravyāṇi indriya saṃyoga abhāve api viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya lakṣaṇena eva sambandhena etāni śatam iti aparokṣa jñāna viṣayāṇi bhavanti iti 
[II,043,15_II,043,20]	tarhi sattā viśeṣeṇa ākṛṣṭānām ākāśa ādīnām api pratyakṣatā syāt na abhiprāya aparijñānāt tathā hi etāni śatam iti aparokṣa jñānasya dṛṣṭa tvāt atra kāraṇa cintā kriyate tatra ca anya sambandhasya anupalabdheḥ śata saṃkhyā kṛṣṭāni viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāveṇa eva pratyakṣāṇi na ca evam ākāśa ādīni upalabdha pūrvāṇi na ca teṣu aparokṣam vijñānam asti iti na evam kalpyate na ca ādya dravyasya indriyeṇa saṃyogāt śata saṃkhyā upalabhyate antya dravye samutpādāt tathā hi gaṇanā dvāreṇa antya dravyasya eka guṇa upalambhāt upalabdha eka guṇeṣu dravyeṣu samavetā śata saṃkhyā utpadyate tena pūrveṣu eva iti tad saṃyoge api asambhavāt agrahaṇam 
[II,043,24]	na ca atra anubhava sahakāriṇaḥ saṃskārasya saṃskāra antara ārambhaka tve ghaṭa ādi anubhava janita saṃskārasya api anubhava antara sahakāriṇaḥ saṃskāra ārambhaka tva prasaṅgaḥ adṛṣṭa kārita tvāt vastu vyavasthāyāḥ tathā hi śata saṃkhyā ādi upabhoga prāpaka adṛṣṭa niyamāt atra eva viśiṣṭa saṃskāra utpattiḥ na ghaṭa ādau tatra hi kārya abhāvāt iti kārya sadbhāvena ca kāraṇa parikalpanā kriyate iti yatra anyathā asambhavaḥ tatra eva niyāmaka tvam adṛṣṭasya na punar dṛṣṭa kāraṇa pratyākhyānam iti tasmāt adṛṣṭa sadbhāve api gaṇanā upalambhāt apekṣā buddheḥ kāraṇa tvam kalpyate anyathā hi īśvara buddheḥ adṛṣṭasya eka guṇa sahakāri tvena śata saṃkhyā ādi ārambhaka tve sarva dravyeṣu śata saṃkhyā ādi utpattau rūpa ādi vat cira utpanna tvāt gaṇanām antareṇa eva upalambhaḥ syāt na ca asti 
[II,044,7_II,044,18]	atha abhivyañjaka abhāvāt anupalambhaḥ iti ced na tat sadbhāve pramāṇa abhāvāt iti ukta uttara tvāt na ca anyadīya buddhi sampāditāni anyasya pratyakṣa upalabdhāni iti īśvara sampāditāsu asmad ādīnām pratyakṣatā na syāt tasmāt ukta nyāyena utpattiḥ grahaṇañca iti alam ati vistareṇa vināśam āha na parama pekṣā buddhi vināśāt kvacid āśraya vināśāt iti katham iti avyutpanna praśnaḥ tatra dvi tvasya āśraya vināśena vināśa abhidhānāt tad samāna tayā anyatra api parijñānam bhaviṣyati iti manyamānaḥ dvi tvasya eva vināśam āha yadā ekatva ādhāra avayave karma utpadyate vibhāgasya utpadyamāna tā tadā eva eka tva sāmānye jñānam utpadyate apekṣā buddheḥ utpadyamāna tā tatas vibhāgasya utpādaḥ dravya ārambhaka saṃyogasya vinaśyattā apekṣā buddheḥ utpādaḥ dvi tvasya utpadyamāna tā ekatva sāmānya jñānasya vinaśyattā tad anantaram saṃyogasya vināśaḥ ekatva sāmānya jñānasya vinaśyattā dravyasya vinaśyattā dvi tvasya utpādaḥ tad sāmānya jñānasya utpadyam āna tā iti eṣām ekaḥ kālaḥ 
[II,045,1_II,045,11]	tatas sāmānya jñānasya utpādaḥ apekṣā buddheḥ vinaśyattā dravyasya vināśaḥ guṇasya vinaśyattā tatas dravya vināśāt guṇasya vināśaḥ sāmānya jñānāt ca apekṣā buddheḥ iti na ca apekṣā buddhi vināśa kāryaḥ guṇa vināśaḥ sama kāla tvāt iti dravya vināśasya eva kāraṇa tvam pūrva kāla tvāt yadā tu apekṣā buddhi sama kālam ekatva ādhāra avayave karma cintyate tadā ubhaya vināśāt api guṇasya vināśaḥ sambhavati iti jñeyam śobhanam etat vidhānam ityādinā para pakṣa pratiṣedha dvāreṇa sva pakṣam upasaṃharati śobhanam yuktam etat dvi tva ādi utpatti vidhānam kasmin pakṣe iti āha vadhya ghātaka pakṣe yadā hi ekasya jñānasya utpādaḥ anyasya vinaśyattā 
[II,045,14]	saha anavasthāna lakṣaṇe tu virodhe dravya jñāna anutpatti prasaṅgaḥ iti aśobhanam tathā hi saha anavasthāna lakṣaṇe virodhe dvi tva sāmānya jñāna sama kālam apekṣā buddhi vināśāt guṇa buddhi sama kālam dvi tva vināśe tad apekṣasya dve dravye iti jñānasya anutpatti prasaṅgaḥ tathā nirhetuka tā ca vināśasya yadā eva dvi tva sāmānya jñānasya utpādaḥ tadā eva apekṣā buddheḥ vināśaḥ iti eka kāla tvāt na sāmānya jñāna kāryaḥ apekṣā buddhi vināśaḥ na ca anyat kāraṇam asti iti nirhetuka tvam prasajyeta na ca etat sambhavati iti uktam eva 
[II,045,21_II,045,24]	atha yadi api guṇa buddhi sama kālam apekṣā buddhi vināśāt guṇasya vināśaḥ tathā api laiṅgika jñāna vat jñāna mātrāt dve dravye iti jñānam bhaviṣyati iti paramatamāśaṅkate laiṅgika vat jñāna mātrāt iti ced matam abhipretam syāt yathā abhūtam avidyamānam liṅgam bhūtasya vidyamānasya liṅginaḥ gamakam iti atra sūtre liṅga abhāve api jñāna mātrāt anumānam iṣṭam 
[II,046,3]	tathā hi jñānena jñānam anumīyate iti jñānasya liṅga tvāt avaśyam grahaṇam tatas tasya vinaśyattā avinā abhau a sambandha smaraṇasya utpadyamāna tā tad anantaram avinā abhāva sambandha smaraṇasya utpādaḥ liṅga bhūtasya jñānasya vināśaḥ tat jñānasya vinaśyattā parāmarśa jñānasya utpadyamāna tā tatas parāmarśa jñānasya utpādaḥ avinā abhau a sambandha smaraṇasya vinaśyattā liṅga jñānasya api vināśaḥ iti nirviṣayāt parāmarśa jñāna mātrāt eva jñātari pratipattiḥ bhavati iti dṛṣṭam tathā guṇa vināśe guṇa jñāna mātrāt dravya pratyayaḥ syāt iti 
[II,046,10_II,046,17]	anye tu yathā abhūtam avidyamānam varṣa karma bhūtasya vidyamānasya vāyu abhra saṃyogasya liṅgam tathā guṇa vināśe api tad jñāna mātrāt dravya jñānam iti manyante na ca etat yuktam tathā hi na avidyamānam varṣa karma vidyamānasya vāyu abhra saṃyogasya sadbhāve liṅgam kim tarhi varṣa karmā anutpādaḥ vyabhicārī sa ca svarūpeṇa asti eva iti katham avidyamānam atha bhāva rūpa tayā tasya asattvam tarhi bhāvasya api abhāva rūpeṇa asattvam iti sarvasya asattvam eva syāt tasmāt varṣa karma anutpādaḥ vidyamānaḥ eva liṅgam iti udāharaṇa antaram eva nyāyyam 
[II,046,20]	pratisamādhānam āha yat uktam laiṅgika jñāna vat dve dravye iti jñānam bhaviṣyati iti etat na viśeṣya jñāna tvāt tathā hi dvi tva anurāgeṇa utpadyamāna tvāt dve dravye iti viśeṣya jñānam atas vidyamānasya eva guṇasya atra vyāpāraḥ kalpanīyaḥ tathā hi yasmāt na viśeṣya jñānam viśeṣaṇa sambandham antareṇa viśeṣaṇa sambandham vinā bhavitum arhati iti tad utpattau viśeṣaṇa tad jñāna tad sambandhānām kāraṇa tvam anyathā hi sakala kāraṇānām viśeṣya jñāna utpattau vyāpāra aviśeṣeṇa niyatasya eva viśeṣaṇa tvam na syāt atas viśeṣaṇa tad jñāna tad sambandhānām kāraṇa tvam 
[II,047,1]	tathā ca āha sūtrakāraḥ samavāyinaḥ śvaityāt śvaitya buddheḥ śvete buddhiḥ te kārya kāraṇa bhūte iti anena sūtrakārasya api ayam arthaḥ abhipretaḥ iti darśayati tathā hi śvetam dravyam tasya bhāvaḥ śvaityam śveta guṇaḥ tasmāt kim viśiṣṭāt samavāyinaḥ samavāyena sambandhāt śvaitya buddheḥ iti śveta guṇa buddheḥ etasmāt kāraṇa trayāt śveta buddhiḥ viśeṣya jñānam śvetam dravyam utpadyate te punar viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya buddhī kārya kāraṇa bhūte kārya kāraṇa svabhāve iti 
[II,047,7_II,047,8]	na ca laiṅgikam jñānam liṅga anuraktam iti liṅga abhāve api utpadyate iti āha na tu laiṅgikam jñānam abhedena liṅga anurāgeṇa utpadyate tasmāt viṣamaḥ ayam upanyāsaḥ iti yaḥ ayam laiṅgika jñāna vat dve dravye iti bhaviṣyati iti upanyāsaḥ sa viṣamaḥ samaḥ na bhavati iti tathā hi viśeṣya jñāne viśeṣaṇa anurāgaḥ iti laiṅgike tu anurāga abhāvaḥ iti vaiṣamyam 
[II,047,13_II,047,18]	yat vā viṣamaḥ ayam upanyāsaḥ upanyasyate sādhya sādhanayoḥ asmin vyāptiḥ iti upanyāsaḥ laiṅgika vat iti dṛṣṭāntaḥ sa ca viṣamaḥ liṅga anurāga śūnya tayā tasya aviśeṣya jñāna tvāt iti anye tu te viśeṣaṇa tad jñāne kāryasya viśeṣya jñānasya kāraṇa bhūte tasmāt guṇam vinā na dravya jñānam iti manyante te ca viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya buddhī kārya kāraṇa bhūte na punar sarvam vijñānam tathābhūtam pramāṇa abhāvāt 
[II,047,20_II,047,24]	etena saṅkalanā jñānam nirastam viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya jñāna vyatirekeṇa jñāna antare pramāṇa abhāvāt iti alam nanu dvi tva utpatteḥ prāk jñāna dvayam ekatva sāmānya jñānam apekṣā jñānañca utpanne tu dvi tve tad sāmānya jñānam guṇa jñānam dravya jñānañca iti jñāna pañcakam yadi krameṇa utpadyate sa kasmāt na upalabhyate anupalambhāt na asti iti paraḥ tad niṣedha artham āha na āśu utpatteḥ iti yat uktam kramasya asattvam iti etat na āśu bhāvi tvena vidyamānasya api kramasya asaṃvedanāt 
[II,048,3_II,048,7]	atha āśu utpatteḥ kramasya agrahaṇam kasmin upalabdham iti āha yathā śabdavat ākāśam iti iti atra śabda jñānam ākāśa jñānam śabda ākāśa sambandha jñānañca iti trīṇi jñānāni āśu utpadyante iti kramasya agrahaṇam tathā dvi tva ādi jñāna utpattau āśu bhāvi tvena eva krama agrahaṇam iti adoṣaḥ na ca jñānānām saha anavasthāna lakṣaṇaḥ eva virodhe jñānānām āśu bhau i tvena utpatteḥ avinaṣṭe hi guṇe dravya jñānam bhaviṣyati iti pratisamādhānam etat iti vācyam śīghram kāraṇa sadbhāvena kāryasya api tathā abhāvāt avaśyam guṇa buddhi sama kālam guṇa vināśe tadāyattasya dravya jñānasya anutpattiḥ iti dūṣaṇasya api āvṛtteḥ yadi jñānayoḥ saha avirodhena avasthānam na asti iti saha anavasthānam vivakṣitam avivādaḥ eva 
[II,048,13_II,048,18]	atha idānīm saha anavasthāna lakṣaṇa virodhāt vadhya ghātaka pakṣe api samānam dūṣaṇam iti paramatamā śaṅkamānaḥ idam āha vadhya ghātaka pakṣe api samānaḥ doṣaḥ iti ced syāt matam abhipretam iti saṅgraha vākyam asya tu vivaraṇam vadhyadhātaka pakṣe api tarhi dravya jñāna anutpatti prasaṅgaḥ iti tathā hi yadi guṇa buddhi sama kālam guṇa vināśe dravya jñāna anutpattiḥ tarhi vadhya ghātaka pakṣe api tasya anutpattiḥ eva katham sāmānya buddhi sama kālam saṃskārāt apekṣā buddhi vināśāt iti 
[II,048,24]	yathā hi apekṣā buddhiḥ dvi tvam janayati evam saṃskāram api iti tatas tasyāḥ vinaśyattā dvi tva sāmānya jñānasya utpadyamāna tā tatas dvi tva sāmānya jñānasya utpādaḥ guṇa jñānasya utpadyamāna tā apekṣā buddheḥ vināśaḥ guṇasya vinaśyattā tatas guṇa jñānasya utpādaḥ apekṣā buddhi vināśāt guṇasya vināśaḥ iti tad apekṣa tvāt dravya jñānasya anutpattiḥ eva na samūha jñānasya saṃskāra hetu tvāt iti pratisamādhānam tathā hi yat uktam apekṣā buddheḥ saṃskārāt vināśaḥ iti tat na samūha jñānasya paṭu abhyāsa ādara pratyayasya saṃskāra hetu tvāt iti 
[II,049,5]	saṅgraha ukteḥ vivaraṇam āha samūha jñānam eva saṃskāra kāraṇam na ālocana jñānam apekṣā jñānam iti tasmāt adoṣaḥ kim atra pramāṇam iti ced smaraṇa anutpattiḥ dravya jñāna utpattiḥ ca tathā hi yatra smaraṇam tatra eva saṃskāra kalpanā kriyate na ca atra tat asti iti abhyupagame dravya jñānam eva na syāt tat dṛṣṭam atas tat anyathā anupapattyā apekṣā buddheḥ saṃskāra ajanaka tvam niścīyate prakāra antara abhāvāt 
[II,049,11_II,049,16]	atha idānīm vadhya ghātaka pakṣe api parāśayam āśaṅkate jñāna yaugapadya prasaṅgaḥ iti ced syāt matam iti saṅgraha ukteḥ vivaraṇam nanu jñānānām vadhya ghātaka vi rodhe jñāna yaugapadya prasaṅgaḥ iti tathā ca yadi jñānānām vadhya ghātaka lakṣaṇaḥ virodhaḥ tadā ekasya avasthāne dvitīyasya utpādāt jñāna yaugapadyam prasajyate iti aniṣṭa āpādanam 
[II,049,21]	tat na aniṣṭam avinaśyatoḥ avasthāna pratiṣedhāt tathā hi jñāna ayaugapadya vacanena prayatna ayaugapadyāt ca pratiśarīram ekam manaḥ iti sūtreṇa yugapad utpattiḥ avinaśyatoḥ ca jñānayoḥ paraspara avirodhena avasthānam pratiṣidhyate vadhya ghātaka vi rodhe tu ubhayam api na asti iti āha na hi vadhya ghātaka vi rodhe jñānayoḥ yugapad utpattiḥ avinaśyatoḥ ca yugapad ava sthānam asti iti adūṣaṇam etat 
[II,050,2_II,050,7]	idānīm uddeśa krameṇa avasara prāptasya parimāṇasya lakṣaṇa parīkṣā artham parimāṇam māna vyavahāra kāraṇam ityādi prakaraṇam vyavahṛtiḥ vyavahāraḥ jñānam vyavahriyate anena iti vyavahāraḥ abhidhānam tayoḥ hetuḥ parimāṇam iti ukte atiprasaṅgaḥ tad artham māna padam tathā api māna vyavahāra hetu tvam ākāśa ātmanoḥ vidyate iti viśeṣaṇa tve sati iti viśeṣaṇam tathā api parimāṇa tva sāmānyena vyabhicāra parihāra artham dravya viśeṣaṇa tve sati iti viśeṣaṇam abhyūhyam tathā hi parimāṇam itarasmāt bhidyate dravya viśeṣaṇa tve sati māna vyavahāra kāraṇa tvāt yaḥ tu itarasmāt aparimāṇān na bhidyate na ca asau evam yathā rūpa ādiḥ iti vyavahāraḥ vā sādhyaḥ 
[II,050,16]	tathā āvartyamānam idam eva vākyam aneka artham iti parīkṣā paratvena sambadhyate tathā hi māna vyavahāraḥ viśeṣya jñāna tvāt viśeṣaṇam apekṣate daṇḍyādi jñāna vat na ca rūpa ādīnām anyatamaḥ tad viśeṣaṇam tad vyavahāra vilakṣaṇa tvāt iti vilakṣaṇena eva nimittena bhavitavyam na ca idam kalpanā jñānam vāsanā prabhavam tasyāḥ pūrvam eva pratiṣedhāt 
[II,050,21_II,050,23]	tat caturvidham iti vibhāgaḥ kena rūpeṇa iti āha aṇu mahat dīrgham hrasvañcā iti nanu ca ayuktam cāturvidhyam catur asra ādi bhedasya api sambhavāt tat na mahatvasya eva avayava racanā viśeṣa upalambha sahakāriṇaḥ caturasra ādi vyavahāra sampādaka tvāt tathā hi avayava racanā viśeṣa upalambhe sati catur asram tri asram parimaṇḍalam iti vyavahāraḥ tad abhāve ca na iti na parimāṇa antara siddhiḥ 
[II,051,1]	nanu evam dīrgha tva hrasva tva vyavahāraḥ api avayava saṃyoga viśeṣa upalambhāt eva bhaviṣyati iti alam dīrgha tva hrasva tva parikalpanayā na tad anupalabdhau api dīrgha tva upalabdheḥ tathā hi manda manda prakāśe sati antareṇa api avayava racana upalambham sthāṇu ādau dīrgha pratibhāsaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ na ca evam caturasra pratibhāsaḥ iti anvaya vyatirekābhyām iti ūhyam 
[II,051,6]	tatra mahattva aṇu tvayoḥ api avāntara bhedāt ṣaḍvidham api parimāṇam iti āha mahat dvividham nityam anityañcaḥ iti nityam ākāśa kāla diś ātmasu vartate tat ca parama mahat tvam na tasmāt ūrdhvam mahat tvam asti iti anityam tri aṇuka ādau eva iti tri aṇukam ādau yasya tat tathā uktam tat tasmin eva tatra hi utpatti kāraṇa sadbhāvāt 
[II,051,11]	tathā na param mahat aṇu api dvividham nityam anityañca keṣu iti āha paramāṇu manaḥsu paramāṇavaḥ ca manaḥ ca iti paramāṇu manāṃsi teṣu vartate pārimāṇḍalyam iti tasya nāma tathā hi parimaṇḍalāni paramāṇu manāṃsi teṣām bhāvaḥ pārimāṇḍalyam tat parimāṇam eva tat tu nityam utpatti vināśa kāraṇa anupalabdheḥ tathā hi paramāṇūnām kāraṇā sambhavāt na tad parimāṇa kāraṇam aneka tva saṃkhyā pracayaḥ vā asti iti etāvat tu kāraṇam parimāṇasya na ca nitya tvāt aṇūnām vināśaḥ sambhavati iti tad parimāṇasya nitya tvam eva anityam dvi aṇukaḥ eva iti āśraya antara vyudāsaḥ 
[II,051,19_II,051,23]	nanu ca ayuktam etat anyatra api aṇu vyavahāra upalabdheḥ na tatra mukhyā sambhavena upacāra abhyupagamāt iti āha kuvalayāmalaka bilva ādiṣu mahatsu api tad prakarṣa bhāva abhāvam apekṣya parimāṇa atiśayaḥ kuvalaya ādi apekṣayā tasmāt vā prakarṣaḥ tasya bhāvaḥ vidyamāna tā bilva ādau tad abhāvam apekṣya āmalake aṇu vyavahāraḥ tathā tad prakarṣaḥ kuvalaya apekṣayā parimāṇa atiśayaḥ tasya bhāvaḥ vidyamāna tā āmalake tad abhāvam apekṣya kuvalaye aṇu vyavahāraḥ yatra hi vāstavam aṇu tvam tatra parimāṇa atiśayasya abhāvaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ tasya anyatra api upalambhāt upacāraḥ pravartate eva
