[II,052,4_II,052,8]	yat vā mukhya asadbhāve kim pramāṇam iti āha bhāktaḥ aṇu vyavahāraḥ yathā hi māṇavake siṃha vyavahāraḥ mukhya apekṣaḥ tadvat ayam aṇu vyavahāraḥ api upacarita tvāt mukhya pūrvaḥ iti aṇu tva siddhiḥ tathā ca kuvalaya ādiṣu aṇu vyavahāraḥ mukhya pūrvakaḥ bhākta vyavahāra tvāt māṇavake siṃha vyavahāra vat yathā ca mahattva aṇu tvayoḥ nitya anitya bhedaḥ na evam dīrgha tva hrasva tvayoḥ āśraya antara anupapatteḥ kva vā tayoḥ vṛttiḥ iti āśaṅkāyām āha dīrgha tva hrasva tve ca dīrghatvañca hrasva tvañca iti dīrgha tva hrasva tve te tu utpādya mahat aṇutva eka artha samavete utpādye ca te mahat aṇu tve ca utpādya mahat aṇu tve tābhyām saha ekasmin arthe samavete tathā hi tri aṇuka ādau utpādyam mahat tvam tatra eva dīrgha tvam dvi aṇuke ca aṇu tvam tatra eva hrasva tvam iti paramāṇūnām parimaṇḍala tvāna hrasva tvam ākāśa ādeḥ vyāpaka tvāt ca na dīrgha tvam tad viparīteṣu tad vyavahāra darśanāt 
[II,052,15_II,052,24]	atha dvi aṇukeṣu eva katham hrasva tvam iti uktam anyatra api tad vyavahāra upalabdheḥ tat na bādhaka sadbhāvena anyatra upacāra abhyupagamāt iti āha samidh ikṣu vaṃśa ādiṣu añjasā dīrgheṣu api tad prakarṣa bhāva abhāvam apekṣya bhāktaḥ hrasva tva vyavahāraḥ iti tathā hi samidh ādiṣu dīrgha tva utpattau kāraṇa sadbhāvāt añjasā mukhyayā vṛttyā dīrgha tvam dīrdheṣu api hrasva tva vyavahāraḥ dṛṣṭaḥ iti mukhyā sambhavāt upacāraḥ kalpyate tatra ca tad prakarṣa bhāva abhāvaḥ nimittam tasya vaṃśa ādeḥ prakarṣaḥ samidh ādi apekṣayā dīrgha tva atiśayaḥ tasya bhāvaḥ vidyamāna tā vaṃśa ādau tad abhāvam apekṣya ikṣau hrasva tva vyavahāraḥ samidham apekṣya ikṣau dīrgha tva atiśayaḥ tatra tad abhāvam apekṣya samidhi hrasva vyavahāraḥ yat vā mukhya hrasva tvasya sadbhāve kim pramāṇam upacaritaḥ hrasva vyavahāraḥ tathā hi samidh ādiṣu hrasva vyavahāraḥ mukhya pūrvakaḥ bhākta vyavahāra tvāt māṇavake siṃha vyavahāra vat iti 
[II,053,2_II,053,9]	evam cāturvidhi am uktvā utpatti kāraṇam āha anityam caturvidham api saṃkhyā parimāṇa pracaya yoni iti saṃkhyā ca parimāṇañca pracayaḥ ca iti saṃkhyā parimāṇa pracayāḥ te yoniḥ kāraṇam asya iti saṃkhyā parimāṇa pracayaiḥ samasta vyastaiḥ janyate iti vākya arthaḥ tathā ca sūtram kāraṇa bahu tvāt kāraṇa mahat tvāt pracaya viśeṣāt ca mahat iti anitya grahaṇam nitya vyudāsa artham caturvidham iti nyūna tā vyavacchedaḥ 
[II,053,12]	sūtra artha prakramasya vivakṣi tvād uddeśa krama atikrameṇa mahat tva utpattau kāraṇam āha tatra īśvara buddhim apekṣya utpannā paramāṇu dvi aṇukeṣu bahu tva saṃkhyā taiḥ ārabdhe tri aṇuka ādi lakṣaṇe kārya dravye rūpa ādi utpatti sama kālam mahat tvam dīrghatvañca karoti tathā ca īśvara buddhiḥ nityā sakala artha viṣayā ca iti ekaika guṇa ālambana asti eva tām apekṣyaka eka guṇaiḥ paramāṇu dvi aṇukeṣu tri tvam ārabhyate paramāṇu dvi aṇukeṣu iti dvi aṇuka vyavaccheda artham paramāṇubhyām eva dvi aṇukam ārabhyate na dvi aṇukābhyām vyartha ārambha prasaṅgāt iti uktam atas paramāṇu dvi aṇuka ārabdhe kārya dravyaḥ iti taiḥ ārabdham rūpa ādi api bhavati iti tad niṣedha artham dravya grahaṇam dravya padañca dravya tve api vartate iti abhivyakti vivakṣayā tat api ārabdham iti kārya grahaṇam tri aṇuka ādi lakṣaṇaḥ iti tri aṇu kañca tad ādi lakṣaṇam kāraṇa kārya svarūpañca iti yat vā sarva mahat dravyāṇām ādau lakṣyate ityādi lakṣaṇam tasmin utpanne rūpa ādi utpatti sama kālam dvi aṇukeṣu vartamānam tritvam mahat tvam dīrghatvañca karoti iti 
[II,053,24]	tathā hi kārya vastunaḥ asamavāyi kāraṇa pūrvaka tvam dṛṣṭam iti tri aṇukasya samavāyi kāraṇa tvāt anyena asamavāyi kāraṇena bhavitavyam dvi aṇukeṣu ca mahat tvasya abhāvāt na kāraṇa guṇa pūrvaka tvam atha aṇu parimāṇāt eva tri aṇuke mahat tvam kāraṇa parimāṇāt kārya pariṇāmasya atiśaya upalabdheḥ tathā ca paṭa apekṣayā sūkṣmāḥ tantavaḥ tad apekṣayā tad aṃśavaḥ iti dṛṣṭam evam dvi aṇuka apekṣayā atiśaya parimāṇa sambandhi tri aṇukam bhaviṣyati iti 
[II,054,3]	tat asat yat śabda vācyam kāraṇa parimāṇam tat śabda vācyam kārye api iti tri aṇuke dvi aṇuka parimāṇam eva syāt yathā mahat śabda vācyāt tantu gaṇāt utpadyamānaḥ paṭaḥ tad śabda vācyaḥ iti evam aṇu parimāṇāt aṇu parimāṇam eva syāt para māṇu parimāṇāt ca dvi aṇuke api parimāṇam iti kalpanāyām aṇu tvasya asambhave katham tasmāt mahattvam iti na ca aṇu tvasya asambhave paramāṇuḥ iti yuktam tathā ca aṇoḥ atiśayena aṇuḥ paramāṇuḥ iti vyapadiśyate anyathā hi viśeṣaṇam anarthakam eva syāt vyavacchedya abhāvāt mahat tvan ca apekṣya aṇu vyavahāraḥ na ca paramāṇuḥ iti na ca mahat tvam aṇu parimāṇasya kāraṇa tva abhyupagame tasmāt aṇvabhāve paramāṇu vyavahāra uccheda prasaṅgāt na paramāṇu parimāṇam kāraṇam 
[II,054,13]	itas ca paramāṇu parimāṇasya aṇu tva utpattau aṇu tvasya mahat tva utpattau asamavāyi kāraṇa tvam ayuktam atyanta samāna jātīyasya asamavāyi kāraṇa tva upalabdheḥ tathā ca atyantam samāna jātīyam asamavāyi kāraṇam yathā śuklatamāt rūpāt śuklatamam eva rūpam atyanta vijātīyañca yathā saṃyogāt śabdaḥ iti na ca evamaṇu parimāṇam mahat tva utpattau paramāṇu parimāṇaḥ ca aṇu tva utpattau iti tasya api parimāṇa tvāt na atyantam vijātīya tvam parama aṇu tvañca aṇu tvasya eva viśeṣaḥ aṇu tvañca mahat tvāt jāti antaram eva iti na atyanta samāna jātīya tvam 
[II,054,20_II,055,1]	na ca atra pracayaḥ sambhavati rūpa ādīnām sva kārye sāmarthya avadhāraṇāt atas saṃkhyā eva asamavāyikāraṇam iti kalpyate pratyāsattiḥ mahatī tathā ca mahat tvam dīrghatvañca tri aṇuke vartate tri aṇukaḥ ca dvi aṇukeṣu tri tvam api teṣu eva iti kārya kāraṇa eka artha samavāya lakṣaṇā pratyāsattiḥ iti nanu evam īśvara buddheḥ nitya tvāt dvi aṇu kānāñca kāla antaram avasthānāt avasthāyi tvam eva saṃkhyāyāḥ nitya dravya samavetāyāḥ ca nitya tvam iti na eṣa doṣaḥ saṃkhyāyāḥ kārya tvāt avaśyam vināśi tvam iti nirhetuka vināśa pratiṣedhena asyāḥ vināśa hetoḥ abhāvāt sthiti hetu adṛṣṭa abhāvāt vināśaḥ kalpyate yat vā īśvara śabdaḥ yogi īśvare vartate iti tad buddheḥ anitya tvāt tad vināśaḥ ghaṭataḥ eva saṃkhyāyāḥ 
[II,055,3]	tathā hi dvi aṇuke kriyā utpannā yadā eva vibhāgam ārabhate saṃyogasya vinaśyattā tadā eva eka tva sāmānye jñānam utpadyate apekṣā buddheḥ utpadyamāna tā tatas saṃyogasya vināśaḥ uttara saṃyogasya utpadyamāna tā apekṣā buddheḥ utpādaḥ tritvasya utpadyamāna tā tatas dvi aṇukasya dvi aṇukābhyām saṃyogasya utpādaḥ tri aṇukasya utpadyamāna tā vibhāga karmaṇoḥ vinaśyattā tritvasya utpādaḥ tad sāmānya jñānasya utpadyamāna tā tatas tri aṇukasya utpādaḥ vibhāga karmaṇoḥ vināśaḥ tri tva sāmānya jñānasya utpādaḥ mahat tva dīrgha tvayoḥ utpadyamāna tā apekṣā buddheḥ vinaśyattā tritva guṇa buddheḥ utpadyamāna tā tatas mahattva dīrgha tvayoḥ utpādaḥ apekṣā buddheḥ vināśaḥ tritva guṇasya vinaśyattā tritva guṇa buddheḥ utpādaḥ dravya jñānasya utpadyamāna tā tatas dravya jñāna sama kālam tritvasya api vināśaḥ iti 
[II,055,13_II,055,15]	mahat tvāt mahat tvam utpadyate iti āha dvi bahubhiḥ mahadbhiḥ ca ārabdhe kārya dravye kāraṇa mahat tvāni eva mahat tvam ārabhante iti dve ca bahavaḥ ca taiḥ dvi bahubhiḥ kim viśiṣṭaiḥ mahadbhiḥ ārabdhe kārya dravye kāraṇa gatāni mahat tvāni eva mahat tvam ārabhante na bahu tvam katham samāna saṃkhyaiḥ kāraṇaiḥ ārabdhe kārye atiśaya darśanāt 
[II,055,20]	tathā hi sthūlaiḥ caturbhiḥ ārabdham kāryam ekam anyaiḥ ca sūkṣmaiḥ caturbhiḥ eva yat tu sthūlaiḥ ārabdham tat atiśayena mahat sampadyate iti mahattvasya eva kāraṇa tvam saṃkhyāyāḥ ca ubhayatra sādhāraṇa tvāt kāraṇa tve parimāṇasya aviśeṣaḥ syāt yatra ca dvayoḥ ārambhaka tvam tatra bahutva asambhavena mahattvasya eva kāraṇa tvam iti 
[II,055,24^1]	anye tu saṃkhyāyāḥ parimāṇa vat anvaya vyatirekābhyām anyatra sāmarthya avadhāraṇāt iha api kāraṇa tvam iti manyante yat ca idam samāna saṃkhyaiḥ ārabdhe api ekatra atiśaya darśanam na tat saṃkhyāyāḥ kāraṇa tva pratiṣedha param parimāṇasya api akāraṇa tva prasaṅgāt tathā hi yathā samāna saṃkhyaiḥ ārabdham apekṣya tatra parimāṇa atiśayaḥ tathā sthūlatamaiḥ samāna saṃkhyaiḥ ārabdham apekṣya tad parimāṇaiḥ asamāna saṃkhyaiḥ ārabdhe tad parimāṇasya anatiśaya upalabdheḥ parimāṇasya api akāraṇa tvam syāt tathā adhika parimāṇa apekṣayā anatiśaya sadbhāve api etat ced kāraṇam anvaya vyatirekābhyām sāmarthya avagateḥ iṣyate tad sadbhāve tasya bhāvaḥ tad abhāve ca abhāvaḥ iti etat saṃkhyāyām api samānam yadi ca atra mahat tva utpattau akāraṇam saṃkhyā 
[II,055,24^2]	tarhi sthūlaiḥ tribhiḥ ārabdham ekam anyat caturbhiḥ iti ubhayatra api kāraṇa parimāṇasya aviśeṣāt kārya parimāṇasya aviśeṣaḥ syāt na ca etat caturbhiḥ ābdhe parimāṇa atiśaya darśanāt atas saṃkhyā api kāraṇam iti tathā samāna saṃkhyaiḥ samāna parimāṇaiḥ ca ārabdhe mahat tvam ubhābhyām sampadyate iti yuktam anyatra ubhayoḥ sāmarthya avadhāraṇāt iha pratyāsanna tvāt ca iti tathā ca tri tantuka ādi parimāṇam tri tantuka ādau vartate tri tantuka ādau ca tantuṣu tad parimāṇañca tad saṃkhyā ca teṣu eva iti kārya kāraṇa eka artha samavāya lakṣaṇā pratyāsattiḥ iti katham tarhi idam vākyam kāraṇa mahat tvāni eva mahat tvam ārabhante na bahu tvam iti 
[II,055,24^3_II,056,23]	avadhāraṇa pratiṣedha artham tathā hi yat uktam samāna saṃkhyaiḥ ārabdhe atiśaya adarśanāt kāraṇa mahat tvāni eva mahat tvam ārabhante iti etat na bahu tvasya api ukta nyāyena kāraṇa tvāt yat vā samāna saṃkhyaiḥ ārabdhe atiśaya adarśanāt iti mahattvasya kāraṇa tva upadarśanam etat na avadhāraṇam iti pracayasya kāraṇa tvam āha pracayaḥ ca tūla piṇḍayoḥ vataṃmānaḥ piṇḍa ārambhaka avayava praśithila saṃyoga apekṣaḥ itaretara piṇḍa avayava saṃyoga apekṣaḥ vā dvi tūlake mahat tvam ārabhate iti 
[II,056,26]	tūla piṇḍaḥ ca tūla piṇḍaḥ ca tūla piṇḍau tayoḥ vartamānaḥ saṃyogaḥ pracayaḥ kiṃviśiṣṭaḥ piṇḍa ārambhaka praśithila saṃyoga apekṣaḥ iti piṇḍa ārambhakāḥ ca praśithila saṃyogāḥ ca tān apekṣate iti tad apekṣaḥ itaretara piṇḍa avayava saṃyoga apekṣaḥ ca iti vā samuccaye na tū vikalpe apekṣā kāraṇa tvena abhyupagatayoḥ ubhayoḥ api atra sadbhāvāt itarasya piṇḍasya itara piṇḍa avayavaiḥ saṃyogaḥ tathā itarasya itara avayavaiḥ iti itaretara piṇḍayoḥ vā ye avayavāḥ teṣām saṃyogāḥ tān apekṣate iti tad apekṣaḥ sa ca dvābhyām tūlakābhyām ārabdhe api tūlake mahat tvam ārabhate iti tritūlaka ādau api etat samānam pratyāsattiḥ tu mahatī dvi tūlaka parimāṇe dvi tūlake vartate dvi tūlake tu tūla piṇḍayoḥ saṃyogaḥ api tatra eva bahu tva mahat tvayoḥ sadbhāve api kāraṇa tva pratiṣedhaḥ iti āha na bahu tva mahat tvāni dvi tūlaka ādau mahat tvam ārabhante kutas samāna saṃkhyā pala parimāṇaiḥ ārabdhe atiśaya darśanāt 
[II,057,10_II,057,20]	tathā hi tribhiḥ tūla piṇḍaiḥ pañca palaiḥ praśithila avayava saṃyogaiḥ ārabdham ekam anyat ca tad viparītaiḥ tatra yat praśithila avayava saṃyogaiḥ ārabdham tatra parimāṇa atiśayaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ iti pracayasya eva kāraṇa tvam na saṃkhyā pala parimāṇānām tad kāraṇa tve ca ubhayatra aviśeṣaḥ syāt atha palasya sarvatra parimāṇa akāraṇa tvāt prasakti abhāve na yuktaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ tathā hi pāṣāṇa ādau pala atiśaya sadbhāve api parimāṇasya atiśaya abhāvaḥ tula piṇḍa ādau ca tad abhāve api atiśaya upalabdheḥ na palasya guru tva viśeṣa tvāt kāraṇa tvam kimarthaḥ tatra pratiṣedhaḥ vyāmoha pratiṣedha arthaḥ tathā ca pare vyāmohāt yadi evaṃvidhasya api palasya kāraṇa tvam pratipadyeran tat api na asti samāna palaiḥ ārabdhe atiśaya adarśanāt anye tu asya eva doṣasya parihāra artham pala śabdasya samāna śabda paryāya tām bruvate samāna saṃkhyā pala parimāṇaiḥ iti samāna saṃkhyaiḥ samāna parimāṇaiḥ iti arthaḥ 
[II,057,22]	nanu ca ayuktam avadhāraṇam pracayasya eva kāraṇa tvam iti bahu tva mahat tvayoḥ api anyatra sāmarthya avadhāraṇe sati iha pratyāsanna tvāt na ca samāna saṃkhyā pala parimāṇa ra ārabdhe api ekatra atiśaya darśanam bahu tva mahat tvayoḥ kāraṇa tva pratiṣedhe hetuḥ anya apekṣayā anatiśaya sadbhāve pracayasya api akāraṇa tva prasaṅgāt tathā hi samāna saṃkhyā pala parimāṇaiḥ praśithila avayava saṃyogaiḥ caturbhiḥ ārabdham ekam anyat ca tathāvidhaiḥ tribhiḥ iti caturbhiḥ ārabdhe atiśaya darśanāt saṃkhyā api kāraṇam tathā sthūlaiḥ caturbhiḥ praśithila avayava saṃyogaiḥ ārabdham ekam anyat ca sthūlatamaiḥ tathāvidhaiḥ eva iti atra kāraṇa parimāṇa atiśayena kārya parimāṇasya atiśaya upalabdheḥ parimāṇasya api kāraṇa tvam yatra tu samāna saṃkhyā parimāṇaiḥ praśithila avayava saṃyoga ārabdhaiḥ mahat tvam ārabhyate tatra aviśeṣeṇa tritayasya api kāraṇa tvam anyatra sāmarthya avadhāraṇe sati iha pratyāsanna tvāt vākyasya tu vyākhyānam pūrvavat 
[II,058,7_II,058,15]	aṇu tva utpattau kāraṇam āha dvi tva saṃkhyā ca aṇvoḥ vartamānā dvi aṇuke aṇu tvam ārabhate iti dvi aṇu kāṇu parimāṇam kāryam tasya hi samavāyi kāraṇam dvi aṇukam iti anyena asamavāyi kāraṇena bhavitavyam paramāṇu parimāṇasya ca ārambhaka tva pratiṣedhe anyasya ca asambhavāt dvi tva saṃkhyā eva aṇvoḥ vartamānā kārya kāraṇa eka artha samavāyena dvi aṇu kāṇu parimāṇa utpattau asamavāyi kāraṇam iti aṇu śabdaḥ ca sāmānya śabda tvāt paramāṇau api vartate eva aṇu tve sati paramaḥ iti viśeṣaṇāt vināśaḥ tu dvi tva saṃkhyāyāḥ pūrvavat vyākhyeyaḥ 
[II,058,18]	dīrgha tva utpattau kāraṇam āha mahattva vat tri aṇuka ādau kāraṇa bahu tva mahat tva samāna jātīya pracayebhyaḥ dīrgha tvasya utpattiḥ iti yathā hi mahat tvam kāraṇa bahu tva mahat tva samāna jātīya pracayebhyaḥ bhavati evam dīrgha tvam api iti tri aṇuke kāraṇa bahu tvāt eva dīrgha tvam dvi tantuke kāraṇa dīrgha tvāt eva iti tri tantuka ādau bahu tva dīrgha tva pracayaiḥ dīrgha tvam ārabhyate iti atideśa arthaḥ tathā aṇu tva vat dvi aṇuke dvi tva saṃkhyātaḥ hrasva tvasya utpattiḥ iti yathā kāraṇa antara asambhavāt dvi tva saṃkhyā aṇu tvasya utpattau asamavāyi kāraṇam evam hrasva tvasya api iti 
[II,058,25_II,059,5]	atha samāna jātīya kāraṇa janya tvāt tri aṇuka ādiṣu vartamānayoḥ mahat tva dīrgha tvayoḥ parasparataḥ kaḥ viśeṣaḥ dvi aṇukeṣu ca aṇu tva hrasva tvayoḥ iti yatas kāraṇa bhedāt bhidyante padārthāḥ mahat tva dīrgha tva ādau tad abhāvaḥ iti tat na pratibhāsa bhedena mahattva dīrgha tvayoḥ bheda sadbhāve sati tad janakayoḥ kāraṇa sāmagryoḥ bheda upatteḥ 
[II,059,10]	tathā hi kārya bhedena sāmagrī bhedaḥ jñāyate sa ca iha asti eva pratibhāsa bhedāt iti āha tatra asti mahat tva dīrgha tvayoḥ parasparataḥ viśeṣaḥ kutas mahatsu dīrgham ānīyatām dīrgheṣu ca mahat ānīyatām iti viśiṣṭa vyavahāra darśanāt anyathā hi mahat tva aviśeṣāt tatas dīrgha tvena atiśayyā nayanam dīrgheṣu ca mahattvena iti na syāt dṛṣṭañca etat tasmāt dīrgha tvam mahat tvāt bhedena pratipannam mahat tvan ca dīrgha tvāt iti pratibhāsa bhedāt rūpa ādīnām iva bhedaḥ 
[II,059,16_II,059,22]	samāna kāraṇa janya tvañca samavāyi asamavāyi nimitta apekṣayā pākajaiḥ vyabhicarati iti nābhede hetuḥ sāmagrī apekṣayā tu samāna kāraṇa tvam asiddham kārya bhedena tad bheda upapatteḥ aṇu tva hrasva tvayoḥ tu parasparataḥ viśeṣaḥ tad darśinām iti yoginām pratyakṣaḥ teṣām atīndriya artha darśi tvāt hrasva tva sadbhāvaḥ tu bhākta vyavahāreṇa pūrvam vyavasthāpitaḥ iti vidyamāna tvāt yoginām avaśyam itara padārtha vyāvṛtta tayā grahaṇam iti alam etat caturvidham api parimāṇam utpādyam āśraya vināśāt eva vinaśyati iti kāraṇa antara pratiṣedha artham avadhāraṇam utpādya grahaṇantu nitya parimāṇa vyavaccheda artham iti 
[II,059,26_II,060,3]	idānīm uddeśa krameṇa avasara prāptasya pṛthaktvasya lakṣaṇa parīkṣā artham pṛthaktvam apoddhāra vyavahāra kāraṇam iti ādi prakaraṇam vyavahṛtiḥ vyavahāraḥ jñānam vyavahriyate anena iti vyavahāraḥ abhidhānam tayoḥ hetuḥ pṛthaktvam iti ukte ati prasaṅgaḥ tad artham apoddhāra grahaṇam apa uddharaṇam apoddhāraḥ pṛthakkaraṇam tathā api apoddhāra vyavahāra hetu tvam ākāśa ātmanoḥ na vyāvṛttam iti viśeṣaṇa tve sati iti pada m ūhyam pṛthaktva tva sāmānya vyavaccheda arthañca dravya padam api iti pṛthaktvam itarebhyaḥ bhidyate dravya viśeṣaṇa tve sati apa uddhāra vyavahāra kāraṇa tvāt yaḥ tu itarebhyaḥ na bhidyate na ca asau evam yathā rūpa ādiḥ iti vyavahāraḥ vā sādhyaḥ 
[II,060,11_II,060,14]	tathā parīkṣā parañca vākyam apa uddhāra vyavahāraḥ hi viśiṣṭa vyavahāraḥ sa ca na ṛte viśeṣaṇāt bhavati iti rūpa ādi vyavahāra vilakṣaṇa tvāt vilakṣaṇena eva nimittena bhavitavyam tathā rūpa ādi anupalabdhau pṛthak iti vyavahāra darśanāt ca na ca idam asmāt pṛthak iti vyavahāraḥ viśeṣa sambandhāt bhaviṣyati iti vācyam anityeṣu nitya viśeṣāṇām abhāvāt atha anityeṣu asādhāraṇa dharma sambandhaḥ pṛthak iti vyavahāre nimittam tat na tad viśiṣṭa tā anupalabdheḥ na hi pṛthak iti vyavahāre dravya rūpa ādi karma sāmānya ātmikā asādhāraṇa dharma viśiṣṭa tā pratibhāti 
[II,060,18]	yat ca abhihitam tebhyaḥ artha antaram viśeṣaṇam na pṛthaktvam atha itaretarābhāvaḥ tarhi nimittam tathā hi idam idam na bhavati idam asmāt vyāvṛttam pṛthak artha antaram vilakṣaṇam iti pratyayāḥ sarvatra tad nimittāḥ eva iti na padārtha antara avadhim vinā eka tva ādi saṃkhyā viśiṣṭasya pṛthak iti vyavahārasya tatas artha antara tvāt tathā hi itaretara abhāva viśiṣṭaḥ vyavahāraḥ padārtha antarau adhi tvena pravartate na ca eka tva ādi saṃkhyā anuraktaḥ tad vilakṣaṇaḥ ca ayam iti artha antara nimittaḥ 
[II,060,25]	anye tu itaretarābhāvasya pratiṣedha artham nānā pratyaya janakam iti na anitya dravyeṣu nityasya guṇasya anupalabdheḥ āśraya vināśena tad vināśe sarvatra anupalabdhiḥ eva syāt anitya tā āyāntu aśeṣa dravya āśritasya utpatti kāraṇa abhāvaḥ teṣām krameṇa utpādāt na ca anyatra samavetam upajātam anyatra samavaitīti adarśanāt ekasya ca nityasya aneka vṛttau sāmānya rūpa tā syāt na ca dravyam dravyam iti pratyaya vat pṛthak pṛthak iti padārtha antara avadhim vinā pratyayaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ sau adhikaḥ tu pratyayaḥ guṇa ādiṣu api itaretarābhāva nimittaḥ na sāmānya nibandhanaḥ tad vilaṇaḥ ca ayam iti uktam 
[II,061,7]	atha pṛthaktva pratyayāḥ vibhinna svabhāvāḥ saṃkhyayā viśiṣyante iti atha pūrvam dvi tva ādeḥ utpādaḥ apekṣā buddhi vināśena vināśa upapatteḥ na dvi pṛthaktva ādi kāle avasthānam dvi pṛthaktva ādeḥ ca pūrvam utpāde dravya jñāna sama kālam vināśāt dvi tva utpatti sama kāle na avasthānam atas viśeṣya jñāna utpattau vyāpāra anupapatteḥ dvi tva ādeḥ na viśeṣaṇa tvam iti 
[II,061,12_II,061,20]	atha ekasmin eva kāle vibhinna puruṣayoḥ apekṣā buddhi dvāreṇa ubhayoḥ utpatti sambhavāt yuktam dvi tva ādeḥ viśeṣaṇa tvam iti ced na puruṣa antara buddhi sampāditasya dvi tva ādeḥ puruṣa antareṇa agrahaṇāt gṛhītañca viśeṣaṇam iti na eṣa doṣaḥ smaryamāṇasya upalakṣaṇa tva abhyupagamāt tathā hi dvi pṛthaktva utpādikāyāḥ sva kāraṇāt apekṣā buddheḥ utpattiḥ dvi tva smaraṇasya utpadyamāna tā dvi pṛthaktvasya utpadyamāna tā tatas dvi tva smaraṇasya utpādaḥ dvi pṛthaktvasya utpādaḥ apekṣā buddheḥ vinaśyattā dvi pṛthaktva guṇa buddheḥ utpadyamāna tā iti ekaḥ kālaḥ tatas dvi tva smaraṇasya dvi pṛthaktva jñāna janaka tvam eva iti manyamānāḥ guṇa ādiṣu api etasmāt ayam vyāvṛttaḥ vilakṣaṇaḥ ityādi vyavahāraḥ pṛthaktva nimittaḥ sa ca nirguṇa tvāt guṇa ādīnām upacāraḥ iti manyante na ca pṛthak iti jñānam nirviṣayam vāsanā prabhavam tasyāḥ pūrvam eva pratiṣedhāt 
[II,061,24]	lakṣaṇena lakṣyamāṇasya eka aneka tva upalabdhau saṃśaye sati tad nirāsa artham vibhāgam āha tat punar eka dravyam aneka dravyañcaḥ iti ekam eva dravyam āśrayaḥ asya iti eka dravyam anekam eva ca dravyam āśrayaḥ asya avinaśyat avastha dravyasya iti aneka dravyam tasya tu dvividhasya api nitya anitya tva niṣpattayaḥ saṃkhyayā vyākhyātāḥ iti atideśaḥ tathā hi eka pṛthaktvam nityeṣu aniṣpadyamāna tvāt nityam kāryeṣu ca kāraṇa guṇa pūrvakam āśraya vināśāt āśu vinaśyati iti atideśa arthaḥ dvi pṛthaktva ādeḥ dvi tva ādi vat apekṣā buddhitaḥ utpattiḥ vināśaḥ tu tad vināśāt kvacid āśraya vināśāt ca śata pṛthaktva ādi utpattiḥ tu śata saṃkhyā utpatti nyāyena iti atideśaḥ 
[II,062,6_II,062,9]	nanu evam tarhi śata saṃkhyātaḥ na viśeṣaḥ syāt iti āśaṅkya āha etāvān tu viśeṣaḥ eka tva ādi vat eka pṛthaktva ādiṣu apara sāmānya abhāvaḥ iti yathā hi saṃkhyātu a vyatirekeṇa aparam eka tva ādi sāmānyam asti na evam eka pṛthaktva ādi iti atha anugata jñānāt ayuktam etat na anyathā tad upapatteḥ tathā hi dravya guṇa karma nimittam abādhyamānam anugatam jñānam sāmānya sattām darśayati pṛthaktve ca eka tva ādi saṃkhyā vaśāt anugata jñānam ghaṭataḥ iti āha saṃkhyayā tu viśiṣyate kutas tad viśiṣṭa vyavahāra darśanāt idam ekam pṛthak dve pṛthak trīṇi pṛthak ityādi 
[II,062,14_II,062,21]	atha aśeṣa dravyeṣu ekam eva astu pṛthaktvam saṃkhyā vat viśeṣaṇa jñāna tvāt viśeṣaṇam apekṣate na ca rūpa ādīnām anyatamam nimittam tad vyavahāra vilakṣaṇa tvāt iti nimitta antareṇa bhavitavyam iti tad kriyayā guṇa buddheḥ utpādaḥ dravya buddheḥ utpadyamāna tā dvi tva smaraṇasya vinaśyattā apekṣā buddheḥ vināśaḥ dvi pṛthaktva guṇasya vinaśyattā tatas dve pṛthak iti dravya buddheḥ utpādaḥ guṇa buddheḥ vinaśyattā dvi tva smaraṇasya vināśaḥ apekṣā buddhi vināśāt guṇasya vināśaḥ saṃskārasya utpadyamāna tā tatas saṃskārāt dravya buddheḥ vināśaḥ iti 
[II,062,26]	yat vā dvi tva utpādikāyāḥ apekṣā buddheḥ utpādaḥ dvi tvasya utpadyamāna tā dvi pṛthaktva utpādikāyāḥ ca apekṣā buddheḥ utpadyamāna tā tatas dvi tva smaraṇasya utpādaḥ tad buddheḥ utpadyamāna tā dvi pṛthaktva utpādikāyāḥ ca apekṣā buddheḥ utpādaḥ dvi pṛthaktvasya utpadyamāna tā dvi tva utpādikāyāḥ apekṣā buddheḥ vinaśyattā tatas dvi pṛthaktvasya utpādaḥ dvi tva guṇa buddheḥ utpādaḥ dvi tva guṇāt tad jñānāt tad eka artha samavāyāt ca dvi pṛthaktva guṇa buddheḥ utpadyamāna tā apekṣā buddheḥ vināśaḥ dvi tvasya vinaśyattā dvi pṛthaktva utpādikāyāḥ ca apekṣā buddheḥ vinaśyattā iti ekaḥ kālaḥ 
[II,063,6_II,063,9]	tatas dvi pṛthaktva guṇa buddheḥ utpādaḥ dravya buddheḥ utpadyamāna tā dvi tva guṇasya vināśaḥ tad buddheḥ vinaśyattā dvi pṛthaktva utpādikāyāḥ ca apekṣā buddheḥ vināśaḥ dvi pṛthaktva guṇasya vinaśyatta iti ekaḥ kālaḥ tatas dve pṛthak iti dravya buddheḥ utpādaḥ guṇa buddheḥ vinaśyattā dvi pṛthaktva guṇasya vināśaḥ dvi tva guṇa buddheḥ ca vināśaḥ saṃskārasya utpadyamāna tā tatas saṃskārāt dravya buddheḥ vināśaḥ iti atra tu vidyamānasya dvi tva guṇasya sva anubhava sahakāriṇaḥ dvi pṛthaktva guṇa jñāna utpattau vyāpāraḥ iti viśeṣaḥ 
[II,063,13]	anye tu ekaika guṇa ālambanakāḥ buddhiḥ utpadyate dvi tvat vipṛthaktvayoḥ utpadyamāna tā iti manyante tatas dvi tvat vipṛthaktvayoḥ utpādaḥ dvi tva guṇa jñānasya utpadyamāna tā tatas dvi tva guṇa jñānasya utpādaḥ dvi pṛktva jñānasya utpadyamāna tā apekṣā buddheḥ vinaśyattā tatas dvi pṛthaktva guṇa jñānasya utpādaḥ dravya jñānasya utpadyamāna tā dvi tva guṇa jñānasya vinaśyattā apekṣā buddheḥ vināśaḥ dvi tvat vipṛthak tvayoḥ vinaśyattā tatas dravya jñānasya utpādaḥ dvi pṛthaktva guṇa jñānasya vināśaḥ dvi tvat vipṛthaktvayoḥ vināśaḥ saṃskārasya utpadyamāna tā tatas saṃskārāt dravya buddheḥ vināśaḥ iti atra tu vidyamānasya dvi tva guṇasya dve pṛthak iti dravya jñānasya utpattau api vyāpāraḥ iti viśeṣaḥ 
[II,063,22]	atha samavetānām eva guṇa karma sāmānyānām viśeṣaṇa tā upalabdheḥ katham dvi pṛthaktva ādāvavartamānam dvi tva ādi viśeṣaṇam iti ced bādhaka upapatteḥ upacāreṇa iti uktam padārtha saṅkare tathā ca sūtram aguṇa karmasu guṇa karma abhāvāt guṇa karma apekṣa na vidyate iti guṇa karmasu samavetānām guṇa karmaṇām abhāvāt tad apekṣam mukhya jñānam na asti iti 
[II,064,2_II,064,5]	idānīm uddeśavataḥ saṃyogasya lakṣaṇa parīkṣā artham saṃyogaḥ saṃyukta pratyaya nimittam ityādi prakaraṇam pratītiḥ pratyayaḥ jñānam pratīyate anena iti pratyayaḥ abhidhānam tayoḥ nimittam sarve api padārthāḥ iti saṃyukta grahaṇam tathā api saṃyukta pratyaya nimitta tvam ākāśa ātmanoḥ vidyate iti viśeṣaṇa tve sati iti kāryam atas saṃyogaḥ itarebhyaḥ bhidyate viśeṣaṇa tve sati saṃyukta pratyaya nimitta tvāt yaḥ tu itara smāt asaṃyogāt na bhidyate na ca asau evam yathā rupādiḥ iti parīkṣā paratvena api sambadhyate saṃyogaḥ saṃyukta pratyaya nimittam iti vākyam 
[II,064,12_II,064,18]	atha viśiṣṭa utpādāt dravyam eva saṃyukta vyavahāra nimittam tathā hi viśleṣa kṣaṇāt saṃśleṣa kṣaṇa utpāde saṃyukta vyavahāraḥ dṛṣṭaḥ na anyathā iti tat asat viśiṣṭa tāyāḥ vyatireka anabhyupagame tasyāḥ dravya rūpa tayā sarvatra aviśeṣāt dravya mātre saṃyukta pratyayaḥ syāt vyatireke tu yena satā rūpa ādi vilakṣaṇena saṃyuktaḥ iti vyavahāraḥ saḥ eva saṃyogaḥ iti na kiñcid bādhyate saṃśleṣasya atra saṃyoga rūpa tvāt iti na ca ayam vyavahāraḥ vāsanā nimittaḥ tasyāḥ pūrvam eva pratiṣedhāt artha kriyām āha sa ca dravya guṇa karma hetuḥ iti saṃyoga sadbhāve pramāṇañca idam iti na hi tantu saṃyogāt ṛte paṭasya utpattiḥ bherī daṇḍa saṃyogañca vinā śabdasya hasta tomara ādi saṃyoga abhāve ca tomara karmaṇaḥ iti dṛṣṭañca atas saṃyogaḥ abhyupagantavyaḥ 
[II,064,22]	katham punar dravya ārambhaka tvam asya iti āha dravya ārambhe nirapekṣaḥ iti yadi api samavāyi ādi kāraṇam apekṣate tathā api anapekṣaḥ paścāt bhāvi kāraṇa anapekṣaṇāt yathā ca vyākhyātam etat tathā bhavati na anyathā iti kutas jñātam iti ced sa apekṣebhyaḥ nirapekṣebhyaḥ ca iti vacanāt asya ca sūtrasya ayam arthaḥ pūrvam antya tantu saṃyoga utpatteḥ sa apekṣāḥ tantavaḥ paṭam na ārabhante tad jātīyānāntu paṭa antare sāmarthya avadhāraṇādantya tantu saṃyoga sampādanāya upādīyante tad utpattau ca anapekṣāḥ tad anantaram eva ārabhante iti dravya ārambhe nirapekṣaḥ saṃyogaḥ atas eva antya saṃyoga vyatirekeṇa na anyā śaktiḥ tasyāḥ caramasahakāri rūpa tvāt iti uktam pṛthivī adhikāre 
[II,065,5_II,065,8]	na ca pūrvasya virala deśa kṣaṇasya vinivṛttau avirala deśa kṣaṇasya viśiṣṭasya utpāde paṭavyavahārāt alam saṃyoga kalpanayā iti vācyam kṣaṇa bhaṅgasya pratiṣedhāt avayava vyatiriktasya ca avayavinaḥ vyavasthāpanāt iti guṇa karma ārambhe tu sa apekṣaḥ paścāt bhāvi nimitta apekṣa tvāt iti katham jñāyate iti āha saṃyukta samavāyāt agneḥ vaiśeṣikam iti vacanāt asya arthaḥ saṃyuktaḥ pārthivena paramāṇunā agniḥ tatra samavāyāt agneḥ sambandhinam vaiśeṣika guṇam uṣṇa sparśam apekṣamāṇaḥ pārthiva paramāṇu agni saṃyogaḥ pāka jān ārabhate agneḥ sambandhinam uṣṇa sparśam apekṣamāṇaḥ vaiśeṣikam rūpa ādikam ārabhate 
[II,065,13_II,065,17]	nanu uṣṇa sparśasya cira utpādāt na paścāt bhāvi tvam asti pūrva utpanna kāraka apekṣi tvam dravya ārambhe saṃyogasya iṣyatas eva iti aviśeṣaḥ syāt na śyāma ādi nivṛtti viśiṣṭasya paścāt bhāvāt tathā hasta ātma saṃyogaḥ paścāt bhāvinam prayatnam apekṣamāṇaḥ haste karma ārabhate nanu evam api ātma manaḥ saṃyogasya buddhi ādi utpattau na paścāt bhāvi nimittam asti śarīra sambandhaḥ iti ced na tasya paścāt bhāva anupapatteḥ yadi api saṃhāra avasthāyām ātma manaḥ sambandha sadbhāve api na jñānam śarīra sambandhe tu bhavati tathā api śukra śoṇita sambandha sama kālam manaḥ sambandha abhyupagamāt avaśyam prāktana saṃyogasya nivṛttiḥ iti na tad apekṣayā śarīra sambandhaḥ carama bhāvī pariniṣpaṇṇe api ca śarīre manasaḥ kriyā dvāreṇa sambandhāt tathā śarīrasya api bhavati iti na tatra pūrva apara bhāve pramāṇam asti iti 
[II,065,24]	na ca evam ātma manaḥ sambandhasya anapekṣi tvam eva sukha duḥkha ādīnām nimitta kāraṇānām tad uttara kāle bhāvāt tathā hi icchā utpattau ātma manaḥ sambandhasya sukham smaraṇam vā paścāt bhāvi tvāt apekṣā kāraṇam evam dveṣa ādi utpattau api duḥkha ādeḥ kāraṇa tvam abhyūhyam śarīra sambandhasya tu niyamena paścāt bhāvi tvam niṣidhyate na kāraṇa tvam iti evam karma utpattau api saṃyogasya na sarvatra carama bhāvi nimitta tvam sambhavati iti tathā śākhā ādau upari pāṣāṇa ādi saṃyogāt guru tva apekṣāt adhas gamanam nadī srotasi ca drava tva apekṣāt tṛṇa udaka saṃyogāt tṛṇa ādau gamanañca guru tva drava tvayoḥ paścāt bhāvi tvam asti iti 
[II,066,6_II,066,23]	nanu evam tarhi guṇa karma ārambhe sa apekṣaḥ iti ayuktam vākyam na ayoga vyavaccheda anabhyupagamāt tathā ca guṇa karma ārambhaḥ eva sa apekṣaḥ na tu sa apekṣaḥ eva anapekṣita tvasya api upalabdheḥ atha kathaṃlakṣaṇaḥ katividhaḥ ca iti vākyam lakṣaṇasya nirṇīta tvāt vyartham na lakṣaṇa antara abhidhitsayāḥ asya upapatteḥ yadi api upasarjanasya prāk lakṣaṇam uktam tathā api svātantryeṇa katham asya lakṣaṇam iti āśaṅkā bhavati eva parīkṣā param eva tat vākyam iti anye yat vā viparyastaḥ ayam kathaṃlakṣaṇam asya iti na sambhavati eva saṃyogasya lakṣaṇam iti manyante katividhaḥ ca iti bheda artham praśnaḥ tatra lakṣaṇam āha aprāptayoḥ prāptiḥ saṃyogaḥ iti prāptiḥ samavāyaḥ api bhavati iti aprāptayoḥ iti padam paryāya śabdasya ca lakṣaṇa tvam iṣṭam eva sa ca pratyakṣeṇa gṛhyate iti na saṃyogasya asambhavena lakṣaṇasya āśrayā siddha tvam iti 
[II,067,1]	sa ca trividhaḥ iti bheda pratipādanam sāmānya lakṣṇasya asambhavi tva parihāra artham kena rūpeṇa traividhyam iti āha anyatara karma jaḥ ubhaya karma jaḥ saṃyoga jaḥ ca saṃyogaḥ iti tatra anyatarasmin karma tasmāt jātaḥ anyatara karma jaḥ yathā sthāṇoḥ śyenena iti vibhūnāñca mūrtaiḥ iti udāharaṇa dvayam avāntara viśeṣa vivakṣayā tathā hi śyena sthāṇu saṃyogaḥ karmaṇā saṃyogena ca janyate vibhūnāntu paramāṇubhiḥ saṃyogaḥ karmaṇā eva iti saṃyoga karmaṇoḥ ca vyāpāra aviśeṣe api karmaṇā eva vyapadeśaḥ saṃgraha artham anyatara karma ja tvam ubhayatra api asti iti avabodhanāya 
[II,067,9]	nanu evam saṃyoga jaḥ karma jaḥ ca iti vācyam tad viśeṣa tvāt anyeṣām iti satyam tathā api karma jasya etāvān eva bhedaḥ iti parisaṃkhyā artham anyatara ādi grahaṇam na saṃyogasya kāraṇa tva pratiṣedha artha param tathā ca prayatna apekṣāt śyena caraṇa saṃyogāt caraṇa kriyāyāḥ utpādaḥ vibhāgasya utpadyamāna tā śyena avayavinya sva kāraṇāt kriyāyāḥ utpadyamāna tā tatas śyena caraṇa vibhāgasya utpādaḥ saṃyogasya vinaśyattā śyena avayavi karmaṇaḥ api utpādaḥ vibhāgasya utpadyamāna tā tatas śyena caraṇa saṃyogasya vināśaḥ uttara saṃyogasya utpadyamāna tā śyena avaya vi vibhāgasya utpādaḥ śyena avayavi karmaṇā ca śyena sthāṇu saṃyogaḥ janyate pratyāsanna tve sati ubhayoḥ sāmarthya avadhāraṇāt atas śyena sthāṇvoḥ samavāyi kāraṇa tvam śyena kriyāyāḥ tad caraṇa sthāṇu saṃyogasya ca asamavāyi kāraṇa tvam pratyāsattiḥ tu śyena caraṇa saṃyogasya mahati api sambhavati iti anyatara avarodhe na viśeṣa hetuḥ asti iti vakṣyāmaḥ 
[II,067,21]	ubhaya karma jaḥ api ubhayoḥ karmaṇī tābhyām jātaḥ yathā mallayoḥ meṣayoḥ vā atra api avayava karmabhyām vibhāga sama kālam avayavinaḥ karma abhyupagame saṃyogaiḥ avayavi karmabhyāñca saṃyogaḥ janyate iti cintyam yathā hi avayava karma avayava antareṇa saṃyogam karoti evam tad avayavinā api itara avayava karmā api itara avayava karma saṃyoga vat tad avayavinā api iti saṃyoga tritayam tat ca pratyāsanna tve sati sāmarthya avadhāraṇāt kāraṇam iti meṣayoḥ samavāyi kāraṇa tvam saṃyukta pratyaye hi viśeṣya avayava avayavi saṃyogasya ca asamavāyi kāraṇa tvam śeṣam nimitta kāraṇam iti kevala ubhaya karma ja tvañca paramāṇu dvaya saṃyogasya draṣṭavyam 
[II,068,3]	anye tu ubhaya padasya lupta vibhaktikasya pūrva uttareṇa sambandhāt saṃyoga karma ja bhedasya api grahaṇam bhaviṣyati eva iti manyante tathā hi saṃyoga kāraṇa tvena ubhayoḥ upalambhāt karmaṇaḥ sva śabdena upādāne anyataraḥ saṃyogaḥ labhyate eva anyataraḥ ca karma ca anyatara karmaṇī tābhyām jātaḥ anyatara karma jaḥ sa ca ubhayaḥ ekena karmaṇā saṅgatya dvitīyena janyate dva abhyāñca saṃyogaḥ sa dvitīyābhyām iti tathā ubhayaḥ kevala karma jaḥ api ekena karmaṇā janyate dvābhyāñca iti saṃyoga jaḥ tu utpanna mātrasya cira utpannasya vā iti ubhayaḥ tasya lakṣaṇam āha akriyasya ityādi 
[II,068,11_II,068,15]	akriyasya iti ayam niyamaḥ kaiḥ saha iti āha akāraṇaiḥ kiṃviśiṣṭaiḥ kāraṇa saṃyogibhiḥ iti kāraṇena saṃyogāḥ te yeṣām tāni tathā uktāni taiḥ kāraṇa saṃyogibhiḥ akāraṇaiḥ saha akriyasya yaḥ saṃyogaḥ sa saṃyoga jaḥ anyasya kāraṇasya abhāvāt saṃgraha ukteḥ vivaraṇam āha kāraṇa akāraṇa saṃyoga pūrvakaḥ kārya akārya gataḥ saṃyogaḥ iti kāraṇam atra samavāyi kāraṇam sva kāryasya tad apekṣayā anyat akāraṇam tayoḥ yaḥ saṃyogaḥ tad pūrvakaḥ kārya akārya gataḥ saṃyogaḥ prakṛtasya kāraṇasya yat kāryam tad saṃyuktañca anya t akāryam tayoḥ saṃyoga jaḥ iti tatra cira utpannasya udāharaṇam vibhāga ja vibhāga avasare vakṣyamāṇam iti utpanna mātrasya vibhāga dvāreṇa udāharaṇam āha sa ca ekasmāt ityādi sa ca saṃyoga ja saṃyogaḥ ekasmāt dvābhyām bahubhyaḥ ca ca śabdāt ekasmāt dvau iti vibhāgaḥ 
[II,068,22]	ekasmāt tāvat tantu vīraṇa saṃyogāt dvi tantuka vīraṇa saṃyogaḥ iti tathā hi tantoḥ vīraṇena saṃsṛṣṭasya tantu antareṇa abhisambandhe sati dvi tantukam utpadyate tasya ca rūpa ādi utpatti sama kālam vīraṇena saṃyogaḥ janyate iti tad utpattau asamavāyi kāraṇam anveṣaṇīyam na ca atra kriyā sambhavati ubhayoḥ niṣkriya tvāt rūpa ādīnāñca sva kārya utpattau eva sāmarthya avadhāraṇāt asamavāyikāraṇañca vinā vastu bhūtasya kāryasya utpattiḥ na upalabdha iti tantu vīraṇa saṃyogaḥ eva samāna jātīya tve sati pratyāsanna tvāt asamavāyikāraṇam iti pratyāsattiḥ tu kārya eka artha samavāyaḥ kāraṇa eka artha samavāyaḥ ca iti ubhaya rūpā na sambhavati eva iti kāryā eka artha samavāyasya eva grahaṇam kāraṇena avyavadhānāt iti kecid mahatī tu yatra kāraṇa vṛttīnām eva kārye guṇa ārambhaka tvam tatra eva grāhya iti 
[II,069,6]	na ca ekasya ārambhaka tve guṇāḥ ca guṇa antaram ārabhante iti sūtra virodhaḥ kāraṇa vṛttīnām samāna jāti ārambhaka tvam eva niyamāt tathā hi ye kāraṇa vṛttayaḥ samāna jātīyam eva ārabhante teṣām aneka tva saṃkhyā yuktānām eva ārambhaka tvam iti niyamaḥ tat evam dvi tantuka vīraṇayoḥ samavāyikāraṇa tvam tantu vīraṇa saṃyogasya asamavāyi kāraṇa tvam śeṣam nimitta kāraṇam iti 
[II,069,11]	dvi tantuka vīraṇa saṃyogasya utpattiḥ dvābhyām tantu ākāśa saṃyogābhyām ekaḥ dvi tantuka ākāśa saṃyogaḥ iti tantoḥ ākāśa sambaddhasya tantu antareṇa abhisambandhe sati dvi tantukam utpadyate tantu kriyā ca tantu antareṇa iva ca ākāśa deśena api saṃyogam karoti pratibandhaka abhāvāt utpanne tu dvi tantuke rūpa ādi utpatti sama kālam ākāśena api saṃyogaḥ bhavati eva kim atra pramāṇam iti ced anumānam 
[II,069,17]	tathā hi dvi tantukam sva kāraṇa saṃyoginā saṃyujyate tad saṃyukta kāraṇa kārya tvāt vīraṇa saṃyukta dvi tantuka vat ākāśam vā sva saṃyukta kāraṇa kāryeṇa saṃyujyate tad kāraṇa saṃyogi tvāt dvi tantuka saṃyukta vīraṇa vat siddhe ca saṃyoge tasya kārya tvāt utpatti kāraṇam cintyam tatra dvi tantuka ākāśayoḥ samavāyikāraṇa tvam iti anyena asamavāyi kāraṇena bhavitavyam na ca rūpa ādi utpatti sama kālam dvi tantuke kriyā sambhavati iti tantu ākāśa saṃyogayoḥ samāna jātīya tve sati pratyāsanna tvāt asamavāyikāraṇa tvam iti pratyāsattiḥ tu ubhaya rūpā api sambhavati iti pūrvavat grāhyā 
[II,069,24]	bahubhyaḥ ca tantu turī saṃyogebhyaḥ ekaḥ paṭa turī saṃyogaḥ tantūnām turyā saha saṃyoge sati antya tantu saṃyoga anantaram paṭe utpadyate tasya tad paṭa ādi utpatti sama kālam turyā saha saṃyogaḥ gṛhyate iti utpatti kāraṇam vācyam tatra paṭa turyoḥ samavāyi kāraṇa tvam anyasya asamavāyi kāraṇasya anupalabdheḥ tantu turī saṃyogānāmasamavāyi kāraṇa tvam pratyāsattiḥ tu pūrvavat vācya iti 
[II,070,3]	nanu ca ayuktam etat tantūnām paṭa utpattau akāraṇa tvāt kāraṇa akāraṇa saṃyoga pūrvakaḥ ca kārya akārya gataḥ saṃyogaḥ saṃyoga jaḥ iti tantoḥ tantu antareṇa abhisambandhe sati dvi tantukam utpadyate punar tantu antareṇa abhisambandhe anyat kāryam iti aneka kārya vyavadhānena paṭa utpatteḥ katham tantūnām paṭa utpattau kāraṇa tvam na ārabdha kāryasya eva saha kāri antara prāptau ārambhaka tve sati ārabhya ārambhaka vādaḥ syāt tatra ca mūrtānām samāna asamāna deśa tvam tathā hi tantubhyām ārabdham tantvā uḥ vartate punar anya sahitābhyām ārabdham tayoḥ tatra ca iti evam uttarottareṣu api ūhyam 
[II,070,11]	atha anya sahitābhyām ārabdham ekasmin eva vartate iti eka dravya vṛtti tvam syāt iha tantuṣu paṭaḥ iti pratyaya abhāvaḥ ca tad vināśe ca avāntara kārya anupalambhaḥ śeṣañcaḥ ārabhya ārambhaka vāde dūṣaṇam pṛthivī adhikāre jñeyam tasmāt vyoma ādi sambandhāt avayava kriyā dvāreṇa avāntara kārya vināśe tantu antara abhisambandha kālam avasthita saṃyogāḥ tantavaḥ punar kārya antaram ārabhante iti eṣa nyāyaḥ tāvat yāvat antya tantu saṃyogāt paṭa utpattiḥ iti 
[II,070,17_II,070,22]	na ca avāntara kārya utpatti vaiyarthyam tad antareṇa abhipreta kārya anutpatteḥ yathā hi viśiṣṭa sthāna prāptiḥ na ava antara sthāna prāptim vinā sampadyate iti akāraṇa tve api tad sadbhāvaḥ tadvat avāntara kāryam vinā abhipreta kāryam na sampadyate iti tasmāt tad sadbhāvaḥ abhyupagantavyaḥ kāraṇatvantu niṣidhyate tad apāye api utpatteḥ iti alam 
[II,071,6^1]	atha ekasmāt saṃyogāt dvayoḥ saṃyogayoḥ utpattiḥ katham iti āha yadā pārthiva apyayoḥ aṇvoḥ saṃyoge sati anyena pārthivena paramāṇunā saha pārthivasya anyena āpyena ca api asya yugapad saṃyogau bhavataḥ tadā tābhyām samāna jātīya dravya sambandhāt pārthivāpye dvi aṇuke yugapadārabhyete tatas dvi aṇuka utpāda anantaram yasmin eva kāle kāraṇa guṇa pūrva prakrameṇa dvi aṇukayoḥ rūpa ādi utpattiḥ tasmin eva kāle itaretara kāraṇā kāraṇa gatāt saṃyogāt itaretara kārya akārya gatau saṃyogau yugapad utpadyete itaraḥ paramāṇuḥ kāraṇam sva kāryasya 
[II,071,6^2]	itaraḥ akāraṇam tad apekṣayā evam anyaḥ api iti tad gatāt tad samavetāt saṃyogāt itaretara kārya akārya gatau itarat pārthivam dvi aṇukam kāryam sva kāraṇasya itaraḥ ca api aparamāṇura kāryaḥ tathā itara dāpyam dvi aṇukam kāryam itaraḥ ca pārthiva paramāṇura kāryaḥ tad gatau saṃyogau yugapad utpadyete tatra ca dvi aṇuka paramāṇvoḥ samavāyikāraṇa tvam iti anyat asamavāyi kāraṇam cintyam na ca atra kriyā sambhavati ubhayoḥ niṣkriya tvāt iti paramāṇvoḥ saṃyogaḥ pratyāsanna tve sati sāmarthya avadhāraṇāt kāraṇam iti 
[II,071,20]	atha pārthiva t vi aṇukasya āpyena aṇunā saṃyogaḥ tathā āpyasya pāthivena iti kim kāraṇam kim pramāṇam iti āha kāraṇa saṃyoginā hi akāraṇena kāryam avaśyam saṃyujyate iti nyāyaḥ pramāṇam tathā hi pārthiva t vi aṇukam sva kāraṇa saṃyoginā saṃyujyate tad saṃyukta kāraṇa kārya tvāt vīraṇa saṃyukta dvi tantuka vat āpyaḥ vā paramāṇuḥ sva saṃyukta kāraṇa kāryeṇa saṃyujyate tad kāraṇa saṃyogi tvāt dvi tantuka saṃyukta vīraṇa vat evam itaratra api vācyam yatas evam atas pārthiva t vi aṇukam sva kāraṇa saṃyoginā āpyena aṇunā sambadhyate āpyam api dvi aṇukam pārthivena iti 
[II,072,1]	atha dvi aṇukayoḥ ita retara kāraṇā kāraṇa sambaddhayoḥ iti itarasya pārthiva t vi aṇukasya yat kāraṇam tad itarasya akāraṇam evam āpya dvi aṇukasya kāraṇam itarasya pārthiva t vi aṇukasya akāraṇam tad sambaddhayoḥ dvi aṇukayoḥ parasparataḥ katham sambandhaḥ iti āha tayoḥ api saṃyoga jābhyām saṃyogābhyām sambandhaḥ iti yau tau kārya akārya gatau saṃyogau ekasmāt saṃyogāt utpannau tābhyām dvi aṇukayoḥ samavāyi kāraṇa tvam kārya akārya saṃyogayoḥ ca asamavāyi kāraṇa tvam pratyāsa sattiḥ tu ubhaya rūpā api sambhavati iti pūrvavat grāhyā adṛṣṭa ādiḥ ca nimitta kāraṇam iti 
[II,072,9_II,072,15]	na ca dvi aṇukasya sva kāraṇa saṃyoginā paramāṇu antareṇa dvi aṇuka antareṇa api rūpa ādi utpatti sama kālam ekasmāt eva kāraṇa akāraṇa saṃyogāt saṃyogaḥ bhaviṣyati iti vācyam tasmin kāle dvi aṇukasya kāraṇa saṃyogi tva abhāvāt kāraṇa saṃyoginā ca api akāryeṇa saṃyogaḥ saṃyoga jaḥ iti tasmāt āpyadvi aṇukasya pārthivena paramāṇunā saṃyogaḥ pārthivasya ca api ena iti pūrvam eva abhidheyam yena kāraṇa saṃyogi tvāt dvi aṇukayoḥ api saṃyogaḥ saṃyoga jaḥ bhavati iti 
[II,072,22]	idānīm vibhāga sūtre aja saṃyoga anabhidhānāt nyūna tvam iti āśaṅkya parihāra artham āha na ajaḥ saṃyogaḥ asti nitya parimaṇḍala vat pṛthak anabhidhānāt yathā bhagavān ṛṣiḥ sakala artha darśī caturvidham parimāṇam utpādyam uktvā āha nityam pārimāṇḍalyam para māṇu parimāṇam asti iti evam anyatara karma ja ādi saṃyogam trividham utpādyam uktvā pṛthak nityam saṃyogam brūyāt na tu evam abravīt tasmāt na astyajaḥ saṃyogaḥ pratijñātañca mahā ṛṣiṇā yad bhāva rūpam tat sarvam abhidhāsyāmi iti 
[II,073,3]	nanu ca atra ajaḥ saṃyogaḥ na asti iti pratijñā vākye padayoḥ vyāghātaḥ yathedañca na asti ca iti na anyathā pratijñānāt tathā hi paramāṇubhiḥ ākāśa ādīnām saṃyogaḥ nitya tvena abhyupagataḥ pareṇa tasya aja tvam eva niṣidhyate na sadbhāvaḥ paramāṇubhiḥ ākāśa ādīnām saṃyogaḥ ajaḥ na bhavati sarvajñena mahā ṛṣiṇā ajāta tvena pṛthak apratipādyamāna tvāt yat ca ajam tat aja tvena pṛthak upadiṣṭam yathā nityam pārimāṇḍalyam iti 
[II,073,9]	atha saṃyogasya aprāpti virodhi tvam tat tu na sambhavati eva ākāśa ādeḥ vibhu tvena tad parityāga anupapatteḥ na ca āśraya vināśāt vināśaḥ atra āśrayasya api nitya tvāt na ca anyat vināśa kāraṇam asti iti aja tvam eva avacanantu vyāmohāt api sambhavati iti anyathā siddham asya pratiṣedha artham āha paramāṇubhiḥ ākāśa ādīnām pradeśa vṛttiḥ anyatara karma jaḥ saṃyogaḥ iti katham ākāśa aparityāgena paramāṇoḥ saṃyogāḥ vibhāgāḥ ca bhavanti iti ced yathā vṛkṣa aparityāgena devadattasya tathā hi mūla pradeśāt ūrdhva pradeśam ārohataḥ puruṣasya vṛkṣa aparityāgena eva saṃyogāḥ vibhāgāḥ ca upalabhyante mūla pradeśe vṛkṣeṇa saṃyuktaḥ madhya pradeśe agra pradeśe ca iti na ca pradeśasya eva te saṃyogāḥ vṛkṣeṇa saṃyuktaḥ iti pratyaya upalambhāt pradeśena eva saṃyoge pradeśena saṃyuktaḥ na vṛkṣeṇa iti jñānam syāt na ca etat asti vṛkṣeṇa saṃyuktaḥ iti jñānasya sarvasyām avasthāyām upalabdheḥ 
[II,073,20]	yadi ca saṃyogasya pradeśa vṛtti tvāt pradeśena eva saṃyogaḥ na vṛkṣeṇa iti tarhi te api pradeśāḥ sva avayava apekṣayā avayavinaḥ iti tad pradeśānām saṃyogaḥ teṣām api avayavi tvāt pradeśānām iti tāvat yāvat nirdeśāḥ paramāṇavaḥ teṣāñca niṣpradeśa tvāt saṃyoga abhāvena dvi aṇuka ādi prakrameṇa kāryam iti kṣiti ādeḥ asambhavaḥ eva 
[II,073,24]	atha niṣpradeśa tve api sati paramāṇūnām pradeśa tvāt iṣyate eva saṃyogaḥ tarhi dvi aṇukānām saṃyoga abhāve na tri aṇukam iti dūṣaṇam tad avastham eva na ca paramāṇuṣu vartamānaḥ saṃyogaḥ dvi aṇuka ādi samavetam dravyam ārabhate vyadhikaraṇasya ārambhaka tve ati prasaṅgāt tasmāt saṃyogasya pradeśa vṛtti tvam āśraya avyāpaka tvam iti avayavena avayavinā ca saṃyogaḥ ghaṭataḥ eva 
[II,074,3_II,074,7]	na ca prāktanasya mūla pradeśe vṛkṣeṇa saṃyogasya avasthāne sati uttara saṃyogena śakyam bhavitum iti tad vināśakaḥ vibhāgaḥ api siddhaḥ yathā ca atra vṛkṣa aparityāgena eva puruṣasya anyatara karma jāḥ saṃyogāḥ vibhāgāḥ ca bhavanti tadvat ākāśa aparityāgena eva paramāṇoḥ saṃyogāḥ vibhāgāḥ ca bhaviṣyanti iti vyāpaka tvam atantram tat evam paramāṇu ākāśa ādi saṃyogasya utpatti vināśa kāraṇa upapatteḥ na ajatvam iti yat ca sūtrakārasya avacanam vyāmohāt api sambhavati iti uktam tat asat tad abhihitānām padārthānām pramāṇa antareṇa api tathā abhāva upalabdheḥ samyak jñāna siddhau tad viruddhasya mithyājñānasya nivṛtteḥ 
[II,074,11]	atha vibhūnām parasparataḥ saṃyogaḥ bhaviṣyati iti tathā hi ākāśam ātma ādinā saṃyujyate mūrta saṃyogi tvāt ghaṭa vat asya pratiṣedha artham āha vibhūnāntu parasparataḥ saṃyogaḥ na asti yuta siddhi abhāvāt yatra yatra saṃyogaḥ tatra tatra yuta siddhiḥ upalabdhā sā ca saṃyogasya vyāpikā vyāvartamānā sva vyāptam saṃyogam gṛhītvā vyāvartate iti anyathā siddham sādhanam 
[II,074,16]	sā punar yuta siddhiḥ dvayoḥ anyatarasya vā pṛthak gatimat tvam yuta āśraya samavāyi tvañca iti dvayoḥ pṛthak gatimat tvam anyatarasya vā iti iyam nityānām yuta siddhiḥ dvayoḥ yuta āśraya samavāyi tvam anyatarasya vā iti anityānām asyāḥ tu vistareṇa vicāraḥ vibhāga avasare draṣṭavyaḥ na ca vibhūnām pṛthak gatimat tvam amūrta tvāt yuta āśraya samavāyi tvam api na sambhavati eva akārya tvāt iti 
[II,074,22_II,075,1]	vināśasya ca sa hetuka tvāt kutas saṃyogaḥ vinaśyati iti āha vināśaḥ tu sarvasya saṃyogasya eka artha samavetāt vibhāgāt iti yayoḥ eva saṃyogaḥ tayoḥ eva vibhāgāt saṃyogasya vināśaḥ tena satā tasya anupalabdheḥ saṃyoga vināśāt tantu vināśaḥ tantu vināśe tad āśritasya tantu antara saṃyogasya vināśaḥ iti yadā tantu saṃyoga vināśa sama kālam tantu antare api karma sambhāvyate tadā āśraya vināśa vibhāgābhyām api saṃyogasya vināśaḥ iti jñeyam 
[II,075,10_II,075,11]	idānīm vibhāgasya lakṣaṇa parīkṣaṇa artham vibhāgaḥ vibhakta pratyaya nimittam ityādi prakaraṇam pratītiḥ pratyayo jñānam pratīyate anena iti pratyayaḥ abhidhānam tad hetu tvam anyeṣām api iti vibhakta grahaṇam tathā api ākāśa ātmabhyām vyabhicāra parihāra artham dravya viśeṣaṇa tve sati iti draṣṭavyam tathā hi vibhāgaḥ itarebhyaḥ bhidyate dravya viśeṣaṇa tve sati vibhakta pratyaya nimitta tvāt yaḥ tu na bhidyate na ca asau evam yathā rūpa ādiḥ iti tathā vibhakta pratyayaḥ viśeṣya jñāna tvāt na ṛte viśeṣaṇāt bhavati iti parīkṣā param vākyam na ca asya vāsanā prabhava tvam tasyāḥ pūrvam eva pratiṣedhāt virala deśa utpādaḥ ca kṣaṇa bhaṅga niṣedhāt eva niṣiddhaḥ 
[II,075,19]	atha saṃyogasya anutpāde vināśe ca vibhakta vyavahārāt na anyaḥ vibhāgaḥ iti ced na vibhāgam vinā saṃyoga vināśasya eva abhāvāt tathā hi guṇānām āśraya vināśāt virodhi guṇa prādurbhāvāt ca vināśa upalabdheḥ yatra āśraya vināśaḥ tatra saṃyogasya avināśāt na vibhakta pratyayaḥ syāt dṛṣṭaḥ ca saṃyoga vināśaḥ tena karmaṇaḥ guṇa vināśe sāmarthya adarśanāt anyasya vināśa hetoḥ abhāvāt vibhāgaḥ abhyupagantavyaḥ saṃyoga abhāve ca bhāktaḥ vibhakta pratyayaḥ iti 
[II,075,25_II,076,7]	artha kriyām āha śabda vibhāga hetuḥ ca vaṃśa dala vibhāgāt śabda utpattiḥ vibhāgāt ca vibhāga utpattiḥ iti vakṣyāmaḥ atha kathaṃlakṣaṇaḥ katividhiḥ ca iti vākyam iha api sambadhyate iti jñeyam pūrvavat pratisamādhānāt lakṣaṇam āha prāpti pūrvikā aprāptiḥ vibhāgaḥ prāptiḥ saṃyogaḥ pūrvam yasyāḥ sā tad pūrvikā aprāptiḥ vibhāgaḥ saṃyoga anutpattiḥ ca aprāptiḥ na ca prāpti pūrvikā iti 
[II,076,10]	atha prāpteḥ pūrva kāla tvāt kim kāraṇa tvam sati bhāvaḥ vā sati bhāva mātram na tu kāraṇa tvam iti kecid tat tu na budhyāmahe kriyāvat anvaya vyatirekābhyām vibhāga janmani saṃyogasya api vyāpāra upalabdheḥ na hi kriyāvat saṃyoga abhāve vibhāgaḥ bhavati tad bhāve tu bhavati iti na ca anvaya vyatirekiṇaḥ saṃyogasya vibhāga kāraṇa tve kiñcid bādhakam asti yasya bhayāt akāraṇa tvam iṣyeta sva kārya virodhitvantu guṇānām iṣṭam śabda ādau pratyāsannaḥ ca saṃyogaḥ vibhāga utpattau iti asamavāyi kāraṇam yathā uktā ca aprāptiḥ vibhāgaḥ iti lakṣaṇe saṃyoga vat ākṣepa pratisamādhānam 
[II,076,18]	sa ca trividhaḥ eva anyatara karma jaḥ ubhaya karma jaḥ vibhāga jaḥ ca vibhāgaḥ iti tatra anyatara karma ja ubhaya karma jau saṃyoga vat iti etena karmaṇā vibhāgena ca vibhāgaḥ janyate yathā sthāṇoḥ śyenena iti atra hi śyena avayavini sthāṇunā tad caraṇa vibhāga sama kālam karma sañcintanāt ubhayoḥ pratyāsanna tve sati vyāpāraḥ sambhavati iti cintanīyam vibhūnāñca mūrtaiḥ iti kevala eka karma jaḥ tathā dvābhyām karmabhyām vibhāgaiḥ ca vibhāgaḥ janyate yathā mallayoḥ meṣayoḥ vā iti yathā hi meṣa śirasi karma utpannam śiraḥ antarāt vibhāgam karoti evam tad avayavinā api iti avayava avayavi vibhāga trayama vaya vi vibhāga utpattau pratyāsanna tve sati sāmarthya avadhāraṇāt kāraṇam iti tathā vibhāga rahitābhyām vibhāgaḥ janyate yathā paramāṇvoḥ iti atideśa arthaḥ 
[II,077,1]	vibhāga jaḥ tu vyākhyāyate etat dvividham kāraṇa bhedāt iti āha kāraṇa vibhāgāt kāraṇa akāraṇa vibhāgāt ca iti nanu anekasmāt api kāraṇāt ekam kāryam utpadyamānam dṛṣṭam iti na kāraṇa bhedāt bhedaḥ yuktaḥ tat na sāmagrī bhedasya vivakṣita tvāt tathā hi ekā kāraṇa vibhāga upalakṣitā anyā tu kāraṇa akāraṇa vibhāga upalakṣitā sāmagri iti tad bhedān ca vibhāgasya bhedaḥ ghaṭataḥ eva sāmagrī bhedena kāryasya ghaṭa ādeḥ bheda darśanāt viruddha dharma adhikaraṇa tvāt ca vibhinna pratibhāsa viṣaya tvāt tathā hi kāraṇa vibhāga pūrvakaḥ vibhāgaḥ sa kriyasya eva kāraṇa akāraṇa vibhāga pūrvakaḥ tu niṣkriyasya eva iti tathā kāraṇa vibhāga pūrvakaḥ vibhāgaḥ śabdam ārabhate kāraṇa akāraṇa vibhāga pūrvakaḥ vibhāgaḥ vibhāgam eva iti dharma bhedaḥ tat bhedāt ca anyatra bheda upalabdheḥ iha api bhedaḥ avaśyambhāvī

[II,079,26_II,080,3]	atha padma avayava karmā api avayava vibhāga sama kālam ākāśa deśena vibhāgam ārabhate iti atīndriya tvāt anumānam pramāṇam vācyam pramāṇam vinā prameya asiddheḥ tatra yadi asvatantra avayava karma tvam vyatireka avyabhicāreṇa gamakam itaretara āśraya tvam syāt eka aprasiddhau itara aprasiddheḥ iti na etat evam ākāśa deśena asvatantra avayava karmaṇaḥ vibhāga janaka tve bādhaka abhāvāt tathā hi svatantra avayava karmaṇaḥ dravya ārambhaka saṃyoga virodhi utpādaka tvam ākāśa deśena vibhāga janaka tve bādhakam asti na evam atra iti 
[II,080,6]	tathā hi padma avayava karma ākāśa deśena vibhāgam ārabhate tad ārambhaka bādhaka anutpattau karma tvāt yat yat evam tad tad ākāśa ādi deśena vibhāgam ārabhate yathā anārabdha kāryam paramāṇu karma iti avaśyañca paramāṇoḥ ākāśa ādi deśena sambaddhasya utpannam karma tad saṃyoga nivartakam vibhāgam ārabhate tad antareṇa pūrva saṃyoga avasthānāt uttara saṃyoga anutpattau dvi aṇuka ādi prakrameṇa kārya anutpatti prasaṅgāt 
[II,080,11]	anye tu asvatantra avayava karmaṇaḥ yathā avayava antara vibhāga sama kālam akāraṇena tṛṇa ādinā vibhāga janaka tvam evam ākāśa ādīnām api iti manyante tṛṇa ādi vibhāgaḥ ca padma avayavasya pratyakṣaḥ iti udāharaṇam na ca evam svatantra avayava karmaṇaḥ api akāraṇena vibhāga janaka tvam pratyakṣa siddham asti na api idam asat uttaram prasaṅga samāpekṣāyām udāharaṇe api kvacid anumāna upanyāsa abhyupagamāt 
[II,080,17]	atas svatantra avayava karma avayava antarāt eva vibhāgam ārabhate vibhāgāt ca dravya ārambhaka saṃyoga vināśaḥ tasmin vinaṣṭe kāraṇa abhāvāt kārya abhāvaḥ iti avayavi vināśaḥ tatas svatantra avayavasya ākāśa deśena vibhāgaḥ vācyaḥ tad antareṇa pūrva saṃyogasya avasthānāt uttara saṃyoga anutpattau karmaṇaḥ kāla antara avasthāyi tvam nitya dravya samavetasya ca nitya tvam syāt na ca etat asti karmaṇaḥ kṣaṇika tva upalabdheḥ na ca vināśa hetum vinā asya vināśaḥ tādṛśa vināśasya pratiṣedhāt atas anyasya vināśa hetoḥ abhāvāt uttara saṃyogasya eva anvaya vyatirekābhyām karma vināśe sāmarthya avadhāraṇāt kāraṇa tvam iti 
[II,080,25]	na ca uttara saṃyogaḥ pūrvasya ākāśa deśena saṃyogasya pratibandhakasya avasthāne bhavati iti tad vināśa hetuḥ vibhāgaḥ niścīyate na ca asau kriyātaḥ sambhavati ukta nyāyāt asamavāyi kāraṇam vinā ca vibhāgasya utpattiḥ na upalabdhā iti anyasya asamavāyi kāraṇasya abhāvāt kāraṇayoḥ vartamānaḥ vibhāgaḥ pratyāsanna tve sati samāna jātīya tvāt asamavāyi kāraṇam iti yatra hi samāna jātīyam na asti tatra vijātīyam eva asamvāyikāraṇam iti kalpyate kriyā tu vidyamānā api atra bādhaka sadbhāvāt akāraṇam eva tasmāt kāraṇayoḥ vartamānaḥ vibhāgaḥ kārya saṃyuktāt kārya saṃyoga upalakṣitāt ākāśa ādi deśāt vibhāgam ārabhate iti ādipadena ātmā ādeḥ avarodhaḥ 
[II,081,8_II,081,11]	kim apekṣya iti āha kārya vināśa viśiṣṭam kālam iti kārya vināśaḥ dravya vināśaḥ tad viśiṣṭam kālam tad vināśāt svatantraḥ avayavaḥ tam ca apekṣya ārabhate iti anye tu kārya vināśa viśiṣṭam kālam iti sāmānya abhidhānāt saṃyoga vināśa viśiṣṭam apekṣya dravya vināśa sama kālam ārabhataḥ iti bruvate svatantram vā avayavam apekṣyaḥ iti dravya vināśāt ūrdhvam svātantryam asya iti upacāreṇa pūrvam eva ucyate svatantram īśvaram vā avayavam vā apekṣya iti 
[II,081,15]	kasya iti āha sa kriyasya eva iti atha kāraṇa vibhāgasya ubhaya vṛtti tva aviśeṣāt sa kriyasya ākāśa ādi deśena vibhāgaḥ na niskriyasya iti kim atra niyāmakam uttara saṃyoga utpattiḥ iti tathā hi vibhāgāt saṃyoga vināśe sati karma uttara saṃyogam karoti tasmāt vibhāgaḥ karma ca vyāvartate niṣkriye tu utpannaḥ vibhāgaḥ katham uttara saṃyoga anutpattau vyāvarteta na ca vibhāgāt pūrvam saṃyoga nivṛttau uttara saṃyoga utpattiḥ yuktā kāraṇasya karmaṇaḥ abhāvāt asaṃyuktasya ca ākāśa ādibhiḥ avasthāne teṣām asarva gata tvam syāt na ca anya karma sampāditaḥ saṃyogaḥ anya kriyā janyasya vibhāgasya nivartakaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ tasmāt sva kāraṇa karma kāryā uttara saṃyogāt vibhāgasya nivṛttiḥ dṛṣṭā iti uttara saṃyoga anutpattau anupabhogya tva prasaṅgaḥ iti niṣprayojana tvasya prasaṅgaḥ vināśi tva prasaṅgaḥ ca iti tasya hi pūrva saṃyoga nivartanāt uttara saṃyoga utpattau sa prayojana tvam vināśitvañca ghaṭate 
[II,082,1]	yat vā niṣkriyasya ākāśa ādi deśena vibhāga abhyupagame sa kriyasya uttara saṃyoga anutpattiḥ kāraṇa abhāvāt na tu niṣkriyasya vibhāga ja vibhāga pratiṣedhe kāraṇa abhāvaḥ hetuḥ samavāyi ādi kāraṇānām sambhavāt tathā hi niṣkriya avayava ākāśa ādeḥ samavāyi kāraṇa tvam vibhāgasya asamavāyi kāraṇa tvam śeṣam nimitta kāraṇam iti asti kāraṇa sadbhāvaḥ tasmāt uttara saṃyoga pratiṣedhe kāraṇa abhāvaḥ hetuḥ tathā hi sa kriyasya ākāśa ādi deśena vibhāga anabhyupagame prāktana saṃyogasya pratibandhakasya avasthānāt uttara saṃyoga anutpattiḥ tad anutpattau anupabhogya tvam niṣprayojana tvam vibhāga karmaṇoḥ iti 
[II,082,9_II,082,12]	anye tu na niṣkriyasya ākāśa ādi deśena vibhāgaḥ iti asat etat kutas kāraṇa abhāvāt pramāṇa abhāvāt iti ukte pareṇa bādhakam āha uttara saṃyoga anutpattau anupabhogya tvam avināśi tvam vibhāgasya iti atha yadi api avayava karma avayava antara vibhāga sama kālam ākāśa ādi deśena vibhāgam na ārabhate tathā api kārya vināśāt ūrdhvam ārapsyate iti tad niṣedha artham āha na tu tad avaya karma ākāśa ādi deśāt vibhāgam ārabhate viramya vyāpāra pratiṣedhāt tat etat āha tad ārambha kāla atīta tvāt iti tasya karmaṇaḥ vibhāga ārambhaka kālaḥ tasya vā vibhāgasya ārambhaka kālaḥ tad ārambha kālaḥ tasya atīta tvāt iti 
[II,082,18_II,082,25]	atha karmaṇaḥ viramya vyāpāra pratiṣedhe katham uttara saṃyogaḥ na viramya vyāpāra pratiṣedhasya aparijñānāt tathā hi karma vibhāgam kṛtvā punar vibhāgam na ārabhate vegañca kṛtvā punar vegam na punar saṃyogam na ārabhate iti āha pradeśa antara saṃyogantu karoti eva akṛta saṃyogasya karmaṇaḥ kāla atyaya abhāvāt kāla atyayaḥ vināśaḥ tasya abhāvāt iti dṛṣṭaḥ ca atra sadbhāve api tasya vināśaḥ tena uttara saṃyoga janaka tvam karmaṇaḥ abhyupeyam tasmāt tasya nivṛttiḥ iti 
[II,083,4]	kāraṇa akāraṇa vibhāgāt api vibhāgaḥ katham bhavati iti āha yadā haste karma utpannam ityādi haste sva kāraṇāt karma utpannam avayava antara vibhāgam dravya ārambhaka saṃyoga virodhinam akurvat ākāśa ādi deśebhyaḥ vibhāgān ārabhate ityādi padena ātma ādeḥ avarodhaḥ tān tu ārabhya yadā pūrva saṃyoga vināśe sati pradeśa antaraiḥ ākāśa ādi deśaiḥ saṃyogān ārabhate tasmin kāle te kāraṇa akāraṇa vibhāgāḥ kārya akārya vibhāgān ārabhante iti hastaḥ śarīrasya kāraṇam ākāśa ādi ca akāraṇam tad vibhāgāḥ kāyam śarīram hastasya akāryam ākāśa ādi tad vibhāgān ārabhante iti tad utpattau śarīra ākāśa ādeḥ samavāyikāraṇa tvam hasta ākāśa ādi vibhāga anāñca asamavāyi kāraṇa tvam pratyāsattiḥ tu ubhaya rūpā api sambhavati iti bādhaka anupapatteḥ grāhyā kāryā eka artha samavāyāt na vyadhikaraṇa tvam evaṃvidhāyāḥ pratyāsatteḥ anyatra karmaṇi upalambhāt 
[II,083,15^1]	atha pratyakṣeṇa eva hasta pustaka vibhāga sama kālam śarīrasya api tena vibhāga upalabdheḥ karma eva asamavāyi kāraṇam iti kalpyate na āśu bhāvi tvena utpala patra śata vyatibheda vat pratyakṣa abhimānasya bhrānta tvāt yathā hi yugapad utpala patra śatam vyatibhinnam iti pratyakṣa jñānam grāhiṇa anumānena bādhyamāna tvāt apramāṇam evam tatra api hasta vibhāga sama kālam śarīrasya api tena vibhāgaḥ iti yaugapadya jñānam anumāna bādhita tvāt apramāṇam kim anumānam iti ced 
[II,083,15^2]	avayava karmaṇaḥ vibhinna āśraya tvam tathā hi vivakṣita avayava karma sva āśraya vyatirikta ādhāra samavetam eva vibhāgam na ārabhate karma tvāt ubhaya abhimata karma vat na ca anuṣṇaḥ agniḥ kṛtaka tvāt iti anumāna vat pratyakṣeṇa asya virodhaḥ pañca rūpa tvāt tathā hi duṣṭam anumānam pratyakṣeṇa sva viṣaya sahakāriṇā bādhyate duṣṭañca pratyakṣam anumānena iti tasmāt anumānasya ābādhita viṣaya tvāt vibhāge api āśu bhauvi tvena yaugapadya grahaṇam na artha tathā bhāvāt iti dṛṣṭaḥ ca aneka kṣaṇa śata vyavadhāne api āśu bhauvi tvam bhrama nimittam utpala patra śata vyatibhede kim punar eka kṣaṇa vyavadhāne kṣaṇa dvaya vyavadhāne vā iti 
[II,084,1]	tathā hi kāraṇa akāraṇa vibhāgāt saṃyoga vināśe sati kārya akārya vibhāga abhyupagamāt eka kṣaṇa vyavadhānam kāraṇa vibhāga pūrvakasya tu vibhāgasya saṃyoga vināśe dravya vināśe ca anantaram bhavanam iti kṣaṇa dvaya vyavadhānam utpala patra avayaveṣu tu vegavat sūcī ādi sambandhāt karma utpattau vibhāgāt saṃyoga vināśe sati patra vināśaḥ punar patra antare sambandhāt avayava karma utpattiḥ iti ayam kramaḥ patra śate api ūhyaḥ iti aneka kṣaṇa śata vyavadhāne api āśubhau i tvasya bhrama nimitta tva abhyupagamāt eka kṣaṇa vyavadhāne tu bhaviṣyati eva tasmāt āśu bhāvi tvena yaugapadya abhimānasya bhrānta tvāt kāraṇa akāraṇa vibhāgāḥ kārya akārya vibhāgān ārabhante iti 
[II,084,9]	tad anantaram kārya akārya vibhāga anantaram prāktana saṃyoga vināśe sati kāraṇa akāraṇa saṃyogaḥ ca kārya akārya saṃyogān ārabhante na pūrvam prāktana saṃyogasya pratibandhakasya avasthānāt idantu cira utpannānām saṃyoga ja saṃyogasya pūrvam pratijñātasya vibhāga ja vibhāga anantara bhāvi tvāt samāna upāya tayā ca atra eva nirūpaṇam iti 
[II,084,14]	atha śarīrasya ākāśa ādinā vibhāgaḥ saṃyogaḥ ca iti kim pramāṇam anumānam tathā hi śarīram sva kāraṇa vibhāginā vibhajate tad vibhāgi kāraṇa kārya tvāt vīraṇa vibhāgi tantu kārya paṭa vat ākāśa ādi vā sva vibhāgi kāraṇa kāryeṇa vibhajate tad kāraṇa vibhāgi tvāt tantu vibhāgi vīraṇa vat evam śarīram sva kāraṇa saṃyoginā saṃyujyate tad saṃyukta kāraṇa kārya tvāt vīraṇa saṃyukta tantu kārya paṭa vat siddhe tu śarīra ākāśa ādi saṃyoge śarīrasya tasmin kāle niṣkriya tvāt avayava kriyāyāḥ ca sattvena āśraya antareṇa eva samaveta kārya janaka tva pratiṣedhāt asamavāyikāraṇañca vinā bhāvasya utpatteḥ adarśanāt anyasya ca asambhave sati kāraṇa akāraṇa saṃyogāt tasya utpattiḥ kalpyate iti śarīra ākāśa ādi samavāyi kāraṇam viśiṣṭā ca diś nimitta kāraṇam iti 
[II,084,24_II,085,6]	evam nirṇīte vibhāga ja vibhāge pūrva pakṣa vādī asat dūṣaṇam āha yadi kāraṇa vibhāga anantaram kārya vibhāga utpattiḥ kāraṇa saṃyogāt ca anantaram kārya saṃyoga utpattiḥ na sama kālam nanu evam avayava avayavinoḥ yuta siddhi doṣa prasaṅgaḥ iti na yuktam etat kutas yuta siddhi aparijñānāt na pareṇa yuta siddhiḥ vijñātā yatas evamāha iti tathā hi paraspara saṃyoga vibhāga yogya tā yuta siddhiḥ avayavānām hi padārtha antaraiḥ saṃyoga vibhāga yogya tā tathā avayavinaḥ sambhavati eva na tu parasparam iti avyabhicāraḥ sambhave vā yuta siddhiḥ eva iti na samavāyaḥ syāt asti ca asau iti vakṣyāmaḥ 
[II,085,14]	idantu sāmānya lakṣaṇam yuta siddheḥ viśeṣa lakṣaṇāt labhyate eva viśeṣasya sāmānya vyāpta tvāt iti viśeṣa lakṣaṇam āha sā punar dvayoḥ anyatarasya vā pṛthak gatimat tvam iti iyam nityānām yuta siddhiḥ dvayoḥ paramāṇvoḥ pṛthak gatimat tvam yuta siddhiḥ ākāśa paramāṇvoḥ ca anyatarasya pṛthak gatimat tvam iti tat ca parasparam saṃyoga vibhāga janana yogya tvam vivakṣitam anyathā hi dvi aṇuka ārambhakayoḥ paramāṇvaḥ rdvi aṇuke vrajati gamana upalabdheḥ dvi aṇukena saha yuta siddhiḥ syāt 
[II,085,20]	anityānāntu yuteṣu pṛthak bhūteṣu āśrayeṣu samavāyaḥ yuta siddhiḥ iti nanu evam api avayava avayavinoḥ yuta āśraya samavāyāt yuta siddhiḥ syāt tathā hi avayavī avayaveṣu vartate avayavāḥ ca sva avayaveṣu iti yuta āśraya samavāyaḥ na abhiprāya aparijñānāt yathā ghaṭa tad āśraya vyatirekeṇa āśraya antare samavāyaḥ paṭasya paṭa tat āśraya vyatirekeṇa ghaṭasya na evam avayavinaḥ avayava vyatirekeṇa āśraya antare samavāyaḥ tasmāt na yuta siddhiḥ atra api dvayoḥ yuta āśraya samavāyi tvam anyatarasya vā iti anuvartate dvayoḥ yathā ghaṭa paṭayoḥ anyatarasya yathā ākāśa ghaṭayoḥ anyatarasya ghaṭasya yuteṣu āśrayeṣu asamavāyaḥ na ākāśasya anāśrita tvāt 
[II,086,3_II,086,13]	nanu evam tarhi nityeṣu iva anityeṣu api pṛthak gatimat tvasya sambhavāt sā eva astu kṛtam yuta āśraya samavāyi tvena avyāpinā na etat evam anityeṣu pṛthak gatimat tvasya anvaya vyatireka abhāvāt yuta āśraya samavāyi tvam eva tad sadbhāvāt sā eva yuta siddhiḥ iti āha tvac indriya śarīrayoḥ pṛthak gatimat tvam na asti yuteṣu tu samavāyaḥ asti iti paraspareṇa saṃyogaḥ siddhaḥ tathā hi tvac indriya śarīra yoḥ āmaraṇam vibhāga anupapatteḥ pṛthak gati mat tva abhāve api paraspareṇa saṃyoga prasiddheḥ yuta āśraya samavāyi tvam eva yuta siddhiḥ tayoḥ itaretara āśraya parihāreṇa sva āśrayeṣu eva samavāyāt evam utpanna mātrasya ghaṭa ādeḥ gati mat tva abhāve api rūpa ādi utpatti sama kālam ākāśa ādinā saṃyoga upalabdheḥ anyatarasya yuta āśraya samavāyi tvam eva yuta siddhiḥ nityānāntu yuta āśraya samavāya abhāve api saṃyoga vibhāga upalabdheḥ pṛthak gatimat tvam eva yuta siddhiḥ iti āha aṇu ākāśayoḥ tu yuta āśraya samavāyi tva abhāve api anyatarasya pṛthak gatimat tvāt saṃyoga vibhāgau siddhau iti 
[II,086,16]	evam anityānām yuta āśraya samavāyi tvasya nityānāntu pṛthak gatimat tvasya anvaya upadarśana antaram vyatirekam āha tantu paṭayoḥ anityayoḥ āśraya antara abhāvāt parasparataḥ saṃyoga vibhāga abhāvaḥ iti yadi api tantavaḥ aṃśuṣu vartante tathā api paṭa dravye na tantu vyatirekeṇa āśraya antaram asti iti yuta āśraya samavāyi tva abhāvaḥ tad abhāvāt na paraspareṇa saṃyoga vibhāgau iti viśiṣṭañca pṛthak gatimat tvasya ghaṭa paramāṇu oḥ tu ubhaya sambhavāt ubhaya avarodhaḥ anyatara avarodhaḥ vā iti ubhaya avarodhaḥ iva anyatara avarodhe viśeṣa hetu abhāvāt tathā hi nitye paramāṇau pṛthak gatimat tvam anitye tu ghaṭe yuta āśraya samavāyi tvam ubhaya urubhayatra anvaya vyatirekābhyām samarthanāt atra sambhavena grahaṇam nyāyyam yatra ca anityam eva tatra pṛthak gatimat tva sadbhāve api yuta āśraya samavāyi tvasya avarodhaḥ yathā ghaṭa ākāśayoḥ dvayoḥ vā ghaṭayoḥ iti alam ati vistareṇa tasmāt kāraṇa vibhāga anantaram kārya vibhāgaḥ kāraṇa saṃyoga antaram kārya saṃyogaḥ yuta siddhiḥ iti aparijñāta yuta siddheḥ vacanam iti 
[II,087,2_II,087,6]	atha idānīm vināśam āha vināśaḥ tu sarvasya vibhāgasya kṣaṇika tvāt ityādinā nanu kṣaṇika tvam āśutara vināśi tvam tat ca vibhāgasya vināśe sādhye sādhyāt na viśiṣyate na vyavahārasya sādhya tvāt tathā hi vibhāgaḥ vināśī iti vyavahartavyaḥ kṣaṇika tvāt yat vā kṣaṇika tvam āśutara vināśa kāraṇa saṃyogi tvam tasmāt vibhāgasya vināśe sādhye na sādhya aviśiṣṭa tā atha kim tat vināśa kāraṇam uttara saṃyogaḥ katham uttara saṃyoga avadhi sadbhāvāt uttara saṃyogaḥ eva avadhiḥ sīmā sadbhāve yasya iti uttara saṃyogam yāvat sadbhāvaḥ tad anantaram abhāvaḥ iti anvaya vyatirekābhyām upalabdham na tu saṃyoga vat asya vināśaḥ iti yathā hi yayoḥ eva saṃyogaḥ tayoḥ eva vibhāgāt saṃyogasya vināśaḥ na evam yayoḥ eva vibhāgaḥ tayoḥ eva saṃyogāt vibhāgasya vināśaḥ kim tarhi tayoḥ anyena vā sva kāraṇa karma jaḥ tad saṃyoga jaḥ vā saṃyogaḥ astu tasmāt vinaśyati iti 
[II,087,18]	atha saṃyogasya vibhāga mātrāt avināśa vat vibhāgasya api saṃyoga mātreṇa avināśaḥ kim iti na iṣyate iti āha saṃyukta pratyaya vat vibhakta pratyaya anuvṛtti abhāvāt asya vināśa prasaṅgāt yathā hi saṃyoge vibhāga mātra utpāde saṃyukta pratyaya anuvṛttiḥ saṃyukta saṃyuktam iti dṛṣṭā na evam vibhāgasya saṃyoga mātra utpāde vibhakta pratyaya anuvṛttiḥ asti tasmāt uttara saṃyoga avadhi sadbhāvāt kṣaṇikaḥ iti upasaṃhāraḥ 
[II,087,24_II,088,13]	anye na tu saṃyoga vat avasthitaḥ vibhāgaḥ kasmāt yayoḥ eva saṃyogāt asya vināśa prasaṅgāt yathā hi avasthitaḥ saṃyogaḥ tayoḥ eva vibhāgāt nivartate vibhāgaḥ api evam tayoḥ eva saṃyogāt nivarteta iṣyate eva iti ced tat asat saṃyukta pratyaya vat vibhakta pratyaya anuvṛtti abhāvāt na hi artha antareṇa vibhāge saṃyukta pratyaya anuvṛtti vat artha antareṇa saṃyoge vibhakta pratyaya anuvṛttiḥ asti iti yat ca aprāpti jñānam tat bādhaka sadbhāvāt saṃyoga abhāve draṣṭavyam iti anyathā hi piṇḍasya deśa antara gamane maraṇe vā avasthita tvāt eka piṇḍa grahaṇe api grahaṇam syāt na ca etat asti tasmāt vidyamāna kriye dravye vibhakta pratyayaḥ mukhyaḥ anyadā tu tad sāmānyāt bhāktaḥ iti 
[II,089,1]	evam saṃyogāt vibhāgasya vināśam pratipādya āśraya vināśena vināśam āha kvacid ca āśraya vināśāt vinaśyati ityādinā katham iti avyutpanna praśna anantaram āha yadā dvi tantuka kāraṇa avayave aṃśau ityādi dvi tantukasya kāraṇam tantuḥ tasya avayavaḥ aṃśuḥ tasmin sva kāraṇāt karma utpannam yadā aṃśvantarāt vibhāgam ārabhate tasmin eva kāle tantu antare api karma utpadyate vibhāgāt ca tantu ārambhaka saṃyoga vināśaḥ tantu karmaṇā tantu antarāt vibhāgaḥ kriyate iti anayoḥ ekaḥ kālaḥ tatas yasmin eva kāle vibhāgāt tantu saṃyogasya dvi tantuka ārambhakasya vināśaḥ tasmin eva kāle tantu ārambhakasya aṃśu saṃyogasya vināśāt tantu vināśaḥ tasmin vinaṣṭe tad āśritasya tantu antara vibhāgasya vināśaḥ anyasya vināśa kāraṇasya abhāvāt tadā eva dvi tantukasya api āśraya vināśāt saṃyoga vināśāt ca vināśaḥ iti 
[II,089,13]	evam āśraya vināśāt vināśe abhihite aniṣṭam upapādayati evam tarhi uttara vibhāga anutpatti prasaṅgaḥ iti uttara vibhāgaḥ tantoḥ ākāśa ādi deśena vibhāgaḥ tasya anutpattiḥ kāraṇa vibhāga abhāvāt kāraṇayoḥ tantvoḥ vibhāgaḥ yat vā kāraṇañca tat vibhāgaḥ ca tasya dravya vināśa sama kālam abhāvāt ākāśa deśena vibhāgasya anutpattiḥ na ca saṃyoga vināśam apekṣya dravya vināśa sama kālam kāraṇa vibhāgasya vibhāga ārambhaka tvam vinaśyat avasthasya asamavāyi kāraṇa tva anabhyupagamāt yathā aśruta granthe vācā udyam etat 
[II,089,20^1]	tatas ca tantoḥ ākāśa ādi deśena vibhāga anutpāde tad saṃyogasya pratibandhakasya avasthānāt na karma uttara saṃyogam kuryāt iti āha pradeśa antara saṃyogavati saṃyoga abhāvaḥ iti atas pradeśa antara saṃyogasya virodhi guṇasya asambhavāt karmaṇaḥ kāla antara avasthāyi tvam tasya ca kṣaṇika tvam pramāṇa siddham iti vyāghātaḥ tathā nitya dravya samavetasya karmaṇaḥ nitya tvam iti doṣaḥ katham iti āha yadā dvi aṇuka ārambhaka paramāṇau sva kāraṇāt karma utpannam aṇu antarāt vibhāgam dravya ārambhaka saṃyoga virodhinam ārabhate tadā eva aṇu antare api anārambhake karma utpadyate tatas anantaram yasmin eva kāle vibhāgāt dravya ārambhaka saṃyogasya vināśaḥ tadā eva anārambha kāṇu karmaṇā dvi aṇukāṇvoḥ vibhāgaḥ kriyate 
[II,089,20^2]	tatas yasmin eva kāle vibhāgāt dvi aṇukasya aṇunā saṃyogasya vināśaḥ tasmin eva kāle saṃyogasya dravya ārambhakasya vināśāt dvi aṇukasya vināśaḥ tasmin dvi aṇuke vinaṣṭe tad āśritasya dvi aṇuka aṇu vibhāgasya vināśaḥ tatas kāraṇa vibhāga abhāvāt uttara vibhāga anutpattau tad saṃyogasya avyāvṛtteḥ na karma uttara saṃyogam karoti iti virodhi guṇasya asambhavāt paramāṇu samavetasya karmaṇaḥ nitya tvam syāt iti prāktana codyasya pratisamādhānam āha tantu aṃśu antara vibhāgāt vibhāgaḥ iti adoṣaḥ 
[II,090,11^1]	nanu tantu aṃśu vibhāgaḥ tantu kriyā kāryaḥ na bhavati eva aṃśoḥ dvi tantuka utpattau ākāśa ādi vat akāraṇa tvāt na api aṃśu kriyā kāryaḥ tantu utpattau tantu antarasya ākāśa vat eva akāraṇa tvāt kāraṇe ca utpannam karma kāraṇa antara vibhāga sama kāla kāraṇena vibhāgam na ārabhate viśiṣṭa vibhāga anutpatti prasaṅgāt iti uktam na ca kāraṇam vinā kāryam bhavati iti tantu aṃśu vibhāga asambhavaḥ eva na etat evam aṃśukriyā janitāt vibhāgāt tasya utpatti abhyupagamāt tathā hi 
[II,090,11^2]	aṃśu kriyā janitaḥ vibhāgaḥ saṃyoga vināśa viśiṣṭam kālam apekṣya tantu vināśa sama kālam ākāśa ādi deśena iva tantu antareṇa api vibhāgam ārabhate tantu vināśa viśiṣṭañca apekṣya dvi tantuka vināśa sama kālañca āśraya vināśāt tantvoḥ eva parasparam vibhāgaḥ vinaṣṭaḥ na tantu antara vibhāgaḥ aṃśukriyā janitāt vibhāgāt utpannaḥ vinaṣṭaḥ iti ekasmāt tantu antara vibhāgāt uttaraḥ vibhāgaḥ tantu ākāśa ādi vibhāgaḥ jāyate aṅguli ākāśa vibhāgāt śarīra ākāśa vibhāga vat iti udāharaṇam yathā aṅguli ākāśa ādi vibhāgāt hasta ākāśa vibhāgaḥ tasmāt ca vibhāgāt śarīra ākāśa vibhāgaḥ tadvat iha api aṃśu kriyā janitāt vibhāgāt tantu aṃśu vibhāgaḥ tasmāt ca vibhāgāt tantu ākāśa vibhāgaḥ jāyate iti tasmin utpanne prāktana saṃyogasya pratibandhakasya abhāvāt karma uttara saṃyogam kṛtvā tasmāt vinaśyati iti na kāla antara avasthāyi tvam doṣaḥ 
[II,091,1]	nanu etasmin pakṣe katham uttara saṃyogāt tantu ākāśa ādi vibhāgasya nivṛttiḥ tantu karmaṇā pāramparyeṇa api ajanita tvāt na vibhāga janite vibhāge niyama anupalabdheḥ anye tu tantau utpannā kriyā tantu antareṇa iva tad ārambhakeṇa aṃśunā api vibhāgam karoti eva pāramparyeṇa aṃśoḥ api kāraṇa tvāt ākāśa ādiḥ ca pāramparyeṇa api dvi tantuka utpattau akāraṇam iti tantu kriyā avayava antara vibhāga sama kālam na tena vibhāgam karoti iti yat vai aṃśu kriyā aṃśvantara ādi vat tantu antareṇa api vibhāgam ārabhate aṃśu kāryeṇa saha eva kārya ārambhaka tvāt atas ca āśraya vināśāt tantvoḥ eva vibhāgaḥ vinaṣṭaḥ na tu tantu antara vibhāgaḥ tasmāt tantu ākāśa ādi vibhāgaḥ jāyate aṅguli ākāśa ādi vibhāgāt śarīra ākāśa ādi vibhāga vat 
[II,091,11_II,091,17]	nanu aṅgulī ākāśa vibhāgāt hasta ākāśa vibhāgaḥ kāraṇa akāraṇa vibhāgasya kārya akārya vibhāga ārambhaka tvāt na tu aṅguleḥ śarīram kāryam iti atas yadi api aṅguli ākāśa vibhāgasya śarīra ākāśa vibhāgena saha ākāśa vṛtti tvāt pratyāsattiḥ asti tathā api akāraṇa tvam eva tasmāt śarīra ārambhaka tvāt upacāreṇa hastaḥ eva śarīram iti yuktam etāvat ca udāharaṇam yathā aṅgulī ākāśa vibhāgāt kāraṇa akāraṇa vibhāgāt hasta ākāśa vibhāgaḥ tathā tantu aṃśu vibhāgāt tantu ākāśa vibhāgaḥ iti 
[II,091,23_II,092,5]	atha vā iti vibhāgasya āśraya vināśena vināśe prakāra antara upanyāsaḥ na tu prakṛta ākṣepa samādhānam kāla antara avasthāyini dravye karmaṇaḥ kāla antara avasthāyitva udbhāvanāt atas aṃśvantara vibhāga utpatti sama kālam tasmin eva tantau vibhajyamāna aṃśau karma utpadyate tatas anantaram aṃśu vibhāgāt tantu ārambhaka saṃyoga vināśaḥ tantu karmaṇā ca tantu antarāt vibhāgaḥ kriyate iti ekaḥ kālaḥ tatas saṃyoga vināśāt tantu vināśaḥ tantu antara vibhāgāt ca tad saṃyoga vināśaḥ tatas dvi tantukasya ubhaya vināśāt vināśaḥ tantu vināśāt ca tad āśritayoḥ vibhāga karmaṇoḥ yugapad vināśaḥ iti 
[II,092,7]	atha nitya dravya samavetasya nitya tvam syāt iti ākṣepa pratisamādhāna dvārakam vākyam tantu vīraṇayoḥ vā ityādi yathā hi tantu vīraṇayoḥ saṃyoge sati dravya anutpattiḥ vijātīya tvāt evam dvi aṇukāṇvoḥ api saṃyogāt dravyam na utpadyate tathā hi eka dvi aṇukam anityam anyaḥ ca paramāṇuḥ nityam iti vijātīya tvam vijātīya saṃyogaḥ ca dravya anārambhakaḥ iti dvi aṇukāṇvoḥ saṃyoge api dravya anutpattau paramāṇau utpannam karma dravya ārambhaka saṃyoga virodhi vibhāga anutpādaka tvāt ākāśa dideśena api vibhāgam ārabhate vīraṇa karma vat evam prāktana saṃyoga nivṛttau uttara saṃyogam kṛtvā vinaśyati iti pūrva uktena vidhānena vināśaḥ 
[II,092,15]	yat vā pūrva ukta vidhānena iti ayam arthaḥ tantu ārambhake aṃśau karma utpatti sama kālam vīraṇe api karma aṃśu karmaṇā ca aṃśvantarāt vibhāgaḥ kriyate vīraṇa karmaṇā ca tantu antarāt iti ekaḥ kālaḥ tatas vibhāgāt aṃśu saṃyoga vināśe vīraṇa vibhāgāt ca vīraṇa tantu saṃyoga vināśaḥ tatas dravya ārambhaka saṃyoga vināśāt tantu vināśaḥ tantu vīraṇa saṃyoga vināśe ca uttara saṃyogaḥ tatas ca āśraya vināśa saṃyogābhyām tantu vīraṇa vibhāga vināśaḥ iti 
[II,092,21]	anye tu vā śabdasya upama artha tvāt tantu vīraṇayoḥ iva dvi aṇukāṇvoḥ saṃyoge sati dravyam na utpadyate dravya anutpattau ca dvi aṇukā aṇu vibhāgasya paramāṇu karmaṇā dvi aṇuka ārambhaka saṃyoga vināśa sama kālam janitasya katham vināśaḥ pūrva uktena vidhānena iti āśraya vināśena iti arthaḥ yadā tu paramāṇau karma utpattau paramāṇu antara vibhāga utpatti sama kālam asmin eva dvi aṇuke karma sañcintanam tadā pūrva uktena vidhānena āśraya vināśāt vibhāga karmaṇoḥ yugapad vināśaḥ iti dvi aṇuka ārambhake ca paramāṇau karma utpatti sama kālam anārambhake api karma sañcintanāt tad āśraya vināśa saṃyogābhyām tantu vīraṇa vibhāga vināśa vat vināśaḥ iti alam 
[II,093,5_II,093,8]	idānīm paratva aparatvayoḥ lakṣaṇa parīkṣā artham paratvam ityādi prakaraṇam abhidhānañca pratyayaḥ ca iti tayoḥ nimittam paratvam aparatvañcaḥ iti ukte ati prasaṅgaḥ tad artham parāpara grahaṇam tathā api para apara abhidhāna pratyaya nimitta tvam ākāśa ātmanoḥ na vyāvṛttam iti viśeṣaṇa tve satī iti ūhyam tathā sāmānyam api viśeṣaṇa tve sati para apara abhidhāna pratyaya nimittam atas dravya grahaṇam tathā hi paratva aparatve anyasmāt bhidyate dravya viśeṣaṇa tve sati para apara abhidhāna pratyaya nimitta tvāt yaḥ tu itarāt na bhidyate na ca asau evam yathā rūpa ādiḥ iti vyavahāraḥ vā sādhyaḥ atra ca abhidhāna padena saṃkhyā ādi lakṣaṇeṣu api karaṇa vyutpattyā abhidhānam bhāva vyutpattyā ca jñānam iti ubhaya rūpaḥ vyavahāraḥ pratyayaḥ ca vivakṣitaḥ iti jñāpayati ekasmin ca prakaraṇe guṇa dvaya nirūpaṇam eka utpatteḥ itaropāya āpekṣika tvāt pṛthak abhidhāne tu grantha bahu tvam syāt iti saṅgraha tvāt ekadā abhidhānam 
[II,093,19]	paratva aparatvayoḥ sadbhāve kim pramāṇam iti apekṣāyām paratvam aparatvañca para apara abhidhāna pratyaya nimittam iti vākyam parīkṣā paratvena ca yojanīyam tathā hi para apara abhidhāna pratyayaḥ viśeṣaṇa pūrvakaḥ viśeṣya abhidhāna pratyaya tvāt daṇḍī iti viśeṣya abhidhāna pratyaya vat na ca rūpa ādīnām anyatamam viśeṣaṇam tad vyavahāra vilakṣaṇa tvāt abādhyamānañca jñānam nimittam vinā na sambhavati eva vāsanā tu nimittam tatra na bhavati iti uktam atha dravyam eva viśiṣṭa utpāda vaśāt parāpara vyavahāra janakam tat na kṣaṇika tva pratiṣedhāt abhyupagamena tu ucyate viśiṣṭa tāyāḥ vyatireka abhyupagame viśiṣṭa vyavahāra janaka tve ca saṃjñā bheda mātram avyatireketu samāna deśa avasthita piṇḍhe samāna vayasi ca parāpara vyavahāraḥ syāt dravya sadbhāvasya aviśeṣāt atas para apara vyavahāre rūpa ādi vilakṣaṇam nimittam asti iti jñātam 
[II,094,4_II,094,17]	tat dvividham kāraṇa bhedāt iti āha diś kṛtam kāla kṛtañcaḥ iti nanu diś kālayoḥ sarva utpattimatām nimitti kāraṇa tva abhidhānāt viśeṣa abhidhānā sambhavaḥ eva na diś kāla piṇḍa saṃyogayoḥ tad śabda vācya tvena tad kṛta tva upapatteḥ dikpiṇḍa saṃyoga kṛtam dikkṛtam kāla piṇḍa saṃyoga kṛtañca kāla kṛtam iti tathā anayoḥ parasparam bhedam āha tatra diś kṛtam deśa viśeṣa pratyāyakam iti deśa viśeṣaḥ pratyāyakaḥ asya iti deśe viśeṣam vā pratyāyayati iti kāla kṛtāt bhidyate kāla kṛtañca vayaḥ bheda pratyāyakam iti vayaḥ bhedaḥ pratyāyakaḥ yasya iti vayaḥ bheda pratyāyakam vayaḥ bhedam vā pratyāyayati iti diś kṛtāt bhidyate 
[II,094,20]	tatra dikkṛtasya utpattiḥ abhidhīyate katham iti avyutpanna praśna anantaram āha ekasyām diśi avasthitayoḥ piṇḍayoḥ ityādi piṇḍayoḥ iti samavāyi kāraṇa nirdeśaḥ ekasyām diśi avasthitayoḥ na vibhinna diśi avasthitayoḥ iti niyama pratipādanam saṃyukta saṃyoga bahu alpa bhāve sati iti bhū pradeśān adhikṛtya etat saṃyuktena saha saṃyogāḥ teṣām bahu alpa bhāvaḥ iti ekasmin piṇḍe saṃyukta saṃyoga alpīyaḥ tvam anyasmin tatas bahu tvam tasmin sati ekasya draṣṭuḥ na vibhinnasya sannikṛṣṭam avadhim kṛtvā etasmāt viprakṛṣṭaḥ ayam iti paratva ādhāre utpatsyamāna paratve buddhiḥ utpadyate tām apekṣya pareṇa diś pradeśena saṃyogāt paratva utpattiḥ iti diś pradeśayoḥ para apara vyapadeśaḥ tad sampādaka tvāt upacāreṇa 
[II,095,4_II,095,8]	viprakṛṣṭañca piṇḍam avadhim kṛtvā itarasmin piṇḍa saṃyukta saṃyoga alpīyaḥ tvāt nimittāt sannikṛṣṭā buddhiḥ utpadyate tām sannikṛṣṭām buddhim apekṣya apareṇa diś pradeśena yogāt paratva utpattiḥ iti piṇḍaḥ samavāyi kāraṇam diś piṇḍa saṃyogaḥ asamavāyi kāraṇam viśiṣṭā ca buddhiḥ nimitta kāraṇam iti nanu ca atra sannikṛṣṭam avadhim kṛtvā viprakṛṣṭe buddhiḥ viprakṛṣṭañca avadhim kṛtvā sannikṛṣṭe buddhiḥ iti viprakṛṣṭa sannikṛṣṭa buddhyoḥ paraspara apekṣi tvāt ubhaya abhāva prasaṅgaḥ tat na nirvikalpaka jñāne pratibhātasya avadhi tvena abhyupagamāt tathā hi sannikṛṣṭa viprakṛṣṭayoḥ pratyakṣeṇa eva nirvikalpaka avabhāse sati etasmāt ayam sannikṛṣṭaḥ viprakṛṣṭaḥ ca iti sa vikalpakam jñānam bhavati eva 
[II,095,13_II,095,21^1]	anye tu nirvikalpa avabhāsa janita saṃskāra ja smṛti upasthāpitayoḥ sannikṛṣṭa viprakṛṣṭayoḥ paraspara avadhibhāvaḥ ghaṭataḥ iti bruvate tasmāt na paraspara apekṣita tvāt ubhaya abhāvaḥ iti sthitam kāla kṛtayoḥ api paratva aparatvayoḥ katham utpattiḥ iti āha vartamāna kālayoḥ ityādi vartamānaḥ kālaḥ yayoḥ piṇḍayoḥ tau ca tathā uktau tayoḥ iti ubhayatra api diś kāla kṛta paratva aparatvayoḥ utpattau niyamaḥ aniyata diś deśayoḥ iti na niyataḥ diś deśaḥ yayoḥ tau tathā uktau tayoḥ iti kāla kṛtayoḥ utpattau aniyama upadarśanam yuvasthavirayoḥ iti vayaḥ bheda upadarśana artham samāna vayasi para apara vyavahāra adarśanāt rūḍha śmaśru kārkaśyavali palita ādi sānnidhye sati rūḍha śmaśru ca kārkaśyañca valayaḥ ca palitāni ca tāni ādiḥ yeṣām tāni tathā uktāni teṣām sānnidhye sati iti rūḍha śmaśru kārka śyā ādi sānnidhyam sannikṛṣṭa buddheḥ kāraṇam 
[II,095,21^2]	valī palita ādi sānnidhyañca viprakṛṣṭa buddheḥ iti ekasya draṣṭuḥ iti yaḥ hi draṣṭā paratva aparatve draṣṭum abhivāñchati tasya yuvānam avadhim kṛtvā sthavire viprakṛṣṭā buddhiḥ utpadyate tām viprakṛṣṭām buddhim apekṣya pareṇa kāla pradeśena yogāt paratvasya utpattiḥ iti viprakṛṣṭañca sthaviram avadhim kṛtvā yūni etasmāt sthavira āt ayam sannikṛṣṭaḥ iti sannikṛṣṭā buddhiḥ utpadyate tām apekṣya apareṇa kāla pradeśena saṃyogāt aparatvasya utpattiḥ iti sannikṛṣṭa viprakṛṣṭa piṇḍayoḥ samavāyi kāraṇa tvam kāla piṇḍayoḥ saṃyogasya ca asamavāyi kāraṇa tvam sannikṛṣṭa viprakṛṣṭa buddhyoḥ ca nimitta kāraṇa tvam iti 
[II,096,12]	nanu ca ayuktam etat āhāra upayoge sati pākaja utpatti nyāyena ekasmin ahani upajāta tva aviśeṣeṇa sannikṛṣṭa viprakṛṣṭa buddhyoḥ abhāvāt paratva aparatvayoḥ asambhavaḥ na etat evam janmanaḥ prabhṛti ekasyām śarīra santatau āditya parivartana apekṣayā tad upapatteḥ tathā hi ekasya januḥ prabhṛti bhūyāṃsi āditya parivartanāni aparasya alpīyāṃsi iti tad apekṣayā sannikṛṣṭa viprakṛṣṭa buddhyoḥ bhāvaḥ sthavire bhūyāṃsi āditya parivartanāni iti viprakṛṣṭa buddhiḥ yūni ca alpīyāṃsi iti sannikṛṣṭa buddhiḥ tad apekṣayā paratva aparatvayoḥ utpattiḥ iti śarīra santānasya āditya parivartana apekṣayā ghaṭataḥ eva etat dikkṛta paratva aparatva vailakṣaṇī añca anayoḥ nimitta antarā sambhave sati kāla kṛta tvam iṣṭam na hi tasmāt eva nimittāt vyatikaraḥ sambhavati iti 
[II,096,21_II,097,4^1]	tat evam paratva aparatvayoḥ utpāde vyavasthite sūtreṇa abhisambandha upadarśanañca tathā ca sūtram eka dikkā ālābhyām sannikṛṣṭa viprakṛṣṭābhyām parama parañcaḥ iti ekā diś kālaḥ ca yayoḥ tau tathā uktau tābhyām iti samavāyi kāraṇa nirdeśaḥ eka digbhyām iti diś kṛta paratva aparatva apekṣayā eva niyamaḥ eka kālābhyām vartamāna kālābhyām ubhayatra api iti na hi asadbhyām sat asat bhyāñca paratva aparatve jāyate sannikṛṣṭa viprakṛṣṭābhyām iti samavāyi kāraṇa upasarjana tayā sannikṛṣṭa viprakṛṣṭa buddhyoḥ nimitta kāraṇa tvam uktam eva tathā hi parama parañca iti buddhi apekṣam iti apekṣā śabdaḥ ca atra kāraṇe vartate iti kāraṇa para tvāt kāraṇa apara tvāt ca paratva aparatve iti asamavāyi kāraṇam darśayati nanu ca kāraṇa para tvāt kāraṇa apara tvāt ca yadi kārye paratva aparatve bhavataḥ tarhi rūpa ādi vat cira utpanna tvāt sannikṛṣṭa viprakṛṣṭa buddhim vinā api samāne deśe samāne vayasi ca piṇḍe tayoḥ grahaṇam syāt na ca etat asti atha anabhivyaktitaḥ anupalabdhiḥ 
[II,097,4^2]	tat na sadbhāve pramāṇa abhāvāt sannikṛṣṭa viprakṛṣṭa buddhi ādi sadbhāve ca idānīm utpanna mātrasya api grahaṇam upapadyate eva tasmāt diś piṇḍa saṃyogaḥ kāla piṇḍa saṃyogaḥ ca paratva aparatva sampādaka tvāt upacāreṇa paratva aparatve iti abhidhīyate na ca paratva aparatvayoḥ paraspara apekṣita tvāt asambaddham utpatti ādi nirūpaṇam iti vācyam sarvatra paraspara apekṣita tva anupalabdheḥ tathā hi na bīja aṅkurayoḥ paraspara apekṣi tvam bīja vināśe sati kāla antare dvi aṇuka ādi prakrameṇa aṅkurasya utpatteḥ evam aṅkura vināśe sati uttarottara kāryāṇām pūrva pūrva vināśe sati bhāvāt na aṅkurāt bījam iti paraspara apekṣi tva abhāvaḥ tathā pitṛ putrayoḥ dharma śarīrayoḥ ca na paraspara apekṣi tvam yatas eva upalabdhiḥ tad kāraṇa tva anupalabdheḥ kārya antare tu kāraṇa tvam na pratiṣidhyate iti alam ati prasaṅgena 
[II,097,17_II,097,26]	tat evam paratva aparatvayoḥ utpattimat tvāt avaśyam vināśaḥ iti tasya sa hetuka tvāt kāraṇam vācyam iti āha vināśaḥ tu apekṣā buddhi saṃyoga dravya vināśāt iti tredhā tritaya vināśāt ca aparaḥ pakṣaḥ iti saptadhā vināśaḥ tatra apekṣā buddhi vināśāt tāvat vināśam āha utpanne paratve sva kāraṇāt viśeṣaṇa tvāt pūrvam tad saṃyukta samaveta samavāyāt sāmānya buddhiḥ utpadyate sā ca yasmin kāle samutpannā bhavati tadā eva tad sāmānya jñānāt apekṣā buddheḥ vinaśyattā vināśa kāraṇa sānnidhyam sāmānya tad jñāna tad sambandhebhyaḥ paratva guṇa buddheḥ utpadyamāna tā utpatti kāraṇa sānnidhyam iti ekaḥ kālaḥ tatas apekṣā buddheḥ vināśaḥ guṇa jñānasya utpādaḥ apekṣā buddhi vināśāt guṇasya vinaśyattā sāmānya jñānasya vinaśyattā guṇāḥ ca tat jñānañca tad sambandhaḥ ca iti tebhyaḥ dravya buddheḥ utpadyamāna tā iti ekaḥ kālaḥ tatas dravya buddheḥ utpattiḥ apekṣā buddhi vināśāt guṇasya ca vināśaḥ anyasya vināśa kāraṇasya anupalabdheḥ 
[II,098,9_II,098,24]	saṃyoga vināśāt api katham vināśaḥ iti avyutpanna praśna anantaram āha apekṣā buddhi sama kālam eva paratva aparatva ādhāre karma utpadyate vibhāga paratva aparatvayoḥ utpadyamāna tā iti ekaḥ kālaḥ tatas tena karmaṇā diś piṇḍa vibhāgaḥ kriyate paratvasya ca utpattiḥ sāmānya buddheḥ utpadyamāna tā diś piṇḍa saṃyogasya vinaśyattā tatas sāmānya buddheḥ utpattiḥ dikpiṇḍa saṃyogasya ca vināśaḥ sāmānya jñānāt apekṣā buddheḥ vinaśyattā guṇa buddheḥ utpadyamāna tā saṃyoga vināśāt guṇasya vinaśyattā tatas yasmin kāle guṇa buddhiḥ utpadyate tasmin eva kāle diś piṇḍa saṃyogasya asamavāyi kāraṇasya vināśāt guṇasya paratvasya vināśaḥ
