[II,104,20]	yat ca idam puruṣasya bhoga utsuka tām manyamānāyāḥ buddheḥ ākṛtiḥ sampadyate tad saṃvedanāt ca indriyāṇām iti asat etat acetana tvāt acetanā hi buddhiḥ tathā indriyāṇi teṣām ākūta saṃvedana abhāve katham niyataḥ viṣaya ākāra tayā pariṇāmaḥ puruṣasya tu cit rūpa tā vyatirekeṇa na aparā bhoga utsukatā asti yaḥ ca ayam indriyāṇām viṣaya ākāra pariṇāmaḥ tasya viṣaya ākāra tāyām na pratikarma vyavasthā pramāṇam tad antareṇa api tad bhāvāt iti vakṣyamāṇa nyāyāt yadi ca buddheḥ pūrvarūpa nivṛttau indriya ākāratayā pariṇāmaḥ tarhi svarūpasya avyatirekāt buddheḥ eva utpattiḥ nivṛttiḥ ca iti anya tve pratisandhāna ādi abhāvaḥ eva na hi ekena upalabdham artham anyaḥ pratisandhātum arhati iti pariṇāmāḥ tu buddheḥ tādātmyena vartante iti teṣām aneka tve buddheḥ api aneka tvam viparyaye tādātmya virahāt 
[II,105,3_II,105,7]	yat api idam buddheḥ pariṇāma viśeṣāḥ pañcāśat pratyayāḥ tad abuddhi pūrvakam tad pariṇāma viśeṣānām ānantyāt na ca teṣām eṣu eva antarbhāvaḥ pratiniyata lakṣaṇa avarodhasya anupalabdheḥ iti alam ati prasaṅgena tat evam buddhi ādi paryāyāḥ para pakṣa vyudāse sati lakṣaṇam iṣyante iti sthite lakṣaṇena lakṣyamāṇasya eka aneka tva upalabdheḥ vipratipatteḥ ca saṃśaye sati tad nirāsa artham sā ca aneka prakārāḥ iti vākyam kutas etat artha anantyāt prati artha niyata tvāt ca 
[II,105,11]	nanu ca artha ānantyam artha dharmaḥ iti vyadhikaraṇa tvam na anyathā tad upapatteḥ tathā hi buddheḥ artha ānantyam iti artha upadarśanam etat sādhanañca ananta artha tvāt iti arthaḥ anantaḥ yasyāḥ sā tathā uktā tasyāḥ bhāvaḥ ananta artha tvam iti arthaḥ tu arthyate anena iti kāraka sāmagryam na kāraka eka deśaḥ tad bhede api kāryasya abheda upalabdheḥ tathā hi aneka kāraka sampādyam ghaṭa ādi ekam dṛṣṭam iti sāmagrī tu pratikārya niyata tvāt na tad bhedam vyabhicarati iti atas aneka prakārāḥ buddhiḥ ananta artha tvāt ananta kāraka sāmagrī janya tvāt ghaṭa ādi vat iti yaḥ ca ekaḥ na ca asau ananta kāraka sāmagrī janyaḥ yathā ghaṭaḥ iti na tu karma vyutpattyai ananta karma kāraka janya tvam sādhanam vivakṣitam iti vyākhyeyam pratyartha niyata tvāt iti anena gata artha tvāt tathā hi artham artham prati niyatam yāvat bheda bhinnam karma kārakam tāvat bheda bhinnā buddhayaḥ iti buddhiḥ aneka prakārā pratyartha niyata tvāt ghrāṇa ādi vat 
[II,105,22]	anye tu pūrvasmin eva vākye karma vyutpattyā ananta karma kāraka janya tvam sādhanam labhyate eva iti pratyartha niyata tvam pratyātma vṛtti tvam vivakṣitam iti manyante tathā hi arthate asmin ityātmā iti arthaḥ tam prati niyata tvam pratyātma vṛtti tvam eva sāmānyasya tu ananta ātma vṛtti tvāt na pratyātma niyata tvam asti iti sambhave api buddheḥ viśeṣa guṇa tvāt viśeṣa guṇa tve sati iti viśeṣaṇam abhyūhyam 
[II,106,1]	anye tu rūpa jñānam rasa jñānam ityādi buddheḥ nānātvasya pratyakṣeṇa eva prasiddheḥ īśvara buddheḥ asmad buddheḥ ca paraspara bheda jñāpana artham artha anantyāt prati artha niyata tvāt ca iti pada dvayam iti bruvate tathā hi īśvara buddhiḥ ananta artha tvāt asmad buddheḥ bhidyate asmad buddhiḥ ca pratyartha niyata tvāt īśvara buddheḥ iti atra ca buddheḥ aneka tvam sāmānyena pratijñātam iti ayam viśeṣaḥ kutas labhyate iti cintyam 
[II,106,6]	atha buddhi vyatirekeṇa arthasya sadbhāve pramāṇa abhāvāt ayuktam artha ānantyam pratyartha niyata tvañca iti tathā hi vijñānam svayam prakāśa rūpa tvāt ātmānam prakāśayati arthāḥ tu jaḍa ātmānaḥ teṣām katham prakāśaḥ yadi jñānam pragṛhītam prakāśakamiṣyeta tasya api jñāna antareṇa grahaṇa abhyupagame jñāna paramparāyām upakṣīṇa tvāt abhipretasya arthasya aprakāśanam eva na ca pūrva jñāna agrahaṇe api arthasya eva grahaṇam iti vācyam teṣām āsanna tve sati grāhya lakṣaṇa prāpta tvāt tat āha tām grāhya lakṣaṇa prāptām āsannām janikām dhiyam agṛhītvā uttaram jñānam gṛhaṇīyāt aparam katham 
[II,106,14_II,106,26]	atha agṛhītam eva artha prakāśakam evam tarhi santāna antara udbhūtānām api sarveṣām prakāśakam syāt yathā hi svasantatau upajātam ajñātam eva artha prakāśakam evam santāna antare api syāt aviśeṣāt atha sva samvedya svasantatau vijñānam artha prakāśakam evam tarhi bodha śarīrāt artha antarasya vastunaḥ aprakāśaḥ eva tathā hi yadi amī padārthāḥ prakāśa rūpāḥ katham bodhāt vyatiricyante bodhasya eva tad rūpa tvāt aprakāśa rūpa tayā ca sarvadā na prakāśaḥ syāt atas jñānam eva prakāśa svarūpa tvāt iti vyavahriyate prakāśa rūpa tayā hi sattvam vyāptam sā ca vyāvartamānā bāhya arthebhyaḥ sva vyāptam sattvam gṛhītvā vyāvartate iti asattvam bodha vyatirekiṇām na ca bodhasya bodha rūpa tayā sarvatra aviśeṣāt viśiṣṭa artha prakāśaka tvam syāt atha nīlasya idam pītasya idam iti pratikarma vyavasthātaḥ sa ākāram vijñānam iṣṭam tarhi vijñānam eva astu tad ākāra malam bāhya artha kalpanayā iti tat uktam dhiyaḥ nīla ādi rūpa tve bāhyaḥ arthaḥ kiṃnibandhanaḥ iti 
[II,107,1]	tathā vijñāna kāle arthasya asadbhāvāt artha kāle tu jñānasya iti katham tayoḥ grāhya grāhaka bhāvaḥ sat asat rūpayoḥ tad abhāvāt ekasmin ca kāle dvayoḥ utpatti abhyupagame kim grāhyam kiñca grāhakam iti aviśeṣāt na ca vijñāna arthayoḥ sva ātmani eva paryavasāne artha adhīna tāyāḥ pratipattum aśakya tvāt grāhya grāhaka bhāvaḥ tathā avayavi pratiṣedha dvāreṇa rūpa ādi samudāya mātram tat ca samudīyamānebhyaḥ na artha antaram iti vyavasthāyām artha abhāvaḥ eva samudāyasya parama artha sattvena apratibhāsanāt ye tu parama artha santaḥ paramāṇavaḥ te asmad darśana viṣayāḥ na bhavanti eva atīndriya tvāt kāryañca aparama artha sattvāt pratibhāsamānam aliṅgam eva tasmāt anādi vāsanā vaśāt vijñāna aṃśaḥ eva grāhya grāhaka pravibhāgaḥ etat āha avibhāgaḥ api buddhi ātmā viparyāsita darśanaiḥ grāhya grāhaka saṃvitti bhedavān iva lakṣyate na tu paramārthataḥ tat āha na anyaḥ anubhāvyaḥ buddhyā asti tasyāḥ na anubhavaḥ aparaḥ grāhya grāhaka vaidhuryāt svayam sā eva prakāśate 
[II,107,15]	nanu tarhi nīlam aham vedmi cakṣuṣā iti pratibhāsaḥ katham tathā hi nīlam iti karma aham iti kartā vedmi iti kriyā cakṣuṣā iti karaṇam eteṣām paraspara vyāvṛtta vapuṣām pratibhāsanāt abheda pratipādanam unmatta bhāṣitam na etat evam taimirikasya dvi candra darśana vadasya api upapatteḥ yathā hi taimirikasya artha abhāve api tad ākāram vijñānam udeti evam karma ādiṣu avidyamāneṣu api anādi vāsanā vaśāt tad ākāram vijñānam iti atha taimirikasya keśa ādi jñānam bādhyamāna tvāt nirviṣayam na ca evam etat tat asat bādhya bādhaka bhāvasya eva asambhavāt tathā hi na vijñānam arthena bādhyate pratīyamānā pratīyamānābhyām bādhya tve ati prasaṅgāt pratīyamānena hi bādhāyām sarvam vijñānam bādhyam syāt evam apratīyamānena api iti 
[II,107,24]	atha jñānena eva jñānam bādhyate tatra api na vibhinna viṣayeṇa rūpa jñānena rasa ādi jñānasya api bādha prasaṅgāt samāna viṣaya tve tu sampādaka tvam eva syāt na bādhaka tvam na ca vijñānasya utpattiḥ vināśaḥ vā bādhāt sarvasya api tathā abhāva prasaṅgāt atha viṣaya antara upasarpaṇā mithyāpattiḥ bādhaḥ tat asat viṣayasya karma kāraka rūpa tvāt yatra utpadyate jñānam saḥ eva tasya viṣayaḥ iti viṣaya antara upasarpaṇam asiddham vijñāne bādhya bādhaka sadbhāvasya eva aprasiddheḥ na mithyājñānam asti iti na api saṃvidi samyak tvam pramāṇa abhāvāt 
[II,108,5]	atha artha kriyā saṃvādaḥ pramāṇam na tatra api saṃvādaka apekṣāyām anavasthā prasaṅgāt saṃvāda kañca vinā na samyaktva siddhiḥ iti na ca artha kriyā api bodhāt bhidyate sarvasya api pratibhāsamānasya bodhāt avyatirekāt yathā uktam prakāśamānaḥ tādātmyāt svarūpasya prakāśakaḥ yathā prakāśaḥ abhimataḥ tathā dhīḥ a ātma vedinī iti 
[II,108,11_II,108,15]	yadi ca padārthānām nijam sva rūpa ādi yathā ekasya pratibhāsaḥ tathā sarveṣām api iti visaṃvādaḥ na syāt na ca etat asti tathā hi mantra ādi upapluta akṣāṇām yathā mṛd śakala ādayaḥ anyathā eva avabhāsante tad rūpa rahitāḥ api iti atha ca upapluta cakṣuṣām anyathā pratibhāsaḥ tatas iti kim pramāṇam anupapluta cakṣuṣām tathā eva darśanam iti tat āha tathā eva darśanāt teṣām anupapluta cakṣuṣām dūre yathā vā maruṣu mahān alpaḥ api dṛśyate iti 
[II,108,19]	avyavasthām eva uttara ardhena darśayati evam ekaśas buddhyā vicāryamāṇeṣu bhāveṣu rūpam na vyavatiṣṭhate yathā hi tantuṣu vicāryamāṇeṣu paṭasya avyavasthānam aṃśu vyatirekeṇa tantūnām ityādyūhyam katham tarhi śākyāḥ snāna ādi kriyāsu pravartante bāhya arthasya asattvāt iti loka vyavahāra anusāritayā yathā hi aparīkṣakāḥ bāhyam artham avidyā vaśāt pratipadyamānāḥ pravartante tadvat parīkṣakā api iti loka vyavahāram prati sadṛśau bāla paṇḍitau iti nyāyāt 
[II,108,25]	tat etat asat artha viśeṣāt utpattim antareṇa buddhi viśeṣasya abhāva prasaṅgāt rūpa jñānam rasa jñānam ityādi parasparam vyāvṛtta svarūpāṇi jñānāni prathantaḥ iti artha viśeṣaḥ abhyupagantavyaḥ atha vāsanā viśeṣāt vijñāna viśeṣaḥ tasyāḥ api viśiṣṭa jñāna janaka tve api jñānāt vyatireke ca saṃjñā bheda mātram avyatireke tu jñāna rūpa ubhayam sarvatra aviśiṣṭam iti rūpa jñānam rasa jñānam ityādi vaicitrya abhāvaḥ na ca ākāra viśeṣāt vijñāna viśeṣaḥ tasya api asambhavāt tathā hi jñāna mātrasya vāstava ākāra tāyām nīla ādi jñānam vāstava ākāra tvāt pramāṇam dvi candra ādi jñānañcau āḥ tava ākāra tvāt apramāṇam iti viśeṣa vyāghātaḥ vāstava ākāra tāyāḥ sarvatra aviśeṣāt atha āvāstava ākāram tathā api viśeṣa abhyupagama hāniḥ vādi prativādinoḥ ca jaya parājaya vyavasthā na syāt ubhayoḥ apramāṇena pravṛtteḥ aviśeṣāt 
[II,109,10_II,109,14]	na ca avāstavasya vijñāna tādātmyam sat asat rūpayoḥ khara viṣāṇayoḥ ivā eka tva adarśanāt atas eva saha upalambha niyamāt abhedaḥ nīla tad dhiyoḥ iti eka tva sādhanam unmatta bhāṣitam asataḥ sat tādātmye sattvam asat tādātmye tu tad rūpa tvam iti tathā para prasiddhyā niyamena saha upalabhyamāna tvam bhedena eva vyāptam iti viruddham syāt atha sāhāyyam yaugapadyam vā vivakṣitam saha upalabhyamāna tvam tathā api tayoḥ bhedena eva vyāpta tvāt viruddha tvam tathā sarvajñaḥ sva cittena saha upalabhate para cittam na ca tasya tasmāt abhedaḥ iti vyabhicāraḥ sarveṣām sarvajña tā prasaṅgāt na ca ekasya eva upalambha niyamaḥ hetuḥ aśabda artha tvāt sādhya aviśiṣṭa tvāt ca tathā aneka rūpa ādi avayavasya hi tasya arthasya upalambhe svarūpa asiddhaḥ api iti 
[II,109,22]	atha bāhya artha abhāvāt eka upalambha niyamaḥ tat na itaretara āśraya tva prasaṅgāt tathā ca eka upalambha niyamāt bāhya artha abhāva siddhiḥ tad siddheḥ ca eka upalambha niyama siddhiḥ iti eka abhāva āditara abhāvaḥ atha ekena eva upalabhyamāna tvam sādhanam na anya vedanā bhāvasya aprasiddheḥ arthaḥ tu tad samāna kṣaṇaiḥ anyaiḥ api upalabhyate iti ekena eva upalabhyamāna tvam asiddham sat candra asat candra dṛṣṭāntaḥ sat asatoḥ eka tva virodhāt sādhya vikalaḥ sādhana vikalaḥ ca asataḥ candrasya sattvena upalambha abhāvāt 
[II,110,1]	tathā jñānam grāhaka svarūpam nīla ādi grāhya svarūpam iti anayoḥ śukla pītayoḥ iva svabhāva bhedāt bhedaḥ abhede hi bodhaḥ api nīlasya grāhyaḥ nīlañca bodhasya grāhakam iti syāt na ca etat asti kāraṇa bhedāt ca nīlāt bodhaḥ artha antaram tathā hi bodhāt bodha rūpa tā indriyāt viṣaya pratiniyamaḥ viṣayāt ākāra grahaṇam iti bhedāt eṣām bhedaḥ eva atha na kāraṇa bhedaḥ kim tarhi vyāvṛtti bheda mātram abodha vyāvṛttiḥ bodhaḥ nirākāra tā vyāvṛttiḥ sa ākāra tvam atad rūpa vyāvṛttiḥ viṣaya pratiniyamaḥ iti evam tarhi nīla avabodha cakṣuṣām ākāra bodha viṣaya pratiniyameṣu vyāvṛtti svarūpeṣu vyāpāra asambhavāt akāraṇa tvam eva vyāvṛtteḥ avastu rūpa tvāt atha vyāvṛttāt bodhāt abodha ādi vyāvṛttiḥ na anyā tarhi bodhasya eka rūpa tvāt kāraṇa bheda pratipādanam asambaddham syāt atas kāraṇa bhedāt eva nīla tad bodhayoḥ bhedaḥ citra pratibhāse tu nīla pīta ādi aneka ākāram vijñānam bodha mātra tāyām katham syāt iti cintyam tathā hi teṣām ākārāṇām eka bodha tādātmyāt eka tvam tad tādātmye vā bodhasya aneka tvam iti durnivāraḥ prasaṅgaḥ 
[II,110,15]	atha yāvantaḥ tatra ākārāḥ tāvanti eva jñānāni iti tarhi teṣām pratiniyata ākāra tvāt citra pratibhāsā bhāvaḥ na ca ākāra sadbhāve pratikarma vyavasthā pramāṇam anyathā api bhāvāt tathā hi sakala kāraka janya tva aviśeṣe api nīlasya karma rūpa tayā vyāpārāt tena eva vyapadeśaḥ na ākāra arpaka tvāt iti sarveṣām janakatvā aviśeṣe api arthasya eva ākāra arpaka tve viśeṣa hetuḥ vācyaḥ atha arthasya karma rūpa tayā vyāpārāt tasya eva ākāra arpaka tvam tarhi karma rūpa tā eva astu vyapadeśa niyame hetuḥ kim ākāreṇa asambhavinā kalpitena iti tathā hi nīla ādeḥ asādhāraṇa ākāra arpaka tve bodha rūpa tā na syāt sādhāraṇa ākāra arpaka tve tu pratikarma vyavasthā bhāvaḥ iti 
[II,110,23]	atha samāropita ākāram vijñānam iti na ayam doṣaḥ tat asat ātmanaḥ avasthitasya abhāve katham jñāna ātmani ākāraḥ samāropyate na tāvat anutpannasya vinaṣṭasya vā samāropaka tvam na ca utpatti sama kālam ātma lābha kāle samāropaṇe vyāpāra asambhavāt tasmāt ākāra sadbhāve pramāṇa abhāvāt artha viśeṣāt eva ayam viśeṣaḥ iti yuktam 
[II,111,1]	atha aprakāśa svarūpa tvāt arthānām kathaṃprakāśaḥ tad viṣaya jñāna utpādaḥ eva tathā hi yasmin viṣaye jñānam utpannam saḥ eva upalabdhaḥ na itaraḥ iti viṣaya viṣayi bhāvasya niyāmaka tvam atas jñānam artha prakāśaḥ na tu prakāśakam iti kim gṛhītam artha prakāśakam uta agṛhītam ityādi vikalpaḥ parama tā sparśī cakṣuḥ ādeḥ kāraka jātasya artha prakāśaka tva abhyupagamāt yatra ca jñānam viśeṣa liṅgam vā tatra gṛhītasya artha paricchede vyāpāraḥ abhyupagamyate eva tasya ca ātma antaḥkaraṇa sambandhāt grahaṇam na avaśyam tatra api jñāna antaram iti anavasthā bhāvaḥ 
[II,111,8]	na ca utpanne jñāne saṃvedana abhāvasya aviśeṣāt santāna antare api artha prakāśaḥ niyata ātma sambandhasya niyāmaka tvāt tathā hi yasmin ātmani samavetam tat jñānam upajātam saḥ eva draṣṭā na anyaḥ tatra vivakṣita jñāna samavāyāt yasya tu sva saṃvedyam jñānam nirādhāram tasya santāna antare artha prakāśaḥ kasmāt na bhavati iti cintyam kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ tu kṣaṇika tve sati pūrvam pratiṣiddhaḥ eva 
[II,111,13]	yat ca idam sva saṃvedyam vijñānam iti artha antarasya asaṃvedanam eva tat asata vikalpa anupapatteḥ tathā hi yadi sva saṃvedyam ātma antaḥkaraṇa saṃyogāt upalabhyam tat iṣṭam eva atha tat eva jñānam pramāṇam prameyam phalañca iti tat na anyatra tritayasya abheda adarśanāt bhede tu anekam daṇḍa ādi udāharaṇam atas na jñāne karaṇa karmaṇā uḥ abhedaḥ sva saṃvedya tvam na api kriyā karmaṇoḥ iti tasmāt jñāna antara saṃvedyam saṃvedanam vedya tvāt ghaṭa ādi vat 
[II,111,19]	yat ca idam prakāśa svarūpa tvāt ātmanā eva prakāśate pradīpa vat iti uktam tatra yadi prakāśaka tvam bodha rūpa tvam vivakṣitam tadā sādhana vikalam udāharaṇam pradīpe bodha rūpa tvasya asambhavāt atha prakāśaka tvam bhāsvara rūpa sambandhi tvam tat vijñāne na asti atas jñāna antarasya tad viṣayasya utpādaḥ eva jñānasya paricchedaḥ iti 
[II,111,24]	yat ca idam kim prakāśa svarūpāḥ tad viparītāḥ vā padārthāḥ jñānena prakāśante iti uktam tatra yadi prakāśa svarūpa tvam bodha rūpa tvam tat na asti arthānām abodha rūpa tvāt teṣām katham prakāśaḥ tad viṣaya jñāna utpādāt yat viṣayam jñānam utpannam asau arthaḥ paricchinnaḥ iti vyavahāraḥ tasmāt nirākāra tve vijñānasya viṣaya viṣayi bhāvaḥ niyāmakaḥ iti dhiyaḥ nīla ādi rūpa tve bāhyaḥ arthaḥ kiṃnibandhanaḥ iti apāstam eva 
[II,112,5]	yat ca idam grāhya grāhakayoḥ eka kāla anubhava abhāvena dūṣaṇam tat api apāstam kṣaṇika tva anabhyupagamāt yaḥ hi kṣaṇika tvam manyate tasya ayam doṣaḥ jñāna kāle arthasya asadbhāvaḥ artha kāle jñānasya iti tayoḥ grāhya grāhaka bhāva anupapattiḥ iti tathā avayavinaḥ pūrvam eva vyavasthāpanāt na rūpa ādi samudāyasya aparamārtha tvena vijñāna viṣaya tvam iti paramāṇūnām sadbhāva siddheḥ vijñāna mātram eva iti adūṣaṇam anabhyupagamāt atas yat āha vijñāna vādī evam grāhya grāhaka pravibhāgaḥ kalpanā vaśāt iti tat api apāstam eva bodha rūpa vyatirekeṇa bāhya arthasya cakṣuḥ ādinā pratibhāsanāt pravṛtti nivṛttyoḥ ca tad viṣaya tvāt iti tathā hi artha avarodhe sati artha kriyā arthinaḥ tad abhimukhāḥ pravartante ca iti dṛṣṭam na ca bhrāntyā eva pravṛttiḥ avisaṃvāda upalabdheḥ 
[II,112,15_II,112,20]	atha pravṛtti nivṛttyoḥ artha kriyāyāḥ ca vijñānāt avyatirekaḥ eva tat na vastu rūpa tayā pratibhāsamānānām paraspara vyāvṛtta ātmanām jñāna abhede pramāṇa abhāvāt artha anabhyupagame ca saṃvāda an utpattiḥ vyāpāra vyāhāra abhyāñca santāna antara anubhavāt artha ākāre saṃvādaḥ tat na tasya asattvāt na ca utpādanā viśeṣeṇa saṃvādaḥ rūpa jñāna antaram rasa jñāna utpattau visaṃvāda prasaṅgāt atha sva santatau vyāpāra vyāhārayoḥ sva citta iha apūrvaka tvena upalambhāt santāna antare api tad pūrvakatva anumānam iti santāna antara siddhiḥ na pratīyamānayoḥ vyāpāra vyāhārayoḥ sva cittāt abhede para citta pūrvaka tva abhāva prasaṅgāt bhede ca bahirmukha avabhāsi tvena pratīyamāna tve katham na bāhya artha sadbhāvaḥ 
[II,112,24]	na ca sva saṃvid vādinaḥ avinā abhāva grahaṇa abhāve anumāna pravṛttiḥ yuktā tathā hi vyāpāra vyāhāraḥ pratibhāsi jñāna ātmanaḥ citta antara pūrvaka tām gṛhṇāti ātmani eva paryavasānāt etat kāraṇam api cittam na tad kāraṇa tām gṛhṇāti na api ubhābhyām vāsanā krameṇa vikalpa jñānam kārya kāraṇa bhāva grāhakam iti vācyam anubhava anurūpa tvāt vāsanāyāḥ katham kārya kāraṇa bhāva agrahe tad adhyavasāyi vikalpaḥ iti na ca atad rūpa samāropitaḥ vikalpaḥ tasya pāramparyeṇa api artha aviṣaya tve kārya kāraṇa bhāva agrahe anumāna apravṛttiḥ eva tasmāt ubhayoḥ liṅga liṅginoḥ idam asya vyāpyam idam asya vyāpakam iti avinābhāva grahe sati anumānam pravartate iti bodhāt anyaḥ arthaḥ abhyupagantavyaḥ 
[II,113,7]	yat ca idam nīlam aham vedmi iti jñānam taimirikasya dvi candra darśana vat bhrāntam iti asat etat abādhyamāna tvāt tathā hi taimirikasya timira vināśāt ūrdhvam eka tva jñāne sati dvi candra darśanam bhrāntam iti pratibhāti anutpanna timirasya anyasya na evam nīlam ityādi jñāne viparīta artha grāhaka pramāṇa anupapatteḥ na mithyātvam iti 
[II,113,12]	nanu uktam kim kena bādhyate jñānam jñānena iti tathā hi udaka jñānasya udakam viṣayaḥ sarva jana pratītaḥ tad parityāgena viṣaya antare marīci ādau utpannam tad grāhiṇā jñānena bādhyate mithyātva viśiṣṭa tayā jñāpyate mithyā idam mama udaka jñānam utpannam iti tad janita saṃskāra nivṛttiḥ vā tathā hi marīci jñāne sati udaka jñāna janita saṃskāra nivṛttau kāla antare api udakam mayā dṛṣṭam iti smaraṇa anutpattau tad deśa abhimukhyena pravṛtti abhāvaḥ iti bādhaka anabhyupagame ca jñānasya satyetara viveka anupapatteḥ vādi prativādinā ūrjaya parājaya vyavasthā na syāt iti uktam 
[II,113,19^1]	yat tu mantra ādi upapluta akṣāṇām ityādi vākyam tat na parihāra arham svatas eva pratibhāsasya anyathā tva abhyupagamāt tathā hi mṛd śakala ādayaḥ anyathā pratibhāsante na sva rūpeṇa upapluta cakṣuṣām na sarveṣām iti iṣyate eva idam mithyājñānam bādhaka upapatteḥ iṣṭañca bādhakam tathā eva darśanam teṣām anupapluta cakṣuṣām iti dūre ca maruṣu alpaḥ api mahān upalabhyate sannikṛṣṭe ca alpaḥ eva iti anena tasya bādhā na ca tena eva asya bādhā pramātṛ mātrasya sarva deśeṣu atad rūpa tayā pratibhāsanāt mahat tvan ca deśa viśeṣaḥ eva pratibhāsate na anyatra iti asat eva tat eva hi padārthānām svarūpam yat avisaṃvādi svastha ātmanām artha kriyā sampāda kañca iti atas mṛd śakala ādayaḥ yena rūpeṇa avipluta cakṣuṣām pratibhāsante artha kriyāñca sampādayanti tena eva rūpeṇa santaḥ na rūpa antareṇa iti katham arthānām avyavasthānāt atha svapna avasthāyām arthānām asattve api pratibhāsaḥ viśiṣṭa artha kriyā ca retasaḥ visargaḥ sambhavati iti nanu evam tarhi svapna avasthāyām arthānām asattvam katham jñātam iti vācyam yadi jāgrat avasthāyām anupalambhāt 
[II,113,19^2]	tarhi yeṣām upalambhaḥ teṣām sattvam āyātam anyathā hi jāgrat avasthāyām anupalambhena svapna avasthāyām asattvam na syāt atas pratīyamāna tvāt svapna avasthāyām iva jāgrat avasthāyām api asattvam iti na vācyam pratibhāsamāna tvasya sādhanasya sadbhāve api asattvasya sādhyasya aniścayāt pratīyamāna tvañca bodhe asti na ca asattvam iti vyabhicāraḥ tathā arthānām asattve pratīyamāna tvasya sādhanasya apakṣa dharma tvam syāt udāharaṇe pratīyamāna tvena na asattvam api tu pramāṇataḥ anupalabdheḥ iti anyathā siddhañca iti na ca sarvam vijñānam iti vādinaḥ svapna avasthā jāgrat avasthā ca iti viśeṣaḥ sambhavati ubhayatra api sva saṃvedyasya jñānasya avasthāna abhyupagamāt vratavaḥ ca pūrvam nirastāḥ eva tasmāt akṣa ādi janita jñāna samavāyaḥ jāgrat avasthā tad viparītā tu svapna avasthā iti yuktam 
[II,114,15]	yat ca idam buddhyā vivecanāt bhāvānām asattvam iti uktam tat asat sva buddhi pratibhāsamāna vapuṣām asattve bodhasya api asattva prasaṅgāt tathā hi rūpa ādayaḥ paraspara svarūpa parihāreṇa vyavasthitāḥ sva buddhi viṣayāḥ paṭa ādayaḥ api evam atas yadi api paṭaḥ tantu ādi buddhau na pratibhāsate tathā api sva buddhi viṣaya tvāt paramārtha san ā iva tat evam paṭa ādayaḥ paraspara vyāvṛtta buddhi viṣayāḥ viśiṣṭa artha kriyā kāriṇaḥ ca iti parama artha santaḥ eva 
[II,114,21]	na ca pramāṇam vinā prameya siddhiḥ iti vijñāna vyatirekiṇām asattve pramāṇam abhidheyam pramāṇam vinā ca padārthānām asattva siddhau sattvam api syāt pramāṇa abhāvasya ubhayatra aviśeṣāt atha arthānām asattva siddhau grāhya lakṣaṇa ayogaḥ pramāṇam na tasya api bhāva dharma tve viruddha tvam abhāva dharma tve ca āśraya asiddha tvam ubhaya dharma tve tu vyabhicārāt asādhanatvam iti vyadhikaraṇa tvāt ca tathā hi grāhya lakṣaṇasya ayogaḥ na grāhya dharmaḥ iti katham tasya asattvam sādhayet svarūpa asiddhaḥ ca grāhya lakṣaṇasya sadbhāvāt tathā ca mahat tva ādi grāhya lakṣaṇam vakṣyamānam iti sādhya aviśiṣṭañca grāhya lakṣaṇa ayogasya api sādhya tvāt na ca pramāṇa antaram asti iti 
[II,115,3]	etena śūnya vādaḥ api nirastaḥ eva iti na pṛthak abhidhīyate tathā hi sarva arthānām asattve vijñānasya api grāhya grāhaka ākāra rahita tvāt asatve ca sarvam śūnyam iti syāt tat ca nirastam eva pramāṇa abhāvena prameyasya asiddheḥ bodhasya artha an āñca pramāṇataḥ vyavasthāpanāt iti tat evam bodha vyatirekeṇa artha sadbhāva siddheḥ ānantyāt pratyartha niyata tvāt ca buddheḥ aneka tvam yuktam iti 
[II,115,8]	anye tu ātmanaḥ pariṇāma viśeṣaḥ buddhiḥ tad rūpa tayā ca anityā ātma rūpa tayā tu nitya iti matam tasya nirāsa artham sā ca aneka prakāra iti vākyam manyante tathā hi buddheḥ aneka tvāt ātmanaḥ api aneka tvam abhedāt ātmā eka tve vā buddheḥ eka tvam na ca bheda abheda pakṣaḥ sambhavati anekānta vādasya pūrvam eva pratiṣedhāt atas buddheḥ guṇa tvāt aneka tve api ātmanaḥ tathā abhāvaḥ na bhavati iti digvāsasām matam niṣiddham 
[II,115,14_II,115,19]	nanu evam tarhi buddheḥ ānantyāt katham tattva jñāna viṣaya tvam iti āha tasyāḥ sati api anekavidha tve samāsatas saṃkṣepataḥ dvividhā iti parijñānam kāryam iti kena rūpeṇa dvaividhyam iti āha vidyā ca avidyā ca iti anye tu vedānta mate vidyā vidyayoḥ śravaṇāt buddheḥ ānantya pratipādanam āgama viruddham syāt iti āśaṅkā niṣedha artham āha tasyāḥ sati api anekavidha tve samāsatas saṃkṣepataḥ dvaividhyam iṣyate eva vidyā ca avidyā ca iti 
[II,115,22]	vidyā hi deśa kāla avasthā ādi bhedena abādhyamānaḥ adhyavasāyaḥ tad viparīta arthā ca avidyati na tu pramāṇa apramāṇa tve vidyā vidya tve vyabhicārāt tathā hi yadi pramīyate anena iti pramāṇam iti vivakṣitam saṃśaya ādeḥ api ātma antaḥkaraṇa adhigame pramāṇa tvam asti iti vyabhicāraḥ sarveṣu ca pratyakṣa ādi jñāneṣu kāraṇa tva anupapatteḥ avyāptiḥ ca phala vivakṣāya antu na smṛteḥ pramāṇa phala tvam iti vidyā tvam na syāt 
[II,116,1_II,116,7]	guravaḥ tu viśiṣṭa vyavahāra kāraṇam vijñānam vidyā viparītañcā avidyā iti bruvate tatra yadi pravṛtti nivṛtti lakṣaṇaḥ viśiṣṭa vyavahāraḥ vivakṣitaḥ tadā saṃśaya ādi jñāneṣu api bhāvāt ati vyāptiḥ na ca pakṣe sarvatra asti iti avyāptiḥ ca atha deśa ādi bhedena api samyaktayā mayā upalabdham iti jñānam viśiṣṭa vyavahāraḥ tad janaka tvam api na sarveṣu vidyā bhedeṣu asti iti avyāptiḥ tathā ca samyak mayā upalabdham iti vyavahāraḥ na sarveṣu vidyā bhedeṣu vidyate iti avyāpaka tvam eva tatra api avidyā caturvidhā iti krama atikrameṇa avidyāyāḥ svarūpa nirūpaṇam artha prakāśasya vivakṣita tvāt tad ucchedya tva jñāpana artham iti ca anye avidyā hi vidyayā samucchidyate iti 
[II,116,10]	atha kena rūpeṇa caturvidhā saṃśaya viparyaya anadhyavasāya svapna lakṣaṇā svarūpa iti nanūha jñānam api asti tasya antarbhāvaḥ na vidyāyām na api avidyāyām ubhayatra api cāturvidhyā abhidhānāt na yuktam etat saṃśaya niścaya vyatirekeṇa ūha jñānasya asaṃvedanāt atha asti saṃśayāt ūrdhvam bāhya āli pradeśe sambandha upalabdheḥ sthāṇu pakṣa pratiṣedhe sati puruṣeṇa anena bhavitavyam iti sambhāvanā pratyayaḥ sa tu tasmin tat iti rūpa tvāt niścayaḥ eva tathā hi kim ayam sthāṇuḥ syāt puruṣaḥ vā iti ubhaya prasaṅge sati ekasya pratiṣedhāt tad anyasya apratiṣiddhasya avasthānam bhavati eva 
[II,116,18_II,117,1]	atha vyadhikaraṇa viśeṣa upalambhāt na yuktaḥ niścayaḥ tat asat saṃyogi viśeṣasya abhyupagamāt yathā hi kāka nilayana ādayaḥ viśeṣāḥ saṃyogini sthāṇau niścayam utpādayanti evam bāhya ālī pradeśe puruṣe api iti tad sambandhaḥ tu samavetaḥ eva viśeṣaḥ iti na vyadhikaraṇa tvam atha na ayam sthāṇuḥ bāhya ālī pradeśa sambandhi tvāt iti viṣayāt sādhanāt na nirṇayaḥ tat na vyāpāra apekṣayā puruṣa viṣaya tvasya api sambhavāt jñāna antara tve tu ūha jñānasya avyabhicāri artha jñāna tvāt pramāṇa rūpa tāyām pramāṇa antaram abhidheyam pramāṇam vinā tad phalasya anupapatteḥ vyabhicāri vā pramāṇa sāmānya lakṣaṇam syāt atha indriya artha sannikarṣa ādi eva pramāṇam ūha utpattau katham tarhi jñāna antaram pratyakṣa phala tvāt iti alam anye tu ūhasya sadbhāve api samāna tantra prasiddha tayā lābhāt iha anabhidhānam iti bruvate na ca pratyakṣa ādeḥ api anena eva nyāyena lābhaḥ sva mata abhāve samāna tantra tā siddheḥ abhāvāt 
[II,117,5_II,117,9]	atha saṃśayasya itarasmāt bheda viṣaya vibhāga nirūpaṇa artham saṃśayaḥ tāvat iti ādi prakaraṇam saṃśayaḥ tāvat vyākhyāyate avasara prāpta tvāt iti prasiddhāḥ aneke viśeṣāḥ yayoḥ tau tathā uktau tayoḥ iti viṣaya nirūpaṇam na tu prasiddhau ca tau aneka viśeṣau ca iti karma dhāraya parigrahaḥ saṃśayasya ca dharmi viṣaya tvāt atha ekasya eva dharmiṇaḥ tatra sadbhāvāt ubhayoḥ katham viṣaya tva sambhavaḥ pakṣa upanyāsāt a doṣaḥ tathā hi yatra aneke viśeṣāḥ prasiddhāḥ tatra eva saṃśayaḥ iti niyamyate na tu ekasmin eva kāle tayoḥ viṣaya tvam ekasya tatra asambhavāt kāla bhedena tu ubhayoḥ viṣaya tvam yat yatra sambhāvyate saṃśaya utpattau sa tasya viṣayaḥ iti 
[II,117,16^1]	kāraṇam iha sādṛśya mātra darśanāt iti sādṛśya mātram dṛśyate asmin iti sādṛśya viśeṣita dharmi darśanam labhyate iti vyākhyeyam na tu sādṛśya mātrasya darśanam iti abhyupagamena dharma upalambhāt dharmiṇi saṃśayasya vyadhikaraṇa tvāt atra sādṛśya mātra darśanāt iti mātrā abhidhānena atyanta viśeṣa anupalabdhim darśayati 
[II,117,16^2]	sāmānyasya viśeṣa sahitasya upalambhe api saṃśaya adarśanāt iti na ca sāmānya upalambham vinā viśeṣa anupalabdhiḥ saṃśaya janikā iti ubhaya abhidhānam tathā api nauvādya ārūḍhasya vṛkṣa ādiṣu ubhaya sadbhāve api na saṃśayaḥ iti ubhaya viśeṣa anusmaraṇāt iti padam viśeṣa anusmaraṇañca na pūrva uktam vinā saṃśaya janakam dṛṣṭam iti samuditam kāraṇam tat evam sāmānya darśanāt viśeṣa adarśanāt ubhaya viśeṣa anusmaraṇāt adharma ādibhyaḥ ca utpadyamāna tvāt saṃśayaḥ itarebhyaḥ bhidyate iti kāraṇa ātmakam lakṣaṇam tathā ca sūtram sāmānya pratyakṣāt viśeṣa apratyakṣāt viśeṣa smṛteḥ ca saṃśayaḥ iti sāmānyam pratyakṣam yasmin dharmiṇī asau tathā uktaḥ tasmāt iti pratyakṣa śabdaḥ ca dṛḍha pramāṇa vacanaḥ atra anumānikasya api saṃśayasya abhyupagamāt viśeṣa apratyakṣāt iti viśeṣa anupalabdheḥ tad smṛteḥ ca saṃśayaḥ iti 
[II,118,5]	nanu ca ayuktam etat devadattasya sva priyatamām parityajya vrajataḥ deśa vyavadhānāt tritaya sadbhāve api tatra saṃśaya anupalabdheḥ tathā hi strī tva sāmānya upalambhe api aneka ādi viśeṣa upalambhāt tad smaraṇāt ca kim madīyāḥ anyadīyā vā iti saṃśayaḥ na dṛṣṭaḥ para pakṣa pratiṣedhakasya deśa kāla viśeṣasya bādhakasya upalabdheḥ ekasmin deśe kāle ca anyā na sambhavati iti atas asya vyavaccheda artham bādhaka sādhaka pramāṇa avyavasthātaḥ ca iti padam kāryam na viśeṣa anupalabdhi padena eva nirasta tvāt tathā hi viśeṣa anupalabdhi padena samasta viśeṣa anupalabdhiḥ vivakṣitā sā ca atra na asti deśa kāla viśeṣasya niścita tvāt atas viśeṣa anupalabdhi padena eva asya nirasta tvāt iti vyavacchedya abhāvam manyamānaḥ muniḥ na viśeṣa antara māhā iti 
[II,118,15]	tasya svarūpam āha kim svid iti ubhaya avalambī vimarśaḥ saṃśayaḥ iti saṃśītiḥ saṃśayaḥ saṃśayyate anena ātmā suptaḥ iva bhavati iti niruktiḥ lakṣaṇam vimarśanam vimarśaḥ kim idam eva āhosvit evam na bhavati iti pratyayaḥ sa ca ubhayam ālambate tad śīlaḥ ca iti ubhaya avalambī vimarśaḥ saṃśayaḥ iti na ca ubhayoḥ viṣaya tvam ghaṭataḥ iti ubhaya ullekhī iti vyākhyeyam atas vimarśaḥ itarasmāt bhidyate saṃśayaḥ iti vā vyavahartavyaḥ vimarśa rūpa tvāt kim syāt iti ubhaya ālambi tvāt vā iti 
[II,118,21_II,119,6]	sa ca dvividhaḥ iti vibhāgaḥ kena rūpeṇa antar bahis ca nanu pañcavidha tvāt saṃśayasya dvaividhyam anupapannam na asya eva avāntara bhedena tad upapatteḥ tathā hi samāna dharma upapatteḥ aneka dharma upapatteḥ vipratipatteḥ ca iti bāhyaḥ trividhaḥ saṃśayaḥ upalabdhi anupalabdhyoḥ ca manaḥ paricchedya tvāt āntaraḥ dvividhaḥ iti abhipretañca etat bhāṣya kartuḥ yatas āha samānaḥ anekaḥ ca dharmaḥ jñeya sthaḥ upalabdhi anupalabdhī punar jñātṛ sthe iti avirodhaḥ saṅgrahānabhyupagame ca pratyakṣa apratyakṣa viṣaya bhedena api saṃśayasya bhedāt pañcatvam asambaddham syāt atha anena eva saṅgrahāt anabhidhānam tarhi dvaividhyena eva saṅgrahāt na pañcatvam abhidhīyate tasya hi tad bheda tvāt iti anekaḥ ca dharmaḥ sādhāraṇa tvāt saṃśaya hetuḥ na bhavati eva viruddha viśeṣaiḥ saha anupalambhena tad smaraṇā janaka tvāt na api viruddha avyabhicārī saṃśaya hetuḥ tasya eva asambhavāt iti vakṣyāmaḥ anaikāntika avasare 
[II,119,8]	tatra antar saṃśayasya svarūpa nirūpaṇa artham antar tāvat ādeśikasya ityādi yathā hi ādeśikena viśiṣṭam nimittam upalabhya ādiṣṭam ekadā vṛṣṭiḥ bhaviṣyati iti samyak jātam anyadā tu viparītam punar tathā eva ādiśataḥ triṣu kāleṣu asatsu tasmin jñāne saṃśayaḥ bhavati kinnu samyak mithyā vā iti atha jñānasya sāmānya darśana viśeṣa anusmaraṇa kāle avasthāna abhāvāt katham saṃśaya viṣaya tvam tathā hi tasmin jñāne bhaviṣyat vṛṣṭi viṣaya tvam samānaḥ dharmaḥ tad viśiṣṭe jñāne jñānam utpadyate tasya tu vinaśyattā samyaktva asamyaktva viśeṣa smaraṇasya utpadyamāna tā tatas viśeṣa smaraṇa kāle jñānam atītam katham viṣayaḥ tad upalakṣita ātmanaḥ viṣaya tvāt adoṣaḥ tathā ca kinnu samyak jñānavān aham mithyā jñānavān vā iti saṃśayaḥ 
[II,119,18_II,119,22]	anye tu vidyamānasya iva atītasya api viṣaya tvam asti iti bruvate bahis dvividhaḥ kena rūpeṇa pratyakṣa viṣaye ca apratyakṣa viṣaye ca iti tatra apratyakṣa viṣaye tāvat abhidhīyate saṃśayaḥ sādhāraṇa liṅga darśanāt iti yat liṅgam viruddha viśeṣaiḥ saha upalabdham tad darśanāt viśeṣa anupalabdheḥ ubhaya viśeṣa anusmaraṇāt adharmāt diś kāla ādibhyaḥ ca saṃśayaḥ bhavati yathā aṭavyām viṣāṇa mātra darśanāt tad gata viśeṣa anupalabdheḥ tad smaraṇāt saṃśayaḥ bhavati gauḥ gavayaḥ vā iti 
[II,120,1_II,120,7]	atha pratyakṣāt asya viśeṣaḥ katham sāmānya viśeṣitasya dharmiṇaḥ pratyakṣa tvam viśeṣa lakṣaṇa anabhidhānāt atha kim go gavaya viṣāṇeṣu sāmānyam tulya avayava racanā yogaḥ yathā bhūtāḥ hi avayava racanā goviṣāṇe dṛṣṭā tathā gavaya viṣāṇe api iti ye tu go viṣāṇa viśeṣāḥ gavaya viṣāṇa viśeṣāḥ ca pūrva upalabdhāḥ teṣām atra anupalambhaḥ iti atas sādṛśya mātra viśeṣitam viṣāṇam upalabhamānasya viśeṣa anupalabdheḥ tad smaraṇāt ca kim gauḥ syāt gavayaḥ vā iti saṃśayaḥ atādi viśeṣa anupalabdhitaḥ sthāṇu tva ādi sāmānya viśeṣa anabhivyaktau ubhaya viśeṣa anusmaraṇāt ubhayatra ākṛṣyamāṇasya ātmanaḥ pratyayaḥ dolāyate kinnu khalu ayam sthāṇuḥ syāt puruṣaḥ vā iti )
[II,120,11]	pratyakṣa viṣaye api sthāṇu puruṣayoḥ ūrdhva tā mātra sādṛśya darśanāt vakra tā ādi viśeṣa anupalabdhitaḥ iti ādi padena kāka nilayana ādayaḥ sthāṇau śiraḥ pāṇi ādayaḥ ca puruṣeṣu viśeṣāḥ teṣām anupalambhāt iti sthāṇu tvam ādiḥ yasya ityādi padena puruṣa tva grahaṇam tat ca sāmānyam eva viśeṣaḥ tasya anabhivyaktiḥ vyañjakasya śiraḥ pāṇi ādeḥ anupalambhāt atas tat anabhivyaktau ubhaya viśeṣa anusmaraṇāt ubhayatra sthāṇau puruṣe ca ākṛṣyamāṇasya ātmanaḥ pratyayaḥ dolāyate na eka koṭau vyavatiṣṭhate sa ca kiṃsvarūpaḥ iti āha kinnu khalu ayam sthāṇuḥ syāt puruṣaḥ vā iti 
[II,120,19]	atha kim idam ekam jñānam āhosvit anekam iti yadi anekam krameṇa utpadyate sthāṇuḥ iti ekam puruṣaḥ iti ca anyat tarhi yat tasmin tat iti rūpam tat samyak jñānam viparītantu mithyājñānam iti saṃśaya ucchedaḥ na aneka tva anabhyupagamāt tathā hi ekam eva kim ayam sthāṇuḥ syāt puruṣaḥ vā iti viruddha ullekhi jñānam viruddha viśeṣa anusmaraṇa upalakṣita sāmagrī janya tvāt ekaḥ tu saṃskāraḥ viśeṣa anubhavāt pūrva pūrva saṃskāra sacivāt utpadyate iti ekam smaraṇam viruddha viśeṣa viṣayam janayati eva 
[II,120,26]	yat vā pratiniyata viśeṣa anubhava janitāḥ saṃskārāḥ saṃśaya upabhoga prāpaka adṛṣṭa niyamitāḥ saṃskāram ārabhante tasmāt aneka viśeṣa viṣayam smaraṇam iti viṣaya saṃśaya utpattau aviśeṣāt pratyakṣa tvañcobhayatra api samānam iti satyam tathā api sāmānya viśeṣitasya liṅga upalambhāt sādhya dharma viśeṣite dharmiṇi saṃśaya abhyupagamaḥ anyatra ca aliṅga bhūte sādhya dharma rahite sāmānyavati pratyakṣe dharmiṇī iti viśeṣaḥ kiñcid sādharmyantu na niṣidhyate sāmānya lakṣaṇa ākrāntiḥ ca anvaya vyatirekābhyām upalabhyate pratyabhijñānāt ca tathā hi mama atra saṃśaya jñānam utpannam iti paścāt vijānāti iti sa viṣaya tvam asya 
[II,121,8_II,121,9]	atha viparyayasya kāraṇa svarūpa viṣaya vibhāga nirūpaṇa artham na param saṃśayaḥ viparyayaḥ api pratyakṣa anumāna viṣayaḥ eva bhavati iti evamādi prakaraṇam yat vā saṃśayasya pratyakṣa anumāna viṣaya tva abhyupagamāt viparyayasya viṣaya abhāvāt asambhavaḥ mā bhūt iti āha viparyayaḥ api pratyakṣa anumāna viṣayaḥ eva bhavati iti na ca viṣaya abhedāt eka tvam svarūpa bhedasya kāraṇa bhedasya ca sambhavāt āgamike api viṣaye visaṃvāda upalabdheḥ viparyaya darśanāt vyāhatam avadhāraṇam pratyakṣa anumāna viṣayaḥ eva viparyayaḥ iti na nirviṣaya tu a pratiṣedha paratvāt 
[II,121,16_II,122,3]	yat ca idam asatī api pratyakṣe pratyakṣa abhimānaḥ iti vākyam tat anyathā vyākhyeyam iti kecid anye tu para abhyupagatasya kalpanā jñānasya nirāsa artham viparyayaḥ api pratyakṣa anumāna viṣayaḥ eva na tu sarvaḥ sa viṣayaḥ kvacid aviṣayasya api sambhavāt yatra hi viṣayaḥ anvaya vyatirekābhyām upalabhyate asau sa viṣayaḥ anyaḥ tu nirviṣayaḥ na tu sarve iti anye tu pratyakṣa anumāna viṣayaḥ bhavati eva viparyayaḥ iti abhavana pratiṣedhaḥ vivakṣitaḥ nitya viparyaya vyavaccheda artham iti bruvate tat ayuktam vyākhyānam tasya eva asiddheḥ na ca nityasya pratyakṣa anumāna viṣaya tvam vyāpārāt ṛte sambhāvyate iti katham asya atra abhavana pratiṣedhaḥ iti alam 
[II,122,5]	pratyakṣa viṣaye tāvat viparyayam āha prasiddha aneka viśeṣayoḥ prasiddhāḥ anekā viśeṣāḥ yayoḥ tau tathā uktau tayoḥ iti viṣaya nirūpaṇam pitta kapha anila upahata indriyasya iti pittañca kaphaḥ ca anilaḥ ca iti pitta kapha anilāḥ taiḥ upahatāni indriyāṇi yasya asau sa tathā uktaḥ tasya viparyayaḥ bhavati kebhyaḥ iti āha ayathārtha ālocanāt ityādi ayathārtham ālā ucyate anena iti ayathā artha ālocanam sādṛśya jñānam 
[II,122,11]	yat vā ālocitiḥ ālocanam ayathārthañca tadālocanañcā iti upacāreṇa sādṛśya jñānam ayatha artha ālocana hetu tvāt vivakṣitam tasmāt asat nihitaḥ ca asau viṣayaḥ ca iti tathā uktaḥ tasmin jñānam tasmāt jātaḥ asat nihita viṣaya jñāna jaḥ sa ca asau saṃskāraḥ ca iti saṃskāra kārya tvāt smṛtiḥ saṃskāra padena vivakṣitā tad saṃskāram apekṣate iti ātma manaḥ saṃyogaḥ tad apekṣaḥ tasmāt asamavāyi kāraṇāt adharmāt ca viparyayaḥ sa ca kim svarūpaḥ atasmin tat iti pratyayaḥ iti tathā hi atasmin tat iti pratyayaḥ itarasmāt bhidyate viparyayaḥ iti vā vyavahartavyaḥ ayathārtha ālocana ādibhyaḥ utpadyamāna tvāt iti yaḥ tu evam na bhavati na ca asau ukta kāraṇebhyaḥ niṣpadyate yathā saṃśaya ādiḥ iti tasya udāharaṇam yathā gavyā iva aśvaḥ iti yathā hi dūrāt viṣāṇa ādi viśeṣam anupalabhamānasya aśva sādṛśya viśeṣita piṇḍa upalambhāt aśva anusmaraṇāt ca gavyeva aśvaḥ ayam iti jñānam utpadyate tathā marīciṣu udaka jñānam śuktikāyām rajata jñānam iti 
[II,122,24]	nanu ca ayuktam etat viparyaya jñāna sampādakasya kārakasya eva asambhavāt tathā hi indriyāṇi samyat jñāna sampādanāya utpannāni tasmin tat iti rūpa tvāt katham mithyājñānam kuryuḥ iti na ca kāca kāmalā ādi doṣa vaśāt viparīta jñāna janaka tvam duṣṭasya kārakasya kārya ajanaka tvāt yathā hi śālibījasya taila ādinā abhyaktasya śāli aṅkurājanaka tvam na punar yava aṅkura sampādaka tvam evam indriyāṇām samyat jñāna sampādaka tvam eva syāt na viparīta jñāna utpādaka tvam iti na ca rajata ādi jñānasya śuktikā ādi ālambana tve pramāṇam asti tasmāt sādṛśya jñāna anantaram su a ākāra paribhraṣṭam smaraṇam utpadyate idam rajatam iti tathā hi idam iti sādṛśya jñānam rajatam iti smaraṇam tat iti ākāra śūnyam 
[II,123,6]	na etat yuktam rajata arthinaḥ pravṛtti nivṛttyorabhāva prasaṅgāt atha jñānayoḥ bhade api idam eva rajatam iti sāmānādhikaraṇyam manyamānaḥ pravartate tarhi idam eva vyadhikaraṇayoḥ sāmānādhikaraṇya jñānam mithyājñānam iti atha idam iti sādṛśyam tatra rajatam iti bheda apratibhāse sati pravṛttiḥ veṣyate tat na pratipatti abhāvasya apravartaka tvāt tathā hi rajata arthī idam eva rajatam iti manyamānaḥ pravartate na itarathā idam iti jñānasya aparokṣata anirdeśaḥ na jñāna antaram anyathā hi idam rūpam ayam rasaḥ iti ādau api smṛti pramoṣaḥ syāt 
[II,123,13]	yat ca idam rajatam iti jñānasya śuktikā ādi ālambana tve pramāṇa abhāvaḥ iti uktam tat asat pratyabhijñāna ādeḥ sambhavāt tathā hi iyam śuktikā mama rajatam iti pratibhātā tathā na idam rajatam iti jñānasya śuktikā viṣaya tvāt rajatam iti jñānasya tat viṣaya tvam anyathā hi rajatam iti jñānasya śuktikā viṣaya tām antareṇa na idam rajatam iti pratiṣedhaḥ na syāt prasakti abhāvāt aprasaktasya ca niṣedhe na ayam ghaṭādiḥ iti api syāt tathā ca sati sarvatra pratiṣedha paramparā prasaṅgaḥ na ca etat asti tasmāt jñāna dvāreṇa rajatam tatra prasaktam iti niṣidhyate 
[II,123,21]	yat ca idam utpatti kāraṇa abhāvāt iti uktam tat asat doṣa anugṛhītasya indriya ādeḥ jñāna janaka tvāt yathā hi doṣa abhāve sati indriyam bhāva vyatirekābhyām samyat jñānasya janakam upalabdham tathā doṣa sadbhāve sati mithyājñānasya api iti ubhaya rūpasya kāryasya indriya vyāpāreṇa upalabdheḥ ubhaya artham indriyāṇām sargaḥ niścīyate mithyā tvañca asya sva viṣaya parityāgena viṣaya antara upasarpaṇāt 
[II,123,26]	atha alaukikam rajatam eva asya viṣayam iti viṣaya antara upasarpaṇam asiddham tat na alaukika rajata adhyavasāye sati pravṛtti nivṛttyorabhāva prasaṅgāt atha ālaukikasya api laukika tām manyamānaḥ pravartate katham tarhi mithyājñānasya sambhavaḥ iti na ca etasmin pakṣe mithyā idam mama utpannam jñānam iti bādhakam jñānam syāt pratyabhijñāna ādi a sambhavaḥ ca asti pratyabhijñānam śuktikā ādau mama atra rajata jñānam utpannam mithyātva pratipattiḥ ca iti katham mithyājñānasya asambhavaḥ 
[II,124,5]	yadi ca idam rajatam iti jñānam rajata ālambanam eva syāt tasya upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta tvāt samīpa vartinaḥ katham agrahaṇam yat vastu upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptam dūra sthena api upalabhyate tat avaśyam samīpa vartinā gṛhyate eva indriya ādeḥ tādavasthyāt na ca etat asti tasmāt rajata ādi jñānam śuktikā ādau utpannam iti 
[II,124,9]	anye tu yat eva rajatam anya deśa kāla viśeṣitam upalabdham tat eva anya deśa ādi viśeṣitam upalabhyate iti mithyātvam bruvate tat asat tasya atra avidyamāna tayā viṣaya tva asambhavāt tasmāt indriya vyāpāra viṣayaḥ aṅguli ādinā vyapadiśyamānaḥ ca śuktikā ādiḥ eva viṣayaḥ anyathā viṣaya antara utpannam rajata jñānam katham śuktikā jñānena bādhyeta vibhinna viṣaya tve bādhya bādhaka bhāvasya eva asambhavāt atas rajata jñānam śuktikāyām upajātam śuktikā jñānena sva viṣaya sahakāriṇā bādhyate mithyātva viśiṣṭa tayā jñāpyate viṣaya antara upasarpaṇāt rajata jñānasya tu rajatam viṣayaḥ sarva jana pratītaḥ tad tyāgena śuktikāyām utpadyamāna tvāt vyabhicāri tvam etena nirviṣayam kalpanā jñānam etat iti apāstam viṣayasya śuktikā ādeḥ pramāṇataḥ vyavasthāpanāt 
[II,124,19_II,124,21]	asati api pratyakṣe pratyakṣa abhimānaḥ ityādinā nirviṣayam viparyayam āha iti kecid udāharaṇantu yathā vyapagata ghana paṭalam acala jalanidhi sadṛśa vapuḥ ambaram añjana cūrṇa puñja śyāmam śārvaram tamaḥ iti vyapagatāni ghanānām paṭalāni yasmin ambare tat tathā uktam tathā na calaḥ acalaḥ sa ca asau jalanidhiḥ ca tena sadṛśam tulyam vapuḥ svarūpam asya iti tat ca jalanidhi sadṛśa vapuḥ ambaram iti jñānam ambarasya atīndriya tvāt ukta rūpasya api na jalanidhinā sādṛśya grahaṇam sambhavati iti nirviṣayaḥ pratyakṣa abhimānaḥ tathā śarvaryām bhavam śārvaram tamaḥ kiṃviśiṣṭam añjana cūrṇa pūñja śyāmam iti na ca abhāva rūpasya tamasaḥ śyāma rūpa sambandhi tvam asti iti nirviṣaya tvam sa viṣaya tva abhyupagame api deśa kāla viśeṣitasya tejasaḥ abhāvasya ālambana tvāt adoṣaḥ 
[II,125,3]	tathā sva āśrayāt vinivṛttāḥ cakṣuḥ aśmayaḥ sva ātmīyam golaka rūpam yathā uktena jalanidhinā sadṛśa vapuḥ ambaram iti upalambham janayanti ādarśāt pratiskhalitānām sva mukha grahaṇa vat iti yathā hi ādarśāt pratiskhalitāḥ cakṣu ḥ aśmayaḥ sva mukhe viparyayam utpādayanti ādarśa mukham iti tadvat iha api dūrāt vinivṛttāḥ sva golakam eva ambaram iti upadarśayanti 
[II,125,8_II,125,15]	anumāna viṣaye api viparyayam āha vā aṣpa ādibhiḥ ityādinā atra ādi padena nīhāra maśaka āvarta ādi grahaṇam taiḥ kimbhūtaiḥ dhūma abhimataiḥ dhūma rūpa tayā jñātaiḥ agni anumānam iti tathā gavaya viṣāṇa darśanāt ca gauḥ iti jñānam viparyayaḥ atra tu liṅge viparyaya jñānam indriya jam tad vyāpāra jañcā anumānikam 
[II,125,19]	idānīm asat darśana abhyāsāt viparyayam āha trayī darśana viparīteṣu śākya ādi darśaneṣu idam śreyaḥ iti mithyā pratyayaḥ ityādinā trayāṇām samāhāraḥ trayī rūḍhi vaśāt ṛc yajuḥ sāma lakṣaṇā gṛhyate trayī ā iva darśanam tad viparītāni śākya ādi darśanāni ityādi padena jaina ādi darśanasya avarodhaḥ teṣu idam śreyaḥ iti sarvam kṣaṇikam iti jñānam śūnyam nirātmakam iti jñānam śreyaḥ sādhaka tvāt śreyaḥ iti śākya darśana abhyāsāt viparyayaḥ kṣaṇikā ādi pakṣe bādhakasya ukta tvāt eṣu artheṣu anekānta jñānena darśane viparyayaḥ tathā itareṣu api ūhyaḥ na ca śākya ādi darśana viparīta tvāt trayyām api viparyayaḥ iti vācyam pradhāna artheṣu ātma ādiṣu artheṣu bādhaka anupapatteḥ śākya ādi darśaneṣu kṣaṇika tva ādi padārtheṣu uktam bādhakam abādhyamānam iti 
[II,126,3_II,126,10]	anye tu trayāṇām pratyakṣa anumāna āgamānām samāhāraḥ trayī tat eva dṛśyate anena iti darśanam tad viparītāni śākya ādi darśanāni taiḥ bādha upapatteḥ tad upalakṣitam vā vaiśeṣika darśanam tad viparītāni śākya ādi darśanāni bādhyamāna tvāt iti uktam tathā śarīra indriya manaḥsu ātma abhimānaḥ viparyayaḥ śarīram eva ātmā iti viparyayaḥ laukāyatikānām indriyāṇi eva ātmā iti indriya caitanya vādinām manaḥ caitanya vādinām manaḥ eva iti kṛtakeṣu nitya tva darśanam viparyayaḥ mīmāṃsakānām tathā hi kṣiti ādeḥ kṛtaka tvam pūrvam eva vyavasthāpitam tatra ca nitya tva darśanam teṣām iti yat vā sāṃkhyānām ayam viparyayaḥ kṛtakeṣu ghaṭa ādiṣu nitya tva darśanam iti na samutpadyate bhāvaḥ na sva ātmānam jahāti iti 
[II,126,14]	ukta kāraṇa vaikalye kārya utpatti jñānam viparyayaḥ svabhāva vādinām tathā ca niruktam kṣiti ādi vaicitryam kartāram antareṇa svabhāvataḥ eva bhavati iti etat ca asat kāryatvasya sva kartṛ pūrvaka tvena vyāptasya upalambhāt kṣiti ādau api kartṛ pūrvaka tvasya vyavasthāpita tvāt svabhāva vādinām viparyaya jñānam etat tathā cetanam adhiṣṭhātāram vinā kāryasya anupalabdheḥ jaiminīyānām śauddhodaneḥ śiṣyāṇāñca kartāram vinā kṣiti ādi kārya vijñānam viparyayaḥ 
[II,126,20_II,126,22]	pradhāne pralīnayoḥ ca dharma adharmayoḥ abhivyakta tvāt na kārya utpattau vyāpāraḥ sambhavati iti tad vaikalye kārya utpatti jñānam viparyayaḥ sāṃkhyānām saugāta anāñca kāraṇa vaikalye kārya utpatti jñānam viparyayaḥ katham utpatti vināśayoḥ tādātmyāt kṣaṇika tve sati yadā eva kārya utpādaḥ tadā eva kāraṇasya vināśaḥ sa ca utpatteḥ na artha antaram iti saha utpannayoḥ na kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ iti kāraṇa vaikalye kārya utpatti jñānam viparyayaḥ 
[II,126,26_II,127,3]	tathā sarvam idam kāryam parameśa pūrvakam tadārādhanañca paramasya śreyasaḥ sādhanam veda anāñca svarūpe api arthe prāmāṇyam iti evam hitam upadiśatsu vaiśeṣikeṣu na evam bhavati iti jñānam viparyayaḥ mīmāṃsaka saugata ja enānām yadā tu na parama śiva ādeḥ sadbhāvaḥ iti vaiyātyāt vadanti vaiśeṣikāḥ tadā na idam paramārthataḥ hitam iti hitam upadiśatsu vaiśeṣikeṣu ahitam eva idam iti jñānam viparyayaḥ teṣām 
[II,127,6_II,127,9]	yat vā saṃsārya ātmanām nānātvam parama śivaḥ ca etebhyaḥ bhinnaḥ tad ārādhanāt ca asmad ādeḥ śreyaḥ bhavati iti evam hitam upadiśatsu vaiśeṣikeṣu ahitam iti jñānam viparyayaḥ dvaita vādinām tad artha anabhyupagamena ca vacanena hitam iti jñānam viparyayaḥ teṣām kṣiti ādi kāryam paramāṇubhiḥ dvi aṇuka ādi prakrameṇa ārabdham īśvara kartṛ kañca iti evam hitam upadiśatsu vaiśeṣikeṣu na evam etat pradhāna pūrvaka tvāt jagataḥ iti jñānam viparyayaḥ sāṃkhyānām pradhāna astitve pramāṇa abhāvāt 
[II,127,13]	atha asti anvaya parimāṇa śakti pravṛtti upakārya upakāraka bhāva vaiśvarūpyebhyaḥ pradhānam tathā hi sarvam idam śarīra ādi kāryam sukha duḥkha moha anvitam upalabhyate yat ca anvitam tat ekasmāt kāraṇāt utpadyamānam dṛṣṭam yathā ekasmāt mṛd piṇḍāt mṛd anvitam aneka ghaṭa ādi tathā ca anumānam bhuvana ādi kāryam ekasmāt kāraṇāt utpadyate anvita tvāt ghaṭa ādi vat tathā ca asya pakṣa dharma tvam sukha duḥkha ādi samanvayasya sarveṣu śarīra ādiṣu bhāvāt na ca atatsvabhāvāt kāraṇāt sukha ādeḥ utpattiḥ iti śarīra ādeḥ sukha duḥkha moha ātmaka tvam tad janaka tvāt tathā prasāda ādi janaka tva upalabdheḥ ca tad svabhāva tvam sukha ādayaḥ tu sattva rajaḥ tamasām pariṇāma viśeṣāḥ tatas artha antaram na bhavanti kāryasya kāraṇāt bheda anupapatteḥ atas sattva rajaḥ tamāṃsi eva śabda ādi ātmanā vyavatiṣṭhamānāni sukha duḥkha moha ātmakam kāryam upajanayanti iti śabda ādayaḥ api na sattva ādibhyaḥ vyatiricyante sattva rajaḥ tamasā añca sāmya avasthā pradhānam 
[II,127,25_II,128,1]	tathā parimita tvāt ca yat parimitam tat ekasmāt kāraṇāt utpadyate yathā aṅkura ādi bījāt parimita tvañca iyattā avadhāraṇa viṣaya tvam tathā śarīra ādi kāryam ekasmāt utpadyate parimita tvāt aṅkura ādi vat śakti pravṛtteḥ ca śaktyā hi kāraṇam kārya arthinā upādīyate iti sarvam kāryam sva kāraṇe śakti rūpa tayā vyavasthitam tāvat yāvat pradhānam iti nanu evam sarvasya api kāryasya pradhānāt abhede vidyamāna tvāt katham utpatti vināśau iti asataḥ khara viṣāṇa ādeḥ iva kāryatva anupapatteḥ sataḥ eva āvirbhāva tirobhāvau iti brūmaḥ śakti rūpa tayā hi vyavasthitam kāryam param vyakti rūpa tām āpadyate punar tu tirobhāve śakti rūpa tayā vyavatiṣṭhate na sat nirudhyate iti 
[II,128,7_II,128,10]	tathā parasparam upakārya upakāraka bhāvena avasthitānām āsandikā aṅgānām ekasmāt kārakāt utpatteḥ upalambhāt śarīra ādeḥ api tathā abhāva upalabdheḥ eka kāraṇa pūrvaka tvam sādhyate tathā dadhi ādi vaiśvarūpyasya ekasmāt kṣīrāt utpatteḥ upalambhāt śarīra ādi vaicitryasya api eka kāraṇa pūrvaka tvam sādhyate yat ca ekam kāraṇam tat pradhānam iti tasmāt ca mahān mahataḥ ahaṅkāraḥ tasmāt pañca tanmātrāṇi ekādaśa indriyāṇi tebhyaḥ bhūtāni iti 
[II,128,14]	sarvam etat asat anvaya ādeḥ gamaka tva anupapatteḥ tathā hi śarīra ādeḥ eka kāraṇa pūrvaka tve sādhye anvita tvam ahetuḥ sandigdha tvāt atha sukha duḥkha ādi samanvita tvam hetuḥ tat na svarūpa asiddha tvāt tathā hi sukha duḥkha ādīnām pūrvam eva ātma guṇa tvena pratipādita tvāt śarīra ādi guṇa tvam asiddham ghaṭa ādi dṛṣṭāntaḥ api sādhana vikalaḥ tatra anvitasya eka kāraṇa pūrvaka tvena vyāptasya anupalambhāt atha mṛd anvita tvam ghaṭādau asti tat ca asiddham pakṣe pratyakṣeṇa ca śarīra ādeḥ upādānam pratiniyata jātīyam anekam upalabhyate iti kāla atyaya apadiṣṭañca sādhanam 
[II,128,21]	evam parimita tvam iyatta avadhāraṇa viṣaya tvam asiddham avāntara bhedena śarīra ādeḥ ānantyāt atha varga apekṣayā parimita tvam tathā api anaikāntika tvam para dṛṣṭyā nityeṣu api bhāvāt sattva rajaḥ tamāṃsi ca parimitāni na ca eka kāraṇa pūrvakāni iti pradhānasya eva tad rūpa tvāt tathā eka kāraṇa pūrvakatva abhāve api paramāṇu ādīni varga apekṣayā parimitāni iti aṅkura ādeḥ api bhauma anala sambandhāt bīja avayava kriyā krameṇa pūrva dravya vināśe sati dvi aṇuka ādi prakrameṇa utpādāt eka kāraṇa pūrvaka tvam asiddham 
[II,129,1^1]	yat ca idam śaktānām kāraṇānām kārya utpattau vyāpārāt śakti rūpa tayā kāryasya avasthānam iti uktam tat asat śakteḥ caramasahakāri rūpa tayā kāryāt artha antara tvāt na ca kārya kāraṇayoḥ ekatvam vibhinna pratibhāsa viṣaya tvāt pratibhāsa bhedaḥ ca padārthānām bheda vyavahāre hetuḥ tad sadbhāve api ekatva abhyupagame sarveṣām eka tā prasaṅgāt na caturviṃśati tattvāni iti syāt tathā svarūpa bhedaḥ artha kriyā bhedaḥ ca kārya kāraṇayoḥ sūkṣmam anekañca samavāyi kāraṇam adhikam ekañca kāryam iti tasya pūrvam kāraṇeṣu asattvam anupalambhāt atha anabhivyakteḥ anupalambhaḥ 
[II,129,1^2_II,129,16]	sadbhāve kim pramāṇam utpatteḥ iti ced na vidyamānasya utpatteḥ ayogāt atha avidyamānasya utpattau khara viṣāṇa ādīnām utpattiḥ syāt na kāraṇa abhāvāt yeṣām hi kāraṇam asti janakam teṣām eva utpattiḥ na khara viṣāṇa ādiṣu etat asti kārya abhāvena eva kāraṇa abhāva pratīteḥ evam tantuṣu ghaṭa ādeḥ mṛd piṇḍe ca paṭa ādeḥ anutpattiḥ vācyā pratiniyata sāmagryāḥ pratiniyata kārya janaka tvāt tantu upalakṣitā hi sāmagrī paṭasya eva janikā upalabdhā anyā tu anyasya iti upādāneṣu kārya niyamaḥ na sattvāt iti yat ca utpadyate tad utpatteḥ pūrvam asat na punar yat yat asat tat utpadyate iti vyāptiḥ yat ca utpadyamāna tvena hetunā sattvam tat asat tasya asādhāraṇa tvena āgamaka tvāt tathā hi sati ākāśa ādau asati ca khara viṣāṇa ādau utpadyamāna tvam na asti iti

[II,130,1_II,130,5]	yat ca idam upakārya upakāraka bhāva āpanna tvāt eka kāraṇa pūrvaka tvam iti uktam tat api asat yadi paraspara apekṣāṇām eka kārya janaka tvam upakārya upakāraka bhāvaḥ vivakṣitaḥ sa ca nityeṣu asti iti vyabhicārī sādhya vikalaḥ ca dṛṣṭāntaḥ vibhinna kāraka janya tvāt āsandikā aṅgānām tathā dadhi ādi vaiśva rūpyam api ukta kāraṇa pūrvakam na bhavati sva avayava kārya tvāt tathā hi sva avayavebhyaḥ dadhyutpadyate na kṣīrāt bhauma anala sambandhāt avayava kriyā nyāyena vinaṣṭe hi kṣīre punar utpanna pāka jaiḥ dvi aṇuka ādi krameṇa dadhi ādeḥ utpattiḥ iti atas vaiśvarūpyasya eka kāraṇa pūrvakatva abhāvaḥ pratyakṣeṇa ca pakṣe pratiniyata jātīyam anekam kāraṇam upalabdham iti kāla atyaya apadiṣṭañca vaiśvarūpyam iti 
[II,130,10]	na ca kiñcid kāryam ekasmāt eva kāraṇāt utpadyamānam upalabdham iti avidyamāna sapakṣasya anvaya ādeḥ vipakṣe sadbhāvaḥ tat evam anvaya ādīnām agamaka tvāt pradhāna asiddhau buddhi ādeḥ a sambhavaḥ eva pratihataḥ ca pradhāna vādaḥ asmad gurubhiḥ vistareṇa iti na iha pratanyate atas sāṃkhyānām ayam viparyayaḥ pradhāna pūrvakam jagat iti 
[II,130,14]	tathā śarīrasya parimāṇa bhedena bheda upapatteḥ śarīram eva ātmā iti abhyupagame pratisandhānam na syāt iti ātmanaḥ śarīra ādi vyatirekeṇa nitya tvam pratipattavyam iti hitam upadiśatsu vaiśeṣikeṣu ahita jñānam viparyayaḥ laukāyatikānām samānañca etat saugata ja enānām tathā hi saṅkoca vikāsa dharmaka tvāt ātmanaḥ sa pariṇāma tve anya tvena bheda upapatteḥ smaraṇam na syāt bodhāt ca bodha rūpa tā iti pratibandha pratiṣedhāt bodha mātre api ātmani smaraṇa anutpattau śreyaḥ buddheḥ abhāvaḥ iti alam vistareṇa iti 
[II,130,21_II,131,1]	san jāyate tatra pratyakṣa viṣaye tāvat prasiddhārtheṣu aprasiddhārtheṣu vā vyāsaṅgāt anarthi tvāt vā kim iti ālocana mātram anadhyavasāyaḥ yathā bāhīkasya panasa ādiṣu anadhyavasāyaḥ bhavati tatra sattā dravya tva pṛthivī tva vṛkṣa tva śākhā ādi apekṣaḥ adhyavasāyaḥ bhavati panasa tvam api panaseṣu anuvṛttam āmra ādibhyaḥ vyāvṛttam pratyakṣam eva kevalantu upadeśa abhāvāt viśeṣa saṃjñā pratipattiḥ na bhavati ) idānīm anadhyavasāyasya kāraṇa svarūpa viṣaya vibhāga nirūpaṇa artham na param viparyayaḥ anadhyavasāyaḥ api pratyakṣa anumāna viṣaye san jāyate ityādi prakaraṇam anadhyavasitiḥ anadhyavasāyaḥ jñānam aniścaya ātmakam tat ca saṃśaya ādibhyaḥ artha antaram kāraṇa bhedāt viṣaya bhedāt ca iti 
[II,131,5]	tatra pratyakṣa viṣaye tāvat vyākhyāyate prasiddha artheṣu aprasiddha artheṣu ca viṣayeṣu bhavati iti atas saṃśayāt bhidyate saṃśayaḥ hi prasiddha artheṣu eva bhavati iti atha prasiddha artheṣu kutas kāraṇāt anadhyavasāyaḥ iti āha vyāsaṅgāt anarthi tvāt vā iti yathā vyāsaṅgāt iṣukārasya iṣau āsakta manasaḥ mahati gate api rājani kinnāmā ayam gataḥ iti anadhyavasāyaḥ anarthi tvāt sva anuṣṭhāna niratasya tapasvinaḥ mahati api rājani anadhyavasāyaḥ kinnāmā ayam gataḥ iti 
[II,131,12_II,131,17]	na ca ayam saṃśayaḥ tasya ubhayollekhitvāt sāmānya upalambha ādibhyaḥ ca utpadyamāna tvāt ca iti atas anadhyavasāyaḥ itarasmāt bhidyate yathā ukta kāraṇa janya tvāt yathā uktam vā jñānam anadhyavasāyaḥ iti vyavahartavyam ukta kāraṇebhyaḥ niṣpadyamāna tvāt yaḥ tu na bhidyate na ca evam vyavahriyate na ca asau ukta kāraṇebhyaḥ niṣpadyate yathā saṃśaya ādiḥ iti tasya svarūpam āha kim iti ālocana mātram kim nāma iti jñānam viśeṣa saṃjñā ullekha śūnyam anadhyavasāyaḥ iti 
[II,131,19]	aprasiddha artheṣu yathā bāhīkasya panasa ādiṣu anadhyavasāyaḥ bhavati bāhīkaḥ hiraṭhakaḥ tasya panasa ādiṣu saṅketa abhāvāt viśeṣa saṃjñā ullekha śūnyam kinnāmā ayam iti jñānam utpadyate tatra hi sattā dravya tva pṛthivī tva vṛkṣa tva rūpa ādi śākhā ādi apekṣaḥ adhyavasāyaḥ eva tathā hi san ayam iti niścaya jñānam tathā dravyam pṛthivī vṛkṣaḥ rūpa ādimān chākhā ādimān ca iti adhyavasāyaḥ eva tathā panasatvam api nirvikalpaka bodhe panaseṣu anuvṛttam āmra ādibhyaḥ vyāvṛttam pratyakṣam eva 
[II,131,26]	nanu evam tarhi kva viṣaye anadhyavasāyaḥ iti āha kevalantu upadeśa abhāvāt saṅketa abhāvāt viśeṣa saṃjñā ullekhinī panasaḥ ayam iti pratipattiḥ na bhavati iti nanu evam tarhi pratipatti abhāvaḥ anadhyavasāyaḥ syāt tasya ca abhāva rūpa tvāt avidyāyām antarbhāvaḥ anupapannaḥ na etat evam kinnāma ayam iti aniścaya ātmaka jñānasya saṃśaya ādi vilakṣaṇasya anubhūyamāna tayā palāpa ayogāt tasya ca avidyā lakṣaṇa yukta tvāt avidyāyām antarbhāvaḥ iti 
[II,132,5_II,132,7]	anumāna viṣaye api nālikera dvīpa vāsinaḥ akṛta samayasya piṇḍa anupalambhe sāsnā mātra darśanāt kaḥ nu khalu atra prāṇī syāt iti anadhi avasāyaḥ bhavati pūrvam hi saṅketa apratipattau api sāsnā prāmāṇya avinābhūta upalabdhā tad upalambhāt piṇḍa anupalambhe api avinā abhā a sambandha smaraṇa anantaram parāmarśa jñāne sati kaḥ nu khalu atra pradeśe prāṇi iti kinnāmā atra prāṇi iti syāt iti anadhyavasāyaḥ 
[II,132,12_II,132,14]	tat evam anadhyavasāyasya kāraṇa ādi bhedena bhedam abhidhāya svapna nirūpaṇam āha uparata indriya grāmasya ityādi uparataḥ sva viṣaya grahaṇam prati nivṛttaḥ indriyāṇām grāmaḥ yasya asau tathā uktaḥ tasya pralīna manaskasya iti pralīnam na indriya deśena saṃyuktam manaḥ yasya asau tasya pralīna manaskasya indriya dvāreṇa iva yat anubhavanam mānasam utpadyate tat svapna jñānam iti manasi bhavam mānasam tat ca smaraṇa sukha ādi api bhavati iti tad nivṛtti artham anubhavana padam anubhavanañca bāhya indriya jam api iti mānasa grahaṇam tathā api sukha duḥkha ādi anubhavaiḥ vyabhicāraḥ tad artham uparata indriya grāmasya iti sukha ādi anubhavaḥ ca indriya jaḥ eva manasaḥ tatra vyāpārāt atha uparata indriya grāmasya mānasam svapna antikam api bhavati iti vyabhicāraḥ tat na tasya smṛti rūpa tayā anubhavana padena eva vyavacchinna tvāt

[II,135,1_II,135,4]	anye tu kuḍya ādayaḥ eva hasti ātmanā vyavasthitāḥ svapna jñānasya ālambanam iti manyante yat ca idam asatsu viṣayeṣu utpadyate svapna jñānam iti uktam tat api hasti ādi svarūpa apekṣayā tena hi rūpeṇa teṣām asattvāt iti tat etat asat kuḍya ādeḥ ālambana tve pramāṇa abhāvāt na ca svapna utthitasya mama ete kuḍya ādayaḥ hasti ādi rūpa tayā pratibhātā iti pratyabhijñānam asti na api indriyāṇām kuḍya ādiṣu hasti ādi jñāna janmani vyāpāraḥ sambhavati tad vyāpāra uparame sati tatra jñānasya bhavanāt manasaḥ api bahis viṣaye svātantryeṇa vyāpāraḥ pratiṣiddhaḥ eva tasmāt nirviṣayaḥ eva svapna jñānam iti 
[II,135,9]	atha svapna jñānam na viparyaya ādibhyaḥ artha antaram tathā hi svapna jñānam atasmin tat iti utpadyamānam viparyaya jñānam eva kim ayam sthāṇuḥ puruṣaḥ vā iti ubhaya ullekhitve sati saṃśaya jñānam kiṃnāma ayam iti ca utpāde anadhyavasāyaḥ iti na svapna jñānam etebhyaḥ artha antaram pṛthak abhidhānantu śubha aśubha sūcaka tvāt iti

[II,137,5_II,137,10]	atha idānīm vidyā svarūpa nirūpaṇa artham na kevalam avidyā vidyā api caturvidhāḥ ityādi prakaraṇam kena rūpeṇa iti āha pratyakṣa laiṅgika smṛti ārṣa lakṣaṇā tad svarūpa iti pratyaṣṭiḥ pratyakṣam liṅga darśanāt sañjāyamānam laiṅgikam smaraṇam smṛtiḥ ṛṣīṇām idam ārṣam iti nanu śābda jñānasya api vidyā rūpa tvāt iha anupanyāse kim prayojanam vipratipatti jñāpanam iti tathā hi śābdam anumāne antarbhavati iti kecid anye tu pramāṇa antaram iti vaiśeṣikāṇām vipratipattiḥ tena iha an abhidhānam atra tu vidyā vibhāga pareṇa api vākyena upasarjana tayā tad janakam api sāmagryām pratijñātam eva prādhānyena tu karaṇa vyutpatti dvāreṇa pratyakṣa ādi vibhāga abhyupagame vidyā vibhāga nirūpaṇam upasarjana tayā syāt tat tu na yuktam buddhi bhedasya pūrvam pratijñātasya iha nirūpaṇāt 
[II,137,17_II,137,21]	tatra pratyakṣasya nirūpaṇa artham āha akṣam akṣam pratītya utpadyate iti pratyakṣam pratigatam akṣam pratyakṣam iti prādi samāsaḥ anyathā avyayībhāva samāsa abhyupagame pratyakṣam rūpam pratyakṣāḥ pumāṃsaḥ pratyakṣā strī iti liṅga bhedaḥ vacana bhedaḥ ca na syāt akṣam akṣam iti vīpsā vidhānam sakala indriya avarodha artham atha akṣam iti sāmānya śabdāt sakala indriya avarodhaḥ bhavati eva na sāmānya śabdasya ubhayathā api pravṛtteḥ tathā hi brāhmaṇaḥ na hantavyaḥ iti sakala brāhmaṇa apekṣayā pratiṣedhaḥ brāhmaṇān bhojaya iti brāhmaṇa viśeṣa apekṣayā niyogaḥ tasmāt vyāpti artham vīpsā karaṇam iti atha vīpsā sadbhāve api vyāptiḥ na upalabdhā yathā antarvedyām grāmaḥ grāmaḥ ramaṇīyaḥ ramaṇīyaḥ puruṣaḥ puruṣe guṇa viśeṣaḥ iti vīpsā karaṇam atra satyam tathā api alpa saṃkhyā yogini padārthe vyāptau eva vīpsā upalabdha iti 
[II,138,6]	anye tu dvitīya akṣa padam avadhāraṇa artham iti manyante akṣam eva pratītya prāpya yat utpadyate jñānam tat pratyakṣam atha jñānasya anutpanna tvāt akṣeṇa prāptiḥ na asti iti katham akṣam prāpya utpadyate upacārasya vivakṣita tvāt adoṣaḥ yathā hi śiśuraya mātaram bhakṣayitvā upajātaḥ iti atas eva akṣa āśritam kāryam iti tattvena tat jñānam iti indriya rūpa ādiḥ ca indriya āśritaḥ na ca jñānam iti

[II,138,22]	nanu ca śabda indriyayoḥ ekasmin eva kāle vyāpāra asambhavāt ayuktam etat tathā hi manasā adhiṣṭhitantu śrotram śabdam gṛhṇāti punar kriyā krameṇa cakṣuṣā sambandhe sati rūpa grahaṇam na ca śabda jñānasya etāvat kālam avasthānam sambhavati iti katham ubhaya jam jñānam atra ekā śrotra sambaddhe manasi kriyā utpannā vibhāgam ārabhate vibhāgāt ca yadā eva saṃyogasya vinaśyattā tadā eva śabda jñānasya utpadyamāna tā tatas śabda jñānasya utpādaḥ saṃyogasya vināśaḥ uttara saṃyogasya utpadyamāna tā tatas viṣaya sambaddhena cakṣuṣā saha saṃyogasya utpādaḥ rūpa jñānasya utpadyamāna tā tatas sva jñāna sahāya śabda sahakāriṇā cakṣuṣā rūpa jñānam utpadyate iti ubhaya jam jñānam 
[II,139,4]	yat vā gṛhītasya śabdasya artha paricchede vyāpāraḥ iti ayam niyamaḥ na avaśyam grahaṇa sahakāriṇā iti kāla antareṇa api manasaḥ cakṣuṣā sambandhe rūpa śabdasya gṛhīta tvāt bhavati eva ubhaya jam jñānam kārya sadbhāvena ca kāraṇa kalpanā kriyate tat ca iha upalabdham iti anena krameṇa utpattiḥ cintyate tathā śabdena vyapadeśāt cakṣuṣā paśyatā api rūpam iti mayā na jñātam rūpa śabdāt ca pratipannam iti ubhaya jam jñānam yādi śabdasya vyāpārāt apratyakṣam tarhi indriya vyāpārāt na śābdam iti pramāṇa antara phalam syāt na etat evam pratyakṣa lakṣaṇe avyapadeśyam iti viśeṣaṇa vat śabda lakṣaṇe anindriya jam iti viśeṣaṇa aśravaṇāt śabde sahakāri niyama abhāvaḥ śābdam hi jñānam śabdāt indriya sahakāriṇaḥ tad rahitāt vā bhavatu sarvathā tad janakam śābdam pramāṇam bhavati 
[II,139,14_II,139,18]	atra ca akṣam pratītya utpadyate yat jñānam tat pratyakṣam iti vākye vivaraṇa vākyeṣū catuṣṭaya ādi sannikarṣa abhidhānāt ṣoḍhā sambandhaḥ labhyate eva sa ca saṃyogaḥ saṃyukta samavāyaḥ saṃyukta samaveta samavāyaḥ samavāyaḥ samaveta samavāyaḥ viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ ca iti nanu evam api indriya artha sannikarṣa padena eva vyavacchinnam atha indriyam manaḥ arthaḥ ca ātmā tad sannikarṣāt anumāna ādi jñānam api bhavati iti pratyakṣa phalam syāt na jñāna mātra utpattau antaḥkaraṇasya indriya tva anupapatteḥ karaṇa tva ādi viśeṣaṇasya aparokṣa jñāna janaka tvam indriya lakṣaṇam iti uktam na ca anumāna jñānam indriya grāhye arthe bhavati iti tat evam indriyam pratītya arthe yat avitatham avyapadeśyam vyavasāya ātmakam jñānam utpadyate tat yatas bhavati tat pratyakṣam iti phala viśeṣaṇa pakṣaḥ etāni tu avyabhicāritva ādīni vyavacchedakāni atīte api viśeṣya jñāne buddhi samāropaṇāt bhavanti iti 
[II,139,26]	sāmagrī viśeṣaṇa pakṣe tu na sākṣāt avyabhicāri tva ādi viśeṣaṇa yogaḥ atha akṣam akṣam pratītya utpadyate sāmagrī tasyāḥ kāraka sākalya rūpa tvāt sākalyantu caramasahakāri prāptau eva na pūrvam iti utpadyate eva tathā jñāyate anayā iti jñānam akṣa ādi upalakṣitā sāmagrī eva avyabhicāri vyavasāya ātmikā avyapadeśya padena jñāna janaka tvena sāmagryāḥ tat vyapadeśaḥ iti sāmagrī viśeṣaṇa pakṣe api viśeṣaṇa yogaḥ satyam tathā api avyabhicāritvā ādi viśeṣaṇāni phalasya tad dvāreṇa tu sāmagryāḥ bhavanti iti param phala viśeṣaṇa pakṣaḥ 
[II,140,7]	sva rūpa viśeṣaṇa pakṣaḥ tu nirastaḥ eva pramāṇa śabdasya karaṇa artha tvāt tathā hi pramīyate anena iti pramāṇam yena kartṛ karma vilakṣaṇena pramā kriyate sva rūpa viśeṣaṇa pakṣe tu na janya janaka rūpa tayā pramāṇasya prāmāṇyam kintva vyabhicāri tva ādi dharma upeta tvena eva tat ca ati vyāpakam avyāpakañca tathā ca parāmarśa ādi jñānasya api evam rūpam asti na ca tasya pratyakṣa tvam anumiti janaka tvena anumāna tvāt sāmagryāḥ tu pratyakṣa tvena abhimatāyāḥ pratyakṣa tvam na labhyate iti avyāptiḥ 
[II,140,14]	saugatānān tu pramāṇa phalayoḥ avyatirekaḥ iti tad pakṣe sva rūpa viśeṣaṇa tā eva ghaṭate tathā hi sautra antikānām ākāraḥ pramāṇam prameyaḥ arthaḥ sva saṃvid phalam iṣyate iti jñānam saḥ eva pramāṇa phala vyavahāraḥ kalpanam vā na ca etat yuktam kriyā karaṇayoḥ abheda anupalabdheḥ na ca bodhe viṣaya ākāraḥ sambhavati iti uktam katham tasya prāmāṇyam na ca meya rūpa tayā viṣaya paricchedye prāmāṇyam yuktam viṣayasya atyanta parokṣa tayā tena saha pratibandha anupalabdheḥ yadi ca agṛhīta pratibandhaḥ vyāpāraḥ viṣaya viśeṣam gamayet atiprasaṅgaḥ syāt tathā ca rūpa ākārasya rūpavat rasa ādi vyavasthāpaka tvam api syāt ubhayatra api pratibandha anupalambhasya aviśeṣāt na ca ākāra mātra saṃvedana vādinaḥ viṣaya viśeṣa antara grahaṇam ākāre sambhavati viṣayasya atyanta parokṣa tve avasthitasya pratisandha ātuḥ abhāve ca anvaya vyatirekayoḥ atyanta parokṣa tvāt 
[II,140,25_II,141,5]	parakīyañca pratyakṣa lakṣaṇam gurubhiḥ vistareṇa nirastam iti na uktam akṣa śabdasya aneka artha tvāt āha akṣāṇi indriyāṇi tāni tu ghrāṇa rasana cakṣuḥ tvac śrotra manāṃsi na karmendriyāṇi para abhyupagatāni nirviṣaya jñānasya pratiṣedhena smṛti vyavaccheda artham āha tat hi pratyakṣam yasmāt dravya ādiṣu padārtheṣu utpadyate tasmāt na nirviṣayam iti atra ca ādi śabdena guṇa karma sāmānyāni gṛhyante samavāyaḥ api iti anye anye tu indriyasya arthena sannikarṣa pratipādana artham tat hi dravya ādiṣu padārtheṣu utpadyate pratyakṣam tasmāt asti indriyeṇa saṃyukta samavāya ādi sambandhaḥ 
[II,141,7]	yatas vā dravya ādiṣu padārtheṣu utpadyate pratyakṣam atas dravye tāvat vyākhyāyate iti kim viśiṣṭe trividhe tisraḥ vidhā yasya tat tathā uktam tasmin mahati mahattva adhikaraṇe svarūpa ālocanam nirvikalpakam jñānam utpadyate kutas aneka dravyavattva udbhūta rūpa prakāśa catuṣṭaya sannikarṣāt aneka dravyavat tvam ca udbhūta rūpañca prakāśaḥ ca catuṣṭaya sannikarṣaḥ ca iti tathā uktaḥ tasmāt dharma ādi sāmagrye ca iti anekañca dravyañca iti aneka dravyam tat yasya asti tat tadvat tasya bhāvaḥ aneka dravyavat tvam rūpañca atra rūpa viśeṣaḥ vivakṣitaḥ tathā ca sūtram mahat tvāt aneka dravyavat tvāt rūpa viśeṣāt ca dravyam pratyakṣam iti aparokṣa jñāna sadbhāve sati samastam vyaḥ tañca idam pratyakṣa jñānasya kāraṇam vivakṣitam iti uktam vāyu adhikāre catuṣṭaya sannikarṣaḥ ca ātmā manasā saṃyujyate manaḥ indriyeṇa indriyam arthena iti catuṣṭaya sannikarṣaḥ tasmāt dharma ādi sāmagrye ca iti ādi padāt diś kāla ādeḥ grahaṇam iti 
[II,141,19]	atha astu evam nirvikalpaka jñāna utpattiḥ sadbhāve kim pramāṇam sa vikalpaka jñāna utpattiḥ eva anyathā hi viśiṣṭa artha anupalabdhau viśiṣṭasya saṅketa smaraṇasya anupapatteḥ sa vikalpakam jñānam na syāt tasya tad kāryatvāt na ca saṅketa smaraṇam eva tasya nimittam akṣaṇika tve sati arthasya nirvikalpa jñāna utpattau iva sa vikalpaka jñāna utpattau anvaya vyatirekābhyām vyāpāra upalabdheḥ iti ukta nyāyāt 
[II,141,24_II,141,26]	tat evam nirvikalpakam pratipādya sa vikalpakam viśeṣya jñānam āha sāmānya viśeṣa dravya guṇa karma viśeṣaṇa apekṣāt ityādinā sāmānyañca sāmānya viśeṣaḥ ca dravyañca guṇaḥ ca karma ca iti tathā uktāni tāni eva viśeṣaṇāni tāni apekṣate iti tad apekṣaḥ samuccaye na kevalam svarūpa ālocana mātra mukta kāraṇebhyaḥ niṣpadyate sāmānya ādi viśeṣaṇa apekṣañca tatas eva utpadyate iti 
[II,142,5_II,142,8]	nanu catuṣṭaya sannikarṣasya apavādam vinā ūrdhvam sarvatra anuvṛtteḥ abhyupagamāt vyartham ātma manaḥ sannikarṣasya abhidhānam na anantara jñāne api asya asamavāyi kāraṇa tva jñāpana artha tvāt tatra sat iti sattā viśeṣaṇam dravyam iti sāmānyam viśeṣa apekṣam pṛthivī iti tathā viṣāṇi iti dravya viśeṣaṇam śuklaḥ iti guṇa viśeṣaṇa apekṣam gauḥ iti sāmānya viśeṣa viśeṣaṇa apekṣam gacchati iti kriyā viśiṣṭam jñānam iti udāharaṇāni 
[II,142,11_II,142,16]	guṇa ādiṣu pratyakṣam āha rūpa rasa gandha sparśeṣu viṣayeṣu aneka dravyeṇa saha samavāyāt sva gata viśeṣāt ca yad kṛtā kvacid viṣaye teṣām upalabdhiḥ yat abhāvāt ca anupalabdhiḥ saḥ udbhava samākhyātaḥ rūpa ādi dharmaḥ sahakāri viśeṣaḥ tasmāt sva āśraya sannikarṣāt ca sva āśrayeṇa dravyeṇa saṃyuktam indriyam tat samavāyāt dharma ādi sāmagrye ca sati pratiniyata indriya nimittam utpadyate jñānam śabdasya traya sannikarṣāt iti ātmā manasā saṃyujyate manaḥ indriyeṇa iti trayasya sannikarṣaḥ śrotra samavetasya iti indriya artha sannikarṣaḥ api upadarśitaḥ eva tena eva śrotreṇa upalabdhiḥ na indriya antaraṇa iti 
[II,142,24_II,143,5]	anye tu trayaḥ ca asau sannikarṣaḥ ca iti indriya artha sannikarṣaḥ api upalabhyate tasmāt śrotra samavetasya tena eva upalabdhiḥ iti saṃkhyā parimāṇa pṛthaktva saṃyoga vibhāga paratva aparatva sneha drava tva vega karmaṇām grahaṇam kutas pratyakṣa dravya samavāyāt cakṣuḥ sparśanābhyām tad samavāyāt saṃkhyā ādīnām grahaṇam iti buddhi sukha duḥkha iccha dveṣa prayatnānām dvayoḥ ātmanasoḥ sannikarṣāt upalabdhiḥ buddhi ādayaḥ hi ātmani samavetāḥ tad sambaddhena manasā gṛhyante 
[II,143,7]	sāmānye pratyakṣam āha bhāva dravya tva guṇa tva karma tva ādīnām upalabhya ādhāra samavetānām āśraya grāhakaiḥ indriyaiḥ grahaṇam bhāvaḥ ca dravya tvañca karma tvañca tathā uktāni tāni ādiḥ yeṣām ityādi padena pṛthivī tva utkṣepaṇa tva ādīnām grahaṇam upalabhyaḥ ca asau ādhāraḥ ca tad samavetānām āśraya grāhakaiḥ indriyaiḥ grahaṇam yena eva indriyeṇa āśraya grahaṇam tena eva tad samavetānām sattā ādīnām grahaṇam iti tathā hi sattā dravye vartamānā saṃyukta samavāyena cakṣuḥ sparśanābhyām upalabhyate gandha rasa rūpa sparśeṣu samavetāḥ ghrāṇa rasana cakṣuḥ tvac indriyaiḥ upalabhyante saṃyukta samaveta samavāyena śabde tu samaveta samavāyāt śrotreṇa sukha ādi tu saṃyukta samaveta samavāyāt manasā gṛhyate guṇa tvam api evam atas sattāyām guṇa tve ca sarva indriyam jñānam iti dravya tvam saṃyukta samavāyena cakṣuḥ sparśanābhyām upalabhyate karma tvañca saṃyukta samaveta samavāyāt rūpa tva ādau api evam grahaṇam iti etat asmad ādīnām pratyakṣam iti upasaṃhāraḥ 
[II,143,19_II,143,24]	tathā asmad viśiṣṭānām yoginām keṣu artheṣu kathañca pratyakṣam utpadyate iti vyākhyāyate tatra yuktānām samādhi avasthānām yoga ja dharma anugṛhītena tad sahakāriṇā manasā aparokṣa svarūpa darśanam janyate keṣu artheṣu sva ātmā ca ātmā antarañcākāśañca diś ca kālaḥ ca vāyuḥ ca paramāṇavaḥ ca manaḥ ca iti tathā uktāni teṣu tathā na param sva ātma ādiṣu saṃyuktena manasā yoginām aparokṣa grahaṇam tad samaveteṣu guṇa karma sāmānya ādi viśeṣeṣu saṃyukta samavāyena samavāye ca saṃyukta viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvena grahaṇam atas eva samavāyasya pṛthak abhidhānam vibhinna sannikarṣa paricchedya tvāt guṇa karmasu paramāṇu ādi gateṣu yat sāmānyam tatra saṃyukta samaveta samavāyena 
[II,144,7_II,144,10]	atha yogī yadā svam antaḥkaraṇam gṛhṇāti tadā kim karaṇam ātma manaḥ saṃyogaḥ tasmin manaḥ paricchedye manaḥ eva karaṇam iti parakīyena ca manasā sūkṣma śarīra stham manaḥ preryam abhisambandhayati tad sambaddhañca tat gṛhṇāti iti viyuktānām punar catuṣṭaya sannikarṣāt asmad ādīnām iva pratyakṣam utpadyate jñānam keṣu artheṣu sūkṣma vyavahita viprakṛṣṭeṣu iti sūkṣmāḥ paramāṇavaḥ vyavahitāḥ nāga bhuvana ādayaḥ viprakṛṣṭāḥ mervādayaḥ teṣu aparokṣam jñānam asamādhi avasthānām yoga ja dharma anugraha sāmarthyāt tat utpadyate yogi indriyāṇām hi dharma viśeṣa anugraheṇa sarvatra apratibandhāt catuṣṭaya sannikarṣa grahaṇam udāharaṇa artham traya sannikarṣeṇa api grahaṇāt tathā hi yogī brahma ādi bhāṣitam yoga ja dharma anugrahāt apratibadhyamāna santāna nyāyena śrotra deśam āgatam gṛhṇāti traya sannikarṣeṇa 
[II,144,17]	nanu sarvam etat asat yoginām sadbhāve pramāṇa abhāvāt bādhaka upapatteḥ ca tathā ca na yogī atīndriya artha draṣṭā prāṇi tvāt asmad ādi vat yogi indriyāṇi vā na sarva viṣayāṇi indriya tvāt asmad ādi indriya vat na etat yuktam svatantre yogi nām aprasiddha tayā prāṇi tva ādi hetoḥ a āśraya asiddha tvāt atha para vyāptyā parasya aniṣṭa āpādanam etat tatra yadi samyak pramāṇena para prasiddhiḥ tena eva bādhyamāna tvāt anutthānam tad pratiṣedha hetūnām na ca kāryeṇa eva kāraṇasya vyāghātaḥ tad antareṇa apakṣa dharma tayā tad mūlasya hetoḥ aprāmāṇya prasaṅgāt atha pramāṇam vinā eva pareṇa abhyupagatāḥ yoginaḥ iti pratiṣidhyante tarhi pramāṇa abhāvena eva prameyasya aprasiddheḥ vyartham tad pratiṣedha anumānam 
[II,144,26]	asti ca yoginām sadbhāve anumānam tathā hi asmad ādīnām pratyakṣeṇa anupalabhyamānāḥ paramāṇu ādayaḥ kasyacid pratyakṣāḥ prameya tvāt ghaṭa ādi vat iti pakṣīkṛteṣu paramāṇu ādiṣu prameya tvasya hetoḥ sadbhāvāt pakṣa dharma tvam tathā kasyacid pratyakṣeṇa sādhyena prameya tvasya hetoḥ ghaṭa ādau vyāpteḥ upalambhaḥ na ca asya pratyakṣa āgamābhyām asti bādhā na ayam sat pratipakṣaḥ iti avyabhicāri tvāt gamakaḥ eva 
[II,145,6_II,145,9]	sarvañca anumānam sāmānyena vyāpti grahaṇa apekṣam pravartamānam pakṣe viśeṣam prasādhayati iti atas kasyacid pratyakṣam eva paramāṇu ādeḥ sāmānyena sādhyate yasya ca pratyakṣāḥ paramāṇu ādayaḥ saḥ asmad ādi vilakṣaṇaḥ yogī tathā abhyāsa vaśāt buddheḥ tāratamyam upalabhyamānam kvacid viśrāntam tāratamya śabda vācya tvāt aṇu parimāṇa tāratamya vat yatra viśrāmaḥ te asmad ādi vilakṣaṇāḥ yoginaḥ iti anumānasya tu nirdiṣṭa tāyām yogi sadbhāva siddheḥ śeṣam vacana mātram na bādhakam iti upekṣyate 
[II,145,13_II,145,17]	tat evam yoginām ayogināñca pratyakṣam vyākhyāya śiṣya vyutpādanāya vipratipatti nirāsa arthañca pramāṇa phala vibhāgam nirūpayati tatra sāmānya viśeṣeṣu svarūpa ālocana mātram ityādinā sāmānya viśeṣeṣu dravya tva guṇa tva karma tva ādiṣu svarūpa ālocana mātram ālocitiḥ ālocanam nirvikalpakam jñānam pratyakṣam pramāṇam tad upalakṣitā sāmagrī pratyakṣam pramāṇam iti mātrā abhidhānāt jñāna antara abhāvam darśayati prameyāḥ iti pramīyante iti prameyāḥ pramāṇa paricchedyāḥ dravya ādayaḥ padārthāḥ pramiṇoti iti pramādhāra tvāt pramātā ātmā pramitiḥ pramāṇa ādi sādhyā pratītiḥ dravya ādi viṣayam jñānam phalam iti evam itaretara vyāvṛtta lakṣaṇa yogi tvāt pramāṇa ādayaḥ parasparam vibhinnāḥ iti tad abheda vādinaḥ nirastāḥ bhavanti 
[II,146,1]	atha pramāṇa phalayoḥ vyatireka abhyupagamāt sāmānya viśeṣeṣu svarūpa ālocanasya pramā rūpa tvāt utpattau kim pramāṇam iti āha sāmānya viśeṣa jñāna utpattau avibhaktam viśeṣaṇa jñāna śūnyam ālocyate anena iti ālocana mātram indriya artha sannikarṣa ādi upalakṣitam kāraka sāmagryam pratyakṣam pramāṇam prameyam sāmānya viśeṣāḥ iti atha tasmin api svarūpa ālocane kasmāt na jñāna antaram iṣyate iti āha na tasmin svarūpa ālocane anyat pramāṇa antaram jñāna antaram asti iti aphala rūpa tvāt niṣprayojana tvāt iti tathā hi viśeṣya jñānam viśeṣaṇa anuraktam anyathā anupapadyamānam viśeṣaṇa jñāna sattām darśayati na ca evam viśeṣaṇa jñāne viśeṣaṇa anurāgaḥ asti jñāna antara abhyupagame ca anavasthā syāt iti viśeṣya jñāna anutpattiḥ eva dṛṣṭañca viśeṣya jñānam atas na viśeṣaṇa jñāne jñāna antaram asti iti 
[II,146,11_II,146,16]	anye tu sāmānya viśeṣeṣu svarūpa ālocana mātram iti mātrā abhidhānena nirākāram pratyakṣam pramāṇa phalam iti bruvate sāmānya viśeṣāḥ ca dravya ādayaḥ eva anugata vyāvṛtta jñāna viṣaya tvāt upacāreṇa vivakṣitāḥ atra hi jñāna viśeṣasya ākāra pratiṣedhe anyatra ākārabhyupagamaḥ syāt śeṣam pūrvavat yathā jñāne na ākāraḥ sambhavati tathā uktam jñāna ākāra vāda pratiṣedha avasare 
[II,146,19]	athavā iti pramāṇa phala vibhāge prakāra antara upadarśanam na tu vikalpana artham heya ādi jñāna utpattau api dravya ādi jñānam pramāṇam iti vākya arthaḥ tat āha sarveṣu padārtheṣu dravya ādiṣu yat avitatham avyapadeśyam jñānam utpadyate tat pratyakṣam pramāṇam prameyāḥ dravya ādayaḥ padārthāḥ pramātā ātmā pramitiḥ guṇa doṣa mādhyasthya darśanam iti guṇa darśanam upādeya jñānam doṣa darśanam heya jñānam upekṣaṇīya jñānañca mādhyasthya darśanam iti 
[II,146,25]	nanu dravya ādi jñāna utpattau aneka kāla vyavadhānena upādeya ādi jñānasya utpatteḥ katham dravya ādi jñāna phala tvam pāramparyeṇa iti tathā hi dravya tva ādi jātīyasya pūrvam sukha duḥkha sādhanatva upalabdheḥ tad jñāna anantaram yat yat dravya tva ādi jātīyam tat tat sukha sādhanam iti avinā abhāva smaraṇam tathā ca idam dravya tva ādi jātīyam iti parāmarśa jñānam tasmāt sukha sādhanam iti viniścayaḥ tatas upādeya jñānam atas pāramparyeṇa dravya ādi jñāna phala tvam samānañca etat heya upekṣaṇīya jñāna utpattau api iti 
[II,147,5]	atha upādeya ādi jñānasya sukha sādhana tva ādi viniścayāt viṣaya bhedaḥ vaktavyaḥ anyathā hi anumāna phala tvam eva syāt pratyakṣa phala tvañca sukha duḥkha ādi sādhana tva ādi viniścaya anantaram indriya artha sannikarṣeṇa upādeya ādi jñānasya utpatteḥ satyam tathā api viṣaya bhedaḥ viśeṣaṇa bhedāt sukha ādi sādhana tva viśeṣaṇam sukha sādhana ādi jñānāt tasmāt ca upādeya ādi jñānam iti 
[II,147,10_II,147,15]	pratyakṣa anantaram uddeśavataḥ laiṅgikasya lakṣaṇa parīkṣā artham āha liṅga darśanāt sañjāyamānam laiṅgikam iti yadi api liṅga darśanāt saṃskāraḥ viparyaya jñānam saṃśaya jñānañca bhavati tathā api vidyā sāmānya lakṣaṇa anuvṛttau viśeṣa lakṣaṇasya abhidhānāt na atiprasaṅgaḥ yat vai avitatham vyavasāya ātmakam avyapadeśyam iti viśeṣaṇam iha api anuvartanīyam avinā abhau a sambandha smaraṇantu vidyā rūpa liṅga darśanāt san jāyate tad vyavaccheda artham dravya ādiṣu utpadyate iti anuvartanīyam tat evam liṅga darśanāt yat avyabhicāritva ādi viśeṣaṇam jñānam anumeye tat yatas parāmarśa jñāna upalakṣitāt kāraka samūhāt bhavati tad laiṅgikam iti parāmarśa jñānam vā liṅga darśanāt yathā ukta viśeṣaṇa jñānam utpadyate sādhakatama tva apekṣayā anumānam 
[II,147,21_II,148,5]	kim punar liṅgam iti āha liṅgam punar yat anumeyena sambaddham ityādi anumeyaḥ pakṣaḥ pratipipādayiṣita dharma viśiṣṭaḥ dharmī tena vyāptyā sambaddham vyāptiḥ tu vivaraṇa vākya sahacarita padāt labhyate anyathā hi pakṣa eka deśe vartamānasya anumeyena sāhacaryam syāt yathā nityāḥ paramāṇavaḥ gandhavat tvāt atas asya vyavacchedaḥ sahacarita padena anye tu punar iti vīpsā abhidhānasya vivakṣita tvāt liṅgam punar punar yat anumeyena sambaddham iti pakṣe vyāptiḥ labhyate iti bruvate 
[II,148,7^1]	anumeyena sambaddham eva iti avadhāraṇāt bhāga asiddha vyudāsaḥ iti ca anye tat asat yatas evakāra karaṇam tatas anyatra avadhāraṇam iti nyāya abhyupagamena anumeya samavyāptam syāt liṅgam anumeyaḥ hi liṅgam na jahāti iti vyāptyā pakṣe sambandhaḥ jñāyate liṅgasya tu anavadhāraṇāt anyatra api vṛttiḥ jñāyate iti vyartham tad anvite prasiddham iti padam avadhāraṇa artham kriyate tatra api tad anvite prasiddham eva iti avadhāraṇa abhyupagame sa pakṣa eka deśa vṛtteḥ agamaka tva prasaṅgāt atha vipakṣa vṛtti pratiṣedha artham tad anvitaḥ eva prasiddham iti avadhāryate nanu evam anavadhāraṇena eva vipakṣāt vyāvṛtti siddheḥ vyartham tad abhāve ca na asti eva iti padam tathā anumeyena eva sambaddham iti avadhāraṇam bādhitam atha samuccīyamāna avadhāraṇam etat tathā hi 
[II,148,7^2]	pakṣe vṛttau siddhāyām vipakṣāt eva vyavaccheda artham avadhāraṇam tathā api avadhāraṇasya vidyamāna jñāpaka tvāt vipakṣāt atyantam vyāvṛttiḥ tatas api labhyate iti vyartham tad abhāve ca na asti eva iti padam tasya api vidya māna jñāpaka tvāt iti na ca anvaya upadarśane sati vyatireka abhidhānam vyatireka abhidhāne tu anvayasya apratipādanam eka abhidhānena aparasya arthāt āpanna tvāt sva śabdena punarvacanam punaruktam eva syāt iti evaṃvidha artha kathana artham tad abhāve ca na asti eva iti vacanam aśabda artha tvāt para artha anumānasya ca aprastuta tvāt tatra eṣa nyāyaḥ iti tasmāt avadhāraṇam vinā eva prakāra antareṇa pakṣa eka deśa vṛtti vyudāsaḥ vācyaḥ 
[II,148,24_II,149,1^1]	yeṣāntu sarvam vākyam sa avadhāraṇam iti matam tad lakṣaṇe hi etat dūṣaṇam anivāryam ūhyam yathā anumeye atha tad tulye sadbhāvaḥ asati na astitāḥ iti anumeyaḥ pakṣaḥ tatra sadbhāvaḥ tad tulyaḥ sa pakṣaḥ tatra ca iti athaśabdaḥ caśabda sthāne asati vipakṣe na astitā vyāvṛttiḥ yasya tāt liṅgam iti vipakṣaḥ tu tatas anyaḥ tad viruddhaḥ tad abhāvaḥ vā trividhaḥ api asati iti anena avaruddhaḥ sādhya abhāva rūpa tāyāḥ sarvatra samāna tvāt tatra anumeye eva sadbhāvaḥ iti avadhāraṇe asādhāraṇasya gamaka tva prasaṅgaḥ na ca asmāt bhāga asiddhi vyudāsaḥ pada antara vaiyarthyañca atha anumeye sadbhāvaḥ eva iti ayoga vyavacchedaḥ tathā api sadbhāvasya anavadhāraṇāt liṅgasya anyatra api vṛttiḥ labhyate iti vyartham tad tulye sadbhāvaḥ iti padam atha avadhāraṇa artham kriyate 
[II,149,1^2]	tatra api tad tulyaḥ eva sadbhāvaḥ iti avadhāraṇe pūrva uttara vyāghātaḥ atha pakṣe vṛttau siddhāyām vipakṣa ādeḥ vyavaccheda artham samuccīyamāna avadhāraṇam etat tathā api asati na astitāḥ iti na kāryam avadhāraṇena gata artha tvāt na ca tulye sadbhāvaḥ eva iti avadhāraṇam yuktam sa pakṣa eka deśa vṛtteḥ api gamaka tva abhyupagamāt atha asati eva na asti iti avadhāraṇa artham padam tathā api vipakṣa eka deśa vṛtteḥ gamaka tva prasaṅgaḥ tasya hi vipakṣaḥ eva na astitā iti asati na asti eva iti avadhāraṇam tathā api na astitāyāḥ vipakṣa vyatirekeṇa anyatra api sadbhāvaḥ labhyate iti asādhāraṇa ādeḥ gamaka tva prasaṅgaḥ tasmāt sarvam vākyam sa avadhāraṇam iti pakṣe dūṣaṇam etat anivāryam 
[II,149,18_II,149,19]	vistareṇa ca avadhāraṇa pakṣaḥ asmad gurubhiḥ nirastaḥ iti na iha pratanyate atha astu avadhāraṇam vinā eva sahacarita padāt bhāga asiddhi vyudāsaḥ tathā api etat rūpam viruddha asā dhāraṇayoḥ asti iti tad vyavaccheda artham prasiddhañca tad anvite iti tena anumeya samāna dharmeṇa anvitaḥ yuktaḥ tasmin tad anvite prasiddham na ca evam viruddha asā dhāraṇau iti tathā api anaikāntikasya pakṣa dharma tvam sa pakṣe sattvañca asti iti tad abhāve ca na asti eva iti padam tasya sādhya samāna dharmasya abhāvaḥ yasmin dharmiṇi tatra atyantam na asti eva iti na ca evam anaikāntikam 
[II,149,25]	nanu evam api prakaraṇa sama kāla atyaya apadiṣṭayoḥ trailakṣaṇya upapatteḥ gamaka tva prasaṅgaḥ tathā ca anuṣṇaḥ tejaḥ avayavī kṛtaka tvāt ghaṭa vat iti sati api trailakṣaṇye pratyakṣeṇa uṣṇatā grāhiṇā bādhyamāna tvāt kāla atyaya apadiṣṭaḥ prakaraṇa samastāvat nityaḥ śabdaḥ anupalabhyamāna anitya dharmaka tvāt ākāśa ādi vat anityaḥ śabdaḥ anupalabhyamāna nitya dharmaka tvāt ghaṭa vat atra api trailakṣaṇī a sadbhāve api agamaka tvam sat pratipakṣa tvāt atas ca anayoḥ vyavaccheda artham abādhita viṣaya tvam asat pratipakṣa tvañca samāna tantra gatam abhyūhyam caśabdasya anukta samuccaya artha tvāt 
[II,150,6]	anye tu pratijñā doṣeṇa gata artha tvāt na kāla atyaya apadiṣṭaḥ hetvābhāsa antaram tathā ca nitya anitya viśeṣa anupalabdheḥ itaretarava ādi abhiprāyeṇa asiddhe antarbhāvaḥ iti bruvate tat ca asat pratijñā doṣa sadbhāve api hetoḥ duṣṭa pakṣa upanyāsa anantaram upanyāsāt kāla atyaya apadiṣṭa tvam ucyate atha bādhā vinā bhāvayoḥ virodhāt na pratyakṣeṇa tri lakṣaṇasya bādhā abhyupagame vā na trailakṣaṇyam iti tat na tejaḥ avayavinaḥ anuṣṇa tve sādhye kṛtaka tvasya hetoḥ trailakṣaṇī a sadbhāve api pakṣeṇa viparīta artha upasthāpanāt bādhita viṣaya tvena avinābhāvasya eva aprasiddheḥ pratyakṣa vyavasthāpitena ca vapuṣā sarva prāṇabhṛtām artha kriyā janakaḥ agniḥ na rūpa antareṇa iti sva viṣaya sahakāri pratyakṣam na ca evam anumānam iti bādhyate
