[II,150,15]	atha duṣṭasya eva anumānasya pratyakṣeṇa eva bādhanāt yena doṣeṇa duṣṭam tat eva astu dūṣaṇa malam pratyakṣa bādhayā na pratyakṣeṇa dūṣaṇasya eva jñāpanāt tathā hi viparīta artham upasthāpayatā pratyakṣeṇa upadarśitam bādhita viṣayam etat anumānam iti atha kāryasya anuṣṇa tve sādhye taijasa paramāṇūnām uṣṇa anuṣṇa tve pramāṇa abhāvāt sandigdha vyatireki tvena kṛtaka tvasya āgamaka tvam na kāla atyaya apadiṣṭa tvāt iti ced na etat evam yaḥ hi paramāṇuṣu uṣṇa tvam abhyupagamya tad kārye anuṣṇa tvam prasādhayet tam prati vyatireka niścaya upapatteḥ na ca sandigdha vyatirekasya api uṣṇa pakṣa upanyāsa anantaram abhidhānāt kāla atyaya apadiṣṭa tvam virudhyate na ca ayam niyamaḥ yatra ekam dūṣaṇam tatra anyat na asti iti yathā aneka viśeṣaṇā siddha tva ādi hetoḥ iti 
[II,150,24]	yat ca idam tattva anupalabdheḥ ita retarava ādi abhiprāyeṇa asiddhatvam iti uktam tat asat ubhayoḥ sandigdha tvāt tathā hi sāmānya upalambha ādi sadbhāve sati viśeṣa anupalambhāt vādi prativādinoḥ pūrvam upajātaḥ saṃśayaḥ tatra ekaḥ sandigdhaḥ para pratāraṇa abhiprāyeṇa saṃśayitam hetum eva dharmi nirṇaya artham upādatte tathā itaraḥ api sandigdhaḥ tat evam ubhayoḥ saṃśayāt na anyatarasya api asiddha tā udbhāvane sāmarthyam iti yadi ca anyataraḥ api nitya anitya viśeṣa upalambham pramāṇena brūyāt tadā asiddha tvam eva na prakaraṇa sama tvam iti na ca sandigdha avasthāyām viruddha avyabhicāriṇaḥ prayogaḥ iti tasmāt vyatirekaḥ na api viruddha avyabhicārī sambhavati iti vakṣyāmaḥ 
[II,151,5_II,151,8]	tat evam anayoḥ vyavaccheda artham abādhita viṣaya tvam asat pratipakṣita tvañca rūpa antaram abhyupagantavyam anyathā hi tri avayavam vākyam syāt na pañca avayavam avayava dvayasya etat vyavaccheda artha paratvāt iti nanu evam api nyūnam lakṣaṇa vākyam kevala anvayinaḥ kevala vyatirekiṇaḥ ca avyāpanāt iti asti ca tayoḥ sādhya sādhana tvam tathā ca yatra sāmānyam eva sādhyam tatra sāmānyam eva hetuḥ yathā abhidheyaḥ viśeṣaḥ prameya tvāt sāmānya vat iti viśeṣāṇām abhidheya tve sādhye anabhidheyasya vastunaḥ asambhavāt vipakṣa abhāvaḥ pramāṇena hi vipakṣam upalabhya tasmāt vyatirekam vacanena upapādayataḥ tatra abhidheya tva prameya tvayoḥ prāpteḥ tasya sa pakṣa tvam eva syāt iti na vipakṣāt vyatirekaḥ asti iti atas anvaya avi abhicāreṇa eva gamaka tvam 
[II,151,15^1]	tathā jīvat śarīram nirātmakam na bhavati aprāṇa ādimattva prasaṅgāt yat yat nirātmakam tad tad aprāṇādimat yathā ghaṭa ādi na ca tathā jīvat śarīram tasmāt nirātmakam na bhavati iti sarvasya nirātmaka tva abhyupagamāt jīvat śarīrasya nairātmya pratiṣedhe sādhye na sa pakṣaḥ asti prāṇa ādimat tvañca vipakṣāt eva atyanta vyāvṛttam atas vyatireka avyabhicāreṇa eva gamaka tvam na ca evam asādhāraṇam tasya pakṣa ādi vat sa pakṣāt api vyāvṛtteḥ vyabhicāreṇa āgamaka tvāt atha nairātmya pratiṣedhena atra sa ātmaka tvam vivakṣitam na ca ātmā prasiddhaḥ iti aprasiddha viśeṣaṇaḥ pakṣaḥ tat nairātmye api samānam aprasiddha tvāt ātmanaḥ katham tat pratiṣedhaḥ 
[II,151,15^2]	na ca kalpanā samāropitasya pratiṣedhaḥ vāstava tvena pratipādanāt pratyakṣa ādi pramāṇaiḥ ca ātmā pratipādakasya prasiddhaḥ tad apekṣayā na aprasiddha viśeṣaṇa tā pakṣa doṣaḥ pratipādya apekṣayā tu na etat dūṣaṇam apratipanna tattvasya pratipādya tvāt sa pakṣe tu aprasiddha tvam na vyatirekiṇaḥ dūṣaṇam tasya vyatireka avyabhicāreṇa eva gamaka tvāt ayam sa pakṣa abhāvaḥ eva sa pakṣaḥ tasmin anuvṛttau anvaya upapattiḥ vyāvṛttau tu asādhāraṇa tvam eva tat uktam nivṛttiḥ yadi tasmin na hetoḥ vṛttiḥ kim iṣyate sā api na pratiṣedhaḥ ayam nivṛttiḥ kim niṣidhyate iti 
[II,152,5]	asya arthaḥ tasmin sa pakṣa abhāve hetoḥ yadi nivṛttiḥ na asti vṛttiḥ syāt tad vyāvṛtti rūpa tvāt vṛtti pratiṣedhe tu nivṛttiḥ eva syāt iti na ca vidhi pratiṣedha vyatirekeṇa aparaḥ śābdaḥ vyavahāraḥ sambhavati iti mūka tā prasaṅgaḥ tat etat asat pakṣa abhāvasya api sādhya an adhikaraṇa tvena vipakṣa tvāt tasmāt ca nivṛttiḥ eva aprāṇa ādimattvāt iti hetoḥ 
[II,152,10]	na ca kalpanā samāropita tvāt pakṣa ādi vyavasthāyāḥ kalpite sa pakṣe hetoḥ vṛttau anvaya vyatireki tvam vyāvṛttau tu asādhāraṇa tvam iti dūṣaṇam vāstava tvāt pakṣa ādi vyavasthāyāḥ kalpita tve tu katham hetu tad ābhāsa vyavasthā kalpanāyāḥ sarvatra aviśeṣāt atha ghaṭa ādau kim sa ātmaka tva vyāvṛttyā prāṇa ādimattva vyāvṛttiḥ uta vastu svābhāvyāt iti sandigdhaḥ vyetiḥ ekaḥ na ca ghaṭa ādau sa ātmaka tvasya sat asat tve pramāṇam asti na etat evam prāṇa ādimattvasya kārya viśeṣasya abhāvena tad kāraṇa viśeṣasya sa ātmaka tvasya tatra vyāvṛtti prasiddheḥ tathā hi prāṇa ādimati śarīre prāṇa ādi utpādana samartha ātma sambandha viśeṣaḥ sa ātmaka tvam sādhayati tad abhāvaḥ tu prāṇa ādi kārya abhāvena eva jñāyate ghaṭa ādau iti 
[II,152,19]	nanu evam kāryasya kāraṇa pūrvaka tvena upalabdha tvāt anvaya upapatteḥ katham kevala vyatireki tvam na kārya viśeṣeṇa kāraṇa viśeṣe sādhye anvaya abhāvāt jīvat śarīre hi prāṇa ādi utpādana samartha ātma sambandha viśeṣaḥ sādhyaḥ tena ca anvaya abhāvaḥ eva yasya tu sarvam nirātmakam iti pakṣaḥ sa katham ghaṭa ādau sa ātmaka tvam vyāvṛttam na vā iti sandeham brūyāt 
[II,152,24]	na api buddhi ādi nivṛttau eva prāṇa ādi nivṛttiḥ ghaṭa ādau iti vācyam ādi śabdena sarveṣām avarodhāt tad utpādana samarthaḥ ca ātma sambandha viśeṣaḥ sādhyaḥ tad abhāve tu katham buddhi ādīnām utpattiḥ jīvat śarīre kāraṇa abhāvena kāryasya abhāva prasaṅgāt kṣaṇika tve ca sati kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ pūrvam pratiṣiddhaḥ iti na bodhāt buddhi ādīnām utpattiḥ tat evam prāṇa ādi kārya viśeṣaḥ kāraṇa viśeṣe sādhye vyatireka avyabhicāreṇa eva gamakaḥ iti 
[II,153,4]	nanu śaśa viṣāṇa ādi vat śarīram prāṇa ādimattvena sādhyam syāt iti dūṣaṇam tad abhāva āyatta vyāvṛtteḥ pratipattum aśakya tvāt iti prāṇa ādi utpattau ca kāraṇa tva abhyupagamena kārya viśeṣa vyāvṛttyā yadi kāraṇa viśeṣa vyāvṛttiḥ iṣyate saṃjñā bheda mātram syāt viparyaye tu sa na syāt tad abhāva āyatta pratipatti abhāvaḥ iti alam 
[II,153,8]	nanu evam katham anayoḥ lakṣaṇa vākyena avarodhaḥ vākya bhedena tathā hi ayat anumeyena sambaddham vipakṣa abhāve ca tad anvitaḥ eva prasiddham iti kevala anvayī pakṣa dharma tve sati sa pakṣa abhāvāt tad abhāvaḥ eva na asti eva iti kevala vyatirekī sāmānya lakṣaṇantu sati sādhane sādhyasya avaśyambhāva niyamaḥ sādhya sādhana tvam anumāpaka tva padena uktam iti liṅga bhāsa nirūpaṇa artham āha viparītam atas yat syāt ekena dvitayena vā viruddha asiddha sandigdhamaliṅgam kāśyapaḥ abravīt iti 
[II,153,15]	atas iti ukta rūpāt liṅgāt yat viparītam ekena dharmeṇa dharma dvitayena vā śabdāt tribhiḥ ca iti tad aliṅagam liṅagapratirūpakam iti kāśyapaḥ abravīt viruddha asiddha sandigdham iti viśeṣa saṃjñā nirdeśaḥ tatra dharma dvaya sadbhāve api sandigdhaḥ na vipakṣāt vyāvṛttaḥ iti ekena dharmeṇa viparītaḥ viruddhaḥ tu pakṣa dharma tva sadbhāve api na sa pakṣe vartate na api vipakṣāt vyāvṛttaḥ iti dharma dvayena viparītaḥ asiddhaḥ tu ekena dvābhyām tribhiḥ ca viparītaḥ bhavati iti 
[II,153,21_II,154,1]	tatra nityaḥ śabdaḥ sāmānyavat tve sati cākṣuṣa tvāt iti ekena viparītaḥ tathā ca asya sa pakṣe ghaṭa ādau sadbhāve api vipakṣāt ca sāmānya ādeḥ vyāvṛttau api na pakṣa dharma tvam asti iti tathā nityaḥ śabdaḥ aprameya tvāt iti dvitayana viparītaḥ aprameya tvasya hi vipakṣāt eva vyāvṛttiḥ na sa pakṣe sadbhāvaḥ na api pakṣaḥ iti tribhiḥ ca viparītaḥ yathā anityaḥ śabdaḥ akārya tva āditi asya hi na śabde pakṣe sadbhāvaḥ na sa pakṣe ghaṭa ādau na api vipakṣāt vyāvṛttiḥ iti 
[II,154,4]	pūrvasya saṅgraha vākyasya spaṣṭa artham vivaraṇam āha yat anumeyena arthena ityādi anumeyena sambaddham iti asya vivaraṇam anumeyena arthena paricchedyamānena sahacaritam ajahat vṛtti iti deśa viśeṣe kāla viśeṣe vā sarvasmin deśe sarvasmin ca kālaḥ iti prasiddhañca tad anvite iti asya vivaraṇam anumeya dharma anvite ca anyatra sarvasmin eka deśe vā prasiddham iti anumeyaḥ pakṣaḥ tasya dharmaḥ tena tad samāna dharmeṇa anvitaḥ yuktaḥ sa pakṣaḥ tasmin sarvatra eka deśe vā prasiddhaḥ ityādi niyamaḥ tad abhāve ca na asti eva iti asya vivaraṇam anumeya viparīte ca sarvasmin pramāṇataḥ asat eva iti anumeya viparītaḥ anumeya dharma rahitaḥ vipakṣaḥ tasmin sarvatra asat eva pramāṇataḥ iti pramāṇena sādhya vyāvṛttyā sādhana vyāvṛttiḥ vācyā iti upadarśayati anumāpakam iti asya vivaraṇam yat etat ukta rūpam liṅgam tat aprasiddhārthasya anumāpakam bhavati iti 
[II,154,15_II,154,18]	dvitīyasya saṅgraha vākyasya vivaraṇam yat tu yathā uktāt trirūpāt liṅgāt iti abādhita viṣaya tvāt sat pratipakṣa tva sahitāt ekena dharmeṇa dvābhyām vā dharmābhyām tribhiḥ ca viparītam tad anumeyasya adhigame kartavye liṅgam na bhavati iti etat eva āha sūtrakāraḥ aprasiddhaḥ anapadeśaḥ asan sandigdhaḥ ca iti sūtrita tva upadarśanam 
[II,154,23]	aprasiddhaḥ anapadeśaḥ iti viruddha avarodhaḥ tasya sa pakṣe aprasiddha tvāt asan iti asiddhaḥ tasya hi pakṣa dharma tvena asattvāt sandigdhaḥ ca anapadaśas iti anaikāntika saṅgrahaḥ kāla atyaya apadiṣṭa prakaraṇa samayoḥ ca aprasiddha padena eva avarodhaḥ tayoḥ abādhita viṣaya tva asat pratipakṣa tvena aprasiddha tvāt samāna tantra nyāyena vā saṅgrahaḥ 
[II,155,1_II,155,8]	yathā ukta rūpam liṅgam nāga hīta avinābhāvasya gamakam iti avinābhāva svarūpa upadarśa nātham vidhiḥ tu yatra yatra dhūmaḥ ityādi vākyam vidhiḥ vyāptiḥ avinā abhāvaḥ iti atha yadi sāmānyayoḥ avinā abhāvaḥ siddha sādhanam apāsta viśeṣasya sāmānyasya siddha tvāt niyata deśa avacchedena viśeṣa arthinām pravṛtti nivṛttyorabhāva prasaṅgaḥ na ca viśeṣayoḥ avinābhāvaḥ teṣām ānantyena aprasiddheḥ tad āyattasya avinābhauvasya aprasiddheḥ anukta dharmāṇāñca sarve eva viśeṣāḥ pratipattum na śakyante iti yāvatām upalambhaḥ tāvatsu eva avinābhāva grahaṇe ca na agṛhīta avinābhāvasya viśeṣa antarasya upalambhāt anumānam syāt 
[II,155,14]	na etat dūṣaṇam sāmānyavatoḥ avinā abhāva grahaṇa abhyupagamāt yadi api agni viśeṣāḥ dhūma viśeṣāḥ ca ānantyena avasthitāḥ tathā api teṣu eva avasthitam agni tvam dhūma tvañca sāmānyam upagrāhakam asti iti tad upagrāhaka vaśāt bhūyas darśana balāt agni dhūmayoḥ deśa ādi vyabhicāre api avyabhicāra grahaṇam tathā hi prātar madhyāhna ādi bhedena kālasya bhede sama viṣama ādi bhedena ca deśa bhede dhūmasya agninā sāhacarya upalabdheḥ deśa antare kāla antare ca dhūmaḥ agnim vinā api bhaviṣyati iti āśaṅkā na syāt atas eva na kulālasya rāsabhena vyāpti grahaṇa prasaṅgaḥ kāla antare ca tena vinā api upalambhāt 
[II,155,22_II,155,26]	anye tu vyāpti grahaṇa kāle pratipattuḥ yoginaḥ iva aśeṣa viṣayam parijñānam asti iti bruvate anyathā hi sarvaḥ dhūmaḥ agnim vinā na bhavati iti vyāpti smaraṇam na syāt vivekena ca apratibhāsaḥ samāna abhivyāhārāt yathā dhānya rāśi nikṣiptāyāḥ dhānya vyakteḥ iti tat evam yatra yatra iti vīpsā arthasya vivakṣita tvāt yatra yatra dhūmaḥ tatra tatra agniḥ agni abhāve ca dhūmaḥ api na bhavati iti evam prasiddha samayasya gṛhīta avinābhāvasya pratipattuḥ asandigdha dhūma darśana anantaram sāhacarya anusmaraṇam ayatra yatra aham dhūmam adrākṣam tatra tatra agniḥ asti iti sāhacarya anusmaraṇāt tad anantaram agniḥ adhyavasīyate anena iti agni adhyavasāyaḥ parāmarśa jñānam tasmāt ca agni pratipattiḥ iti 
[II,156,6_II,156,10]	anye tu parāmarśa jñānasya abhāvam eva bruvate tat ca asat avinā abhau a sambandha smaraṇasya aniyata tvāt niyata pradeśe agni pratipattiḥ na syāt upanaya vaiyarthyañca upanaya arthasya anabhyupagamāt tasmāt vyutpattyā upacāreṇa vā agni adhyavasāyaḥ parāmarśa jñānam vyākhyeyam iti anye tu kārya kāraṇa bhāvāt svabhāvāt ca niyāmakāt avinābhāva grahaṇam iti manyante tat ca asat kārya kāraṇa bhāve api avaśyam bhūyas darśana balāt eva avinābhāva grahaṇam iti vācyam anyathā hi deśa antare kāla antare vai agnim vinā api dhūmaḥ bhaviṣyati iti āśaṅkā syāt atha agni dhūmayoḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāva avagatau katham agnim vinā dhūmasya sambhavaḥ iti āśaṅkā tasya nirhetuka tva pratiṣedhena avaśyam sva kāraṇāt eva utpatteḥ iti satyam etat yadi nāma sarvaḥ dhūmaḥ agni kāryaḥ iti jñānam api bhūyas darśanam vinā na bhavati iti tat abhyupagantavyam 
[II,156,17]	na ca agneḥ asādhāraṇam kāryam dhūmaḥ tasya dhuma antarāt api utpatti abhyupagamāt tathā hi gopāla ghuṭikā ādiṣu cira nivṛtte vahnau dhūma kṣaṇāt eva dhūma utpattiḥ iti katham atad kāryasya dhūmasya upalabdheḥ agni anumānam atha agni kāryasya upalambhāt anumānam iti ced na agni pratipattim vinā dhūme tad janya tva viniścayasya asambhavāt pratipattau vā kim anumānena dhūma svarūpa pratipatti vat ca agṛhīta analasya nārikela dvīpa vāsinaḥ dhūme agni janya tva pratipattiḥ dṛṣṭā tathā prayoga anupapatteḥ ca tathā hi parvatasya agnimat tve sādhye kāryatvam anaikāntikam eva atha dhūmasya agnimat tvam sādhyeta tatra api kāryatvam anaikāntikam eva dhūma tve sati kārya tvam hetuḥ tarhi dhūma tvam eva samartham iti vyartha viśeṣya tā hetoḥ doṣaḥ na ca agni kārya tvam dhūmasya agni sambandhāt pūrva dravya nivṛttau utpanna pāka jaiḥ dvi aṇuka ādi prakrameṇa utpatteḥ iti alam 
[II,157,1]	tathā vṛkṣa tva śiṃśapā tvayoḥ na tādātmya pratibandhaḥ tathā ca sati sādhya sādhana bhāva anupapatti prasaṅgāt tathā hi dharmiṇī upalabdhe tad tādātmyāt ubhayoḥ api upalambhe katham sādhya sādhana bhāvaḥ tad upalambhe api anupalabdhau tu tādātmyam na syāt iti atha sāmānya viśeṣavat tvāt anumānasya samāropa vyāvṛttyoḥ gamya gamaka bhāvaḥ tatra ca tādātmya tad utpattyoḥ asambhavaḥ eva tādātmya abhyupagame api na sādhya sādhana tvam ekatā prasaṅgāt iti tathā ubhayoḥ tādātmya aviśeṣe api śiṃśapā tvena vṛkṣa tvasya pratipatti vat vṛkṣa tvena śiṃśapātu apratipattiḥ api syāt 
[II,157,8]	na ca tādātmya tad utpatti lakṣaṇa pratibandha abhyupagame rūpa darśanāt sparśa anumānam udayāt astamaya pratipattiḥ kṛttikā udayāt ca rohiṇī udaya anumānam syāt tādātmya tad utpatti abhāvāt atha eka sāmagrī adhīna tayā rūpāt sparśa anumānam tat asat samāna kṣaṇayoḥ gamya gamaka bhāva upalabdheḥ tathā hi rūpa kṣaṇāt samāna kālaḥ sparśaḥ anumīyate na pūrvaḥ tatra ca eka sāmagrī adhīna tva asambhavaḥ eva na ca rūpa sparśayoḥ paraspara utpattau kāraṇa tve pramāṇam asti itara anvayasya itaratra anupalabdheḥ iti alam ati prasaṅgena 
[II,157,15_II,157,18]	evam sarvatra deśa kāla avinābhūtam itarasya sādhyasya liṅgam iti upasaṃhāraḥ deśāvinābhūtam yathā kedāragirim āroha tām kalakalā śabda śravaṇāt aśani pāta anumānam iti atha asya sūtreṇa asaṅgrahaḥ tathā ca sūtram asya idam kāryam kāraṇam saṃyogi samavāyi virodhi ca iti laiṅgikam na ca kalakalā śabdaḥ aśani pāta kāryaḥ tad antareṇa api sva kāraṇāt eva utpatteḥ na api kāraṇam aśani pātasya pratibandhaka abhāva viśiṣṭa guru tva kārya tvāt ubhayoḥ ca adravya tvāt na saṃyogi tvam parasparam ekasmin arthe samavāya abhāvāt sva ātmani anārambhaka tvāt na samavāyi tvam paraspara virodha abhāvāt ca avirodhi tvam iti artha antara tvam 
[II,157,24]	atha kārya ādeḥ katham liṅga tvam avinābhūta tvāt tathā hi kāryam kāraṇa pūrvaka tvena upalambhāt upalabhyamānam sat gamakam yathā hi viśiṣṭa nadī pūra upalambhāt upariṣṭāt vṛṣṭaḥ devaḥ iti tathā ca bahula svarūpa phena phenila parṇa kāṣṭha ādi vahana viśiṣṭasya nadī pūrasya vṛṣṭi kārya tvena pūrvam upalambhāt punar tad upalambhe sati yuktam anumānam ayam nadī pūraḥ vṛṣṭi kāryaḥ viśiṣṭa nadī pūra tvāt pūrva upalabdha nadī pūra vat iti pūraḥ tu ubhaya taṭa vyāpaka udaka saṃyogaḥ sa pāramparyeṇa vṛṣṭi kāryaḥ iti kāraṇam api kārya janaka tvena pūrvam upalabdheḥ upalabhyamānam tat liṅgam 
[II,158,5]	yathā ca viśiṣṭa megha unnatiḥ varṣa karmaṇaḥ iti atha kāraṇasya avaśyam kārya janaka tvena anupalambhāt kārya aṇāñca aniyatāt kāraṇāt utpatteḥ vyabhicāraḥ tathā hi megha unnati sadbhāve api ekadā vṛṣṭiḥ na dṛṣṭā kāryañca aniyatāt kāraṇāt utpadyamānam dṛṣṭam yathā vṛścikāt vṛścikaḥ jāyate gomayāt sarpāt ca iti evam anyatra api aniyatam kāraṇam abhyūhyam iti katham kāryāt kāraṇa viśeṣa pratipattiḥ kāraṇāt ca kārya viśeṣasya iti na etat evam kāraṇa viśeṣasya kārya viśeṣa gamaka tvam iti abhyupagamāt yaḥ tu vidyamānam api viśeṣam na avabudhyate tasya aparādhaḥ na anumānasya iti adoṣaḥ 
[II,158,13_II,158,24^1]	tathā dhūmaḥ agneḥ saṃyogī atha saṃyogasya ubhaya niṣṭhatvā viśeṣe katham ekam niyamena sādhanam itarat ca sādhyam iti vyavasthā tad avinā abhāve api samānam tasya api ubhaya niṣṭha tvāt katham eṣā vyavasthā syāt atha yasya upalambhāt anumeye pratipattiḥ tat eva sādhanam na anyat iti ced saṃyogi tve api samānam etat avinābhūtasya avāntara viśeṣa nirūpaṇāt samavāyī ca uṣṇa sparśaḥ vāri stham tejaḥ gamayati iti virodhī ca yathā ahiḥ visphūrjana viśiṣṭaḥ nakula ādeḥ liṅgam iti atha sūtre kārya ādi grahaṇam udāharaṇa artham avadhāraṇa artham vā iti āha śāstre kārya ādi grahaṇam nidarśana artham kṛtam na avadhāraṇa artham katham etat jñāyate 
[II,158,24^2]	vyatireka darśanāt tat yathā adhvaryurom śrāvayan vyavahitasya hotuḥ liṅgam iti na ca hotuḥ om śrāvaya iti śabdaḥ kāraṇam kāryam vā anvaya vyatireka abhāvāt tathā ca hotāram vinā eva upapattiḥ hotuḥ ca anena vinā api iti saṃyoga ādiṣu api antar bhāva anupapattiḥ sa ca yāga bhūmau eva asya avinā abhāvaḥ na ca deśa antare iti tathā ca ayam adhvaryuḥ api dūra deśena hotrā tadvān om śrāvaya iti śabda kartṛ tvāt pūrva upalabdha adhvaryu vat candra udayaḥ samudra vṛddheḥ kumuda vikāśasya ca liṅgam samudrasya ca vṛddhiḥ avayava upacayaḥ 
[II,158,24^3_II,159,14]	sa ca sva avayavebhyaḥ niṣpadyate na candra udayāt kumuda vikāśaḥ api avayavānām ārabdha kāryāṇām parasparam vibhāgaḥ dravya ārambhaka saṃyoga avirodhi kriyā kāryaḥ iti kāraṇañca atra abhivyaṅgyasya janakam vivakṣitam na pratipatteḥ sarveṣām kāraṇa bhāvaḥ eva antar bhāva prasaṅgāt śaradi jala prasādaḥ agastya udayasya liṅgam asya api tad kārya ādiṣu anantarbhāvaḥ śaradi jala prasādaḥ agastya udayavān jala prasāda tvāt pūrva upalabdhā evaṃvidha jala prasāda vat iti evamādi ityādi padena udaya ādiḥ udaya ādeḥ astaḥ ca asta ādeḥ liṅgam iti ūhyam atha katham eṣām sūtreṇa saṅgrahaḥ tat āha tat sarvam asya idam iti sambandha mātra vacanāt siddham tathā hi idam asya gamakam idam asya gamyam iti sāmānyena sarva liṅga parigrahaḥ viśeṣa apekṣayā tu idam asya kāryam kāraṇam ityādi yojyam 
[II,159,18_II,160,3]	anye tu avadhāraṇa artham etat sūtram iti manyante śāstre kārya ādi grahaṇam nidarśana artham iti vākyam anyathā vyākhyāyante tathā hi tat uktam paraiḥ vyatireka darśanāt śāstre kārya ādi grahaṇam nidarśana artham kṛtam iti jñāyate iti etat na kintu avadhāraṇa artham sarveṣām atra eva antar bhāvena vyatireka darśanasya asiddha tvāt tathā ca hotari sannihite adhvaryurom śrāvaya iti śabdam uccārayati yāga bhūmau na tena vinā api iti katham na tasya kāraṇa tvam evam candra udayaḥ api samudra vṛddheḥ kāraṇam anvaya vyatirekavat tvāt tathā ca tena satā jalanidheḥ vṛddhiḥ na tad abhāvaḥ iti kāryeṇa megha paṭala antaritaḥ candraḥ anumīyate gṛhīta vyāptikasya deśa antare api candra udaya upalambhāt ambhaḥ nidheḥ vṛddhi anumānam evam kumuda vikāśe api iti yat vā raśmi dvāreṇa saṃyogi tvam eva tathā agastya udayaḥ api jala prasādasya kāraṇam saṃyogi vā raśmi dvāreṇa iti pakṣa dvaye ca guṇa doṣa nirūpaṇam svatas eva kāryam parīkṣakaiḥ iti 
[II,160,4_II,160,10]	bhedam āha tat anumānam dvividham kena rūpeṇa dṛṣṭam sāmānyatas dṛṣṭañcaḥ iti tatra dṛṣṭam prasiddha sādhyayoḥ jātya bhede anumānam prasiddhaḥ ca sādhyaḥ ca iti prasiddha sādhyau tayoḥ prasiddha sādhyayoḥ dṛṣṭānta dārṣṭa antikayoḥ jātya bhede sati yat anumānam tat dṛṣṭam yathā hi sādhya dharmaḥ dṛṣṭānta dharmiṇi pratyakṣa arhaḥ tathā dārṣṭa antike api iti sādhya dharma abhedaḥ na tu jāteḥ sāmānyasya tathā hi brāhmaṇa kartṛkam citra ādi kāryam pratipadya punar kṣatriya ādi kartṛkasya api upalambhāt kenacid kartrā sampāditam etat citra ādi kārya tvāt pūrva upalabdhā evaṃvidha citra ādi kārya vat iti anumānam jāteḥ sāmānyasya bhede api dṛṣṭam eva sādhya dharmasya anumānāt pūrvam ūrdhvañca pratyakṣa grahaṇa artha tvāt 
[II,160,19_II,160,24]	anye tu prasiddhau ca tau sādhyau ca iti prasiddha sādhyau iti samāsam kurvate tatra dṛṣṭānta dharmī prasiddha tvāt sādhyaḥ na bhavati dārṣṭa antikaḥ ca na prasiddhaḥ iti katham etat upacārasya vivakṣita tvāt adoṣaḥ tathā hi dṛṣṭānta dhamā sādhya samāna dharma adhikaraṇa tvāt upacāreṇa sādhyaḥ dārṣṭa antikaḥ tu anumānāt ūrdhvam prasiddhim yāsyati iti pūrvam api prasiddhaḥ śeṣam pūrvavat iti asya udāharaṇam yathā gavyā iva sāsnām upalabhya punar deśa antare gopiṇḍa vyavadhāne api sāsnā darśanāt gavi pratipattiḥ gauḥ iyam sāsnāvat tvāt pūrva upalabdha sāsnā ādi vat iti 
[II,161,1]	sāmānyatas dṛṣṭañca prasiddha sādhyayoḥ dṛṣṭānta dārṣṭa antikayoḥ atyantam sarvathā jāti bhede sādhya dharma bhede anumānam tathā ca sādhya dharmaḥ anumānāt pūrvam ūrdhvañca sarvadā aprasiddhaḥ eva iti atha sādhya dharmasya bhede avinābhauvasya eva aprasiddheḥ katham anumānam iti āha liṅga anumeya dharma sāmānya anuvṛttitaḥ iti liṅgañca anumeya dharmaḥ ca tayoḥ sāmānyena anuvṛttiḥ yatra yatra idam sādhana sāmānyam tatra tatra idam sādhya sāmānyam iti tad grahaṇe anumānam pravartate eva yathā karṣaka vaṇi grāja puruṣāṇām pravṛtteḥ abhipreta phala tvena phalavat tvam upalabhya varṇa āśramiṇām api kim viśiṣṭānām dṛṣṭam bhikṣā lābha ādikam prayojanam anuddiśya pravartamānānām abhipreta phala anumānam tathā hi varṇa āśramiṇāñca pravṛttiḥ abhipreta phalena phalavatī prekṣā pūrva kāri pravṛtti tvāt karṣaka ādi pravṛtti vat 
[II,161,11]	na ca dṛṣṭa prayojana apekṣayā siddha sādhanam iti dūṣaṇam dṛṣṭam prayojanam anuddiśya iti pakṣa viśeṣaṇena nirasta tvāt ye tu dṛṣṭam eva uddiśya pravartate na te pakṣīkriyante iti na api adṛṣṭa phalena phalavat tvam sādhyate yena dṛṣṭāntaḥ sādhya vikalaḥ hetuḥ ca viruddhaḥ syāt kim tarhi sāmānyena abhipreta phalena phalavat tvam sādhyate tat ca karṣaka ādi pravṛttau asti eva iti na dṛṣṭāntasya sādhya vikala tvam viruddha tvam vā hetoḥ doṣaḥ 
[II,161,17]	sarva anumāneṣu samānañca viśeṣa viruddha anumānam iti anumāna mātrasya uccheda prasaṅgaḥ atha iṣyataḥ eva anumānasya aprāmāṇyam tathā ca sāmānye siddha sādhanam viśeṣe anugama abhāvaḥ dharmiṇoḥ ca samudāye sādhye na hetoḥ pakṣa dharma tvam na ca anvayaḥ samudāyasya anyatra āvṛtteḥ atha samudāya eka deśe api vartamānaḥ samudāye varteta iti upacaryate tarhi pramāṇasya gauṇa tvāt anumāna artha niścayaḥ durlabhaḥ tathā hi pramāṇam pratyakṣam gauṇam anumānam upacarita pakṣa dharma apekṣi tvāt gauṇam iti apramāṇam dharmasya api sādhya tve anvaya sadbhāve api na pakṣadhama tvam samudāyasya anyatra atha pratipādyamāna dharma viśiṣṭaḥ dharmī sādhyaḥ tena ca anvaya abhāvaḥ eva iti sarvam anumānam apramāṇam 
[II,161,26]	tat atat asat pratipādya dharma viśiṣṭasya dharmiṇaḥ sādhya tve pakṣa dharma tva upapatteḥ anvayaḥ tu sādhya samāna dharmeṇa nahi ekatra deśe hetoḥ vṛttiḥ vyatirekaḥ tu tad abhāve vyāvṛttiḥ iti liṅga upalambhāt ca sādhya dharmiṇi pratipatteḥ dṛṣṭa tvāt ittham bhūta anvaya parikalpanā kriyate anabhyupagame ca vyabhicāri jñānam eva na syāt tat tu dṛṣṭam iti viśeṣaḥ viruddhena tu niyata viśeṣa pratiṣedhe viśeṣa antara upagamaḥ syāt samasta viśeṣa pratiṣedhe tu tat niyatasya sāmānyasya api asiddhiḥ sādhana sāmānya vyāpakam vā avaśyam sādhya sāmānyam sidhyati iti atas sādhya sāmānyasya eva ākṣipta viśeṣasya eva anumānāt prasiddheḥ varṇa āśramiṇām phalantu adṛṣṭam viśeṣa atītam eva sidhyati iti 
[II,162,8_II,162,11]	śiṣya vyutpādanāya pramāṇa phala vibhāgam darśayati tatra liṅga darśanam pramāṇam anumeyam jñānam phalam prameyaḥ agniḥ pramātāḥ ātmā iti nanu liṅga darśanam vyadhikaraṇa tvāt katham agni jñāna utpattau pramāṇam vyāpāra apekṣayā tad viṣaya tvāt yathā hi dhūma jñānam dhūma viṣayam ātma lābha apekṣayā tathā agni pratipattau vyāpāra apekṣayā agni viṣayam api iti sva avayava samavetasya cakṣuṣaḥ samutpāde vyāpāra apekṣayā rūpa viṣaya tvam iva iti 
[II,162,17_II,163,1]	nanu evam ekasmin viṣaye vyāpāra apekṣayā karaṇa ādi vyavasthā anupapattiḥ vibhinna lakṣaṇa yogi tvena tad bhāvāt tathā hi pramādhāra tvam pramātuḥ lakṣaṇam uktam evam pramiteḥ viṣayaḥ prameyam tad vyatiriktañca pramājanakam pramāṇam tad sādhyañca phalam iti evam lakṣaṇa bhedāt eṣām bhedaḥ iti athavā iti pramāṇa phala vibhāge prakāra antaram āha agni jñānam eva pramāṇam pramitiḥ agnau guṇa doṣa mādhyasthya darśanam iti agni jñāne satya vinābhāva sambandha smaraṇāt parāmarśa jñānāt sukhaṃsādhana tva avabodhe sati upādeya jñānam duḥkha sādhanatva avabodhe ca heya jñānam yasya na idam sukha sādhanam na api duḥkha sādhanam iti evam bodhaḥ tasya upekṣaṇīya jñānam iti agni jñāna phala tvañca upādeya ādi jñānasya pāramparyeṇa iti pūrvavat vācyam iti etat sva niścaya artham anumānam iti upasaṃhāraḥ para artha anumāna saṃsūcakaḥ 
[II,163,3_II,163,16]	atha idānīm pramāṇa vibhāgasya nyūna tā parihārāya tad sāmānya lakṣaṇasya vyabhicāra parihāra artham śabda ādīnām api anumāne antarbhāvaḥ ityādi prakaraṇam nanu pūrvam anyeṣām anumāne antarbhāvasya anukta tvāt api śabda vaiyarthyam na anumāna padena abhisambandhāt na param pratyakṣaḥ eva anumāne api antarbhāvaḥ iti pramāṇa vibhāgaḥ ca vidyā vibhāga pareṇa api vākyena pūrvam upadarśitaḥ eva tatra ca śabda ādīnām api pramāṇānām sadbhāvāt anupapannaḥ ayam iti āśaṅkā tad vyudāsā artham antar bhāva prakaraṇam tathā śabda ādeḥ kāraka jātasya anumāna sāmagryām antarbhāve tad phalasya api phale antarbhāvaḥ jñāyate eva tatra śabdaḥ ādau yeṣām tāni tathā uktāni atas teṣām anumāne antarbhāvaḥ lakṣaṇa aikyam iti tad guṇa saṃvijñāna bahu vrīhi abhyupagame śabdasya api anumāne antarbhāvaḥ atad guṇa saṃvijñāne śabdam vinā apareṣām iti 
[II,163,19]	antarbhāva vyavahāre ca samāna vidhi tvāt samāna lakṣaṇa yogi tvāt iti hetu upanyāsaḥ katham sādhyāt na viśiṣyate lakṣaṇa eka tvasya tad vyavahārāt anya tvāt samānaḥ vidhiḥ upāyaḥ lakṣaṇam yeṣām tāni tathā uktāni teṣām bhāvaḥ tattvam tasmāt iti tat eva āha yathā prasiddha samayasya asan digdha liṅga darśana prasiddhi anusmaraṇābhyām atīndriye arthe bhavati anumānam evam śabda ādibhyaḥ api iti yathā hi gṛhīta sambandhasya liṅga darśana anantaram avinā abhau a sambandha smaraṇam tābhyām atīndriye arthe paricchedye bhavati anumānam anumīyate anena iti parāmarśa jñānam eva upacāreṇa vyutpattyā vā tat vivakṣitam evam śabda ādibhyaḥ api iti dārṣṭa antika vyākhyānam 
[II,164,1_II,164,4]	anye tu parāmarśa jñānasya asattvam eva iti manyante tat ca asat avinā abhau a sambandha smaraṇasya aniyata tvāt niyata deśe pratipattiḥ na syāt upanaya vaiyarthyañca iti uktam atas pūrvam eva nyāyyam atra tad guṇa saṃvijñāna pakṣe śabdasya api anumāne antarbhāvaḥ tathā ca śabda śravaṇāt samaya anusmaraṇe sati parāmarśa jñānam tasmāt parokṣa artha pratipattiḥ iti ayam go śabdaḥ kakudādimad arthavān go śabda tvāt pūrva upalabdhā evaṃvidha go śabda vat iti sambandha avagamena artha pratipādaka tvāt ca dhūma vat 
[II,164,8]	tat etat asat go śabdasya kakudādimad arthavattāyāḥ pratipādayitum aśakyatvāt tathā hi śabdasya arthena anya sambandha abhāvāt vācya vācaka tvena artha pratipādaka tve sādhye go śabda tvam ahetuḥ pratipādaka tvasya pratipatti avaseya tvāt svābhāvika sambandha anupapatteḥ ca dhūmaḥ hi svābhāvika sambandhena sarva prāṇabhṛtām anumeya artha pratipādakaḥ na ca evam śabdaḥ puruṣa icchā sampādita samaya apekṣasya artha pratipādaka tvāt svābhāvika sambandhe hi vinā api saṅketam mleccha ādi śabda śravaṇāt artha pratipattiḥ syāt saṅketa apekṣasya tu artha pratipādaka tve saḥ eva astu alam nitya sambandhena iti na ca nitya sambandha abhāve ati prasaṅgaḥ naimittika śabdānām dravya tva ādi nimitta sadbhāve sati eva saṅketāt yādṛcchika śabdānāntu puruṣa icchā anuvidhānāt iti yatra ca viśiṣṭa ānupūrvī mattva sadbhāvaḥ tat eva niyamena vācakam itarat ca vācyam iti vyavasthā saṅketa jñānasya ubhaya niṣṭhatva aviśeṣāt iti 
[II,164,20]	saṅketaḥ tu śabdāt vṛddha vyavahārataḥ ca pratīyate tathā hi idam asya vācakam idam asya vācyam iti vākyāt saṅketa pratipattiḥ vṛddha vyavahārāt yathā devadatta gām abhyāja śuklām daṇḍena iti prayogāt avyutpannaḥ anvaya vyatirekābhyām deva datta ādi śabdeṣu saṅketam pratipadyate vṛddha vyavahartṝṇām api saṅketa pratipattiḥ anyatas vyavahārāt iti anādi tvam parihāraḥ yat vā ādipuruṣaḥ sākṣāt draṣṭā keṣāñcid saṅketakartā asti iti vākya rūpaḥ tu śabdaḥ artha pratipattau samayam api na apekṣate iti sambandha balena artha pratipādaka tvam asiddham 
[II,165,1_II,165,6]	na ca śabdasya anumāna tvam eva niṣidhyate vivakṣā ākāśayoḥ adhigame liṅga tvāt yathā hi ākāśa adhigame sarvaḥ śabdaḥ anumānam vivakṣā kāryaḥ tu vivakṣā adhigame api iti na ca śabda jñāna vallaiṅgika jñānam āpta ukta tvam apekṣate tathā hi śabda jñāne kim idam samyak mithyā vā iti saṃśaya utpatta avāpta uktam anāpta uktam vā anvīkṣate laiṅgikantu pakṣa dharma tva ādikam iti vyatirekaḥ tat āha śruti smṛti lakṣaṇaḥ api āmnāyaḥ vaktṛ prāmāṇya apekṣaḥ iti na ca param laukikaḥ śabdaḥ vaktṛ prāmāṇyam apekṣate śruti smṛti lakṣaṇaḥ api iti 
[II,165,8]	nanu vaktṛ prāmāṇyena āmnāya prāmāṇya abhyupagame bahūnām anyaḥ anya āśraya tvam syāt tathā hi artha prāptyā āpta ukta tvam śabde niścīyate niścayāt ca artha avabodhe sati pravartamānasya artha prāptiḥ iti tathā pauruṣeye vacasi satyāsatya tva upalabdheḥ vede api puruṣa anupraveśe tad āśaṅkāyām aprāmāṇyam eva syāt na ca sākṣāt atīndriya artha draṣṭā puruṣaḥ sambhavati iti katham tad vācakāni vacāṃsi tad pūrvakāni iti 
[II,165,14_II,165,18]	yadi ca anyasmāt veda vākyāt artham pratipadya vacana racanām kuryāt tasya api nitya tvena kiñcid bādhitam syāt anitya tve tu tat kartuḥ api anyasmāt vākyāt artha avabodhaḥ iti anavasthā syāt na ca anitya tvam veda vākyānām pramāṇa prasiddham iti katham vaktṛ viśeṣa apekṣam prāmāṇyam artha pratipattau ca śabdasya sva abhidhā śakti balena eva vyāpāraḥ na āpta ukta tvam apekṣamāṇasya iti sā ca tasya sva ātma bhūtā eva na paścāt pareṇa sampādyate iti svatas eva prāmāṇyam na ca āpta ukta tvam śakyate pratipattum pratibandha ādeḥ aviṣaya tvāt aprāmāṇyantu duṣṭa puruṣa praṇīta tva apekṣam iti paratas 
[II,165,22_II,166,3]	tathā sarva pramāṇānām api prāmāṇye na para apekṣitā sambhavati sva kāraṇebhyaḥ artha avabodha svarūpāṇām utpatteḥ yadi ca avidyamānam artha paricchedaka tvam pariniṣpanne vijñāne kāraka antarāt utpadyate pratipadyemahi paratas prāmāṇyam na ca etat asti iti āha svatas sarva pramāṇānām prāmāṇyam iti gṛhyatām na hi svatas asatī śaktiḥ kartum anyena śakyate na ca jñānasya artha paricchedaka tvam kāraṇa guṇa pūrvakam indriyeṣu tad abhāvāt tat āha vyāpāraḥ kārakāṇām hi dṛṣṭaḥ janma atirekataḥ pramāṇe api tathā mā bhūt iti janma vivakṣyate 
[II,166,7]	yathā hi indriyāṇām janma vyatirekeṇa aparaḥ vyāpāraḥ na evam jñānasya anantaram eva phala sampādaka tvāt dṛṣṭañca pareṇa api viśeṣaṇa ādi jñānasya viśeṣya ādi jñāna janmani prāmāṇyam iti atha upajātam api jñānam na kāraka pariśuddheḥ bodham vinā artha paricchedaka tva bhāj tarhi tatra api kāraka pariśuddhi grahaṇam vācyam iti anavasthā tat āha jāte api yadi vijñāne tāvat na arthaḥ avadhāryate yāvat kāraṇa śuddha tvam na pramāṇa antara āgatam tatra jñāna antara utpādaḥ pratīkṣyaḥ kāraṇa antarāt yāvat hi na paricchinnā śuddhiḥ tāvat asat samā tasya api kāraṇe śuddhe tad jñānasya pramāṇa tā tasya api evam iti itthañca na kaścid vyavatiṣṭhate 
[II,166,18_II,166,23]	atha vidyamānam api pramāṇasya prāmāṇyam na pramāṇa antara saṃvādam vinā pramāṇa vyavahāra kāraṇam tarhi pramāṇa paramparāyām apakṣīṇa śakteḥ vivakṣita jñāne pramāṇa vyavahāraḥ na syāt tat āha sammatyā yadi ca iṣyeta pūrva pūrva pramāṇa tā pramāṇa antaram icchantaḥ na vyavasthām labhemahi yadi ca kasyacid svatas eva prāmāṇyam iṣyeta param ādyasya eva astu iti āha kasyacid tu yadīṣyeta svatas eva pramāṇa tā prathamasya tathā abhāve pradveṣaḥ kim nibandhanaḥ 
[II,167,1_II,167,5]	prathama uttarayoḥ paraspara apekṣam prāmāṇyam iti abhyupagame ca itaretara āśraya tvam syāt atas svatas eva prāmāṇyam aprāmāṇyantu paratas tathā hi laukikānām eva śabdānām aprāmāṇyam puruṣa doṣa anupraveśāt vaidikānāntu tad abhāvāt aprāmāṇya śaṅkā eva na asti iti atha indriyāṇām kāca kāmalā ādi doṣa vaśāt aprāmāṇyam na svarūpataḥ tathā hi kāca kāmalā ādi doṣa sadbhāve sati mithyājñāna janaka tvam na tad abhāvaḥ iti 
[II,167,7]	jñaptau ca avabodhaka tvena mithyāmateḥ autsargika māna tvam na nivṛttam iti bādhaka pratyayāt mithyātva avagatau vyāvartate na ca asmad pakṣe śuktikā jñānena api aśuktikā jñānasya bādhāyām anavasthā kāraka śuddhi grahaṇa paramparā vā iti vācyam avabodhaka tvena autsargikasya pramāṇa tvasya doṣa adarśana mātreṇa eva anavasthānāt tat āha yadā svatas pramāṇa tvam tadā anyam na eva mṛgyate nivartate ca mithyātvam doṣa jñānāt ayatnataḥ doṣa jñāne tu anutpanne na āśaṅkā niṣpramāṇikā evam tri catur ajñāna janmanaḥ na adhikā matiḥ iti anavasthā parihāraḥ 
[II,167,17]	tat etat sarvam avidita artham sarva pramāṇānām utpattau jñaptau ca para apekṣita upalabdheḥ tathā hi āpta ukta tvam apekṣamāṇaḥ śabdaḥ arthe samyak jñānam upajanayati na tad antareṇa iti dṛṣṭam yat ca bahūnām anyonya āśraya tvam uktam tat na yuktam āpta ukta tvasya āgṛhyamāṇasya eva śabda sahakāri tva abhyupagamāt artha prāptau ca pramāṇa antareṇa paścāt tat grahaṇam iṣyate eva tathā hi laukika śabdānām artha prāpti āpta ukta tvam niścīyate pratyakṣeṇa api gṛhyate iti anye tathā ca śrotra vyāpārāt vākya śravaṇe sati cāṇakyā uktam kāli dāsa uktañca etat iti abādhyamānaḥ pratyayaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ vadika vākyānāntu pradhāna artheṣu avisaṃvādāt āpta ukta tva niścayaḥ 
[II,167,25]	yadi pauruṣeye vacasi dvaividhya upalabdheḥ vede api puruṣa anupraveśe aprāmāṇya śaṅkā syāt iti dūṣaṇam tat na tad kartuḥ doṣa abhāvāt tathā hi yasya rāga ādi doṣaḥ asti tad vacanam eva apramāṇam iti upalabdham veda kartuḥ ca tad sadbhāve pramāṇa abhāvaḥ sākṣāt atīndriya artha draṣṭā puruṣaḥ sambhavati iti uktam adhastāt atas tad vacanāt āmnāyasya prāmāṇyam iti sūtrakāreṇa uktam 
[II,168,4]	atha śabdasya anitya tve satya āpta ukta tvena prāmāṇyam syāt tat tu na asti iti āśaṅkya āha liṅgāt ca anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti param pratyakṣeṇa uccāraṇāt prāk ūrdhvañca anupalambhāt anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti pratīyate liṅgāt ca iti tat tu vakṣyāmaḥ śabda parīkṣāyām veda an āñca anitya tve anumānam anityāni veda vākyāni vākya tvāt ubhaya abhimata vākya vat tathā buddhi pūrvā vākya kṛtiḥ vākya racanā vede buddhiḥ pūrvā vākya racanā tvāt ubhaya abhimata vākya racanā vat yat ca idam veda racanāyāḥ sarvadā anyathātva upalambhāt iti vaidhamyeṇa pratyavasthānam tat sarva anumāneṣu samānam iti evam buddhi pūrvaḥ dadātiḥ vede buddhi pūrvaḥ dadāti śabdaḥ dadāti iti ukta tvāt ubhaya abhimata dadātī iti śabda vat 
[II,168,14]	yā ca iyam puruṣa anupraveśe satya prāmāṇya śaṅkā sā nitya tve api na nivartate śrotuḥ puruṣasya tatra api anupraveśāt tad vaiguṇyena ca aprāmāṇya upalabdheḥ tathā hi śroturapratibhādeḥ mithyā jñāna utpattau kāraṇa tvam tad abhāvaḥ ca samyak jñāna utpattau iti upalabdham eva na ca nitya tvam vedānām ekāntena prāmāṇya hetuḥ tad bhāve api śrotra antaḥkaraṇayoḥ pratipattṛ doṣa anupraveśena kvacid aprāmāṇyāt 
[II,168,19_II,168,24]	sva abhidhā śakti balena eva śabdasya prāmāṇyam iti abhyupagame ca aṅguli agre kariṇaḥ tiṣṭhanti iti evamādeḥ aprāmāṇyam na syāt atha anāpta praṇīta tvena visaṃvādāt aprāmāṇyam eṣām tarhi yat āpta praṇītam tat eva pramāṇam iti prāptam yathā hi puruṣa gatasya rāga ādeḥ aprāmāṇye anvaya vyatirekābhyām vyāpāraḥ tathā tad guṇa ādeḥ prāmāṇye api iti ubhayam paratas abhidhānasya ca varṇa ānupūrvī saṅketa vyatirekeṇa atīndriyā śaktiḥ na vidyate tasyāḥ pūrvam eva pratiṣedhāt varṇa tva ādi sadbhāve ca kārya karaṇāt sa ca paratas eva pratiniyata jāti sambandhasya adṛṣṭa kāryatvāt saṅketasya api anyat kāraṇam uktam iti 
[II,169,1]	yat tu sākṣāt darśana ādiḥ puruṣasya rāga ādi vināśe vyāpriyate na jñāna utpattau iti uktam tat asat samyak jñāna utpattau anvaya vyatireka upapatteḥ yathārtha draṣṭā tad śiṣyāṇām upadeṣṭā ca iti samuditam āpta lakṣaṇam yathārtha upadeśe hetuḥ tad antareṇa anupadeśāt yadi ca anvaya vyatirekavataḥ api yathā artha darśi tvāde rāga ādi vināśaḥ eva vyāpāraḥ tarhi rāga ādeḥ api etat vināśaka tvam eva iti ubhayam paratas syāt tasmāt rāgdera prāmāṇya utpattau iva yathārtha upalambha ādeḥ api samyak jñāna utpattau vyāpāraḥ abhyupagantavyaḥ 
[II,169,8]	tathā indriyāṇām api kāca kāmalā ādi doṣa sadbhāve api mithyājñānam eva tad bhāve samyak jñāna jananāt ubhayam paratas pareṇa api abhāvasya kāraṇa tvam anekadheṣṭam yathā sat upalambhaka pramāṇa pañcaka vyāvṛtteḥ mānasa jñāna utpattau pakṣa dharmatā ādi anyatama apāye ca liṅgasya mithyājñāna utpattau ityādi atha kācakāmalā ādeḥ doṣasya mithyājñāna utpattau kāraṇatā upalabdheḥ tad abhāve tasya eva anupalabdhiḥ na samyak jñānam iti ced na anvaya vyatirekavataḥ akāraṇa tve ati prasaṅgāt tathā ca doṣa abhāve anvaya vyatirekavān api na samyak jñāna utpattau kāraṇam tad sadbhāve api na mithyājñāna utpattau iti ubhayam svatas syāt sargaḥ ca indriyāṇām ubhaya rūpasya kāryasya upalabdheḥ ubhaya artham iti jñāyeta 
[II,169,17]	nanu doṣa sadbhāve sati indriyam mithyājñānam janayati tad abhāve ca samyak jñānam iti abhyupagamāt ubhaya abhāve ca ubhaya vikalam vijñānam kuryāt iti etat acodyam ubhaya vikalasya indriyasya asambhavāt yathā hi pūrvam asatām doṣāṇām utpattiḥ ūrdhvañca pradhvaṃsaḥ iti na asti ubhaya vikalam indriyam na ca ubhaya viśeṣa vikalam jñāna tva sāmānyam sambhavati sāmānyavataḥ viśeṣa yogāt yathā go tva sāmānya ādhārasya śāvaleya ādi viśeṣaḥ iti 
[II,169,22]	yat ca idam na kāraṇa guṇa pūrvakam paricchedaka tvam tat iṣyate eva anubhava jñānasya indriyāt utpannasya artha paricchitti rūpa tvāt tad jana kañca indriya ādi kārakam kāraka antara apekṣañca iti paratas prāmāṇyam kāraka sāmagryantu na paścāt abhāvi nimittam apekṣate iti tad apekṣayā tu ubhayam svatas iti na mithyājñānam paratas syāt 
[II,170,1]	atha jñātṛ vyāpāraḥ jñānam tat ca artha paricchede anapekṣam iti svatas tad mithyā jñāne api samānam atha mithyājñānam doṣam apekṣate tarhi samyak jñānam api tad abhāva ādi apekṣate iti na ca jñātṛ vyāpāraḥ sambhāvyate artha pratipatteḥ anyathā bhāvāt tathā hi sarvam kārakam caramasahakāri sadbhāve sati kāryam karoti iti na tasmāt anyaḥ vyāpāraḥ sadbhāve api nityatāyām sarva kārya utpatti prasaṅgaḥ tasya anapekṣa kāraṇa tva abhyupagamāt anitya tve tu tad utpattau api nirvyāpārasya kāraṇa tva ayogāt anyaḥ vyāpāraḥ tad utpattau api anyaḥ iti anavasthā syāt caramasahakāri rūpe tu vyāpāre na ayam doṣaḥ tad sadbhāve kārya karaṇam na tad abhāvaḥ iti 
[II,170,10_II,170,17]	yat ca idam kāraka śuddheḥ grahaṇa apekṣitāyām dūṣaṇam tad apāstam anabhyupagame na iti atha pramāṇasya prāmāṇyam vinā eva pramāṇam vijñāyate iti tat asat sarvasya prameyasya pramāṇa paricchedyatva upalabdheḥ tathā ca prāmāṇyam pramāṇa paricchedyam prameya tvāt ghaṭa ādi vat na ca anavasthā sarvatra avaśyam prāmāṇya grahaṇa anabhyupagamāt yatra hi jñāna udaye sati kim idam samyak mithyā vā iti saṃśaya utpattiḥ tatra eva pramāṇa antara apekṣā artha prāpti paryanta vyavahāra sambhave vai apekṣā vinivṛtteḥ na anavasthā ādi doṣaḥ yadi ca jñāna dharma tvāt prāmāṇyasya sva saṃvedya tvam iṣyeta aprāmāṇyam api evam syāt iti katham paratas tathā mithyājñāna utpāde na pravartate mithyātvasya pratipanna tvāt samyak jñāna utpattau ca samyakta adhyavasāye kim idam samyak mithyā vā iti saṃśaya ādi abhāvaḥ 
[II,170,21_II,171,1]	yat ca idam avabodhaka tvena pramāṇasya prāmāṇyam doṣa adarśana mātreṇa eva avatiṣṭhate iti uktam tatra yadi doṣa adarśana doṣa jñāna anutpattiḥ na tayā prāmāṇyam jñāpyate na api kriyate iti katham aniścita sthiteḥ avasthāna vacanam atha doṣa darśanasya bādhaka pratyayasya mithyātva jñāpaka tvam iva tad abhāva jñānasya prāmāṇyajñāpaka tvam iṣyeta tarhi tasya api prāmāṇyam anyasmāt vijñāyate iti anavasthā syāt atha jñāna utpattau saṃśayam vinā na sarvatra prāmāṇya grahaṇa apekṣā iti parihāraḥ tarhi na svatas prāmāṇyam utpattau jñaptau ca para apekṣi tva abhyupagamāt atha indriya ādi kārakeṣu vidyamānam samyaktvam na kāraṇa guṇa prakrameṇa jñāneṣu utpadyate iti svatas tad aprāmāṇye api samānam tatra api hi viparyaya ādi rūpa tā na indriya ādiṣu vidyamānā jāyate iti 
[II,171,4]	bodha ātmaka pramāṇa apekṣayā tu svatas prāmāṇyam vivakṣitam iti abhyupagamasya codanāyāḥ vaktṛ viśeṣa apekṣam prāmāṇyam iti abhyupagamena avirodhāt avivādaḥ eva syāt asya hi samarthana artham anya pramāṇānām paratas prāmāṇya upadarśanāt na ca codanāyāḥ svatas prāmāṇya abhyupagame codanā janitam jñānam pramāṇam doṣa varjitaiḥ kārakaiḥ janyamāna tvāt liṅgāt pratyakṣa buddhi vat iti parīkṣā artham prayāsaḥ ghaṭate atha apareṣām vyāmoha vyāvartana dvāreṇa samyak jñāna sampādana artham parīkṣā vākyam tad janita jñāne api vyāmohe sati anyā parīkṣā syāt iti anavasthā sā ca ukta nyāyena eva parihriyate iti katham na paratas pramāṇasya prāmāṇyam utpadyate jñāyate vā iti 
[II,171,12_II,171,14]	śeṣañcā atra dūṣaṇa pratisamādhānam asmad gurubhiḥ vistareṇa abhihitam iti na iha uktam atas śabdasya āpta ukta tvena prāmāṇyāt na anumāne antarbhāvaḥ atha śabdānām arthena pratibandha abhāvāt aprāmāṇyam eva tathā ca dṛśya vikalpyau arthau ekīkṛtya tad samāropeṇa śrotuḥ pravṛtti nivṛttī iti uktam yaḥ ayam vikalpa gataḥ ākāraḥ saḥ eva bāhyaḥ arthaḥ iti manyamānaḥ pratipattā pravartate na bāhya artha pratipattau artha darśane sati vivakṣā krameṇa śabda utpatti kāle arthasya kṣaṇika tvena atikrānta tvāt 
[II,171,19_II,171,22]	pratyakṣa anumāna viṣaya atiriktā viṣaya abhāvāt ca na śabdaḥ pramāṇa antaram tathā hi sva lakṣaṇa viṣayam pratyakṣam sāmānya viṣayam anumānam prameya dvaividhyāt pramāṇa dvaividhyam iti katham śabdaḥ artha antara tve sati pramāṇam yadi ca indriyeṇa samāna viṣayaḥ śabdaḥ bhavet andha anandhayoḥ aviśeṣaḥ syāt tat āha anya deva indriya grāhyam anyaḥ śabdasya gocaraḥ śabdāt pratyeti bhinna akṣaḥ na tu pratyakṣam īkṣate 
[II,171,26_II,172,7]	anyat eva rūpa ādi sva lakṣaṇam indriya grāhyam tasmāt anyaḥ śabdasya gocaraḥ apoha viṣayaḥ iti gṛhyatām yatas śabdāt pratyeti bhinna akṣaḥ pradhvasta nayanaḥ na tu pratyakṣam yathā bhavati tathā īkṣate samāna viṣaya tve vā anandhasya iva andhasya api śabdāt aparokṣā eva pratipattiḥ syāt tathā tve indriya agni sambandha ādi vat dāha śabdāt api dāha artha pratipattiḥ syāt iti āha anyathā eva agni sambandhāt dāham dagdhaḥ abhimanyate anyathā dāha śabdena dāha arthaḥ sampratīyate tasmāt na indriyeṇa samāna viṣaya tvam śabdasya tathā pada ādi śabdasya sva lakṣaṇa viṣaya tve tasya nirbhāga tayā śukla ādi śabdānām api paryāyatā bhavet apoha viṣaya tve tu na ayam doṣaḥ vibhinnānām samāropa vyavaccheda paratvāt iti 
[II,172,10]	vāstava artha viṣaya tve ca śabdānām puruṣa icchā vaśena aniyata artha tvam na syāt vyavahāraḥ tu śabdāt mayā pratipannam śabdena ca pratipādayāmi iti pratipādya pratipādakayoḥ tamirika dvaya dvi candra darśana vat bhaviṣyati iti yathā ekaḥ taimirikaḥ candra dvayam pratipadya pratipādayati aparaḥ ca pratipadyate tathā sarvatra vyavahartṝṇa ām ayam śabdaḥ vyavahāraḥ iti atha parīkṣakāḥ tarhi śabda artha adhyavasāye sati mithyātvam manyamānāḥ pravartante loka vyavahāra anusāritayā loka vyavahāram prati sadṛśau bāla paṇḍitau iti nyāyāt mithyājñānasya ca artha pratipādaka tvam kvacid upalabdham yathā maṇi pradīpa prabhayoḥ maṇi buddhyā abhidhāvatoḥ mithyā jñāna aviśeṣe api viśeṣaḥ artha kriyām prati 
[II,172,19_II,172,23]	tat etat asat śabdāt artha adhyavasāye sati pravartamānasya artha avisaṃvādena akṣaja jñāna vat abhrānta tvena prāmāṇya upapatteḥ tathā hi indriya jñānasya api samyaktve na artha avisaṃvādam vinā pramāṇa antaram asti sa ca śābda jñāne api asti iti katham apramāṇam pratibandhaḥ api kārya viśeṣa upalabdheḥ indriyāṇām iva śabdasya api arthena vācyaḥ sa ca vācya vācaka ālambanam saṅketa jñānam eva anyasya asambhavāt tasya ca viśeṣāṇām ānantye api eka sāmānyasya upagrahāt upapattiḥ iti uktam eva yadi ca śabdānām aprāmāṇyam pramāṇa ādi svarūpa avabodha artham śāstram anarthakam syāt pramāṇa ādi svarūpasya pāramparyeṇa api tasmāt apratīteḥ 
[II,173,1_II,173,11]	yadi ca vivakṣā sūcaka tvena eva prāmāṇyam iṣyeta tarhi sarva vākyānām tatra avyabhicārāt aviśeṣeṇa prāmāṇye vādi prativādinoḥ vivāde jaya parājaya vyavasthā na syāt atha yat vākyam artha pratibaddhām vivakṣām sūcayati tat eva pramāṇam na sarvam iti ced na śabda vat vivakṣāṇām api ekāntena artha pratibandha abhāvāt tathā ca artha darśana anusmaraṇa krameṇa vivakṣā kāle na arthasya avasthānam asti iti atas bāhya artha adhyavasāye sati eva pravartante na dṛśya vikalpyau arthau ekīkṛtya tad samāropeṇa iti na ca dṛśyasya anupalabdheḥ vikalpyenakīkaraṇam yuktam upalabhyamāna padārthe hi candra ādau dvi tva ādi samāropasya anyatra upalabdheḥ śabda artha pratipattau bādhaka anupapatteḥ ca mṛṣā eṣā kalpanā yat ca idam vivakṣā krameṇa śabda utpatti kāle na arthasya avasthānam asti iti tad apāstam kṣaṇika tva anabhyupagamena 
[II,173,13]	atha sāmānya viśeṣa vyatirikta viṣaya abhāvāt apramāṇa tvam śabdānām tat asat ekāntena pramāṇeṣu vyavasthā anabhyupagamāt tathā ca āgamāt ātmā pratīyate punar utpāda liṅgaiḥ yoga balāt ca pratyakṣataḥ api iti saṃplavaḥ kvacid vyavasthā ca yathā āgamasya medhya amedhya pratipattau indriyāṇām sva viṣayeṣu iti atas pratyakṣa ādi viṣaye api śabdasya pravṛtteḥ na viṣaya antara abhāvaḥ tad aprāmāṇye hetuḥ iti viṣaya dvaividhyena ca pramāṇa dvi tva avadhāraṇe dūṣaṇam gurubhiḥ vistareṇa abhihitam iti na iha ucyate 
[II,173,20]	yat tu śabdānām sva lakṣaṇa viṣaya tve andha anandhayoḥ aviśeṣa prasaṅgaḥ iti uktam tat asat viṣaya eka tve api karaṇa bhedena pratipattyoḥ bhedāt andhasya hi śabdāt rūpa viṣayam vijñānam utpadyate na tu cākṣuṣam iti yasya ca aparokṣam cākṣuṣam vijñānam asti asau anandhaḥ śabdaḥ hi vyavahitam api artham prakāśayati sannikṛṣṭañca indriyam iti anayoḥ vibhinna pratipatti janaka tvam 
[II,173,25]	yat tu tvac indriya agni sambandhāt iva dāha śabdāt api dāha arthaḥ sampratīyeta iti uktam tatra yadi dāhaḥ duḥkham tat pratīyate eva dāha śabdāt na ca evam śrotuḥ duḥkhi tva prasaṅgaḥ duḥkha asamavāyāt yasya hi duḥkham samavetam upajātam saḥ eva duḥkhī na tu dāha śabdāt ātmani samavetam duḥkham utpadyate kim tarhi parātma samavetam api tatas vijānāti iti sphoṭa ādi lakṣaṇaḥ tu dāhaḥ tvacaḥ agni sambandhāt upajāyate na dāha śabdāt iti tasmāt edhā agni sambandhāt utpanna sphoṭa ādi kāryaḥ tad janita duḥkham ātma antaḥkaraṇa sambandhāt anubhavati iti duḥkhī iti atidiśyate dāha śabdañca anyathā eva anutpanna sphoṭa ādi kāryaḥ duḥkham parātma gatam pratipadyate iti adūṣaṇam etat 
[II,174,8_II,174,12]	na ca sva lakṣaṇasya nirbhāga tayā śukla ādi śabdānām paryāyatva prasaṅgaḥ dharma dharmiṇoḥ vyatirekāt pratyaya bhedasya bheda lakṣaṇa tvāt iti uktam tasmāt bhinna pravṛtti nimittānām śabdānām ekārtha tve api na paryāya tvam iti na ca apohaḥ śabda arthaḥ tasya eva asambhavāt iti vakṣyāmaḥ yat tu vāstava artha viṣaya tve puruṣa icchā vaśena aniyata artha tvam na syāt iti tat asat naimittika śabdānām nimitta vaśena pravṛtteḥ na aniyata artha tvam yādṛt chikānāntu puruṣa icchā vaśena aniyata artha tvam iṣyate eva bādhaka anupapatteḥ ca na taimirikasya dvi candra darśana vat śā abdaḥ vyavahāraḥ tathā hi taimirikasya dvi candra darśane timira utpatteḥ prāk ūrdhvañca bādhakam asti anupajāta timirasya tu sarvadā na ca evam śabda vyavahāre 
[II,174,18_II,174,25]	yat tu mithyājñāna aviśeṣe api artha kriyā siddhiḥ yathā maṇi pradīpa prabhayoḥ iti uktam tad aparijñānāt tathā hi samīpa vartinaḥ yat maṇau eva vijñānam tat eva artha kriyā janakam na prabhāyām iti śābda jñānantu artha prāpti paryanta vyavahāra upalabdheḥ indriya ja jñāna vat bhrāntam na bhavati iti na ca vāstava sambandha abhāve śabdānām aśva śabdāt aśva adhyavasāyaḥ go śabdāt ca gavya dhyavasāyaḥ iti vikalpa niyamaḥ ghaṭate dṛṣṭaḥ ca asau iti tathā aśva śabde api sambandha agrahe sambandhi pratyayaḥ na syāt iti alam ati vistareṇa tat evam tādātmya tad utpatti pratibandhasya pūrvam eva pratiṣedhāt śabdānāntu samaya vaśena artha pratipādaka tvāt upapannam anumānāt artha antara tve sati prāmāṇyam iti 
[II,175,3_II,175,4]	atha ceṣṭā pramāṇa antaram iti kecid tad niṣedha artham āha prasiddha abhinayasya ceṣṭayā pratipatti darśanāt tat api anumānam eva prasiddhaḥ abhinayaḥ ceṣṭā kāyikaḥ vyāpāraḥ artha viśeṣa a inābhūtaḥ yasya asau tathā uktaḥ tasya ceṣṭayā artha viśeṣe pratipattiḥ yathā mukha añjali saṃyogāt viśiṣṭāt pipāsā pratipattiḥ tasya tayā pūrvam avinā abhāva upalabdheḥ tathā ca ayam pipāsā anvitaḥ viśiṣṭa mukha añjali saṃyogavat tvāt tad anyā evaṃvidha deva datta vat atas pakṣa dharma tva ādi balena gamaka tvāt etat api anumānam eva iti evam anyā api ceṣṭā nāṭya śāstra prasiddhā anumāne antar bhāvanīya iti 
[II,175,12_II,175,13]	atha upamānam pramāṇa antaram iti kecid tad niṣedha artham āha āptena aprasiddha gavayasya gavā gavaya pratipādanāt upamānam āpta vacanam eva iti āptena prasiddha goga vaya sārūpyeṇa aprasiddha gavayasya gavā gavaya pratipādanāt iti yathā gauḥ evam gavayaḥ iti upamānam iṣṭam tat āpta vacanam eva na pramāṇa antaram iti na ca asya upamā rūpa tvāt pramāṇa antara tvam vidhi artha vāda ādi bhedena api pramāṇa ānantya prasaṅgāt atha sati api avāntara bhede na amīṣām āpta upadeśāt bhedaḥ tad upamāne api samānam 
[II,175,20]	atha vākyāt upalabdha sādṛśyasya aṭavyām aṭataḥ gavaya arthinaḥ madīyā gauḥ anena sadṛśī iti jñānam upamānam asat etat phala abhāvāt ajñāna nivṛttiḥ phalam iti uktam nivṛtteḥ pradhvaṃsa tvāt tathā hi yadi jñāna anutpattiḥ viparītam vā jñānam ajñānam ubhayathā api tad nivṛttiḥ pradhvaṃsaḥ eva pramājana kañca pramāṇam na ca heya ādi buddhayaḥ phalam tad apāye sati kāla antareṇa sukha duḥkha ādi viniścaya anantaram utpatteḥ na ca sādṛśyasya prameya tvam tat jñānasya aphala tvāt abhyupagame vai anyat pramāṇam vācyam iti 
[II,176,1_II,176,10^1]	atha gavaya jñānam upamānam madīyā gauḥ anena sadṛśī iti jñāna phalam sādṛśya avacchinnaḥ piṇḍaḥ tad avacchinnam vā sādṛśyam prameyam iti na ca idam jñānam indriya jam aṭavyām vyavasthitasya gṛha avasthita piṇḍa viṣaya tvena utpatteḥ na ca anumāna jam liṅga vyāpāra anupalabdheḥ gosādṛśyantu gavaye gṛhyamāṇam api asiddham vyadhikaraṇa tvāt tathā ca madīyā gauḥ anena sadṛśī asya tad sadṛśa tvāt iti vyadhikaraṇa tā eva anupapadyamānasya arthasya abhāvāt na artha āpatti jam śabdam vinā api utpatteḥ na śābdam abhāvasya ca niyata viṣaya tvam na ca idam smaraṇam gavaya sādṛśyasya gopiṇḍe pūrvam ananubhūta tvāt atas pramāṇa antara phalam etat iti āśayaḥ parasya yadi ca gosādṛśya avacchinnam gavaya piṇḍam indriya artha sannikarṣāt eva upalabhyate tadā pratyakṣa phalam eva na pramāṇa antara phalam tatra kim smaraṇa apekṣam indriyam evam jñānam janayati anapekṣam vā 
[II,176,10^2]	anapekṣasya jñāna janaka tve aprasiddha gopiṇḍasya smaraṇe api etat syāt atha piṇḍa mātra smaraṇe aśva ādi piṇḍa smaraṇe api syāt atha gavaya sādṛśya avacchinna smaraṇa apekṣam janakam tatra api yadi smaraṇa mātram apekṣeta gaja ādi smaraṇe api syāt atha gopiṇḍa smaraṇa apekṣam tatra api kim gopiṇḍa mātra smaraṇam apekṣate gavaya sādṛśya avacchinnam gopiṇḍa smaraṇam vā gopiṇḍa mātra smaraṇe aśva ādi piṇḍe api syāt gavaya sādṛśya avacchinna go piṇḍa smaraṇa apekṣi tve pūrvam eva anubhavaḥ vācyaḥ tad antareṇa saṃskārānutpatteḥ smaraṇasya eva abhāvāt atas sa vikalpaka jñāna abhāve api gavaya sādṛśya avacchinne gopiṇḍe pūrvam anubhavaḥ abhyupagantavyaḥ yena hi saṃskāra utpattau smaraṇāt madīyayā gavā sadṛśaḥ ayam gavayaḥ iti jñānam syāt pūrvañca gavaya sādṛśya avacchinna gopiṇḍe anubhava prasiddhau gavaya upalambhāt madīyā gauḥ anena sadṛśī iti katham etat smaraṇam na syāt tathā pṛṣṭaḥ bravīti etad sadṛśī mayā upalabdhā na tu pramāṇa antaram nirdiśati iti manyamānaḥ praśastaḥ bhagavān antarbhāva māha iti 
[II,176,25]	anye tu yathā gauḥ gavayaḥ tathā iti vanecara vākyāt sādṛśya upalambhe sati upajāta saṃskārasya aṭavyām paribhramataḥ go śādṛśya avacchinna gavaya darśane sati avinā abhā a sambandha smaraṇa anantaram tathā ca ayam go sadṛśaḥ iti jñānam upamānam manyante tasmāt ca anantaram gavayanāmā ayam iti saṃjñā saṃjñi sambandha pratipattiḥ phalam saṃjñā saṃjñi rūpam saṃjñā avacchinnaḥ vā piṇḍaḥ prameyam iti na ca vākyāt eva saṅketa pratipattiḥ gavaya piṇḍasya parokṣa tvāt pratyakṣam saṃjñā karmaḥ iti sūtra vyāghātāt ca 
[II,177,5]	na yuktam etat vākyāt eva saṅketasya pratīta tvāt tathā hi sādṛśya vākyasya ayam arthaḥ yaḥ go sadṛśaḥ sa gavayaḥ iti evam vyavahartavyaḥ sa ca vākyāt upalabdha saṅketaḥ sādṛśya avacchinnam piṇḍam upalabhamānaḥ param vyavaharati ayam gavayaḥ iti na tu saṅketam pratipadyate pratipiṇḍam anyatra api saṅketa prasaṅgāt tathā hi yatra yatra go tvam paśyasi tatra tatra go śabdaḥ prayoktavyaḥ tasmāt ca asau arthaḥ pratipattavyaḥ iti saṅketa grahe sati gopiṇḍa upalambha āt ayam gauḥ iti pratipadyate na tu gonāmā ayam iti vyavahāra abhāva prasaṅgāt na tu sūtra vyāghātaḥ pratyakṣa śabdasya dṛḍha pramāṇa upalakṣaṇa tvāt dṛḍha pramāṇa paricchinne arthe saṃjñā pravartate yathā deśa antara vyavasthitaḥ api pitā sva putrasya nāma karoti yajñadatta nāma asau iti 
[II,177,15]	atha jāti śabdasya pratyakṣaḥ eva arthe saṅketaḥ na atīndriyeṣu asaṅketa prasaṅgāt dṛṣṭañca manaḥ śabdasya atīndriye api manasi dṛḍha pramāṇa paricchinne saṅketaḥ tathā ayam gavayaḥ iti katham punarbhavān jānāti iti pareṇa pṛṣṭaḥ vanecareṇa mama ākhyātam iti vacanam eva nirdiśati na tu sādṛśyāt pratipannam iti kārakeṇa ca vyapadeśaḥ yathā cakṣuṣā pratipannam anumānāt ca pratipannam iti tathā nirviṣaya vācya pramāṇam upamānam atha asti saṃjñā saṃjñi rūpam prameyam na sambandha pratipatteḥ phalatve sambandhinaḥ prameya tva anupapatteḥ atha sambandhaḥ iva sambandhinaḥ pratipattiḥ eva ubhaya niṣṭhatayā upacāreṇa abhidhīyate tathā api na saṃjñā saṃjñi rūpam prameyam saṃjñāyāḥ tad abhāvāt atha svayam uccārya śabdam pratipadyate na vivakṣā krameṇa śabda utpatti kāle sādṛśya jñānasya pramāṇasya asambhavāt atha jagataḥ vistīrṇa tayā kvacid utpannaḥ gavaya śabdaḥ prameyaḥ na tasya aśrūyamāṇasya prameya tva anupapatteḥ atha apratibandha nyāyena dūra sthasya āgamane brahma bhāṣitasya āgamanam syāt 
[II,178,1]	na ca sannihitaḥ kvacid tadā eva śabdam uccarati asaṃvedanāt atha smṛti samāropitasya gavaya śabdasya prameya tvam na tad kalpanāyām kāraṇa abhāvāt sādṛśya jñāna anantaram ayam gavayanāma iti pratipadyate na ca antarāle tad smṛteḥ anupraveśe pramāṇam asti iti saṃjñā avacchinnasya tu piṇḍasya prameya tvena sambandha jñānam syāt tasya ubhaya ālambana tvāt iti tathā pareṇa api anumānāt upamānasya bhedam upadarśayatā yathā tathā iti upasaṃhārāt upamāna siddheḥ na aviśeṣaḥ iti vākya rūpam upamānam iṣṭam ava tasya ca āgame antarbhāvaḥ na doṣāya iti 
[II,178,8_II,178,9]	atha arthāpatteḥ anumāne antar bhāva artham darśana arthāt arthāpattiḥ tat api anumānam eva iti vākyam dṛśyate iti darśanam tasmāt upalabhyamānāt arthāt anyathā anupapadyamānāt arthasya āptiḥ prāptiḥ prasaṅgaḥ iti tat uktam pramāṇa ṣaṭka vijñātaḥ yatra arthaḥ na anyathā bhavet adṛṣṭam kalpayet anyā sārtha āpattiḥ udāhṛtā iti ṣaṭ bhedāḥ arthāpattiḥ tatra pratyakṣa pūrvikā tu yathā sphoṭa ādi lakṣaṇam kāryam upalabhya tat anyathā anupapattyā vahneḥ dāhikā śaktiḥ pratīyate na ca atra pramāṇa antareṇa avinā abhāva grahaṇam śakteḥ pramāṇa antara agocara tvāt anupalabdha avinā bhāvaḥ ca liṅgam na bhavati eva atas pramāṇa antaram etat 
[II,178,19_II,179,1]	anumāna pūrvikā tu yathā dhūmāt agnim pratipadya tat anyathā anupapattyā tad viśeṣa pratītiḥ iti upamāna pūrvikā ca yathā aṭavyām gavaya darśana antaram madīyā gauḥ anena sadṛśī iti gām pratipadya tat anyathā anupapattyā vāha doha ādi sāmarthya pratipattiḥ arthāpatti pūrvikā tu rūpa upalambhāni atha anupapattyā avagatasya cakṣuṣaḥ paricchedikā śaktiḥ pratīyate iti āgama pūrvikā tu jīvati devadatte gṛhe na asti iti vākyāt gṛhe asattvam pratipadya tat anyathā anupapattyā bahirbhāva pratipattiḥ na bahirbhāvauvinābhūtam kiñcid liṅgam asti iti pramāṇa antara phalam etat abhāva pūrvikā tu yathā sat upalambhaka pramāṇa pañcaka vyāvṛttyā devadattasya gṛhe asattvam pratipadya tat anyathā anupapattyā bahis deśa sambandhaḥ pratīyate 
[II,179,3]	antarbhāvam āha tat api anumānam eva na pramāṇa antaram tathā ca sphoṭa ādi kāryeṇa agneḥ atīndriyā śaktiḥ pratīyate iti asat etat tasyāḥ caramasahakāri vyatirekeṇa pūrvam eva pratiṣedhāt pratibandhaka abhāva viśiṣṭaḥ agni saṃyogaḥ eva agneḥ śaktiḥ tad sadbhāve kārya karaṇāt agnitvantu nijā śaktiḥ sā api pratyakṣā eva yat ca anumānāt sāmānya avabodhe satya āpattitaḥ viśeṣa avabodhaḥ iti tad apāstam eva sāmānya viśeṣasya sādhya tvāt iti vadatā upamānasya tu smaraṇāt abhede api tad pūrvikā artha āpattiḥ anumānam eva vyāpteḥ pūrvam eva grahaṇāt tathā ca sādṛśya avacchinnaḥ gopiṇḍaḥ vāha ādi samarthaḥ tad piṇḍa tvāt pūrva upalabdhā evaṃvidha gopiṇḍa vat arthāpatti pūrvikā api arthāpattiḥ anumita anumānam eva tathā ca rūpa upalabdhiḥ karaṇa kāryā kriyā tvāt chidikriyā vat iti cakṣuḥ prasiddham tat ca anumitam śaktimat karaṇa tvāt vā asya ādi vat iti 
[II,179,14_II,179,19]	yā ca iyam jīvati devadatte gṛhe na asti iti anyathā anupapattyā bahirbhāva pratipattiḥ sā api anumānam eva vyāpteḥ pūrvam eva grahaṇāt tathā hi devadattaḥ bahis deśa sambandhī jīvana sambandhi tve sati gṛhe anupalabhyamāna tvāt viṣṇu mitra vat jīvana sambandhi tvan ca devadattasya arthāpatti vādinā api āgamāt eva pratipattavyam anyathā atha āpattiḥ na pravarteta samānañca etat abhāva pūrvikāyām api artha āpattau iti pramāṇa pañcaka abhāvena api jīvataḥ devadattasya gṛhe asattva pratipattau bahis deśa sambandhaḥ anumīyate evam anyat api udāharaṇam artha āpatteḥ avinā abhāva upadarśanena anumānaḥ eva antar bhāvanīyam tathā utpattim vinā anyathā anupapatteḥ upadarśayitum aśakya tvāt iti 
[II,179,23]	atha virodhinaḥ sarpa ādeḥ visphūrjana ādi śabda śravaṇāt tad anumitau virodhinī eva nakula ādau pratipattiḥ pramāṇa antaram iṣṭam kaiścid tad anumita anumānam eva vyāpteḥ pūrvam eva grahaṇāt prayogaḥ tu visphūrjana śabdaḥ bhujaṅga kāryaḥ visphūrjana śabda tvāt pūrva upalabdhā evaṃvidha visphūrjana śabda vat evam anumitaḥ sarpaḥ sannihitena virodhinā tadvān visphūrjana śabda kartṛ tvāt pūrva upalabdhā evaṃvidhāhi vat iti 
[II,180,1_II,180,2]	sambhavaḥ pramāṇa antaram iṣṭam paraiḥ tad niṣedha artham sambhavaḥ api avinābhauvi tvāt anumānam eva iti vākyam yatra hi sahasram tatra avaśyam śatam sambhavati iti avinābhāvasya grahaṇāt tathā ca sahasram sva samudāyi śata vat sahasra tvāt pūrva upalabdha sahasra vat 
[II,180,6_II,180,8]	kārya anutpādena kāraṇa abhāvaḥ pratīyate iti abhāva rūpa tayā eva pramāṇa antaram iti kecid tad niṣedha artham na param sambhavaḥ abhāvaḥ api anumānam eva iti yathā utpannam kāryam kāraṇa sadbhāve liṅgam avinā abhāvasya pūrvam eva grahaṇāt tathā anutpannam kāryam kāraṇa asadbhāve kārya anutpādasya kāraṇa abhāvena avyabhicārāt tathā ca kārya anutpattiḥ kāraṇa abhāvavatī kārya anutpatti tvāt ubhaya abhimata kāryān utpatti vat 
[II,180,14]	atha sat upalambhaka pramāṇa pañcaka vyāvṛttyā vastunaḥ abhāvasya grahaṇam iti pramāṇa antaram abhāvaḥ yathā hi bhāva aṃśa paricchede bhāvasya vyāpāraḥ tathā tad abhāva paricchede abhāvasya api abhyupagantavyaḥ tat uktam pratyakṣa ādi avatāraḥ tu bhāva aṃśaḥ grahyate yadā vyāpāraḥ tad abhāvasya api abhāva aṃśe jighṛkṣate 
[II,180,20_II,180,23]	tathā hi na pratyakṣeṇa abhāvasya grahaṇam tena sambandha abhāvāt sambaddham vartam ānañca gṛhyate cakṣuḥ ādinā pratyakṣa abhāvāt anumānasya api apravṛttiḥ tasya sambandhi grahaṇa apekṣi tvāt evam śabdasya api upamāna artha apattyoḥ ca avyāpārāt pramāṇa pañcaka abhāvena eva prameya abhāvasya grahaṇam iti tat uktam pramāṇa pañcakam yatra vastu rūpe na jāyate vastu sattā avabodha artham tatra abhāva pramāṇa tā 
[II,181,4_II,181,16]	nanu evam tarhi vyavahite api arthe pramāṇa pañcaka vyāvṛtteḥ sadbhāvāt abhāva grahaṇa prasaṅgaḥ na vastu grahaṇa pratiyogi smaraṇa ādeḥ api vyāpārāt tat uktam gṛhītvā vastu sadbhāvam smṛtvā ca pratiyoginam mānasam na astita ajñānam jāyate akṣa anapekṣayā vastunaḥ bhū tala ādeḥ sadbhāvam gṛhītvā pratiyoginam ghaṭañca smṛtvā indriya vyāpāram vinā eva manasā pratipadyate na iha bhū tale ghaṭaḥ asti iti tathā devakulam dṛṣṭavā bahis nirgataḥ hastinā deśa antara vyavadhānāt indriya sambandham vinā api pareṇa pṛṣṭaḥ tadā eva hastinaḥ na astitām pratipadyate tat uktam vastu mātram gṛhītvā api paścāt kiñcid smaran api tatra anyena astitām pṛṣṭaḥ tadā eva pratipadyate tathā pratyakṣa ādeḥ anutpattiḥ pramāṇa abhāvaḥ ucyate sa ātmanaḥ pariṇāmaḥ vā vijñānam vā anya vastunī 
[II,181,20]	sarvam etat asat pratyakṣa ādinā eva abhāvasya pratīteḥ tathā ca akṣa vyāpārāt iha bhū tale ghaṭaḥ na asti iti jñānam aparokṣam utpadyamānam dṛṣṭam atha indriyāṇām bhū tala grahaṇe vyāpāraḥ na abhāvaḥ iti ced na bhū tala grahaṇe pramāṇa abhāvāt viśeṣaṇasya hi pūrvam grahaṇam paścāt viśeṣyasya bhū ta lañca viśeṣyam iti na tasya pūrvam grahaṇe pramāṇam asti upetya vādena tu ucyate yadi vastu mātra grahaṇe sati pratiyogi smaraṇam ghaṭa avaruddha bhū tala upalambhe api tad smaraṇe nāstita ajñāna prasaṅgaḥ atha viśiṣṭa vastu grahaṇe sati pratiyogi smaraṇam tarhi yena viśeṣaṇena viśiṣṭam tat vastu pūrvam pratipattavyam iti kim indriyāt eva pratīyate prāmāṇa antarāt vā iti indriyāt eva pratipatti abhyupagame katham na abhāvaḥ pratyakṣa viṣayaḥ viśiṣṭa tāyāḥ tad rūpa tvāt na ca anumāna ādeḥ vyāpāre pramāṇam asti 
[II,182,5]	yadi ca anyayā pramāṇa pañcaka vyāvṛttyā eva viśiṣṭa tā pratīyate tatra api anya vastu grahaṇa abhyupagame viśiṣṭa tā grahaṇam eva abhyupeyam iti anavasthā syāt tasmāt indriyeṇa eva itara padārtha viviktam bhū talam upalabhya pratiyoginam smarati iti abhyupagame ghaṭa abhāvasya pratīta tvāt alam pramāṇa pañcaka vyāvṛttyā iti 
[II,182,9]	sa daṃśa prakāśakasya eva asat aṃśe api anvaya vyatirekābhyām vyāpāra upalabdheḥ na pramāṇa pañcaka aparicchedya vastuni abhāvasya pramāṇa tā iti vācyam na ca indriyeṇa sambandha abhāvāt agrahaṇam tasya kāryeṇa eva sadbhāva siddheḥ tathā ca pareṇa api aparokṣa jñāna sadbhāvena indriya arthayoḥ yogya tā lakṣaṇaḥ sambandhaḥ abhyupagataḥ sa ca rūpa ādau iva abhāve api abhyupagantavyaḥ kāryasya ubhayatra aviśeṣāt tathā vaiśeṣikaiḥ api aparokṣa jñāna sadbhāvena indriya arthayoḥ ṣoḍhā sambandhaḥ abhyupagataḥ iti abhāvena viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ asti eva tena hi satā aparokṣa jñāna utpatteḥ 
[II,182,16]	sat upalambhaka pramāṇa pañcaka vyāvṛttyā tu abhāva grahaṇe katham ṣaṭ eva pramāṇāni iti avadhāraṇam pramāṇa agrahe tasya anupapatteḥ na hi sat upalambhaka pramāṇa abhāvasya paricchedya tve anyat tasya paricchedakam pramāṇam asti atha pramāṇa pañcaka abhāvasya aneka tvāt kaścid kasyacid grāhakaḥ bhavati evam tarhi tasya api anyena grahaṇam tasya api anena iti anavasthā syāt na ca pramāṇa vyakteḥ aneka tvāt tad agrahaṇe tad niṣṭhasya ṣaṭ eva iti avadhāraṇasya sambhavaḥ syāt vaiśeṣi kāṇa an tu pramāṇa vyaktīnām ānantye api ekam lakṣaṇam upagrāhakam asti iti yuktam pramāṇa grahaṇe sati avadhāraṇam iti 
[II,182,24]	yat ca idam devakula mātram dṛṣṭavā niṣkrāntaḥ anyena pṛṣṭaḥ tadā eva hasti ādeḥ na astitā pratipadyate iti uktam tat na asya smaraṇa tvāt yadi api pūrvam hastī ityādi sa vikalpakam jñānam na utpannam tathā api hasti ādi abhāva viśiṣṭe devakule nirvikalpakam jñānam utpannam anyathā hi yadā aham devakulam adrākṣam na tadā tam samīpa vartinam hastinam iti praśna anantaram smaraṇam na syāt tat tu dṛṣṭam yasya vastunaḥ pūrvam na abhāvaḥ paricchinnaḥ tatra para praśna anantaram saṃśete na nirīkṣitam mayā kim tatra devadattaḥ asti uta na asti iti na ca id ānīm abhāvam niścinoti āgamasya api pramāṇa antareṇa artha tathā bhāva pratipattiḥ na āpta upadeśena kadācid sambhavāt atas pūrvam eva hasti ādi abhāvasya pratīteḥ yuktam etat smaraṇam na mayā tatra hastī dṛṣṭaḥ ityādi abhāvasya ca prameya tvam kṣaṇa bhaṅga avasare vyavasthāpitam eva iti 
[II,183,8_II,183,14]	atha anirdiṣṭa pravaktṛkam pravāda pāramparyam yathā iha vaṭe yakṣaḥ prativasati iti asya api yadi pramāṇa antareṇa artha tathā bhāva pratipattiḥ na āpta upadeśāt artha antara tvam iti āha tathā aitihyam a vitatham āpta upadeśaḥ eva tathā hi pūrva pramāṇāni na artha antaram tathā aitihyam api avitatham yathārtham āpta upadeśaḥ eva na pramāṇa antaram viparyaye tu aprāmāṇyam iti 
[II,183,17]	atha prāk sūcitasya para artha anumānasya vyākaraṇa artham pañca avayavena ityādi prakaraṇam para artha anumitiḥ iti lakṣya nirdeśaḥ pañca avayavena vākyena sva niścita artha pratipādanam iti lakṣaṇam sva niścita arthaḥ sādhyaḥ pratipādyate anena iti sva niścita artha pratipādanam liṅgam tat pañca avayavena vākyena sahitam para artham anumānam pratipattiḥ vā pratipādanam sva niścita artha viṣayam jñānam pañca avayavena vākyena janitam yatas kāraka samūhāt bhavati tat para artha anumānam iti sādhya artha vākya artha vādinā vyākhyānam liṅga vākya artha pakṣe tu arthyate anena iti arthaḥ liṅgam pratipādyate iti pratipādanam pañca avayavena vākyena pratipādyamānam liṅgam para artha anumānam iti yat vā sva niścita artha pratipattiḥ pratipādanam tat ca pañca avayavena vākyena janitam para artha anumānam iti 
[II,184,1]	nanu etasmin pakṣe katham sva arthāt viśiṣyate para artha anumānam cakṣuḥ ādinā śabdena vā liṅgam pratipadya tasmāt sādhyam pratipadyate iti kutas sva artha para arthaḥ iti bhedaḥ na ca para sampāditāt śabdāt liṅgam pratipadyate iti viśeṣaḥ cakṣuḥ ādeḥ api para sampādita tvāt śabda rūpa tā vailakṣaṇyantu vaidharmya mātram eva atas sādhya vākya artha pakṣaḥ doṣa anupapatteḥ grāhyaḥ iti tathā ca kevalam liṅgam cakṣuḥ ādinā pratipannam sādhya pratipattau sva artha anumānam aśabda sahitam śabda sahitantu para artha anumānam iti viśeṣaḥ tasmāt iti anena samartha liṅga parāmarśa anantaram anityaḥ eva ayam iti sādhya pratipatteḥ saṃvedanāt ca sādhyam eva vākya arthaḥ tasmāt iti evam antam eva vākyam śeṣañca abhiprāya nivedanam iti na tvā artham sādhya vākya artha pakṣe bādhaka anupapatteḥ iti alam ati vistareṇa 
[II,184,11_II,184,14]	pūrvasya saṅgraha vākyasya vivaraṇam pañca avayavena eva vākyena na dvi avayavena daśa avayavena vā iti keṣām saṃśayita viparyasta avyutpannānām sva niścita artha pratipādanam para artha anumānam vijñeyam atha niravayava tvāt vākyasya anupapannam etat pañca avayavena iti tathā ca varṇānām na samuditānām artha pratipādaka tvam krama bhāvinām āśu vināśi tvena samudāya asambhavāt na vyastānām ekasmāt eva artha pratītau anyeṣām uccāraṇa vaiyarthyāt upalabhyate ca śabdāt uccarita artha pratipattiḥ atas tat anyathā anupapattyā varṇa kalāpāt atiricyamānaḥ sphoṭa ātmā pratīyate iti tathā gauḥ iti śabda uccāraṇāt abhinna ākāram vijñānam śrotra vyāpārāt utpadyamānam dṛṣṭam na ca idam saṃśaya viparyaya vyatirekāt avayavi jñāna vat abhinnam artham vinā bhavati iti varṇa uccāraṇantu sphoṭa svarūpa abhivyaktaye kriyate iti na vyartham 
[II,184,22_II,185,3]	asat etat pūrva varṇa anugṛhītasya antya varṇasya sva anubhava sahakāriṇaḥ artha pratipādaka tvāt yathā ca ekasmin varṇe jñānam tena kriyate saṃskāraḥ punar dvitīya varṇa jñānam tena api pūrva varṇa saṃskāra sahakāriṇā saṃskāraḥ iti krameṇa antya varṇa jñānam tasmāt pūrva saṃskāra abhivyakta avaśeṣa varṇa anusmaraṇe sati antya varṇāt artha pratipattiḥ na ca evam ghaṭa ādi anubhava janita saṃskārasya anubhava antara sahakāriṇaḥ saṃskāra ārambhaka tvena atiprasaṅgaḥ tatra viśiṣṭa adṛṣṭa abhāvāt tad abhāvaḥ tu kārya abhāvena eva jñāyate iti atra ca kāryasya sadbhāvāt viśiṣṭaḥ adṛṣṭaḥ kāraṇa tvena kalpyate iti anye tu śabda artha upabhoga prāpaka adṛṣṭa niyamitāḥ pūrva varṇa anubhava janita saṃskārāḥ pūrva varṇeṣu ekam smaraṇam ārabhante tad sahakārī ca antyaḥ varṇaḥ padam yat vā saṃskāram ekam vicitram ārabhante tasmāt ca pūrva varṇeṣu ekam smaraṇam iti 
[II,185,6_II,185,15]	anye tu pūrva varṇānām tad jñāna anāñca atītānām api antya varṇa sahakāri tvam anvaya vyatireka upapatteḥ yathā hi vartamānasya kāraṇa tvam anvaya vyatirekābhyām vijñātam evam atītasya api iti yat vā pūrva varṇa vināśāḥ tad jñāna pradhvaṃsāḥ ca samīpa vartinaḥ antya varṇa sahakāriṇaḥ iti kṣīṇa arthāpattiḥ evaṃvidha kalpanā anabhyupagame ca varṇa uccāraṇa vaiyarthyam eva syāt na ca sphoṭa abhivyañjakam uccāraṇam samasta vyasta vikalpa anupapatteḥ na samastaiḥ abhivyajyate samudāya anabhyupagamāt na vyastaiḥ ekena eva abhivyaktau śeṣa uccāraṇa vaiyarthya prasaṅgāt atha kalpanā āśrīyate sā artha pratipattau api samartha iti alam sphoṭa parikalpanayā abhinna ākārañca jñānam antya varṇa viṣayam varṇa tva viṣayam vā yat vā ghana avasthiti pratyakṣeṣu iva varṇeṣu bhrāntam abhinna ākāram vijñānam iti na sphoṭa siddhiḥ śabda abhivyaktau iva sphoṭa abhivyaktau api doṣāḥ iti samāna tayā śabda parīkṣāyām eva abhidhāsyante iti alam 
[II,185,18]	vākya kalpanā tu ekasmin pade jñānasya utpādaḥ saṃskārasya saṅketa smaraṇasya ca utpadyamāna tā tatas saṃskārasya saṅketa smaraṇasya ca utpādaḥ padārtha pratipatteḥ utpadyamāna tā pada jñānasya vinaśyattā tatas padārtha pratipatteḥ utpattiḥ smaraṇasya vinaśyattā pada jñānasya vināśaḥ saṃskārasya dvitīya pada jñānasya ca utpadyamāna tā tatas dvitīya pada jñānasya utpādaḥ pūrva saṃskāra sacivena padārtha jñānena saṃskārasya utpādaḥ saṃskāra antarasya utpadyamāna tā saṅketa smaraṇasya api utpadyamāna tā padārtha pratipad tevina śyattā pūrva saṅketa smaraṇasya vināśaḥ tatas dvitīya pada jñāna saṃskārasya utpādaḥ saṅketa smaraṇasya api utpādaḥ pada jñānasya vinaśyattā padārtha pratipatteḥ utpadyamāna tā pūrva padārtha pratipatteḥ vināśaḥ iti ayam nyāyaḥ tāvat yāvat antyapade jñānam tena ca kalpanayā tad saṃskāra abhivyakteḥ aśeṣa padārtha viṣayam smaraṇam janyate tena ca sva anubhavena ca viśiṣṭam antya padam eva vākyam tasmāt ca vākya artha pratipattiḥ iti 
[II,186,4]	nanu pada jñāna utpatteḥ pūrvam adṛṣṭa vaśāt pada padārtha viṣaya smaraṇa utpāda abhyupagame tasya pada jñānāt saṅketa smaraṇa kāle na avasthānam iti padārtha pratipatteḥ ūrdhvam katham vākya artha pratipattiḥ na ca padārtha pratipattim vinā eva vākya artha pratipattiḥ adarśanāt atha pada jñānāt ūrdhvam kalpanayā tad saṃskāreṇa smaraṇam janyate tatas pada jñānasya vinaśyatta iti saṅketa smaraṇa kāle tasya anavasthānāt padārtha pratipatti abhāve na vākya artha pratipattiḥ iti dūṣaṇam tad avastham eva 
[II,186,10]	asat etat vākye saṅketa anupapatteḥ antya padam vākyam eva tat antya arthaḥ tu vākya arthaḥ iti yadā ca pūrva varṇa tad jñānāt ūrdhvam kalpanayā tad saṃskāreṇa smaraṇam janyate tatas pada jñānasya vinaśyatta iti saṅketa smaraṇa abhāva viśiṣṭaḥ antyaḥ vaṇaḥ padam tat eṣā vākya kalpanā anyathā pūrva varṇeṣu jñāna dvāreṇa saṃskārāt vicitra smaraṇa anugṛhītaḥ antyaḥ varṇaḥ padam iti abhyupagamena padārtha jñāna anantaram pada jñānam syāt varṇa jñāna vyavadhānāt 
[II,186,16_II,186,20]	anye tu pūrva arthasya pratisamādhāna artham antya pada jñāna anantaram kalpanayā tad saṃskāraḥ saṅketa anubhava janita saṃskāraḥ ca ekam smaraṇam ārabhate tatas padārtha jñānasya utpādaḥ pada jñānasya vinaśyattā smaraṇa anubhavayoḥ ca avirodhaḥ iti tatas smaraṇa anubhava viśiṣṭāt antya padāt vākya artha pratipattiḥ iti anye tu yadi api antya pada jñāna anantaram saṅketa smaraṇāt padārtha avabodhe sati pada jñānam vinaṣṭam tathā api punar tasmin eva jñānam utpadyate tatas kalpanayā tad saṃskārāt smaraṇa utpāde sati antya padāt vākya artha pratipattiḥ iti 
[II,186,23_II,186,25]	asat etat śabdasya viramya vyāpāra pratiṣedhāt ekadā padam sva viṣaya jñānam kṛtvā punar na karoti iti anye tu pratijña ādi padasya pada antara uccāraṇa kāle api ākāśe pada antara ambhaka tvena avasthānam tāvat yāvat antyapadam tatas pañcabhiḥ padaiḥ śrotra deśe vākyam avayavi bhūtam ārabhyate tatas vākya artha pratipattiḥ iti niraḥ tañca etat anubhavena na hi pūrva pūrva padasya uttarottara pada kāle sarveṣāñca vākya kāle anubhavaḥ asti iti 
[II,187,4]	anye tu ekasmin pade jñānam tena kriyate saṃskāraḥ punar dvitīya pada jñānam tena prāktanena saṃskāreṇa anyaḥ saṃskāraḥ iti tāvat yāvat antyapade jñānam iti tatas prāktana saṃskāra abhivyaktī pada catuṣṭaya viṣayam smaraṇam utpayate tad viśiṣṭañcā antya padam vākyam iti na ca atra anubhavena virodhaḥ karaṇa aṃśasya eva kīrtanāt 
[II,187,9]	anye smaraṇena anubhavasya avirodham manyamānāḥ kalpanām āśrayante pada jñānāt saṅketa smaraṇasya utpādaḥ padārtha pratipatteḥ utpadyamāna tā tatas padārtha jñānasya utpādaḥ pūrva pada jñānasya vinaśyattā dvitīya pada jñānasya utpadyamāna tā tatas dvitīya pada jñānasya utpādaḥ padārtha jñānasya vinaśyattā pada jñānasya vināśaḥ saṅketa smaraṇasya utpadyam āna tā iti anena krameṇa antya pada jñāne sati vākya artha pratipattiḥ na ca atra pūrva pada padārtha anusmaraṇena prayojanam asti tad kāryasya vinaśyat avastha pada jñānena eva kṛta tvāt pūrva pada anurakte hi dvitīya pade jñānam utpannam tat anuraktam tṛtīya padam iti aśeṣa pada anuraktam antya padam vākyam iti 
[II,187,17]	etat ca asat pūrva pada anurāgasya antya pade apratibhāsanāt yathā hi daṇḍī iti jñānam daṇḍa anuraktam eva na evam dvitīya ādi pada jñānam pūrva pada anuraktam iti na ca ayam niyamaḥ sambhavati pūrva pada anantaram eva dvitīya ādi pada uccāraṇam katipaya kāla vyavadhāne api uccāraṇe artha pratipatti darśanāt iti pūrvā eva kalpanā nyāyyā 
[II,187,21]	atha astu evam vākya parikalpanā vācakatvantu niṣidhyata anvaya vyatireka abhāvāt padārthabhyaḥ tu vākya artha pratipattiḥ yatra hi pramāṇa antareṇa api padārtha prasiddhiḥ tatra antareṇa api vākyam vākya artha prattipatiḥ dṛṣṭā yathā paśyataḥ cakṣuṣā rūpam heṣa aśabdaḥ ca śṛṇvataḥ khura nikṣepa śabdañca śvetaḥ aśvaḥ dhāvati iti dhīḥ 
[II,188,1_II,188,6]	tathā ca dūrāt cakṣuṣā śvetam rūpam upalabhya heṣā śabdena vā aśva tva jātim anum inoti khura nikṣepa śabdena ca dhāvana kriyām avagatya vākyam vinā api vākya artham pratipadyate sati api ca vākye padārthānām apratipatteḥ na vākya artha pratipattiḥ yathā prasiddha padārthaiḥ kavibhiḥ viracite vākyaḥ iti tasmāt abhihita padārthānām ākāṅkṣa ayogya tā sannidhi dvāreṇa vākya artha gamaka tvam iti na yuktam etat śabdasya aprāmāṇya prasaṅgāt tathā ca pada rūpasya tāvat aprāmāṇyam anuvādaka tvāt tat uktam padam abhyadhika abhāvāt smārakāt na viśiṣyate yat ca ādhikyam bhavet etat sa padasya na gocaraḥ 
[II,188,11]	vākyantu pāramparyeṇa api avācakam iti katham śabdaḥ pramāṇam syāt atha padaiḥ abhihitānāñca padārthānām gamaka tvāt iti pāramparyeṇa śabdaḥ pramāṇam tarhi śrotra paricchinnasya śabdasya artha paricchede vyāpārāt iti pāramparyeṇa pratyakṣasya api codanā viṣaye sannidhi prāmāṇya upapatteḥ katham codanā eva dharma pramāṇam pramāṇam eva codanā iti na asya avadhāraṇasya vyāghātaḥ vākyasya artha paricchedaka tva anabhyupagame ca pramāṇa antara asambhavāt padārthānām pratyakṣa ādiṣu antarbhāvaḥ cintanīyaḥ 
[II,188,17_II,188,20]	tatra indriya artha sannikarṣeṇa saha vyāpāra anupalabdheḥ na pratyakṣe antarbhāvaḥ avinābhau asya anupapatteḥ na anumāne anupapadyamāna artha asambhavān na artha āpattau upamāna abhāvayoḥ ca niyata viṣaya tvam eva pramāṇa antarasya ca anabhyupagamāt ayuktam etat na ca padānām sva artha pratipattau eva caritārtha tvam ukta nyāyena vākya artha pratipattau api vyāpārāt viramya vyāpāraḥ tu ekam artham pratipādya punar tam pratipādayanti iti pratiṣiddhaḥ 
[II,188,23_II,189,1]	yat ca idam vinā api vākyam vākya artha pratipattiḥ iti uktam tad aparijñānāt vākyena hi janitā vākya artha pratipattiḥ pratyakṣa anumāna sampāditāḥ śvetaḥ aśvaḥ dhāvati iti buddhayaḥ yat api idam padārtha apratipattau sati api vākyena vākya artha pratipattiḥ iti tat asat pūrva padārtha smaraṇa anugṛhītasya antya padasya vākya tvāt ca avaśyam artha pratipādaka tvam iti vyabhicāra abhāvaḥ anvitā abhidhānantu na sarva padānām ekena eva kriyā kāraka saṃsarga anvitasya padārthasya abhidhāne śeṣa pada uccāraṇa vaiyarthya prasaṅgāt atha antyam padam anvita abhidhāyakam tasya api pūrva pada an apekṣi tve tad uccāraṇa vaiyarthyam sa apekṣi tve tu na asmad siddhāntāt bhedaḥ 
[II,189,6_II,189,16]	ke punar avayavāḥ tat āha pratijñā apadeśa nidarśana anusandhāna pratyāmnāyāḥ vākya eka deśa tvāt na punar para upagatāḥ jijñāsā ādayaḥ teṣām aśabda rūpa tvāt tatas upadeśa krameṇa avasara prāptāyāḥ pratijñāyāḥ tāvat lakṣaṇam ucyate anumeya uddeśaḥ avirodhī pratijñā iti anumeyaḥ pratipipā dāyiṣita dharma viśiṣṭaḥ dharmī dharma viśiṣṭa tā hi astitva ādi apekṣayā sarva padārtheṣu asti iti pratipipādayiṣita padam yaḥ hi dharmaḥ pratipādayitum iṣṭaḥ tad viśiṣṭaḥ dharmī pakṣaḥ tasya uddeśa mātram pratyakṣa ādi aviruddham pareṣām aniścita artha abhidhāyakam vacanam pratijñā iti apadeśasya hetoḥ viṣaya āpādanam arthaḥ prayojanam asya iti prayojana upanyāsaḥ prayogaḥ tu pratijñā itarasmāt bhidyate pratyakṣa ādi aviruddha anumeya uddeśa tvāt yaḥ tu na bhidyate na ca asau evam yathā udāharaṇa ādiḥ iti anumeya uddeśaḥ vā pratijñā iti vyavahartavyaḥ yathā ukta anumeya uddeśa tvāt yaḥ ca evam na vyavahriyate na ca asau evam yathā apadeśaḥ iti udāharaṇantu yathā dravyam vāyuḥ iti 
[II,189,26]	nanu ca asādhana aṅgam pratijñā vacanam tad antareṇa api sambandha vacana mātrāt artha pratīteḥ tathā hi yat yat kṛtakam tat tat anityam dṛṣṭam yathā ghaṭaḥ tathā ca kṛtakaḥ śabdaḥ iti atra sāmarthyāt eva pratijñā artha siddheḥ vyartham tat abhidhānam atra ca prameyasya pramāṇena eva siddheḥ sāmarthyam kiṃrūpam iti cintyam na pratyakṣa svarūpam indriya artha sannikarṣeṇa vipratipatti viṣayasya aparicchedāt evam āgamena api iti atha anumānam eva sāmarthyam tat avaśyam artha pratipattau pakṣa dharma tva ādikam apekṣate iti pratijñā vacanam antareṇa sa pakṣa āsa pakṣa apravibhāge sati tad artha apratīteḥ na gamakam iti atha abhidhīyamāna anumāna vyatirekeṇa anyat anumānam prastuta anumāna sāmarthyam na tasya api avinā abhāva anapekṣi tve na gamaka tvam pratijñā avacanañca vinā tad artha apratīteḥ iti pūrva doṣa anuṣaṅgāt na ca abhipreta artha pratipādanāya anumāna upanyāsa kāle tad artha siddhaye anumāna antaram paśyāmaḥ 
[II,190,11_II,190,14]	na ca kṛtaka tva anitya tvayoḥ sāmānyena vyāpti abhidhāne samartha sādhanasya śabdaḥ eva upasaṃhārāt vijñāyate atra eva anitya tvam asya abhipretam iti sambandha abhidhānasya viruddha aviruddha abhiprāyeṇa api samāna tayā viveka pratipatteḥ abhāva prasaṅgāt atha yat yat kṛtakam tat tat nityam dṛṣṭam iti vyāpti vacane viruddha vādī anitya tvena ca kṛtaka tvasya vyāpti vacane tattva vādī iti viniścayaḥ tat na kṛtaka tva nitya tvayoḥ vyāpteḥ pratipādayitum aśakyatvāt tathā ca na kṛtakeṣu ghaṭa ādiṣu nitya tvam nityeṣu ca ākāśa ādiṣu kṛtaka tvam iti dṛṣṭānta doṣeṇa gata artha tvāt katham viruddha tvam yadā ca nityaḥ śabdaḥ iti pratijñāya kṛta katva anitya tvayoḥ vyāptim brūte tadā abhipreta artha viparītena vyāpti kathanāt viruddha vādyayam iti viśeṣa adhyavasāyaḥ bhavati eva 
[II,190,21]	nanu nitya anitya abhiprāyeṇa eva api nityaḥ śabdaḥ iti vacana sambhavāt pratijñā vacane sati api tattva atattva vādinoḥ aniścayaḥ eva na vacanena eva abhiprāya viśeṣa prasiddheḥ na hi vaktṝṇām vacanāt ṛte abhiprāya avabodhe pramāṇa antaram asti iti nitya vacanāt nitya abhiprāyaḥ eva niścīyate abhiprāya antara kalpanāyām pramāṇa abhāvāt atas eva vādi prativādinā ūrjaya parājaya vyavasthā prāśnikaiḥ kriyate yatra api anyathā pratipadyamānā vicitra abhiprāya tayā prakaraṇa artham anyathā bruvate tatra api vacana viśeṣeṇa eva abhiprāya viśeṣaḥ anumeyaḥ vivakṣā antarāt vacana antara anutpatteḥ abhyupagame vā sambandha vacanāt api aniścayaḥ eva syāt kim nitya tva vivakṣātaḥ kṛta ka tva anitya tvayoḥ sambandha vacanam uta anitya tva vivakṣātaḥ iti 
[II,191,3]	atha hetu tad abhāva vyavasthāyāḥ vāstava sambandha apekṣi tvāt viparīta vivakṣayā api kṛtaka tva anitya tvayoḥ asti eva sambandhaḥ iti gamaka tvam tarhi nitya tva abhiprāyeṇa api evaṃsambandham upadarśayataḥ tattva vādi tvam syāt prakāra antareṇa sambandha upadarśanasyava abhāvāt tathā pratijñā vacanam vinā sandigdha viparyasta avyutpanna puruṣa viśeṣāṇām prameya viśeṣeṣu ākāṅkṣā pratipattau vādinaḥ viśeṣeṇa puruṣa mātrasya prameya mātra pratipādanāya pravartamānasya unmatta vādi tvam syāt 
[II,191,9]	atha vivādāt puruṣa viśeṣasya prameya viśeṣa apekṣi tva pratipattiḥ tarhi pratijñā abhyupagatā eva vivādasya tad rūpa tvāt pratijñā hi pratiyogi pratijñā antaram apekṣamāṇaḥ vivādaḥ sādhana sahitā tu pratijñā iti na ca śāstrāt eva yathā ukta pratipattiḥ anumāna upanyāsa kāle tasya apramāṇa tvāt prāmāṇye vā kim anumānena iti tasmāt para artha anumānam icchatā avaśyam kāryam pratijñā vacanam iti yat ca idam arthāt artha gatau śaktiḥ pakṣa hetu abhidhānayoḥ na arthe tena tayoḥ na asti svatas sādhana saṃsthitiḥ iti utkam tatra arthasya artha gatau sāmarthyam na niṣidhyate kevalayoḥ ca pakṣa hetu abhidhānayoḥ na artha paricchede sāmarthyam avayava antara sadbhāve ca sva artha upasthāpana dvāreṇa sāmarthyam iṣyate eva anyathā hetu abhidhānasya api asāmarthye para artha anumānasya apravṛttiḥ eva 
[II,191,21_II,191,25]	atha hetu vacanam svayam asamartham api samartha hetu saṃsūcaka tvāt para pratipattau upādīyate na ca evam pratijñā iti āha sādhya abhidhānāt pakṣoktiḥ pāramparyeṇa na api alam śaktasya sūcakam hetu vacaḥ aśaktam api svayam tatra pakṣoktiḥ pratijñā vacanam pāramparyeṇa api alam samartham na bhavati iti asādhana aṅgam iti sādhye sādhya abhidhānam asādhāraṇam eva sa pakṣa āsa pa kṣayoḥ aprasiddheḥ tathā sādhya abhidhānasya pakṣa ukteḥ paryāya tvāt sādhya aviśiṣṭa tā ca iti atha sādhya anupayogi tvāt sādhyān abhidhānam tat api avayava antara sahitasya sādhya pratipādaka tvāt asiddham viparyaye tu anaikāntikam kevalasya hetu vacanasya api asādhaka tvāt tathā pratijñā vacanam api asādhana aṅgam iti vadatā abhyupagatā eva pratijñā iti vyāghātaḥ
