[II,192,6_II,192,12]	atha sva pratipattau pratijñā vacanasya anupalambhāt para pratipattau anupādānam evam tarhi hetu vacanasya api adarśanāt anupādānam syāt atha hetu arthasya upalambhāt yuktam hetu vacanam tarhi pratijñā arthasya upalabdheḥ kāryam pratijñā vacanam yathā hetu arthaḥ kāraṇam sādhya pratipattau evam pratijñā arthaḥ karma iti ubhayoḥ kāraṇa tva aviśeṣāt pakṣasya avacane pramāṇam na asti iti upasthāpite ca karmaṇi karaṇānām pravṛtteḥ upalambhāt tad upasthāpana artham avaśyam kāryam pratijñā vacanam iti alam vistareṇa avirodhi grahaṇāt pratyakṣa anumāna abhyupagata sva śāstra sva vacana virodhinaḥ anumeya uddeśāḥ nirastāḥ bhavanti iti vyavacchedyam darśayati yaḥ hi anumeya uddeśaḥ na pratyakṣa ādinā virudhyate sā pratijñā iti 
[II,192,15]	anye tu pratyakṣa ādi aviruddhaḥ anumeyaḥ tasya uddeśaḥ pratijñā iti vyākhyām kurvate yadi api anumeyasya sādhyasya sādhana arha tayā pratyakṣa ādi virodha abhāvāt na vyavacchedya tvam asti tathā api kimbhūtam sādhyam iti apekṣāyām svarūpa upavarṇana artham pratyakṣa ādi aviruddha padam pratyakṣa śabdena eva viśiṣṭa artha pratītau indriya artha sannikarṣa ādi pada vat iti tat ca asat avirodhi padasya uddeśa padena sāmānādhikaraṇyāt karmaṇaḥ karaṇena virodha abhāvāt ca iti yathābhūtam upalabhyamānam karma tathābhūtam anupalabhyamānam api iti uddyota kara pādaiḥ uktam pratijñā tu karaṇam iti yuktaḥ tatra virodhaḥ 
[II,192,23]	tatra pratyakṣa virodhī yathā anuṣṇaḥ agniḥ iti uṣṇa tāyāḥ tvac indriyeṇa pratibhāsanāt ghanam ambaram iti anumāna virodhī ākāśasya anumānāt eva amūrta tva vibhu tva prasiddheḥ ghanam niviḍa avayavam iti uddeśaḥ tena virudhyate eva ghana tve sati asmad ādīnām asañcāra prasaṅgāt ca iti abhyupagata śāstra virodhī yathā vaiśeṣikasya sarva kāryam utpatteḥ pūrvam sat iti bruvataḥ vaiśeṣika śāstre hi asat utpadyate iti prasiddham na śabdaḥ artha pratyāyakaḥ iti sva vacana virodhī yadi hi śabdaḥ artha pratyāyakaḥ na bhavati katham asya arthasya jñāpana artham śabda uccāraṇam na virudhyeta iti 
[II,193,4]	atha pramāṇa tri tve sati katham virodha bahu tvam loka prasiddha yapekṣayā yadi api āgama viruddhasya pratyakṣa viruddhasya ca amī bhedāḥ tathā api sva vacana viruddhaḥ sva śāstra viruddhaḥ ca ityādi vyapadeśaḥ janānām atas tathā eva abhidhānam anumānasya tu anumāna antareṇa virodha asambhave api svakīya anumānasya balavat tvāt ayam vyapadeśaḥ anumānena pratijñā bādhyate iti 
[II,193,10_II,193,16]	pratijñā anantaram hetu lakṣaṇam āha liṅga vacanam apadeśaḥ iti artha lakṣaṇa tvāt vacasām iti liṅga lakṣaṇa anuvādena apadeśasya lakṣaṇa abhidhānam iti yat anumeyena sahacaritam tad samāna jātīye sarvatra ca sāmānyena prasiddham yathābhūtaḥ dharmaḥ pakṣe tad samānaḥ sa pakṣe prasiddhaḥ na punar viśeṣaḥ anya dharmāṇām anyatra āvṛtteḥ sarvatra ca iti vyāpaka avyāpaka bhedam darśayati tad viparīte ca vipakṣe sarvatra na asti eva iti vipakṣa ādi atyanta vyāvṛttim darśayati prakaraṇa sama kāla atyaya apadiṣṭayoḥ ca vyudāsaḥ pūrvavat iti etat liṅgam uktam iti lakṣaṇa anuvādaḥ tasya vācakam vacanam tṛtīya antam pañcamī antam vai apadeśaḥ tathā ca ayam itarasmāt bhidyate yathā ukta liṅga vacana tvāt yaḥ tu na bhidyate na ca asau evam yathā pratijñādiḥ iti 
[II,193,26]	tasya vyāpaka avyāpaka svarūpa upadarśana artham udāharaṇa dvayam yathā kriyāvat tvāt guṇavat tvāt ca iti caśabdena prakāra antaram kriyāvat tvena guṇavat tvena ca iti darśayati anayoḥ lakṣaṇena abhisambandha upadarśana artham anuvādaḥ tathā ca tat kriyāvat tvam guṇavat tvañca anumeye pakṣe asti tad samāna jātīye ca sa pakṣe sarvasmin guṇavat tvam asarvasmin kriyāvat tvam asti iti ubhayam api etat adravye sattā ādau na asti eva iti tasya guṇavat tvasya kriyāvat tvasya ca yathoktam vacanam apadeśaḥ iti siddham 
[II,194,8_II,194,15]	etena sāmarthyāt apadeśa ābhāsāḥ nirastāḥ bhavanti iti sva vākye parivarjana artham para vākye ca udbhāvanā artham saṃlakṣyate tatra idam sāmānya lakṣaṇam apadeśa vat ābhāsamānāḥ samyak matau apadeśa ābhāsāḥ ahetuḥ api viparyasta buddheḥ hetu vat bhāsate iti samyak matau iti padam etasmin ca pakṣe anyatara asiddhasya samyak matau hetu vat ābhāsamāna tvam cintyam tasya hi pakṣa dharma tva ādimattvam iti atas hetu vat ābhāsamāna tvāt hetvābhāsāḥ iti siddham lakṣaṇam yasya tu hetuḥ api tasya pakṣa dharma tva ādi upadarśanena hetu tva pratipattau yatnaḥ kāryaḥ tad pratipatteḥ hi artha pratipattau kāraṇa tvāt iti atas eva anyatara asiddhaḥ yadi api vastu vṛttyāḥ hetuḥ tathā api pakṣa dharma tayā pareṇa apratipanna tvāt asiddha buddhim janayati iti pratipanne ca pramāṇataḥ pakṣa dharma tvena sādhya siddheḥ bhāvāt hetuḥ eva iti 
[II,194,25_II,195,1]	anye tu ahetavaḥ pakṣa dharma tva ādi anyatama rūpān anuvidhānāt samāna dharmāṇaḥ hetvābhāsāḥ iti atha kiyatām punar evam anapadeśa tvam iti āha asiddha viruddha sandigdha anadhya vasita vacanānām anapadeśa tvam uktam bhavati iti tatra asiddhaḥ caturvidhaḥ iti vibhāgaḥ sāmānya lakṣaṇañca āśaṅkya māna pakṣa vṛtti tvam arthāt labhyate āśaṅkyamāne hi pakṣe vattiḥ sarvasya viśeṣaṇa asiddha ādi prapañcasya asti iti pakṣa vyāpī idam sāmānya lakṣaṇam na ca evam pakṣa āvṛtti tvam tasya asamartha viśeṣaṇa ādi bhedeṣu asambhavāt 
[II,195,7_II,195,17]	kena rūpeṇa caturvidhaḥ iti āha ubhaya asiddhaḥ anyatara asiddhaḥ tad bhāva asiddhaḥ anumeya asiddhaḥ ca iti tatra ubhayoḥ vādi prativādinā uḥ asiddhaḥ yathā anityaḥ śabdaḥ sa avayava tvāt iti śabde hi sāvayava tvam nitya anitya vādinoḥ na prasiddham iti anyatara asiddhaḥ yathā anityaḥ śabdaḥ kāryatvāt iti mīmāṃsakasya hi pratyabhijñāna ādikam upalabhamānasya śabde kāryatvam tāvat asiddham yāvat anyatara pakṣa vyudāsa dvāreṇa pramāṇataḥ vyavasthāpyate iti niścīyate niścite tu pakṣadhama tve tatas sādhyam pratipadyate eva tad bhāva asiddhaḥ yathā dhūma bhāvena agni adhigatau iti dhūma tvena aniścitam vāṣpa ādikam upalabhamānasya agni adhigatau kartavyāyām tad bhāva asiddhaḥ dhūma bhāvasya aniścita tvāt iti anumeya asiddhaḥ yathā pārthivam dravyam tamaḥ kṛṣṇa rūpavat tvāt iti sāṃkhya abhyupagatasya tamasaḥ aprasiddha tvāt ayam āśraya asiddhaḥ na tu abhāva rūpatamaḥ apekṣayā tasya tu pramāṇena prasiddheḥ pakṣīkaraṇe kṛṣṇa rūpavat tvam svarūpa asiddham na tu āśraya asiddham iti 
[II,195,20]	nanu evam viśeṣaṇa asiddha ādi prapañcasya asaṅgrahaṇāt ayuktaḥ ayam vibhāgaḥ na ubhaya siddhe anyatara asiddhe vā antarbhāvāt tathā ca ubhayoḥ viśeṣaṇā siddhaḥ yathā nityaḥ śabdaḥ anabhidheya tve sati bāhya indriya pratyakṣa tvāt bāhya indriya pratyakṣa tve ca sati anabhidheya tvāt iti ubhayoḥ viśeṣya asiddhaḥ anyatara viśeṣaṇā siddhaḥ yathā nityaḥ śabdaḥ kṛtaka tve sati amūrta tvāt evam anyeṣu api puruṣa viśeṣa abhiprāyeṇa asiddha tvāt yuhyam iti asamartha viśeṣaṇā siddhaḥ yathā nityaḥ śabdaḥ prameya tve sati kṛtaka tvāt viparyayeṇa asamartha viśeṣya asiddhaḥ iti vyadhikaraṇa viśeṣaṇā siddhaḥ yathā nityaḥ śabdaḥ cākṣuṣa tve sati kṛtaka tvāt viparyayeṇa vyadhikaraṇa viśeṣya asiddhaḥ iti viruddha viśeṣaṇā siddhaḥ yathā anityaḥ śabdaḥ kāryatve sati amūrta tvāt iti anyathā siddha viśeṣaṇa asiddhaḥ yathā nityaḥ śabdaḥ abhyasyamāna tve sati amūrta tvāt iti 
[II,196,4_II,196,14]	nanu evam api eṣām ubhayā siddhe anyatara asiddhe antarbhāva vat tad bhāva asiddha anumeyā siddhayoḥ api antarbhāvaḥ syāt iti katham cāturvidhyam tayoḥ avāntara bheda apekṣayā tad bhāva asiddhaḥ para artha anumānasya prastuta tvāt ubhaya asiddhaḥ anyatara asiddhaḥ ca iti bhidyate evam anumeya asiddhaḥ api iti cāturvidhyam anye tu ubhaya asiddham yatra viśeṣaṇam viśeṣyañca asiddham iti anyatara asiddhantu viśeṣaṇā siddham viśeṣya asiddham vā iti manyante na ca etat bhāṣya kartuḥ abhipretam vādī abhiprāyeṇa udāharaṇa upanyāsāt anye tu sva artha anumānasya tad bhāva asiddhaḥ anumeya asiddhaḥ ca iti bhadaḥ sakala bheda saṅgrāhakaḥ para artha anumānasya tu ubhaya asiddhaḥ anyatara asiddhaḥ ca iti atra tu sva artha anumānena para arthasya bheda nirūpaṇam iṣṭam eva svātantryantu niṣidhyate 
[II,196,17]	viruddha lakṣaṇam āha yaḥ hi anumeye pakṣe vyāptyai avidyamānaḥ api tad samāna jātīye ca sa pakṣe sarvasmin na asti tad viparīte ca vipakṣe asti sa viparīta sādhanāt viruddhaḥ yathā yasmāt viṣāṇī tasmāt aśvaḥ iti viṣāṇinām piṇḍam pakṣīkṛtya aśvaḥ ayam iti sādhayataḥ viṣāṇi tvāt iti hetuḥ viruddhaḥ asya hi anaśvena eva vyāpta tvāt ayantu vipakṣa eka deśa vṛttiḥ vidyamānasapakṣaḥ tathā vipakṣa vyāpakaḥ nityaḥ śabdaḥ kāryatvāt iti avidyamānasapakṣaḥ vipakṣa vyāpakaḥ sarvam kāryam sarvajña kartṛkam prameya tvāt iti vidyamānasapakṣaḥ vipakṣa eka deśa vṛttiḥ jīvat śarīram sa ātmakam kārya tvāt iti atas caturvidhaḥ 
[II,196,25_II,197,4]	ekasmin ca dvayoḥ hetvoḥ i atha ukta lakṣaṇayoḥ viruddhayoḥ sannipāte sati saṃśaya darśanāt ayam anyaḥ sandigdhaḥ iti kecid yathā mūrta tva amūrta tvam prati manasaḥ kriyāvat tva asparśava tvayoḥ iti nanu ayam asādhāraṇaḥ eva acākṣuṣa tva pratyakṣa tva vat saṃhatayoḥ anyatara pakṣā sambhavāt tatas ca anadhyavasitaḥ iti vakṣyāmaḥ 
[II,197,6]	nanu śāstre tatra tatra ubhayathā darśanam saṃśaya kāraṇam apadiśyate iti na saṃśayaḥ viṣaya dvaita darśanāt saṃśaya utpattau viṣaya dvaita darśanam eva kāraṇam tulya bala tve ca tayoḥ paraspara virodhāt nirṇaya anutpādaka tvam syāt na tu saṃśaya hetu tvam na ca tayoḥ tulya bala tvam asti anyatarasya anumeya uddeśasya āgama bādhita tvāt ayantu viruddha bhedaḥ eva 
[II,197,11]	yaḥ tu san anumeye vyāptyā tad samāna asamāna jātīyayoḥ sa pakṣa vipakṣayoḥ san ā iva sa sandigdhaḥ anaikāntikaḥ sandeha janaka tvāt iti kārya upanyāsaḥ na tu lakṣaṇam indriya ādiṣu api sadbhāvena ati vyāpaka tvāt udāharaṇantu yathā yasmāt viṣāṇī tasmāt gauḥ iti viṣāṇinam piṇḍam pakṣīkṛtya gauḥ iti sādhayataḥ viṣāṇi tvāt iti hetuḥ anaikāntikaḥ pakṣa traya vṛtti tvāt ayantu sa pakṣa vyāpaka tve sati vipakṣa eka deśa vṛttiḥ agauḥ ayam viṣāṇi tvāt iti sa pakṣa eka deśa vṛtti tve sati vipakṣa vyāpakaḥ sa pakṣa vipakṣa eka deśa vṛttiḥ ca nityaḥ śabdaḥ asparśavat tvāt iti caturvidhaḥ anaikāntikaḥ 
[II,197,19]	atha cāturvidhyam anupapannam anaikāntikasya lakṣaṇañcāvyāpakam viruddha avyabhicārya sādhāraṇayoḥ avyāpanāt iti āśaṅkā pratiṣedha artham ekasmin ca dvayoḥ ityādi prakaraṇam dvayoḥ hetvoḥ vibhinna dharmi sthayoḥ sannipāte saṃśaya adarśanāt yathā nityaḥ śabdaḥ kāryatvāt nityam ākāśam akārya tvāt iti ekasmin dharmiṇī iti padam tathā tathā api ekasmin dharmiṇi dvayoḥ sannipāte api na saṃśayaḥ yathā anityaḥ śabdaḥ kāryatvāt nityaḥ tu amūrta kārya tvāt iti tad artham yathā ukta lakṣaṇayoḥ 
[II,197,26]	tathā api aviruddha artha sādhakayoḥ evaṃvidhayoḥ api na saṃśaya hetu tvam yathā nityaḥ śabdaḥ kāryatvāt āśritaḥ guṇa tvāt atas viruddhayoḥ viruddha artha sādhakayoḥ sannipāte saṃśayasya darśanāt ayam anyaḥ sandigdhaḥ anaikāntikaḥ iti kecid udāharaṇantu yathā mūrta tva amūrta tvam prati manasaḥ kriyāvat tva asparśavat tvayoḥ iti mūrtam manaḥ kriyāvat tvāt chatra vat iti ekaḥ amūrtam manaḥ asparśavat tvāt ākāśa vat iti aparaḥ ubhayoḥ ca pakṣa dharma anvaya vyatirekavat tva upalabdheḥ kim mūrtam manaḥ syāt uta amūrtam iti saṃśayaḥ 
[II,198,7]	tat asat ubhayoḥ prayoga asambhavāt tathā hi ekasmin sādhane prayukte tasya nirduṣṭa tāyām sādhya siddheḥ anyasya upanyāsa anupapattiḥ duṣṭa tāyām vā sā eva asya abhidheya iti na ca paraspara viruddha artha sādhaka tvam eva anumānayoḥ doṣaḥ pramāṇena ubhayoḥ ekatra sadbhāva siddhau virodhasya abhāva prasaṅgāt avyabhicārya anumānayoḥ ca avaśyam artha vyavasthāpaka tvam avyabhicārasya tad lakṣaṇa tvāt viparyaye tu vyabhicāri tvam eva yathā mūrtam manaḥ asparśavat tve sati kriyāvat tvāt amūrtañca kriyāvat tve satya sparśavat tvāt iti samastayoḥ prayogaḥ 
[II,198,14]	tatra api asādhāraṇam iti āha nanu ayam asādhāraṇaḥ eva acākṣuṣa tva pratyakṣa tva vat saṃhatayoḥ anyatara pakṣa asambhavāt iti yathā hi rūpa ati indriya guṇa vyatirekeṇa anya guṇānām guṇa vyavahāre sādhya sāmānyavat tvāt dravya tve sati niyamena ācākṣuṣa tvam hetuḥ na sa pakṣe rūpa ādau asti na api vipakṣe ghaṭa ādau iti a sādhāraṇaḥ tadvat sahacarayoḥ kriyāvat tva asparśavat tvayoḥ anyatara pakṣā sambhavāt iti anyatarasmin sa pakṣe vipakṣe vā asambhavāt asādhāraṇa tvam na ca asya asaṅgrahaḥ iti āha tatas ca anadhyavasitaḥ iti vakṣyāmaḥ 
[II,198,21]	yat vā cākṣuṣa tva pratyakṣa tva vat iti vaidharmya udāharaṇam yathā hi guṇaḥ śabdaḥ sāmānyavat tvāt dravya tve sati niyamena acākṣuṣa pratyakṣa tvāt andha ādi vat iti asya sa pakṣa eka deśe vartamānasya vipakṣāt atyantam vyāvṛttiḥ na ca evam kriyāvat tva asparśavat tvayoḥ iti āha saṃhatayoḥ anyatara pakṣa asambhavāt iti 
[II,198,25]	evam viruddha avyabhicāriṇaḥ asādhāraṇasya ca saṃśaya hetu tve nirākṛte sūtra virodham udbhāvayan āha nanu śāstre tatra tatra ubhayathā darśanam saṃśaya kāraṇam apadiśyate iti tatra tatra śāstre tasmin tasmin sūtre dṛṣṭañca dṛṣṭa vat dṛṣṭvā saṃśayaḥ bhavati dṛṣṭañca manasi kriyāvat tvam punar dṛṣṭena tulyam vartate iti dṛṣṭa vat asparśavat tvam atas viruddha sādhāna abhisambaddham manaḥ dṛṣṭvā saṃśete kim mūrtam uta amūrtam manaḥ iti ayathā dṛṣṭam ayathādṛṣṭañca ubhayathā dṛṣṭa tvāt saṃśayaḥ iti asādhāraṇasya ca saṃśaya hetu tvam uktam yathā dṛṣṭam pakṣe punar ayathā dṛṣṭam sa pakṣe vipakṣe ca na dṛṣṭam atas ubhayathā dṛṣṭa tvāt saṃśayaḥ 
[II,199,7^1]	yat vā yathādṛṣṭam kriyāvat tvena punar ayathā dṛṣṭam asparśavat tvena atas ubhayathā ubhābhyām saha dṛṣṭa tvāt saṃśayaḥ iti uktam pareṇa āha na yuktam etat saṃśayasya viṣaya dvaita darśanāt utpatteḥ asya eva vivaraṇam saṃśaya utpattau viṣaya dvaita darśanam eva kāraṇam iti viṣaya dvaite dṛśyate iti viṣaya dvaita darśanam sāmānayam eva viṣayasya vā dvaitam dvaividhyam yasya tat tathā uktam sāmānyam tad darśanam eva viruddha viśeṣa anuvṛtti hetu tvāt saṃśaya kāraṇam na viruddha hetu sannipātaḥ asādhāraṇa dharmaḥ vā 
[II,199,7^2]	viruddha viśeṣaiḥ saha anupalambhena tasya tad smāraka tva anupapatteḥ viruddha viśeṣa anusmṛti hetuḥ ca dharmaḥ saṃśaya kāraṇam na paraspara virodhī samāna balaḥ iti samāna bala tve ca tayoḥ paraspara virodhāt itarasya itareṇa pratibandhāt nirṇaya anutpādaka tvam syāt na saṃśaya hetutvam taila ādinā abhyaktasya śālibījasya sva aṅkura anutpādaka tva vat iti abhyupagamya etat uktam paramārthataḥ na ca tayoḥ tulya bala tvam asti anyatarasya amūrtam manaḥ iti anumeya uddeśasya āgama virodhi tvāt iti tathā ca āgamaḥ tad abhāvāt aṇu manaḥ iti mūrta tvañca avyāpi parimāṇa sambandhi tvam eva 
[II,199,21]	atha idam vacanam apramāṇam tarhi manaḥ sadbhāva asiddheḥ āśraya asiddham anumānam iti yathā ukta lakṣaṇa anupapattiḥ na ca mūrta tva anabhyupagame yugapad jñāna anutpattyā api manaḥ sadbhāva siddhiḥ amūrtasya sakala indriya adhiṣṭhāyaka tvena yugapad jñāna utpatti prasaṅgāt atas pratijñā vacanasya āgamena virodhāt amūrta anumānam na yathā ukta lakṣaṇam iti ayantu viruddha bhedaḥ pratijñā avasare abhihitaḥ eva viruddhāt bhidyate iti viruddha bhedaḥ kāla atyaya apadiṣṭaḥ duṣṭa pakṣa upanyāsa anantaram upanyāsāt 
[II,200,1]	sūtra dvitayañcaḥ eka dharmi viṣaya tvena saṃśaya pratipādana artham iti vyākhyeyam tathā ca niyata sāmānya vastu pratiniyata viśeṣaiḥ sahacaritam ekadā dṛṣṭam punar tad tulyam anya viśeṣa a inābhūtam atas kāla antare deśa vyavadhāna vaśāt tat dṛṣṭvā saṃśete kim idam evam āhosvit evam na bhavati iti tathā eka dharmi viṣaya tve api yathādṛṣṭam iti kiñcid sāmānya vat vastu kenacid viśeṣeṇa saha dṛṣṭam ayathādṛṣṭam tat eva upalabdhi viśeṣa śūnyam viśeṣa antara sahitam dṛṣṭam atas ubhayathā dṛṣṭa tvāt ubhābhyām saha dṛṣṭa tvāt ubhaya śūnyasya upalabdhau tad smaraṇe tu asati saṃśayaḥ bhavati iti yathā devadattam sa keśam upalabhya punar niṣkeśam atas kāla antare tam eva veṣṭita śirasam upalabhamānasya kim ayam sa keśaḥ niṣkeśaḥ vā iti saṃśayaḥ bhavati iti 
[II,200,11_II,200,21]	samasta sapakṣe tu asādhāraṇasya anadhyavasi tvam āha yaḥ ca sannanumeye tad samāna asamāna jātīyayoḥ sa pakṣa vipakṣayoḥ asan eva saḥ anyatara asiddhaḥ anadhyavasāya hetutvāt niścaya anutpādaka tvāt atas tad hetu tvāt anadhyavasitaḥ yathā sat kāryam utpatteḥ iti udāharaṇam sakalam kāryam utpatteḥ prāk sat utpadyamāna tvāt iti hetar naḥ ākāśa ādau na api khara viṣāṇa ādau iti anadhyavasitaḥ
[II,201,1^1]	na ca asya sūtreṇa asaṅgrahaḥ iti āha ayam aprasiddhaḥ anapadeśaḥ iti vacanāt avaruddhaḥ sa pakṣa vipakṣayoḥ aprasiddha tvāt iti evam asādhāraṇasya saṃśaya hetu tve niraste satra virodham udbhāvayan āha nanu ca ayam viśeṣaḥ saṃśaya hetuḥ abhihitaḥ śāstre tulya jātīyeṣu sa pakṣeṣu artha antara bhūteṣu vipakṣeṣu ca viśeṣasya asādhāraṇa dharmasya ubhayathā dṛṣṭa tvāt sa pakṣe vipakṣe ca dṛṣṭa tvāt iti anena asādhāraṇasya saṃśaya hetu tvam uktam iti āśaṅkya āha na sūtrasya anya artha tvāt sattā sambandhi tvāt artha śabda vācya tvāt ca kim dravyam guṇaḥ karma vā śabdaḥ iti saṃśayaḥ na param sattā sambandhāt śrāvaṇa tvāt ca iti ukte sūtrakāreṇa paraḥ brūte śrāvaṇa tva viśeṣasya upalabdheḥ katham śabde saṃśayaḥ iti āśaṅkya āha na ayam dravya ādīnām anyatamasya iti na dravyasya guṇasya karmaṇaḥ vā viśeṣaḥ śrāvaṇa tvam kintu sāmānyam eva sampadyate kasmāt 
[II,201,1^2]	yasmāt guṇa tve śabdasya sādhye tulya jātīyeṣu rūpa ādiṣu śukla tva ādi viśeṣaḥ guṇa tvena sahacaritaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ artha antara bhūteṣu utkṣepaṇa ādiṣu karma tvena sahacaritaḥ utkṣepaṇa tva ādi viśeṣaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ tathā pṛthivī ādiṣu pṛthivī tva ādiḥ dravya tvena iti dravya ādi bhedānām dravya guṇa karmaṇām ekaikaśas pratyekam viśeṣasya ubhayathā dṛṣṭvāt dravya guṇa tva ādi sahacaritasya dṛṣṭa tvāt upalabhyate ca śabde śrāvaṇa tvam viśeṣaḥ tat dravya tva ādi viṣayam smaraṇam bhavati eva atas kim dravyasya sataḥ ayam viśeṣaḥ śrāvaṇa tvam guṇasya karmaṇaḥ vā iti uktena nyāyena saṃśaya kāraṇam śrāvaṇa tvam na tu asādhāraṇa tvena ṣaṭsu api padārtheṣu asādhāraṇa dharma upalabdhau saṃśaya prasaṅgāt utkṣepaṇa tva ādi viśeṣa anupalabdheḥ ca saṃśaya kāraṇa tvam anvaya vyatirekābhyām upalabdham na tad upalabdheḥ 
[II,201,23_II,202,2]	na ca sarvasmāt vyāvṛttam viśeṣam upalabhamānasya viruddha viśeṣa anusmṛteḥ abhāvāt saṃśayaḥ yuktaḥ sadbhāve api anucchedaḥ syāt nirṇaya utpatti kāraṇa abhāvāt tasmāt sāmānya pratyakṣāt eva saṃśayaḥ na viśeṣa darśanāt iti upasaṃhāraḥ yat vā viśeṣavat tvasya ubhayathā sa pakṣa vipakṣā viśeṣitasya upalabdheḥ tad upalambhāt ca śabde saṃśayaḥ na saṃśaya kāraṇam asādhāraṇaḥ dharmaḥ ṣaṭsu api padārtheṣu saṃśaya prasaṅgāt iti śeṣam pūrvavat 
[II,202,7]	atha apadeśa anantaram nidarśana svarūpa nirūpaṇa artham dvividham nidarśanam ityādi prakaraṇam dvividham iti vibhāgaḥ nidarśanam iti niruktiḥ lakṣaṇam nidarśyate sādhya sādhanayoḥ bahis vyāptiḥ asmin iti nidarśanam dṛṣṭāntaḥ tathā nidarśyate sādhya sādhanayoḥ vyāptiḥ anena iti nidarśanam vyāpti pratipādakam dṛṣṭānta vacanam tathā hi nidarśanam itarasmāt bhidyate yathā ukta dṛṣṭānta vacana tvāt yaḥ tu na bhidyate na ca asau evam yathā pratijñādiḥ iti 
[II,202,13_II,202,27]	tat kena rūpeṇa dvividham sādharmyeṇa vaidharmyeṇa ca iti tatra anumeya sāmānyena sādhya sāmānyena liṅga sāmānyasya sādhana sāmānyasya anuvidhāna darśanam sādharmya nidarśanam sādhana sāmānyam vyāpyam vyāpakam ca sādhya sāmānyam iti yat yat kriyāvat tat tat dravyam dṛṣṭam yathā śaraḥ iti udāharaṇam atra hi dravya tva vyāptau kriyāvat tvam sādhanam asti iti anumeya viparyaye sādhya viparyaye liṅgasya sādhanasya abhāva darśanam vaidharmya nidarśanam tat yathā yat yat adravyam tat tat kriyāvat na bhavati yathā sattā iti sattāyām hi dravya tva vyāvṛttyā kriyāvat tva vyāvṛttiḥ asti iti vaidharmya udāharaṇam 
[II,203,3]	anena nidarśana ābhāsāḥ nidarśana vat ābhāsantaḥ iti nidarśana ābhāsāḥ tad samāna dharmāṇaḥ nirastāḥ bhavanti iti sva vākye parivarjana artham para vākye ca udbhāvanā artham nirūpyante tat yathā nityaḥ śabdaḥ amūrta tvāt yat yat amūrtam dṛṣṭam tat nityam dṛṣṭam yathā paramāṇuḥ iti sādhanasya amūrtasya paramāṇau abhāvāt sādhana vikalam udāharaṇam asmin eva sādhye yathā karma iti sādhya vikalam nitya tvasya karmaṇi abhāvāt yathā sthālī iti ubhaya vikalam nitya tvasya amūrta tvasya ca sthālyām abhāvāt yathā tamaḥ iti dharma asiddham sāṃkhya abhyupagatasya tamasaḥ aprasiddha tvāt ambara vat iti sādhya sādhana adhikaraṇa tve api ananugataḥ vacana doṣaḥ yat yat amūrtam dṛṣṭam tat tad nityam dṛṣṭam yathā ambaram iti vacanam vinā anugatasya apratīteḥ 
[II,203,13_II,203,18]	yat vā samyak dṛṣṭāntaḥ api ākāśā sattva vādinaḥ na sādhya siddhim karoti yāvat na pramāṇataḥ vyavasthāpyate iti ābhāsaḥ ucyate anye tu ābhāsā avasare samyak dṛṣṭānta upadarśanam ābhāsānām ābhāsata ājñāpana artham ittham bhūtam hi nidarśanam etad pratirūpakāṇi ca tad ābhāsāḥ iti yat yat dravyam tat tat kriyāvat dṛṣṭam iti ca viparīta anugamaḥ tathā ca evam bruvataḥ dravya tvam vyāpyam kriyāvat tvan ca vyāpakam syāt iti viparītā vyāpya vyāpaka bhāva pratipattiḥ na ca etat asti ākāśa ādau kriyāvat tvam vinā api dravya tva upalabdheḥ samavyāptike api sādhanasya vyāpaka tva abhidhāne sādhyasya pratipattiḥ na syāt iti dūṣaṇam viṣama vyāptike viparīta anugamaḥ doṣaḥ na samavyāptike iti ca anye atra upasaṃhāra vākyam liñgañca anumeyaḥ ca ubhayañca āśrayaḥ ca iti liṅga anumeya ubhaya āśrayāḥ te asiddhāḥ yeṣu ābhāseṣu te tathā uktāḥ te ca ananugatāḥ ca viparīta anugatāḥ ca iti liṅga anumeya ubhaya āśraya asiddhān anugata viparītān anugatāḥ sādharmya nidarśana ābhāsāḥ 
[II,204,1^1]	vaidharmya nidarśana ābhāsān darśayati yat anityam tat mūrtam dṛṣṭam yathā karma iti sādhana avyāvṛttam tasya hi amūrta tvāt iti tasmin eva sādhye yathā paramāṇuḥ iti sādhya avyāvṛttam vyatireka udāharaṇam paramāṇoḥ nitya tvāt iti yathā ākāśam iti ubhaya avyāvṛttam amūrta tvasya nitya tvasya ca tatra avyāvṛttiḥ iti yathā tamaḥ iti dharma asiddham sāṃkhya abhyupagatasya tamasaḥ aprasiddha tvāt iti ghaṭa vat iti ubhaya avyāvṛttau api avyatirekaḥ yat yat nityam na bhavati tat tat amūrtam na bhavati iti vacanam vinā vyatirekasya apratipatteḥ ghaṭā sattva vādinaḥ vā pramāṇena apratipāditaḥ na sādhya siddhim karoti iti ābhāsaḥ ucyate 
[II,204,1^2_II,204,17]	yat niṣkriyam tat adravyam dṛṣṭam iti vyatirekaḥ sādhya vyāvṛttyā hi sādhana vyāvṛttiḥ vācyā na tu sādhana vyāvṛttyā sādhya vyāvṛttiḥ kriyāvat tva abhāve api ākāśa ādau dravya tvasya sādhyasya avyāvṛtteḥ sādhana abhāvaḥ hi vyāpakaḥ sādhya abhāvaḥ vyāpyaḥ iti eteṣām upasaṃhāraḥ liṅgañca anumeyaḥ ca ubhayañca iti liṅga anumeya ubhayāni tāni avyāvṛttāni yeṣu ābhāseṣu te liṅga anumeya ubhaya avyāvṛttāḥ te ca āśraya asiddhañca avyāvṛt tañca viparīta vyāvṛttañca iti liṅga anumeya ubhaya avi āvṛtta āśraya asiddha avi āvṛtta viparīta vyāvṛttāḥ vaidharmya nidarśana ābhāsāḥ iti 
[II,204,22]	evam saha ābhāsaiḥ nidarśanam upadarśya anusandhāna nirūpaṇa artham āha nidarśane anumeya sāmānyena saha ityādi nidarśane dṛṣṭānte anumeya sāmānyena sādhya sāmānyena saha dṛṣṭasya liṅga sāmānyasya anumeye pakṣe anvānayanam anusandhānam ānayanam pratipādanam anyasya api sambhavati iti liṅgasya iti padam tathā api liṅgasya nidarśane pratipādanam asti iti tat vyudāsāya anumeya padam anumeye ca gṛhīta avinābhāvasya liṅgasya pratipādakam hetu vacanam api iti nidarśane anumeya sāmānyena saha dṛṣṭasya liṅga sāmānyasya iti padam atas anusandha ānam itarasmāt bhidyate nidarśane gṛhīta vyāptikasya liṅgasya anumeye anvānayana rūpa tvāt yaḥ tu na bhidyate na ca asau evam yathā pratijñādiḥ iti 
[II,205,4]	saṅgraha ukteḥ vivaraṇam āha anumeya dharma mātra tvena abhihitam liṅga sāmānyam na tu samartham iti mātrā abhidhānena darśayati anupalabdha śaktikam iti anupalabdhā śaktiḥ avinā abhāvaḥ yasya tat tathā uktam punar nidarśane anumeya dharma sāmānyena saha dṛṣṭam anumeye pakṣe yena vacanena anu paścāt sandhīyate pakṣa dharma tayā khyāpyate tat anusandhānam 
[II,205,9]	tat api dvividham sādharmyeṇa vaidharmyeṇa ca tatra anumeya sāmānyena saha liṅga sāmānyasya nidarśane sattvam upalabhya abhisandhatte tathā ca ayam kriyāvān vāyuḥ iti vaidharmya nidarśane tu anumeyasya dravya tvasya abhāve ca tasya kriyāvat tvasya asattvam upalabhya na ca tathā vāyuḥ niṣkriyaḥ iti upasaṃhāraḥ niṣkriya tva pratiṣedhena kriyāvat tvam upasaṃharati iti pṛthak vacanantu pratiṣedha abhiprāyeṇa eva 
[II,205,14]	nanu vyartham anusandhāna vacanam tad antareṇa api hetu vacanāt gṛhīta vyāptikāt sādhya siddheḥ na anena vinā abādhita viṣaya tvasya apratipatteḥ hetu vacanantu kāraṇa mātra upasthāpakam na tu gṛhīta vyāptikasya antar vyāpti pratipādakam iti yathābhūtena dravya tva avinā bhāvinā pramāṇa antara aviruddhena kriyāvat tvena kriyāvān karaḥ tathā ca vāyuḥ iti antar vyāpti pratipattiḥ tad abhāve tu bahis vyāpti sadbhāve api na gamaka tvam yathā śabdasya anitya tve sādhye sāmānyavat tve sati cākṣuṣa pratyakṣaḥ tasya kāla atyaya apadiṣṭa tvam ca iti atas eva atra upanaya vacanam na nirviṣaya tvāt apramāṇam 
[II,205,22]	na ca upasaṃhāram vinā dharmi viśeṣeṇa sambandha aprasiddhau tatra eva sādhya viśeṣa pratipattiḥ syāt sva artha anumāna kāle ca upanaya arthasya upalabdheḥ kāryam tat vacanam sva pratipatti anusāreṇa para artha anumāna pravṛtteḥ na ca sva pratipattau etasya asatvam avinā abhau a sambandha smaraṇa anantaram parāma śaṃjñānasya anubhavāt anabhyupagame ca sambandha smaraṇasya aniyata tvāt niyata pradeśe pratipattiḥ na syāt iti uktam 
[II,206,1_II,206,7]	tasmāt ayam iti aparokṣatā nirdeśasya avinā abhāva sambandha smaraṇa anantaram upalabdheḥ asti parāmarśa jñānam atas tad upanyāsa artham kāryam anusandhāna vacanam iti atha pratyāmnāya svarūpa upadarśana artham anumeya tvena uddiṣṭe ityādi prakaraṇam anumeya tvena anumāna yogya tvena uddiṣṭe ca aniścite ca pareṣām saṃśayita viparyasta avyutpannānām punar niścaya āpādana artham pratijñāyāḥ punarvacanam pratyāmnāyaḥ 
[II,206,11]	saṅgraha ukteḥ vivaraṇam āha anumeye dharma mātre pratipādya tvena sādhya tvena uddiṣṭe ca aniścite ca pareṣām kim viśiṣṭānām hetu ādibhiḥ avayavaiḥ āhita śaktīnām iti āhitā śaktiḥ avinā abhāvaḥ yasya liṅgasya yaiḥ taiḥ tathā uktaiḥ teṣām etasmāt sādhanāt bhaviṣyati sādhya siddhiḥ iti evam kṛta āsthānām iti bhāvaḥ niścaya āpādana artham pratijñāyāḥ punarvacanam pratyāmnāyaḥ iti punarukta mātra vyavaccheda artham pratijñāyāḥ punarvacanam iti padam tathā api anityaḥ śabdaḥ anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti punar ukta vyudāsa artham niścaya āpādana artham iti padam avipratipannasya etasmāt api niścayaḥ bhavati iti tad artham pareṣām iti tathā api teṣām madhye kasyacid eka avayava upadarśanena anvaya vyatireka anusmaraṇa dvāreṇa artha pratipattiḥ bhavati iti parisamāptena vākyena iti grahaṇam yasmin avayave sati vākyam parisamāpyate iti tat evam pratyāmnāyaḥ itarasmāt bhidyate yathā ukta lakṣaṇa tvāt iti 
[II,206,23]	nanu pratijñā vacanasya tu vināśi tvena avasthāna asambhavāt katham punarvacanam iti tad samāna śabda uccāraṇāt yathā kṣaṇika tve api karmaṇaḥ pūrvam samāna abhinaya karaṇāt punar nṛtyati iti vyapadeśaḥ tadvat pratijñā samāna śabda prayoga karaṇāt punarvacanam iti vyapadeśaḥ bhavati eva atiśaye pūnaḥ śabdaḥ vivakṣitaḥ iti pratijñā pakṣaḥ tasya punarvacanam ghaṭataḥ eva 
[II,207,1_II,208,11]	liṅga vākya artha vādinaḥ tu pratijñāyate anena iti pratijñā liṅgam tasya punarvacanam pratyāmnāya iti udāharaṇantu tasmāt dravyam eva iti etena adravya tva pratipādaka pramāṇa abhāvaḥ api upadarśitaḥ eva atha vyartham pratyāmnāya vacanam sambandha abhidhānāt eva vivakṣita artha prasiddheḥ tat uktam ḍiṇḍika rāgam parityajya akṣiṇī nimīlya cintaya tāvat kim iyata artha pratipattiḥ bhavati nava iti yadi iha bhavati kim anayā śabda mālayā na bhavati iti na vācyam dṛṣṭa tvāt na etat evam pratijñā vacanam vinā anvayanī atireka aprasiddhau sambandha abhidhānasya āgamaka tvena pūrvam eva vyavasthāpita tvāt 
[II,208,13]	atha pratijñādeḥ eva artha pratipādaka tvam astu kim pratyāmnāyena tathā hi pratijñā vacanaiḥ viṣaya vyavasthāpanāt hetu udāharaṇābhyām bahis vyāpti prasiddhau upanayena antar vyāpti upadarśane sati avaśyam abhipreta artha siddhiḥ iti satyam etat tathā api avaśyambhāvinaḥ arthasya pratijñādinā pratipāditasya pratipādana artham avaśyam kāryam nigamanam iti āha na hi etasmin iti na pūrveṣām avayavānām samastānām tad artha vācaka tvam asti vyastānām itaretara vyāvṛtta sva artha vyavasthāpane caritārtha tvam iti anyat atas vācyam yasya sahakāriṇām pūrva padānām samastānām api smṛti upasthāpitānām vākya artha pratipādaka tvam iti 
[II,208,21]	atha sādhanasya antar vyāpti bahis vyāpti abhidhāne sati sādhya viśeṣaḥ gamyate eva iti āha gamyamāna artha tvāt iti ced na atiprasaṅgāt tathā hi pratijñā anantaram hetu mātra abhidhānam kartavyam svatas eva viduṣām hetu upalambhe sati anvaya vyatireka anusmaraṇam tasmāt ca adhigatiḥ bhaviṣyati iti viśeṣa abhidhāna vaiyarthyam syāt 
[II,208,25]	atha param pratipādayatā vacanena eva pratipādanam kāryam iti śeṣāṇām prayogaḥ tarhi vākya artha pratipādana artham nigamanam api kāryam na ca pratipādya abhiprāyeṇa prayogaḥ yuktaḥ tasya manuṣya dharmaṇā sākṣāt apratīteḥ avyavasthāpanāt ca tathā hi kaścid ekasmāt eva avayavāt artham pratipadyate kaścid dvābhyām anyaḥ tribhiḥ iti anavasthita tvāt pratipādyānām tad abhiprāyā niścaye prayoga anupapattiḥ eva syāt atas param pratipādayatā sva pratipatti upāya upadarśanam kāryam iti pañcānām prayogaḥ yuktaḥ tathā hi pradeśa stham dhūmam upalabhya avinā abhau a sambandham smṛtvā tathā ca ayam dhūmavān iti parāmṛśati tatas sādhyam pratipadyate tasmāt agnimān iti nigamana arthasya api upalabdheḥ para pratipādanāya tad upanyāsaḥ yuktaḥ eva iti pañcānām prayogaḥ kāryaḥ iti āha bhāṣya kāraḥ tasmāt atra eva artha parisamāptiḥ iti 
[II,209,8_II,209,10]	anye tu antar vyāpti pratipādana artham nigamanam iti manyante anusandhānāt pakṣa vyāpaka tva prasiddhau viparīta prasaṅga pratiṣedha artham nigamanam iti viparīta artha vyavasthāpaka pramāṇasya aprāmāṇya upadarśane sati pakṣe vyāptiḥ pratīyate eva yatra ca para pakṣa apratiṣedhaḥ tatra hetoḥ na gamaka tvam yathā mūrkhaḥ asau tad putra tvāt upalabhyamāna tat putra vat iti atra hi tad putrasya amūrkha tve na kiñcid bādhakam asti iti tad sādhaka pramāṇa abhāvaḥ ca niścitaḥ eva iti anyathā siddham sādhanam etat 
[II,209,15]	atha avinābhūtasya pramāṇa virodha abhāvāt na yuktam viparīta pramāṇasya aprāmāṇya upadarśanam iti ced na tad antareṇa avinābhā asya eva aprasiddheḥ tathā hi nitya tva pratipādaka pramāṇasya prāmāṇye sati na śabde kṛtaka tvasya anitya tvena vyāptiḥ syāt iti na ca para pakṣa pratiṣedhakāt eva sva pakṣa siddhiḥ vyadhikaraṇa tvāt hetoḥ api vaiyarthya prasaṅgāt ca iti para pakṣa pratiṣedhe tu upadarśita bahis vyāptikam pakṣe ca upalabhyamānam bhavati eva sādhanam iti nigamana prayogaḥ kāryaḥ 
[II,209,21]	atha pratijñā vacanam eva para pakṣa pratiṣedha sahāyam sādhanam iti ced na tasya sādhya mātra abhidhāyaka tvāt sādhyam iti arhati arthe śakya arthe vā kṛta abhidhānāt katham tad vacanāt tasya siddhiḥ tasmāt bahis vyāpti vat antar vyāptim samarthayatā abādhita viṣaya tva asat pratipakṣa tva pratipādana artham eva avayava antaram abhidheyam 
[II,209,25]	atha prakaraṇa sama kāla atyaya apadiṣṭayoḥ api bahis vyāpti sadbhāvāt gamaka tvam asti ca tayoḥ pakṣa vyāpaka tve satya nvaya vyatireka sadbhāvaḥ iti ayuktam etat tādātmya tad utpatti lakṣaṇa pratibandha āyattaḥ tu avyabhicāraḥ na bhavati iti uktam vyāpti samarthana avasare tasmāt ukta nyāyena atra eva artha parisamāptiḥ iti 
[II,210,3_II,210,17]	evam vibhinna prakaraṇeṣu avayavānām svarūpa upadarśane api ekatra tad svarūpa parijñāna apekṣayā praśnaḥ katham iti anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti anena aniścita anitya tva mātra viśiṣṭaḥ śabdaḥ kathyate iti pratijñā eṣā prayatna anantarīyaka tvāt iti anena anitya tva sādhana dharma mātram abhidhīyate na tu samartham iti hetu vacanam iha yat prayatna ānantarīyakam tat anityam dṛṣṭam yathā ghaṭaḥ iti anena sādhya sāmānyena sādhana sāmānyasya anugama mātram ucyate iti sādharmya udāharaṇam nityam aprayatna ānantarīyakam dṛṣṭam yathā ākāśam iti anena sādhya abhāvena saha sādhanasya asattvam pradarśyate iti vaidharmya udāharaṇam tathā ca prayatna anantarīyakaḥ śabdaḥ na ca tathā prayatna ānantarīyakaḥ na bhavati iti anvaya vyatirekābhyām dṛṣṭa sāmarthyasya sādhana sāmānyasya śabde anusandhānam gamyate tasmāt anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti anena anityaḥ eva śabdaḥ iti pratipipādayiṣita artha parisamāptiḥ gamyate iti abhipreta artha siddhiḥ bhavati iti atas pañca avayavena eva vākyena pareṣām sva niścita artha pratipādanam kriyate iti siddham atra ca śabda viśeṣasya pakṣīkaraṇe prayatna ānantarīyaka tvam sādhanam vivakṣitam iti jñeyam anyathā hi śabda mātra parigrahe prayatna ānantarīyaka tvam bhāga asiddham syāt na hi prayatna anantaram sarva śabdānām janma asti iti 
[II,210,21_II,211,3]	atha nirṇayaḥ vidyā antaram iti kecid tad niṣedha artham viśeṣa darśana jam ityādi prakaraṇam para artha anumāna anantaram asya antar bhāva nirūpaṇam atra api antar bhāva jñāpana artham nirṇayaḥ iti lakṣya nirdeśaḥ avaśiṣṭam lakṣaṇam avadhāraṇa jñānam hi viparyaya jñānam api bhavati na tu viśeṣa darśanāt jāyate viśeṣa darśana jam ca saṃśaya jñānam api iti avadhāraṇa grahaṇam 
[II,211,8]	tathā api viśeṣa darśana jam avadhāraṇa jñānam nirṇayaḥ iti ukte vyabhicāra abhāvāt vyartham saṃśaya virodhi iti padam na viśiṣṭa nirṇaya lakṣaṇa artha tvāt yadi api viśeṣa darśana jam avadhāraṇa jñānam iti sakala nirṇaya vyāpi idam sāmānya lakṣaṇam tathā api saṃśaya virodhi iti padam saṃśaya pūrvakasya nirṇayasya lakṣaṇa artham tathā ca naiyāyikaiḥ uktam vimṛśya pakṣa pratipakṣābhyām artha avadhāraṇam nirṇayaḥ iti saṃśaya pūrvakasya lakṣaṇam vimṛśya iti vimarśam kṛtvā pakṣa pratipakṣābhyām iti tad vacanābhyām sa punar sādhana dūṣaṇābhyām nirṇayaḥ iti 
[II,211,15_II,211,17]	atha viśeṣa darśanāt saṃśayaḥ vyāvartate na nirṇayāt iti katham tat virodhi tvam upacāreṇa nirṇaya kāraṇasya saṃśaya virodhi tvāt nirṇayaḥ tat virodhi iti uktam asya antarbhāvam āha etat eva pratyakṣam anumānam vā na jñāna antaram pratyakṣa sāmagrī janyam hi pratyakṣam anumāna sāmagrījanyantu anumānam iti yat viśeṣa darśanāt saṃśaya virodhi utpadyate sa nirṇayaḥ iti prāktanasya vivaraṇam 
[II,211,21]	atra sthāṇu puruṣayoḥ ūrdhva tā mātra sādṛśya ālocanāt viśeṣeṣu apratyakṣeṣu ubhaya viśeṣa anusmaraṇāt kim ayam sthāṇuḥ puruṣaḥ vā iti saṃśaya utpattau satyām śiraḥ pāṇi ādi viśeṣa darśanāt puruṣaḥ eva ayam iti avadhāraṇa jñānam indriya artha sannikarṣāt utpatteḥ pratyakṣa nirṇayaḥ viṣāṇa mātra darśanāt iti piṇḍa vyavadhāne api sādṛśya viśiṣṭa viṣāṇa darśanāt gauḥ gavayaḥ vā iti saṃśaya utpattau satyām sāsnā mātra darśanāt avinā abhau a sambandha smaraṇe sati parāmarśa jñāna anantaram gauḥ eva ayam iti avadhāraṇa jñānam anumāna nirṇayaḥ 
[II,212,2_II,212,5]	atha smṛteḥ kārya kāraṇa viṣaya svarūpa nirūpaṇa artham liṅga darśana icchā anusmaraṇa ādi apekṣāt ityādi prakaraṇam liṅga darśana icchā anusmaraṇa ādi apekṣāt liṅgadarśanañca icchā ca anusmaraṇañcā iti tathā uktāni tāni ādiḥ yeṣām ityādi padena praṇidhāna ādeḥ grahaṇam tāni apekṣate iti tad apekṣaḥ tasmāt ātma manasoḥ saṃyoga viśeṣāt iti asamavāyi kāraṇa nirdeśaḥ liṅga darśana icchā anusmaraṇa ādi apekṣāt paṭu abhyāsa ādara pratyaya janitāt ca saṃskārāt iti nimitta kāraṇa nirdeśaḥ dṛṣṭa śruta anubhūteṣu artheṣu iti dṛṣṭaḥ pratyakṣeṇa śrutaḥ śabdena anubhūtaḥ anumānena 
[II,212,13_II,212,19]	anye tu dṛṣṭaḥ cakṣuṣā anubhūtaḥ tvac indriyeṇa iti tatra liṅgam darśayati śeṣa anuvyavasāya anusmaraṇa icchā dveṣa hetuḥ iti upayuktāt liṅgāt anumeyaḥ śeṣaḥ saḥ anuvyavasīyate anena iti śeṣa anuvyavasāyaḥ parāmarśa jñānam tasya hetuḥ avinā abhāva sambandha smaraṇam tathā pada smaraṇāt vākya smaraṇam sukha smaraṇāt icchā duḥkha smaraṇāt dveṣaḥ iti atīta viṣayāḥ iti sva rūpa kathanam atītaḥ viṣayaḥ yasyāḥ sā tathā ukta iti nanu ayuktam etat vidyamāne api vastuni smaraṇasya darśanāt iti a vyāptiḥ ativyāptiḥ ca anumāna ādeḥ atīta viṣaya tvāt iti 
[II,212,21]	atha codanā eva bhūtam bhaviṣyantam viprakṛṣṭa ādikam artham prakāśayati na anyat kiñcanaḥ indriya ādikam iti ced na anumānasya api atīta ādi artha prakāśaka tvena upalambhāt tathā ca megha unnatyā bhaviṣyati vṛṣṭiḥ iti anumīyate nadī pūrāt viśiṣṭāt upariṣṭāt vṛṣṭiḥ iti uktam pratyakṣañca atra avinābhāva grāhakam abhyupeyam anyathā vyāpti grahaṇa abhāve anumānam eva na pravarteta na ca anumānena eva avinābhāva grahaṇam anavasthā prasaṅgāt vartamānena ca avinā abhāva grahaṇe katham atīta ādi artha anumānam syāt anyena avinābhāva grahaṇe anyasya anumitau atiprasaṅgāt tasmāt atīta viṣaya tvam vyākhyeyam upacāreṇa yatra hi viṣaye anubhavaḥ atītaḥ tatra smṛtiḥ utpadyate iti 
[II,213,4_II,213,7]	anye tu atītaḥ vyavahitaḥ viṣayaḥ yasya anubhavasya asau atīta viṣayaḥ sa viṣayaḥ yasyāḥ sā atīta viṣaya iti prāpte sati ekasya viṣayasya lopaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ iti atīta anubhava viṣaya tvam labhyate iti manyante atha artha ja tvam eva smṛteḥ kasmāt na iṣyate artha vināśe api utpādāt na ca yad deśa kāla āliṅgite anubhava jñānam utpannam tad ālambanam eva nyāyyam smṛti kāle tasya avidyamāna tayā viṣaya tva abhāvāt bāhya indriyāṇāñca smṛti janmani pratyekam vyabhicārāt antaḥkaraṇasya vyāpāraḥ niścīyate na ca tasya svātantryeṇa bahis viṣaye vyāpāraḥ sambhavati iti anartha ja tvam eva nyāyyam avaśyañca artha ja tve sati avyabhicāri tvā ādi dharma upeta tvāt pramā rūpa tāyām smṛteḥ pramāṇāt utpattiḥ vācyā anumāna ādeḥ ca vyāpāra anupalabdheḥ antaḥkaraṇasya svātantryeṇa tad utpattau prāmāṇye sati smṛteḥ aparokṣa tvam syāt na ca etat asti tasmāt nirviṣaya tvam eva 
[II,213,17_II,213,22]	atha ārṣa jñānasya kāraṇa viṣaya pramāṇa nirūpaṇa artham āmnāya vidhātṝṇām ityādi prakaraṇam āmnāyaḥ vedaḥ śruti smṛti lakṣaṇaḥ tasya vidhātāraḥ kartāraḥ teṣām ṛṣīṇām utpadyate yat prātibham jñānam iti pratibhayā saṃskāra viśeṣeṇa nirvartitam yathā ātma nivedanam yathā tasya padārthasya ātmā svarūpam tat nivedanam tad ālambanam utpadyate tat ārṣam iti ācakṣate keṣu artheṣu utpadyate atīta anāgata vartamāneṣu kiṃviśiṣṭeṣu atīndriyeṣu dharma ādiṣu ādipadena paramāṇu ādeḥ grahaṇam iti grantha upanibaddheṣu anupanibaddheṣu ca grantha upanibaddheṣu ātma ādiṣu anupanibaddheṣu ca paramāṇu ādiṣu iyān dharmaḥ iti kutas kāraṇa ādeṣu yathārtha vijñānam ātma manasoḥ saṃyogāt asamavāyinaḥ dharma viśeṣāt ca nimittāt iti tat tu prastāreṇa ṛṣīṇām atas tat ārṣam tat tu kadācid eva laukikānām api arṣīṇām evaṃvidham vijñānam asti iti kim atra pramāṇam iti āha kadācid eva laukikānām tat prātibham jñānam iti yathā kanyakā bravīti śvas me bhrātā āganta iti na ca indriya jam tat tat vyāpāram vinā api utpatteḥ 
[II,214,10_II,214,19]	atha bāhya indriyāṇām vyāpāra asambhave api antaḥkaraṇasya vyāpārāt pratyakṣa phala tvam sambandhaḥ api indriyeṇa saha bhrātuḥ saṃyukta viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ tathā hi tad viśiṣṭam ātmānam deśam kālam vā ālambya utpadyate jñānam etat iti uktam paraiḥ tat ca asat asya aparokṣa tva anupapatteḥ yatra hi aparokṣa jñānam tatra eva indriya vyāpāra kalpanā kriyate na ca atra tat asti iti na ca bahis viṣaye viśeṣaṇe api manasaḥ svātantryeṇa vyāpāraḥ sambhavati iti uktam liṅga liṅgi sambandha anusmaraṇān anubhavāt ca na anumāna jam śabdam vinā api utpatteḥ na śābdam atas pramāṇa antara phalam etat tathā praśne kṛte sati na pratyakṣa ādikam nirdiśati api tu hṛdayam me kathayati iti brūte atha kasmāt pratyakṣa anumāna anantaram ārṣa jñānasya na nirūpaṇam asmad ādīnām tena vyavahāra abhāvāt yatas tat tu prastāreṇa ṛṣīṇām eva kadācid eva laukikānām iti 
[II,214,23_II,215,3]	siddha darśanam vidyā antaram iṣṭam paraiḥ tad niṣedha artham āha siddha darśanam na jñāna antaram iti ārṣa jñāna anantaram asya antarbhāva nirūpaṇam ārṣe api antar bhāva artham yat siddhānām darśanam utpadyate tat pratyakṣam eva keṣu artheṣu sūkṣma vyavahita viprakṛṣṭeṣu iti sūkṣmāḥ paramāṇavaḥ vyavahitā nāga bhuvana ādayaḥ asmad ādi indriya apekṣayā na tu siddha indriyāṇām vyavadhāyakam asti viprakṛṣṭāḥ meru ādayaḥ teṣu siddhānām kim viśiṣṭānām mukta ātma vyavaccheda artham dṛśya draṣṭṝṇām iti kiñca teṣām sadbhāve pramāṇam iti āha dṛśyānām kadācid añjana ādi viyuktāḥ pratyakṣeṇa api upalabhyante kā punar teṣām siddhiḥ iti āha añjana pāda lepa khaḍga gulikā ādi siddhānām iti ādipadena cintāmaṇi prabhṛtīnām grahaṇam añjana ādi vaśāt ca siddha indriyāṇām sūkṣma ādi artha prakāśanam atas tat pratyakṣam eva na jñāna antaram iti 
[II,215,14]	atha jyotiṣām ayanam dṛṣṭvā prāṇinām śubham aśubham vā bhaviṣyati iti jñānam jña antaram iṣṭam tad niṣedha artham divya antarikṣa bhaumānām ityādi divi bhavam divyam ulkā pāta ādi antarikṣe bhavañca antarikṣam digdāha ādi bhūmau bhavam bhaumam bhū sañcala na ādi teṣām graha nakṣatra sañcāra ādi nimittam upalabhya prāṇinām dharma adharmayoḥ vipākaḥ phala dāna sāmarthyam tad darśanam na jñāna antaram iṣṭam tat api anumānam eva liṅga darśana anubandha smaraṇa ādi janya tvāt 
[II,215,20_II,215,22]	yat vā divya antarikṣa bhaumānām sura siddha manuṣyāṇām prāṇinām graha nakṣatra sañcāra ādi nimittam upalabhya dharma adharmayoḥ vipāka darśanam iṣṭam tat api anumānam eva iti atha liṅaga anapekṣam dharma adharma ādiṣu darśanam iṣṭam tat api yadi indriya artha sannikarṣāt aparokṣam utpadyate pratyakṣam eva atha indriya artha sannikarṣam vinā eva dharma viśeṣāt utpadyate tathā api ārṣam iti āha pratyakṣa ārṣayoḥ anyatarasmin antarbhūtam iti evam buddhiḥ iti upasaṃhāraḥ para upagatāyāḥ buddheḥ vināśa paraḥ iti 
[II,215,27_II,216,6^1]	atha buddheḥ anantaram sukhasya kārya kāraṇa svarūpa upadarśana artham anugraha lakṣaṇam sukham ityādi anugraha lakṣaṇam anugraha svarūpam yasmin utpanne sati ātmā anugṛhītam ātmānam manyate iti sraj ādi abhipreta viṣaya sānnidhye sati iti sraj ādayaḥ ca te abhipreta viṣayāḥ ca iti teṣām sānnidhyam anabhipretāḥ rāga ādayaḥ sukha hetavaḥ na bhavanti iti abhipreta grahaṇam iṣṭa upalabdhiḥ ca indriya artha sannikarṣaḥ ca iti tathā uktam tasmāt dharma ādi apekṣāt ityādi padena diś kāla ādeḥ grahaṇam tāni apekṣate iti tad apekṣaḥ tasmāt iṣṭa upalabdhi indriya artha sannikaṣāt dharma ādi apekṣāt ātma manasoḥ saṃyogāt asamavāyi kāraṇāt ātmani sukham utpadyate anugraha abhiṣvaṅga nayana ādi prasāda janakam iti kārya nirūpaṇam anugṛhītiḥ anugrahaḥ sukha viṣayam jñānam 
[II,216,6^2_II,216,21]	āsattiḥ abhiṣvaṅgaḥ nayana ādi prasādaḥ prasanna tā ādipadena mukha ādi prasanna tā gṛhyate iti tat etat asādhāraṇa tvāditarasmāt bhedakam iti jñeyam na ca sarvam vivekinaḥ svarūpataḥ duḥkham anugraha ātmakasya sukhasya api anubhavāt atas eva na duḥkha abhāve sukha vyavahāraḥ iti vācyam vibhinna kāraṇa janyasya tīvratara ādi bheda bhinnasya pratibhāsanāt evam duḥkhasya api na sukha abhāva rūpa tā iti yat etat uktam sukham tat sannihite vastuni indriya artha sannikarṣāt utpadyata atīta anāgateṣu smaraṇa saṅkalpābhyām iti āha atīteṣu sukha sādhaneṣu smṛti jam anāgateṣu saṅkalpa jam iti etat heyam upadarśitam

[II,217,5_II,217,9]	duḥkha nirūpaṇa artham āha upaghāta lakṣaṇam upaghāta svarūpam duḥkham iti upahanyate anena iti upahatam ātmānam manyate iti kāraṇam āha viṣa ādi anabhipreta viṣaya sānnidhye sati viṣa ādayaḥ ca te anabhipreta viṣayāḥ ca iti teṣām sānnidhye sati iti abhipretāḥ ca viṣaya ādayaḥ sūkha hetavaḥ eva iti anabhipreta grahaṇam anniṣṭa upalabdhi indriya artha sannikarṣāt adharma ādi apekṣāt aniṣṭa upalabdhiḥ ca indriya artha sannikarṣaḥ ca iti tathā uktaḥ tasmāt adharma apekṣāditya ādi padena diś kāla ādeḥ grahaṇam tasmāt aniṣṭa upalabdhi indriya artha sannikarṣāt adharma ādi apekṣāt ātma manasoḥ saṃyogāt asamavāyi kāraṇāt ātmani samavetam yat utpadyate tat duḥkham amarṣa upaghāta dainyānām nimittam kāraṇam tat itarasmāt bhedakam iti jñeyam atīteṣu sarpa ādiṣu iti kārya nirūpaṇam amarṣaḥ asahiṣṇu tā upahatiḥ upaghātaḥ duḥkha ālambanam jñānam iti dainyam dīna rūpa tā duḥkhāt utpadyate iti tat etat asādhāraṇa tvāt itarasmāt bhedakam iti jñeyam atīteṣu sarpa vyāghra caura ādiṣu duḥkha sādhaneṣu smṛti jam anāgateṣu saṅkalpajam iti

[II,218,12]	anye api guṇāḥ kāma ādayaḥ santi te ca kim na sucitāḥ iti ca udyasya parihāra artham antarbhāvam nirūpayati kāmaḥ abhilāṣaḥ rāgaḥ saṅkalpaḥ kāruṇyam vairāgyam upadhā bhāvaḥ iti evamādayaḥ icchā bhedāḥ tad viśeṣāḥ iti maithuna icchā kāmaḥ tad sadbhāve kāmī iti vyapadeśāt na icchā mātram iti abhyavaharaṇa icchāḥ abhilāṣaḥ abhilāṣa lakṣaṇa icchā sāmānyena sarvasmin vastuni abhyavaharaṇam ādānam vivakṣitam tad icchā abhilāṣaḥ iti ca anye punar punar viṣaya anurañjana icchā rāgaḥ tena hi satā rāgī iti vyapadeśāt anāsanna kriyāyām anāgata kriyāyām icchā saṅkalpaḥ sva artham anapekṣya para duḥkha prahāṇa icchā tad vināśa icchā kāruṇyam doṣa darśanāt viṣayeṣu parityāga icchā vairāgyam tad sadbhāve virakta vyavahārāt para vañcana icchā upadhā antar nigūḍha icchā bhāvaḥ iti yadi api icchā sarvāḥ antar na bāhya iti tathā api iyam anya apekṣayā kathañcid vijñāyate iti antar nigūḍhā iti ucyate cikīrṣā aji hīrṣā iti ādi kriyā bhedāt icchā bhedāḥ bhavanti kartum icchā cikīrṣā hartum icchā jihīrṣa iti 
[II,218,27_II,219,4]	dveṣa nirūpaṇa artham āha prajvalana ātmakaḥ prajvalana svarūpaḥ dveṣaḥ yasmin sati prajvalitam iva ātmānam manyate sa dveṣaḥ iti pūrvasya vivaraṇam sa ca ātmanasoḥ saṃyogāt asamavāyi kāraṇāt duḥkha apekṣāt smṛti apekṣāt vā ātmani utpadyate iti prayatna smṛti dharma adharma hetuḥ iti kārya nirūpaṇam yathā hi dveṣāt vadha ādau pravartamānasya adharmaḥ bhavati evam yajana ādau pravartamānasya dharmaḥ api iti bheda nirūpaṇa artham āha drohaḥ krodhaḥ manyuḥ akṣamāḥ amarṣaḥ iti dveṣa bhedāḥ tad viśeṣāḥ iti svāminaḥ apakāraḥ drohaḥ krodhaḥ tu yasmin utpanne śarīra indriya avayavānām vikāraḥ sampadyate manyuḥ apakṛtasya apakartum asamarthasya kaṇṭha akṣa vikāra janakaḥ akṣamā asahiṣṇu tā amarṣaḥ apakartuḥ varṣa ādi vya vadhānena api apakaraṇam

[II,220,8_II,220,14^1]	atha prayatnasya kāraṇa svarūpa vibhāga nirūpaṇa artham āha prayatnaḥ sa rambhaḥ utsāhaḥ iti paryāyāḥ lakṣaṇam asādhāraṇa tvāt tathā hi prayatnaḥ itarasmāt bhidyate anādi kāla pravāha āyāta ittham bhūta paryāya abhidheya tvāt yaḥ tu na bhidyate na ca asau evam yathā rūpa ādiḥ iti sa dvividhaḥ kāraṇa bhedāt iti āha jīvana pūrvakaḥ icchā dveṣa pūrvakaḥ ca jīvanam pūrvam kāraṇam asya iti jīvana pūrvakaḥ sa katham vijñāyate iti āha suptasya prāṇa apāna santāna prerakaḥ iti yā iyam suptasya prāṇa apāna santāna kriyā sā prayatna kāryā śarīra kriyā tvāt 
[II,220,14^2]	jāgrat avasthāyām prāṇa kriyā ādi vat iti na param prāṇa ādi santāna prerakaḥ prabodha kāle ca antaḥkaraṇasya indriya antareṇa prāpti hetuḥ iti yathā hi prabodha samaye yena eva indriyeṇa upalambhaḥ tena eva sambandha artham antaḥkaraṇasya nirindriya ātma apradeśe vartamānasya avaśyam karma abhyupeyam tat ca prayatna kāryam parigṛhīta antaḥkaraṇa karma tvāt jāgrat avasthāyām tat karma vat atas eva na adṛṣṭasya eva atra kāraṇa tvam anumānena prayatna kārya tva upalabdheḥ kāraṇa antara asambhave ca adṛṣṭasya eva nimitta kāraṇa tvam iṣyate iti 
[II,221,1]	sthite hi sadbhāve jīvana pūrvakasya utpatti kāraṇam āha ātma manasoḥ saṃyogāt asamavāyi kāraṇāt viśiṣṭa dharma adharma apekṣāt utpattiḥ iti itaraḥ tu icchā dveṣa pūrvakaḥ hita ahita prāpti parihāra samarthasya vyāpārasya kāyika vyāpārasya hetuḥ tathā śarīra vidhārakaḥ ca tena hi pratibaddham śarīre guru tvam na patanam ārabhate tasya utpatti kāraṇam āha ātma manasoḥ saṃyogāt asamavāyi kāraṇāt icchā pekṣāt dveṣa apekṣāt vā utpadyate iti 
[II,221,8_II,221,11]	guru tvasya lakṣaṇa parīkṣā artham guru tvam jala bhūmyoḥ ityādi prakaraṇam apratyakṣa tve sati patana karma kāraṇa tvāt guru tvam itarasmāt bhidyate vegaḥ api patana karma kāraṇam iti apratyakṣa grahaṇam jala bhūmyoḥ iti āśraya nirūpaṇam itara pada apekṣam vā lakṣaṇam jala bhūmyoḥ eva vartamāna tve sati patana karma kāraṇa tvāt guru tvam rasaḥ api jala bhūmyoḥ eva vartate na tu patana kāraṇam abhyupagame ca kāraṇa atiśayena kārya atiśayasya anyatra upalabdheḥ pāṣāṇa āde rasa atiśaya abhāvena pāta atiśaya abhāvaḥ pippalyādau ca tad sadbhāvena sadbhāvaḥ syāt sa na asti iti na rasaḥ kāraṇam patana utpattau rūpa ādeḥ ca kāraṇa tve anala ādau api sadbhāvāt pātaḥ syāt na ca asti iti atas rūpa ādi vyatiriktam kāraṇam anumīyate iti atas āha patana karma anumeyam iti ādyasya hi patana karmaṇaḥ asamavāyi kāraṇam guru tvam dvitīya ādeḥ tu saṃskāraḥ api iti sa ca asau jala bhūmyoḥ eva vartate 
[II,221,22]	nanu tvac indriyasya vyāpārāt pañca palam daśa palam iti pratibhāsanāt guru tvam pratyakṣam na tvac indriyeṇa sambandha upapatteḥ pṛthivī ādi guru tvasya api pratyakṣatā prasaṅgāt atha ādheya gatam eva guru tvam paricchinatti tvac indriyam na ca tat pṛthvī ādi guru tve asti iti nanu evam api makṣikā ādi guru tvam paricchindyāt tasya api ādheya gata tvāt iti na ca tasya aviśiṣṭa tvāt aparicchedaḥ pratyakṣa dravya samavāyasya aviśeṣāt atha adhas gati hetu tvam vaiśiṣṭyam tarhi tvac indriya sambandhena adhas gati viśeṣam upalabhamānasya pañca palam daśa palam iti ānumānikaḥ eva pratyayaḥ 
[II,222,5]	atha daśa palaiḥ tantubhiḥ ārabdhe paṭe guru tva atiśayasya anupalabdheḥ kāraṇaḥ eva guru tvam na tu kārye tat asat ubhayatra api pāta upalabdheḥ na ca sva gata guru tva abhāve api āśraya antara guru tvāt eva patanam vāyu ādeḥ api pāta prasaṅgāt tasmāt ubhayatra api kāryeṇa sadbhāva siddheḥ guru tvam asti iti avanati viśeṣa anupalambhaḥ ca kārye makṣikā ādi guru tva samparkeṇa api samānaḥ iti tathā hi tantuṣu mīyamāneṣu makṣikā ādi samparke api avanati viśeṣāḥ na upalabhyante na ca tad guru tvasya asattvam iti alam 
[II,222,12]	atha guru tvasya pāta hetu tve kim iti sarvadā pātaḥ na bhavati pratibandhāt iti āha saṃyoga prayatna saṃskāra virodhi iti vṛnta phala saṃyogena pratibaddham na phale patanam ārabhate prayatna pratibandhāt ākāśa avasthiteṣu śakuniṣu guru tvam na patanam karoti dhanuḥ nikṣipteṣu śareṣu guru tvam na patanam karoti vega ākhya saṃskāra pratibandhāt eṣām apāye phala ādiṣu pāta darśanāt 
[II,222,17]	tasya ca ābādi paramāṇu rūpa ādi vat nitya anitya tva niṣpattayaḥ iti ap ādayaḥ ca te paramāṇavaḥ ca iti tathā uktāḥ tad paramāṇu rūpa ādīnām iva iti yathā āpya paramāṇu rūpa ādīnām aniṣpadyamāna tvāt nitya tvam evam eva guru tvam nityeṣu aniṣpatteḥ nityam anitye tu kāraṇa guṇa pūrva prakrameṇa niṣpadyamāna tvāt tad rūpavat eva anityam iti atideśa arthaḥ 
[II,222,23_II,223,10]	drava tvasya lakṣaṇa parīkṣā artham āha drava tvam syandana karma kāraṇam iti syandana karma vakṣyamāṇam tad kāraṇam drava tvam iti ukte vegena vyabhicāraḥ tad artham tri dravya vṛtti iti tathā api tri dravya vṛtti tvam vegasya api sambhavati iti niyamena iti pada m ūhyam rūpantu niyamena tri dravya vṛtti na tu syandanakam akāraṇam atas drava tvam itarasmāt bhidyate niyamena tri dravya vṛtti tve sati syandana karma kāraṇa tvāt iti 
[II,223,15]	tat tu dvividham iti vibhāgaḥ kena rūpeṇa sāṃsiddhikam naimittikañca iti tayoḥ parasparam vailakṣaṇya nirūpaṇa artham āha sāṃsiddhikam apām viśeṣa guṇaḥ naimittikam pṛthivī tejasoḥ sāmānya guṇaḥ iti paraspara bhedaḥ sāṃsiddhikasya guru tva vat nitya anitya tva niṣpattayaḥ iti yathā guru tvam nityeṣu aniṣpadyamāna tvāt nityam anityeṣu niṣpatteḥ anityam kāraṇa guṇa pūrvakam āśraya vināśāt ca vinaśyati evam sāṃsiddhika drava tvam api iti atideśa arthaḥ 
[II,223,21]	nanu ca ayuktam etat apām sāṃsiddhika drava tvam iti himakaraka ādau anupalambhāt tat āha saṅghāta darśanāt sāṃsiddhika tvam ayuktam iti ced na etat evam anyatra salile sāṃsiddhika drava tvasya upalabdheḥ āpya paramāṇuṣu tad sadbhāva siddhau himakaraka ādau tasya anutpādāt pratibandhakam asti iti niścīyate tat ca anyasya anupalambhāt divya tejaḥ saṃyogaḥ eva iti āha divya tejaḥ saṃyuktānām āpyānām paramāṇūnām parasparam saṃyogaḥ dravya ārambhakaḥ sa ca saṅghāta ākhyaḥ tena paramāṇu drava tvasya pratibandhāt kārye himakaraka ādau drava tva anutpattiḥ iti tejaḥ sadbhāvaḥ tu sphoṭa ādi kārya anumeyaḥ tathā ca himakaraka asambandhāt upalabhyate sphoṭa ādi lakṣaṇam kāryam śarīre vṛkṣa ādau ca dāhaḥ iti vilayanañcā asya divya tejaḥ sambandhāt avayave kriyā tatas vibhāgaḥ tasmāt saṃyoga nivṛttau dravya vināśe sati paramāṇavaḥ kāryam ārabhante tatra ca divya tejaḥ saṃyogasya pratibandhakasya nivṛtteḥ paramāṇu drava tvam kārye drava tvam ārabhate 
[II,224,6_II,224,9^1]	na ca idam naimittikam sarpiḥ ādau iva punar saṃgraha anupalabdheḥ yathā hi naimittika drava tvam sarpiḥ ādau iti drutasya saṃgrahaḥ tathā iha api syāt na ca etat asti iti naimitti kañca pṛthivī tejasoḥ agni saṃyoga jam katham iti avyutpanna praśnaḥ tatra āha sarpiḥ ādīnām kāraṇeṣu ityādi padena sūtra uktānām saṃgrahaḥ tathā hi sa pirjatu madhūcchiṣṭānām pārthivānām agni saṃyogāt drava tvam adbhiḥ sāmānyam trapu sīsa loha rajata suvarṇānām taijasānām agni saṃyogāt drava tvam adbhiḥ sāmānyam iti atas sa pira ādi kāraṇeṣu ca paramāṇuṣu agni saṃyoga apekṣāt vega apekṣāt karma utpattau satyantataḥ vibhāgāḥ jāyante tebhyaḥ vibhāgebhyaḥ dravya ārambhaka saṃyoga vināśaḥ tatas kārya dravya nivṛttiḥ tasya añca satyām agni saṃyogāt auṣṇya apekṣāt svatantreṣu paramāṇuṣu drava tvam utpadyate paramāṇavaḥ samavāyi kāraṇam 
[II,224,9^2]	agni saṃyogaḥ asamavāyi kāraṇam uṣṇa sparśaḥ nimitta kāraṇam iti tatas anantaram utpanna drava tveṣu bhoginām adṛṣṭa apekṣāt ātma aṇu saṃyogāt karma utpadyate iti paramāṇuḥ samavāyi kāraṇam ātma aṇu saṃyogaḥ asamavāyi kāraṇam bhoginām adṛṣṭaḥ nimitta kāraṇam iti tatas vibhāgebhyaḥ prāktana saṃyoga vināśe sati tebhyaḥ karmabhyaḥ paramāṇu antareṇa saṃyogāḥ jāyante tebhyaḥ saṃyogebhyaḥ dvi aṇukāṇi utpadyante tad ādi krameṇa tri aṇuka ādi kāryam utpadyate tasmin ca dvi aṇuka ādau rūpa ādi utpatti sama kālam kāraṇa guṇa pūrva krameṇa drava tvam utpadyate iti pākaja utpatti nyāyaḥ atra draṣṭavyaḥ etāvān tu viśeṣaḥ tatra avaśyam rūpa ādi nivṛttiḥ na ca evam drava tvasya iti 
[II,224,27_II,225,4]	snehasya lakṣaṇa parīkṣā artham snehaḥ apām viśeṣa guṇaḥ saṅgrahamṛja ādi hetuḥ iti apām viśeṣa guṇaḥ rūpa ādiḥ api iti saṅgrahamṛja ādi hetuḥ iti padam saṅgrahaḥ piṇḍīkaraṇam mṛjā tu viśada tvam tad hetu tvāditarasmāt bhidyate nanu snehasya abhinava pallava ādau upalambhāt udaka viśeṣa guṇa tvam asiddham na saṃyukta samavāyena upalambhāt saṃyuktam hi pallava ādinā udakam tad samavetasnehaḥ gṛhyate tad apāye tasya anupalabdheḥ tathā snāna uttara kālam keśa ādau snigdha pratyaya darśanāt yathā ca saṃyogi āśraya vaiguṇya abhāve sarvasmin udake snigdha jñānam na evam sarvasyām pṛthivyām iti asya api guru tva vat nitya anitya tva niṣpattayaḥ iti nityeṣu nityaḥ anityeṣu kāraṇa guṇa pūrvaḥ āśraya vināśāt vinaśyati iti 
[II,225,11_II,225,15]	saṃskāra nirūpaṇa artham āha saṃskāraḥ trividhaḥ kena rūpeṇa vegaḥ bhāvanā sthiti sthāpaka tvena iti vibhāgaḥ eva asādhāraṇa tvāt lakṣaṇam iti tad lakṣaṇa vaicitrya jñāpana artham etat tatra vegasya samāna jātīyāt bhedam āśrayañca nirūpayan āha mūrtimatsu ityādi mūrtimatsu dravyeṣu na jñāyate kiyatsu tad artham pañcasu tathā api na jñāyate keṣu tad artham mūrtimatsu iti āśraya nirūpaṇam yat vā saṃskāra tve sati pañcasu mūrtimatsu eva vartamāna tvāt vegaḥ iti lakṣaṇam 
[II,225,21]	kāraṇam āha nimitta viśeṣa apekṣāt karmaṇaḥ jāyate iti saṃyoga vibhāgayoḥ karma ja tvam iti nimitta viśeṣa apekṣāt iti viśeṣaṇam nimitta viśeṣaḥ nodana abhighāta saṃyukta saṃyogāḥ tad apekṣāt iti karma asamavāyi kāraṇam sva kāraṇa viṣeṣaḥ nodana ādiḥ nimitta kāraṇam vega ādhāraḥ tu samavāyi kāraṇam iti asādhāraṇa tvāt lakṣaṇam ca idam kāryam āha niyatāyām diśi kriyā prabandhasya kriyā santānasya hetuḥ iti 
[II,225,27]	nanu ca ayuktam etat aniyata diś deśasya bhramaṇa ākhyasya api karmaṇaḥ kāraṇa tvāt satyam etat tathā api adoṣaḥ niyata dikkriyā prabandhasya eva hetuḥ iti avadhāraṇa anabhyupagamāt saḥ api niyatāyām eva diśi kriyā prabandhaḥ iti ca anye aniyata dikkriyā prabandha hetuḥ iti avadhāraṇasya atra pūrva rūpa tām manyamānā vyākhyā antaram kurvate tasya vināśa kāraṇam āha sparśavat dravya saṃyoga viśeṣa virodhī iti sparśavat dravya saṃyoga mātra virodhi tve vāyu saṃyogena virodha ādiṣoḥ gamanam na syāt tad hetoḥ vegasya vināśāt iti viśeṣa grahaṇam kaṭhina avayava saṃyogena ādau api tad vināśa upalabdheḥ 
[II,226,8]	nanu evam api ākāśe prakṣiptasya īṣoḥ nibiḍa avayava saṃyogasya vega vināśakasya abhāvāt apātaḥ syāt na aneka kārya karaṇe sparśavat dravya saṃyoga mātreṇa api vināśasya anvaya vyatirekābhyām upalambhāt tathā ca kṣiptasya iṣoḥ vega vināśa upalabdheḥ avaśyam kāraṇam abhidheyam nirhetuka vināśa pratiṣedhāt atas vāyu saṃyogena api aneka kārya karaṇe sati virudhyate adṛṣṭa prakṣayāt vā iti kvacid kāraṇa guṇa pūrva prakrameṇa utpadyate yathā parvata srotasām adhas patatām saṃyoge sati ekasmin udake samutpanne rūpa ādi vat kāraṇa vegāt vegaḥ api iti 
[II,226,15_II,226,24]	bhāvanā saṃjñakaḥ tu ātma guṇa tvāt itarasmāt bhidyate na ca buddhi ādibhiḥ vyabhicāraḥ saṃskārasya sataḥ avāntara viśeṣa nirūpaṇāt smṛti pratyabhijñāna hetuḥ iti kārya nirūpaṇam sadbhāve pramāṇañca iti smṛtiḥ vāsanā ākhyāt bhavati tathā uktam ātma adhikāre keṣu smṛti pratyabhijñāna hetuḥ iti āha dṛṣṭa śruta anubhūteṣu iti nirṇīta artheṣu iti bhāvaḥ 
[II,227,3]	nāśa kāraṇam āha jñāna mada duḥkha ādi virodhī iti jñānam pratipakṣa jñānam vivakṣitam tena virudhyate yathā ātma ādi jñāna janitaḥ saṃskāraḥ nairātmya ādi abhyāsena iti tasmin sati tatra asmaraṇāt sva madena virodhaḥ bāla avasthā anubhava janita saṃskārasya punar yuvā avasthāyām viṣaya abhibhūtasya tatra asmaraṇāt duḥkhena yathā śāstra anubhava janita saṃskārasya tīvreṇa dāra ādi duḥkhena iti tena satā tatra asmaraṇāt ādi padena tu krodha ādeḥ api saṃskāra nivartaka tvam uktam 
[II,227,9^1]	tasya utpatti kāraṇam āha paṭu abhyāsa ādara pratyayebhyaḥ jātaḥ tad pratyaya jaḥ iti paṭu pratyaya apekṣāt ātma manasoḥ saṃyogāt asamavāyi kāraṇāt ātmani āścarye arthe paṭuḥ saṃskāraḥ jāyate yathā dākṣiṇāti asya uṣṭra darśanāt sa ca atiśayena smṛti hetuḥ bhavati iti vidyā śilpa vyāyāma ādiṣu abhyasyamānaṣu tasmin eva arthe pūrva pūrva saṃskāram apekṣamāṇāt uttara uttarasmāt pratyayāt ātma manasoḥ saṃyogāt saṃskāra atiśayaḥ jāyate pūrva pūrva saṃskāra apekṣaḥ hi uttarottara pratyayaḥ abhyāsaḥ tam apekṣamāṇāt ātma manasoḥ saṃyogāt asamavāyi kāraṇāt ātmani saṃskāra atiśayaḥ jāyate tatra vidyāyām upādhyāya uccarita pada śravaṇe sati saṃskāraḥ punar vivakṣā ādi krameṇa svayam uccāraṇe sati tu jñānam pūrva saṃskāra apekṣam saṃskāra antaram ārabhate punar tad uccāraṇe sati tat jñānam pūrva saṃskāpa īkṣam saṃskāra antaram ārabhate iti evam tri catur ādi parivartane satyanti apada anubhavāt saṃskāra apekṣāt saṃskāra atiśayaḥ jāyate etat ca avaśyam abhyupeyam 
[II,227,9^2]	anyathā abhyāsa vaiyarthyam syāt na ca atiprasaṅgaḥ adṛṣṭasya vyavasthā hetu tvāt na ca tasya asti sarvatra sadbhāvaḥ kāryasya smaraṇasya sarvatra anupalabdheḥ yatra hi smaraṇam asti tatra eva pūrva saṃskāra apekṣam jñānam saṃskāram ārabhate iti āntare ca abhyāse pūrva pūrva saṃskāra apekṣam niyata artha smaraṇam eva saṃskāram ārabhate iti cintyam evam śilpe api upādhyāya likhita citra darśanāt saṃskāraḥ punar svayam sampādya upalabhate tad anubhavaḥ pūrva saṃskāra apekṣaḥ saṃskāra antaram ārabhate punar svayam likhitvā upalabhate tad anubhavaḥ pūrva saṃskāra apekṣaḥ saṃskāra antaram ārabhate iti evam dvi tri ādi parivartanena saṃskāra atiśayaḥ vyāyāme api upādhyāyena dhanurveda paripaṭhita nyāyena prayukteṣu upalambhāt upajāte saṃskāre punar tad anusāritayā svayam prayukte tad anubhavena pūrva saṃskāra apekṣeṇa saṃskāra antaram ārabhyate punar tathā eva prayoge sati tad anubhavena pūrva saṃskāra apekṣeṇa anyaḥ saṃskāraḥ iti evam antya anubhavāt saṃskāra atiśayaḥ iti 
[II,228,6]	ādara pratyaya ja saṃskāram āha prayatnena manaḥ cakṣuṣi sthāpayitvā apūrvam artham didṛkṣamāṇasya iti draṣṭum icchataḥ vidyut sampāta darśanena tulyam vartate iti tad darśana vat ādara pratyayaḥ tam apekṣamāṇāt ātma manasoḥ saṃyogāt asamavāyi kāraṇāt ātmani saṃskāra atiśayaḥ jāyate yathā devahrade sauvarṇa rājata padma darśanāt iti tatra hi sauvarṇa rājata padmayoḥ utthānam āgamāt loka pravādataḥ vā samupalabhya punar viśiṣṭayā trā samaye prayatnena saṃskāra atiśayaḥ bhavati iti

[II,228,22_II,229,4]	sadbhāve pramāṇam āha sthāvarāḥ ca jaṅgamāḥ ca iti tathā uktāḥ teṣām vikāreṣu dhanuḥ śākhā danta śṛṅga asthiṣu sūtra vastra ādiṣu ca bhugneṣu saṃvartiteṣu piṇḍīkṛteṣu tasya kāryam saṃlakṣyate tathā hi dhanuṣi śākhā ādī ca ākarṣaṇa karmaṇi upajāte nodana ādibhyaḥ tad nivṛttau api karma upalambhāt avaśyam asamavāyi kāraṇam vācyam vastunaḥ tad antareṇa anutpatteḥ na ca nodana ādeḥ anyatamaḥ sambhāvyate iti anyena asamavāyi kāraṇena bhavitavyam kriyā vibhāgayoḥ ca kriyā utpattau akāraṇa tva upalambhāt tathā tad nivṛttau api pratibandhaka abhāve sati śākhā ādau pūrva avasthā avasthāpaka karma upalambhāt nimitta antaram eva nyāyyam adṛṣṭa viśeṣasya tu sādhāraṇa tvāt kāraṇa tvam na pratiṣiddhyate iti nitya anitya tva niṣpattayaḥ api asya guru tva vat draṣṭavyāḥ iti yathā hi guru tvam nityeṣu nityam utpatti vināśa kāraṇa abhāvāt anityeṣu kāraṇa pūrvakam āśraya vināśāt vinaśyati evam sthiti sthāpaka saṃskāraḥ api iti kārye tu sthiti sthāpaka saṃskāra prasiddheḥ tad ārambhaka paramāṇuṣu api tad kalpanā kriyate

[II,235,7_II,235,25]	tpādakāni ) na param dharmaḥ adharma upya ātma guṇaḥ kartuḥ ahita pratyavāya hetuḥ atīndriyaḥ antya duḥkha saṃvijñāna virodhī iti atīndriya tve satyanti aduḥkha saṃvijñāna virodhi tvāt adharmaḥ itarasmāt bhidyate śeṣam pūrvavat tasya sādhanāni śāstre vipratiṣiddhāni dharma sādhana viparītāni hiṃsā anṛta steya ādīni hiṃsā prāṇi vadhaḥ anṛtam asatyam steyam cauryam ādipadena anyeṣām api dharma sādhana viparītānām avarodhaḥ avaṣya kartavyasya saṃdhyā vandana ādeḥ akaraṇam vihita kāla atikrameṇa api ananuṣṭhānam pramādaḥ ca ālasyam etāni nimittāni duṣṭa abhisandhim duṣṭa abhiprāyam ca apekṣyātma manaḥ saṃyogāt asamavāyi kāraṇāt ātmani adharma utpādakāni iti khedañca utpādya rāga ādi nivṛttau nivṛtti lakṣaṇaḥ kevalaḥ dharmaḥ parama artha darśana jam sukham kṛtvā nivartate tadā nirodhāt nirbījasya ātmanaḥ śārīra ādi nivṛttiḥ punar śarīra ādi anutpattau dagdha indhana anala vat upaśamaḥ mokṣaḥ iti )

[II,236,14^1]	pravartakāt dharmāt saṃsāra utpattim upadiśya nivartakāt tat nivṛttim āha jñāna pūrvakāt tu kṛtāt iti jñānam pūrvam yasya sa tathā uktaḥ tasmāt kim rūpāt asaṅkalpita phalāt iti ittham me śarīra indriya viṣayāḥ sampadyantām na ittham iti evam na saṅkalpitam phalam yasya sa tathā uktaḥ tasmāt viśuddhe kule janma bhavati tasya jātasya duḥkha vigama upāya jijñāsā sampadyate kutas sādhanāt atyantam duḥkha santateḥ viyogaḥ sampadyate iti evam jijñāsoḥ ācārya upasaṅgamaḥ sampadyate tañca upasaṅgamya duḥkha santāna vyāvṛtteḥ upāyam vijānāti tattva jñānāt śreyaḥ sampadyate iti tatas śāstra abhyāsāt ṣaṭpadārtha tattva jñānam utpadyate tasya ca utpanna ṣaṭpadārtha jñānasya ajñāna nivṛttiḥ bhavati tad nivṛttau virāgaḥ kāraṇa abhāvena kāryasya anutpatteḥ viraktasya rāga dveṣa abhāvāt tābhyām jāyate yau dharma adharmau tau tad jau

[II,239,22_II,240,1^1]	atha śabdasya upalambha anantaram anupalabdhiḥ vyañjaka abhāvāt na asattvāt iti ced na sadbhāve pramāṇa abhāvāt āvaraṇa ādeḥ anupalambhāt ca nahi aindriyakasya atīndriyam āvaraṇam pramāṇena kvacid upalabdham abhyupagame api kvacid śabdasya abhivyaktau tasya vyāpaka tayā sarva deśa avasthita puruṣāṇām upalambhaḥ syāt nirāvaraṇasya vyāpaka tva aviśeṣāt yadi ca śabda ātmakā niyata artha pratipādakāḥ ca eka deśāḥ saṃjñā bheda mātram eva atha bherī daṇḍa saṃyogāt vega apekṣāt utpanna kriyaḥ vāyuḥ vegavān śrotra deśena āgatya abhisambadhyate tad gatāni tu stimita vāyu antarāṇi protsārayati tatas pratibandhaka abhāve sati śrotram śabdasya grāhakam iti 
[II,240,1^2]	nanu evam api aśeṣa śabda upalambha prasaṅgaḥ saṃskṛte hi śrotre sarveṣām sānnidhyam na ca go śabda abhivyakti artham preritaḥ vāyuḥ na aśva śabdam vyanakti iti vācyam vyañjakeṣu niyama anupalabdheḥ yathā ghaṭa abhivyakti artham utpāditaḥ pradīpaḥ samāna indriya grāhya samāna deśa avasthita padārtha abhivyañjakaḥ iti tathā hi na śrotram pratiniyata saṃskāraka saṃskāryam samāna indriya grāhya samāna deśa avasthita vastu prakāśaka tvāt cakṣuḥ vat pradīpa avaṣṭabdha deśa vyatireka tā jñānam pradīpa saṃskṛtam na cakṣuṣā grahaṇam iti samāna deśa avasthita padam evaṃvidhāḥ ca rūpa rasa ādayaḥ na gṛhyante iti samāna indriya grāhya grahaṇam śabdāḥ vā vivāda viṣayāḥ pratiniyata vyañjaka vyaṅgyāḥ na bhavanti 
[II,240,1^3]	samāna indriya grāhya samāna deśa avasthita tvāt ghaṭa ādi vat atra ca ye pratiniyata saṃskāraka saṃskāryāḥ na bhavanti cakṣuḥ ghaṭa ādayaḥ te sa pakṣāḥ tatra hetoḥ sadbhāvaḥ tad viparītāḥ tu vipakṣāḥ tasmāt atyantam vyāvṛttiḥ iti pradīpena ca saṃskṛtam cakṣuḥ yugapad ghaṭa ādi prakāśakam iti dṛṣṭam evam śrotram api aśeṣa śabda upalambhakam syāt atra ca apekṣā buddhi vat aneka padārtha ālambanam eva ekam jñānam āśu bhāvena vā yugapad śabda prayogaḥ iti nanu ekasyām api pṛthivyām śukla ādi bhedānām saṃskṛtena api cakṣuṣā na yugapad prakāśanam evam ghrāṇa ādinā gandha ādeḥ iti evam api na hetoḥ vyabhicāraḥ sa pakṣa eka deśa vṛtteḥ api gamaka tvāt 
[II,240,20^1]	atha yathā cakṣuḥ samāna indriya grāhya samāna deśa avasthitānām api śukla ādi bhedānām na yugapad prakāśakam evam śrotram api syāt iṣṭañca pṛthivyām aneka rūpa adhikaraṇa tvam api citra rūpa samarthana avasare satyam etat tathā api rūpa bhedānām agrahaṇam saha kārya bhāvāt tathā ca nānā rūpa avayava upalambha sahakāri indriyam avayavini aneka rūpa grāhakam iti uktam tad sadbhāve vicitra pratibhāsanāt na ca evam śrotrasya vāyunā saṃskṛtasya sarva śabdānām tatra sānnidhyāt agrahaṇe kāraṇam asti iti sāmānyāni tu pratiniyata vyañjaka vyaṅgyāni 
[II,240,20^2]	na tu samāna deśāni sva viṣaya sarva gata tvāt eva iti vyabhicāra abhāvaḥ tathā ātapa samparkāt taiile gandha abhivyaktiḥ grīṣma avasāne tu dagdha sthalīṣu prathama jala dhara dhārā samparkāt na ca samāna deśa tvam yat vā jaladhara dhārā samparkāt bhū gata anila udbhave satya vayava kriyā krameṇa pūrva dravya nivṛttau utpanna pākaiḥ dvi aṇuka ādi prakrameṇa dravya antara utpāde sati gandhaḥ abhivyajyate iti yat ca abhivyajyate sāmānya rūpa ādi tat āśraya stham eva iti dṛṣṭam evam śabde api syāt tat tu na asti iti vyakti dharmaka tva abhāvaḥ

[II,241,26_II,242,3]	tat evam anitya tve vyavasthite vināśa kāraṇam āha kārya kāraṇa ubhaya virodhi iti ādyaḥ śabdaḥ kāryeṇa virudhyate antyaḥ tu kāraṇam viruṇaddhi madhya gatāḥ tu kāryeṇa virudhyante kāraṇañca virudhanti iti saṃyoga vibhāga śabda jaḥ iti utpatti kāraṇam saṃyogāt vibhāgāt śabdāt ca śabda niṣpattiḥ iti sa dvividhaḥ kena rūpeṇa varṇa lakṣaṇaḥ avarṇa lakṣaṇaḥ ca iti akārāt ihakāra paryantaḥ varṇa lakṣaṇaḥ śaṅkha ādi nimittam yasya asau tad nimittaḥ avarṇa lakṣaṇaḥ iti ādipadena anyeṣām api nimitta kāraṇānām avarodhaḥ 
[II,242,6]	tatra varṇa lakṣaṇasya utpattiḥ abhidhīyate ātma manasoḥ saṃyogāt asamavāyi kāraṇāt smṛti apekṣāt varṇa uccāraṇa icchā bhavati tad anantaram prayatnaḥ tam apekṣamāṇāt ātma vāyu saṃyogāt asamavāyi kāraṇāt vāyau samavāyi kāraṇe karma sa ca utpanna karmā vāyuḥ ūrdhvam gacchan kaṇṭha ādīn abhihanti iti ādipadena tālu oṣṭha ādeḥ grahaṇam tatas sthāna vāyu saṃyoga apekṣāt sthāna ākāśa saṃyogāt varṇa utpattiḥ iti ākāśam samavāyi kāraṇam sthāna ākāśa saṃyogaḥ asamavāyi kāraṇam sthāna vāyu saṃyogaḥ ca apekṣā kāraṇam iti 
[II,242,13]	avarṇa lakṣaṇaḥ api bherī ākāśa saṃyogāt utpadyate bherī daṇḍa saṃyogāyapekṣāt ityādi padena diś kāla ādeḥ grahaṇam atra api ākāśam samavāyi kāraṇam bherī ākāśa saṃyogaḥ asamavāyi kāraṇam bherī daṇḍa saṃyoga ādiḥ nimitta kāraṇam iti tathā veṇu parva vibhāga apekṣāt parva ākāśa vibhāgāt asamavāyi kāraṇāt ākāṣe śabdaḥ niṣpadyate iti 
[II,242,18]	śabda jam śabdam upadarśayati evam saṃyogāt vibhāgāt ca pariniṣpannaḥ śabdaḥ samantāt śabda antarāṇi ārabhate tasmāt api asamavāyi kāraṇāt sva kāraṇa pratyāsatti apekṣāt ākāśe anyaḥ śabdaḥ iti vīcī santāna vat śabda santānaḥ yathā hi mahataḥ pāṣāṇa ādi abhighātāt upajātā vīcī vīci antaram ārabhate sā api punar vīci antaram iti santānāḥ tadvat śabda santānaḥ iti evam santāna nyāyena śrotra deśam āgatasya grahaṇam 
[II,242,24_II,243,1]	etat ca kalpyate anyathā karṇa śaṣkulī a ākāśa saṃyoga upalakṣita nabhaḥ pradeśa vyatirekeṇa pradeśa antara samavāyāt teṣām avyāpya vṛtti tvena viśiṣṭa pratyāsatteḥ abhāvāt agrahaṇam eva syāt tat āha śrotra śabdayoḥ gamana asambhavāt santāna anabhyupagame na parasparam prāptiḥ prāptasya ca upalambhaḥ iti santānaḥ kalpyate nanu etasmin pakṣe śabdāḥ sva avaruddha nabhaḥ deśaḥ eva yadi śabda antaram ārabheran na kasya api upalambhaḥ syāt sarveṣām ekatra eva upakṣayāt atha pradeśa antare tarhi brahma bhāṣitasya api upalambhaḥ asmad ādi śrotra deśe śabda antara ārambhāt 
[II,243,4]	atha aṇu vivara mātre sva deśa anantaram ārabhate tarhi teṣām kṣaṇa śata ādi vya vadhānena grahaṇam syāt tat tu na dṛṣṭam kṣaṇa dvaya ādi vyavadhānena śravaṇāt yāḥ ādyaḥ śabdaḥ śabda antaram na ārabhate śabda tvāt antya śabda vat antya śabdaḥ vā śabda antaram ārabhate śabda tvāt ādya śabda vat atas santāna pratiṣedhe śabda upalambhāni atha anupapattyā vāyoḥ vyañjakasya āgamanam kalpyate iti manyante 
[II,243,9^1]	na ca etat yuktam vyakti pakṣasya pūrvam eva pratiṣedhāt vāyoḥ āgamane pramāṇa abhāvāt ca na ca śabda upalabdhiḥ eva pramāṇam santāna nyāyena api tad upapatteḥ yat ca atra dūṣaṇam upanyastam tad vīcī nidarśana upanyāsāt nirastam yathā hi mahataḥ pāṣāṇa abhighātāt upajātā vīcī sva deśa anantara deśaḥ eva vīci antaram ārabhate na taṭa ādau evam śabdaḥ api sva kāraṇa pratyāsattim apekṣya anantara deśaḥ eva śabda antaram ārabhate iti na ca kṣaṇa śata ādi vya vadhānena grahaṇa prasaṅgaḥ ṣaṇṇām eva śabdānām tīvra ādi bhedānām utpatteḥ tathā hi bherī daṇḍa abhighātāt upajāte śabde sannihitasya tīvratamaḥ śabdaḥ iti jñānam tad anantaram vyavahitasya ca tīvataraḥ śabdaḥ iti jñānam 
[II,243,9^2]	tatas tīvraḥ mandaḥ mandataraḥ mandatamaḥ ca iti ṣaṭ bhedāḥ krameṇa anubhūyante iti naḥ ānantya pakṣa uktaḥ doṣaḥ tathā hi bherī daṇḍa abhighātāt ekaḥ eva śabdaḥ kalpitam bhūyāṃsam pradeśam vyāpya upajāyate iti anekaiḥ api upalabhyate eva iti na sarvatra santānaḥ yat ca id am uktam na ādyaḥ śabdaḥ śabda antaram ārabhate śabda tvāt antya śabda vat iti tat na svatantra sādhanam svayam ādi anta śabda aprasiddheḥ na ca dṛṣṭānta dārṣṭa antika dharmiṇoḥ aprasiddhau hetoḥ pakṣa dharma tvam bahis vyāptiḥ vā sambhavati iti atha para vyāptyā parasya aniṣṭa āpādanam etat tat na yadi pramāṇa pūrvikā para vyāptiḥ tayā eva bādhyamāna tvāt viparīta anumānasya anutthānam atha apramāṇa pūrvikā 
[II,243,9^3]	tarhi prameya aprasiddheḥ āśraya asiddham sādhanam dharmya siddhaḥ ca dṛṣṭāntaḥ iti śabdasya śabda antara ārambha pratiṣedhe svayam ādi anta viśeṣaṇa aprasiddheḥ tasmāt vyakti pakṣa pratiṣedhe śabda upalambhāni atha anupapattyā santāna kalpanā kriyate iti na ca antya śabdasya ārambhaka tva parikalpanāyām pramāṇam asti sarvadā upalambha prasaṅagāt atas antya śabdasya sparśavat dravya saṃyoga eka artha samavāyena pralayaḥ sva jñānāt upabhoga prāpaka adṛṣṭa apakṣayād vā iti vināśasya pramāṇena upalabdheḥ tasya ca nirhetuka tva pratiṣedhāt ukta kāraṇāt eva vināśaḥ kalpyate iti alam 
[II,244,8_iti^1]	idānīm itara padārtha vaidharmyeṇa sva bheda vyāpakam utkṣepaṇa ādīnām sādharmyam tathā paraspara vyāvṛttam vaidharmyam kāraṇañca nirūpayan āha utkṣepaṇa ādīnām na param dvayoḥ trayāṇāñca kim tarhi pañcānām api karma tva sambandhaḥ karma tva upalakṣitaḥ samavāyaḥ tathā ca utkṣepaṇa ādīni itarasmāt bhiyante karmāṇi iti vā vyavahartavyāni karma tva abhisambandhāt iti eka dravyavat tvam iti ekañca tat dravyañca iti eka dravyam tat asya asti iti eka dravya vat tasya bhāvaḥ eka dravyavat tvam ekam karma ekasmin eva dravye vartate tathā ekam eva ekasmin iti kutas etata ekasmin calite sarveṣām calana anupalabdheḥ yatra api bahūnām eka kālam calanam tatra api aneka tvam eva 
[iti^2]	kāraṇasya abhighāta ādeḥ pratyāśrayam bhedāt anyatra ca samavetam abhighāta ādi anyatra samavāyi kāraṇam iti abhyupagame ca aśeṣa dravya āśritasya utpattiḥ aviśeṣāt tathā ekasmin dravye saṃyogāt vinaṣṭe karmaṇi āśraya antare api tasya ekatāyām vināśaḥ syāt ekasmin ca aneka karma abhyupagame viruddha diś abhimukha tāyām parasparam pratibandhāt agamanam eva syāt eka diś abhimukha tā yāñca ekena eva karmaṇā saṃyoga vibhāgayoḥ janita tvāt na dvitīyasya sadbhāve pramāṇam asti tad uttara saṃyogāt ca prāktana karma vināśaḥ karma antara utpattiḥ ca kvacid iṣi ate eva tasmāt yatra karma dvaya pratibhāsaḥ tatra āśu bhāvi tvena eva iti draṣṭavyam atha eka dravyavat tvam rūpa ādeḥ api iti kṣaṇika grahaṇam tathā api buddhi ādibhiḥ vyabhicāra parihāra artham mūrta dravya vṛtti tva padam 
[II,245,6]	atha kṣaṇika tve sati mūrta dravyeṣu eva vartamāna tvāt karma iti ukte vyabhicāra abhāvaḥ satyam tathā api pada antaram sādharmya mātra pratipādana artham parīkṣā arthañca iti guru tva drava tva prayatna saṃyogebhyaḥ jāyate iti guru tva drava tva prayatna saṃyoga jam tasya bhāvaḥ tattvam iti udāharaṇañca etat anyasmāt api kāraṇāt tad utpatteḥ vyaḥ tañca guru tva ādikam kāryantara sampādakam api na samuditam karma vyatirekeṇa anyasya iti asādhāraṇam eva na ca evam sakala karma bheda vyāpakam iti vaidharmya mātram eva yat vā guru tva ādi anyatama kāraṇa janya tvam vivakṣitam tathā sva kārya saṃyoga virodhi tvam iti saṃyoga mātreṇa vināśa adarśanāt iti sva kārya grahaṇam karma kārya tvañca vibhāga vegayoḥ api iti tatra vyabhicāra vāraṇāya saṃyoga grahaṇam atas sva kārya saṃyoga virodhi tvam asādhāraṇam api kvacid āśraya vināśena api vināśāt na pakṣa vyāpakam iti vaidharmya mātram eva tathā vibhāge saṃyoge api ca kartavye nirapekṣa kāraṇa tvam karmaṇaḥ svarūpam 
[II,245,19_II,245,23]	nanu vibhāge anapekṣa kāraṇa tvam iṣṭam saṃyoge tu paścāt bhāvinam prāktana saṃyoga vināśam apekṣate iti anapekṣa tvam asiddham vastu bhūta kāraṇa apekṣayā tad upapatteḥ abhāva vyatirekeṇa ca vastu bhūtam kāraṇam na apekṣate iti anapekṣam iti uktam na ca anyasya etat sambhavati iti asādhāraṇam asamavāyi kāraṇa tvam iti asādhāraṇam itarasmāt vyāvṛttam guṇānām hi dvaividhyam asamavāyi tvam nimitta tvañca utkṣepaṇa ādīnām ca asamavāyi kāraṇa tvam eva na dvaividhyam asti iti vipakṣāt atyantam vyāvṛttiḥ eva dvaividhya pratiṣedhasya vivakṣita tvāt tathā sva para āśraya samaveta kārya ārambhaka tvam yasmin āśraye samavetam karma tatra āśraya antare ca samavetam vibhāgam saṃyogam ca ārabhate iti samāna jātīya anārambhaka tvam tathā ca utpannam karma vibhāgam saṃyogam ca ārabhamāṇam upalabdham na karma antaram iti ekasmin dharmiṇi anekasya karmaṇaḥ pūrvam eva pratiṣedhāt dravya anārambhaka tvam na karma dravyam ārabhate tasya uttara saṃyogena vinaśyat avasthasya kāraṇa tva asambhavāt iti sva bheda vyāpakam sādharmyam pratiniyata jāti yogi tvam iti pratiniyata jātiḥ utkṣepaṇa tva ādikā tad yogi tvam pañcānām api diś viśiṣṭa kāri ārambhaka tvañca viśeṣaḥ parasparam iti 
[II,246,8_II,246,17]	tat eva āha tatra utkṣepaṇam yad ūrdhvam bhajantaḥ iti ūrdhva bhājaḥ taiḥ saṃyoga kāraṇam adhobhāgbhiḥ ca vibhāga kāraṇam karma utpadyate kebhyaḥ keṣu ca iti guru tva drava tva prayatna saṃyogebhyaḥ samasta vyastebhyaḥ tad utkṣepaṇam iti udāharaṇa artham vega ādeḥ api tat kāraṇa tvāt śarīra avayaveṣu hasta pāda ādiṣu tad sambaddheṣu musala ādiṣu iti āśraya nirūpaṇam 
[II,246,22_II,247,5]	tad viparīta saṃyoga vibhāga kāraṇam karma apakṣepaṇam iti ūrdhva bhāgbhiḥ vibhāga kāraṇam adhobhāgbhiḥ ca saṃyoga kāraṇam iti ākuñcanam ṛjunaḥ dravyasya ye agrāvayavāḥ teṣām tad deśaiḥ tad upalakṣita ākāśa ādi pradeśaiḥ vibhāgaḥ saṃyogaḥ ca mūla pradeśaiḥ iti tad upalakṣita ākāśa ādi pradeśaiḥ eva yena karmaṇā samutpannena avayavī kuṭilaḥ san ṛjuḥ sampadyate tat prasāraṇam iti yat aniyata diś deśa saṃyoga vibhāga kāraṇam tat gamanam iti ukta pradeśebhyaḥ anye aniyata diś pradeśāḥ taiḥ saṃyoga vibhāga kāraṇam iti 
[II,247,7_II,247,21^1]	upasaṃhāram āha iti etat pañcavidham api karma sat pratyayam asat pratyayañca iti pratyayaḥ kāraṇam tat ca sāmānya padena api sat iti viśeṣaṇāt prayatna ākhyam eva vivakṣitam pāramparyeṇa vā pratyaya kārya tvāt prayatnaḥ pratyayaḥ iti uktaḥ atas sat pratyayaḥ yasya tat tathā uktam karma prayatna pūrvakam iti yāvat asat pratyayam ayatna pūrvakam tat ca śarīra avayaveṣu tad sambaddheṣu bhavati iti etasmāt yat anyat tad apratyayam ayatna pūrvakam asmad ādi prayatnasya tatra avyāpārāt tat ca eteṣu anyeṣu ca dravyeṣu bhavati utkṣepaṇa ādi vilakṣaṇa tvāt gamanam eva iti karmaṇām jāti pañcatvam ayuktam kutas gamana aviśeṣāt gama nāt abhedāt iti ākṣepaḥ tat eva āha sarvam kṣaṇikam kṣaṇika tvam nāma sarva karmasu samānam iti na svarūpa bhedāt bhedaḥ calana mātram utpannam sva āśrayasya saṃyoga vibhāgān karoti kaiḥ saha 
[II,247,21^2]	ūrdhvam adhas tiryak paramāṇu vivara mātraiḥ pradeśaiḥ iti yāvati pradeśe paramāṇoḥ aṇu praveśaḥ sambhavati iti na kārya bhedāt api bhedaḥ sarvasya api etat kārya janaka tvāt tathā sarvatra ca gamana pratyayaḥ aviśiṣṭaḥ iti ūrdhvam gacchati agra pradeśāt ca mūlapradeśam gacchati mūlapradeśāt ca agra pradeśam gacchati iti tasmāt gamanam eva sarvam iti upasaṃhāraḥ na vargaśas pratyaya anuvṛtti vyāvṛtti darśanāt iti pratisamādhāna vākyam yat uktam sarvam gamanam iti etat na utkṣepaṇa ādi vargeṣu pratyaya anuvṛtti vyāvṛtti darśanāt tat eva āha iha utkṣepaṇam para tra apakṣepaṇam iti evamādi sarvatra vargaśas iti varge varge pratyaya anuvṛttiḥ vyāvṛttiḥ ca dṛṣṭā tathā hi utkṣepaṇam utkṣepaṇam iti utkṣepaṇa varge anuvartate 
[II,247,21^3]	apakṣepaṇa ādi vargāt ca vyāvartate tathā apakṣepaṇam sva varge anuvartate bheda antarāt ca vyāvartate iti tad hetuḥ anugata vyāvṛtta jñāna hetuḥ utkṣepaṇa tva ādi sāmānya viśeṣaḥ avagamyate iti na gamana tvam ekam eva sāmānyam utkṣepaṇa ādi bhedānām paraspara vyāvṛtta jāti sambandhinām sadbhāvāt udādi upasarga viśeṣāt teṣām paraspara viśeṣaḥ tathā hi utpūrvam kṣepaṇam utkṣepaṇam apapūrvam apakṣepaṇam āt pūrvam kuñcanam ākuñcanam prapūrvam sāraṇam prasāraṇam gamanam tu upasarga abhāvāt eva viśiṣyate pratiniyata diś viśiṣṭa kārya ārambha tvāt upalakṣaṇa bhedaḥ api utkṣepaṇa ādīnām siddhaḥ iti tathā ca ūrdhvam saṃyoga kāraṇam adhas ca vibhāga kāraṇam utkṣepaṇasya upalakṣaṇam iti evamādi uktam upalakṣaṇasya ca utkṣepaṇa tva ādeḥ bhedaḥ iti 
[II,248,15_II,249,4]	evam api pañca eva iti avadhāraṇa anupapattiḥ utkṣepaṇa ādibhyaḥ atiricyamāneṣu niṣkramaṇam praveśanam ityādiṣu vargaśas pratyaya anuvṛtti vyāvṛtti darśanāt sāmānya viśeṣa sadbhāve sati karmaṇām ānantyam aniṣṭam anuṣajyate atha kārya bhedāt niṣkramaṇa ādiṣu pratyaya anuvṛtti sadbhāvaḥ na sāmānya viśeṣa sadbhāvāt iti parāśayam āśaṅkya āha utkṣepaṇa ādiṣu api kārya bhedāt eva pratyaya anuvṛtti vyāvṛtti prasaṅgaḥ iti 
[II,249,10]	yathā bahis deśena saṃyoga karaṇāt antardeśena ca vibhāga jananāt niṣkramaṇam viparītañca praveśanam evam ūrdhva deśena saṃyoga jananāt adhas deśena vibhāga jananāt ca utkṣepaṇam ityādi bhaviṣyati iti atha utkṣepaṇa ādiṣu niṣkramaṇa ādiṣu ca samāne vargaśas pratyaya anuvṛtti vyāvṛtti sadbhāve sati utkṣepaṇa ādīnām eva jāti bhedaḥ na niṣkramaṇa ādīnām iti atra na viśeṣa hetuḥ asti iti 
[II,249,15^1]	etat na jāti saṅkara prasaṅgāt tat āha niṣkramaṇa ādīnām jāti bhedāt pratyaya anuvṛtti vyāvṛttau satyām jāti saṅkaraḥ viruddha jāti samāveśaḥ prasajyate sa ca anyatra anupalabdheḥ aniṣṭaḥ yadi api sattā dravya tva ādi para apara bheda bhinnam ekasyām vyaktau asti tathā api na go tva aśva tva ādi upalabdham atra ca ekasyām vyaktau niṣkramaṇa tva praveśana tva jāti prasaṅgaḥ katham iti āha dvayoḥ draṣṭroḥ ekasyām karma vyaktau yugapad niṣkramaṇa praveśana pratyayau dṛṣṭau iti kasya tat karma iti āha ekasmāt apavarakāt apavaraka antaram gacchataḥ puruṣasya iti tathā hi dvayoḥ apavarakayoḥ ekam eva dvāram iti ubhayatra vyavasthitayoḥ puruṣayoḥ anyasmin ca vrajati puruṣe viśiṣṭa saṃyoga vibhāga upalambhāt yugapad niṣkramaṇa praveśana pratyayau dṛṣṭau eva 
[II,249,15^2]	tathā ca dvāra pradeśe praviśati niṣkramati iti ca yaḥ hi draṣṭā svāpa varaka antar deśe vibhāgam bahis deśe ca saṃyogam upalabhate tasya niṣkramati iti pratyayaḥ bhavati yaḥ tu svāpa varaka antar deśe saṃyogam bahis deśe ca vibhāgam upalabhate tasya praveśana pratyayaḥ bhavati yadā tu pratisīra ādi javanikā ādi apanītam bhavati ityādi padena anyasya api kuḍya ādeḥ āvaraṇasya apanayanaḥ tadā viśiṣṭasya kārya bhedasya anupalabdheḥ na niṣkramaṇa pratyayaḥ na api praveśana pratyayaḥ kim tarhi 
[II,249,15^3_II,250,7]	gamana pratyayaḥ eva bhavati tasmāt etasyām gamana vyaktau viruddha jāti samāveśa prasaṅgāt kārya bhedāt eva pratyaya bhedaḥ iti uktam tathā nālikāyām vaṃśa patra ādau patati draṣṭṝṇām ūrdhva adhas tiryak vyavasthitānām yugapad bhramaṇa patana praveśana pratyayāḥ dṛṣṭāḥ iti jātīnām bhramaṇa tva ādīnām saṅkara prasaṅgaḥ iti sva pakṣe doṣa parihāra artham āha na ca evam utkṣepaṇa ādiṣu pratyaya saṅkaraḥ dṛṣṭaḥ yasya bhayāt viruddha jāti samāveśa prasaṅga parihāra artham kārya bhedena bhedaḥ abhyupagamyate iti upasaṃhāram āha tasmāt utkṣepaṇa ādīnām eva jāti bhedāt pratyaya anuvṛtti vyāvṛttī niṣkramaṇa ādīn āntu kārya bhedāt iti 
[II,250,11_II,250,20^1]	paramatamāśaṅkate katham yugapad pratyaya bhedaḥ iti ced iti asya tu vivaraṇam atha matam yathā jāti saṅkaraḥ na asti evam aneka karma saṅkaraḥ api ekasmin vastuni na asti iti uktam eva atas katham ekasmin karmaṇi kāraṇa abhāvāt yugapad draṣṭṝṇām bhramaṇa patana praveśana pratyayāḥ paraspara vyāvṛtta ātmānaḥ bhavanti kāraṇa abhāvena kāryasya anutpatteḥ iti atra brūmaḥ ityādi pratisamādhānam yat tvayā uktam kāraṇa abhāvena anutpattiḥ eva bhramaṇa ādi pratyayānām iti etat na avayava avayavinoḥ diś deśa saṃyoga vibhāga bhedāt tad upapatteḥ avayavaḥ ca avayavī ca iti avayava a ayavinau tayoḥ digdeśa viśiṣṭa saṃyoga vibhāgāḥ
