[II,250,20^2]	tad bhedāt iti tat eva āha yaḥ hi draṣṭā avayavānām pārśvatas paryāyeṇa diś pradeśaiḥ saṃyoga vibhāgān paśyati tasya bhramaṇa pratyayaḥ bhavati yaḥ tu avayavini ūrdhva pradeśāt vibhāgam adhas saṃyogañca avekṣate tasya patati patram iti patana pratyayaḥ bhavati yaḥ punar nālika antar deśe garta antar deśe saṃyogam bahis deśe ca vibhāgam paśyati tasya praviśati patram iti praveśana pratyayaḥ tasmāt siddhaḥ kārya bhedāt niṣkramaṇa ādīnām pratyaya bhedaḥ na jāti bhedāt iti 
[II,251,8_II,251,13]	anye tu bhramaṇa recana syandana ūrdhva jvalana ādi bhedena karmaṇā ām asaṅkhyāta tvāt niṣkramaṇa ādīnām jāti bhedāt pratyaya bheda siddhau na kiñcid bādhakam asti iti atas na idam sva matam iti na ca bhramaṇa recana ādīnām gamanaḥ eva antarbhāvaḥ iti manyante etat tu na yuktam tasya karma tva paryāya tvena vakṣyamāṇa tvāt jāti saṅkara prasaṅgasya ca bādhakasya dṛḍha tvāt iti 
[II,251,26]	bhavatu utkṣepaṇa ādīnām jāti bhedāt bhedaḥ na niṣkramaṇa ādīnām atha gamana tvam kim karma tva paryāyaḥ ghaṭaḥ kalaśaḥ iti paryāya vat āhosvit aparam sāmānyam utkṣepaṇa tva ādi vat iti cintyam kutas kāraṇāt te saṃśayaḥ iti ācāryasya praśnaḥ sa ca anupapannaḥ tathā hi sandigdhena praśne kṛte sati tad pratisamādhānam nyāyyam na tu saṃśaya karaṇena vacanam tasya sāmānya dharma ādibhyaḥ pūrvam eva utpatti nirūpaṇāt na eṣa doṣaḥ saṃśaya kāraṇa jñāne sati tad ucchittau upāya anuṣṭhānam upalabdha vyādhi kāraṇasya vaidyasya iva aprayāsena eva ghaṭataḥ iti manyamānaḥ kāraṇam praśnayati iti tat āha samasteṣu utkṣepaṇa ādiṣu bhramaṇa ādiṣu ca karma pratyaya vat gamana pratyaya aviśeṣāt karma tva paryāyaḥ iti gamyate yathā hi utkṣepaṇa karma apakṣepaṇa karma ityādi vyavahāra upalambhāt aśeṣa bheda vyāpakam karma tvam evam ūrdhvam gacchati adhas gacchati ityādi vyavahāra upalambhāt gamanam api aśeṣa bheda vyāpakam iti atas karma tva paryāyaḥ iti jñāyate 
[II,252,11^1]	na ca atra niścayaḥ eva iti āha yatas tu utkṣepaṇa ādi vat viśeṣa saṃjñayā abhihitam tasmāt aparam sāmānyam syāt iti na hi viśeṣa darśanena gaṇanāyām tad avasare sāmānya saṃjñā nirdeśaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ yathā pṛthivī ādi saṃjñā vasare dravya saṃjñāyāḥ tasmāt ubhaya rūpa dharma upalambhāt viśeṣa anupalambha ādibhyaḥ ca kim karma vat gamana tvam param sāmānyam āhosvit utkṣepaṇa tva ādi vat aparam iti saṃśayaḥ kāryaḥ 
[II,252,11^2]	na saṃśayaḥ kāryaḥ karma tva paryāya tvāt ātma tva puruṣa tva vat paryāyaḥ eva gamana tvam iti sarvatra karma pratyaya vat gamana pratyaya upalambhāt iti nyāyāt atha viśeṣa saṃjñayā kimartham gamana grahaṇam kṛtam iti viśeṣa saṃjñā avasare sāmānya saṃjñā upadarśanasya adarśanāt na bhramaṇa ādi avarodha artha tvāt utkṣepaṇa ādi śabdaiḥ anavaruddhānām asaṅgṛhītānām bhramaṇa patana syandana ādīnām avarodha artham karma tva jñāpana artham iti anyathā hi gamana grahaṇam antareṇa yāni eva catvāri viśeṣa saṃjñā uktāni utkṣepaṇa ādīni tāni eva sāmānya viśeṣa saṃjñā viṣayāṇi prasajyeran iti sāmānya saṃjñā karma saṃjñā viśeṣa saṃjñā ca utkṣepaṇa ādi saṃjñā tad viṣayāṇi catvāri eva prasajyeran na bhramaṇa ādīni kutas etat viśeṣa saṃjñā viṣayāṇām eva sāmānya saṃjñā viṣaya tvāt tasmāt utkṣepaṇa ādi vat bhramaṇa ādīnām api karma tva jñāpana artham gamana grahaṇam kṛtam iti na ca etasmin pakṣe bhramaṇa ādīnām apara jāti sambandhe api dūṣaṇam tad apekṣayā ānantyasya abhyupagamāt yat ca gamana grahaṇāt bhramaṇa ādayaḥ saṅgṛhītāḥ iti vākyam tat anyathā vyākhyātam 
[II,253,1_II,253,13]	athavā astu aparam sāmānyam gamana tvam aniyata diś deśa saṃyoga vibhāga kāraṇeṣu bhramaṇa ādiṣu eva vartate na utkṣepaṇa ādiṣu katham tarhi teṣu gamana vyavahāraḥ iti āha gamana śabdaḥ tu utkṣepaṇa ādiṣu bhāktaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ kasmāt upacāra bījāt sva āśraya saṃyoga vibhāga kartṛ tva sāmānyāt iti yathā utpannam utkṣepaṇa ādi sva āśrayasya padārtha antaraiḥ saṃyoga vibhāgān karoti tathā gamanam api iti na ca etasmāt eva nimittāt utkṣepaṇa ādiṣu gamana vyavahāra vat gamane api utkṣepaṇa ādi vyavahāra prasaṅgaḥ kārya sadbhāvena kāraṇa kalpanāyāḥ pravartanāt na ca utkṣepaṇa ādiṣu gamana vyavahāra vat gamane api utkṣepaṇa ādi vyavahāraḥ dṛṣṭaḥ tasmāt acodyam etat atha pakṣa dvaya upanyāsāt kim atra ācāryasya abhipretam pañcānām pratiniyata jāti yogitva abhidhānāt gamana tvam aparam samānyam iti etat anye tu vāstava dūṣaṇasya para sāmānya pakṣe anabhidhānāt tat eva abhipretam iti manyante 
[II,253,17_II,254,18^1]	pūrvam sat pratyayam asat pratyayañca karma uktam tatra sat pratyaya karma vidhiḥ katham iti āha cikīrṣiteṣu kartum abhīṣṭeṣu yajña adhyayana dāna kṛṣi ādiṣu ityādi padena bhojana ādeḥ grahaṇam yajña ādiṣu ca tila ādi grahaṇa artham yadā hastam utkṣeptum icchati apakṣeptum vā tadā hastavati ātma pradeśe prayatnaḥ san jāyate tad utpattau ātmā samavāyi kāraṇam ātma manaḥ saṃyogaḥ asamavāyi kāraṇam icchā nimitta kāraṇam tat prayatnam gurutvañca apekṣamāṇāt ātma hasta saṃyogāt asamavāyi kāraṇāt haste samavāyi kāraṇe karma utpadyate hasta vat sarva śarīra avayaveṣu pada ādiṣu śarīre ca iti yathā ātma hasta saṃyogaḥ asamavāyi kāraṇam prayatnaḥ tu nimitta kāraṇam hasta karma utpattau tathā sarva śarīra avayaveṣu śarīre ca samaveta karma utpattau ātma saṃyogaḥ asamavāyi kāraṇam prayatnaḥ nimitta kāraṇam iti atideśa arthaḥ tad sambaddheṣu api musala ādiṣu katham karma bhavati iti avyutpanna praśna anantaram āha hastena musalam gṛhītvā icchām karoti kim viśiṣṭām 
[II,254,18^2]	utkṣipāmi hastena musalam iti evam rūpām tad anantaram hastavati ātma pradeśe prayatnaḥ tad anurūpaḥ tam apekṣamāṇāt ātma hasta saṃyogāt asamavāyi karaṇāt yasmin kāle haste samavāyi kāraṇe karma utpadyate tasmin eva kāle tam eva prayatnam apekṣamāṇāt hasta musala saṃyogāt asamavāyi kāraṇāt musale api kāraṇe karma tatas dūram utkṣipte musale tad artha icchā utkṣepaṇa icchā nivartate sva kāraṇāt punar api apakṣepeṇa icchā utpadyate tad anantaram hastavati ātma pradeśe prayatnaḥ tad anurūpaḥ tam apekṣamāṇāt yathā uktāt saṃyoga dvayāt iti ātma hasta saṃyogāt musala hasta saṃyogāt ca prayatna apekṣād hasta musalayoḥ yugapad apakṣepaṇa karmaṇī bhavataḥ tatas antyena āvasānikena musala karmaṇā ulūkhala musalayoḥ abhighāta ākhyaḥ saṃyogaḥ kriyate sa saṃyogaḥ asamavāyi kāraṇa bhūtaḥ musala gatam vegam apekṣamāṇaḥ apratyayam aprayatnam musale api utpatana karma karoti tat karma asamavāyi karaṇam abhighāta apekṣam musale samavāyi kāraṇe saṃskāram ārabhate tam apekṣya musala hasta saṃyogaḥ apratyayam aprayatna pūrvakam haste api utpatana karma karoti 
[II,255,6]	nanu musala ulūkhala saṃyogāt musale karma utpatti sama kālam prāktana saṃkāra vināśe apekṣā kāraṇa bhāvāt na musale karma saṃskāram ārabhate tad abhāve ca hasta musala saṃyogaḥ katham haste apratyayam utpatana karma kuryāt iti āśaṅkya āha yadi api prāktanaḥ saṃskāraḥ vinaṣṭaḥ tathā api musala ulūkhala saṃyogaḥ paṭu karma utpādakaḥ kutas saṃyoga viśeṣa bhāvāt atas tasya karmaṇaḥ saṃskāra sācivye samarthaḥ bhavati sacivasya bhāvaḥ sācivyam sāhāyyam tatra samarthaḥ bhavati iti 
[II,255,12_II,255,17]	athavā prāktanaḥ eva paṭuḥ saṃskāraḥ abhidhātāt avinaśyan avasthitaḥ iti pakṣa antaram darśayati prāktanasya paṭu saṃskārasya avasthāne saṃskāravati punar saṃskāra ārambhaḥ na asti iti atas yasmin kāle saṃskāra apekṣāt abhighātāt apratyayam musale utpatana karma tasmin eva kāle tam eva saṃskāram apekṣamāṇān musala hasta saṃyogāt apratyayam haste api utpatana karma iti 
[II,256,1^1]	pāṇi mukteṣu tomara ādiṣu gamana vidhiḥ gamana prakāraḥ katham iti āha yadā tomaram hastena gṛhītvā icchām karoti hastena utkṣipāmi tomaram iti tad anantaram tad anurūpaḥ prayatnaḥ tam apekṣamāṇāt yathā ukta saṃyoga dvayāt iti ātma hasta saṃyogāt hasta tomara saṃyogāt ca tomara hastayoḥ yugapad a ākarṣaṇa karmaṇī bhavataḥ prasārite ca haste dūramatkṣipte tad ākarṣaṇa arthaḥ tasya tomarasya ākarṣaṇa arthaḥ prayatnaḥ vyāvartete tad anantaram tiryak ūrdhvam adhas dūram āsannam vā kṣipāmi iti icchā san jāyate tiryak kṣipāmi ūrdhvam adhas dūram āsannam kṣipāmi iti tad anantaram tad anurūpaḥ prayatnaḥ iti āsanne mandaḥ dūre tīvraḥ eva iti tam apekṣamāṇaḥ tomara hasta saṃyogaḥ nodana ākhyaḥ 
[II,256,1^2]	na udyana udakayoḥ saha gamanāt na udyaḥ tomaraḥ na udakaḥ hastaḥ iti tayoḥ saṃyogaḥ prayatna apekṣaḥ tasmāt tomare karma utpannam nodana apekṣam tasmin saṃskāram ārabhate tomaraḥ samavāyi kāraṇam karma asamavāyi kāraṇam prayatnaḥ nimitta kāraṇam iti tatas saṃskāra nodanābhyām tāvat karmāṇi bhavanti yāvat hasta tomarayoḥ vimocana arthena karmaṇā parasparam vibhāgaḥ iti tatas vibhāgāt nivṛtte nodane saṃskārāt asamavāyi kāraṇāt tad anurūpāṇi karmāṇi bhavanti āpatanāt patanam yāvat iti saṃskārasya tīvratara ādi bheda bhinna tvāt karmāṇi api evam bhavanti iti 
[II,256,16_II,257,9]	tathā yantra mukteṣu śara pāṣāṇa ādiṣu gamana vidhiḥ katham kim viśiṣṭaḥ ca puruṣaḥ tān prayuṅkte kena vā prakāreṇa iti āha yaḥ balavān kṛta vyāyāmaḥ hi astra yantra siddhaḥ vāmena kareṇa dhanuḥ viṣṭabhya dakṣiṇena śaram sandhāya iti bāhulya apekṣayā etat saha śareṇa vartate iti sa śarā tām jyām muṣṭinā gṛhītvā icchām karoti sa jya iṣum ākarṣayāmi enam dhanuḥ iti saha jyayā vartate iti sajyaḥ sa ca āsauviṣuḥ ca iti tathā uktaḥ tam enam sajya iṣum ākarṣayāmi dhanuḥ ca iti 
[II,257,15]	na ca enam iti padam dhanuḥ śabdena abhisandhānīyam tasya napuṃsaka liṅga tayā etat dhanuḥ iti syāt atho arddhā ṛcca ādi pāṭhāt prayoga darśanāt vā kathañcid ubhaya liṅgatā iṣyate tathā api enam dhanuṣam iti syāt na tu enam dhanuḥ iti puṃliṅga vivakṣāyām api iti śabdena karmaṇaḥ abhihita tvāt dvitīyā vibhaktiḥ na bhavati iti anye tad anantaram icchā anantaram prayatnaḥ tam apekṣamāṇāt ātma hasta saṃyogāt asamavāyi kāraṇāt haste samavāyi kāraṇe yadā eva ākarṣaṇa karma utpadyate tadā eva prayatnam apekṣamāṇāt hasta jyā śara saṃyogāt asamavāyi kāraṇāt jyāyām śare ca samavāyi kāraṇe karma utpadyate prayatna viśiṣṭam hasta jyā saṃyogam apekṣamāṇābhyām jyā koṭi saṃyogābhyām asamavāyi kāraṇābhyām dhanuṣkoṭyoḥ samavete karmaṇī bhavataḥ dhanuṣi ca samavetam karma jyā dhanuḥ saṃyogāt asamavāyi kāraṇāt hasta jyā saṃyogam viśiṣṭam apekṣamāṇāt iti etat sarvam yugapad ekasmin kāle bhavati kāraṇasya yaugapadyāt 
[II,258,1^1]	evam ākarṇāt karṇam yāvat ākṛṣṭe dhanuṣi na atas paramanena gantavyam iti yat jñānam tatas tad ākarṣaṇa arthasya prayatnasya vināśaḥ tatas punar mokṣaṇa icchā san jāyate tad anantaram tad anurūpaḥ prayatnaḥ tam apekṣamāṇāt ātma aṅguli saṃyogāt asamavāyi kāraṇāt aṅguliṣu mocana artham karma utpadyate tasmāt aṅguli jyā vibhāgaḥ tatas vibhāgāt tad saṃyoga vināśaḥ tasmin vinaṣṭe pratibandhaka abhāvāt maṇḍalībhūtam dhanuḥ yathā avasthitam sthāpayati iti sthiti sthāpaka saṃskāraḥ dhanuṣi karma ārabhate tatra dhanuḥ samavāyi kāraṇam sthiti sthāpaka saṃskāraḥ asamavāyi kāraṇam adṛṣṭa ādiḥ nimitta kāraṇam iti yadā eva dhanuṣi ākarṣaṇa karmaṇā maṇḍalīkṛte sthiti sthāpana artham sthiti sthāpaka saṃskārāt karma utpadyate tadā tam eva saṃskāram apekṣamāṇāt dhanuṣaḥ jyā saṃyogāt jyā śara saṃyogāt asamavāyi kāraṇāt jyāyām śare ca karma utpadyate tat utpannam sva kāraṇa apekṣam jyāyām saṃskāram ārabhate tam apekṣamāṇaḥ iṣu jyā saṃyogaḥ nodanam 
[II,258,1^2]	tayoḥ saha gamanāt tasmāt iṣau ādyam karma utpadyate tat ca nodana apekṣa miṣau saṃskāram ārabhate tatra iṣuḥ samavāyi kāraṇam karma asamavāyi kāraṇam nodanam nimitta kāraṇam iti tasmāt saṃskārān nodana sahāyāt tāvat karmāṇi bhavanti yāvat iṣujyā vibhāgaḥ tad utpattau jyeṣvoḥ samavāyikāraṇa tvam iṣu karmaṇaḥ asamavāyi kāraṇa tvam śeṣam nimitta kāraṇam tatas vibhāgāt nivṛtte nodane karmāṇi uttarottarāṇi iṣu saṃskārāt eva āpatanāt iti patanam yāvat tāvat iti bahūni karmāṇi kramaśas kasmāt saṃyoga bahu tvāt tad sadbhāve api avināśe sarvadā iṣoḥ apātaḥ syāt 
[II,258,21]	atha ekam api karma anekam saṃyogam kṛtvā śaktimān dyāt vinaśyati iti tarhi saṃskārasya anārabdha kāryasya avasthānāt anyat karma antaram iti apātaḥ eva syāt na ca saṃskārasya saṃyoga janaka tvam yena aneka kārya karaṇe śakti mān dyāt vināśaḥ syāt teṣām karma kāryatvāt tatas tad utpāde karmaṇām eva vināśaḥ yuktaḥ na ca saṃskārāt abhinnam eva karma iti vācyam pratyaya bhedasya bheda lakṣaṇa tvāt tathā ca vegena gacchati iti vega anuraktaḥ gamana anuraktaḥ ca pratyayaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ tasmāt vegaḥ saṃyoga vat karmaṇaḥ artha antaram iti abhede tu manda gamana ādau api vegena gacchati iti pratyayaḥ syāt na ca etat asti 
[II,259,1_II,259,4]	atha saṃyoga vibhāga upalambhāt anumīyate karma iti ced na saṃyoga vat indriya vyāpāreṇa eva karmaṇi api aparokṣa jñāna sadbhāvasya aviśeṣāt yathā hi vastunaḥ pradeśa antaraiḥ saṃyoga vibhāgāḥ pratyakṣeṇa pratīyante tadvat karma api iti yat ca pradeśa antaraiḥ saṃyoga vibhāga upalambhe sati calati iti jñānam ānumānikam iti iṣṭam tat na yuktam nadī srotasi u ūrdhva avasthitasya sthāṇoḥ tad sadbhāve api calana pratyaya adarśanāt ākāśe prakṣiptasya īṣoḥ tad abhāve api tad sadbhāva darśanāt 
[II,259,8_II,259,11]	yat ca idam ekasmin sthāne pratikṣaṇam utpādāt tiṣṭhati iti vyavahāraḥ deśa antare ca tad bhāvāt gamana vyavahāraḥ iti uktam tat na yuktam kṣaṇa bhaṅga pratiṣedhāt atha saṃyoga bahu tvāt bahūni karmāṇi iti satyam na ca evam saṃskārasya api saṃyoga bahu tvāt bahu tvam tasya saṃyoga mātreṇa avināśāt vināśe vā karma antarāṇām utpattiḥ na syāt asamavāyi kāraṇa abhāvāt na ca ātmā iṣu saṃyogaḥ eva adṛṣṭa apekṣaḥ asamavāyi kāraṇam pratyakṣa anumānābhyām kāraṇa antara anupalambhe sati tat kalpanāyāḥ samāśrayaṇāt upalabhyate ca akṣa vyāpāreṇa eva vegaḥ tasya pratyākhyānam aśakyam 
[II,259,17]	atha saṃskārāt upajāta karmaṇi uttara saṃyogāt vegasya karmaṇaḥ ca vinaśyattā anyayoḥ ca vega karmaṇoḥ utpadyamāna tā atas tayoḥ utpādaḥ prāktanayoḥ ca vināśaḥ iti kalpanāyām kim dūṣaṇam vinaśyat avasthasya asamavāyikāraṇa tvasya abhāvaḥ iti etat tathā hi na prāktanam karma saṃskāra antaram ārabhate na api prāktanaḥ vegaḥ karma antaram ubhayoḥ vinaśyat avastha tvena asamavāyi kāraṇa tva abhāvāt na ca anyat asamavāyi kāraṇam antarāle karmaṇaḥ sambhavati iti uktam yat ca saṃskārāt utpannam karma tat na saṃskāra antaram ārabhate apekṣā kāraṇa abhāvāt na api prāktanaḥ saṃskāraḥ apekṣā kāraṇam saṃskāravati saṃskāra ārambha pratiṣedhāt avaśyam karma antara utpatti sama kālam uttara saṃyogāt pūrva karma nivṛtti vat pūrva saṃskārasya api nivṛttiḥ vācyā na ca saṃyoga mātram apekṣā kāraṇam karmaṇaḥ saṃskāra ārambhe manda gatau adarśanāt tathā hi manda gatau saṃyoga sadbhāve api na karma saṃskāram ārabhate iti upalabdham tasmāt ekaḥ eva saṃskāraḥ antarāle karmaṇaḥ apekṣā kāraṇa abhāvāt iti 
[II,260,4_II,260,15]	nanu evam tarhi saṃskārasya eka rūpa tvāt katham tīvratara ādi bheda bhinnānām karmaṇām utpattiḥ sahakāri bhedāt sa ca kārya bhedena eva jñeyaḥ tatra dṛṣṭasya anupalabdheḥ adṛṣṭa ākhyaḥ kalpate iti kṣiptasya iṣoḥ pāta upalambhena ca vega vināśa prasiddheḥ tasya sa hetu tvāt anyasya ca vināśa hetoḥ abhāvāt aneka kārya karaṇe sati śakti prakṣayāt vināśaḥ kalpyate iti sā ca śaktiḥ adṛṣṭa viśeṣaḥ eva aneka karma sampādakaḥ etat ca aneka saṃskāra vādinā api abhyupagantavyam anyathā hi punar saṃskāra utpatteḥ iṣoḥ apātaḥ eva syāt tasmāt ukta nyāyena ekaḥ eva saṃskāraḥ iti upasaṃhāram āha evam ātma adhiṣṭhiteṣu prayatna dvāreṇa anadhiṣṭhiteṣu sat pratyayam asat pratyayañca karma uktam 
[II,260,20^1]	idānīm anadhiṣṭhiteṣu bāhyeṣu śarīra asambaddheṣu ākāśa ādi nivṛtti artham caturṣu mahābhūteṣu iti paramāṇu nivṛtti artham apratyayam aprayatna pūrvakam karma gamanam eva nodana ādibhyaḥ bhavati ādipadena abhighāta saṃyukta saṃyoga guru tva ādeḥ grahaṇam tatra nodanam vyākhyāyate guru tva drava tva prayatna vegān samasta vyasta anapekṣamāṇaḥ yaḥ saṃyoga viśeṣaḥ nodanam parasparam avibhāga kṛtaḥ karmaṇaḥ kāraṇam iti yaḥ saṃyogaḥ tad nodanam iti ukte ati prasaṅgaḥ tad artham karmaṇaḥ kāraṇam iti abhighātaḥ api evam bhavati iti avibhāga kṛtaḥ iti padam tathā api utpannasya karmaṇaḥ avaśyam vibhāga janaka tvam atas parasparam iti padam tathā api parasparam saṃyoginaḥ vibhāga janakasya karmaṇaḥ kāraṇam saṃyukta saṃyogaḥ api iti atas guru tva drava tva prayatna vegān samasta vyasta anapekṣamāṇaḥ iti tatra yadā culukena udakam gṛhītvā vegena pratikṣipati tadā sarve guru tva ādayaḥ sambhavanti iti tad apekṣam culuka udaka saṃyogaḥ nodanam vyasta pakṣe tu guru tvam apekṣamāṇaḥ saṃyogaḥ nodanam 
[II,260,20^2]	yathā sūkṣma śāśā khā upari vyavasthāpitam atiśayena guru dravyam adhas gati hetuḥ bhavati śākhāyāḥ drava tvam apekṣamāṇaḥ tṛṇa udaka saṃyogaḥ tṛṇe gamanam ārabhate vegam apekṣamāṇaḥ vāyu vanaspati saṃyogaḥ vṛkṣa ādiṣu calana kāraṇam prayatna apekṣaḥ tu hasta musala saṃyogaḥ musala karma utpattau yadā ca prayatnena paṅke pādam upakṣipati tadā prayatna guru tve ca apekṣya pāda paṅka saṃyogaḥ paṅkam adhas nayati iti yadā ca pāṣāṇa ādeḥ vegena pāte sati paṅkena saṃyogaḥ tadā pāṣāṇa ādi gatam guru tvam vegañca apekṣamāṇam pāṣāṇa paṅka saṃyogaḥ nodanam iti yadā kaścid vegena kūpa ādau patati tadā guru tva prayatna vegān apekṣya devadatta udaka saṃyogaḥ adhas gati hetuḥ bhavati yadā ca jaladhara dhārā sambandhāt tṛṇa ādeḥ adhas gamanam tadā guru tva drava tva vegān apekṣate ityādi draṣṭavyam tasmāt yathā uktān nodanāt caturṣu api mahābhūteṣu karma bhavati iti udāharaṇam āha yathā paṅka ākhyāyām pṛthivyām pāda ādi saṃyogāt yathā ukta viśeṣaṇāt iti 
[II,261,17_II,261,24]	abhighātasya itarasmāt bheda artham āha vega apekṣaḥ yaḥ saṃyoga aviśeṣaḥ parasparam vibhāga hetoḥ ekasya karmaṇaḥ kāraṇam saḥ abhighātaḥ iti vibhāga hetu karma kāraṇam na udanādiḥ api iti parasparam vibhāga hetoḥ iti padam tathā api ātma manaḥ saṃyogena vyabhicāra parihāra artham vega apekṣaḥ iti padam na ca ātma manaḥ saṃyogaḥ paraspara vibhāga hetu sampādakaḥ vega apekṣaḥ iti 
[II,262,3]	nanu ekasya iti padam vyartham abhighātāt ubhayatra api karma upalabdheḥ satyam tathā api ekasya iti ādya karma jñāpana artham uttarottarāṇi vegāt eva bhavanti iti nodana ādiḥ ca uttara karmaṇām bahūnām api kāraṇam iti anye tu ekasya kāraṇam eva na tu ekasya eva iti avadhāraṇam manyante nodane api ekasya iti viśeṣaṇam evam vyākhyeyam udāharaṇantu yathā pāṣāṇa ādiṣu pāṣāṇa ādi abhighātāt iti saṃyukta saṃyoga nirūpaṇa artham āha tathā pāda ādibhiḥ nudyamānāyām ityādi 
[II,262,9_II,262,17]	parasparam avibhāga kṛtaḥ karmaṇaḥ kāraṇam nodanam api iti atas nodana abhighātayoḥ anyatara apekṣaḥ ubhaya apekṣaḥ vā yaḥ saṃyogaḥ sa saṃyukta saṃyogaḥ kvacid nodana apekṣaḥ kvacid abhighāta apekṣaḥ kvacid ubhaya apekṣaḥ iti udāharaṇantu yathā paṅka ākhyāyām pṛthivyām kim viśiṣṭāyām pāda ādibhiḥ nudyamānāyām abhihanyamānāyām pṛthivyām vā ye pradeśāḥ na nudyante na sākṣāt pādena sambadhyante na api abhihanyante na sākṣāt pāṣāṇa ādinā sambadhyante teṣu api karma san jāyate pradeśāḥ samavāyi kāraṇam pāda ādibhiḥ ca sambaddha pradeśaiḥ saha saṃyogaḥ asamavāyi kāraṇam pāda ādi saṃyogāḥ ca nimitta kāraṇam 
[II,262,20]	patana nirūpaṇa artham āha guru tvāt yat adhas gamanam tat patanam vāyoḥ api adhas gamanam vṛkṣa koṭara ādiṣu ūrdhva pradeśena praviṣṭasya sambhavati iti tad vyavaccheda artham guru tvāt iti pṛthivī udakayoḥ iti āśraya nirūpaṇam patana āśrayaḥ samavāyi kāraṇam guru tvam asamavāyi kāraṇam guru tva vidhāraka saṃyoga prayatna vega abhāve satī iti nimitta kāraṇam darśayati iti yathā musala śarīra ādiṣu iti udāharaṇam hasta musala saṃyoga abhāvāt musale patanam prayatna abhāvāt śarīre vega abhāva ādiṣau iti tatra ādyam guru tvāt eva asamavāyi kāraṇāt utpadyate patanam tat ca utpannam sva kāraṇa apekṣam saṃskāram ārabhate tasmāt dvitīya ādīni tu patanāni guru tva saṃskāra abhyām asamavāyi kāraṇābhyām utpadyante 
[II,263,3_II,263,13]	syandana nirūpaṇa artham āha srotaḥ bhūtānām apām sthalāt nimna abhisarpaṇam yat tat drava tvāt syandanam iti sthalāt nimna abhisarpaṇam pāṣāṇa ādeḥ api iti srotaḥ bhūtānām iti padam sarpa ādeḥ api evam pravāhaḥ sambhavati iti apām iti grahaṇam tathā api apām dṛḍha hasta parigṛhītānām sthalāt nimna abhisarpaṇam na bhavati iti atas srotaḥ bhūtānām iti apām iti ca bāhulya apekṣayā na tu apām eva iti avadhāryate taila ādau api sadbhāvāt atas yat ukta rūpam abhisarpaṇam tat syandanam drava tvāt bhavati iti 
[II,263,20^1]	katham iti avyutpannasya vistara parijñāna apekṣayā praśna antaram āha samantāt rodhaḥ saṃyogena avayavi drava tvam pratibaddham ityādi samantāt sarvatas rodhasā saha saṃyogena setu saṃyogena avayavi drava tvam pratibaddham udake kriyām na karoti na api avayava drava tvam syandanam ārabhate iti āha avayava drava tvam api ekārtha samavetam yatra hi avayava drava tvam tatra eva rodhaḥ saṃyogaḥ api iti atas tena eva pratibaddham uttara uttara avayava drava tvāni tu saṃyukta saṃyogaiḥ pratibaddhāni rodhaḥ saṃyukta avayavena anyaḥ saṃyogaḥ 
[II,263,20^2]	tena api anyaḥ iti uttarottara avayava saṃyogaiḥ tad gata drava tvāni pratibaddhāni kriyām na ārabhante yadā tu setu bhedaḥ kṛtaḥ bhavati tadā samantāt pratibaddha tvāt avayavi drava tu asya karma ārambhaḥ na asti iti ayam asya arthaḥ mahā parimāṇa sambandhi tvāt avayavinaḥ na sūkṣma randhra deśa niṣkramaṇam setoḥ tu samīpa sthasya avayava drava tvasya kārya ārambhaka tvam tad pratibandhakasya saṃyogasya vyāvṛtteḥ tatas krameṇa uttarottara avayava drava tvānām vṛtti lābhaḥ kārya janaka tvam tathā hi setu samīpa sthasya avayavasya calane sati avayava antareṇa vibhāgāt tad saṃyogaḥ nivartate tatas dvitīya avayava drava tvam pratibandhaka abhāvāt kriyām ārabhate tatas tṛtīyā avayava saṃyoga nivṛttau tad gatam drava tvam karma ārabhate iti evam uttarottarāṇām vṛtti lābhaḥ tatas saṃyuktānām eva abhisarpaṇam iti 
[II,264,10_II,264,17]	yadi api saṃyogasya pratibandhakasya vināśe sati anyasya sarpaṇam tathā api tad jñāpana artham kramaśas saṃyuktānām eva abhisarpaṇam iti uktam tatas dravya ārambhaka saṃyoga vināśe sati pūrva dravya vināśaḥ tasmin sa pratibandhena santānena avasthitaiḥ avayavaiḥ dīrgha dravyam ārabhyate tatra ca dravye kāraṇa guṇa pūrva krameṇa drava tvam utpadyate kāraṇa drava tvāni asamavāyi kāraṇam avayavini drava tva utpattau iti tatra kāraṇānām prabandhena paripāṭyā gamane avayavini yat karma utpadyate tat syandana ākhyam iti 
[II,264,21_II,265,5]	upasaṃhāram āha saṃskārāt karmeṣu ādiṣu uktam guru tva ādibhyaḥ ca tathā abhramaṇam saṃskārāt eva bhavati iti āha cakra ādiṣu tad avayava anāñca pārśvatas pratiniyata diś deśa saṃyoga vibhāga utpattau iti pratiniyatāḥ hi diś deśāḥ cakra avaṣṭabdhāḥ taiḥ saha saṃyoge vibhāge ca kartavye yat avayavini karma utpadyate kutas saṃskārāt iti ādya daṇḍa cakra saṃyogāt asamavāyi kāraṇāt daṇḍa hasta saṃyoga apekṣāt upajātam cakre karma sva kāraṇa viśeṣa apekṣam saṃskāram ārabhate tatas saṃskāra nodanābhyām karmāṇi punar punar saṃskārāt eva avayaveṣu ca ādya karma utpattau nodana apekṣaḥ saṃyukta saṃyogaḥ asamavāyi kāraṇam tatas saṃskāra utpāde sati saṃskāraḥ api iti aniyata diś deśa saṃyoga vibhāga nimittam karma tat bhramaṇam iti aniyataiḥ diś deśaiḥ saṃyoga vibhāgān karoti iti 
[II,265,10]	kārya bhedena bhedam darśayati prāṇa ākhye tu vāyau karma kutas bhavati iti āha ātma vāyu saṃyogāt asamavāyi kāraṇāt icchā dveṣa pūrvaka prayatna apekṣāt utpadyate kim viśiṣṭasya iti āha jāgrataḥ iti kutas etat icchā anuvidhāna darśanāt iti recana icchātaḥ recanam pūraṇa icchātaḥ ca pūraṇam iti suptasya tu jīvana pūrvaka prayatna apekṣāt ātma vāyu saṃyogāt asamavāyi kāraṇāt prāṇa ākhye vāyau karma utpadyate iti kim atra pramāṇam suptasya jīvana pūrvakāt prayatnāt vāyau karma iti anumānam tathā hi suptasya vāyukriyā prayatna kāryā parigṛhīta vāyu kriyā tvāt jāgrat avasthāyām tad vāyu kriyāvat yatra ca pratyakṣa anumānābhyām anyat kāraṇam na upalabhyate tatra adṛṣṭasya eva kāraṇa tvam atra ca anumānāt prayatna kārya tva prasiddhau icchā dveṣa pūrvaka prayatna abhāvāt suptasya jīvana pūrvaka prayatna kārya tvam niścīyate iti 
[II,265,21]	evam caturṣu mahābhūteṣu nodana ādibhyaḥ karma vyākhyāyām ākāśa ādau kriyā śūnya tve kāraṇam āha ākāśa kāla diś ātmanaḥ sati api dravya bhāve niṣkriyāḥ sāmānya ādi vat amūrta tvāt yathā hi sāmānya ādeḥ amūrta tvāt niṣkriya tvam tadvat ākāśa ādeḥ api iti mūrta tvena hi kriyāvat tvam vyāptam tat ca vyāvartamānam ākāśa ādibhyaḥ sva vyāptam kriyāvat tvam gṛhītvā vyāvartate iti tat eva āha mūrtiḥ asarva gata dravya parimāṇam tad anuvidhāyinī ca kriyā yatra yatra kriyā tatra tatra mūrtiḥ iti sā ca mūrtiḥ ākāśa ādiṣu na asti tasmāt na teṣām kriyā sambandhaḥ asti iti 
[II,266,3_II,266,20^1]	atha yadi mūrti anuvidhāyinī kriyā manasaḥ tarhi mūrta tvāt kriyā sambandhaḥ vācyaḥ iti āha sa vigrahe śarīra avaruddhe manasi indriya antara sambandha artham yat jā agratas karma utpadyate tat kutas iti āha ātma manasoḥ saṃyogāt asamavāyi kāraṇāt icchā dveṣa pūrvaka prayatna apekṣāt kutas etat itthaṃbhūtāt prayatnāt jāgratas manaḥ kriyeta 
[II,266,20^2]	tat āha anvabhiprāyam indriya antareṇa viṣaya antara upalabdhi darśanāt abhiprāyam anu iti abhiprāyān atikrameṇa yena eva indriyeṇa viṣaya grahaṇa abhiprāyaḥ bhavati tena eva viṣaya upalabdhi darśanāt vijñāyate antaḥkaraṇasya icchā anuvidhāyi kriyā āśraya tvam tena anadhiṣṭhitasya indriyasya viṣaya grāhaka tva asambhavāt iti manaḥ sambandhaḥ niścīyate sa ca icchā anuvidhānāt tad pūrvaka prayatna janita kriyā kāryaḥ iti suptasya tu yat manasaḥ nirindriya ātma pradeśe pralīnasya indriya antara sambandha artham prabodha kāle karma tad ātma manasoḥ saṃyogāt asamavāyi kāraṇāt jīvana pūrvaka prayatna apekṣāt upajāyate tathā hi suptasya manaḥ kriyā prayatna kāryā parigṛhīta antaḥkaraṇa kriyā tvāt jāgrat avasthāyām tat kriyāvat apasarpaṇa karma upasarpaṇa karma ca ātma manasoḥ saṃyogāt asamavāyi kāraṇāt adṛṣṭa apekṣāt utpadyate iti mṛta śarīrāt vibhāga artham karma apasarpaṇam garbha śarīreṇa saṃyoga artham upasarpaṇam iti kadā punar tad apasarpaṇam 
[II,266,20^3]	katham bhavati iti āha yadā jīvana sahakāriṇoḥ ityādi jīvanam vyākhyātam tad sahakāriṇoḥ dharma adharmayoḥ upabhogāt sukha duḥkha saṃvedanāt prakṣayaḥ tadā tena śarīreṇa bhoktavyasya karmaṇaḥ abhāvāt śarīra antara upabhoga sampādaka karma sadbhāve api śarīrasya pātaḥ eva anyonya abhibhavaḥ vā iti sambhāvinaḥ pakṣa antarasya upanyāsaḥ tathā hi śarīra antara upabhoga dāyakena balīyasā paripakvena karmaṇā ārabdha śarīrasya upabhoga dāyaka tvena abhipravṛttasya karmaṇaḥ abhibhavaḥ bhoga dāna sāmartha apagamaḥ tīvra śabda upalambhena mandasya agrahaṇam iva iti tatas jīvana sahāyasya karmaṇaḥ vaikalye sati tad pūrvakasya prayatnasya vaikalyāt ca prāṇa nirodhaḥ tad nirodhe sati anyābhyām vṛtti labdha dharma adharmābhyām iti vṛttiḥ sahakāri kāraṇam 
[II,266,20^4]	tayā labdhau tad saha kṛtau yau dharma adhamau tābhyām ātma manaḥ saṃyoga sahakāribhyām mṛta śarīrāt vibhāga kāraṇam apasarpaṇa karma utpadyate tatas tasmāt śarīrāt bahis apagatam tābhyām eva dharma adharmābhyām sampāditam yat ātivāhikam sūkṣmaśarīram tena abhisambadhyate tad saṅkrāntaḥ ca svargam narakam vā gacchati gatvā ca āśaya anurūpeṇa śarīreṇa saṃyujyate tad saṃyoga artham karma upasarpaṇa ākhyam iti ātivāhika śarāram ca āgama balāt abhyupagatam antaḥkaraṇasya parigṛhīta tvāt iti tathā na kevalam etat adṛṣṭāt bhavati yogināñca bahis udrecitasya iti bahis deśaiḥ udrecitasya manasaḥ abhipreta deśa gamanam punar punar pratyāgamanañca tathā sarga kāle pratyagreṇa śarīreṇa sambandha artham karma adṛṣṭa kāritam iti na kevalam etat anyat api ca mahābhūteṣu yat karma kim viśiṣṭam 
[II,266,20^5]	pratyakṣa anumānābhyām anupalabhyamāna kāraṇam upakāra apakāra samartham iti arthaḥ tat api adṛṣṭa kāritam tat eva āha yathā sarga ādau sṛṣṭi ādau aṇuṣu karma śarīra ādi sampādana artham agni vāyvoḥ ūrdhva tiryak gamane iti agneḥ ūrdhva jvalanam vāyoḥ tiryak gamanam prāṇinām upakāra apakāra samartham iti mahābhūtānām bhū golaka deva kula ādīnām prakṣobhaṇam tad kampanam maṇīnām taskaram cauram prati gamanam ayasaḥ lohasya ayaskānta abhimukha tayā abhisarpaṇañca iti 
[II,268,8_II,268,17]	atha sāmānyasya lakṣaṇa parīkṣā artham parama parañca dvividham sāmānyam iti ādi prakaraṇam atra ca pūrvam vibhāgasya abhidhānāt aniyama jñāpanena kārya kāraṇa bhāva āśaṅkā vyudāsaḥ sāmānya lakṣaṇa vibhāgayoḥ yathā dravyam pṛthivī aptejaḥ ityādi prayojanam iti upadarśayati sva viṣaya sarva gatam iti vipratipatti vyudāsaḥ tathā hi pare manyante sarvam sāmānyam sarva gatam go tvam aśva piṇḍeṣu api asti aśvatvañca gopiṇḍa ādiṣu api iti anupalambhaḥ tu vyañjaka abhāvāt yatra ca vyañjaka sadbhāvaḥ tatra abhivyaktiḥ yathā gopiṇḍeṣu go tvasya aśva piṇḍe aśva tvasya iti 
[II,268,20^1]	tat ca asat go tvasya aśva ādi piṇḍeṣu sadbhāve pramāṇa abhāvāt vyavasthite hi sadbhāve abhivyañjaka abhāvāt anupalabdhiḥ kalpyate atha sāmānyam sarvaiḥ sambadhyate vyāpaka tvāt ākāśa vat iti atra kiṃpramāṇam tatra sarvaiḥ samavāye sādhye sādhya vikalam udāharaṇam ākāśasya sarvatra samavāya abhāvāt saṃyogi tve tu sādhye sāmānyasya dravya rūpa tā prasaṅgaḥ na ca etat yuktam guṇa karmasu samavetasya upalambhāt dravyasya ca dravyaḥ eva saṃyogaḥ na anyatra iti tathā yuta siddhi abhāvāt ca yuta siddhānāñca saṃyogaḥ iti atha sāmānyena sambandha mātram sādhyate 
[II,268,20^2]	tatra api siddha sādhanam sva ādhāreṇa saṃyukta saṃyogasya sarvatra sadbhāvāt tathā hi go tva ādhāreṇa saṃyuktam ākāśa ādi tena ca saṃyuktam sarva mūrtam iti evam vyāpaka tvam api yadi sarvaiḥ saṃyogi tvam tat asiddham pakṣe tat eva hi sarva gata tvam iti sādhyena aviśeṣaḥ eva tathā ākāśa ādeḥ vyāpaka tve api na sarvaiḥ sambandhaḥ iti anekāntaḥ atha sarvaiḥ sambandhaḥ sādhyate sarvatra sannihita tvāt iti hetunā tat api asat ākāśa ādeḥ tad bhāve guṇa karma ādinā sambandha abhāvāt na ca viśiṣṭa sambandha anabhyupagame bhāvasya anya sānnidhyam paśyāmaḥ atas sva viṣaya sarva gatam eva sāmānyam go tvam gopiṇḍeṣu eva aśva tvam aśva piṇḍeṣu eva tatra eva upalambhāt 
[II,269,12]	abheda ātmakam aneka vṛtti iti lakṣaṇam darśayati abheda ātmakam eka svabhāvam anekatra vṛttiḥ yasya tad aneka vṛtti iti eka tve sati anekatra vartamāna tvāt sāmānyam tathā api avayavi saṃkhya ādibhiḥ vyabhicāra parihāra artham nitya tve satī iti viśeṣaṇam arthāt vyākhyeyam tathā api salila ādi paramāṇu rūpa ādayaḥ nityāḥ ca anekatra vartante tad artham eka tve sati iti viśeṣaṇam te tu aneka tve sati anekatra vartante iti tathā api ekatve nitya tve ca sati anekatra vartate samavāyaḥ tad artham sva vyatiriktayā vṛttyā vartamāna tve satī iti ca viśeṣaṇam adhyāhāryam 
[II,269,19]	sarvam atra eva vākye labhyate adhyāhāraḥ na kāryaḥ iti ca anye tathā hi na vidyate bhedaḥ nānātvam vināśaḥ ca yasya iti tathā uktam tat eva ātmā svarūpam asya iti abheda ātmakam ekam avināśi ca iti labhyate anekatra vṛttiḥ yasya iti bahu vrīhiṇā vṛtteḥ vṛttimataḥ bhedā api upadarśitaḥ eva tasmāt ekatve nitya tve ca sati samavāyena anekatra vartamāna tvāt sāmānyam itarasmāt bhidyate 
[II,269,24]	nanu āśraya asiddham etat lakṣaṇam sāmānya sadbhāve pramāṇa abhāvāt yat ca anugata jñānam na tat sāmānya sattām darśayati kalpanā jñāna tvāt tathā ca anādi va āsanā vaśāt anugata jñānam utpadyate na punar vāstavam sāmānyam asti tat uktam para rūpam svarūpeṇa yayā saṃvriyate dhiyā eka artha pratibhāsinyāḥ bhāvān na āśritya bhedinaḥ 
[II,270,3]	asya arthaḥ bhedinaḥ parasparam vyāvṛtta ātmānaḥ bhāvāḥ teṣām rūpam bhinnam sva rūpeṇa abhinnena saṃvriyate pracchādyate yayā dhiyā kim viśiṣṭayā eka artha pratibhāsinyā iti ekaḥ ca arthaḥ pratibhāsate asyām sva gata ākāraḥ eva bāhyaḥ tasyāḥ nirviṣaya tvāt iti tayā saṃvṛta nānātvāḥ saṃvṛtyā bhedinaḥ svayam abhedinaḥ iva ābhānti bhāvāḥ rūpeṇa kenacid 
[II,270,9_II,270,14]	asya arthaḥ svayam bhedinaḥ api bhāvāḥ tayā saṃvṛtyā saṃvṛta nānātvāḥ santaḥ abhedinaḥ iva ābhānti na paramārthataḥ katham tarhi sāmānyam ucyate tat āha tad abhiprāya vaśāt sāmānyam sat prakīrtitam tat asat parama arthena yathā saṅkalpitam tayā paramārthataḥ asat api sāmānyam sat prakīrtitam tad abhiprāya vaśāt eka ākāra pratibhāsa vaśāt iti na ca sāmānyam vyaktīnām vyāvṛtta rūpa tvāt anyasya ca apratibhāsanāt iti āha vyaktayaḥ na anuyanti anyat anuyāyi na bhāsate jñānāt avyatiriktañced katham artha antaram vrajet 
[II,270,18]	tasmāt buddhiḥ eva tad anya vyatirekiṇaḥ padārthān āśritya utpadyamānā vikalpitā sva vāsanā prakṛtim anuvidadhāti iti bhinnam eṣām rūpam tirodhāya abhinnam ātmīyam rūpam adhyavasyati saṃsṛjantī saṃdarśayati sā ca eka sādhana sādhya tayā buddhi vartinām eva bhāvānām bahis iva parisphurantī sāmānyam iti ucyate sā ca sva vyatirikteṣu bhāveṣu bhavati iti viśeṣa viṣaya iti ucyate na paramārthataḥ tasmāt anugata vyāvṛtta svarūpa tvāt sāmānyam viśeṣaḥ ca na tu bāhyāḥ vivekinaḥ padārthāḥ na ca teṣu vikalpa vṛttiḥ katham teṣu bhavati iti parīkṣakāḥ khalu evam vivecayanti jātyā na tu vyavahartāraḥ te tu sva ālambanām eva buddhim anugata ākārām bahīrūpa tayā manyamānāḥ dṛśya vikalpau arthau ekīkṛtya pravartante pratipādayanti ca iti na tu nityam ekam anugatam viśeṣa vyatiriktam sāmānyam pratibhāsate iti 
[II,271,1_II,271,5]	punar api uktam śabdaḥ artha aṃśaka māhā iti tatra anya apohaḥ ucyate ākāraḥ sa ca na arthe asti tam vadan artha bhāj katham iti vṛtti anupapatteḥ ca na vāstavam sāmānyam asti iti tathā ca ekatra vartamānam sāmānyam na eka deśena vartate tad abhāvāt na sarva ātmanā anyatra vṛtti abhāva prasaṅgāt tathā yena eva rūpeṇa ekatra vartate tena eva anyatra api iti abhyupagame sarva piṇḍānām eka tā prasaṅgaḥ atha svarūpa antareṇa tarhi svarūpa bhedāt tasya nānātvam prasajyate svabhāva antara nivṛttau ca anekatra vṛtti tvam virudhyate iti uktam deśa kāla avasthā viśeṣa viniyata eka saṃsarga avyavacchinna svabhāva antara virahāt anekatra vṛtteḥ ekasya na deśa ādi viśeṣavatā anyena yogaḥ iti 
[II,271,12]	tatra deśa viśeṣaḥ nagara ādiḥ kāla viśeṣaḥ vasanta ādiḥ avasthā viśeṣaḥ bālya ādiḥ teṣu viniyataḥ sarva ātmanā pratiṣṭhitaḥ yathā ukta svabhāvaḥ ca asau ekaḥ ca tena saṃsargaḥ sambandhaḥ tad saṃsargeṇa avyavacchinnam akroḍīkṛtam ukta svabhāvāt svabhāva antaram tena virahaḥ viyogaḥ tad rahita tvāt iti hetu arthaḥ aneka vṛtteḥ ekasya iti dharmi nirdeśaḥ na deśa ādi viśeṣavatā anyena yogaḥ iti sādhya dharma nirdeśaḥ rūpa ādi vat iti dṛṣṭāntaḥ prayogaḥ punar evam bhavati yasya yathā ukta svabhāva antara virahaḥ na tasya deśa ādi viśeṣavatā anyena yogaḥ yathā rūpa ādiḥ asti ca sāmānya ādeḥ asau iti viruddha upalabdhiḥ yadi ca ekam tena ca svarūpeṇa sarvaiḥ sambadhyeta sāmānyam sarva piṇḍānām eka deśa kāla avasthāyogita aprasaṅgaḥ tad deśa ādi viśeṣita piṇḍa vṛtti svarūpa tvāt sāmānyasya yadā ca ekasmin piṇḍe deśa ādi viśeṣite samupalabhyate tadā eva aśeṣasya āśraya viśeṣitasya upalambhaḥ syāt tasya eka rūpa tvāt iti aneka vṛtti tva anabhyupagame ca rūpa ādi vat eka āśraya tvāt sāmānya rūpa tā na syāt iti 
[II,271,25]	na ca sāmānyasya svabhāva antaram asti yena aneka vṛtti tvam syāt iti uktam na ca sāmānyasya niyata āśrayeṇa sambandhe niyama hetuḥ asti iti tathā go tvam sambadhyamānam na gavā sambadhyate go tva sambandhāt pūrvam piṇḍasya tad rūpa tva asambhavāt atha agavā sambadhyate tarhi tasya aśvena api sambandhaḥ syāt go tva abhisambandhāt pūrvam agorūpatāyāḥ sarvatra sādhāraṇa tvāt yatra ca gopiṇḍa ādiḥ vartate na tatra go tva ādi sāmānyam samavaiti iti tad āśrayiṇā tu sambadhyate iti citram yatra asau vartate bhāvaḥ tena sambadhayate na tu tad deśinantu vyāpnoti kim api etat mahā adbhutam 
[II,272,9]	tathā piṇḍe vrajati na sāmānyasya gamanam asti niṣkriya tvāt na api avasthānam piṇḍasya tad śūnyatā prasaṅgāt na bhāgena gamanam avasthānañca niraṃśa tvāt na api paścāt āgatya abhisambadhyate pūrvam tat śūnyasya anupalabdheḥ tat uktam na yāti na ca tatra āsīt asti paścāt na ca aṃśa vat jahāti pūrvam na ādhāram aho vyasana santatiḥ 
[II,272,16]	tat etat asat jāti pradveṣa andhatayā pramāṇa mārga paribhraṣṭaiḥ abhihitam iti samādhīyate tathā hi cakṣuḥ ādi vyāpāreṇa anugata jñānasya abādhyamānasya upalabdheḥ avaśyam anugatam nimittam vācyam na ca vāsanā eva nimittam tasyāḥ pūrvam eva pratiṣedhāt yadi ca vāsanā viśiṣṭa pratyaya hetuḥ bāhyā ca iti saṃjñā bheda mātram eva syāt bodha antarbhāve tu bodha rūpa tayā tasyāḥ sarvatra aviśeṣāt vikalpa vaicitryam na syāt gopiṇḍa darśanāt gavā ākāraḥ vikalpaḥ aśva piṇḍa darśanāt ca aśva adhyavasāyī ityādi na ca deśa ādi bhedena api abādhyamānaḥ adhyavasāyaḥ nirviṣayaḥ sambhavati iti para rūpam svarūpeṇa yayā saṃvriyate iti apāstam eva 
[II,272,25^1_II,272,25^2]	yat ca idam vyaktayaḥ na anuyanti anyat anuyāyi na bhāsate iti asat etat anugata jñānena tasya pratibhāsanāt yathā hi sva lakṣaṇam vyāvṛtta rūpa tayā pratibhāsanāt asti evam anugata svarūpa tayā pratibhāsanāt sāmānyam api asti iti yadi ca vyāvṛtti jñāne sāmānyasya apratibhā āsanāt asattvam syāt anugata jñāne api sva lakṣaṇasya apratibhāsanāt asattvam eva syāt tasmāt yathā abādhyamāna jñāne nīla ādeḥ pratibhāsanāt sattvam evam anugata jñāne pratibhāsanāt sāmānyasya api sattvam abhyupagantavyam vṛtti vikalpa ādeḥ bādhakasya apramāṇa tvāt iti tathā hi vṛtti anupapatteḥ asattvam iti na idam svatantra sādhanam anekāntāt svatantre hi rūpa ādīnām sattvam anupapadyamāna vṛtti tvañca iti evam para pakṣe anupapadyamāna vṛtti tve api ākāśa ādīnām sattvam iti svarūpa asiddhaḥ ca vṛtteḥ samavāyasya sattvāt eka deśena sarva ātmanā ca na vartate iti ayuktaḥ viśeṣa pratiṣedhaḥ 
[II,272,25^3]	prakāra antarasya asambhavāt abhinna svarūpa tvāt ca sāmānyasya na tatra eka deśa sarva śabdayoḥ pravṛttiḥ tayoḥ bhinneṣu eva pravṛtti darśanāt samavāyena ca vartate sāmānyam na eka deśena svarūpeṇa vā tasya eka deśasya svarūpasya ca āvṛtti rūpa tvāt iti yat eva ca ekasmin piṇḍe svarūpam sāmānyasya tat eva piṇḍa antare api anugata jñāna janaka tvasya sarvatra sambhavāt tat āha eka dvi bahuṣu piṇḍeṣu ātma svarūpa anuvṛtti darśanāt sva pratyaya kāraṇam iti sāmānyasya ātma svarūpam anuvṛttam abhinnam atas anuvṛtti pratyayasya anugata jñānasya kāraṇam iti 
[II,273,16]	na ca sāmānyasya abhede padārthānām tathā abhāvaḥ tatas anya tvāt atas eva na ekasmin deśa ādi viśeṣite piṇḍe sāmānyasya upalambhāt aśeṣa viśeṣitasya api upalambha prasaṅgaḥ teṣām aniyata diś deśa sambandhi tvena upalambha abhāvāt yathā eva ca krameṇa viśeṣāḥ upalabhyante tathā eva tad viśeṣitam sāmānyam api iti yadā hi pañca purā avasthita gopiṇḍānām vasanta samaye bāla ādi avasthā viśeṣitānām upalambhaḥ tadā tad viśeṣitam sāmānyam upalabhyate anyadā tu anyaiḥ viśeṣitam iti piṇḍeṣu anugata jñāna janaka tvam sāmānyasya sarvatra avyabhicāri svarūpam tasmāt abheda ātmakam aneka vṛtti ca sāmānyam pratyakṣeṇa upalambhāt abhyupagantavyam yathā hi rūpam ekam eva ekatra vartamānam pratyakṣeṇa upalabdham tadvat ekam sāmānyam anekatra iti 
[II,273,26]	yat ca idam deśa ādi viśeṣita svabhāvāt aneka vṛtteḥ ekasya na deśa ādi viśeṣavatā anyena yogaḥ iti uktam tatra vyartha viśeṣaṇatā hetoḥ dharmiṇaḥ ca tathā hi eka saṃsarga avyavacchinna svabhāva antara virahāt na sāmānyasya viśeṣa antareṇa yogaḥ iti pratiṣedhe sādhye vyabhicāra abhāvāt sādhya sādhanayoḥ deśa ādi viśeṣaṇam anarthakam vyavacchedya sadbhāve hi viśeṣaṇasya arthavat ta upapatteḥ 
[II,274,3]	atha yathā ukta svabhāva antara virahe katham anya yogaḥ sāmānya ādeḥ anya yoge vā katham yathā ukta svabhāva antara virahaḥ tayoḥ anyatra rūpa ādau pratibandha siddhiḥ iti ced na vyabhicārāt tathā hi rūpa āśrayasya rūpa saṃsarga avyavacchinna svabhāva antara virahe api rasa ādibhiḥ yogaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ tadvat sāmānyasya api āśraya antareṇa yogaḥ kena vāryate rūpa āśraya vat sāmānye api yathā ukta svabhāva antara asattvasya aviśeṣāt iti asti ca rūpasya āśrayaḥ dravyam iti uktam 
[II,274,9]	atha eka tvāt sāmānyasya anekatra samavāyaḥ pratiṣidhyate tarhi yat anekatra samavetam tat anekam eva iti abhyupagame hetoḥ vyatireka avyabhicāreṇa eva gamaka tvāt ekatra samavetānām rūpa ādīnām ekatā prasajyeta na ca etat asti atha eka tvāt ekatra eva samavāyaḥ sādhyate tat api anaikāntikam ākāśa ādeḥ eka tve api ekatra eva samavāya abhāvāt yadi anekatra samavāyāt aneka tva prasaṅgaḥ abhidhīyeta tathā api yat ekam tat ekatra samavetam iti vyatireka abhāvaḥ sati api ākāśa ādau eka tve tad abhāvāt ekatra samavāyāt eka tvam iti etat api rūpa śabda ādibhiḥ anaikāntikam eka tvasya sāmānya viśeṣa rūpa tvāt tasmin sādhye hetoḥ anvaya vyatireka abhāvāt agamaka tvam evam nirviśeṣaṇasya hetoḥ antaraḥ sādhya sādhana bhāva prakāraḥ nirastaḥ tathā sa viśeṣaṇasya api hetoḥ ākāśa ādinā anaikāntika tvam tasya hi deśa ādi viśeṣavatā anyena yoge api tathā ukta svabhāva antara viraha upalabdheḥ 
[II,274,20^1]	yat ca idam pradīpa prabhāyāḥ deśa ādi viśeṣaṇa viśiṣṭāyāḥ na deśa ādi viśeṣavatā anyena yogaḥ iti udāharaṇam tatra api utpatteḥ ūrdhvam avayava kriyā krameṇa vināśa abhyupagamāt aneka kāla vyavadhāne deśa ādi viśeṣavatā anyena api yogaḥ sambhavati eva na ca pradīpa prabhāyām sādhya sādhana sadbhāve api hetoḥ vyabhicāra upadarśanāt gamaka tvam tathā sāmānyasya svabhāva antara virahaḥ asiddhaḥ tad ādhāra antarasya tad viśeṣaka tvena tad svabhāva antara tvāt pratīyate ca ādhāra ādheyayoḥ viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ yathā sat dravyam 
[II,274,20^2]	dravyasya sattā iti tasmāt svabhāva antara virahaḥ api sādhyaḥ eva iti tathā aneka vṛtteḥ ekasya na deśa ādi viśeṣavatā anyena yogaḥ iti prasaṅga nirdeśe sva vacana virodhaḥ tathā hi anya yoga pratiṣedhe na aneka vṛtti tvam bhavati iti atha sāmānya ādi paryāyaḥ ayam anekatra vṛttiḥ iti tathā api aneka vṛtti tva pratiṣedhaḥ anupapannaḥ sāmānyasva nitya tva ekatve sati aneka vṛtti tva lakṣaṇa tvāt pratyakṣeṇa ca sāmānyasya aneka vṛtti tva prasiddheḥ tena bādhya tvāt anumānam apramāṇam tathā hi eka dvi bahuṣu piṇḍeṣu akṣa vyāpārāt anugata jñānam utpadyamānam dṛṣṭam na ca idam bhrāntam pratyakṣa āgama saṃvādena visaṃvāda nivṛttau tad vyāptasya bhrānta tvasya nivṛtteḥ iti 
[II,275,8_II,275,12]	na ca apohāt eva anugata jñānam tasya vyāvṛtti rūpa tā āyām avastu tvena ajanaka tvāt janaka tve vā tasya artha kriyā kāritvāt vastu tva prasaṅgaḥ atha vyāvṛttāt anyā vyāvṛttiḥ na iṣyate tarhi teṣām paraspara vyāvṛtta svarūpa tayā anugata jñāna janaka tvam na syāt yat ca idam ago vyāvṛttiḥ go tvam iti uktam tatra gavām svarūpa pratipattim antareṇa tatas anyeṣām ago rūpatāyāma prasiddhiḥ tad aprasiddhau ca na gavām svarūpa pratipattiḥ iti anyonya āśraya tvam syāt yadi ca ekasmāt gopiṇḍāt anyeṣām ago rūpa tā tarhi gopiṇḍānām api anyeṣa āma go rūpatā prasaṅgaḥ teṣām api ekasmāt gopiṇḍāt anya tvāt 
[II,275,17]	atha sarvasmāt gopiṇḍāt anyeṣām ago tvam tat asat vargīkaraṇa nimitta asambhave sarveṣām gopiṇḍa nāma pratipattau tatas anyeṣām pratipattum aśakyatvāt yeṣāñca anugatam abhinnam nimittam asti teṣām go sva rūpa prasiddhau tatas anya vyāvṛttiḥ pratīyate eva atha artha kriyā sāmānyāt anuvṛtti pratyayaḥ iti ced na artha kriyāṇām api parasparam vyāvṛtta tayā anugata jñāna ajanaka tvāt atha artha kriyāṇām anugatam abhinnam nimittam upagrāha kamiṣyeta tat eva tarhi sāmānyam 
[II,275,24_II,276,1]	kā ca iyam artha kriyā yat sāmyāt anugata jñānam iti vācyam yadi vāha ādi rūpā sā ca manuṣya ādau api sambhavati iti tatra api gauḥ gauḥ iti anugata jñāna prasaṅgaḥ na ca pakṣe sarvatra etat asti iti anugata jñāna abhāva prasaṅgaḥ atha jñānam eva anugata vyāvṛtta ākāram sāmānyam iti ced saḥ ayam aśva ārūḍhasya vismṛtaḥ aśvaḥ iti nyāyaḥ na hi anugata nimittam vinā anugata jñānam sambhavati vāsanādeḥ nimittasya pratiṣedhāt 
[II,276,4]	yat api idam sāmānyasya ādhāre vrajati gamane kriyāvat tvam avasthāne ca anādhāra tvam iti tat asat bādhaka upapattau gamana pratyayasya bhākta tvāt tathā ca mūrta tvena kriyāvat tvam vyāptam tat ca sāmānya ādibhyaḥ vyāvartamānam sva vyāptam kriyāvat tvam gṛhītvā vyāvartate iti niṣkriyam sāmānyādi mūrta tve sati eva anvaya vyatirekābhyām artheṣu kriyā upalabdheḥ sā eva yogya tā tad abhāvāt ca ākāśa ādau kriyā bhāvaḥ na vibhu tva pratibandhāt tad abhāve hi guṇa karma ādau api kriyāvat tva prasaṅgāt yadi ca kasyacid sāmānya ādhārasya gamanāt sāmānyasya api gamanam tarhi tasya avasthāne avasthānañca iti na gacchet na api tiṣṭhet iti duruddharam vyasanam āpadyeta tasmāt saṃyoga vibhāga eka artha samavāyāt ādhāra gatam gamanam ādheye api āropya pratipadyate sāmānyam gacchati iti 
[II,276,14_II,276,22]	yat ca idam na yāti na ca tatra āsīt asti paścāt na ca aṃśa vat iti uktam tad sāmānya svarūpa upavarṇanam na tasya pratiṣedha param dravya svarūpa anupalambhena sāmānyasya asattve sarvasya api asattvam syāt tad itara asattvasya sarvatra aviśeṣāt sāmānyañca viśeṣeṣu anuvartamānam pratyakṣeṇa eva prasiddham iti tasya anupalambhaḥ asiddhaḥ yadi ca asattvam sāmānyasya katham sva lakṣaṇa viṣayam pratyakṣam sāmānya viṣayam anumānam iti syāt atha atad rūpa parāyatta vastu mātra prakāśanāt sāmānyam sat iti proktam liṅga bheda apratiṣṭhiteḥ iti ayam asya arthaḥ dāha pāka ādi samartha agni vyatirekiṇaḥ jala ādayaḥ atad rūpāḥ tebhyaḥ vyāvṛttasya tārṇa pārṇa ādi viśeṣa rahitasya agni mātrasya jñāpanāt sāmānya viṣayaḥ dhūmaḥ tathā dhūma jñānam api adhūma vyāvṛtta tā arṇā ādi viśeṣa rahita dhūma mātra viṣayam iti 
[II,276,26]	na etat yuktam sāmānya anabhyupagame mātrā abhidhānasya artha asambhavāt na ca apohaḥ eva mātrā abhidhānasya arthaḥ tasya avastu tvena ajanaka tvāt vastu tve ca vāstavam eva sāmānyam abhyupagatam iti kaḥ pratikūlaḥ anukūlam ācarati iti na ca agni vyaktīnām sāmarthyam tad grāhaka avinā abhāvasya eva aprasiddheḥ na ca dhūma upalambhāt agni sāmastya pratipattiḥ dṛṣṭā iti atha tārṇa ādīnām anyatamaḥ viśeṣaḥ mātrā abhidhāna viṣayaḥ tarhi katham sāmānya viṣayam anumānam na ca agni vyaktiṣu viśiṣṭa artha kriyā kāritayā samānā buddhiḥ kriyāṇām api parasparam vyāvṛtta tvāt iti ukta nyāyāt etena yat uktam liṅga liṅgi dhiyoḥ eva pāramparyeṇa vastuni pratibandhāt tad ābhāsa śūnyayoḥ api avañcanam iti etat apāstam bhavati iti tayoḥ dvayoḥ sāmānya abhāve pāramparyeṇa api vastu pratibandha abhāvāt 
[II,277,11]	na ca adhūma vyāvṛtta ākārāt vikalpāt anagni vyāvṛtta ākāraḥ vikalpaḥ tayoḥ avinā abhau asya aprasiddheḥ agni pratipattim antareṇa anagnayaḥ na pratīyante tad apratipattau na agni pratipattiḥ itaretara āśraya tva prasaṅgāt na ca kāryatvena dhūmasya gamaka tvam iti uktam vyāpti samarthana avasare tasmāt sāmānyavatām avinā abhāva prasiddheḥ anumānam icchatā avaśyam sāmānyam abhyupagantavyam anyathā hi vāstava sāmānyam vinā bhāvasya aprasiddhau saṅketa apratipatteḥ ca na anumāna śabdayoḥ pramāṇatā syāt iti asti ca tayoḥ prāmāṇyam tasmāt artha pratipattau pravartamānasya artha kriyā saṃvādena visaṃvādi nivṛttau tad vyāptasya bhrānta tvasya nivṛttiḥ iti uktam pūrvam atas sva ātma rūpa anuvṛtti pratyaya kāraṇam iti 
[II,277,21]	saṅgraha vākyasya vivaraṇam āha svarūpa abhedena eka rūpeṇa ādhāreṣu śābaleya ādi piṇḍeṣu prabandhena anuparameṇa pūrva piṇḍā parityāgena samavāya vṛttyā vartamānam anuvṛtti buddhi kāraṇam iti eka dvi bahuṣu iti asya vivaraṇam ādhāreṣu iti abheda ātmaka padasya tu svarūpa abhedena iti katham iti avyutpanna praśnaḥ viparyasta ākṣepaḥ vā tathā ca eka piṇḍa upalambha kāle na anugatam sāmānyam pratibhāti dvitīya piṇḍa upalambha kāle api prathama piṇḍasya agrahaṇāt anugata jñāna abhāvaḥ eva yatra api ekam jñānam aneka piṇḍa ālambanam tatra api anugajñānasya anupalambhaḥ eva iti ākṣepe sati pratisamādhānam āha pratipiṇḍam sāmānya apekṣam ityādi 
[II,278,1]	piṇḍam piṇḍam prati prabandhena sātatyena jñānānām utpattiḥ tasya añca satyām pūrva pūrva anubhava janita saṃskāra apekṣaḥ uttarottara pratyayaḥ abhyāsaḥ tena janitaḥ saṃskāraḥ tasmāt ca atīta jñāna prabandha pratyavekṣaṇam bhavati atītaḥ ca asau jñāna prabandhaḥ ca tasmin pratyavekṣaṇam smaraṇam bhavati jñāyate iti jñānam jñaptiḥ ca jñānam iti ubhaya viṣayam smaraṇam bhavati iti etat sadṛśaḥ mayā prāk upalabdhaḥ iti evam smaraṇāt samanugatam yat asti iti jñāyate tat sāmānyām iti tad sadṛśaḥ ayam iti pratyabhijñānāt ca yat tad sādṛśyam bhinneṣu abhinna pratyaya janakam tad sāmānyam iti vyavasthitam 
[II,278,9_II,278,15]	bhedam nirūpayati tatra sattā param sāmānyam atra ca mahā viṣaya tvāt iti uktam eva sādhanam sā tu sattā sāmānyam eva kutas yatas anuvṛtti pratyayasya eva kāraṇam yadi api abhāva ādibhyaḥ vyāvṛtti jñānasya api hetuḥ tathā api sāmānyavatsu anuvṛttām eva buddhim janayati na vyāvṛttām atas sāmānyam eva iti 
[II,278,20^1]	tatra sāmānya mātrasya sadbhāve vyavasthāpite vispaṣṭa artham sattāyāḥ sadbhāva anumānam āha yat vā pūrvam pratyakṣam uktam idānīm anumānam ucyate tatra vyāpti samarthana artham dṛṣṭāntam vyācaṣṭe yathā paraspara viśiṣṭeṣu vyāvṛtteṣu carma vastra kambala ādiṣu anyasmāt artha antara bhūtāt nīla dravya sambandhāt nīlam nīlam iti pratyaya anuvṛttiḥ tathā paraspara viśiṣṭe dravya guṇa karmasu aviśiṣṭā sat sat iti pratyaya anuvṛttiḥ iti dārṣṭa antika nirūpaṇam sā ca pratyaya anuvṛttiḥ artha antara sambandhāt bhavitum arhati yat tad artha antaram sā sattā iti siddhā sattā sambandhāt sat sat iti pratyaya anuvṛttiḥ tasmāt sāmānyam eva prayogaḥ tu dravya guṇa karmasu sat sat iti pratyayaḥ 
[II,278,20^2_II,279,21]	viśeṣya vyatirikta anugata nimitta nibandhanaḥ bhinneṣu anugata pratyayāt kambala ādiṣu nīla dravya sambandhāt nīlam nīlam iti jñāna vat sāmānyena ca viśeṣya vyatirikta anugata nimitta nibandhana tve sādhye na pācaka ādi jñānaiḥ vyabhicāraḥ teṣām api sa pakṣa tvāt tathā hi pācakaḥ iti jñāne paci kriyā nimittam tad abhijña tā vā tad sadbhāve kriyā uparame api pācakaḥ iti vyavahārāt evam daṇḍī iti jñāne daṇḍaḥ nimittam śuklaḥ iti jñāne ca guṇaḥ nimittam iti sarvatra vyatiriktam eva nimittam daṇḍa ādeḥ tu parasparam vilakṣaṇa tvāt anugata jñāna utpattau ekam abhinnam nimittam upagrāhakam abhyupagantavyam anyathā hi anugata jñāna ajanaka tvam eva syāt atas daṇḍeṣu daṇḍa tvam śukla ādiṣu ca tad sāmānyam iti vācyam yat ca idam sāmānyam sāmānyam iti anugata jñānam atra api ekatve nitya tve sati anekatra samavāyaḥ nimittam evam sarvatra nimitta antaram abhyūhyam 
[II,279,25]	aparam dravya tva guṇa tva karma tva ādi ityādi padena pṛthivī tva ādeḥ grahaṇam anuvṛtti vyāvṛtti pratyaya hetu tvāt sāmānyam viśeṣaḥ ca bhavati iti tat eva āha tatra dravya tvam paraspara viśiṣṭeṣu vyāvṛtta svarūpeṣu pṛthivī ādiṣu anuvṛtti pratyaya hetutvāt sāmānyam guṇa karmabhyaḥ vyāvṛtti pratyaya hetu tvāt viśeṣaḥ yathā dravya tvam tathā guṇa tvam api paraspara viśiṣṭeṣu rūpa ādiṣu anuvṛtti pratyaya hetutvāt sāmānyam dravya karmabhyaḥ vyāvṛtti pratyaya hetu tvāt viśeṣaḥ tathā karma tvam paraspara viśiṣṭeṣu utkṣepaṇa ādiṣu anuvṛtti pratyaya hetu tvāt sāmānyam dravya guṇebhyaḥ vyāvṛtti pratyaya hetu tvāt viśeṣaḥ evam pṛthivī tva rūpatva utkṣepaṇa tva go tva ghaṭa tva paṭa tva ādīnām api prāṇi aprāṇi gatānām anuvṛtti vyāvṛtti pratyaya hetutvāt sāmānya viśeṣa bhāvaḥ siddhaḥ iti atideśaḥ prāṇa sambandhini piṇḍe gatāni go tva aśva tva ādīni aprāṇi gatāni pṛthivī tva ādīni prāṇa śūnya ādhāra gatāni sva bhede anuvṛtti pratyaya hetu tvāt bheda antarāt vyāvṛtti pratyaya hetu tvāt ca teṣām sāmānya viśeṣa bhāvaḥ siddhaḥ iti 
[II,280,12]	na ca ekasya vastunaḥ dvairūpya anupalabdheḥ katham tat eva sāmānyam viśeṣaḥ ca iti atha ekam atra pāramārthikam anyat ca upacaritam iti avirodhaḥ tatra kim mukhya vṛttyā sāmānyāni viśeṣāḥ vā iti āha etāni dravya tva ādīni prabhūta viṣaya tvāt prādhānyena mukhya vṛttyā sāmānyāni na hi viśeṣāṇām prabhūta viṣaya tvam sambhavati ekaika dravya vṛtti tvāt sva āśraya viśeṣaka tvāt bhaktyā upacāreṇa viśeṣa ākhyāni iti vyāvṛtti pratyaya janaka tvam viśeṣāṇām svarūpam tasya iha api upalabdheḥ upacāraḥ pravartate eva tathā hi dravya tva ādi sāmānyam sva āśrayam āśraya antarāt vyāvṛttam viśinaṣṭi vyāvartayati iti iti atas viśeṣa ākhyām api labhate 
[II,280,20_II,280,26]	atha dravya tva ādīni dravya guṇa karmabhyaḥ artha antaram svarūpāṇi vā iti āha lakṣaṇa bhedāt eṣām dravya guṇa karmabhyaḥ padārtha antara tvam siddham tat ca uktam abheda ātmakam aneka vṛtti iti padena atas eva ca nitya tvam yatas eva dravya ādibhyaḥ padārtha antara tvam atas eva ca nitya tvam dravya guṇa karma ātmakasya bhāvasya anitya tva upalabdheḥ 
[II,281,4]	nanu ca anutpattimat tvena nitya tvam na dravya ādibhyaḥ padārtha antara tvena sāmānya ādi trayasya api nitya tvena sādhya tvāt na etat evam yatas dravya ādibhyaḥ vibhinna svarūpa sambandhi tvena pratibhāsanāt artha antara tvam atas eva ca nitya tvam utpatti vināśa kāraṇā sambhavāt tathā hi sāmānyasya utpatti kāraṇam na asti tad ādhārāṇām yugapada sambhavena samavāyi kāraṇa abhāvāt iti evam nirṇītam padārtha saṅkare 
[II,281,10]	atha ekam eva sāmānyam sattā lakṣaṇam upādhi bhedāt bhinna pratyaya sampādakam iti etasya nirāsa artham āha dravya ādiṣu vṛtti niyamāt pratyaya bhedāt ca parasparataḥ ca anya tvam iti dravyeṣu eva dravya tvam guṇeṣu eva guṇa tvam ityādi vṛtti niyamaḥ pratyaya bhedaḥ tu dravyeṣu eva dravyam dravyam iti dravya tva vaśāt jñānam guṇeṣu ca guṇa tva yogāt guṇaḥ guṇaḥ ityādi tasmāt pratyaya bhedāt dravya ādiṣu vṛtti niyamāt ca parasparataḥ api anya tvam anyathā hi sarva padārtheṣu eka tvāt sāmānyasya vṛtti niyamaḥ pratyaya bhedaḥ ca na syāt 
[II,281,17]	atha astu parasparataḥ anya tvam tathā api sva āśrayeṣu dravyam iti dravya tva vaśāt jñānam guṇeṣu ca guṇaḥ ityādi yasmāt tat kim ekam anekam vā iti āśaṅkā nirāsāya āha pratyekam sva āśrayeṣu ekam dravya tvam guṇeṣu ekam guṇa tvam iti evam śeṣeṣu api iti kutas etat lakṣaṇa aviśeṣāt anugata svarūpā viśeṣāt yat vā lakṣyate anena iti vā lakṣaṇam dravyam dravyam ityādi anugata jñānam tasya aviśeṣāt eva dravyeṣu dravya tvam guṇeṣu guṇa tvam anyathā hi ananugata jñānam eva syāt 
[II,281,23]	atha rūpa bhedānām aneka tve api rūpam rūpam iti jñānam asti satyam etat nīla ādi jñānasya bheda vyavasthāpakasya upapatteḥ na ca evam atra bheda vyavasthāpakam pramāṇam asti iti āha viśeṣa lakṣaṇa abhāvāt ca ekatvam iti atha ekasmin eva deśe samutpadyamānasya ghaṭa ādeḥ pratiniyata sāmānya sambandhe hetuḥ vācyaḥ anyathā hi aniyata deśa tvāt sāmānyānām niyatena dharmiṇā sambandhaḥ na syāt iti āha yadi api aparicchinna deśāni sāmānyāni tathā api upalakṣaṇa niyamāt kāraṇa sāmagrī niyamāt ca sva viṣaya sarva gatāni iti upalakṣyate anena iti upalakṣaṇam anugata jñānam eva tathā hi dravyam dravyam iti anugatam jñānam dravyeṣu eva na guṇa ādau atas sva viṣaya sarva gatam eva dravya tvam viṣaya antare tad sadbhāve pramāṇa abhāvāt evam guṇa tva ādau api iti upalakṣaṇam sāmānya abhivyañjakam vā tat niyamāt sva viṣaya sarva gatam tathā hi sāsna ādi upalakṣita piṇḍasya go tvena abhisambandhaḥ kesara ādi upalakṣitasya aśva tvena abhisambandhaḥ iti evam sarvatra niyatam sat vyañjakam abhyūhyam 
[II,282,9]	atha astu vyañjaka niyamāt sva viṣayaḥ eva upalambhāt sva viṣaya sarva gata tvam atra kāraṇam vācyam niyāmaka abhāve niyata āśraya sambandhasya eva abhāva prasaṅgāt iti āha kāraka sāmagrī niyamāt ca sva viṣaya sarva gatam iti tathā hi go tva jāti sambandha upabhogi tva prāpaka adṛṣṭa upalakṣita sāmagrī sampāditaḥ gopiṇḍaḥ na aśva ādi itaraḥ tad niyamāt saḥ eva go tvena abhisambadhyate na anyaḥ tathā aśva tva jāti sambandha upabhoga prāpaka adṛṣṭa upalakṣita sāmagrī janya tvāt aśvapiṇḍaḥ aśva tvena abhisambadhyate iti evam anyatrā api iti atas yat uktam yatra asau vartate bhāvaḥ tena sambadhyate na tu ityādi tad apāstam niyata āśraya samavetasya eva upalambha siddhau niyama kāraṇasya anabhidhānāt 
[II,282,18_II,282,22]	yat ca idam kim gaurga utvena abhisambadhyate atha agauḥ iti codyam tat na pratisamādhāna arham niṣṭhā sambandhayoḥ eka kāla tvāt iti sva kāraṇaiḥ sattā ādibhiḥ ca piṇḍasya abhisambandhaḥ eva ātma lābhaḥ na pūrvam tasya go rūpatā ago rūpatā vā tad sattvasya eva asambhavāt atha yayā maṇi mantra auṣadha ādīni viśiṣṭa artha kriyā sampādana samarthāni sva kāraṇāt utpannāni evam gopiṇḍāḥ gauriti jñāna utpādana samarthāḥ sva kāraṇāt eva utpannāḥ na aśva ādi jñānam utpādayanti iti ced tarhi yat tat sāmarthyam yena satā gauḥ iti anugata jñānam utpādayanti tat yadi artha antaram saṃjñā bheda mātram avyatireke tu anugata jñāna abhāva prasaṅgaḥ tasmāt anugatasya vastunaḥ pratyakṣeṇa pratibhāsanāt sāmānya nirākaraṇe sarvam dūṣaṇam asādhanam eva iti 
[II,283,1]	atha sva viṣaya sarva gata tve gopiṇḍayoḥ antarāle api sāmānyam upalabhyeta na ca etat tat asti tasmāt katham sva viṣaya sarva gatam iti āśaṅkya āha antarāle ca saṃyoga samavāya vṛtti abhāvāt avyapadeśyāni iti saṃyukta samavāyena go tva ādi sāmānyasya upalambhāt go tvam iti vyapadeśaḥ na ca asau iha asti atas avyapadeśyāni iti tathā kim idam antarālam nāma yatra sāmānyasya upalambha prasaṅgaḥ codyate yadi mūrta dravya abhāvaḥ na tatra go tva ādi sāmānyam abhāva tvāt eva atha śabda anumeyam atīndriyam ākāśam antarāla avasthitam vā ghaṭa ādi dravyam tatra api na go tva ādeḥ samavāye pramāṇam asti iti anupalambhaḥ ghaṭataḥ iti alam 
[II,283,11_II,284,6^1]	ca ayoga jāḥ ddharmāt aśukle śukla pratyayaḥ san jāyate atyanta adṛṣṭe ca pratyabhijñānam yadi syāt mithyā bhavet tathā iha āpi antyaviśeṣam antareṇa yoginām na yoga jāt dharmāt pratyaya vyāvṛttiḥ pratyabhijñānam vā bhavitum arhati ) viśeṣāṇām parīkṣā artham āha anteṣu bhavāḥ antyāḥ sva āśraya viśeṣaka tvāt viśeṣāḥ iti utpatti vināśayoḥ ante vyavasthita tvāt anta śabda vācyāni nitya dravyāṇi iti tathā hi paramāṇūn avadhim kṛtvā dvi aṇuka ādi kāryasya utpattiḥ tathā pṛthivī ādīnām api tāvat utpādaḥ yāvat ākāśa ādi iti pāṭhā apekṣayā tasya api anta śabda vācya tvam evam vināśa ante vyavasthānam paramāṇu ādīnām tathā ca tāvat dravyam vinaśyati yāvat paramāṇavaḥ pāṭhā apekṣayā pṛthivī ādīnām api ākāśa ādikam yāvat vināśaḥ iti teṣu bhavāḥ tad vṛttayaḥ antyāḥ iti apadiśyante tathā hi bhūḥ iti ayam dhātuḥ sattāyām vā api upalabdhau 
[II,284,6^2]	yathā idānīm devadattaḥ gṛhe bhavati āste iti saṅgraha ukteḥ vivaraṇam āha vināśa ārambha rahiteṣu ityādi tatra anta padasya vivaraṇam vināśa ārambha rahiteṣu nitya dravyeṣu eva aṇu ākāśa kāla diś ātma manassu iti viśeṣa saṃjñāyāḥ nirdeśaḥ spaṣṭa artham pratyaya artham vyācaṣṭe pratidravyam ekaikaśas vartamānāḥ iti dravyam dravyam pratyeka ekaḥ viśeṣaḥ vartate na ekasmin anekaḥ vaiyarthya prasaṅgāt tathā ca ekena eva viśeṣeṇa vyāvṛtta pratyayasya janita tvāt viśeṣa antara vaiyarthyam eva na api ekaḥ anekasmin sāmānya rūpa tā prasaṅgāt iti dvitīya padasya tu vivaraṇam atyanta vyāvṛtti buddhi hetavaḥ iti nitya dravyeṣu eva vartante eva iti ayoga ani ayoga vyavacchedena nityeṣu vartamāna tvāt viśeṣāḥ itarasmāt bhidyante iti lakṣaṇam pūrvam eva uktam 
[II,284,23]	atha viśeṣāṇām sadbhāve kim pramāṇam anumānam tatra vyāpti samarthana artham dṛṣṭāntam nirūpayati yathā asmad ādīnām gavā ādiṣu aśva ādibhyaḥ pratyaya vyāvṛttiḥ dṛṣṭā tulya ākṛti guṇāt api sajātīyāt vyāvṛtta tad kriyā avayava saṃyoga nimittā tatra jāti nimittā pratyaya vyāvṛttiḥ yasmāt gaurayam atas aśva ādi vilakṣaṇaḥ iti sajātīya tve api kṛṣṇa ādi guṇa sambandhibhyaḥ śuklaḥ iti pratyaya vyāvṛttiḥ tathā śīghra gatiḥ iti kriyā viśeṣa nimittā tena hi satā samāna guṇāt api sajātīyāt vyāvartate iti pīnaḥ iti avayava upacaya nimittā tena satā samāna guṇa kriyāt api samāna jātīyāt vyāvartate kakudmān iti avayava viśeṣa nimittā tena satā anyasmāt vilakṣaṇa pratyaya jananāt iti mahāghaṇṭaḥ iti saṃyoga nimittā tad sadbhāve vyāvṛtta pratyaya jananāt 
[II,285,6^1]	tat dārṣṭa antika vyākhya artham āha asmat viśiṣṭānām yoginām nityeṣu tulya ākṛti guṇa kriyeṣu paramāṇuṣu mukta ātma manassu ca pratyaya vyāvṛttiḥ etasmāt vilakṣaṇaḥ ayam vilakṣaṇaḥ ayam iti dṛṣṭā sā ca anya nimitta asambhavāt viśeṣa sambandhāt eva bhavati iti tathā ca tulya ākṛti guṇa kriyā dhārāḥ paramāṇavaḥ viśeṣa sambandhinaḥ vyāvṛtta jñāna viṣaya tvāt gavā ādi vat na ca gavā ādiṣu iva jāti guṇa kriyā ātmakāḥ eva viśeṣāḥ bhaviṣyanti iti vācyam 
[II,285,6^2]	samāna jāti guṇa kriyā ādhāra tvena viśeṣita tvāt iti tathā api sarve taijasāḥ paramāṇavaḥ tejaḥ tu asambandhinaḥ samāna guṇa ādhārāḥ samāna akriyā sambandhinaḥ ca pakṣīkṛtāḥ iti na teṣu tad nimittā pratyaya vyāvṛttiḥ tathā ca bhāsvaram rūpam uṣṇa sparśaḥ parimāṇam ekatva eka pṛthaktva ādayaḥ sādhāraṇa tvāt na vyāvṛtta jñāna hetavaḥ kriyā api vāta āhatānām eka diś abhimukha tayā gamanāt sādhāraṇa tayā vailakṣaṇya pratipattau na kāraṇam atas dravya ādi svarūpasya viśeṣasya asambhavāt yatas nimittāt pratyaya vyāvṛttiḥ te antyāḥ viśeṣāḥ tathā mukta ātmānaḥ mukta manāṃsi ca vyāvṛtta jñāna viṣaya tvāt viśeṣam apekṣante śarīra sambandhasya ca atyantam vyāvṛtteḥ na ātmani buddhi ādi viśeṣaḥ vyāvṛtta jñāna hetuḥ asambhavāt manasaḥ api śarīra sambandha śūnyasya saṃkhyā ādi guṇānām sādhāraṇa tvāt viśeṣam vinā na vyāvṛtta jñāna utpattau kāraṇam asti iti yathā ukta viśeṣaṇa adhyāsiteṣu vyāvṛtta pratyayaḥ viśeṣa kāryaḥ vyāvṛtta pratyaya tvāt gavā ādi vyāvṛtta pratyaya vat 
[II,285,24]	atha atīndriya tvāt paramāṇu ādeḥ vyāvṛtta jñāna viṣaya tve kim pramāṇam anumānam eva tathā hi paramāṇu ādayaḥ vyāvṛtta jñāna viṣayāḥ dravya tvāt gavā ādi vat saṃśaya viṣaya tvañca paramāṇu ādeḥ sattā sambandhi tvāt sthāṇu ādi vat yatra ca saṃśayaḥ tatra avaśyam nirṇayaḥ iti paramāṇu ādayaḥ viśeṣa sambandhinaḥ nirṇaya viṣaya tvāt sthāṇu ādi vat eva atas idam āha anya nimitta asambhavāt yebhyaḥ nimittebhyaḥ pratyādhāram vilakṣaṇaḥ ayam vilakṣaṇaḥ ayam iti pratyaya vyāvṛttiḥ te antyāḥ viśeṣāḥ tathā deśa kāla viprakṛṣṭe adṛṣṭe paramāṇau saḥ eva ayam iti pratyayaḥ pramāṇam viśeṣa sambandhe sati pratyabhijñānasya devadatta ādau upalabdheḥ atas vyāvṛtta pratyaya viṣaya tvāt pratyabhijñāyamāna tvāt ca paramāṇu ādeḥ viśeṣa sambandhi tvam asti ca yoginām pūrva upalabdhe paramāṇau saḥ eva ayam paramāṇuḥ yaḥ pañca purā avasthitaḥ vasanta samaya upalabdhaḥ iti 
[II,286,7_II,286,13]	atha itaretara abhāvāt pṛthaktvāt vā pratyaya vyāvṛttiḥ pratyabhijñānam vā iti na tatas anyaḥ viśeṣaḥ iti ced na tad upalambhe api sthāṇu ādau saṃśaya darśanāt tathā hi itaretara abhāva upalabdhau pṛthaktvā upalambhe ca sati sāmānya darśana ādibhyaḥ kim ayam sthāṇuḥ puruṣaḥ vā iti saṃśayaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ tad vyatirikta śiraḥ pāṇi ādi viśeṣa upalambhe ca sati puruṣaḥ eva ayam iti ca nirṇaya darśanāt itaretarābhāva pṛthaktvā anyaḥ eva viśeṣaḥ paramāṇu ādau vācyaḥ iti anye tu itaretarābhāvasya niṣidhyamāna jñāna janaka tvam eva vyāvṛtta jñānañca tasmāt vilakṣaṇam atas nimitta antara kāryam iti manyante pṛthaktva vaśāt ca pṛthak iti vyavahāraḥ na vilakṣaṇaḥ iti 
[II,286,16]	atha yoginām yoga ja dharma ādeḥ pratyaya vyāvṛttiḥ pratyabhijñānañca iti tat eva āha yadi punar antya viśeṣam antareṇa yoginām yoga ja dharmāt pratyaya vyāvṛttiḥ pratyabhijñānañca syāt kaḥ doṣaḥ tat āha evam na eva bhavati iti yathā ca ayoga jāt dharmāt aśukle śukla pratyayaḥ san jāyate atyanta adṛṣṭa pūrve ca pratyabhijñānañca iti yadi kadācid syāt yogi nām aśukle śukla pratyayaḥ pratyabhijñānañca mithyā bhavet tathā iha āpi antyaviśeṣam antareṇa yoga ja dharmāt na pratyaya vyāvṛttiḥ pratyabhijñānam vā bhavitum arhati iti 
[II,286,23^1]	atha antya viśeṣāṇām paramāṇūnām iva vyāvṛtta jñāna viṣaya tvāt viśeṣa antara sambandhe tatra api anyaḥ viśeṣaḥ tatra api anyaḥ iti anavasthā syāt na ca vyāvṛtta pratyaya viṣaya tve samāne api paramāṇūnām eva ayam viṣaya sambandhaḥ na viśeṣāṇām iti viśeṣa hetuḥ asti iti abhyupagame vā viśeṣeṣu viśeṣa antara sambandham vinā vyāvṛtta pratyaya vat paramāṇuṣu api syāt iti āha atha antya viśeṣeṣu iva paramāṇuṣu kasmāt na svatas pratyaya vyāvṛttiḥ kalpyate iti asya pratiṣedha artham āha yat uktam paramāṇuṣu viśeṣa abhāvaḥ viśeṣeṣu ca viśeṣa antaram iti etat na kutas etat 
[II,286,23^2]	tādātmyāt tad svarūpa tvāt viśeṣāṇām ye hi aviśeṣa svarūpāḥ te vyāvṛtta jñāna janmani viśeṣam apekṣante yathā paramāṇu ādayaḥ na ca evam viśeṣāḥ tad ātmakāḥ na bhavanti atas tāt ātmyāt viśeṣāḥ samāna lakṣaṇam viśeṣam na apekṣante tathā ca iha atad a ātmakeṣu atad svarūpeṣu anya nimittaḥ pratyayaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ yathā ghaṭa ādiṣu pradīpāt tathā hi ghaṭa ādiṣu aprakāśa svarūpeṣu anvaya vyatirekābhyām pradīpāt vijñānam dṛṣṭam na tu pradīpe pradīpāt tasya prakāśa rūpa tayā pradīpam vinā api prakāśanāt na ca evam ghaṭa ādiṣu api prakāśam vinā eva prakāśaḥ astu adarśanāt āgamikam udāharaṇam darśayati yathā gavāśva māṃsa ādīnām svatas eva aśuci tvam tad yogāt anyeṣām modaka ādīnām na tu śva māṃsasya api aśuci antara sambandhāt aśuci tvam adarśanāt na api śva māṃsa vat bhakta ādīnām api svatas eva aśuci tvam adarśanāt eva tathā iha api tādātmyāt viśeṣa svarūpa tvāt antya viśeṣeṣu svatas eva pratyaya vyāvṛttiḥ tad yogāt paramāṇuṣu iti upasaṃhāraḥ 
[II,287,15]	atha viśeṣāṇām nitya tvam uta anitya tvam utpatti vināśa kāraṇa anupalabdheḥ nitya tvam eva tathā hi viśeṣāṇām sva āśrayaḥ samavāyi kāraṇam asamavāyyādikāraṇañca na asti iti vināśa abhyupagame api viśeṣāṇām punar vyāvṛtti jñāna utpattau na kāraṇam asti iti atha viśeṣa antarāt vyāvṛtta jñānam tat na anya tve pramāṇa abhāvāt iti alam ati vistareṇa 
[II,287,23_II,289,10^1]	atha samavāyasya lakṣaṇa parīkṣā artham ayuta siddhānām ityādi prakaraṇam ayutasiddhānām eva ādhārya ādhāra bhūtānām eva yaḥ sambandhaḥ sa samavāyaḥ iti lakṣaṇam vyākhyātam eva atha keṣām ayuta siddhānām asau sambandhaḥ tat āha dravya guṇa karma sāmānya viśeṣāṇām aniyama upadarśana artham kārya kāraṇa bhūtānāntu paṭa ādīnām akārya kāraṇa bhūta anāñca sāmānya ādi tadvatām iti ayuta siddhānāmādhārya ādhāra bhūtānām iti ca ayam niyamaḥ iha idam iti buddhiḥ yatas nimittāt bhavati sa samavāya ākhyaḥ sambandhaḥ tathā ca sūtram iha idam iti yatas kārya kāraṇayoḥ sa samavāyaḥ iti iha iti adhikaraṇam idam iti ādheyam tayoḥ sambandham vinā iha idam buddhiḥ na bhavati iti yatas ca asarva gatānām iti niyama āśaṅkā nirāsa artham tathā hi sarva gatānām api ākāśa ādīnām sva guṇa ādibhiḥ samavāya upalabdheḥ asarva gatānām iti vākyam niyama āśaṅkā nirāsa artham vyākhyeyam tathā ca sarva gatānām eva samavāyaḥ iti ayam niyamaḥ na ghaṭate 
[II,289,10^2]	yatas ca asarva gatānām api samavāyaḥ dṛśyate iti caśabdasya ca anukta samuccaya artha tvāt asarva gatānām sarva gatānāñca iti labhyate adhigata anyatvānām iti adhigatam anya tvam nānātvam yeṣām te tathā uktāḥ teṣām iti tādātmya vyudāsaḥ tathā api adhigata anyatva āgavāśva ādayaḥ bhavanti iti aviṣvagbhāvena avasthitānām iti padam aviṣvagbhāvaḥ apṛthagbhāvaḥ deśāpṛthaktvam na tu abhedaḥ svarūpa bhedasya upalabdheḥ tathā hi tantavaḥ vibhinna jāti sambandhinaḥ vibhinna svarūpāḥ ca pṛthaktve paṭaḥ api evam iti parasparataḥ anya tvam eva viruddha dharma adhyāsāt pratibhāsa bhedāt ca iti tathā ca rūpa ādayaḥ api viruddha dharma adhyāsāt ca bhidyante sa ca tantu paṭa ādīnām asti iti anya tvam eva sūtram api evam vyākhyeyam kārya kāraṇayoḥ ekatva pṛthaktva abhāvāt parasparam pratibhāsa bhedāt ekatva pṛthaka tve na vidyete tasmāt adhigata anyatvānām aviṣvagbhāvena avasthitānām iha idam iti buddhiḥ yatas sambandhāt bhavati sa samavāya ākhyaḥ sambandhaḥ katham iti avyutpanna praśnaḥ viparyasta ākṣepaḥ vā tathā ca na samavāya sadbhāve pramāṇam asti iti 
[II,290,11_II,290,15]	sarvam etat asambaddham atha iha buddhiḥ pramāṇam na tasyāḥ samavāya ālambana tvam ādhāra viṣaya tvāt tat uktam iha iti ca anayā buddhyā samavāyaḥ na gṛhyate ādhāra grāhiṇī ca eṣā samavāya apratiṣṭhitā atha sambandha nimittā sa tu tādātmya lakṣaṇaḥ eva bhaviṣyati samavāya pakṣe bādhaka upapatteḥ tathā hi na aniṣpannayoḥ samavāyaḥ ghaṭate sambadhya bhāve sambandhasya adarśanāt atha niṣpannayoḥ sambandhaḥ samavāyaḥ tarhi yuta siddhiḥ syāt tathā samavāyasya api sambandha anabhyupagame sarvatas anya tva aviśeṣāt anayoḥ sambandhinoḥ sambandhaḥ na padārtha antarāṇām iti pratiniyame hetuḥ na asti iti athavā gṛhītam viśeṣaṇam viśeṣya jñāna utpattau liṅgañca liṅgi jñāna utpattau vyāpriyate samavāye tu tad rūpa tā na asti iti tad grahaṇe pramāṇa abhāvaḥ tathā hi iha tantuṣu paṭaḥ iti jñānam ādheya anurakta ādhāram viśeṣayan na samavāya anuraktam iti sva ātma gata saṃvedana abhāvāt iha buddhau apratyakṣaḥ eva samavāyaḥ nirvikalpake tu avayava a ayavinoḥ saṃśleṣa jñāne samavāyaḥ pratyakṣaḥ eva kevalam iha iti buddheḥ sambandha nimitta tvena anyatra upalabdheḥ iha api tad upalambhāt anumānam pravartate yatas evam tasmāt ihabuddhi anumeyaḥ samavāyaḥ na tu ihabuddhau pratyakṣaḥ iti upasaṃhāraḥ 
[II,291,1_II,291,4]	grantha parisamāptau ca santoṣāt ācāryaḥ punar aparasya guroḥ namaskāram karoti yoga ācāra vibhūtyā yaḥ toṣayitvā maheśvaram cakre vaiśeṣikam śāstram tasmai kaṇabhuje namaḥ iti iti viracitam etat vyoma nāmnā śivena pratihata para pakṣam sva artha siddhau samartham kaṇacara mata vṛtteḥ vartanam bādha
